śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ /
tantravārtikam /
āmrāyasya kriyārthatvādānarthakyamatadarthānāṃ tasmādanityamucyate 
siddhapramāṇabhāvasya dharme vedasya sarvaśaḥ /
yarthavāda mantrāṇāmupayogo 'dhunocyate 
tathā phalābhāvāt 
yadi tāvadgargatrirātrabrāhmaṇavedānumantraṇajñānakāle vidyamānayoreva mukhaśobhāvājijanmanoḥ saṃkīrtanaṃ na dharmaṃ prati pramāṇyam /
 atha tvavidyamānayostataḥ svārthe 'pi /
vartamānāpadeśācca pratyakṣānupalabdhivirodhaḥ karmānuṣṭhānayogyapuruṣakaraṇādvidyāsaṃskārasya dīkṣitatīrthasnānādivannirākāṅkṣatvāt phalavidhitvaṃ nirākariṣyate /
paunaruktyāttatra na vicārayitavyamata āha tena phalavidhitvānnirākṛtasyehā nartha kyārthavādatvavicāra iti /
stutyarthatāpi cāsatyasya nāstīti vyavasthitameva 
abhāgipratiṣedhāt 
trīṇyapi pṛthivyādivacanāni apratiṣedhabhāginamarthaṃ pratiṣedhanti /
antarikṣe divi ca tāvadaprāptatvātpratiṣedhāviṣayatvam /
ataśca paryudasitavyābhāvānna paryudāsaḥ /
anantarikṣe  hyadivi ca pṛthivyāṃ nityaṃ cayanaṃ prāptamiti tadvidhiranarthako 'thāpi nityānuvādastathāpya kriyārthatvameva /
pṛthivīcayanapratiṣedhaparyudāsau tu cayana vidhyabādhenāśakyau /
bādhe ca vidhyānarthakyam /
vika lpe'pi pakṣe bādhaḥ /
kāmasaṃyogāccāgnerastyeva pākṣikatvam /
durbalaśca pratiṣedhaḥ /
pṛthivīparatve sati cayane kalpyatvāt /
etadevāsya svayamākulatvam/
vidhyanantarameva hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya ce tavyamiṣṭakābhiragniṃ cinutaetaccākulayet /
prarocanābuddhistu naivotpadyate 
vidhinā tvekavākyatvātstutyarthatvena vidhīnāṃ syuḥ 
pūrvapaścodāhṛteṣveva vākyeṣu siddhānte 'bhidhātavye kimarthaṃ vāyavyavākyama panyasyate /
ke cidāḥ /
samānanyāyatvādidamapi tatra tānyapi cehodāhṛtāni draṣṭavyānīti /
yadyapyevaṃ tathāpyapūrvodāharaṇamabhiprāyāntaramākāṅkṣati /
tadabhidhīyate /
pūrvodāhṛteṣu sarvatra svārthāsatyatvamapyāśa ṅkyate /
tatra kaḥ prathamameva tatpratipādanakleśamaṅgīkuryāditi prasiddha svārtha satyatvānāṃ stutidvāraikavākyabhāvena dharmapramāṇaśeṣatvamātrapratipattisau karyārthaṃ vāyavyavākyopanyāsaḥ /
tatra bhāṣyakārāḥ prasiddhenaivai kavākyatvena stutya rthopayogaṃ vadanti /
etāvattvatra prathamaṃ vaktavyam /
kimarthaṃ rūpabhaṅgo na balādekavākyatā puruṣārthatvaṃ vā vedasyocyataiti /
laukiprathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
kavākyetu dṛṣṭatvāditi yadyucyeta tatrābhidhīyate /
yuktaṃ loke vākyārthasya pramāṇāntaragamyatvādanyathāpi kalpanamiha tvatyantātīndriyatvādyathāśrutādoṣadapyanyathātve pauruṣeyatvamāpadyeta /
loke'pi ca yāni pramāṇāntarānavagatārthāni āptapratyayamātreṇa śrotṛṇāṃ pramāṇāni bhavanti teṣāṃ naivānyathātvakalpanaṃ la bhyate /
tatra ke cidvadanti /
tulyaṃ ca sāṃpradāyikamiti yadvakṣyati tena samasto vedaḥ puruṣārtha iti sādhyate /
na hyātmānupakāriṇaḥ santamenaṃ buddhipūrvakāriṇaḥ puruṣāḥ prayatne na dhārayeyuḥ /
yadyapi ca keṣāṃ cidajñānaṃ bhavettathā pyasmatpūrvātikrāntānekaparīkṣaka pramādakalpanā niṣpramāṇikā /
tasmādyathāyathā puruṣārthatā bhavati tathātathā bhakkāpirūpaṃ vyākhyāyataiti /
na tvetadyuṛmiva /
kutaḥ puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt /
yadi hyārānupāto'pyartho'smadādibhirevaṃ kalpyate /
yasmādayaṃ prayatnena dhārayāmastasmādasya puṣārthateti /
tathāsatyātmaceṣṭitavaśena prāmāṇyamabhyu pagataṃ syāt /
atha puruṣāntaradhāraṇamucyeta evamapi tadaśena tairapyevamanyavaśenetyanāditvepi satyandhaparaṃparānyāyena sarveṣāṃ parapratyayānna kacitprāmāṇyāvasthānam/
sarvatra hyevamayaṃ puruṣo vedeti pratyayo naivamayamartha iti /
tena yadyapi teṣu teṣvadhyeṭaṣu nūnaṃ puruṣārthaṃ vedaṃ manyantaityabhiprāyo 'numīyate /
tathāpi nimūlatvāttanmātreṇāsiddhiḥ/
ato yāvadveda eva puruṣārthatayā sakalamātmānaṃ na pratipādayati tāvadapramāṇam /
taducyate /
sakalasya tāvadvedasya svādhyāyo'dhyetavya ityadhyayanabhāvanā vidhīyate /
tatra kiṃ bhāvayedityapekṣāyāmadhyayanamityāgatamapi puruṣapravarttanāśaktiyuktena vidhāyakenāpuruṣārthasādhyāyāṃ bhāvanāyāṃ pravarttanāśaktiprasaktastadaṃśātantravārtika /
nnirākriyate /
tataścādhyayanenetya virodhātsaṃnidheśca karaṇāṃśe niviśate /
tena kimityapecine yaccakyata ityupabandhādaścaragrahaṇamityāpatati /
tasyāpyapuruṣārthatvāttena kimiti padāvadhāraṇamityapatiṣṭhate tenāpi padārthajñānaṃ tena vākyārthajñānaṃ tena cānuṣṭhānamanuṣṭānena svargādiphalaprāptirityetāvati prāpte nirākāṅkṣī bhavati/
evaṃ sarvavidhīnāṃ prāk puruṣārthalābhādaparyavasānam/
na ca sahasaiva vidhidarśanātvargādyeva phalaṃ kalpyate /
yogyatayā hi yasya yatrānantarabhāvini vyāpāro lakṣyate tadeva tasya kāryamityavadhāryate /
tatra yadi tāvattadanusāreṇaiva kiyatyapyadhvani phalamāsādyate tato nāntarakalpanamarhati /
pāraṃparyaprayojanenāpi śrutavidhyupapattyā 'nyathānupapattilakṣaṇārthāpattyanutpādāt /
yatra tvanantaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kāryaṃ na svayaṃ puruṣārtho nāpi pāraṃparyeṇa tamānoti yathā homasyāhavanīyaprāptirbhasmasādbhāvo vā tatra tadatikrameṇa sākṣātkarmaṇa evādṛṣṭakalpanā /
sarvatra caitanaścayitavyam /
yatra tu vihite phalākāṅkṣiṇi tadanātmaka kārya paraṃparāyāṃ satyāmāntarālikaṃ kiṃ citkratave puruṣārthāya vā codyate tatra tadeva tatsādhanaṃ pūrvasya tu vidhestadupakārārthatayā paryavasānam /
yāni tūttaravidheḥ kāryāṇi prāktāni sādhyasādhanabhāvenācodinatvān nāntarīyakatvena kāṣṭhādīnāmiva jvalanādīni pūrvavihita karmasvavyāpāramātratayā mantavyāni /
yatra tu pāraṃparyajanyaṃ na kiṃ cidantarā vidhīyate tatra sarvāṇi svavyāpārīkṛtya vi dheyasyaiva svayaṃ phalasādhanatā /
tatra yāni tāvatklapta kalpayiṣyamāpāpuruṣārthasādhana vidhivākyāni tāni tatpratipādanaṃ yāvatsvādhyāyādhyayana vidhinā noyante paratastu phalavatvaṃ jñātameveti na ta prathamādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
dyāvatprāpyante/
yāni tu tatprakaraṇe padyante tānyapi tathaivācaragrahaṇādikrameṇa svārthāvabodhanaṃ yāvadgatāni na sākṣātkratvaṅgaṃ bhavanti /
kutaḥ /
kathamityadṛṣṭopāyāpekṣeṇa kratunā dṛṣṭārthatvādaśarādiṣvanavasajatā tahiddinaṃ karmamātrameva hi prayojanadvāreṇopādīyate nānyat /
ataḥ pradhānavākyatulyānyaṅgāni bhavanti /
tadākyāni tu bāhyatarā eyadhyayanādivat /
evaṃ prokṣaṇādivākyānāṃ trīhyādisaṃskāramātraphalāvasitānāṃ tandulapiṣṭapuroḍāśayavadānādibhirvyavahitataraḥ pradhānasaṃbandhaḥ /
evamevānārabhyādhītārādupakārakasāmavāyikāṅgavākyāni yojayitavyāni /
tatra tvetāvānviśeṣaḥ /
yadaprakaraṇasthatvādārā eyaspaśan pradhānamarthaireva saṃbaddhyate /
yāni tvādhānādivākyāni tānyapi phalavatkratvaṅgāhavanīyādisaṃskārapratipādanāvasāyoni dūrasthenaiva phalena nirākāṅkṣīkriyante/
etena kāryakartapratipādanahāraṇo paniṣadāṃ nairākāṅkṣacaṃ vyākhyātam /
mantranāmadheyayostu svādhikāre yojanā vacyate /
tena sarveṣāṃ bhāvanāntargatirupapannā /
yattvarthavādānāṃ bhāvanāṃśatrayānantaḥ pātitvādagrahaṇamiti /
tatrābhidhīyate /
satyamatiriktaṃ na gṛhyate/
astitvantargatiḥ/
katham /
iha hi liṅādiyukteṣu vākyeṣu dve bhāvane gamyete /
śabdātmikā cārthātmikā cātatrārthātmikayā 'rthavādā nāpekṣyante śabdātmikayā tu grahīṣyante /
sā hyevaṃ pravarttate /
svādhyāyādhyayanavidhinetare sarve vidhāyakāḥ svādhyāyapadopāttaścātmā niyujyate bhāvayediti /
tatra liṅādīnāṃ prayojakakarttṛtvaṃ puruṣaḥ prayojyaḥ tena kimityapekṣāyāṃ puruṣapravarttanamiti saṃbaddhyate/
atha tu yogyatathaiva liṅādiviṣayā kriyocyate pravarttayediti tataḥ kimityape kena ścite puruṣa mityeva saṃbaddhyate /
yadyapi cācetanatvāliṅādiṣvevaṃvidhaṃ prayojakatvaṃ na saṃbhavati tathāpi puruṣasya prayojyasya prayojakatvānupapattestadgata caitanyadvāreṇa vidhāyakānāṃ prayojakatā/
yadi caivaṃ na kalpyeta naivaiṣāṃ vidhāyakatvavyapadeśo bhavet /
atha kanetyapecitepūrvasaṃbandhānubhavāpeceṇa vidhivijñāneneti sambadhyate /
kathamiti prāśastyajñānānugṛhīteneti /
kuta etat /
buddhipūrvakāriṇo hi puruṣā yāvatpraśasto 'yamiti nāvabuddhyante tāvanna pravarttante /
tatra  vidhivibhaktiravasīdati tāṃ prāśastyajñānamuttamnāti /
tacca purupārthātmake phanjāśe sarvasya svayamevānuṣṭhānaṃ bhavatīti prasiddhatvānna vedādutpadyamānamapekṣyate /
sādhanetikarttavyatayostvapravṛttapuruṣaniyogācchākhameva prāśastyapratipādanāyākāṅcyate /
tatpunaḥ kriyeteti sādhanāpekṣāyāṃ yadi vā phalapadena nivartyeta praśasto 'yaṃ bhūtiphalatvāt /
atha vā vidhinaiva sarvadoṣāśaṅkāvinirmuktavedavihitatvāditi /
athavā viśiṣṭadravyadevatetikarttavyatāyuktatvāditi/
tatra phalapadādīnāmarthāntaropayogātpu naranya trāpyupayogo na yujyate /
viddhyuttarakālā ceyamākāṅkṣā pūrvaṃ ca phalapadādiniveśaḥ /
tasmādapi na tairnivaryate /
lakṣaṇayā caitebhyaḥ kalpyate /
na ca śrautārthasaṃbhave sā yuktā /
yugapaccobhayavṛttivirodhātprāśastyaparatve phalādīni na syuḥ na hyanyaśākha satyupāyamātratvenopāttānāmekāntena pāramārthikatvamiti vacyate /
ata eva cārthādgamyamānamanyaparatvācchabdānāṃ na prāśastyaṃ prayojanaṃ bhavati/
na hi yadyatpratīyate tattacchātraphalamavasīyate /
yathā pūrvī dhāvatītyukte yadyapyaparo gamyate tathāpi na kāryeṇa yujyate tadvatprarocanā gamyamāprathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
nāpi na kāryāntaropayuktaśāstrārthatvenāvatiṣṭhate /
anyathānupatyā ceyaṃ tebhyaḥ kalpyeta /
sarvapramāṇapratyastamaye cānyathānupapattirbhavati /
pramāṇābhāvaśca yaḥ sarvaprakāraṃ prayatamānasya sa pramāṇam /
tadyadi kena cidupadeśena vātideśena vā na lapsyāmahe tato darbihomanyāyena vidhyuddeśasyaiva dve śakto kalpayiṣyāmaḥ /
atha tu kena cid dūrasthenāpi setsyati tatastadanusārastāvatkarttavya ityevaṃ sākāṅkṣo vidhirāste /
tathā vāyurvai kopiṣṭhā devatetyeva mādyapi svādhyāyādhyayana vidhinā puruṣārthatayopanītaṃ yacchakyate tatkuryādityupabandhācca sahasaiva tenāsaṃbaddhyamānamapuruṣārthatvena ca pūrvavadakarādiṣvaparyavasyadbhūtānyākhyānavākyārthaṃ yāvadbhūtam /
tacāpitu sākāṅkṣameveti yastena lakṣyamāṇaḥ sādhanānurūpasādhyotpattidvāreṇa kṣipradevatāsādhyaṃ karma kṣiprameva phalaṃ dāsyatīti prāśastyarūpo 'rthaḥ sonantarapravṛttavidhyuddeśākāṅgitatvātpuruṣārtho dvāratāṃ śaknoti pratipattumiti parigṛhyate /
soyaṃ naṣṭāśvadagdharathavatsaṃprayogaḥ /
evaṃ cana prarocanānyakṛtā karmāṅgam /
na cārthavādapadaiḥ prayojanāntaraṃ sādhanīyamityāmnānasāmarthyādubhayorniyamaḥ /
etena pratiṣedhāpekṣita dveṣa siddhyarthaṃ nindāpada saṅgatirvyākhyātā /
tatrāpi hi nadveṣāhate vidyānnivarttate /
dveṣaścāpraśastapratyayādhīnotpattiḥ /
na cāpraśastajñānaṃ nakārādibhiḥ padaiḥ praśastāpraśastānabhidhānena niṣedhatatphaletikarttavyatāmātra paryavasitaiḥ śakyamavalambitumityananyaprayojana nindā vākyagamyameva bhavati /
takavākyatvasiddhiḥ /
nityaṃ ca vidhipratiṣedhayoḥ krameṇa vākyaśeṣāḥ stutinindā nirṇaya hetavo bhavanti /
na hi stutinindenāma vyavasthite nindārūpāsu stutiṣu stutirūpāsvapi ca nindāsu viparyayadarśanāt /
yathā vakṣyati nahi nindā nindyaṃ nindituṃ pravarttate api tu vidheyaṃ stotumiti /
tathā traiyyambakavākyeṣu yadabhighārayettadrudrāyāsye paṭannidadhyāditi stutamapyanabhighāraṇaṃ nāśrayiṣyate ninditamapi cāntevidhidarśanādabhighāraṇameva praśastaṃ bhaviṣyati /
saṃdigdhastutinindānāmapi ca prakramādeva nirṇayo, yathā vakṣyati na vayaṃ ninditānaninditāncā 'surānvidmaḥ /
kadā ciddhi yasmādasurānapyeṣā vaśīkṛtyānayati kriyā tasmānnūnaṃ praśasteti stutiḥ syāt /
atha vā vidhvaṃsakāsurāgamananimittatvādaśobhaneti nindā /
tatrānte sāmavidhānāttatpraśaṃsārthamṛcāṃ nindeti gamyate /
sarvatra ca kiṃ citpadaṃ stauti nindati cetarāṇi tvekavākyatayā tādarthaṃ pratipadyante /
yatrāpi tādṛśaṃ padaṃ na syāttatrāpi lakṣaṇā lakṣitalakṣaṇā vā'nyathānupapatterāśrayaṇīyā /
vidhipratiṣedhayośca stutinindābhyāmavinābhāvādanyataradarśanenetaradanumāya vākyaṃ pūrayitavyam /
evaṃ bhāratādivākyāni vyākhyeyāni/
teṣāmapi hi śrāvayeccaturo varṇānnityevamādividhyanusāreṇa puruṣārthatvānveṣaṇādaścarādivyatikramya dharmārthakāmamocā dharmānarthaduḥkhasaṃsāra sādhyasādhanaṃ pratipattirūpādānaparityāgāṅgabhūtā phalam /
tatrāpi tu dānarājamoścadharmādiṣu ke cit sācādvidhayaḥ ke citpunaḥ parakṛtipurākalparūpeṇārthavādāḥ /
sarvopākhyāneṣu ca tātparye sati śrāvayediti vidherānarthakyātkathaṃ ciṃdgamyamānastutinindāparigrahaḥ /
tatparatvācca nātīvopākhyāneṣu tattvābhiniveśaḥ kāryaḥ /
vedaprasthānābhyāsena hi vālmokidvaipāyanaprabhṛtibhistathaiva svavākyāni praṇītāni /
pratipādyānāṃ ca vicitrabuddhitvādyuktamevaitat /
iha ke cidvidhimā prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
ca ceṇa pratipadyante/
apare sārthavādena apare 'spenārthavādenāpare mahatā /
sarveṣāṃ ca cittaṃ grahītavyamityevamārambhaḥ /
tatra tu ke cidvidhipratiṣedhāḥ śrutimūlāḥ ke cidarthasukhādiṣu lokamūlāstathārthavādāḥ ke cidvaidikā eva ke cillaukikā eva ke cittu khayameva kāvyanyāyena racitāḥ /
sarve ca stutyarthena pramāṇam /
tu vākyaśeṣatvaṃ na pratipadyante te 'pi ke citsvayameva śrayamāṇamandhamādanādivarṇakaprabhṛtayaḥ prītiṃ janayanti/
ye tu yuddhavarṇakāste sarveṣāṃ śūrāṇāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ cotsāhakarāḥ pārthivānāmupayujyante /
yatra tu na kiṃ cidduṣṭamupalabhyate tatra viśiṣṭadevatādistutidvāramadṛṣṭaṃ kalpanīyamityeṣā dik /
vidhyuddeśenaikavākyatvāditi /
ke cidāhuḥ /
kimarthā stutiriti cet kathaṃ roceta tato'nuṣṭhīyetetyevaṃ stutinindābhyāṃ pravṛttinivṛttipratipādanaṃ liṅādibhiścābhidhānamatastulyārthatvam/
na ca tulyārthānāṃ samuccayaḥ/
tatra yetāvadarthavādarahitā liṅādayastadrahitācārthavādāsteṣāṃ yathāviṣayaṃ vyavasthitaṃ nivartakatvaṃ pravarttakatvamaviruddham /
yatra tu iyasaṃnipātastatrānyatareṇa kṛtārthatvādavaṇyāvaceye 'nyatarasminbhūyasāmanugraho yuktaḥ /
tyajedekaṃ kulasyārtha itivadvidhipratyayaḥ parityajyate /
kevalaprakṛtiprayogābhāvāt tadanugrahārthaprarocanālavdhavidhitvānuvādena pravarttate /
yathā satrādudavasāyapṛṣṭhaśamanīyena yajeranniti tkkāpratyayasiddhapravṛttyanuvādakatvaṃ vacyate /
tasmāḍāyavyaśvetālambha ityetāvanmācaṃ vivaścitam /
sa eva ca vidhyuddeśaḥ phalādisaṃbandhottarakālaṃ svayataityetadbhūtikāma ityevamanto viddhyuddeśa ityanena kathyate /
anyathā punaruddeśagrahaṇamanarthakameva syāt /
sūtroktena tu vidhinaikavākyatvaṃ na saṃbhavatītyatikramya aur tantravārtika /
tadviṣayaḥ parigṛhyate /
tathā cāha nāyamabhisaṃbandha iti /
vidhividheyasaṃbandhaniṣedhena stutistutyasaṃbandhaṃ vivacitaṃ vadati yatastato bhūtiriti /
saiva ca bhūtinimittasya yojanā /
bhinnāvi māviti pūrvoktau saṃbandhāvabhidhatte /
kimarthāṃ stutiriti cediti /
pratyayaścedutkhātastenāvidhīyamānasya kiṃ stutyeti /
athavā yadanayā sādhyate tatpratyayenaiva sekyatoti manasi kṛtvā vadati /
ācāryaskhāte'pi pratyaye 'rthavādādeva tadarthāvāptimubhayasaṃbhave cārthavādānugrahaṃ matvāha kathaṃ rocateti /
itaraḥ praśnābhiprāyaṃ vi vṛṇoti /
prāgeva siddheḥ stutivacanamanarthaka miti /
na hīti granthacchedaḥ /
sarvatrāvāntaravākyāni mahāvākyeyvapramāṇaṃ mahāsaṅkhyāsvivāntarasaṅkhyā bhavanti /
tānyeva tu yadā kevalāni prayujyante tadā nirapekṣatvādbhavanti pramāṇam /
yathā paṭo bhavatīti /
na ca kadā cidetāvanmātreṇa samāpternerākāṅkṣayadarśanātmarvatra nairākāyam /
yogyapadāntarānuccāraṇena hi sarvavākyāni paryavasyanti /
itarathā punaḥ śrutapadātirekeṇāpi nipuṇadṛśāṃ bhavatyevāpekṣā /
sā cānupalabdhyā nivarttate /
tathā ca yatropalapsyante tatraikavākyatā gamayiṣyante /
anyathā hyasau taduccāraṇe'pi na syāttadiha mahāvākyena vinā 'vāntaravākyaṃ pramāṇaṃ tatsadbhāve tu netyetadāha /
yadā na stutipadānīti /
nanvevaṃ satīti /
yatra mahāvākyāvāntaravākyayoḥ phalaṃ bhidyate yathā paṭabhavanarāgabhavane tatraivaṃ yuktaṃ iha tvanatiriktārthasya sataḥ kimavāntaravākyanirākaraṇameva ma hāvākyasya yuktaṃ phalam /
tadetadāha /
yasmin satyavidhāyakamavāntaravākyaṃ bhavati mābhūttanmahāvākya miti/
satyaṃ vinā 'pi teneti /
yo nāma vedasya karttā syātma evaṃ paryanayujyeta laghunopāyena prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
siddhe kiṃ mahāvākyamāśrayasīti /
tadabhāvānna paryanuyogaḥ /
parihārapathagrāmagamanavacca śramātirekamātraṃ syānnārthānavāptiḥ /
dṛṣṭaṃ caitraṃjātīyakeṣa gauravāśrayaṇam/
yathā tamevārthaṃ khamityetāvatā siḍyantamākāśaprabhṛtibhirabhilapanti na ca jāyaṃ labhante tathā'tra liṅādibhirapi siddhyantamarthavādebhyo gṛhṇata iti /
śakyate cedamiha vaktuṃ yathaivānekopāyaprasaṅge mantreṇa smṛtaṃ kriyamāṇamabhyudayakāri bhavati tathā 'nyenāpi vidhisidvārthavādapratipāditavidhivihitamiti /
nanu satkhapi stutipadedhviti /
yatra laghumupāyamanupādāya gurūpāya āśrīyate tatra tathāpi bhavedana tu pūrvameva laghutara āśritaḥ samarthataraśca tasmādyathaiva prayukta khaśabde nākāśādayastadānīmeva prayujyante tathā 'tra vidhau sati stutirnā śrayitavyeti /
tatrottarasākāṅkṣatvātstutipadānyanarthakāni syuriti /
bhavanviti cet /
noktena nyāyenārthavattvādavivaścitārthatā yukteti /
dvayasaṃbhave hi pratyakṣa dekavākyatvādarthavādānugraho yukta iti /
nanu satkhapītyanena gatārthatvād nanu nirapekṣādityavaktavyam /
taducyate /
tatrārthavādaparityagāyoktamidānoṃ tu bhavantu nāma stutisaṃbandhaḥ samastasya pūrvasyāpi tu svarūpāvagato vidhisaṃbandho na bādhitavyaḥ /
athāsya kacidapi śaktirapahiyate tataḥ pratiprasavahetvabhāvāt sarvacāśaktatvaprasaṅga iti/
tadabhidhīyate/
bhavatu pūrvasya vidhiśaktirna tviyaṃ kva civādhitetyanyatrāpi bādhyate/
kadā cidāvirbhūteti sarvacāvirbhavati /
yatra tvarthāntarastutyādinopādīyate  tatrāvirbhūtā śaktiḥ kāryamārabhate /
yatra tvapavādabhūtaśaktyantarābhivyaktistatra vākyabhedaprasaṅgātpūrvā tirodhīyate /
praśnottaratvenāyaṃ pūrvokta eva vākyabhedaḥ parāmpṛśyate /
tasmādekārthyātprarocanayaivātra vidhiriti /
prarocayamānā anuṣṭhāvṛṇāmiti /
“ruccarthānāṃ prīyamāṇa” iti sampradānatvaṃ kasmānna bhavati /
prarocayateḥ prakṛtyantaratvāditi cenna/
tatrāpi rucisaṃmbandhānapadbhvāt /
atha sāmānyavivaśayā ṣaṣyucyate sāpyupātte viśeṣe durlabhā /
tasmādanuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ kriyāyā iti sambandhaḥ kebhyaḥ prarocayamānā ityapecate 'rthāttabhya eveti gamyate/
atha cānuṣṭhātṝṇāmupakariṣyantīti sambandhaḥ /
kriyāyā iti pañcamī kriyāto 'pi hi taeva prarocakā iti /
athavā kriyārthamiti ṣaṣyarthaḥ kalpyaḥ /
kaṃ cidarthaṃ stuvantītiśatrantaṃ kaṃ ciditi vidheyaṃ tatsambandhinaṃ vā kaṃ cidvā vidadhati kriyāṃ tatmambandhinaṃ vā tacca stutidvāreṇetyupapannaṃ  pratyayodvāreṇārthavādaprāmāṇyam /
idaṃ tu vyākhyānaṃ nānumanyante/
yadi hi pratyayotkhātiḥ syāttataḥ kena stutirākācyeta na tāvacchabdabhāvanā kathaṃ bhāvo'sti /
yā'pikasmādityapekṣā kalpyeta sāpi vidhītikarttavyatāviṣayaiva tadanugracārthatvāt /
śabdāntaravyapadeśamācaṃ tu bhidyate /
sāpi ca niyujyamānasyaiva puruṣasya bhavati na kriyāmātraśravaṇṇāt /
na hi vāyavyaśvetālambha ityukte karttavyatā'kartavyatokteḥ prāk praśasto 'praśasta iti vā 'pecyate /
tadanapeścitaṃ ca śrutimātreṇaiva vadanto nārthavādāḥ pratipādayanti /
na ca dhātvarthena saha kasya citmambandho 'pekṣā vā vidyate /
sarvasya bhāvanāgāmitvāt /
bhāvanā tu pratyayodvāreṇāpanītā kimapekṣeta /
tasmāttadgatāṃśatrayocchedānna bhṛtiḥ phalaṃ na yāgaḥ karaṇaṃ na veti karttavyatā kā cisyāt /
ukta 'pi ca prāśastye kasmādityanapekṣitatvātpraśasto 'yamityetāvanmātre 'vadhṛte praśastatvādityanuccamāne karttavyatābuddinaiva syāt /
bhavanto vā tanniṣṭhā bhavetpraśasto 'yaṃ karttavyaḥ paṭo raktaḥ karttavya itivata/
akalpite vi dhāvānarthakyameva syāt/
pratyakṣaṃ ca vidhimutsṛjya pāramparyalakṣaṇayārthavādebhyaḥ parigṛhyataityapūrvā vācoyuktiḥ /
na caitatkalpanāvasaro 'styanyataḥ siddhatvān /
anukto hi sannarthavādādeva vidhiḥ kalpyeta yadyanyathā nopapadyeta /
pratyakṣapratyayopapannatvānnānyathānupapattistathārthavādo'pi yadyapākhyānādiṣviva prarocanāya niṣprayojanaḥ syāttato dūraṃ nīyeta /
yathoktena tu nyāyena prarocanopayogānnānyatra gacchatotyavaśyakarttavyā ca prarocanā yadyanyataḥ siddhyettato 'rthavādānnāpekṣeta /
sāpi tvananyagatikatvāttamevāśrayati /
sarvatra ca vaidike'rthe 'rthāpattyā śabdaḥ kalpyeta tato 'rthasiddhistena prarocanayā vidhiśabdaḥ kalpyeta nārthaḥ tatkalpanāvelāyāṃ ca yathaindravāyavādivākyeṣu somena yajetetyasminnupatiṣṭhamānenānyayajikalpanā tathaivālabhetetyanenānyānumānapratibandhaḥ /
tulyārthayośca bādhavikalpau bhavataḥ /
pratyayārthavādayoḥ punaratyantabhinnānugrāhyānugrāhakārthaviṣayatvenārthabhedātmamuccaya ityeka vākyatā /
yadi ca pratyayotkhātiḥ syāttataḥ karttṛsaṃkhyopagrahaviśeṣāvagatakriyāphala svārthaparārthatvādyucchedaprasaṅgaḥ /
syādetat /
vidhitvamātramavivāyitvāśeṣavivaśayā karttṛsaṃkhyādilābha iti /
etaccāśakyaṃ yatastadarthamapyupāttaḥ /
pratyayaḥ sāmarthyāda vi dhitvaṃ vadatyeva /
pratītasya ca hayyevāvivacā vidhyasaṃsparśo vā gra caika vavadanuvādakatvaṃ vendrikāma homavat /
na tāvadvigheravidhitvaṃ nāma kiṃ cit/
nāpyanuvādastasyāmavasthāyāmaprāpteḥ na hyevaṃ sambhavati yo 'yaṃ vāyavyaśvetālambhaḥ karttavyaḥ sa praśasta iti /
bhavati tvevaṃ karttavyaḥ praśastatvāditi /
yattadavasānīyavaditi tatrāpi hakkāvaśena vidhipratiṣedhāvanapekṣya kriyāmātrākṣepād vidhitvamāśritamevetyadṛṣṭāntatā/
yadi ca vidhyavivaśā syāttataḥ pratyāsatterdhātvartha eva sādhyāṃśe nipatediti niṣphalatvaṃ syāt /
tasmātsūtrāvināśenaiva vidhinaikavākyatvam /
tathā ca bhāṣyakāraḥ /
savidhikameva bhūtikāma ityevamanto vidhyuddeśa ityāha /
anyathā dhātvartha ityevāvakṣyat /
tatrāsya kriyāmātratayā vidhyaddeśatvaṃ śakyate vaktum /
tasmātpratyaya eva vidhyavidhāyitvādvidhyaddeśaḥ /
vidhyarthena tvekavākyatvāsambhavātsūtrātirekeṇoddeśagrahaṇam /
bhūtikāma ityevamanta iti ca phalādisaṃgatyuttarakālaṃ stutyavasarapradarśanārtham /
nanvevaṃ sati varttamānāpadeśeyvanākāṅkṣaṇādarthavādā na sa mbadhyeran/
evamevaitattathāpi tu pramāṇāntara prāptyabhāvākka citprayogavacanena va citpañcamalakāreṇa /
atha vā śrutavarttamānānyathānupapattyā kalpite vidhitve 'rthavādasaṃgatiḥ /
yatrāpi kevalārthavādadarśanādeva vidhitvaṃ tatrāpyanyathānupapattimācaṃ śaraṇam /
sambhavantyāṃ tugatau nātigauravaṃ yuktamiti /
yastvasminyate vākyabhedaḥ sambandhadvayāśrayaṇāditi sa ālabheta praśastatvādityekaprasaropapatteḥ parihṛtaḥ /
vidhīyamānasyaiva hi stutyākāṅgretyavairūpyādupapannaṃ tantratvam /
yadi caivaṃvidhaiḥ sambandhabhedairvākyaṃ bhidyeta tataḥ sādhyasādhanetikarttavyatāsambandhairapi bhidyeta tasmānnāyamabhisambandhī vivacita ityādibhāṣyamevaṃ netavyam /
na pūrvacaiva sāṅgavidhiparyavasānaṃ vivaścitam /
vidhitvādidvāraprarocanāprathamādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
kalpanāyāmatigaurava nimittādvākyabhedāt /
kimarthā stutiriti /
pūrveṇaiva prarocanāpi siddhetyabhimānātkathaṃ roceteti vidhyanugrahakathanam /
nanu prāgiti pūrvābhiprāyavivaraṇam /
na hoti /
stutyabhāve tasya śaktidvayamagatyāśroyate na sambhavantyāmapītyetanna tadā bhūtikāmasya vidhiḥ samāpyataityāha /
yathā paṭa iti /
gatārtham /
vidhiśabdena tadā prarocaneti vivṛtaṃ kāryanānātvaṃ vi dhistutyoḥ/
nanvevamiti/
asti cetprarocayinumapi śaktiḥ kasmādanyadapecyataiti /
satyamiti tasmādidyamāne tasminnā vidyamāne yo 'rthaḥ sa gamyate/
kaścāsaiau/
stutiḥ prayojanaṃ tayorna tasyaiva pūrvasyāpītyarthaḥ /
stutiviṣayopakalpanācca vidherapi stutiprayojanavyapadeśo na hi nirviṣayā stutirupapadyate /
arthavādābhāve tvagatyā kevalo 'pigauravamaṅgīkariṣyati /
nanu satsvapīti /
pūrvava deva vyākhyeyam /
ato'smādvidheriti /
idānīṃ ṣaṣṭhīvākyaśeṣasambandhādita evāsya stutimavagacchāmo na svata ityarthaḥ /
nanu nirapebādapoti/
yadi kvacidanitikarttavyatā kasya vidheḥ pravarttanaśaktiḥ kasmādanyadapekṣate tena satsvapyanādaraḥ syāt /
ācāryastu so pahāsamāha yatrāsau kevalaḥ prayujyamāno nirapekṣastatra bhavatu na kaścidvirodhaḥ /
iha tu na tatsaṃbhavaḥ sākāṅkṣaḥ padāntarairākṣiptatvāt /
vākyaṃ hyekamekasyaiva saṃbandhasya vidhāyakaṃ tatra yadi hai/
vidhyuddeśaeva kuryāttathā sati bhidyeta /
vidhyuddeśotyāpitānāmevaiṣa  hi guṇo bhavatīti prarocanāṃ darśayati /
tasmādidhinaikavākyatvāttadanugraheṇārthavanto 'rthavādā iti 
aprāptā cānupapattiḥ  prayoge hi virovaḥ syācchabdārthastva prayogabhūtastasmadupapadyeta 
uktadoṣaparihāro 'taḥ param /
śāstradṛṣṭavirodhikā yātrānupapattividhikalpanāyāmuktā tāmasmatpakṣaprāptāṃ  manyāmahe /
atha vedaṃ stutivyākhyānaṃ tāmanupapattimaprāptamiti vyākhyeyaṃ yeṣāṃ hakhaḥ pāṭhaḥ /
prayoge hyanuṣṭhāne rodanavapotkhananadiṅmoisteyānṛtavādādīnāṃ kalpyamāne virodhaḥ syāt /
asmākaṃ tu punarya eṣāṃ śavdānāṃ śrauto'rthaḥ sa naiva vivaścitaḥ /
na cādhyāhārādibhirvidhiḥ kiṃ tarhi stutimātraṃ vivaścitam /
na ca tadvirujyate tasmādupapadyeta /
atha vā śavdārthastviti vidhāyaka śabdānugrahārthaḥ sannayamarthavādo na svārthānuṣṭhānena saṃbadhyate prayogamaprāpto 'prayogabhūtastasmādupapadyeta /
trayo'tra pāṭhāḥ /
aprāptāṃ cānupapattimityatra manyāmahaiti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
aprāptaṃ cānupapattimityaparasta trāmākhyānamityadhyāhāraḥ /
aprāptā cānupapattirityaparastatrāsmatpaśe vijñeyeti 
rūpātprāyāt 
ica sarvaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ manasā saṅkalā vācā cābhidhāya kriyate tadatyantāntaraṅgabhūtayorapyanayordūreṇa hiraṇyādūnatvaṃ steyānṛtavādayogāditi/
yā nindā tanmātraparyavasāyino sā niṣedhaphalā bhavati /
vidhiparātu stutyarthā jāyate tadupapādanasya dṛṣṭārthatvāt /
yathā vakṣyati nacedanyaṃ prakalpayetpraklṛptāvarthavādaḥ syāditi 
svyaparādhātkartuca putradarśanam 
pravare prabriyamāṇe yajamāno vadeddevāḥ pitara ityādi /
tatpraśaṃsārthamuktamabrāhmaṇo'pi brāhmaṇo bhavati pravarānumantraṇeneti /
tatra prasiddhabrāhmaṇatvānāmeva brāhmaṇyalābho niṣprayojana iti tadupapatyarthamuktaṃ na caitaddidma iti /
jñāyamāne tvajñānavacanaṃ durjñānatvāt /
yatsukhenājñānaṃ tadajñānameva /
tacca tryaparādhaniprathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
mittam/
satyapi ca khyaparādhe yadi mātureva kṣetriṇo vā putraḥ syāttatastayoḥ prasidvṛjātitvānnaiva darjñānatā bhavet /
tayoradhyevamevaṃ tatpūrvajayorityanādinyāyena jātiravadhāryetaiva /
yatastu mātā bhastrā pituḥ putra iti smartṝṇāṃ darśanam /
janayituśca nānājātitvopapattistena varṇasaṅkaraḥ /
vede 'pi cāpramattā rakṣata tantumena miti jātivicchedadarśanaṃ tryaparādhakarttṛputranimittamevopapadyate/
anyathā hyaparirakṣamāṇe 'pi naiva svajātitantu vi cchedo bhavet /
tenāsti praśaṃsāvakāśaṃ iti /
nirūḍhabrāhmaṇya pravarasaṅkīrttanāttatprabhavo 'yamiti jñānādbrāhmaṇaḥ kṛto bhavatīti stutiḥ 
vidyāpraśaṃsā 
adhyayana vidhiśeṣatvādaphalavidhiḥ san yathā vijñāta mukhaśobhā vājimattvānuvādo  vijñāyate na caika eva prakāro mukhaśobhāyāḥ saṃsthānaṃ ramaṇīyatā lāvaṇyaṃ ceti /
strīviṣayaṃ hyetat /
viduṣāṃ punaḥ padavākyanyāyodgāri mukhaṃ śobhate tenātmanā mukhyayaiva vṛtyā śobhate /
putraśca vājavānbrahmavarcasahāreṇa /
athāpigauṇatā tathāpi stutiparatvādadoṣaḥ 
phalasya karmaniṣpattesteṣāṃ lokavatparimāṇataḥ phalaviśeṣaḥ syāt 
taccaitat samānasvargādiphaleṣvagnihotrādiṣūpayocyataityupanyastaṃ sādhanānurūpatvātsādhyānām /
sarve hi kāmāḥ pūrṇātyāvāpyamānāḥ stokastokāḥ prāpyante tatra phalabhūmārthinaḥ karmāntaravidhirarthavān bhaviṣyatīti sthite codyate /
yuktaṃ loka kṛṣyādi phalānāṃ pratyaścāvagatatvātmādhanānurūpaṃ janma /
pūrṇātyādiṣu tvatyanta śākhādhīnatvādaviśeṣaśrute phale kiṃmūlā viśe ṣakalpanā /
na hyagnihotrajyotiṣṭomasvargayoḥ kaścidviśeṣaḥ śrū yate /
na cānumānamodṛśe viṣaye samartham /
tadabhidhīyate /
vidhiprathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
sāmarthyādevedaṃ siddhama/
katham /
yadi hyalpānmahataśca karmaṇaḥ samaṃ phalaṃ jāyeta tato'kke cenmadhu vindetetyanenaiva nyāyenālapena siddhe mahati na kaścitpravarttate /
tatra vidhiśaktivādhaḥ syāta vita śaktistu san ardhādvā kalpanaikadeśatvāditi vidhireva phalādhikyamaṅgīkaroti /
ato yathā viśvajidādau phalanadbhāvaḥ pramāṇavānevamiha tadviśeṣa iti /
kiṃ ca 
yathaiva kramāmnātānāmaṅgāṅgināṃ prathamasya prathamaṃ dvitīyasya dvitīyamiti viniyogavyavasthā tathaiva karmagocare 'paya karmaṇaḥ parimāṇasāmānyena phalagocare 'lpamevopatiṣṭhate /
madhyamasya madhyamaṃ mahato mahaditi sthānameva viniyojakam/
smaraṇamapyevameva /
cāturmāsyasomeṣu ca phalārthavādo yadāgnihotraṃ juddotyatha daśa gṛhamedhina āpnotyekayā rātriyetyārabhya nyanāgnihotradaśasaṃvatsaraprayogādibhirekadarśapūrṇamāsādiprayogāvāpnivacanaṃ karmālapatvamahattvakṛtaṃ phalabhedaṃ darśayati 
tantravārtika /
vidhirvā syādapūrvatvādvādamāvaṃ hyanarthakam 
evamānārthakyopākhyānādipratiyogidhvarthavādeṣu vyākhyāteṣu idānīṃ vidhipratiyogino vicāryante /
kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ /
pūrvatra hi svārthānupayogitvena dūralakṣitastutigrahaṇamaṅgīkṛtam /
tatsaṃbhave tu stutirapyanarthakatulyā ''padyate /
vidhyaṃśaśca na kathaṃ ca nānyasmātsiddhyati/
prarocanā punaḥ kathaṃ cidvidhyuddeśādapyupapadyate ityu ktaṃ purastāt /
api ca pradhānaṃ vidhiraṅgaṃ stutistatra pradhānaviśeṣaṇasaṃbhavinastadgāmitvameva yuktam /
samāpte ca viddhyuddeśe'rthavādaḥ pravarttate tatprakramāvasthāyāmeva tu bhāvanāṃśāḥ sannipatanti /
viśe tu phalaṃ prāthamyaprādhānyāmyāmityādi manvāno 'pūrvatvāditi vaditi/
tadapekṣayā ca stutimātramanarthakaṃ manyate /
nanu caivaṃjātīyakaḥ phalavidhiḥ phalārthavādavicāraścaturthe'pi dravyasaṃskārakamasviti bhaviṣyati /
ato neha prastotavyaḥ /
tatra ke cidāhaḥ /
anena gatārthatvāt tatraivaiṣa paryanuyogo yujyate na tvidaṃ punaruktamiti /
satyamevaṃ yadi tu tatkāla pratīkṣaṇātkiṃ citparihārāntaraṃ svabhyate 'tastatrāncicchema/
atha punaricaiva śakyate vaktuṃ tathā satīdānomapyucyamāne mando doṣa iti /
atrāpara vadanti tena phalavidhinvanirākaraṇamātramiha tvarthavādanāya tvarthavādaḥ syāditi tatra vakṣyati tadvidhitvanirākaraṇamātraparameva praṣṭavyam /
tadayuktam /
yatastena phala vidhitvātpracyā vitānā mānarthakyaprasaktī pūrvādhikaraṇenaiva stutyarthatā sādhitā/
tathā ca darśitaṃ śobhate 'sya mukhamityādiṣu /
ke citpunarāḥ /
yuktaṃ vāyurvai kṣepiṣṭhetyādīnāṃ prathamādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
stutitvam /
ūrjā 'varudhyā iti punaryathā phalavidhitvātpracyāvyate tathaiva visaṃvādana stutitvādapoti kāmaṃ vidhirbhavatu yena kālāntarabhāvitvena kathaṃ cihnisaṃvādo nivarttataityārambhaḥ /
tadapyayuktam /
api ca vede vyaktamasaṃvāda iti hyatyuccaya heturapunaruktaḥ syāt/
adhikaraṇaśarīraṃtu tadeva /
visaṃvādo'pi ca guṇavāda svityanena na kaścidaparihṛtaḥ /
punarapi ca tāvanmāmevottaraṃ bhaviṣyati /
tasmādvidhirvā syāditya viśeṣopādānāccaturthe ca phalaśrutigrahaṇādihāśeṣadravyaguṇakriyā dividhisarūpāstatra phalavidhisarūpā evodāharaṇamityapare /
tathā ca vidhiśvānarthakaḥ kva citprakaraṇe ca sambhavanniti cāpsuyonirvā aśvo'bhujo vetaso yo vidagdha iti codāhiyate /
anyathā phalavidhimātropanyāse nadasaṃbaddhameva syāt /
icāpi tasya tāvadviśeṣaviṣayatvādidamagatārthaṃ bhavet /
anena ta sāmānyataḥ sarvaviṣayāvarodhinā tu tatpunaruktamevati vyavasthayā ke cidudāharanti /
atra dravyādividhīneva tatra phala vidhīneva bhāṣyakārodāharaṇamatantrīkṛtyodāharaṇāntaraṃ dātavyamiti /
atra vadāmaḥ /
kimadhikaraṇadvayamavagyāravdhavyaṃ yenaivamudāharaṇavyavasthāśrīyate na cudāharaṇabhedādadhikaraṇaṃ bhidyate /
mā bhūdyathā vyavasthite 'pi khādirai/
dumbara tvabheṭāḍhaponaruktyama/
nyāyaviṣayatvena tvadhikaraṇānāṃ tadbheda evāpaunaruktye hetuḥ/
dravyādividhayo 'pi na sarve vicāritāḥ /
ke ci ttatmidvisūtre /
ke cinnivītādyadhikaraṇeṣu /
parakṛtipurākalpadvāreṇānye ṣaṣṭhe /
yadṛcā stuvataityādayo 'rthakatvādikalpa iti navame /
jarttila gavīdhukavidhisarūpā daśame /
ataśca na punaruktatā mahāndoṣa ityeva vaktavyam /
atha vaikasyaiva nyāyasya va ci kaścidaṃśaḥ śodhyata iti punarārambhaḥ /
spaṣṭaṃ vā viṣayanānātvamevaṃ varṇanīyam /
sarvavidhisarūpāṇāṃ kevalaṃ vidhitvanirākaraṇenārthavādatvamiha siddham/
yastu caturthe punarārambhaḥ so 'rthavādakalpite vidhau phalākāṅkṣā velāyāmanyārthopāttamapi ṛtuprayogavacanātadeva saṃnihitataraṃ klṛptasaṃbandhasya ca viśeṣamācaṃ sukaram /
ita rathā saṃbandhastadviśeṣaścopakārakatvaṃ kalpanīyamiti rātrisatrapratiṣṭhādivatphalavidhitvamapīti pūrvapakṣābhiprāyaḥ /
kathaṃ citpra yojanāntare labhyamāne naikasyāne kārthatā yuktā tasmādarthavādatvameveti siddhāntaḥ /
etena nivatāvadhikaraṇāni vyākhyātāni /
atha vai/dumbarādhikaraṇapūrvapacaṃ kṛtvā citāstāḥ pratyetavyāḥ /
vidhitvābhyupagamena hi kasya śeṣaḥ kratoḥ puruṣasya vetyādi vicāryeha siddhenārthavādatvenopasaṃhāraḥ /
tathā parakṛtipurākalpayoḥ kiṃ tadgotrāṇāmuta sarvapuṃmāmiti cintitam /
evamūhabāghaprasaṅgena navamadaśamagatā cintā tatsidvisatre'nuguṇavāda nimittamātrakathanam/
atha vā phalavidhāveva yatra bhedena stutiphalapadāni bhavanti tadihodāharaṇam/
yathā caivorgudumbara ūrkapaśava ityetaireva stutiḥ /
ūrjāvaruddhyā ityanena phalamiti /
yatra punastāvanmātreṇaiva phalaṃ vā stutirvā vaktavyeti bhavati te caturthaiti /
athavā tatra parārthatvāditi hetuvyapadeśātprasiddhena ca hetunā vyavahārādye vijñātapārārthyāstaudāharaṇaṃ yathā yasya parṇamayī juhūriti /
hyavaśyaṃ juṅkanuvādena parṇamayītvaṃ vidhātavyaṃ svātantreṇa phalasaṃbandhāśaktaḥ /
sarvatra hi guṇaḥ phalāya codyamānaḥ kaṃ cidāśrayamapeśate /
na ca prakaraṇamantareṇāśrayaprāptiḥ /
tadiha yadi parṇamaprathamādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
yotvena phalaṃ bhāvayediti vacanaṃ vyajyeta kimāśritenetyapekṣāyāṃ kiṃ saṃbaddhyatām /
juhūriti cenna /
vākyabhedaprasaṅgān /
sāpi ca prākkiyālābhānnaiva nirākāṅkṣo bhavati/
na ca kriyāmambandhe pramāṇamasti /
tasmādanirvahaṇādetadvacanavyaktiparityāgenetarāyaṇam /
tatra ca juhvā juhotītyasyāḥ prakaraṇe nirjñānaprayojanātvādavihitajātiviśeṣāyāstadākāṅkṣāyāṃ satyāṃ yāvadevaparṇatvajātirupanītā tāvaḍhavijñāta prayojanāvasthatvādaṅgatāṃ pratipadyate /
tataśca nirākāṅkṣībhūtāyāstasminneva vākye phalakalpanā nimittaṃ nāstīti yuktamarthavādatvam /
iha punarvaikṛtapaśuprakaraṇe śrūyamāmaudumbaratvamuḍhāhiyate /
na ca tasya prasiddhaṃ pārārthyaṃ yena caturthādhikaraṇaviṣayatā bhavet /
katham /
atra hi na tāvadaprāpte yūpe jātividhānaṃ śakyam/
tatprāptiścedavaśyaṃ klṛptopakāra prakṛtakhādiratvādinaiva nirākāṅkṣaṇa bhavitavyam /
tatkuto jātyantarasya tādarthyena vidhirataḥ phale vidhānam /
yāpi cāśrayāpekṣā sāpi prākṛtakarmasambandhicodaka prāptayapagrahaṇānnivarttata itya vighātaḥ /
tena prāgeva pārārthyātphala sambandhaprasaktiravaṇyaṃ nyāyāntareṇa nirākarttavyetyetada dhikaraṇārambhaḥ /
idamapara matam /
audumbara k juhā divākyaṃ cobhayamubhayatrodāharaṇam /
kathaṃ bhāvanāṃśāntaravicārādapaunaruktyam/
sādhyasādhanasambandhastāvaddayorapi yogyatvenopāttayoravakalpate nānyathā /
tatra caturthe sādhanāṃśayogyavicāramanāityābhyupetya vā kevala sādhyāṃśavicāraḥ/
kimīḍaśena kāmaśabdopabandhara hitena varttamānaphalaṃ sambandhābhidhāyitā phalatvaṃ śakyate gamayituṃ na veti vicāraḥ /
iha punaḥ sādhyāṃśamanāhatyābhyupetya vā kevala sādhanāṃśavicāraḥ /
kimohaśena vidhivibha ktirahitena dravyaguṇakriyāḥ kaṃ citprati sādhanatvena pratipādyante neti /
yacca yadātmanā pratipāditaṃ bhavati tatpratiyogiviśeṣāpekṣaṃ satpadāntarādyapāttena tena sambaddhyate /
tatra sādhyamityavadhṛte pariśeṣādavaśiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ gamyate /
evaṃ sādhanāvadhāraṇepīti ḍāvapyaṃśā svarūpeṇa nirūpayitavyau /
tadiha sādhanāṃśe vicāryamāṇa yo nāma phalāṃśasya saṃsparśaḥ sa caturthe siddhaḥ prasaṅgādvetutveneti mantavyaḥ /
tathā yastatra sādhanāṃśaparāmarśa sa iha siddhastatra prasaṅgādityapunaruktam /
nanvevaṃ sati vidhyuddeśacinteyamityarthavādādhikaraṇena na sambadhyate/
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
tadaśenaivārthaparicchedāt/
yadi hyasau vidhoyamānatayā pūrveṇāvagatastatonārthavādatvamatha stutyarthatayā tato 'rthavādatvamiti /
tatra pūrvapacābhiprāyaḥ /
sarvathā sādhyasaṃnidhāne yaduccaritaṃ tadākāṅkṣāvaśena tādrapyeṇānupāttamapi sādhanaṃ bhavati yathaiva yāgenetyanuditaṃ sambadhyate ta thaivodumbareṇeti/
tatra vidhiḥ kiṃ kuryātpuruṣaṃ pravarttayet/
sa ca phalārthitayaiva pravṛtta iti kiṃ vidhinā /
atha vā prayogavacana vihitasya phala sambandhamātramanena kriyate /
pañcamo vā lakāro vidhāsyati/
arthavāḍhaikadeśo vetyuktameva tasmādūrjāvaruddhyā iti tādarthyacaturthyevaivaṃ kāmaśabdādapi sphuṭataraṃ phalamupāttamiti tasminnaumbaduratāvidhiḥ/
nanu phalasya vidhānamiti grahītavyaṃ bhāvārthādhikaraṇe phalavidhiniṣedhāt /
ūgudumbara ityataḥ stutirityavirodhaḥ /
tasmānmukhya vidhisambhave lacaṇayā na stutiḥ pratipattavyeti 
na pūrvatvāt 
nāyaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ stuteḥ pramāṇāntarāvagatyapekṣatvālloke tatsaṃbhavādupapattiḥ /
vede tvaviditavādatvānna śraddadhoran /
atha vā loka eva yadyaviditaṃ kaściddadettadā naiva śraddadhīran /
pūrvavacanādiveti vidhyuddeśādi vā/
atha vā vaidharmyepamā /
yathādhigatapūrvavacane śraddadhante naivama viditavāda/
na coktimātreṇaite bahuścorādayaḥ prarocayante kiṃ tarhi viditatvādeva /
vede tvarthavādāsatyatvena vidhau jātāśako na pravartteta /
atha vā yo vidhimutkramyārthavādaṃ prārthayate nūnamasya vidhāvaviśramaḥ /
tatra cedanāśvāso 'rthavāde kutaḥ pratyaya iti /
api ca vede vyaktamasaṃvādo varttamānenorjevarodhaneneyaṃ stutirna ca tadasti/
tatrāvidyamānabahukṣīrasaṅkīrttanavadetatsyāt /
svarūpatastāvadudumbaro 'nnatvaṃ paścadharmeṇāprasiddhaṃ anvayāprasiddheśva hetutvāprasiddhiḥ /
na hi yadyadannaṃ sa sa yūpa iti loke vede vā prasiddhamityasambaddhaṃ tasmādasaṃvādādaraṃ vidhireva kiṃ stutyā saṃvādāpeściṣayeti 
vidhiścānarthakaḥ kva cittasmātstutiḥ pratīyeta tatsāmānyāditareṣu tathātvam  tantravārtike /
yadi caivañjātīyakā vidhayo bhaveyustataḥ pūrvodāhṛtāḥ sarvava dravyaguṇakriyāvidhayo bhaveyuḥ /
vāyuḥ kṣepiṣṭhā devatā karttavyā ayoniraśvaḥ karttavyaḥ /
asujo vetaso 'vakāśca karttavyāḥ /
āpaḥ śāntāḥ ūrgudumbara ityādi /
tatra yadyapi ke citkriyādividhayaḥ śakyante kartum /
ete tvaśakyāḥ svabhāvasiddheḥ prayatnenāpi cāniṣpatteḥ /
vāyuvetamāvakādiṣu svabhāvasiddhiḥ /
aśvaudumbarādīnāmaśakyatā /
kīdṛśī stutistāṃ darśayati /
śamayitrībhiradbhirityādi /
tatrāsaṅgateragrantha iti vyākhyātāraḥ sa marthayante /
yasmādihāvakātatmambandhayoḥ śamayitṛtvasya ca naivopanyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ vetasa upanyastaḥ so 'pistutivelāyāṃ na pradarśita iti tatra tviyaṃ gamanikā /
vetasodāharaṇenaiva tulyatvādavakādonyapyudāhṛtāni /
na cāyamaśvāvakayoḥ paraspareṇa sambandhaḥ kathyate /
kena tarhyadbhiḥ /
tāvatā tu na stutiḥ kā cidunmīlitetyarthavādāntarāpekṣāpravṛttāṃ tāṃ darśayati /
āpo vai śāntā iti /
anena hi vidhitvātpracyutenāpāṃ prāśastyamucyate tatra kasya ci tprasidvābhambandhasya tanmātra saṅkīrttanādeva stutirbhavati /
anyeṣāṃ tu sambandhi sambandhātmambandhaḥ kīrttyate /
prasiddhaśāntatva sambandhābhiradbhiḥ sambandhād aśvādirapi śāntātmakastatmambaddhena ca karmaṇā yajamānasya kaṣṭaṃ śāmyatītyevaṃvidhaprāśastyajñāpanārtham /
evaṃ kṣipradaivatena śīghraṃ phalaprāptirannamayena ca yūpenānnaprāptiriti stutitve siddhe tatmamānanyāyānāmapyevamātmakatvam 
vidhau ca vākyabhedaḥ syāt 
stutitvena vidhivibhaktimupajanavya punastenaiva phalakalpanāya vākyabhedastasmādarthavāda eveti /
heturvā syādarthavattvopapattibhyām 
iha ye hetuvannigadyante hi śabdādibhirna ca paramārthahetavastaudāharaṇam /
tatra yadi tāvadvetutvaṃ vidhīyate tataḥ pūrveṇaiva gatam /
yadiha hetutvaṃ tacchrarpahomasambandhaṃ prati na cāvihito 'sāvastīti kasya heturucyate /
atha bhūtānuvādamācaṃ tattu vāyucepiṣṭhatvavadgatamityanārabdhavyametat /
uccate /
na tāvadanenaiva vākyena he tutvaṃ vidhīyate na ca bhūtānuvādamātraṃ kiṃ tarhi hetoḥ prasiddhipūrvakatvātmidvavadupadiṣṭasya yāvatyasiddhyāśaṅkā tatrārthāpattilabhyāicanātmiddhiḥ /
yāpi cārthavādākāṅkṣā kasmāditi sāpyanenaiva hetunā nivarttyata iti manyate /
athāpyarthavādatvaṃ tathāpi tadantaniṇata hetutvameveti sarvānnakaraṇaviṣayaṃ vijñāyate tataśca heturapya tu sviti pūrvaḥ paścaḥ /
sambandhasya ca vidheyatvāttadgatameva hetutvaṃ homasyeti vadati /
nanvaprasiddhe kāryakāraṇabhāvaiti /
ke cir̤hāḥ /
kāryakāraṇayorevānumānam /
tathā ca dadhnendriyakāmasyetyatrāpi vakṣyati /
tattvayuktam /
kāryakāraṇabhūtānāmapi kṛttikādīnāmacirodgatarohiṇyādipratipattihetutvadarśanāt /
ato gamyagamakatvameva kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ manyate /
nanu sopyanumānottarakālonatvādanaṅgam /
satyam/
anyasminneva ta sambandhe sati paścātprasiddhyantamenamanu mānavyavahāropalakṣaṇatvenopanyasyati /
yadvā śa tyabhiprāyaṃ yayoreva hi vyāptigrahaṇakāle gamyagamakasāmarthyātmanā kāryakāraṇabhāvitvena sāvadhatā tatraiva hetutā /
atha vodāhṛtaviṣayahetulakṣaṇametat /
avinābhāvo hyanekakāryakāraṇasvasvāmisahacarabhāvādiprabheda bhinnastatrānna karaṇatā home hetutvenoccamānasambandhāntarābhāvātkāraṇatvena syāt /
taccāprasiddhaṃ tasmānna cetvapadeśaḥ /
satyaṃ loke hetuvyavahārakālā prathamaṃ pramāṇāntareṇa sambandhaprasiddhirapecyate vede tu hi śabdapratipādita hetutvānyathānupapattyā sambandhābhidhāyi dṛṣṭāntavacanaṃ kalpyeta yadyadannakaraṇaṃ tena tena juhotīti tena copapannaṃ hetṛtvam/
kiṃ prayojanamiti yadi ca heturavatiṣṭhetetyanenābhiprāyeṇa /
aparasvāda vyāptī siddhāyāṃ sarvānnasādhanasādhanako homaḥ siddho bhavati /
kuta iti /
sa eva siddhāntābhiprāyaḥ /
athavā kuto darvipiṭharādeḥ sādhakatamatvam /
itarastvācānnakriyāyāṃ tāvattasyārthavattāsti tāvanmācaṃ vāśrayiṣyate /
śakyate ca tenāpītyupapattiśabdasyārthaḥ /
pūrveṇa tu samānārthatā gamyate /
tena vivakṣā /
śaktyabhiprāyametat /
yadeva hi tadupayogimācaṃ tadeva śakyate kathaṃ ci prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
mādhakatamatvena vivaścitum /
atha vārthavattvaṃ karaṇavibhakti nirde śālambanamupapattyā punarvarttamānānna kriyasya hetutvābhidhānāttādṛśasya homaṃ pratyanupapattyā śaṅkayopapattiṃ vadani, śakyate ca teneti/
tatra codayati /
etaddhi kriyataityucyate tatkathaṃ śakyatai tyabhidhīyate /
varttamānakriyasyāsambhavādittyuttaram /
yadvā svayamevāśaya pariharati /
yadi ca na darvipiṭharādītyubhayoḥ parāmaśaḥ sādhakatamatvavarttamānatve cettatra na vidyete ṭarpe 'pi tathaiveti stutirna syāt /
tena yathā tava stutyarthaḥ kathaṃ cidvidyate tathā mama hetvartha ityaviśeṣaḥ /
hetau ca śrutirityādyasambaddhavākya sambandhi doṣādante draṣṭavyam /
stutau lakṣaṇetyannakaraṇatvena sarvajanābhimatena prāśastyaṃ lakṣyate/
śūrperṇeti cāsminpakṣe nityānuvādo'nnakaraṇasāsānyenaiva prāptasya /
itthaṃ vā sūtragamanikā tatrārthavattvaṃ tāvadarthavādātprayojanavattaratvamupapattirityaprasiddhaṃ sambandho 'pi kālpanikavāyat tasmādvetuḥ 
vyarthe stutiranyāyyeti cet 
yatpunaḥ śūrpe 'pyannakaraṇatvānupapatteḥ stutirna prāpnotītyuktaṃ kiṃ tatrābhidhīyate 
yadi ca heturavatiṣṭheta nirdeśātsāmānyāditi cedavyavasthā vi dhīnāṃ syāt 
abhyupetya vādo 'yam /
yadyapi hetuvidhānaṃ tathāpi na darvipiṭharādeḥ prasaṅgaḥ /
kutaḥ śūrpaṃ hi vidhāyānnakaraṇaṃ heturucyate /
so'pi ca na loke prasiddhaḥ śavdameva dṛṣṭāntavācinamanumāya sādhayitavyaḥ /
tadanumāne ca śrutahetutvānyathānupapattiḥ pramāṇaṃ sāca yāvatyeva hetuttramupapannaṃ tato 'dhikakalpanāyai na prabhavati/
śūrpeca homasambandhitvena pratijñāte 'nyadharmasyā hetutvādavaśyaṃ tadgatamevānnakaraṇatvaṃ vaktavyam /
saṃnidheśca tavadacchinnameva tadgamyate /
loke 'pi ca yaṃ dharmiṇaṃ pratijñāya yo heturupadiśyate sa prathamaṃ tāvattadgata viśeṣātmanaiva pratīyate /
tadātmakasya tu sādhyāṃśānugamābhāvātmāmānyamātraṃ vivaścitamiti dṛṣṭāntaprayogavelāyāmevāvadhāryate vedacetūnāṃ punarna sāmānyātmanā sādhyasambandho 'vagato na viśeṣātmanā so 'dhunaivārthāpatyā kalpanīyaḥ /
tatra viśeṣasyopādānātmāmānyāprasiddheśca tatparityāganimittasyāsambhavādupāttaviśeṣamā copasaṃhṛtānyathānupapattistadrutameva dṛṣṭāntavacanaṃ kalpayati /
tadakalpane hi hetunirdeśa śruto virudhyate /
yadi tu darvipiṭharādigatānnakaraṇatvahomasa prathamādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
mvandhāvinābhāvo na kalpyate /
na kiṃ cicchutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vā nāvakalpate tasmādodṛśaṃ dṛṣṭāntavacanaṃ kalpyaṃ yadyaccūrṇamannakaraṇaṃ tena tena juhotīti/
tadeta dviśeṣa dṛṣṭa manumānam/
loke'pi tṛṇadhūmadarśanāttṛṇāgnirevānumīyate nāgnimātram /
yathā ca gamanaṃ gośabdavyutpattinimittatvenopādīyamānaṃ sāsnādimatmāmānyapratyayottarakālaṃ tadgatameva nimittatvaṃ pratipadyate na gantṛ mātra viṣayamiti gośabdavyavasthā tathā śūrpagatānnakaraṇahetvapadeśānnānyagatahetutvaprasaṅgaḥ /
tatraināvānarthaḥ syāt /
yadyadannakaraṇasamarthaṃ śa tena tena hotavyaṃ na darvipiṭharādigrahaṇam /
yathā balavadupadhmāte 'gnau dahanahetutvenokte sa evānupadhmāto na dadded, na tu śaṅkhādayo balavadupadhmātā dahanti /
tasmāyavasthā /
yadi punaḥ śūrpagatānnakaraṇabyatirekeṇa mahāsāmānyaṃ vivakṣyate tato yadyadgahītaṃ tasya tasya kā cidannanimittatā vidyataityavyavasthitatvāvomākṣiptadravyamācānuvādaḥ sannanathako 'nnakaraṇaśabdastasmādannahetutvena stutitvameva varamiti 
vākyaniyamāt 
agnirmūrddheti yo 'rthaḥ pratoyate sa mūrddhāgnirityanenāpītyanartha ko niyamaḥ /
yasya tvadṛṣṭārthatā tasya kramānyatve taduccāraṇajanyādṛṣṭapramāṇābhāvāt kramānyatvaṃ na yuktamiti niyamārthavattā /
atha niyatapratyāyanādadṛṣṭaṃ kalpyeta taduccāraṇādevopapadyate tadadhīnatvānniyatapratoteḥ /
yastu dṛṣṭārtheṣu prakṛtipratyayasamāseṣu niyamo dṛśyate /
yathendrāgnī nīlotpalaṃ rājapuruṣaścitragurniṣkāśāmbiriti /
yuktaṃ tatra viparyaye 'paśabdārthānyatvānarthakyaprasaṅgāt/
ajādyadantaviśeṣaṇatvādinimitto hi tatra niyataḥ pūrvanipātaḥ smaryate /
tenāgnīndrāvitya sādhutvaṃ puruṣarāja ityarthānyatvaṃ kauśāmbini rityanarthakatvam/
yastvagnīndrāviti kva citprayogaḥ sa chāndaso grervā 'bhyarcitatvasya vivaśvayeti mantavyam /
tuncakaśārthapratītāvindrāgnīparameva vyavasthitam /
nanvihāpi kramānyatvādamantratvaṃ syāt /
tadevārthaparatve mati tadavināśe tu kiṃ nimittamiti na vidmaḥ /
tena mantraprasiau vākyaniyamādityapi sūtram /
atha vā 'stvaprakaraṇādhītavākyaniyamāt /
na hārthābhidhāne'nyadīyasyātmīyasya ca viśeṣaḥ /
atha vā mantrapauruṣeyavākyayostunye 'rthābhidhānasāmarthya mantravākya niyamo 'dṛṣṭārthaḥ /
athavā 'neka dhyānādismaraṇopāyaprasaṅge vākyaniyamāt /
na hi dṛṣṭe 'rthe mantrasya dhyānādervā kaścidviśeṣa ityadṛṣṭārthatā 
avidyamānavacanāt 
na catuḥśṭaṅgādi kiṃ citkarma tatsambandhi vā prakṛtī vikṛtī vā vidyate /
yadyapi ca guṇavādena kiṃ citsyāttathāpi tadanuṣṭhānābhāvānna tatsmṛtyā kāryam /
na ca jñāyate kva pradeśe prayujyatāmiti /
tatra mantrapāṭhakamānurodhenoccāraṇamāpatatīti si ddhaḥ pūrvaḥ paścaḥ /
mā mā hiṃsīrmā mā santāptamityādīni vedihaprathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
vinādi viṣayatvāda cetanārtha bandhanādityatrāpyudāharaṇam /
iha tvaprasaktāyāṃ hiṃsāyāṃ pratiṣedhānarthakyam 
arthavipratiṣedhāt 
dyutvamantaricatvaṃ cāditerekā nekatvaṃ carudravyasya vipratiṣiim/
na caiṣa vipratiṣiddho 'rthaḥ kapathikaḥ /
kathaṃ vāditirdevatā antarikṣaṃ dyaurvā bhavet /
na ca stutyarthatayāpi hetuiyaṃ pa riharttu śakyaṃ brāhmaṇe hi vidhiśeṣabhūtāḥ stutayo 'rthavantyo bhavanti /
mantrastutistvaprayojanatvānnādarttavyā 
avijñeyāt 
ke citpadārthā jñānenāvijñeyāḥ /
keṣāṃ cittu vākyārtha eva na jñāyate /
na ca mantrārthaḥ sattāmātreṇopakaroti kriyāvelāyāmasmaryamāṇa iti yadekāntenaśakyaṃ karttumuccāraṇaṃ tadeva kāryami vyavadhāryate 
aviśiṣṭastu vākyārthaḥ 
mantroccāraṇaṃ tāvadaścaragrahaṇena nirākājīkṛtaṃ na sākṣātkratvaṅgatvaṃ pratipadyate /
rāṇāṃ ca dravyavadanitikarttavyatātmapramagandasya vedo naicāśākhaṃ maghavan randhayānaḥ 
 katvātprakaraṇenāgrahaṇam /
evaṃ padārthajñānasya vākyārthapratyayena nairākācyādagrahaṇam /
vākyārthapratyayastvakṛtārthaḥ prakaraṇe viparivarttamānaḥ kriyātmakatvātprayogavacanākāṅkṣitaḥ karmasamavetānuṣṭhāsyamānārthasmṛtiphalatvenetikarttavyatā bhavati /
tatrādṛṣṭakalpanānimittābhāvaḥ samāmnānānyathānupapattyā hi tatkalpyeta nopapanne 'rthavattve /
yadyapi ca tatkalpanāvasaro bhavet tathāpi kāmaṃ vākyārthapratyayādeva na tvaupayikārthapratītinirākāṅkādākyāt/
avaśyaṃ ca dṛṣṭādṛṣṭayorviniyujyamānasya pramāṇamupanyasitavyamiha ca prakaraṇādadṛṣṭārthatā liṅgācca dṛṣṭārthatā /
na ca pra karaṇamaśakye 'rthe viniyoktumarhatītyekāntenaitadāpatati yaccanuyāttanmantreṇa kuryāditi/
na cāsāvadṛṣṭaṃ śaknototi laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ vā pramāṇaṃ vidyate /
tasmādubhayorliṅgaprakaraṇayordṛṣṭārthaprayogeṇaikavākyatā /
evaṃ ca sati yājñikaprayogaprasiddherna mūlāntarakalpanā kleśo bhaviṣyati/
ataḥ svābhāvikamevārthaprādhānyamavasthitam/
naivamiti/
na dṛṣṭo'rthe/
nirvṛtta ityetāvataiva tādarthyamavasīyate /
paruṣārthānupayogena svādhyāyādhyayana vidherānarthakyāt /
naca buddhaśākhā vidyamānavacanāceta nārthabandhanānmantrārthopayogaḥ /
tatra yadi dūre'pyadṛṣṭa kalpanāto na mucyāmahe tato 'tikramakāraṇābhāvāduccāraṇādeva kalpanīyam /
ubhayavādisiddhatvāduccāraṇakarttavyatāyāstatprabhavatvāccādṛṣṭa kalpanasya /
tatrocyate /
yajñe yajñāṅgaprakāśanameva prayojana miti /
yadyapi lokavattairna saṃvyavahārastathāpi tatsvarūpaprakāśana mātra mevānuṣṭhātṝṇāmupakara vyati/
ataśca yāvanmātramevānaupayikaṃ sambodhanādi kāmaṃ tanna vivakṣyeta na tu tadarśana sarvameva vyaktatryaṃ na hokarūpyaṃ nāma kena tantravārtike /
cinniyatam /
tasmādyathādarśanābhyupagamāirhidevasadanaṃ dāmotyevamādīnāṃ tāvadavihatamarthaprādhānyam/
tāṃ caturbhirādattadtyatrāpi vadāmaḥ 
parisaṃkhyā 
yāvaddhi mantrāmnāna manavagataprayojanaṃ prakaraṇī cākṛtāthastāvadyattatsiddhyarthaṃ kalapyate tatsarvaṃ vaidikaṃ bhavati/
nairākāṅkṣyottarakālaṃ tu kaccitamapi pauruṣeyatvādapramāṇaṃ syāt /
na ca śrutimakampayitvā liṅgādeḥ svātantryeṇa prāmāṇya miti vacyate /
tadetadāha /
sati ca vākye liṅgaṃ viyojakaṃ taccāsya nāstīti /
yadaiva hi prakaraṇādanena yajeta raśanāṃ vā gṛhṇīyāditi kalpayitumighyate tadaivāśvābhidhānomityanenāpahāromantrasya /
yadapi naiva saṃbandha ityādattaiti kathaṃ tatyaśvābhidhāno miti tatkārakasaṃbandhāsaṃbhavātkriyayaiva saha na sāmānyābhiprāyeṇa draṣṭavyam /
tasmānādānamātre vidhīyate kiṃ tarhyaśvābhidhānīviśiṣṭe /
athavā prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
phalataḥ paścāttanakāraka saṃbandha upanyasyate /
sarvathā darśaśāvatā nāsti/
yadi hi yadeva mantravacanātprāpnayāttadeva pratyakṣavacanenocyate tato vayamupālabhyemahi /
nanvevamaprāpta vidhirevāyaṃ saṃjāta iti na vaktavyaṃ parisaṃkhyeti phalenaivamabhidhānādadoṣaḥ /
sarvatra hi parisaṃkhyāśabdādevakārādvā vinā na śrutyā parisaṃkhyāniyamo vocyate vidhireva tvevaṃ jātīyakasya phalenaivaṃ vyapadeśaḥ /
kastarhi vidhiniyamaparisaṃkhyanāṃ bhedaḥ /
uccate /
vidhiratyantamaprāpte niyamaḥ pākṣike sati /
tatra cānyatra ca prāpte parisaṃkhyeti korcyate/
vidhireva hi kena cidviśeṣeṇaivaṃ bhidyate /
tatra yo 'tyantamaprāpto na ca prāpsyati prāgvacanādityavagamyate tatra niyogaḥ śuddha evaṃ vidhiryathā brohīnprokṣatīti /
yatra tu prāgvacanātyākṣi kī prāptiḥ sambhāvyate tatrāprāptipaścaṃ pūrayanyo vidhiḥ pravarttate sa niyantṛtvānniyama ityucyate /
yathā broddīnavahantīti /
tandulaniṣpattyaryākṣepādeva tatmidverna tatprāptimātraṃ vidheḥ phalaṃ kiṃ ta rhyaprāptāṃśapūraṇam /
tadaprāptipakṣe ca taṇḍulairupāyāntarāṇyāci pyeran pūraṇe tu sati yā teṣāṃ nivṛttirasāvarthānna vākyāt /
na ca tadāraṇaṃ niyamaḥ /
parisaṅkhyā hi tathā syāt /
pratyāsannāṃ vāvahantiniyatatāmutsṛjya nānyanivṛttiphalakalpanāvasaraḥ /
tatprasaktidvārā tvavahanteraniyatirāsoditi niyamāntargataivārthānnivṛttirgamyate /
na ca prāpte sati vidhirayaṃ pravṛtto yenāsyānyavṛttyarthatā kalpyeta /
prāgeva tu pravarttamānenārthasya prāpakaśaktinirodhādanyā prāptiḥ kṛtā sā cārthalabhyeti na tayaiva vyapadiśyate /
yaḥ punaḥ prāṅgiyogāttatra cānyatra ca prāpnuyāditi sambhāvyate yatra vā yaccānyacca sā parisaṅkhyā /
yathā'traivodāhate /
yathātantravārtika /
ca gṛhamedhīye pañcame pakṣe /
atrāpi ca na prāpte satyeṣā pravarttate prāpakasya śākhasyānanumitatvātkathaṃ tarhi yadyetadvākyaṃ nābhavivyattata enaṃ prāpsyaditi /
sarvasya pratyakṣasya vākyasya nānumānikavākya pratibandhamātraṃ phala miṣyate /
kiṃ hi tena paṭhitena yasyānyato 'pyarthaḥ siddhyati tadarthaṃ gaībharaśanānivṛttiḥ phalaṃ kalpyate/
tenaivaṃ kalapyate kṛtvācintānyāyena yadi nāmaivaṃ vākyaṃ na bha vettataḥ kīdṛśamanuṣṭhānaṃ syāt /
tatra mantraprāptistāvadekāntena siddhyedaśvābhidhānyāṃ tahadeva tu gaībharaśanāyāmapi prasajyeta /
yadā tvanena vākyena pratyakṣeṇa nairākāṅacyāda viśeṣa viniyogasamarthavākyānumānaṃ niṣiddhaṃ tadā kevalāśvābhidhānīviṣayatvasidvirityapaunaruktyādarthavadvākyam 
aviruddhaṃ param 
prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
dṛṣṭārthoccāraṇavādino 'pi tanniyamādaparamavaśyaṃ kalpanīyamadṛṣṭaṃ tanmamāpi pratyāyananiyamādbhaviṣyatītyavirodhaḥ /
etena mantratvādiniyamaḥ pratyuktaḥ /
satkhapyupāyāntareṣu viśiṣṭānupūrvīkamantra viśeṣāmnānādupāyāntaranivṛttī niyamādṛṣṭamātrakalpa nayā siddhamarthābhidhānam 
abhivāne 'rthavādaḥ 
catvāri śṭaṅgeti rūpakadvāreṇa yāgastutiḥ karmakālautsāha karoti/
hautre tvayaṃ viṣuvati hoturājye viniyuktaḥ/
tasya cāgneyatvādaścāḍhityadaivatatvasaṃstavāḍhādityarūpeṇāgnistutirupavarṇya ta/
tatra catvāri śṛṅgeti divasayāmānāṃ grahaṇam/
trayo asya pādā iti śītoṣṇavarṣakālāḥ /
dve śīrṣa iti ayanābhiprāyam/
sapta hastā ityaśvastutiḥ /
tridhā baddha iti savanābhiprāyeṇa /
vṛṣabha i ti vṛṣṭihetutvena stutiḥ /
roravīti stanayitnunā/
sarvalokaprasi tantravārtikam /
dvermacāndevo marttyānāviveśetyutsāhakaraṇopakāraṇa sarvapuruṣahṛdayānupraveśāt /
evamanena margeṇāsti tāvaddharmasādhanasmṛtiḥ 
vidyā'vacanamasaṃyogāt 
yadyapi pūrvapace 'yamabhiprāyo nopanyastastathāpi saṃbhava dupanyamyate /
yadi hi svādhyāyakāne 'rthavacanamupayujyeta tatastadāśrīyeta na tvevamasti karmabhira saṃyogāt /
tadanabhyāmastu prokṣapādivatmaukaryāt 
prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
uktaścānityasaṃyogaḥ 
paraṃ tu śrutisāmānyamātramiti /
yajamānastāvatprārthayitā indraśca prārthyamānaḥ sarvadārita/
kokaṭā nāma yadyapi janapadāstathāpi nityāḥ/
atha vā sarvalokasthāḥ kṛpaṇaḥ kī kaṭāḥ pramagandaḥ kusīdavṛttiḥ sa hi prabhūtataramāgamiṣyatītyevaṃ dadāti/
nīcāśākhaḥ ṣaṇḍhastadīyaṃ dhanaṃ naicāśākham /
tacca sarvamayajñāṅgabhūtaṃ teṣāṃ karmaṇya pravṛttestadasmākamāharati /
śeṣaṃ gatārtham 
ūhaḥ 
ūhadarśanaṃ na mātā vaīnaityarthye ca puṣṭyādivṛddheḥ pratyakṣatvātpratiṣedhāsaṃbhavādānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣviti śabda vijñāyate /
tatrāpi sthaulyādivṛddhyasaṃbhavādadhikārthavācitvena dvivacana bahuvaca nayoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sa cārthaparatve sarvapaśu viśeṣaṇamātrādyupāditsāyāṃ satyāmavakalpate /
yā cānyapadavṛddhisadbhāvapratītiriyaṃ ca /
yadyapi mātṛprabhṛtīnāṃ pārārthyātsaṃbandhibhedādeva ca bhedasiddhenūhyatvaṃ sadevānuvadati tathāpi nyāyāvaga tānūhasaṃkīrttanā nyāyaratantravārtika /
hiteṣūhasaṃpratyayātprakṛtau vivaścitārthatā vijñāyate /
anyathā tu taddṛṣṭamavikṛtaireva sādhyeta /
tathā yadyapyanyadaivatyaḥ paśśurāgneyyeva manotā kāryetyūhaprāptidarśanamevamutrāṇāṃ meṣāṇāmityevamādīnāṃ yathārthamūhitānāmevāmnānamapi vivakṣitārthaṃ bhaviṣyati /
itarathā prākṛtapadatyāge 'nyakalpane ca dṛṣṭadvayaṃ kalpyeta 
arthānāśrayaṇe hi sarvaṃ tadanarthakaṃ syāt /
tasmādivaścitavacanā mantrā iti siddham 
tantravārtike /
dharmasya śabdamūlatvādaśabdamanapekṣaṃ syāt 
evaṃ tāvadvidhyarthavādamantranāmadheyātmakasya vedasya dharmaṃ pratyupayogaḥ sādhitaḥ /
idānoṃ pauruṣeyoṣu smaryamāṇārthāvadhiṣu ma nvādipraṇotanivandhanāsu smṛtidhvanivadveṣu cācāreṣu cintā /
tatra kiṃ cidudāhṛtya vicāraḥ kartavya ityaṣṭakāḍhismaraṇāni manvādisthāni /
tadgandhasamarpitāni pramāṇāpramāṇavicāraviṣayatvenodāhriyante /
sandeha hetuśvābhidhīyate 
manvādivacanaṃ smṛtyapekṣaṃ smṛtiśca mūlapramāṇāpekṣiṇīti naikasyāpi vedavannirapekṣaprāmāṇya niścayaḥ /
yatastu vedavādināmevāvigānenāvicchinnapāramparyaparigrahadārḍhyamato nāprāmāṇyādhyabasānamiti yuktaḥ sandehastatra pūrvapakṣavādī vadati naiṣāṃ prāmāṇyamevāpekṣitavyamiti /
kutaḥ 
sarvasmaraṇāniddi pratyakṣādyavagate 'rthe tadānurūpyepopajāyatantravārtika /
mānānyarthaṃ samarthayanti /
tadihāṣṭakādīnāṃ svargādisādhyasādhanabhāvaṃ pratyakṣādīni tāvanna gṛhṇantīti sādhitam /
śabdo 'pi yathāgnihotrādiṣu pratyaśeṇopalabhyate naivaṃ mantrāḥ 
śabdasya tāvadekameva pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam /
ma cettenānavagamyamāno 'pyastītyucyate tato varaṃ dharmāstitvameva niṣpramāṇa kamabhyupagata miti/
na vānumānamapyasminnakā śrutikalpane/
na hi smṛtistathā vyāptā dṛṣṭā'nyadvānumāpakam /
yathaiva dharme sambandhādarśanānna kiṃ cilliṅgaṃ kramate tathāṣṭakādiśrutāvapi na vāgamena tadbodho nityena kṛtakena vā /
visrambhaḥ kṛtake nāsti nityo naivopapadyate 
na ca vijñāyate vākyaṃ kohaśata nirūpitam /
prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
arthavādādirūpāddhi paśyāmo bhrāmyato bahūn 
upamānaṃ tvadṛṣṭe 'rthe sahaśe cānirūpite /
naiveṣṭamiti tenāpi na mūlaśrutisādhanam 
yadi hi śrutikalpanena vinā smṛtinrnopapadyate tataḥ samyaṅmalā syāt/
saṃbhavati tu svapna malatvena tenānai kāntyādarthāpatteḥ sāmānyato dṛṣṭasya vānavakāśaḥ /
tasmādanupalabdhigocarāpannāryā śrutau satkhapi mṛjāntareṣvabhipretamūlābhāvānnirmūlatvābhidhānam/
nanu ye vidurevamitikarttavyatāka evaṃphalakaścāsau padārthaḥ karttavya iti /
atha vā ye karttavyo 'sāvitītyaṃ viduste tathā vijñānantastādṛśāḥ kathamivāsmānvipralabdhaṃ na karttavyo 'sāviti vadeyuḥ/
nanvanye evaṃ vadanti karttavya ityanye na vā karttavya ityāhuḥ  /
kathamanyatvaṃ yadā teṣāmadhyevamayaṃ smarthyataiti kathite bhavatyevaṃ pratipattiḥ /
atha vā ye manvādayo vidurakarttavyo 'yaṃ padārtha iti /
kathamiva te vināparādhena lokaṃ vaccayituṃ vadiṣyanti karttavya evāyamiti /
smaraṇānupapattyeti /
ye tāvanmanvādibhyo 'rvātantravārtika /
cvaḥ puruṣāsteṣāṃ yajjñānaṃ tattāvadanavagatapūrvārthatvānna smṛtiḥ/
manvādīnāmapi yadi prathamaṃ kiṃ citpramāṇaṃ sambhāvyate tataḥ smaraṇaṃ bhavennānyathā /
kasmātpunaḥ putraṃ duhitaraṃ vātikrasya vandhyādauhitroḍhāharaṇaṃ kṛtam /
sthānatulyatvāt /
putrādisthānīyaṃ hi manvādeḥ pūrvavijñānaṃ dauhitrasthānīyaṃ smaraṇamataśca yathā duhiturabhāvaṃ parāmṛgya dauhitrasmṛtiṃ bhrāntiṃ manyate tathā manvādibhiḥ pratyakṣādyasambhavaparāmarśadaṣṭakādismaraṇaṃ mithyeti mantavyam/
yathaiva pāramparyeṇāvicchedādayaṃ veda iti vākyānumānābhiprāyeṇoktam /
itarastvarthasyaivāviccheda smaraṇamayamāīti matvā punarnirmūlatvamāha /
vedaḥ punaḥ saviśeṣaḥ pratyakṣagamyastatra ghaṭādivadeva puruṣāntarasthamupalabhya smaranti tairapi smṛtamupalabhyānyepi smaranto 'nyebhyastathaiva samarpayantītyanāditā /
sarvasya cātmīyasmaraṇātparvamupalabdhiḥ sambhavatīti na nirmyūlatā/
śabda sambandha vyutpattimātrameva ceca vṛddhavyavahārādhīnam/
prāgapi hi vedaśabdādanyavastu vilakṣaṇaṃ vedāntaravilakṣaṇaṃ vādhyeṭasthamṛgveḍhādirūpaṃ mantrabrāhmaṇādirūpāṇi cānyavilacaṇānyupalabhyante /
sarveṣāṃ cānādayaḥ saṃjñā iti taddāraṇottarakālamapi ga myamānānāṃ pratyakṣatvaṃ sādhitam /
nanvaṣṭakādiṣu puruṣāntarastheghvapi kumbhakāra kriyāviva kiṃ cidvijñānamūlamasti yadi hi karmasvarūpamātraṃ sāta tataḥ pākādi tadindriyairanyānanutiṣṭhato dṛṣṭvā pare smareyuḥ /
yatasvica svargādisādhyasādhana sambandhaḥ smarthyate /
nāsaiau puruṣāntareṣūtpadyamānaḥ kaiścidṛśyataityandhaparamparānyāyenāpramāṇatā/
sarvasyānādivyavahāropanyāsena vedavatprasiddhyabhimāno bhavatyato 'ndhaparamparā nidarśanam /
vede hi prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
prāmāṇyasyānāditvamihāprāmāṇyasya /
katham 
tādṛśaṃ vāṣṭakādismaraṇam/
na ca codanā mūlabhūtopalabhyate /
na cānanubhūtasambandhā 'numātuṃ śakyate /
yadi ca vedādupattabhya smṛtayaḥ pravarttitāḥ syuḥ tatorthammaraṇavadita upalabhyāyaṃ manvādibhiḥ praṇīta ityapi pāramparyeṇa smaryeta /
syādetad /
artha smaraṇona kṛtārthīnāṃ niṣprayojanaṃ mūlasmaraṇamanārāṣṭamiti /
tadayuktam /
na hi yatkṛtaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ tadeva vismattuṃ yujyate /
a rthasmṛteḥ svataḥ prāmāṇyābhāvāt /
sarve puruṣāstāvadetajjānanti yathā vedamūnajñānādinā prāmāṇyaṃ na niścīyataiti /
te kathamiva tatrānādaraṃ kuryyaḥ /
api ca 
yadi hi tairapyarthamātramevānyebhyo 'dhigataṃ na vedo iṣṭa iti tatastatpūrvakeṣvapyayameva paryyanuyoga iti nirmūlasaṃpradāyatvaprasajānimtvānna mucyase /
yadi tu pratīnaśākhāmūnatā kalpyeta tataḥ sarvāsāṃ buddhādimṛtīnāmapi taddāraṃ prāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate /
yasyaiva ca yadabhipretaṃ sa eva tatpralīnaśākhāmastaka niściṣya pra māṇī kuryyāt /
atha vidyamānaśākhāgatā evaite 'rthāstathāpi manvādaya iva sarve puruṣāstata evopalapsyante /
yuktatarā ca svādhyayādhyayana vidheḥ sāḍhādeva pratītiriti smṛtipraṇayanavaiyarthaṃ syāt /
na catadvijñāyate /
kīdṛśāḍākyādidaṃ manvādibhiḥ pratipannaṃ kiṃ vidhiparādutārthavādarūpāditi /
paśya 
na ca manvādivacanādvedamūlatvaṃ niścinumaḥ /
te hi nirmūlamapi viprannambhādihetorutkā lokaṃ vañcayitumevaṃ vadeyuḥ /
tasmādapramāṇam 
sarvacaiva cādṛṣṭakalpanāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kalpayitavyaṃ yaddṛṣṭaṃ na viruṇaddhi na vādṛṣṭāntaramā sañjayati /
tatra bhrāntau tāvat /
samyaṅgibavaśāstradarśanavirodhāpattiḥ sarvalokābhyupagatadṛḍhaprāmāṇyabādhaśca /
idānoṃtanaiśca  puruṣairapi bhrāntimanvādonāmanuvarttitā /
tatparihāropanyāsaśca manvādīnāmityanekādṛṣṭakalpanā /
anubhave 'pi sa eva tāvadanubhavaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ /
punaśvedānīṃtana sarvapuruṣajātiviparītasāmarthyakalpanā manvādestaccaitat sarvajñavāde nirākṛtam /
puruṣavākyaparamparāpi andhaparamparayā nirākṛtā /
na hi niṣpratiṣṭhapramāṇātmalābho dṛśyate /
tathā prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
vipralambhe 'pi tatkalpanā /
vipranliāprayojanaṃ lokasya ca tatra bhrāntistasyāśceyantaṃ kālamanuvṛttirityādyāśrayaṇīyam /
utpannasya ca dṛḍhasya pratyayasya prāmāṇyanirākaraṇād dṛṣṭavirodhaḥ /
tasmātmavebhyaścodanā kalpanaiva jyāyasī /
tatra hi tanmātrādaṣṭābhyupagamaḥ /
śeṣāstu mahājanaparigrahādayaḥ sarve 'nuvidhīyante /
saṃbhāvyate ca manvādīnāṃ codanāpūrvavijñānakāraṇatvena /
tadarthamevāha tenopapanno vedasaṃyogastraivarṇikānāmiti /
yāni punaranupapannavedasaṃbhāvanānāṃ mlecchādīnāmatīndriyārthasmaraṇābhi teṣāṃ mūlakalpanāvelāyāmeva codanā saṃbhāvanāpadaṃ nārūḍheti mithyātva hetu mūlacatuṣṭayapāriśeṣyādapramāṇatvam /
saṃbhāvitāyāṃ punaścodanāyāṃ kāraṇāntaraniṣedhe kṛte nirmūlatvāsaṃbhavātpariṃśeṣasiddhaṃ codanāmūlatvam /
yattu kimarthaṃ codanā nopalabhyantaiti /
tatra ke cidāhuḥ /
nityānumeyāstā na kadā ciduḥccāryyante /
yathāliṅgādikalpitāḥ /
kathamanuccāritānāṃ mūlatvopapattiriti cet /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
pāṭhāvicchedavatpāramparyeṇa smaraṇāttatmidveḥ yathaiva hi granthaḥ saṃpradāyādavicchinno 'stitvaṃ bhajate tathaiva pratijñayānityānumeyaśrutisaṃpradāyāvicchedasiddhiḥ /
tattvayuktam /
andhaparamparānyāyādeva /
yā hi codanā na kadāciduccāryyate tasyāḥ sarvapuruṣapratyacādiprasarābhāvāddarlabhataramastitvam/
tathā ca smṛterapi saiva vandhyādauhitrasulyatā /
liṅgādīnāṃ tu nityatvānnityamanucaritaśrutyanumāna kāra ṇatvamaviruddham /
tena varaṃ pralonaśrutyanumānameva /
na ca pralayo na saṃbhāvyate /
dṛśyate hi pramādālasyādibhiḥ puruṣacayāccālpaviṣayatvam /
na caivaṃ sati yatkiṃ citpramāṇamāpatsyate /
śiṣṭacaivarṇikatantravārtika /
dṛḍhasmaraṇānyathānupapattilabhyatvācchrutyanumānasya /
yahā vidyamānaśākhāgata śrutimūlatvamevāstu /
kathamanupalabdhiriti ceducyate 
yattu kimarthaṃ vedavākyānyeva nopasaṃgṛhītānīti /
saṃpradāyavi nābhabhoteḥ /
viśiṣṭānupūrvyāvyavasthito hi svādhyāyo 'dhyetavyaḥ śrūyate /
smārttāścācārāḥ ke cit kva citkasyāṃ cicchākhāyām /
tatrāpi tu ke citpuruṣamevādhikṛtyāmnāyante /
yena ṛtuprakaraṇāmnātāḥ kena cinnimittanotkṛṣyamāṇāḥ puruṣadhamatāṃ bhajante /
yathā malavadvāsasā saha na saṃvadettasmānna brāhmaṇāyāvagurodityevamādayaḥ /
tatra yadi tāvattānyeva vākyānyuddhṛtyādhyāpayeyustataḥ kramānyatvātsvādhyāyavidhivirodhaḥ syāt /
anena ca nirdeśena anye 'pyarthavādodvāreṇa vidhimātramadhīyoran kopayikamātraṃ vā /
tatra vedapralayaḥ prasajyeta /
na cāvaśyaṃ manvādayaḥ sarvaśākhādhyāyinaḥ /
te hi prayatnena śākhāntarādhyāyibhyaḥ śrutvārthamātraṃ svavākyaira vismaraṇārthaṃ nivanīyuḥ /
na ca vākyaviśeṣo jñāyate/
yathaiva hi smṛterdṛḍhatvāddhāntimūlatvaṃ nāstyevamarthavādamūlatvamapi /
śaknuvanti hi te vidhyarthavādī vivektum /
tatra smṛ te  vidhyātmakatvātprakṛtitādātmyānumānalavyāspade 'rthabādapūrvakatvaṃ niṣpramāṇakam /
api ca /
vedo'khilo dharmamūlaṃ sarvo'bhihito veda iti ca svayameva smartṛbhirātmā badhvāsamarpita staccaitanniyogatastatkālaiḥ kartṛbhirbuddhikāritvādupalabdhamataḥ siddhaṃ vedadvāraṃ prāmāṇyam /
yastu kartṛsāmānyāt svataprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
ntrameva prāmāṇyaṃ vedamūnatvaṃ vānumānena sādhayati tasvārthakāmānusāribhirhṛṣṭa/rthairācārairanekāntaḥ /
śrayamāṇaśrutyadhīnaprāmāṇyāpatteśca viruddhatā /
tasmādarthāpattirevācāvyabhicārādupacārāt paścānmānādanumānatvenoktā asyā eva smṛterbrūḍhimnaiti /
dṛḍhatvātkāraṇānumānamatha vā dṛḍhatvasya /
na hi manuṣyā icaiveti niḥśeṣasaṃskāracchidā maraṇenāntaritvāt karmaphana saṃbandhānusandhānāsaṃbhavanocyate /
smṛtivaidikapadārthayoḥ kartṛmāmānyādupapanno vedasaṃyogastraivarṇikānāmiti codanāmūlasaṃbhāvanāpadalābhārthaṃ vismaraṇamapyupapadyataiti /
dṛśyate hyadyatve 'pyarthasmaraṇaṃ granthanāśaśca /
yaḍhātu śākhāntareṣu vidyantaeva tāḥ yastadāpi kasyāṃ śākhāyāṃ kāḥ padyantaiti syāṃśasya vismaraṇam /
vaidikatvamātraṃ tu prāmāṇya siddhaye paripālayanti /
taviśeṣajñānaṃ punaranaupayikatvādanādarttavyameva /
tathā pratyupasthita niyamānāmityāgatamāgataṃ nimittaṃ prati ye niyamyante vṛ ddhavayaḥ pratyutthānādayasteṣāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvādeva prāmāṇyamiti /
etadyuktam /
kutaḥ 
nahi yāvakiṃ cidācaraṇaṃ tasya sarvasya mūlamitra pramāṇī kriyate /
dharmmajijñāsādhikārāt /
yadi ca gurvanugamādīnāṃ kevalaṃ dṛṣṭārthatvameva syāttata ṛṣyādivaḍammeṃ pratyaprāmāṇyamaveti nopanyasitavyāḥ /
syādetadapramāṇatvenaiṣāmupanyāsa iti /
na /
tathā sati hetudarśanāccetyatrodāharttavyā bhaveyuḥ /
tasmācchreyāṃ samiti ca darśanaṃ niṣphalam /
na ca niyogataḥ śāstrāta prāptiḥ / śakyate chupāyāntareṇāpi sāmadānādinā gururadhyāpanādīni kārayitum /
tatrāsti niyamavidheravakāśaḥ /
sarvatra ca yathā kathaṃ cillokapakimahāyopāḍhānātmarakṣaṇaprītyutpādādikā ṭārthatā bhāṣyakāroktā śakyā vaktum /
na cāvaghātādīnāṃ vṛṣṭikāmayāgādīnāṃ ca dṛṣṭārthānāmavaidikatvam /
tasmāt satyapi dṛṣṭārthatve sambhāvyate vedamanatve niyamādṛṣṭasiddherananyapramāṇakatvādataśca gurvanugamanādernaimittikatvāḍha kriyāyāṃ pratyavāyaḥ ka raṇe ca na bhavati /
dṛṣṭaṃ ca prīto gururadhyāpayiṣyatītyevamādi niṣyadyate /
niyamāccāvighnasamāptyarthāpūrvasiddhiḥ /
evaṃ cācārādgṛhyamāṇeṣu tathā syādityatra sakṛdasakṛddānuṣṭhānamiti vi cāro yuktaḥ /
itarathā tu dṛṣṭārthatvavaśenaivodakapānādivadavadhāraṇaṃ syāt /
yattu bhāṣyakāreṇa dṛṣṭārthatvādeva prāmāṇya mityuktaṃ tatpūrvapaśavādyatiśayārthametaduktaṃ bhavati /
yāstāvadahaṣṭārthāḥ smṛtayastāḥ kathaṃ cidapramāṇī kuryyādbhavānimāḥ punagurvanugamanādiviṣayāḥ kathamivāpramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyantīti /
sabhāprapādīnāṃ yadyapi viśaṣaśrutinaiva kalpyate tathāpi paropakāraśrutyaiva samastānāmupādānātprāmāṇyam /
tasmācchreyāṃsamityave gaībhenānugantavye siddhavacchreyasāmūnairanugamanaṃ darśayati /
yathā dhanvani nirudake kṛtāḥ prapāḥ pareṣāmupakurvantyevaṃ tvamiti devatāstutipare vākye siddhavatprapāsadbhāvaḥ tasyāśca pārāyaṃ dṛśyate /
goṛcihnaṃ śikhākarma tatrāpyācāraniyamasyādṛṣṭārthatvānnaiva tāvanmātrameva prayojanam/
śakyaṃ pāyāntareṇāpi gocaṃ smarttu tenānya evābhiprāyaḥ /
karmāṅgabhūnaṃ tāvaccaturavattapañcāvattādivibhāgasiddhyarthamavaśyaṃ smarttavyaṃ gotram /
ataśca taccinhārthamapi prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
tāvacchikhākalpasmṛtaḥ prāmāṇyamastu /
tanniyamādṛṣṭasya tvakāntenaivānanyagatitvāt puruṣārthatā setsyatīti /
tena sarvasmṛtīnāṃ prayojanavato prāmāṇyasiddhiḥ /
tatra yāvadvamokṣasambandhi tadvedaprabhavam /
yattvarthasukhaviṣayaṃ tanokavyavahārapūrvaka miti vi vektavyam /
eṣaivetihāsapurāṇayorapyupadeśavākyānāṃ gatiḥ /
upākhyānāni tvarthavādeṣu vyākhyātāni /
yattu pṛthavīvibhāgakathanaṃ tadbarmmādharmmasādhanaphalopabhogapradeśavivekāya kiṃ cidarśanapūrvakaṃ kiṃ cidvedamūlam /
vaṃśānukramaṇamapi brāhmaṇakṣatriyajātigotrajñānāthaṃ darśanasmaraṇamūlam /
deśakālaparimāṇamapi lokajyotiḥśā khavyavahārasiddhyarthaṃ darśanagaṇita saṃpradāyānumānapūrvakaṃ bhāvikathanamapi tvanādikālapravṛttayugasvabhāvadharmmādharmmānuṣṭhānaphalavipāka vaicityajñānadvāreṇa vedamūlaṃ aṅgavidyānāmapi kratvarthapūruṣārthapratipādanaṃ lokavedapūrvakatvena vivektavyam /
tatra śikṣāyāṃ tāvadyadvarṇakaraṇasvara kālādipravibhāgakathanaṃ tatpratyakṣapūrvakam /
yattu tathā vijñānātprayoge phalaviśeṣasmaraṇama /
mantro honaḥ svarato varṇato veti ca pratyavāyasmṛtistadvedamūlam /
evaṃ kalpasūtreyvarthavādādimiśraśākhā ntara viprakīrṇanyāyalabhyavidhyupasaṃcāraphalamarthanirūpaṇaṃ tattatpramāṇamaṅgīkṛtam /
lokavyavahārapūrvakāca ke cid ṛtvigādivyavahārāḥ sukhārthahetutvenāśritāḥ vyākaraṇe 'pi śabdāpaśabdavibhāgajñānaṃ sākṣācādi vibhāgavatpratyānimittam /
sā dhuśabdaprayogātphalasiddhiḥ, apaśabdena tu phannavaiguṇyaṃ bhavatīti vaidikam /
chandovicityāmapi gāyavyādiviveko lokavedayoḥ pūrvavadevapratyaścaḥ /
tadjñānaparvakaprayogāttu phalamiti śrautam / tathā cāniṣṭaṃ śrūyate /
yo ha vāviḍhitārṣeyachandodaivata brāhmaṇena mantreṇa yajati yājayati vetyādi /
jyotiḥśāstre 'pi pugaparivarttaparimāṇahāreṇa candrādityādigativibhāgena tithinakṣatrajñānamavicchinnasaṃpradāyagaṇitānumānamūlaṃ graha sau sthya dāsthya ni mittapūrvakṛtabhāśubhakarmmaphala vipākasūcanaṃ tadgataśāntyādivi dhānadvāreṇa vedamūlam /
etena sāmudravāstuvidyādi vyākhyānam/
īdṛśā vā vidhayaḥ sarvatrānumātavyāḥ /
īdṛśe gṛhaśarīrādimanniveśe satyetadetacca pratipattavyamiti /
mīmāṃsā tu lokādeva pratyaścānumānādibhiravicchinnasaṃpradāyapaṇḍita vyavahāraiḥ pravṛttā /
na hi kaścidapi prathamametāvantaṃ yuktikalāpamupasaṃdattuṃ kṣamaḥ /
etena nyāyavistara vyācaśīta 
svalaṇa viviktestaiḥ pratyakṣādibhirañjamā /
parīścakāpitaiḥ śakyāḥ pravivektuṃ na tu svataḥ 
tathā ca mānave 'pyabhihitam /
pratyaścamanumānaṃ ca śābdaṃ ca vividhāgamam /
trayaṃ suviditaṃ kāyeṃ dharmaśudvimabhīmatā 
ityādibhistarkaviśśuddhirāśritā /
prāyeṇa ca manuṣyāṇāmadharmabhūyiṣṭhatvāttajjñānaprativaddāḥ pratibhāsteṣu teṣu kumārgeṣu pravatante /
tatra lokārthavādopaniṣatpravata starkaśāstraiḥ sarvavipraprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
tipattimukhapradarśanam /
tadupapattayasta ilā balapūrvakaṃ ca niścayadvāraṃ kathyate /
anyathā punaḥ 
virodhe tvanapekṣaṃ syādasati hyanumānam 
smṛtiprāmāṇyamutsṛṣṭaṃ prasaktaṃ sarvagocaram /
sati vedaviruddhabe tadidānīmapodyate 
yāvatī smṛtiḥ pratyakṣavedavākyavirudvā tāṃ sarvāmudāhṛtya saṃpradhāryate /
kiṃ punastādṛśyapi dharmapramāṇatvenāvadhāryyate /
kiṃ vā parthyodasyataiti /
kutaḥ saṃśaya iti ceducyate 
ekaviṣaye viruddhārthopasaṃhāriṇī vijñāne virudhyete balavadabalabattvanirṇayācca bādhyavādhakabhāvaṃ pratipadyete tadyadi śakitavirodhayorapi śrutismṛtyoḥ kena citprakāreṇa bhinnaviṣayatvena vyavasthā siddhyet /
vidheyapratiṣedhyayorvā virodhābhāvādekasminnapi viṣaye samuccaya sambhavāde kaprayogagatatvā sambhavādobhayoḥ prāmāṇyāṅgīkaraṇena prayogāntare cobhayānugrahaḥ syādityevaṃ vikalpāśrayaṇe'pyatyanta virodhābhāvātpratyakṣānumitaśrutijanitajñānayośca vaidikatvā viśeṣe tulyabalatvakalpanādubhayaprāmāṇyamupapatsyate /
tato yathopanyastaviṣaye'pi smṛtiprāmāprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
eyamapeśitavyam /
atha ta prayatnenāgviṣyamāṇe 'pi na viṣayāntarakṛtā vyavasthā, nāpi prameyāntarāvirodhātsamuccayo, nāpi vikalpenobhayānugrahaḥ, kiṃ tarchubhayapīḍanādatyantavirodha eva /
pratyaśānumeya śrutyoca laukika pratyaśānumānavanma hānbala viśeṣastadā gatyantarābhāvādubhayānugrahāsambhava śratibalīyasvena sṭa tiprāmāṇyamapekṣaṇīyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti 
anāśaṅkita vipralambhabhrāntyādimūnā hyavyāhata  vedamūlatvāvadhāraṇāḥ smṛtayo nirvyājaprāmāṇyāḥ śakyante dharmavyavahārāṅgatvena sthāpayitum /
yadā tu vedaviruddhatvahetudarśanaparasparavigānādinā kena cidapi senāsāmaprāmāṇyaṃ kalpyate /
tadā bahuśākhākhilaprakaraṇādibheda bhinneṣu veṭeṣu śrutiliṅgādyātmakopadeśanāmādidvārātideśātmaka vicitra pramāṇabhāgeṣu ko jānāti kā smṛtiḥ kośena vedabhāgena viruddhyamānā kadānumāsyataiti /
ataścaivaṃjātāśakannaiva ka cidapi viśvasyeta aviśvāsācātyantameva prāmāṇyaṃ pratihamyeta /
tathā hi 
eka mūla vyavasthāyāṃ mūlāntaranirākriyā /
aprāmāṇya nivṛttyarthaṃ śakyā na tadupekṣaṇe 
smṛteḥ śrutivirudvāyāstato mūlāntaraṃ bhavet 
tasmādyathā virodhe 'pi padyamānapramāṇatā /
paṭhitasmaryyamāṇānāṃ tathaivetyavadhāryyatām 
mūlāntaraṃ nirastaṃ ca sāmānyenaiva yatpurā /
tadanuprāṇyate paścādhirodhe netyatikriyā 
kiṃ ca bhrāntyādimūlānāṃ sambhavāsambhavāśrayaḥ /
smṛtīḥ prati viruddho 'yaṃ bādhapakṣo na yujyate 
viruddhatvaṃ ca jānanti smartārastāḥ smaranti yat /
vedamūnnabalaṃ tyaklā kimanyattatra kāraṇam 
rāgadveṣamadonmādapramādālasyalubdhatāḥ /
kva vā notpredituṃ śakyāḥ smṛtyaprāmāṇya hetavaḥ 
kā vā dharmmakriyā yasyāṃ dṛṣṭo hetuna yujyate /
kathaṃ ciḍā viruddhatvaṃ pratyaśśśrutibhiḥ saha 
vaidikānyapi karmāṇi dṛṣṭārthānyeva te viduḥ /
alpenāpi nimittena virodhaṃ yojayanti ca 
prasaraṃ na labhante hi yāarka cana markaṭāḥ /
nābhidravanti te tāvatpiśācā vā svagocare 
tasmāllokāyatasthānāṃ dharmanāśanaśālinām /
evaṃ mīmāṃsakaiḥ kāryyaṃ na manorathapūraṇam 
tattathaivānumantavyaṃ karttavyaṃ nāntarā latham /
savai lathayataḥ moded durbraddaśakaṭādivat 
vedaśca yadi dṛṣṭārthaṃ śrayamāṇavirodhi vā /
na vidadhyāttatastādṛk smṛtistanmūjatāṃ tyajet 
ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇādānaṃ tānūnaprādikarmma ca /
yaha tvigyajamānānāṃ dṛṣṭārthaṃ sarvamiṣyate 
tadā kiṃ nāma dṛṣṭārthaṃ buddhyā siddhyedavaidikam /
tenādāveva yā klṛptā smārttānāṃ vedamūlatā 
tasmādedavirudvānāṃ dṛṣṭārthānāṃ ca hetubhiḥ /
smṛtīnāṃ na pramāṇatvaṃ vihantavyaṃ manāgapi 
virodhe tvanapekṣaṃ syātprāmāṇyaṃ smṛtibandhanam /
avirodhe hi vedena tanmūlamanumoyate 
svātantryeṇa pramāṇatvaṃ smṛtestāvanna sammatam /
vedamūlānumānaṃ ca pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate 
pratyaśce śrūyamāṇe tu na vidyetānumānikama /
nahi hastini dṛṣṭe 'pi tatpadenānumiṣyate 
tāvadeva spharantyarthāḥ purastādānumānikāḥ /
yāvatpratyakṣa śāstreṇa mūtrameṣāṃ na kṛntyate 
na hi sāścātpramāṇatvaṃ smṛtīnāmupapadyate /
nānyamūlaṃ yatastatsyāttattu mūlaṃ na vidyate 
prameyaṃ yatparicchedyaṃ bhavetkana cidātmanā /
tasya syāttatparicchedātmāvakāśapramāṇatā 
tadvi dūramapi prāpta me kamapyagataṃ padam / itareṇa gate nādāve kāntenaiva jīyate 
na hi yena pramāṇatvaṃ labdhapūrvaṃ kadā cana/
tena tatsarvadā labhyamityājñāpayatīśvaraḥ 
yasya tūtpadyamānasya mūnameva nikṛntyate /
mukhaṃ vā rudhyate tasya nātmanābhaḥ kaढ़ā cana 
na cāpi bādhakābhāvāllabdha ātmati sarvadā/
labdhavyaḥ sa virodhe 'pi pūrvasāmānyadarśanāt 
apavādena vā yasmādutsargo bādhitaḥ kva cit /
tasmātsarvatra bādhyo 'sāvityetadapi neṣyate 
yo hi sāmānyadṛṣṭena vyavahāra ninoṣati /
tṛṣṇācchedo bhavettasya mṛgatṛṣṇājalairapi /
bādhitāṃ mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ vā dṛṣṭvā hadagato'pyasaiau /
vipralambhabhayādeva na snānādi samācaret 
anumānaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca tāvadartheṣu jāyate /
rudhyate viṣayo yāvannāsya pratyakṣajanmanā 
ataḥ va citpramāṇatvaṃ ka cidapyapramāṇatām /
vyavasthāpayatāṃ nyāyainna bhavedarddhavaiśasam 
tasmādevaṃ na vaktavyaṃ sarvāsāṃ vā pramāṇatā /
athavā sā na kasyāścidyadi ka cidanāśritā 
vikalpaḥ kiṃ punastāsāṃ neṣyate śrutibhiḥ saha 
vikalpasyāṣṭadoṣatvānna tāvatkhabhyupeyatā /
pāścike cāpramāṇatve smṛtayaḥ sunirākarāḥ 
pramāṇapadavoṃ yāvannārohatyeva hi smṛtiḥ/
bādhyate tāvadatyantaṃ śrutyā 'nyanirapekṣayā 
parādhīnapramāṇatvānna pramāṇapaḍhe sthitā /
tyā bādhitamācāsau punarnojjīvituṃ kṣamā 
pramāṇatvaṃ pratītaṃ yadujjvanantadapadbhutam /
ekastāvadayaṃ doṣaḥ syātpratītiviparyyayāt 
so 'pi syādaparo doṣaḥ pramāṇārthaviparthyayāt /
aṅgīkṛtyāpi tau doṣau pūrvaṃ kenāpi hetunā 
sampratyapahavānasya doṣa eko hi jāyate /
pratyakṣaṃ dṛḍharūpaṃ ca yatpurastānnirākṛtam 
etaeva prasajyerandritīye 'pi prakalpite /
evameṣo'ṣṭadoṣo 'pi yadrohiyavavākyayoḥ 
śrotā tatra pravṛtto 'pi brohiśāstreṇa kṛpyate /
dābhyāmaśvamukhīvacca śrutibhyāmabhitaḥ samam 
prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
ubhayorapramāṇatvaṃ pratighātātprasajyate /
tatra prāmāṇyayogyasya yadaprāmāṇyakalpanam 
ekasya vā pramāṇatvaṃ paricartuṃ na śakyate /
tadaprāmāṇyamātre tu na iyorapramāṇatā 
sa cāyamubhayornāśa ubhayārthāparigrahāt /
miśrarvā yajamānasya miśrāṇāṃ vidhyadarśanāt 
brohayo nirapekṣā hi jñāyanta yāgasādhanam /
yavāścaivatasteṣāṃ miśratvaṃ nāvakalpate /
naiva vroddibhiriṣṭaṃ syādyavairna ca yathāśrutaiḥ /
miśrairijyeta cettatra bhavedubhayabādhanam 
sayamatyantamanyāyyā iyorapyanavasthitiḥ /
avyavasthā na yuktā hi vyavasthā yatra labhyate 
tena yasya pramāṇatvaṃ pramāṇaṃ sarvadāstu tat /
yasyāpi tvapramāṇatvamapramāṇaṃ taducyatām 
na hi tatraikarūpatve cihnaṃ kiṃ ciyavasthitam /
yenaikatra pramāṇatvaṃ syādanyatrāpramāṇatā /
śrutismṛtyoḥ punaḥ spaṣṭaṃ vyavasthākāraṇadvayam /
yena śruteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ syātsmṛteścāpramāṇatā 
yo yasya svadhaḥ prāptaḥ sa bacavatā kāraṇāntareṇa viparyyayaṃ pratipadyate 
smātasya bādhakaḥ śrauto balavattvātpratīyate /
pratyakṣaṃ cānumāne ca prāgetaddhyavadhāritam 
smṛtyā pratīyate yāvacchutyā tāvatpramīyate /
viruddhadharmmatāmeko na ca dharmaḥ pratīcchati 
smṛtvā cārthaṃ parāmṛśya yāvattadviṣayāṃ śrutim /
anumātuṃ pravarteta tāvatmo 'rtho 'nyato gataḥ 
yugapatpramimīyātāṃ yadi cārthaṃ śrutismṛtī /
prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
gṛhīta viśeṣatvātsyātāṃ tulyabale tataḥ 
tato 'rthaviprakarṣe 'pi pramāṇatvena tulyatā /
bhavedeva śrutismṛtyorarthaḥ śrutiparigrahāt 
jāyate klṛptayā tasmātmā bādhyetāpratiṣṭhitā/
smṛtimūlānapekṣā hi smṛtitvādeva hīyate /
tadapekṣā punaḥ śrutyā bādhyate mūnavarjjitā 
dvitīyena prakāreṇa vikalpapaढ़vīṃ gatā /
pannā pākṣikaṃ bādhamatyantaṃ bādhyate smṛtiḥ 
kiṃ tu tasyāḥ pramāṇatvaṃ śrutimūlatvakāritam /
yatastasmādatanmūlā tadānīṃ sāvadhāryyate 
śrutiṃ mukkāca yanmūlaṃ smṛteranyatprakalpyate /
tenaivāsyāḥ pramāṇatvamatyantaṃ pratihanyate 
na tu smṛteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ punarujjīvituṃ kṣamam /
vicchinnaśrutimṛlatvādgastaṃ bhrāntyādihetubhiḥ 
tatastvaduktamārgeṇa pratihanyeta sarvadā /
na tvetasya prasaṅgo 'sti smṛtaḥ pūrvaparigrahe 
na paścācchrayamāṇāpi śrutiḥ syātpratibandhikā /
gaībhenāpanītaṃ hi harennāśvaśvidgataḥ 
śrādye prapāṭhaka yena vrīhiśāstraṃ pratīyate /
dvitoye yavaśāstraṃ ca na tattatprati durbalam /
svaśākhāvihitaiścāpi śākhāntaragatānvidhīn /
kalpakārā nibadhnanti sarvaeva vikalpitān 
pūrvaprāptau pramāṇatvaṃ paratvenāpramāṇatām /
prasajyamānikāmeva ko 'dhyavasthetmacetanaḥ 
sarveva śrutimalātaḥ sarvā vā bhrāntimūlikā /
smṛtirevaṃ nirūpyeta na tu syānmūlasaṃkaraḥ 
tataśca pūrvavijñānaṃ mithyaitaditi cintayan /
dāvevāpramāṇatvaṃ smṛtarityadhyavasthati 
samānaviṣayatvādvi pūrveṣāmapi bādhanam /
na hi teṣāmamithyātve mithyedānīntanaṃ bhavet 
naitadevam /
pratiprayogaṃ pramāṇaparthyālocanāt /
yadi hyeka prayogagatā  locanenaiva prayogāntarāṇyapyanutiṣṭheyustato yena trīhiśāstramapramāṇīkṛtya yavāḥ parigṛhyeransa yāvajjovaṃ taireva yajeteti naiva pratipuruṣamubhābhyāṃ vikalpyamānābhyāṃ vyavahāraḥ siddhyet /
tena yāvatprayogabhāvipramāṇālocanavaśātpūrvānumitāṃ śrutiṃ cidapyaśṭaṇvanpunarapi smṛtimevopacabhya kartṛsāmānyatiṅgenaiva śrutimanumimānaḥ pratyakṣayā śrutyāściptacittatayā tatprāmāethenānyathānupapadyamānena smṛtyaprāmāṇyaṃ kalpayanpūrvāvadhāritamūlavyatyayameva pratipadyate, na pūrva kṛptamanjasyāprāmāṇyādhyāropam /
padyamānatayaivāsya sulabhāva jñānatvāt /
yaccaitadanavasthānaṃ tvayā māṃ prati codyate /
bhavato 'pi tadastyeva tenācodyatvamekataḥ 
kālāntare 'pi yo bādhaḥ sphuṭatvenāvadhāryyate /
yattenāpya pramāṇatvaṃ kṛtaṃ tanna nivarttyate 
nanu yavaśruterapi tarhi pramāṇatvena parigṛhyamāṇāyāḥ puruṣāprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
ntarabādhastadānī mastīti mithyātvaprasaṅgaḥ 
smṛtistu yāvatāṃ puṃsāṃ prathamaṃ gocaro bhavet /
tāvatāṃ sarvadā 'bhāvānnāprāmāṇyena mucyate 
adhyāropyeta mithyātvamujjvalāyāḥ śruteḥ punaḥ /
labdhameva smṛtau taccatkimarthaṃ kalpyate śruteḥ 
nanu śrutya viruddhāyāḥ śrutimūnnatva niścayaḥ /
anumānādapi prāpsyan kena citpratibadhyate 
tataścāīvaiśasaprasaṅga nivṛttiḥ /
yathā 
yadyapyaudumbarīsarvaveṣṭanaṃ dharmaśākhādhyetasmṛti vilakṣaṇa pratyakṣaśrutyarthopapatrakāropanibaddhaṃ tathāpyupariṣṭāhacyamāṇātyāntaratvābhiprāyeṇa paruṣopadiṣṭatvā viśeṣācca smṛtivadevodāhṛtam /
krītarājakabhojyānnatvavacanaṃ yadyapyatharvavede 'sti tathāpi tasyāhavanīyasaṃbaddhayajñakarmopakārābhāvāttada dhikṛtatrayīpratipāditāgnīṣomīyasaṃsthāvadhibhojanapratiṣedhavirodhātprakaraṇaviśeṣādikatau virodhi syādityanena nyāyenādhikṛtānadhikṛtabalāvala viśeṣābhiprāyeṇa smṛtipaścaniḥkṣepābhāṣyakāraṇoḍhāhiyate /
kṛṣṇa keśatvaṃ ca yadyapyanavasthitavayovasthākāla viśeṣaṃ jātaputratvapakṣe saṃdigdhasamāveśaṃ ca tathāpi yuvaiva dharmamanvicchedityevamādismaraṇāprakāśitārthaṃ yauvanāvasthāparigrahādantato vā vayonatikramāśrayaṇādaṣṭācatvāriṃśadvarṣa brahmacarya prāgupanayana sambaddhakālasya ca vayasaḥ sātireka dvipañcāśañcatuṣpañcāśanmātrasaṃvatmaraparimitatvenāparihāryyavayotikramāvaśyaṃbhāvitvāyakta eva virodho hagyate /
nanu ca pūrvakṛta sarvaveṣṭanottarakāla vihita veṣṭitāyā eva sparśanaṃ sambhavatītyavirodhaḥ /
kathamavirodho yadā sparśanaṃ nāma tvagindriyadvāraṃ spṛśyasaṃvedanam /
na ca vastrāntaritāyā udumbaryāḥ sparśo gṛhyate /
na ca vastre spṛśyamāne audumbarī spṛṣṭa/
bhavati /
vastraudumbarojātivyakti sparśānāmatyantabhedāt 
nanu bhūmābaudumbarībuddhyabhāvādvakhāntaritāyāṃ ca taddudvyavyatirekādṛṣṭāntavaiṣamyam /
tathāhi 
satyaṃ tatreṣyate snānaṃ tadvasparśakāritam /
kāraṇaṃ tadvi caṇḍāla sparśavanmatam 
kathaṃ punarayaṃ dharmaśāstreṣvanupanibaddho 'pi caṇḍālaspṛṣṭavalasparśana nimitto doṣo 'dhyavasīyate /
kathaṃ vā neṣyate doṣaḥ kāṣṭhaloṣṭaṭaṇādiṣu /
tatspṛṣṭaspṛśyamāneṣu na kramante 'tra yuktayaḥ 
yathā kāṣṭhaṇādīnāṃ mārutādeva śuddhatā /
smaryate vāsaso naivaṃ toyaprakṣālanādinā 
amedhyasyaivaṃ yasmātpaṭhanti /
caṇḍālaspṛṣṭavāsasañcāstyevāmedhyatā /
tasmādasti salilādiśadviḥ /
nanu ca manuṣyasyaiva caṇḍālasparśanimittaprāyaścittavidhānāda śuddhirūpamamedhyatvaṃ gamyate na dravyāntarasya gavāśvādaḥ /
tataśca vastraṃ kiṃ gavāśvādivadaduṣṭamuta puruṣavad duṣṭa miti sandehe gavāśvāditulyamevāvadhārayituṃ yuktam 
puruṣasya sacailasya snānaṃ yasmādvidhīyate /
tasmātpuruṣavahastraṃ na gavāśvādivanmatam 
pūrvoktenaiva mārgeṇa vyāmocaikāntakacanām /
vikalpe 'vaśyamāpannāṃ smṛtāveva niyacchati 
nahi pramādapāṭhatvaṃ śakyaṃ kalpayituṃ śruteḥ /
duḥśruta svapnavijñānamūnnā tvāpadyate smṛtiḥ 
parasparavirudve hi viruvāvyabhicārivat /
pramāṇe yatra dṛśyete tatrānyenaiva nirṇayaḥ 
pramāṇamayate yāti mūlabhūtāṃ śrutiṃ yataḥ /
vivantādayatestasmātpramāṇā smṛtirupyate  na ca varṇāśrayatvena yalopo na bhaviṣyati /
vyorvaloti yalopo hi vanādipratyayāśrayaḥ 
yalope ca kṛte 'kāro yaḥ śuddhaḥ pariśiṣyate /
tadantāvadhikātpaścāṣṭa kriyate striyām 
tadetaditarāśrayaṃ bhavatītyuktam /
yadvā śrutyapramāṇatvātsmṛteḥ prāmāṇya miṣyate /
siddhācca tatpramāṇatvācchratyaprāmāṇya kalpanā 
tadidaṃ vikalpavādina ubhayacetaretarāśrayatvam ekāntavādinatvanyataratra 
tatra sparśanasya lṛptaṃ mūlaṃ kalpyaṃ smṛteriti 
svataḥ sthitātpramāṇatvācchruteḥ syāt klṛptamūlatā /
smṛteḥ śrutyanumāpakaprāmāṇyātkalpyamūlatā 
na cādhyāropyamāṇāpi śruteḥ syādapramāṇatā /
na ca tasyāmasiddhāyāṃ smṛtiprāmāṇya sambhavaḥ 
evaṃ tāvatsmatiprāmāṇyaṃ kalpayanneva tadādī parājīyate /
ya ḍhā tu śrutiprāmāṇyagata mitaretarāśrayatvamālocyate tadā tatrāpi pratipacabhūtasmṛtyaprāmāṇyāpekṣayā nirapavādaprāmāṇyāvadhāraṇasiddheḥ parādhīnatvātpūrvasidvasmṛtyaprāmāṇya limāyām 
tena yattadādye padake 'nanumitāvasthāyāṃtapakṣaṇamātre smṛteraprāmāṇyaṃ dṛśyate tāvataiva labdhapramāṇatvā śrutiḥ sarvadā nirapavādaprāmāṇyā bhavatītyanyataḥ paricchedaḥ 
kṛtvaikamavadhiṃ tasmātsidvamādye kṣaṇe dṛḍham /
ānupūrvyā brajettāvadyāvatmidvo 'paraḥ sphuṭaḥ 
hetudarśanāca 
itaśca na pramāṇatva mūlahatvantare kṣaṇāt /
vyabhicāre hi notpattirarthāpattyanumānayoḥ 
ka ciyānti va cinobhaḥ ka cidyuktivikalpanam /
