te cānyatrāpi dṛśyante tathā jātyantareṣvapi /
śāvaleyādibhedosti tadapatyāntareṣvapi 
pravibhaktā hi ye dṛṣṭā dṛśyante saṃhatāḥ punaḥ /
piṇḍā sādhāraṇatvena tairvyaktirupalacyate 
“astyarthaḥ sarvabhavdānāmiti pratyāvyanacapaṇam /
apūrvadevatā svargaiḥ samamārgaṃvādiṣu” 
tattu kacyāvibhāgena sāmānyānāṃ nirūpaṇāt /
prayuktaṃ na gavādīnāṃ tatra vācakaśaktatā 
sattāmete vadantaśca na śuddhāṃ saviśeṣaṇām /
vadantītya bhidhātuṃ hi śakyaṃ dvedhāpyasaṃbhavāt /
śuddhavacanatve tāvat sarveṣāme kārya pratyāyanātparyāyatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
punaruktatvācca astiśabdaprayogānupapattiḥ 
deśakālādyapekṣāyāmapi naiva sattāyāṃ nāstitvamabhidhātuṃ yuktam /
vibhutvanityatvābhyāṃ sarvadeśakālavyāpitvāt 
ya eva stiśabdena dvitīyo bhāvavikāra uccate/
jāyamānavipariṇāmādyavasthasarvatrastuṣu vinaśyattāparyanteṣu vastvākṛtipratipattirdṛśyate /
tena yadi nāma mahāsāmānyamabhidheyaṃ pratijñāyate tato vastvarthaḥ sarvaśabdānāmiti pratyāyyajacaṇamiti kāmaṃ vaktavyaṃ nāstyartha iti /
na cāvayavārthaparityāgena sacchabdasattāśabdau varttete iti bhavacchabdavadevāstīti sadbhāvaḥ satteti na tu vaiśeṣikaparibhāṣayā yato dravyaguṇakarmasu saditi pratītiḥ sā satteti /
evaṃlakṣaṇā jātiḥ pratipattavyā 
astitvamastitetyevaṃ dṛśyete pratyayau yataḥ /
sa vastuvacanaḥ śabda ākhyātapratirūpakaḥ 
astitīrā gauriti tiṅantasamāsatvenānupasaṃkhyānādavaprayaṃbhāvipratyayāntadāṇadvāra subantatvayogyāvyayapadena saha kṣīrāśabdasyānyapadārthe bahuvrīhirabhyupagantavyaḥ /
tatra cāyaṃ sadarthavacanaḥ sacīrā gauriti pratyayotpādāt /
tataśca vastuni sati ca prayuprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
jyamānamastiśabdamapacabhya tadarthānusaraṇapratyāsannaṃ sacchandaṃ ca devāttaliti ca svārthikaṃ devane tivattala mihāpyastidhātuvācyārthaviśiṣṭa kartṛpratītimanaṅgīkṛtya śuddhadhātvarthamātravacanāveva sacchabdasattābhandau gṛhītvaivaṃ tārkikaiḥ kalpitaṃ sacchandavācyā sattā mahāsāmānyamiti /
taduktāntamananānādarācca padavākyavidbhirapyupekṣitaṃ prasiddhamivemāmavasthāṃ prāptaṃ yena gavādiśabdavāyatvenāpi saṃbhāvyate 
vastuśabdo hi rūḍhitvādyaktijātyantarāśritam /
sāmānyaṃ yadravītyetadgamyaterthairgavādibhiḥ 
yadevākṛtiviśiṣṭavyaktyabhidhānapate vyaktiviśiṣṭākṛtipakṣe vā nirākaraṇakāraṇaṃ tadatrāpi sulabham /
viśeṣaṇasya pūrvaṃtarābhidhānaprasaṅgāt 
tatra 
viśeṣaṇamanabhighāya tadviśiṣṭaviśeṣyābhidhānasaṃbhavāviśeṣaṇasya ca viśeṣyeṇātyanta saṃbandhātpūrvatarābhihita viśeṣaṇabhūtagotvasaṃbandhādeva sattāvagama siddheḥ /
na tatrābhidhānaśaktikalpanāyāma rthāpattirapyanyathāpyupapadyamānaphalatvapratijñatā satī na pravarttate/
tathā vyaktiviśiṣṭasattābhidhānepyeṣa eva nirākaraṇa hetuḥ /
anityasaṃbandhajñānānantaśabdaśaktivyaktyabhidhānapūrvakaikasattā bhidhānakalpanāyāśca kevalavyaktyabhidhānapacavadanupapattiḥ /
yattu “apūrvadevatā svargaiḥ samamā” riti 
ke cicchatārthāpatyā ke cidvākya śeṣavākyāntaraparthyapasthāpi tārthaviśeṣavacanā eva santotyantāvyabhicārisvārthadvāreṇa sattāṃ gamayanto 'nabhidhāyakatvenāvadhāryante na sattāpadārtho vyabhicaratīti lakṣaṇayaiva tebhyaḥ sattāpratītiḥ 
sarvapadārthānāmiva kāryārthāpattigamyāni sāmarthyāni santi yāgādijanitaṃ ca puṃsāṃ phalaprāptimāmarthyamapūrvaśabdavācyaṃ yāgānuṣṭhānātpūrvamabhūtamanuṣṭhānottarakālaṃ cāpūrvaṃ jāyataiti yaugikatvādevāpūrvaśavdābhidhānaṃ sarvatra labhyate, tathā dīvyanti dyotante vā candrādityāgnigrahanakṣatratārakādirūpeṇa vāyavaśva satatagatyā stūyante sarvairmantrairiti devāḥ sujñānaśabdasaṃbandhā viśeṣa rūpai reveti na sattāgocaratvaṃ pratipadyante /
tathā svargaśabdenāpi nacacadeśovā vaidika pravāda paurāṇika yājñikadarśane nocyate yathā hi veḍhe ye hi janāḥ puṇyakṛtaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti teṣāmetāni jyotīṃṣi nakṣatrāṇi tathā caiṣa jyotimantaṃ puṇyanokaṃ jayaprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
toti /
yadi vetihāsapurāṇopapannaṃ merupṛṣṭham /
atha vānvayavyatirekāmyāṃ vibhaktaṃ kevantameva sukhaṃ yatsaṃvatsara/
didhvanubhūyamānaṃ duḥkha sādhanaśatoṣṇapipāsādisamasta inharahitārthapattisihṛdeśāntarānubhavanīyaṃ, tacca yadyapi tādṛśamadṛṣṭapūrvvaṃ tathāpi miśrānubhavādeva vivekenoddhṛtya svargaśabdārthatvena jñāyamānaṃ sattāṃ gamayatīti na tadabhidhānamapecyate 
ataśca naiva gośabdo gosattāmabhidhāsyati /
gotvākhyākṛtivācyatvasaṃdehāttu vicāryyate 
uccate kāryayogitvādgamyate vyaktivācyatā /
śabdaśaktyanurodhāttu nākṛtervyatiricyate 
kiṃ tāvatprāptam 
nityaṃ yathaiva śabdānāmānātānāṃ prayojane /
arthapratyāyanārthatvātta śenāvadhāraṇā 
ākṛtirthyādi śabdārthaḥ kasya syuḥ prokṣaṇādayaḥ / kena cejyeta na tyāga ākṛtarupapadyate /
amūrtā hyākṛtirnityā nāvaghātādibhājanī /
tadvidhiḥ pratiṣedho vā tenāsyā nāvakalpate  vroddīnavahanti, paśuṃṃ saṃjñapayati, somamabhiṣuṇoti, pāvayati, somena paśunā brīhibhiśva yajataiti yāvanta evamādayo vināśimūrttimadviṣayāḥ saṃskārāḥ prayojanasiddhyarthā vā teṣāṃ prayogacodanāyā ākṛtāvabhāvātau tu bhāvātkāryyapradhānatvācca padārthapratītervidhyadhīnatvācca sarvapuruṣaceṣṭānāmavaśyaṃ vidhiviṣayatva yogya vākyārthapūraṇasamarthapadārthakalpanamaṅgī karttavyam /
tathā yadapi brāhmaṇo na hantavyona kalajaṃ bhavayitavyamityādipratiṣedhavidhānaṃ tadapi prāptipūrvakatvaṃ sāpekṣatvāktau ca prāptisaṃbhavādākṛteścāna dhikārādasatyāṃ prāptāvanarthaṃkameva syāt /
ta smādyena śabdārthena prayogacodanānāṃ bhāvo bhavati sa evābhyupagantuṃ nyāyyo na tattvajñānamātradṛṣṭasiddhyarthapadārthakalpanā yukteti /
syādetaḍyaktisaṃbhavatprayogacodanāsu vyaktyarthastatonyatrākṛtyartha eva bhaviṣyatīti /
tadasat /
nyāyena hi sthitamekasya śabdasyāyeṃ kyamanava sthita saṃvandhāne kādṛṣṭa vācaka śakti kalpanavikalpadoṣaprasaṅgāt /
saṃbadvānāṃ cārthānāmanyatarābhidhānenaivetaratra pratipattisiddheḥ /
kathaṃ tarjñākṛtipratyaya iti ced ata āha /
vibhāgāditi /
yatastu nityameva vyaktyā kṛtyoravibhāgastasmādyaktirabhihitā satī śaknotyevākṛtiṃ gamayitum /
taduktaṃ tadbhūtādhika raṇe /
yasya tu padasya yorthobhidheyatvenāśritastasya tatparihārāsaṃbhavāḍhavaṇyaṃ tatrasthasyaivārthāntaraṃ lākṣaṇikatvenābhyupagantavyaprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
mityapi cākṛtipadārthakasya vyaktiṣu sādhāraṇānaikāntikatvānirṇayo na syāhyaktipadārthakasya punaratyantāntarbhūtākṛtiniścayasiddherna śabdavyāpārakalpanopapattiḥ /
tasmādyaktireva śabdārtho nākṛtiḥ /
na ca vikalpasamañcaya saṃbandha samudāyānyatara viśiṣṭānyatarābhidhānapaścāḥ saṃbhavantyavibhāgādeva sarveṣāmapi jñānasiddheḥ 
gośabdādīnāmākṛtivacanatve gauḥ śuklo 'ruṇayā piṅgācyaikacāyanyā gavā krīṇātīti ṣaḍ gāvo deyā ekāṃ gāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādityevamādiṣu prayogeṣu sarveṣāṃ jātiguṇamātravacanatvātmāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na prāpnoti 
nahi gotvākṛtiḥ śuklā nāruṇā nāpi ṣaḍguṇā /
vyaktistvevaṃguṇā tasmādyakterevābhidheyatā 
jātiguṇaviśiṣṭa vyaktivacanatvena śuddhavyaktivacanatvena vā pratyase bhavati sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ tacca tatra dravyama evaṃvidhamapi samānadravyaśabdatvaṃ tvatpace na syāditi nañā tadabhāvaprasaṅgaṃ darśayati /
yatta bhāṣyakāro viparītārthena dravyaśabdenaiva tadāśrayagulāyā nanñaścāsamartha samāsamaṅgīkṛtya na dravyāśrayavacanaḥ śabdo bhavedākṛtivādina ityāha /
tadatikliṣṭaṃ vyadhikaraṇanirdiṣṭaguṇaprayogāheṃ cetyupeścitavyam /
tatrāpi caivamaścarārthaṃ mā trasaṃbhavayojanā /
dravyāśrayasya guṇasya yaḥ śabdo 'dravyaśabdaḥ sa ākṛternirguṇatvādekavākya saṃbandhaṃ gotvaṃ śuklamityādivanna pratipadyate/
sāmānādhikaraṇyacodyaṃ tu svapakṣepya viśeṣāttadānīmapyanupapannameveti pūrvaiva vyākhyā karttavyā /
kiṃ ca naiveṣṭakābhirākṛtisaṃpādanamabhyupagataṃ yataḥ svabhāvātsnāyvādyārabdhadravyasa bhavāyitvenopālambhaḥ syātpiṣṭa piṇḍasiṃhavatmādṛśya saṃpattiḥ pakṣadvayepi codanārthaḥ sā tvākṛtyantaravilaśaṇaśyenākṛtyā syānna tu vyaktyantara vilavaṇaśyena viśeṣeṇāsādhāraṇena vā /
nirvika rūpatvātsāmānya viśeṣānapekṣaṃ vyaktimātrasādṛśyama vidheyaṃ, sarvadravyeṣu tulyatvāt /
ekavyaktiparigrahācca vyaktyantareṇa sādṛśyaṃ na kāryyaṃ syāt /
tasmācyena vitkriyā vyaktau śabdārthena saṃbhavati /
na sādhakatama iti/
nayevaṃ smṛtiḥ prayenaiścīyate iti śyenaci “tkarmaṇyagnyākhyāyā” miti hi sā prayenaṃ cayanena sādhayeditīmitatamatvam /
tatrāpi mukhyāsaṃbhavātmādṛgyaparigrahaḥ /
asādhāraṇe śabda pravṛttya saṃbhavādavyapadegyatvena ca sarvatrāviśeṣātmāmānyākāreṇa ca nirūpaṇe vikalpāyāpakāpekṣayā vyāpyasāmānyasya naivaṃ viśeṣavyāpyāpekṣayetaradākṛtiḥ /
tatra viśeṣapakṣe saṃbandhānanvākhyānavyabhicāra sāmānyabuḍyabhāvapratyarthaśaktikalpanādayo doṣāḥ /
na ca yatra saṃśayastatpratyāyyaṃ bhavatīti nirviṣayatā śabdasya /
etena svatantrobhayābhidhānamārgaḥ pratyuktaḥ /
vyaktiviśiprākṛtimārgopi nāgṛhītaviśeṣaṇetinyāyākteḥ prathamagrahaṇaprasaṅgāt /
saṃbandhasamudāyayorapi svarūpapratyayābhāvātsarvatra cā viśeṣādavaṇyaṃ saṃbandhisamudāyiviśeṣaṇatābhyupagantavyā bhavati /
tatrāpi śaktitraya kalpanā /
vyaktyaṃśe coktadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ /
na ca prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
vyaktyā kṛtyorbhinna kāryayorguṇapradhānanānāvasthayoḥ samudāyopagamanaṃ yuktamanatyantabhedācca bhinnadhamma saṃbandhasamudāyau na yuktau /
ākṛtiviśiṣṭopi vyaktiviśeṣo naiva pratīyate vyaktiviśeṣabuddhyabhāvād vyaktimātramiti cenna /
tadānīṃ tasyākṛtitonyatvenānirūpaṇāt /
mātraśabdo hi sāmānyavācītyākṛtirevocyate /
nānākāreṣu ca vastuṣa tadbhedānusāritvācchaktīnāmanvayavyatire kābhyāṃ gotvākāranibandhanaiva gośabdavācyatvaśaktirgamyate /
ta dekādhārasāmānyāntarāvagatirviśeṣākāṅkṣā vetyarthavyāpyavyāpti bhyām /
anatyantavyatirekāccā kṛtera mūrttatvādyāśrayadoṣāprasaṅgaḥ /
sāhi pratīyate niṣṭarūpā kriyāyoginī tu vyaktyupetā bhavatyeveti prokṣaṇāveśaṇādi tu na kathaṃ cinna saṃbhavati /
viśasanādyapi tu vyaktyavyatirekāpekṣayā saṃbhavatyeva /
tathāhi /
paśvādisvapanītāṅgeṣu viśeṣabuddhyabhāvātmāmānya rūpaiva viśasanādiviśiṭā buddhirdṛṣṭā /
nanvevamanityā ''kṛtiḥ syāt tenāṃśeneṣṭaivāśra yāntarāvināśāttu sarvairapyavināśovaṇyamevaiṣṭavyaḥ /
tena yattāvanmātrameva tasya vināśo 'nekadeśasya tu na kathaṃ cidvināśaḥ syādityubhayathā vyavahāraḥ /
atyantavyatireke tu naiṣa dharmavidhiviṣayo vyatratiṣṭheta /
na ca paśutva, mamūrttatvāt /
tadupalacitaṃ tu yaddavyaṃ taddavyatvāhate na tādrūpyeṇa gamyataityekārthaṃ samavāyāvyāpakatvācca dravyaṃ gamayitavyaṃ, tatrāpyamūrttatve doṣaḥ /
āśrayopakṣaṇācca dravyamātraprasaṅgaḥ /
viśeṣastu paśutvasya vā dravyatvasya vā 'vyāpakatvādagamyaḥ /
na vā pratītaṃ vidhinā saṃbadhyate /
na ca yatra saṃśayastatpratītam /
na cānyatrokto dharmastatrāsaṃbhavādanyatra kā ryyastasmānna sāmānyakṛto viśeṣeṣu yuktaḥ, viśeṣā api vyapade śātsāmānya mevetyamūrttatā /
asādhāraṇena tu naiva vyavahārastasmādanirūpyo dharmavidhiviṣayaḥ /
sāmānādhikaraṇyādi ca prasidviviparītaṃ lakṣaṇayā kalpyam /
bhāṣyakāreṇa tu vyatirekābhyupagamenāśrayamācagatiruktā, viśeṣarūpā na kadā cid vyaktiḥ pratīyate /
yopyāyibhāvaḥ sopyaupacārikaḥ /
sāmānyāñca viśeṣalacaṇaṃ tatra nāśrayitavyam /
ākṣepa  mātrabhāvādatha vaitadviṣaya evāyaṃ prapañcaḥ /
kiṃ śabdenākṛtyā veti /
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ cākṛtyeti nirṇayaḥ /
yo hi dhūmādagnitvaṃ pratipadyate tasya naicyepyākāṅkṣā sidvā /
mānasādapacārāditi /
yo hi jā yātmāmānyavācitāṃ hitvā kaṃ cideva viśeṣaṃ yatra saṃbandhānubhavastaṃ vācyaṃ manyate tasya sāmānyāpratīterna viśeṣāntarāpekṣā bhavatyatha vā yathā śabdātkhatantrāmākṛtiṃ buddhyate naivaṃ kadā cidākṛtimabuddhvā vyaktimiti/
kena tarhi gotvagobdayorviśeṣaḥ /
vyatirekāṃśasyaikatra vivaścā /
gotvavāniti tu sphuṭaṃ pratyayena jātimadabhidhānaṃ vibhāgopapatteḥ /
sāmānyasya vopalakṣaṇatvānna bhedapaṇadoṣaḥ /
bhedānāmeva cāyaṃ pratyekaṃ sarveṣāṃ vācakaḥ /
yastūpādīyamānatve saṃśayaḥ sa saṃkhyādhāra viṣayaḥ /
uddiśyamāneṣu nirṇaya eva/
gavādiśabda grahaṇaṃ sarvanāmākhyāta śabdānāmantarbhāvārtham /
prayojanaṃ sāmānya viśeṣa bhabda yoreka viṣayatvātsāmānyabhisṛsya viśeṣaśiṣṭenābādhaḥ pūrvapakṣe /
evaṃ vā 
caturvidhe pade cātra dvividhasyārthanirṇayaḥ /
prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
kriyate saṃśayotyatternaipasarganipātayoḥ 
vācakatvepi pāścātyamanuyātyevamādiṣu /
pratīyate viśeṣo yaḥ saṃśayena sa nāpyate 
ākhyātasyāpi nanvatra na yuktārthavicāraṇā /
dvitīyādāviyaṃ yasmādvistareṇa kariṣyate 
pratyayārthasya bhāvasya vācyatā pratipāditā /
prakṛtyarthavivekārthaṃ vicāraḥ kriyate 'dhunā 
yā coktā bhāṣyakāreṇa yāgāderabhidheyatā /
siddhā seha vivekārthaṃ tatra bhāvasya bhāṣitā 
nāmākhyātapade tena kasyārthasyābhidhāyake /
kimākṛteruta vyaktariti cintā pravarttate 
kathaṃ lacaṇasaṃbandhaścintāyāḥ prakṛtena vā /
smṛtimūla vicāreṇa vaktavyaṃ tvidamāditaḥ 
vaktavyaḥ pūrvamartha śvecchabdarūpanirūpaṇāt /
nahi vācyamavijñāya sādhutvamavadhāryyate 
vācyamātre hi sādhutvamavijñāte na labhyate /
na cākṛtyā na ca vyaktyā vinā tannopapadyate 
vyaktirvācyeti vijñānaṃ na sanmūlamasaṃbhavāt /
tena vyākaraṇepodṛg na pramāṇaṃ smṛtirmatā 
nanu cākṛtipakṣepi vyaktāveva kriyākriye /
śabdārthe saṃbhavāttena kimarthaiṣā vicāraṇā 
vyaktipaśce vikalpaḥ syātkauṇḍinye dadhitakrayoḥ /
sāmānya vākyada /
rbalyā ttakramevetaratra tu 
procaṇaṃ pūrvapakṣepi karttavyaṃ laukikeṣvapi /
brīhiṣu śrutisāmarthyādvādhitvā sannidhikramam 
evaṃ homepi dadhyādau prakṛte prakṛte 'tha vā /
prakṛte śrutivācyasya homatvasyāpi saṃbhavāt 
nanu gauritiśabdādau sarvametadvicāritam /
tena tena gatārthatvātpunaścintā na yujyate 
yathā cākṛtirityādau bhāṣyakāreṇa coditam /
punarasyāḥ pratijñāyā heturapya bhidhāsyate 
ukte vāpyabhidheyatve jāteḥ sadbhāvasiddhaye /
vyaktirvācyā na vetyetadgatārthaṃ vicāryyate 
ekatve sati karttavyo vicāraḥ śabdavācyayoḥ /
bheṭeta saṃśayābhāvānna cintāvasaro yataḥ 
alaukikeca śabdārthe vācyavācakarūpayoḥ /
ajñātayorna jāyeta saṃdeho vācyavastuni 
abhedakāraṇaṃ cātra pratyabhijñānameva te /
anyattūpacayatvena tena cintā na yujyate 
vyapadeśādibhedācca kathaṃ bhedo na jāyate /
tatrānuktamidaṃ vaktuṃ vicāroyaṃ pravarttitaḥ 
arthābhede ca cinteyaṃ śabdābhede tu satyapi /
ghaṭate kasya vācyatvaṃ vyaktyā kṛtyoīyorapi 
bhedābhedanimittābhyāṃ kriyate saṃśayodbhavaḥ /
kiṃ prāptamucyate bhinnau śabdārthai/
lokavedayoḥ /
vyapadeśasya bhinnatvādākhyāyā lakṣaṇasya ca /
kharoccāraṇabhedācca lopavyatyayadarśanāt 
tadayuktaṃ kriyābhede kartṛbhedo hi neṣyate /
dantikartṛtvamagneśca padārthebhyaḥ pratīyate 
asatā kathamanyattvaṃ karmāṇātaḥ pratīyate /
apūrve vṛtraśabdārthe kriyāśabde'pyalaukike 
akriyatvācca bhāṣyoktairvā kyairityabhidhāsyate /
tenoktasyaiva śabdasya trivṛḍhādernavādiṣu 
tadaṃ satyaṃ na śabdasya bhedorthaguṇakāritaḥ /
tena svarādibhedana vaktavyā bhinnarūpatā 
tāveva vede śabdārtho loke yāviti bhāṣyate /
vedasyaiva prasajyeta sakalasyāpramāṇatā tantravārtike /
bhāvaḥ pratyayārthasya vidherapratipādanāt /
arthāntare ca śabdasya na prayogo vidhīyate 
vaidikeṣvapi śabdeṣu pratyakṣeṇa punaḥ punaḥ /
yahā vibhāgaśabdena śabdasyoccāraṇe sati 
sarvathā śakyate bhedo na vaktuṃ śabdavācyayoḥ /
ekatve yājñikānāṃ ca prasiddhiranugṛhyate 
pratyakṣapratyabhijñāte vedaśabde 'nyarūpatā /
vyapadeśādibhedaśca svarabhedādikāritaḥ 
nānyatvaṃ yujyate bādhātpratyakṣa pratyabhijñayā /
vacanāmabhedastu śūdravarjitatāpi vā 
na ca bhinnatvamanyeṣu prajñātārtheṣu yujyate /
uttānānāṃ ca keṣāṃ cidahatāṃ na vidhīyate 
prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
uttānetyādikā tena nāto bhedaḥ pratīyate /
tasmādyāveva śabdārthoṃ loke pūrvaṃ nirūpitā 
kimākṛteḥ padārthatvaṃ, kiṃ vyaktaḥ, kiṃ iyoriti /
bahavaḥ pratibhāntyatra pakṣāḥ pratipadaṃ ca ye 
jātirvyaktiśca saṃbandhaḥ samūho liṅgakārake /
saṃkhyā ca saptamī teṣāmaṣṭapakṣī dayodvayoḥ 
jātirvyaktiviśiṣṭā vā vyaktirjātiviśeṣitā /
jātisaṃbandhayorevaṃ sāmānya samudāyayoḥ 
aṣṭau paścā niyoktavyāḥ ṣaḍḍiḥ pratyekamuktavat /
evamānantyameteṣāṃ pacaṇāmi gamyate 
vyakterjātiviśiṣṭāyā viparītamathāpi vā /
upanyāsena caiteṣāṃ jñeyāḥ sarve prapañcitāḥ 
tenādya dāveva pacau vicāryeta kimākṛtiḥ śabdārtho, vyakti riti /
bhāṣyakāreṇa ca saṃśayakāraṇamuktaṃ sāmānyapratyayādyaktī ca kriyāsaṃbhavādityetadayukta, vyakterapi pratoyamānatvātkathaṃ jātereva pratītirupanyasyate /
yadi ca vyakti saṃpratīyeta tataḥ saṃśaya eva na syātkimabhidhīyate 'neneti /
na ca kriyāsaṃbhavo 'bhidheyatve kāraṇavyaktyanta rāṇāmapi prasaṅgāt /
tena pūrvoktameva saṃśayakāraṇaṃ mantavyam /
prayogapratītyoḥ sādhāraṇatvācchāstrāntare vyaktipaścābhyupagamātsaṃśayaḥ /
yadvā śabda uccārite sāmānyapratyayād vyaktyākṛtyoḥ sāmānyāttulyātpratyayād vyaktau ca prabdādākṛtāvālambhana sparśana śyena sadṛśacayanādi kriyāsaṃbhavātmā mānye vyaktau ca pratyayākriyāsaṃbhavāditi coktam /
kā panarākṛtiḥ kā vyaktiriti /
kathaṃ punarayaṃ praśno yadā gaurityetasya śabdasya kortha ityatra jātinirūpitā /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
yenaitantra jñātamasau pṛcchati kā punarākṛtiḥ kā vyaktiriti /
saṃdehāḍā 'tra punarubhayasminpratīyamāne kā vyaktiḥ kiyatī vā jātiriti /
vaiparītyena vā kaścitpṛcchati yadā śāvaleyādipiṇḍānna kiṃ cid vyaktaṃ vastvantaraṃ bhinnamupalabhyate tadā kuto 'yaṃ viveko vyaktiriyaṃ jātiriyamityatha vā vyavahārārthaṃ sarvaiva cintā kriyate jāteśca padārthatvepi vyaktī kriyāsaṃbhavānniṣpayojanā cintā yatastvasaiau prayatnenaitadvicārayati tena nūnaṃ kāpyasya piṇḍādatyantabhinnavyavahārayogyā jātirabhipretetyabhiprāyaḥ /
tatrāca dravyaguṇakarmaṇā sāmānyamātramākṛtiriti /
yau tāvadajñānasaṃśayavādinau tayoḥ svarūpakathanamātreṇaiva nirākaraṇaṃ vaktavyam /
yastu viparītavādī tasyaiva nirākaraṇamabhidhīyate /
yadyapi jātirvyakteratyanta bhinnā nopalabhyate, tathāpi śavalākāra tasmiprathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
nupalabhyamāne sāmānyabuddherālambanaṃ prathamapādoktena nyāyenākatiritarā vyaktiḥ /
na cānena granthena jāteḥ sadbhāvaḥ pramāṇaṃ vā pratipādyate vyaktarvivekaḥ kevalaḥ kathyate /
tenaivābhiprāyeṇa mātraśabdaprayogo 'nyathā tasya gatārthataiva bhavet /
yadapyukta nūnaṃ kāpyatyantabhinnā jātirabhipreteti /
tasyāpyuttaraṃ dravyaguṇakamaṇāṃ sāmānyamātramākṛtirabhipretā nātyantavyatiriktati /
dravyādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ yatmāmānyaṃ sattārūpaṃ tadanena nirdiśyate, tannirdeśanāvāntara sāmānyānāmapi nirdeśasiddhiḥ /
yaddā /
sāmānyaśabdasya pratyekaṃ saṃvandhāhavyatvādīni cīṇi sāmānyāni nirdiśyante sattayā vyavahārābhāvāt /
atha vā /
mātraśabdaprayogāhavyādiṣu yāvantyavāntarasāmānyāni mahāsāmānyaṃ ca tatsarvamabhidhīyate /
asādhāraṇaviśeṣā vyaktiriti bahuvrīhiḥ /
asādhāraṇa viśeṣā yasyāṃ vyaktau seyamasādhāraṇa viśeṣā, na tvasādhāraṇāśca te viśeṣāśceti sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ saṃbhavati /
upariṣṭādviśeṣādhārasya vyaktitvābhidhānāt /
smṛteśca /
tena samyagabhihitaṃ kimākṛtirvā vyaktiriti /
kiṃ prāptam ālambhanaprocaṇaviśasanādiprayogacodanāyā vyaktipaśce bhāvādākṛtipakṣe cābhāvādvāhāṇo na intavyaḥ surā na pātavyetyādipratiṣedhacodanāyāśca vyaktipaścaeva saṃbhavāddevadatta gāmabhyājetyevamādilokikavyavahāra codanāyāścopapattevyaktiḥ śabdārtha iti niścīyate /
saṃkhyākārakopapatteśca /
yadi hi vyaktiḥ śabdārtho bhavati tato vṛkṣau vṛkṣābhyāmiti prātipadikābhihitāsu vyaktiṣu pratyayābhihitadvitvādisaṃkhyākaraṇādikārakaṃ vobhayamupapadyate, itaratra tu jāterasaṃkhyeyatvāt kārakatvāccobhayamapyanupapannam /
lākṣatantravārtika /
pikavyaktyāśrayaṇaṃ cāpadyetā tathā ca sarvavaidikavākyārthānāṃ lākṣaṇikatvaṃ syāt /
vyaktipaśce ca puruṣo devadatta iti mukhyaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyopapattiḥ /
jātipakṣe lākṣaṇikadāraṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ kalpayitavyaṃ bhavet tenāpi vyaktaḥ padārthatvamava soyate /
paśumālabheteti ca śruterhṛdayajihādibhirvyaktyavayavairupariṣṭād vyavahāro dṛśyate /
na jātyā karmmabhiśca dravyasyāpekṣitatvād vyaktipakṣepeścitābhidhānaṃ netaratra siddhasvarūpāyāśca vyaktarabhidheyatvaṃ yuktaṃ nāprasidvāyā jāterato vyaktiḥ śabdārthaḥ /
kimityubhayaṃ vācyaṃ nāśrīyate prayogapratotikriyopapatteriti cet /
na /
aneka śaktikalpanāprasaṅgādekābhidhānenaiva saṃbandhāditaratra pratīterupapannatvād vyakterevābhidheyatvam /
sāmānyapratyayaḥ katha miti ced vyaktisaṃbandhādupapatsyate /
yatraiva kriyānupapattistacaivārthāpattyā vyaktivacanatvaṃ yuktam, anyatra tu pūrvapratīterjātivaca natvameva nyāyyamiti cet /
na /
uktamārgeṇā nekaśakti kalpanādidoṣaprasaṅgāt /
anavasthita śabdārthasaṃbandhāpatteḥ saṃśayāpatteśca vyaktivādinaḥ kathaṃ ninimittā vyaktyantare śabdasya pravṛttiriti cedākṛticihnanimittatvād vyaktyantare prayogasyāvirodhaḥ /
bhāṣyakārastu kathaṃ sāmānyāvagatirityupanyasyā kṛtiścibhūtā bhaviṣyatītyuttaraṃ dadāti, tadasaṃbaddham /
kathaṃ sāmānyāpratyayakāraṇe pṛṣṭe vyaktyantaraprayoganimittaṃ kathyate /
tenādhyāhāreṇaitad vyākhyeyam /
kathaṃ sāmānyāvagatiriti cet /
vyaktisaṃbandhāt /
kathaṃ vyaktyantare prayogaḥ, cihnatvādākṛtarityevam /
yadā kathaṃ sāmānyāvagatiriti cedityupanyaste pūrvapañcavādī sāmānyāvagatimapotumaśakkutrannā kṛtiviśiṣṭavyaktyabhiṣāmapakṣaṃ pa prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
rigṛhṇātyākṛtiścihabhūtā viśeṣaṇabhūtābhidheyā bhaviṣyati/
prataśca tatpratītiracodyā /
tena kevalā viśiṣṭā vā vyaktiḥ śabdārthaḥ /
tathā ca ṣaḍ deyā ityevamādiṣu ṣaḍādikā saṃkhyopapatsyate /
anyaṃ tadvayamiti ca vyaktyantare 'nyaśabdopapattistadurmatā ca bhaviṣyati /
anyathā vyaktyantarānayanepi jāterananyatvādaguṇatvāccobhayamanupapannaṃ, tasmād vyaktiḥ śabdārtha iti prāpte 'bhidhīyate/
naitad vyaktiḥ śabdavācyeti kiṃ tvākṛtiḥ padārtha iti vi jñāyate /
śyenacitaṃ cinvīteti śravaṇādana hi śyenavyaktiṃ cayanena kuryyād ākṛtiṃ veti vākyārthī/
syātām /
yāvadiṣṭakādiḥ prayenavyaktaḥ karttumaśakyatvāt snāyvādibhirapyanirvṛtteriṣṭakābādhāccyenavyaktaḥ prayojanakalpanācinotera mukhyārthatvāt /
'karmaeyagnyākhyāyā' miti smṛtiparityāgaprasaṅgācca /
cayanena śyenavyaktiṃ kuryyādityevaṃ tāvannopapadyate /
tathā ''kṛterapoṣṭakābhiḥ kartumaśakyatvāddai vanirmitatvātprayojanakalpanāccinotera yathārthatvaprasaṅgātsmṛtibādhāccākṛtiṃ kuryyādityapi nopapadyate /
pariśeṣāyenamiva citamagnisthannaṃ cayanena nirvarttayediti vākyārthaḥ /
tatava yayā kayā ciccyenavyaktyā sadṛśasyāgneśvetu maśakyatvātsarvaṃ vyakti sādṛśyāsaṃbhavādatītānāgatavyakti sādṛśyānupapatteśca śyenākṛtisādṛśyasaṃpattisaṃbhavāccākṛtiḥ śavdārtha iti niścīyate 
pūrvaṃ sāmānya vijñānāccitrabuddheranubhavāt /
gāmānayetivākyācca yathā ruciparigrahāt 
tasmādākṛtipaśceṣyācammanādisaṃbhavādākṛtireva śabdārtha iti siddham tantravārtike /
uktaṃ samānāyaidamarthya tasmātsarvaṃ ta dartha syāt 
evaṃ smṛtisahitasya vedasya prāmāṇye siddhe 'dhunā vākyārthavyākhyānāvasare satyaparisamāpyaiva pramāṇalakṣaṇa kena saṃbandhena nāmadheyacintāyāḥ prastāvaḥ kriyate /
ke cittāvadāḥ /
kimuhnidādayo guṇasya pramāṇam, uta kriyāṇāmeva nāmadheyatveneti /
tadayuktam /
evaṃ sati hi samastameva śāstraṃ pramāṇanjayaṇādabhinnaṃ syāt /
sarvatra hotadvicāryate, kimidaṃ vākyamasyārthasya pramāṇamutānyasyeti /
ye 'pi caite he api sūtre pūrvottarapakṣau parikalpyaikādhikaraṇatvena vyācakṣate tairapyuktaṃ samāmnāyaidamarthya mi tyanena sūtreṇa kaḥ siddhāntānabhipretaḥ pūrvapaścānuguṇo 'rtho vidhīyataiti vaktavyam/
nayuktaidamarthyāntarbhāvavacanamudbhidādīnāmaniṣṭam/
tasmād iyorapyadhikaraṇayoranu mitapūrvapañcayoruttarapañcasūtradvayametaditi vyākhyeyam /
tatra prathamaṃ tāvadudbhidādīnudāhṛtya saṃdehaḥ kriyate, kimate kaṃ cidvameṃ pratyupayogaṃ gacchanti, uta neti /
kiṃ tāvatprāptam /
nāyasya kriyārthatvādityānarthakyam /
āha ca 
nahote vidhyādiṣvantarbhavanti /
sādhyasādhanetikartavyānabhidhāyitvāt tāvaccodanābāhyatvaṃ stutibuddhyabhāvādarthavādātirekaḥ /
karmāṅgabhūtaivaṃsaṃjñakaprakāśayitavyārthābhāvānmantra kāryanivṛttiḥ /
na cānyadvedaprayojanamastītyapramāṇamevaṃjātīyakā iti /
atrābhidhīyate 
yadā tadarthatrayānyatamārthamiti sthitaṃ tadā vicāraḥ kimarthamiti/
na tāvadarthavādatvaṃ vākyaśeṣatvābhāvāt /
kathaṃ punarayaṃ na vākyaśeṣo yāvatā vāyurvai kṣepiṣṭhetyādivadekavākyatā 'vagamyate /
naitadasti /
vidhātavyasya hi yaḥ śeṣaḥ so 'rthavādaḥ /
ayaṃ tu vidhyuddeśādeva nātiricyataityavākyaśeṣaḥ /
tatsaṃbhavinaśca stutyupayogitvaṃ na yujyataityuktamaudumbarādhikaraṇe /
na caikapadena stutirdṛṣṭā /
na ceca tāṃ pratipadyāmahe /
yadapyuṅgedanaṃ paśūnāmanena kriyataityevaṃ prāśastyaṃ kalpyeta tadapi tṛtīyāntasamudāyāśrayabalavattarakaraṇatvaprasiddhyā bādhyate /
anyathā hi prātipadikaprādhānyādā vāyurvai kṣepiṣṭhetivatprathameva prāyojyata /
na cāsya mantratvaṃ, tādrapyeṇāpratīteḥ /
adhyetvasmaraṇābhāvācca /
na caikapadatvātmākāṅkṣatvaṃ karaṇapratītyā vā smārakatvam /
na caitadabhidheyaḥ kaścitprayogasamavāyyartho dṛśyate /
na cāsamavetaprakāśane karmāṅgatvam /
māntravarṇikadravyakalpanāyāmapi gauravam /
na cāsya sūktavākavadviniyojikā śrutirasti yena māntravarṇikadravyakalpanā syāt /
na cāsya rūpaṃ prayogāīm /
ataścāvi niyuktatvādiṣe tvādivadapi nādhyāhāreṇa nirākāṅkṣīkṛtya pra yogaḥ /
sphuṭaṃ ca brāhmaṇenaikavākyatvamityamantratvam /
tasmādidhyuddeśāntargatasyaivottarādhikaraṇena vicāryate guṇavidhirnāmadheyamiti /
tatra tāvat 
prātipadikaṃ tāvadudbhedanasamarthe dravye khanitrādāvayavaprasiddhyā pravartate /
na ca samudāyo 'rthāntaravācī loke prasiddhaḥ /
na ca lokādanavagato  'rtho vedādavagamyate saṃvandhasya śāstrā hetutvāt /
tṛtīyāpi ca karaṇavācinī, kriyāyāśca śaktimad dravyaṃ tadādhārā vā śaktiḥ karaṇaṃ, tenodbhitsādhanako yāgo 'vagamyate /
na ca yāgasyodbhittvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kva citprasiddham /
arthavattvātpravṛttiviśeṣakaratvaṃ vidhāyakositpadapuruṣāṇāṃ pravṛttau viśeṣo 'nyathā hyanuccaritasamaiva pravṛttireṣāṃ syāt /
atha vā prasiddhatvāguṇavidhirarthavattvamabhidheyavattvaṃ nāmadheyatve tvartho na vijñāyataiti yojyate /
atha vā bhedenārthavattvaṃ hetuḥ, uṅgitpadasya yajitaḥ phalāntaratvāt tataśca vidhipuruṣayoḥ pravṛtiviśeṣa iti vāccam /
nanu nāmadheyamapi ṛtuṃ viśiṃṣadarthavatpravṛttiviśeṣakaraṃ ca syāt /
naitadasti /
kutaḥ 
yadā tāvadvātunaiva lakṣaṇayā vidhiviṣayatvayogyatvādyāga viśe ṣaḥ pratipādyate tadā kimaparaṃ tatra nāma kariṣyati /
atha sāprathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
mānyamātramabhidhīyate tatastasyāniṣṭamevaitannāmetyasaṃbaddhaṃ siddhatvādeva ca viśeṣyasya na nāmadheyaṃ vidhāyiṣyataiti vacyati /
yadā ca kenāpi prakāraṇodbhidādīnāṃ viśeṣavacanatvaṃ tadā tadatyantāvinābhūtasāmānyavacanatvena yajeranarthakatvam/
lāghavaṃ ca vidherguvidhau bhaviṣyati /
yāgānuvādāt /
yadyevaṃ guṇāścitatvādidhiśakterna tarhi karma vidhīyate, tathā ca vihite karmaṇi kasya guṇo vidhīyataityānarthakyam /
ata /
prakṛtau jyotiṣṭoma iti /
nanu guṇavidhipace jyotiṣṭomenetyasyāpi tatparatvādavihitameva karma gatyabhāvādidamekaṃ karmavidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati /
tayāvṛtte ca vidhāyake ca guṇasya vidhātumaśakyatvād jyotiṣṭomapadamevaikaṃ nāmadheyam /
athavā tadekaṃ guṇaviśiṣṭaṃ karmavidhānamitarāṇi karmānuvādena guṇavidhānāni /
nanvevaṃ sati sarvā ekāhāhīnasatracodanā jyotiṣṭomasyaiva guṇavidhidvāreṇa prakaraṇādanatiriteti karmāntarābhāvānna jyotiṣṭomaḥ kasya citprakṛtiriti ta cchabdena nābhidhātavyaḥ /
sidvāntābhiprāyeṇāti ke cit /
athavā prakriyataiti prakṛtiḥ, prakṛte jyotiṣṭoma ityarthaḥ /
atha vā athaiṣa jyotirityevamādīnāṃ karaṇavibhaktyākhyāta saṃsparśābhāvādguṇavidhitvānupapattere kāntena bhedakatayā karmanāmatvaṃ tadapecayā ca jyotiṣṭomaḥ prakṛtiḥ /
nanūtpattivākya śiṣṭena somena jyotiṣṭomena vāvarodhājjyotiṣṭome guṇāntara vidhānamayuktam /
kāmyatvādudbhidādayo bādhakā bhaviṣyanti /
nitye prayoga ca pūrvaguṇasyārthavattā /
atha vā viśiṣṭavihitamapi karma svarūpamātraṃ niṣkṛṣya guṇāntare vihitaṃ naiautpattikādviśiṣyate /
anyathā ga tyasaṃbhavādikalpa iti manyate 
phalaṃ prati tāvadvidhīyamāne parapadasaṃbandha vidhānaṃ vyavahitakalpanā dhātoḥ pārārthyamai/tpattikasomabādhaḥ /
anadanīyana ca khanitrādinā 'tyantāprasiddhena yāga iti doṣāstathā yāgaṃ prati guṇavidhau phalapadānarthakyam /
sārvakāmyaprāpta jyotiṣṭomaviśeṣaṇatve vākyabhedaḥ /
pratyayavyāpāraviprakṛṣṭatā dhātupārārthyānadanīyayāgasomabādhavikalpāścātyantāyuktāḥ /
tathā viśiṣṭa vidhā sarvapārārghya maneka vidhiśaktikalpanā /
matvarthalakṣaṇāgamyamānasāmānādhikaraṇyatyāgo 'nadanīyayāgaśceti doṣāḥ /
tasmānna guṇavidhistadarśayati /
itarathā śrutirudbhidādīn vacyati tadvato lāyet /
vayantī jāyediti vā granthaḥ /
prātipadika sāmarthya mukkā vibhaktisaṃbandhādaṇyetadevāvagamyataiti darśayati /
yāgena kuryādityādinā /
kiṃ ca 
yatkaraṇābhidhāyinyā tṛtīyayetyevamādiṣu kārakāṇāṃ vibhatyarthatvābhyupagamātkathaṃ karaṇavācino hi prātipadikādityuccate /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
karaṇāśrayavācino hītyabhiprāyaḥ /
atha vā karaṇaśabdo yādṛśamarthaṃ bravīti tādṛśasya prātipadikaṃ vācakameva /
kṛdantena hi kāraka viśiṣṭaṃ dravyamevocyate na vibhaktivaniṣkṛṭā śaktiḥ /
tathā ca karaṇaṃ karaṇena karaṇāyeti ca kārakāntarayogo dṛśyate /
anyathā hi vibhaktyabhihitenaivai kena kāra keṇa vaśīkārānna dravyaṃ kārakāntarayogaṃ pratipadyeta /
śaktestu śaktyantaraṃ nāstyeva /
tasmācchaktyupasarjanadravyavacanatvāt kṛdantānāmupapannaṃ karaṇaśabdārthavācitvaṃ prātipadikasya /
tenaitaduktaṃ bhavati /
yadasmin vākye karaṇaṃ tadācinaḥ prātipadikāttṛtīyayotpattavyaṃ yāgaścātra phalabhāvanāyāḥ karaṇaṃ na dravyamiti vakṣyati /
taca yadyudvitpadaṃ yāgavacanamevaṃ tṛtīyāntaṃ sadekavākyatāṃ yātvarthāntaravacanatve  tvasaṃbaddhaṃ syāt /
nanu ca 
yathaiva brohibhiryajeta somena yajetetyādīnāṃ karaṇabhūtayā gaikavākyatve sati tṛtīyāntatvaṃ vaiyadhikaraṇyepyavirudvamevamicāpīti /
chaṭha iti /
cirantanataḍāgoda kācchādita caritadravyamucca/
yathā tadutmāryamāṇamapi svacchandataḥ punaḥpunarudakaṃ chādayatye vaṃ yonyopi svacchandavyavacāraḥ sa chaṭha iti prasiddhaḥ /
taducyate 
śrīhyādayo hyatyantarūḍhāste svārthamaparityajantaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyamapratipadyamānā gatyantarābhāvādguṇaviṣayo vijñāyante /
ye punarudbhidādayo yaugikāsteṣāṃ yenaiva prakāreṇa yatnena dravyavacanatvaṃ tenaiva karmavacanatvamapyupapadyataiti pratyaśaprasidvānudāsīnāyāmanu mānenāpyajñānasaṃśayavyudāsa karaṇaṃ na duṣyati /
sarvaśabdārthāvadhāraṇe hyayamabhyupāyo, yatprasiddha sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ nāma /
pradhānaṃ ca karaṇatvaṃ yāge labdhātmakaṃ śaknoti prātipadikamātmaviṣayamāpādayitum /
kiṃ ca 
tvatpate hyavaśyaṃ kā cidvibhaktyarthepi pratyayasya vidhiśaktiḥ kalpyā syāt /
tasmādavayavadvāreṇāsti karmaṇyapi prasiddhiḥ /
jyotiṣṭomāderapi svaphalodbhedanakāritvādetannāmaprasaṅga iti ce t /
na /
sāmānādhikaraṇyāvadhārita viṣaya viśeṣasyāvayavāncākhyānāt/
na cāsya jyotiṣṭomādibhiḥ samabhivyāhārosti /
atha vārthāpattivaśenaita dviśeṣaviṣayamevodbhedanaṃ nimittaṃ, na cānyatra tadastīti vyavasthā /
yathā sāsnādimadgatagamana viśeṣa nimittatvaṃ vidhāyiṣyataiti /
saṃjñāsaṃjñisaṃbandha rūpeṇa vṛdvirā daijityādivadavidhānaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyāvayavaprasidvibhyāṃ tatmiddheḥ /
nanu nāmaprathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
dheyārtho na vidhīyate tadadhīnatvādyāgaviśeṣasiddheḥ /
iha hi yadyapi saṃjñāsaṃjñisāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ nāsti tathāpyātmarūpavyavacchinamevārthaṃ saṃjñā gamayatīti viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvānna bhidyate /
nanvevaṃ śabdasvarūpābhidhānaṃ prasajyeta /
pratyakṣāvagatasvarūpaviśiṣṭārthābhidhānādaprasaṅgaḥ /
sarvatra hyagṛhītaviśeṣaṇā viśiṣṭabudvirna dṛṣṭā, na tvanabhihita viśeṣaṇā /
na caitāvatā śabdasvarūpāropaprasaṅgaḥ /
tadanurodhena vidyamānātha bhaviśeṣodvaraṇādityuktaṃ prāk /
nāmnaiva caivamādīnāṃ prakṛtito bhado'nyathā hi tadanavacchinno yajirguṇaphancādyarthaṃ punaḥ śrutiḥ prakṛtigāmitvānnaiva karma bhindyāt /
atha vā sarvanāmadheyeṣu kiṃ cidarthagatamapi viśeṣaṇamastītyaruṇaika cāyanyādivadeva viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatā /
na ca yajyuccāraṇamantareṇāsya yāgaviśeṣanāmatvamiti na sāmānya syānarthakatvam /
parasparasaṃnidhānena hi nāmāpi yāgaviṣayaṃ yāgopyetadavacchinno na sāmānyamātraṃ prakṛto veti labhyate /
tasmādubhayorarthavattā vi śiṣṭabhāvanā vidhānā ccobhayo rapi vidhānamiti nānuvādatvam/evaṃ ca sati na nāmatvaṃ vidhitvamātrapratiyogīti ye pūrvapa vidhyantarbhāvaṃ siddhānteta vidhyarthavādamantrātirekaṃ nāmnāṃ varṇayanti teṣāmayuktameva /
viśeṣa  vyavahārāṅgabhāvācca nāpravṛttivi śeṣakaratā /
nātvigvaraṇādiṣvanenācaṃ yacyaiti laghurākhyānopāyaḥ syāt /
darśapūrṇamāsāvārapsyamānaḥ sa me darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti guṇopabandho darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāma iti ca phalopabandho 'nyathā na syāt /
tasmānnāmadheyānyevaṃjātīyakānīti siddham 
utpattau nāmadheyaṃ vā guṇo vā 'pyavadhāritaḥ /
vyavahārāṅgatāṃ yāti saivodāharaṇakṣamā 
citratvalītvayogo hi prāṇijātau svabhāvataḥ /
tenaite prāṇiyāgāṅgaṃ prakṛtiṃ daiśamāśrite vārtika /
sarvatrākhyāta saṃbaddhe śrayamāṇe padāntare /
vidhiśaktyupasaṃkrānte syāddhātoranuvādatā /
yāva dyāvadvidheyāntaramupādīyate tāvattāvatpūrvatrānekaśaktikalpanābhayādanuvādatvākāṅkṣā bhavatyagatyā tu tatrāpi vidhyaṅgīkaraṇam /
asti cātra strītvacitratvabhāgagnīṣomīyayāga ityanūdyate /
gaṇe phalakapanāyāṃ yajate ravivakṣeti kimarthaṃ guṇavidhimvapakṣa eva sannirākriyate /
siddhāntagrantho'yaṃ pramādānikhita iti ke cit /
apare tvāhaḥ /
phalasaṃbandhe kila pradhānatvādguṇoktivighātaḥ syāditi /
tadayuktam /
sarvathā nāmadheyapratipakṣo guvidhiḥ sa ca phalasaṃbandhe 'pyanapagataḥ /
tathā ca vakṣyati sthita e tasminnadhikaraṇe guṇavidhirnāmadheyamiti vicāra iti /
phalasaṃbandhe hokāntena yāgasāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvādguṇa vidhireva syāditi, tenaivaṃ vācyam /
iddatu trayaḥ pakṣāḥ pratibhānti /
guṇavidhiḥ phale yāge vā nāmadheyaṃ vetyekaikasya ca dayaṃdayaṃ nirākartavyam /
tatra pūrvapakṣasthaeva durbalataratvāttṛtīyaṃ pakṣaṃ nirākaroti /
dhātupārārthyaprasaṅgāditi /
ataśca vīhibhiryajenetivadyāge guṇavi dhānam/
karaṇabhūtasyāpi ca yāgasyotpattivākyāvagata karavāthakṣipta sādhyāṃśānuvādena guṇe vidhīyamāne na matvarthalakṣaṇā /
guṇavādyeva vānabhibhavasamarthaṃ yāge guṇavidhānamāśrayati /
phale guṇavidhikalpanāyāṃ pūrvādhikaraṇoktadoṣaprasaṅgāditi /
tathā pa śvadaśānyājyānītyatrāstirbhavantipara iti sattopakalpanaṃ prayogavacanācca vidhiḥ /
nanu ca pañcadaśāni saptadaśānīti caivarūpaḥ śabdo na saṃkhyāmātravācī stome ḍavidhiḥ pañcadaśādyartha iti smaraṇāt /
nahi stoma iti stotrīyasaṃkhyāto 'nyā vidhīyate /
A prathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
naṣa doṣaḥ /
stotrasādhanamātraparicchedena stutimānātmakastomasiddheḥ sadṛśamṛkaparicchede ghṛtaparicchede ca stutimānanimittastomavācitvam /
na cātra matvarthalakṣaṇā /
kutaḥ 
arthādane kamapyarthaṃ vidhāpayati bhāvanā/
viśeṣaṇa vidhistvanyanna gṛhṇāti viśeṣaṇam 
utpattiva/kyavijñātaṃ karma sarvaṃ hyanūdyate / na cāśritaguṇe śakyaṃ tadvirodhi guṇāntaram 
prathamaṃ hi svavākyasthairguṇaiḥ saṃbadhyate kriyā /
vākyāntaragataiḥ paścānna śuddā sā hyavāpyate 
puruṣārtho hi sarveṇa kharasādeva kāmyate /
tatsādhanatadaṅgeṣu pravṛtti prārthanāhate 
nāvāntarakriyāyogāte vākyopakalpitāta/
guṇadravye kathaṃbhāvairgṛhṇanti prakṛtāḥ kriyāḥ 
guṇavākyopapattyarthaṃ samabhivyāhatena ca /
anvākhyānārthavādācca nāmadheyatvamāśritam 
prathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
tatprakhyaṃ cānyaśāstram 
nanu sarvatra dviprakārameva nāmapadaṃ sāṃvijñāyika yaugikaṃ cobhayamapi cādhikaraṇaiyena pratipāditaṃ, kimidānīmavaśiṣyate yena punarvicāryate /
uccate /
yaugikānāmeva matvarthalāṇāparihāreṇātra cintā, uttarādhikaraṇe tu sāṃvijñāyikānāṃ vākyabhedāsaṃbhavāt /
tatrāgnaye chotrama sminniti siddhānte'pyabhyupagamādanyasamāsārthānupalabdheśvāntarṇotamatvarthe/
bahuvrīhira khedena guṇaṃ vidhatte taeva ca prasiddhyādayo cetavaḥ satyāmapi ca sāyaṃ home 'gniprāptau tadarjaṃ prātarhe/me homamātrānuvādādā sarvadarvihomedhvavicitadevatākeṣu vidhāprati vākyasāmarthyāt /
tathā ''ghāyaṃtaityāghāra iti vāraṇasamarthaṃ dravyamājyapayaḥprabhṛtyabhidhīyate /
tacca dvitīyānirdeśāt cāraṇa kriyā saṃskāryatvenādhyavasoyamānamanupayujyamāna saṃskārānupapatteḥ prayojanamapekṣate /
dharmamātraṃ cāsya śaraṇaṃ śabdārtha mātrāpavargitvānnāśeṣacāraṇaṃ karoti /
tatvāritaikadeśena kiṃ kartavyamityastyapeśā lokepi ca dravadravyāṇāṃ ka citpānādāvupayocyamāṇānāmīṣatścāraṇa saṃskāraṃ kurvanti /
tenābhiṣavayuktapūtokavadbhakṣaṇayuktaphala camamavacca saṃskāyeṃ dravyaṃ karmamātrābhilāṣi /
prakaraṇavaśena darśapūrṇamāsa pradhānānyupasarpati /
tatrāpi cāgneyādīnāṃ vicitadravyakatvādupagyājaḥ kevalaḥ sākāṅkṣa iti tādarthaṃ pratipadyate /
āha ca 
athavā yatkaronīti pratyayārthamācaṃ sākāṅkṣatvādevopāṃśatantravārtika /
yājabhāvanāmanūdyāghāradravye vākyena vidhīyamāne tatmādhyatvādeva dhātvarthaḥ prāpto 'nudyate /
śrāvaprāptyaiva vā tasya kṣaraṇātmakatve vijñāte kṣaraṇamamarthamātrapayaḥprabhṛtividhiṃ manyate /
na ca dhātvathāṃdeva siddhenamnā prayojanam /
na ca saṃskārakarmāṇi ka ci nnāmavanti dṛśyante /
śrutyaiva guṇo vidhīyataiti dvitīyāśrutyaiva saṃskāryatvādavagyaṃ ka cidasya guṇatvamityavagamābhiprāyam /
atrocyate 
atra vadāmaḥ 
yadā tvadevate home devatāvidhirucyate /
dravyaṃ copāṃśuyājamya tadā tatprakhyatā katham 
vidhiśvedagnihotraṃ syāttato'mya viṣayaiṣiṇaḥ /
niveśaḥ prakṛte vā syādyukteraprakṛte 'pi vā 
anū cāpi dhātvarthaṃ guṇaḥ sarvo vidhīyate /
na cānuvādaḥ prakṛtātkarmaṇo prakṛtaṃ cedanūdyāyaṃ guṇo home vidhīyate /
tatra tatprakhyatā'nyatra na vidhistatparigrahāt 
dūrasthasyānuvādaśca vyavadhānānna yujyate /
tasya buddhāvanārohātkauṇḍapāyinahomavat 
na caturthīsamāsasya lakṣaṇaṃ cātra vidyate /
na ca tena vinā śakyā devatāvidhikalpanā 
vidhātavyaśca saṃbandho bhavetparapadārthayoḥ /
prātame 'pi tenaiṣa vahinaiva vidhīyate 
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca sādhyāṃśeneca karmaṇaḥ /
vispaṣṭaṃ dravyanāmatvaṃ na cāghārasya gamyate tadvyapadeśaṃ ca 
athaiṣa jyotirityādivarjamudāharaṇam /
teṣāṃ tṛtīyā nirde śābhāvād guṇavidhitvānupapatteḥ /
te 'pi ca vākyāntareṣu yadā tṛtīyānirdeśaṃ pratipadyante tadā vicāryante /
atha vā prathamānirde śena dravyamapi prastutya paścāttatmādhyopanyāsaḥ saṃbhavatītyete 'pi udāharaṇameva /
tatra taireva prasiḍyādibhirguṇavidhiḥ /
na cātra karmaṇi pravṛttinimittaṃ kiṃ cidasti /
vatyarthopādānena karmaṇi pravṛttau cātyantaviprakṛṣṭā gauṇatā syāt /
tatra varaṃ matvarthalanathā/
sādhanaṃ hi pratīta matyanta vinābhāvātvasādhyāṃ kriyāmakleśena pratipādayati vinaiva matublopena /
kiṃ ca 
guṇavidhipakṣe hi svārthāparityāgenaiva śyenapadaṃ taddantamuttarakālaṃ laśśayati /
ātmoccāraṇakāle tu svārthameva viniyuko /
bhavatastu yenārthānapayogādādita eva sāhagyavivaścayā padaṃ pravṛttamityupagamāt śrutibādhaprasaṅgaḥ /
taducyate 
śyenādivākyeṣu hi yathā vai śyeno nipatyādattaevamayamapītyupagamānna stutirdṛśyate /
tayā ca vidhīyamānasya bhavitavyam /
guṇavidhāne ca prayenadravyaṃ vidhīyataiti tadeva stotavyam /
na ca tasyātmanaivopamānaṃ yuktam /
athocyetānanyattvena sutarāṃ stutirbhavati, ananya saṃbhavicaritatvāt /
tathā 
nāmadheye guṇaśruteḥ syādvidhānamiti cet 
tantra saṃbandhenākhyāta padasyadhātvarthaḥ phalaṃ prati karaṇaṃ guṇaṃ ca prati sādhyo bhavanna virodayate /
tenodbhidā yāgaṃ yāgena ca paśṭhan bhāvayediti yugapadvidhivyāpārādvinaiva matvarthacakṣaṇayā saṃbandhasiddhiḥ /
tathājyādipadasya tantreṇa stotrasaṃkhyādiyogaḥ /
tasmātmarvatra tvatparikalpite nāmadheye guṇaśruteḥ prasiddhyādibhirgu pratyayānapagamāttadvidhānameva bhavatvalaṃ nāmadheyatveneti yathāsaṃbhavaṃ sarvādhikaraṇākṣepeṇedamārabhyate /
tatredamapi vākyaṃ śuddhaṃ bhaviṣyatīti vājapeyopanyāsaḥ /
sarvāṇyeva tvihodāirtavyāni /
ha ca 
tulyatvāt kriyayorna 
aikaśabdye parārthavat 
tantratvamaikarūpyeṇa bhavettunyopakārataḥ /
upakārānyathātve tu bhavatyāvṛttilakṣaṇam 
na cedanyena śiṣṭāḥ syuryāgāḥ śabdena kena cit /
te guṇā copadiśyeran vidhinā hyavibhāgataḥ 
na dravyasya svarūpeṇa mantrākāṅkṣā 'vakalpate /
na cānyavācinā tasya saṃbandhaḥ saṃpratīyate 
yadi hi prathamaṃ yāgatvamavadhāyata tato devatākāṅkṣāyāṃ satya devatāvācino mantrāḥ saṃbadhyeran, na tu tadbhavatiśabdenoktam /
na ca yāgasaṃbandhātprāk puroḍāmādīnāṃ viṣvamavadhāryate /
saṃbandhiśabdo hyayaṃ na dravyasvarūpaprayuktaḥ /
tadeva hi dravyamayāgasaṃbaddhaṃ payaḥprabhṛti na loke haviḥ śabdavācyaṃ bhavati /
etena catu ravattacodanākalpitakarmanāmatvaṃ pratyuktam /
āghārādiṣu tu kriyātmakatvānmantrākāṅkṣāyāṃ vacanaviniyogavaśācca bhavati māntravarṇikadevatākalpanā /
sarvajaghanyaścāyaṃ devatāvidhiḥ sarvajyeṣṭhe tadvitadevatāvidhau saṃbhavati kimityāśrīyate /
anyathātantravārtika /
nupapattimūlaścāsau na ca taddhite saṃbhavatyanyathānupapattiḥ /
tasmādanenaiva kṛte dravyadevatāsaṃvandhe 'rthavādapuraḥsareṇa bhavatiśabdena vihite viśeṣārthaṃ krameṇa mantrāmnānam /
agatyā cānekārthavidhiraṅgīkriyate/
vidhānārthe tadvitānte śabda iti vidhiprayojanatvābhiprāyeṇa /
sarvaṃ caitattasmādavibhaktaṃ gamyate /
devatā tāvatprātipadikenoktā tadviśiṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ tadvitena saṃbandho 'pi tatraivārthagṛhītastatmāmānādhikaraṇyāccā śeṣātmīyopasarjanayuktamaṣṭāka pālapadaṃ viśeṣaṇatvena tatraivāntargatam /
dravyasya cāgneyatvena bhavanamabhāvyamānasya na siyatīti tadākṣiptā bhāvanāpi tatraiva /
na ca yāgena vināgneyatvaṃ bhāvayituṃ śakyamiti puruṣavyāpāra viśeṣopi yāgastadantargataḥ /
tataśca tadvitāntapadopāttavidhinā sarvamanyadarthādātipyamāṇaṃ na vākyaṃ bhinatti /
bhāvanāvidhipūrvaka ca sarvatra dhātvarthakārakavidhirbhavatītyaśrayamāṇāpi saiva tāvadiśiṣṭā vidhīyate /
tato viśeṣaṇānyathānupapattyā sarvasaṃsargātmakatvācca tāmeva saṃvandhaśabdenābhidhatte, na tvavyāpārātmakatvād dravyadevatāsaṃbandhaḥ śakyate vidhātum /
avibhāgādityarthāścepahetuḥ /
na cedanyenetyanyathānupapattiśaraṇābhidhānam 
puroḍāśādibhirloke vyavahāro na dṛśyate /
tasmādyapādivaḍedātteṣāṃ saṃskārahetutā 
ekadeśe'pi yo dṛṣṭaḥ śabdo jātinibandhanaḥ /
tadatyāgāna tasyāsti nimittāntarakalpanā /
yaeva laukikāḥ śabdāstaeva vaidikāstaevāmīṣāmarthā iti sthitatvānokaprasiddhipratīce vede yatraikadeśe 'pi jātinimittatā labhyate na tatra punarnimittāntaraśaktikalpanā saṃbhavati /
saṃskṛteṣvapi jāteranapagamāttannimittatātikramo na śakyo vaktumataśca śākhasthairapya virodhānna bādhaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
tena jātimete na vyabhicaranti /
vyabhicaranti tu saṃskārān avihitatvānokavyavahāravelāyāṃ saṃskārāṇāmabhāvāt 
yadi hi chedana vidhivelāyāṃ bandhanavidhau vā kaściaukiko 'tha labhyeta tataḥ kimevaṃ vyavasthitavacanavyaktiviparyayeṇa kalpyeta yaśchidyate sa nūnaṃ yūpa iti /
asti ca barddirādergatistasmādatulyatā 
va budhyante samudāyaprasiddhiṣu /
arthabhāgopasaṃhārāditarā viprakṛṣyate 
asatkhavayavārtheṣu yo 'nyatrārthe prayujyate /
tatrānanyagatitvena samudāyaḥ prasidhyati 
bhavetāṃ yadi vṛkṣeṣu vājikarṇo kathaṃ cana /
adṛṣṭāṃ samudāyasya kaḥ śakti jātu kalpayet 
tathā nirmanthye 
nirmanthye 'pi pūrvādhikaraṇavajjātisaṃskāranimittapaścāvaḍāvyānantareṇa yaugikatvaṃ sādhanīyam 
loke karmārthalacaṇamityaśabdārthenāpi vyavahārābhavedaciranirdagdhaghṛtapratītiḥ /
sarvaghṛtānāṃ ca navanītavikāratvātpunaḥ śrutera ciranirdagdhanavanītārthatā syāt /
iha tu śabdapramāṇake 'nyakriyājanitanivṛttamātracaritārtho nirmanthyaśabdaścirāciraviśeṣopādānāsamarthaḥ kathamacira nirmathitaviṣayaḥ kalapyate /
nacatrāciratvamapi yoge 'ntargataṃ, kriyāyogamātra nimittatvāt /
tasmādasadetat /
naiṣa doṣaḥ 
yathaiva lohitoṣṇīṣādividhiṣu viśeṣyāṇāṃ prāptatvāhiśeṣaṇaparatvameva mihāpi viśeṣyānuvādana viśeṣaṇabhūtā kriyaiva pākāṅgatvena vidhīyate /
aṅgānāṃ ca pradhānenaikadeśakāla kartṛtvaṃ va cyate /
tenāciranirmathitenādūra nirmathitenānanya kartṛ nirmathitenetantravārtika /
ti vaktavye pradarśanārthamaciragrahaṇam 
na samastānuvādasya kiṃ cidasti prayojanam /
viśvedevā na ca prāptāḥ pratyekaṃ saṃhateṣu vā 
prakṛtatvāviśeṣe 'pi yatra prāptirna vidyate /
vidhestatropasaṃhārānna vairūpyaṃ bhaviṣyati 
guṇāntarāvaruddhatvānnāvakāśo guṇo 'paraḥ /
vikalpo 'pi na vaiṣamyāttasmānnāmaiva yujyate 
mithaścānarthasaṃbandhaḥ 
vaiśvadevamupādāya devatā nopadiśyate /
saha vidhyanuvāda/
hi naikaḥ śabdaḥ samaśnute 
parārthatvād guṇānām 
pūrveṇaikasūtramapi sambhavati /
mithaḥ saha pradāne kriyamāṇe triṃśatsaṃpattyabhāvāda nartha sambandhaḥ syāt /
kutaḥ 
tena sakṛttyāgaḥ karttavya iti  satyāṃ sahapradānaśaktau nāvattiryuktā ktā /
saṃpratipannadevatātvācca sahapradānamaviruddhaṃ śakyaṃ ka prathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
rtu' tataśca triṃśattvavirodhaḥ /
triṃśatpūraṇaṃ ca keṣāṃ cidevaṃ, nava prayājāḥ, navānuyājāḥ, dvāvāghārau, dvāvājyabhāgau, aṣṭau pradhānājataya iti /
apareṣāṃ tu sviṣṭakṛdājinejyāgrahaṇādāghārau na gaṇitau/
sarvathā tu pradhānācutibhedadarśanasiddhiḥ 
pūrvajñātārthavācitve nāmadheyārthavādane /
aprāptatvādicaite syurvaiśvadevavikalpavat 
yadyapyarthātmanāstyeva mahāsaṃkhyāsvavāntarā/
aparicchedakatvāttu nāsau karmaviśeṣaṇam 
guṇasya tu vidhānārthe 'taguṇāḥ prayoge syuranarthakā nahi taṃ pratyarthaprathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
vattāsti 
prakṛtāprakṛte yāge tathā dravyepi vā guṇaḥ /
dravyaṃ guṇavadevaṃ ca na kathaṃ cidvidhīyate 
vaiśvānarapadaṃ nāpi yāgāyātrānuṣajyate /
vibhaktyantarayogitvānna carte 'smādanarthakam 
taccheṣo nopapadyataiti ced avibhāgādvidhānārthe stuyarthenopapadyeran  
prathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
aṣṭatvādyavidhānatvārtheyaṃ tatprarocanā /
tasmādavayavadāraṃ dvādaśatvaṃ prarocyate 
sarvatra hyalpairbahubhirvākṣaraiḥ stutayo dṛśyante, śroḍhaprakārānekatvācca va citkāścidarthaṃvatyo bhavanti /
yathaiva keṣāṃ cihnidhyaddeśamātreṇa pravṛttau siddhyantyāmanyārthā stutirāśrīyate tathaivālpastutyupapanne'pi kārye mahāstutyāśrayaṇamiti 
yaduktaṃ dvādaśatvāvarodhāda narthaka maṣṭatvādividhānaṃ stavanaṃ ceti/
tannānarthakam /
nityaṃ hi dvādaśakapālatā /
yastu guṇaphalāni bramharvacasādīni prārthayate tasyāṣṭatvādīni dvādaśatvopamardaina nivecyante /
tathā hi 
puruṣārthasiddhyartho hi sarvaḥ prayāsa iti tatpratyāsannaṃ vastu balīyo bhavati /
dūre ca dvādaśatvaṃ puruṣārthasya tatmādhanayāgadravyasaṃskārārthakapālaparicchedād aṣṭatvādayastu tadāśritāḥ santaḥ sākṣād bramhavarcasādi sādhayantīti pratyāsatterbalīyāṃso bhavanti tasmādarthavanta iti /
nanu ca 
tatra ke cidāhuḥ /
audumbara rādhikaraṇapūrvapaścanyāyenātra pratyavasthānamiti tanna yuktam /
tatraiva dattottaratvāt /
atoyamabhiprāyaḥ /
pūta eva sa tejasvītyādinā phalamucyate /
gāyavyaivaitamityādistateḥ prātyātmiko vidhiḥ /
yadaṣṭākapāla ityādibhiḥ sārthavādakaḥ pratyekaṃ vihitānāṃ yathāsaṃkhyena pūta evetyādibhiḥ phalasaṃbandhaḥ kriyate 
patre jāte dvādaśakapāla miti yadevopakrāntaṃ tadevāṣṭatvādīnāmante yaddādaśakapālo bhavatīti yasmin jāte etāmiti copasaṃdriyamāṇaṃ paśyāmaḥ /
tāvati ca nāṣṭatvādayaḥ pṛthag bhavituṃ prathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
labhante tadekavākyatā ca na stutyā vinopapadyate /
arthāntaraparatāyāmānarthakyāt /
yadi hi kartṛsaṃbandhīnyetāni bhaveyustatastasya kāraṇāni prayojakāni syuḥ /
vaiśvānarasavandhīni tvetāni /
tasmādguṇārthonyāsaṃbhavāditi stutyarthe/
vidhīyate /
pūta eva sa ityevamādīnāṃ ca tacchabdayuktānāṃ yasmin jātaityanenāpekṣitatvā na pūrvaiḥ saha phanatvena saṃbandhaḥ /
na cātrānupayogo yena bajādācchidya nīyeran /
na cāṭatvādi bramhavarcasādīnāme bhirbhāgena saṃbandhaḥ/
yatra tu vibhāgo gāyavyaivenamityādau tatra stutitvamabhyupagatameva /
ato yā nāma pūta ityevamādīnāṃ phalakarūpanā sā yāgameva prati nāṣṭatvādīn /
prathamopanipāte tu yā gasyāpi stutireva /
evaṃ kāmakārarahitatvena phalavidhyasarūpatvāt /
etaireva svayamāne yadaṣṭākapāla ityādīnāmupapattyarthatā nasmānna guṇavidhaya iti siddham 
abhidheyāvinābhūte pravṛttirlakṣaṇeṣyate /
lacyamāṇaguṇairyogādṛtteriṣṭā tu gauṇatā 
vanhitvalakṣitādarthādyatyaiṅgalyādi gamyate /
tena māṇavake buddhiḥ sādṛṇyādupajāyate 
na tāvatkāryayogitva me kasyāpyupapadyate /
virodhādyajamānasya prastarādaracodanā pitaprasahyakāritvādyanekadharmapratyayāddevadattapratyaya iti pūrvaiva śaktirnimittamiti na saṃśayahetutvena vyavahārocchedakāraṇaṃ prasiddhahānāprasiddhakalpanamāśrayaṇīyam /
anyeṣāṃ tu darśanaṃ sarvaeva hi siṃhādiśabdā jātiguṇakriyāsamudāyavācinaḥ samastārthāsambhave devadattādiṣu katipayaguṇakriyāyogādupacaryantaiti /
tatrābhidhīyate 
bhavati tu jātimātre dṛṣṭe sarvakriyā guṇapratyastamaye 'pi pra yogaḥ /
pratyayaśca mukhyātmanaiva na devadattādiṣviva siṃhaśavdādupacaritaḥ /
sāmānyavācitā cākṛtyadhikaraṇasiddhā bādhyate / tantravārtike /
kriyāguṇānāṃ cānantyānna śakyaḥ prativyakti sambandho 'nubhavitum 
na cāsāmānyāt sāmānyaṃ śakyate kalpayituṃ jātyantare 'pi va citkāsāṃ citmadbhāvāt 
na hyanabhihitaṃ siṃhatvaṃ guṇakriyāṇāṃ vyavacchedakaraṃ bhavati apratīteḥ/
abhihitaṃ cettu pratyayādevāśeṣaguṇakriyāvagamādabhi dhānaśaktyanavasāya iti samudāyavācināmekadeśeṣu na gauṇatvasambhavaḥ /
kaścitpunarāha samāropitatadbhāvo gauṇa iti /
tasyaitamataṃ na kathaṃ cana paraśabdastayā jātyā khanibandhanabhūtayā vi nātyantāna bhidheya kriyāguṇamātradvāreṇānyatra varttitumarhati /
na ca siṃhaśabdenā pravarttamānena siṃho devadatta iti sāmānādhikaraṇyaprayogo ghaṭate /
kathaṃ tarhi 
siṃdādi sadṛśa kriyāguṇadarśanena hi devadattādayaḥ sāmayaparikalpanayā sārūpyamāpadyante /
tataśca svārthaeva śabdaḥ prayujyate na caitāvatā mukhyaprasaṅgo 'rthasyādhyāropitatvāt /
yatra tu sa evārtho na samāropyate tatra mukhya ityadoṣaḥ /
tatredamucyate naitatkalpanāyā aśakyatvāt /
tathā hi 
yadā tāvaḍbhāntyā mṛgatṛṣṇāyāṃ toyamadhyāropya śabdaṃ prayaṅkte, tadobhayoḥ mukhyārthādhyavasānarūpeṇa toyapratītarbhrānti mukhyatvam /
athāpi vaktā vivekī sannitaravacanārthaṃ prayukta, śrotā ca na viviṅakta, tadāpye kasya vivekenādhyāropābhāvāditarasya a ntyādhyavamānānnaikamapi prati gauṇatvopapattiḥ /
yadā tu dvāvaṣyabhrāntau tadobhayoḥ sādṛśyādinimittānta tavatyarthādhyavasānādāropābhāvaḥ /
tathā hi 
yathaitra hyasadṛśānāmarthānāṃ tiktamadhurādīnāṃ na kathaṃ cidapi pratītyabhāvātparaparādhyāropaṇa, mevaṃ sahaśanāmapi vivekajñānaṃ nopapadyate /
na hyarthādhyavasānādanyādṛśaṃ nāmajñānaṃ vyavahārāṅgaṃ bhavatīti /
kiṃ ca 
na cārtharahitā buddhirātmākāramātramanubhavantī jāyate ityuktaṃ śūnyavāde /
api ca 
sarvathā tāvadayaṃ gauṇamukhyavibhāgaḥ śrotṛṇāmarthaviśeṣāvadhāraṇe vyāpriyate te ca padavelāyāmanadhyāropita svārthavṛtyeva siṃhādipadamadhyavasāya devadattādipadasāmānādhikaraṇyā nyathānupapatyā gauṇatāṃ kalpayanti tatra caiṣāṃ svayamanāropyaiva siṃhatvaṃ tantravārtike /
tatmādṛśyādipratītirbhavati /
sā ca kiṃ śabdādathārthādityanvicchatāmanvayavyatirekābhyāmākṛtyadhikaraṇanyāye nārthāditi nistrayo jāyate /
katham 
yadā ca śrotṛṇāṃ svayamadhyāropābhāvaḥ, tadā vaktaryyapi naivaiṣāmevaṃ kalpanā bhavati, yathā nūnamanena siṃhatvamadhyāropitamiti/
kathaṃ tarhi siṃhatvā vinābhūtāne kakriyā guṇasamudāyonena vivakṣitaḥ yatnagauravabhayānna khairabhidhānairbravīti /
na cāsya samastasya kiṃ cidekaṃ vācakaṃ padamasti tenāvinābhāvitayā kathaṃ nu siṃhatvāttatpratītirbhavediti tattāvadabhidhīyate yataḥ /
sthitiyā śabdaśaktyā puṃsāṃ vyavahāro na tadaśena śaktyantaropajana iti /
kiṃ ca 
tasmādguṇapravṛttiprayojano gauṇa ityeva lakṣaṇaṃ nyāyyaṃ nānyathā /
nanvevaṃ sati khapuṣpādīnāṃ svārthāvinābhūtaguṇābhāvāṅga prayo gābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ, sāṃkhyādikalpitapradhānādiniṣedhe ca bauddhāde vinādhyāropeṇa prayogāsambhavo 'nabhyupagate hi pratiṣedhānarthakyamabhyupagate tavirodhaḥ syādadhyāropitaniṣedhe tvadoṣa iti /
a cābhidhīyate /
tavaivāyaṃ doṣaḥ /
kutaḥ /
adhyastekhapuṣpatvamasatkathamavastuni /
prajñātaguṇasattākamadhyaropyeta vā na vā 
anyatra jñātasadbhāvaḥ padārthonyatra vāyaṃte /
na tvekacaiva sadrūpamamadrūpaṃ ca gamyate 
yāṃ niṣedhāḥ kriyāmāharna yātītyevamādayaḥ /
tiṣṭhatītyādibhiḥ saiva vasturūpā pratīyate 
paramāṇu śarīrādikāraṇātmā divādibhiḥ /
tato'nyāhaka pradhānātmarūpaṃ nāstīti varṇyate 
jātiḥ /
tatrāgneyādiśabdānāṃ brāhmaṇādiṣu mukhatvameva yena kena cisambandhena tadvitotpādān /
devatāsambandha eva vāsti na hi yadeva tyajyate tasyaiva kevalaṃ devatāsambandhaḥ, tyakturapi tenaiva sambandhena saiva devatā bhavati /
yathā ca vakṣyati 'bhavati puruṣasyāpi yaṣṭuḥ sā devate'ti /
tasmādanuḍhāharaṇatvam /
ato yatrāgnivai brāhmaṇa ityādiprayogāstadudāharttavyam /
agnirhi pratīto mukhaprabhavatvasāmānyena brāhmaṇādīnupasthāpayati /
jātiriti cātra ja nmopāḍhānaṃ vivakṣitaṃ yadyapi ca tathā vastu nāsti tathāpyarthavādāntare tathoktatvādidda tacchabdanimittatā pratipatsyate 
praśaṃsā /
nanu sarvvatra praśaṃsānimittatvaṃ guṇavādasyoktam /
satyaṃ, phannamanyatra guṇavādasya praśaṃsā, atra tu guṇasārūpyādivatpravṛttini mittam /
kathamiti cet 
na tāvanmahiṣādīnāṃ paśutvasvarūpābhāvaḥ śakyate vaktuṃ pratyaśca virodhā, ttatkāryapratiṣedhaḥ kalpyeta tadapi tatra tatra vacanavihitatvāt na śakyameva /
na ca vikalpo vaiṣamyāt /
kalpyo hyatra vi dhiritaratra kṛptaḥ stutyā vārthavattvānnāgatyā taḍhāśrayaṇam/
tulyaśca mukhyārthatyāgaḥ paśavo govā iti ca punarupādānamanarthaṃkaṃ na ca paśśutvaikārthasamavāyinaḥ kriyāguṇāḥ śakyāḥ pravivektum /
atha gavāśva samavāyino viśeṣāḥ pratiṣidhyeran evamapi mandaṃ phalam /
anyaśabdenaiva ca nāvānarthaḥ siddha ityanarthakam /
avaśyaṃ cottarapadena pratiṣedhyerthe prathamamupāttena tatrānuvarttitavyaṃ viṣayaracitapratiṣedhāsambhavāt /
na ca praśastatvādanyadupādoyamānamupayujyate /
śaknuvanti ca gavāśvādisambandhāttadūtaṃ prāśastya gamayitum /
yadyapyapraśastatvamapi śaknuvanti tathāpi prakramāpeśayā tadihānākāṅkṣitamiti prāśastyameva niṣidhyate /
tatpratiṣedhamānamapi ca naivopayikamiti tadvāreṇānyeṣāṃ praśastataratvaṃ ka dhyate /
etaduktaṃ bhavati /
gavāśvādonapekṣya naivānyasya prāśastya prathamādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
vidyataityevamanyagata praśaṃsānimittaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sā ceha prathamataramāśritetyananyaprayojanatayā paścādavagamyate /
anyatra punaruttarakālamevaiṣā bhavantī nimittatvenocyate 
prāpnuvantyapi vaktavyā punarevaṃvidhā kriyā /
dhvargyavasamākhyānaṃ tathā hi pratipadyate 
pratyakṣabrāhmaṇoktānāṃ madhyamā citirāśrayaḥ /
tadarthamapi sambandhaḥ kāryo mantropadhānayoḥ 
bhāṣyakāreṇa tu vidhau lacaṇāṃ pariharatānuvādatvamāśritam /
ekayā stuvataiti hyanuvākādyasyaivā sṛṣṭiciṅgatvādātmaparityāgenetaralacaṇārthatā syāt, tallacayitvā ca punarātmāpi pratipādanoya ityatigauravamupadhānastutyarthatvena punaranuvādatvādaduṣṭā lakṣaṇā 
āha ca yatra lakṣaṇamuddiśya lakṣye kāryyaṃ niyujyate /
tanmātragrahaṇaṃ tasminnupādāne iyorapi 
kiṃ punaratra saṃdehakāraṇaṃ vidhau sāmānyagrahaṇamiti ke cit /
tadayuktam /
tatra tāvanmātra nirṇayāt /
syādetat /
kathaṃ nirviśeṣaṃ sāmānyaṃ saṃbhavatīti, ghṛtavaditi vadāmaḥ /
tatrāpi ca navapurāṇagavyamāhiṣādisaṃdehastadava sthastena yathāca ghṛtamātra nirṇayādasaṃdeho viśeṣānabhidhānepi sarvaiḥ kāryasiddhirevamicāpi snehana samarthadravya mātragrahaṇādasaṃdehaḥ /
tasmādarthavāde ghṛtaśravaṇāt saṃ bhaya ityapare /
tathāpi na yukto, viśeṣapratipattyā nirṇītatvāt /
na hi gaiaurānīyatāṃ śukla ityatra kaiścitsaṃdihyate /
viṣama upanyāsaḥ /
katham 
yadi hyevaṃ bhavedaktāḥ śarkarā upadadhāti ghṛteneti /
tato naiva kiṃ cidvicārkhetātha tvacanavākyavadāpyevaṃ śrayeta gāmānaya śuklaḥ praśasta iti tato 'styeva saṃdehakāraṇamiti etadapyudācaraṇameva syāt /
ato 'nyatra sāmānyamanyatra ca viśeṣa ityetasmātsaṃdehaḥ /
ke ciñca saṃśayadarśanādeva vidhistutyorvā kyāntaratvamācakṣate 
vākyabhede punarekaṃ sāmānye parisamāptamanyadviśeṣaparamiti yuktaḥ saṃdeha /
'yattu vidhinā tvekavākyatvādi'ti tadaṅgapradhānavākyānāmiva paścātsaṃbandhasadbhāvābhiprāyeṇa 
stutīnāṃ vidhyadhīnatvādanuvādācca lakṣaṇā /
mukhyatvāttu vidhernāsāvavirodhācca kalpyate 
kāmaṃ vā so 'rthavādo'stu sāmānyastho ghṛte vidhiḥ /
prathamādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
vinā stutyā vidhānaṃ tu strecadravyāntare bhavet 
samāpyate vidhiḥ kaścitkadā cinnāprarocitaḥ /
ghṛte prarocanāṃ dṛṣṭvā vidhistatrānumīyate 
arthādvākalpanaika deśatvāt 
atha yatreti saṃndigdhe vākyaṃśeṣo na vidyate /
tatra sāmarthya siddhena vidhyaṃśenaiva nirṇayaḥ 
yathaiva pāṭhaḥ pratipattyupāyastathaiva sāmarthyamapi śrutīnām /
tenaiva caitā na samāmananti sahasrabhāgaṃ tu samāmaneyuḥ 
iti śrībhaṭṭakumārilaviracite mīmāṃsāvārttike prathamasyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ tantravārtika /
śrīmahāgaṇapataye namaḥ 
lakṣaṇārtho'tra tattvena bhedaḥ śabdetarādibhiḥ /
tamancapūrvabhedo 'pi prādhānyaṃ tatprasiddhaye 
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
śeṣaśeṣyādayaḥ sarve karmabheda nibandhanāḥ /
kārye jñāte 'dhikāraḥ syādupadeśetideśadhīḥ /
prāk tāvatpramāṇalakṣaṇāḍedārtha vicārātmakatvānna kasya ciṅgedalakṣaṇādeḥ prastāva ityattarakālamārambhaḥ /
tatrāpi śeṣaśeṣitvaṃ prayojakāprayojakatvaṃ kramaśca bhinnānāṃ bhavatīti na bhedalakṣaṇāprāgārabhyate /
tathā 'dhikāraḥ karmasvarūpe 'vadhārite tadyogyatayā śakyo nirūpayitumiti pañcāpi lakṣaṇāni pratīkṣate /
tathottaraḥ ṣaṭko 'tideśaviṣayatvā dupadeśajñānādhīnasiddhiḥ samastaḥ samastaṃ pūrvaṣaṭkamapekṣate /
tataśca pariśeṣasiddho 'yaṃ bhedalakṣaṇasya sabandha ityatrārabhyate /
yadvidhaḥ karmabheda iti sādhanabhedopacārād vakṣyamāṇasūtrakramānurodhānnāmadheyaṃ saṃkhyānantaraṃ paṭhitavyaṃ sadanādarādante paṭhitam /
itikaraṇo hetvarthaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ karmabheda etaiḥ kāraṇairiti yāvat /
śratha vā karaṇe bhedaśabdaṃ vyutpādya sāmānādhikaraṇyenaiva śabdāntarādīni vyākhyeyāni saṃjñāśabdāntarayoḥ saṃkhyāguṇayoścāpaiaunaruktyaṃ svasthāne vacyāmaḥ /
sarvatra caiṣāṃ bhinnaviṣayatvā śrutyā divasālacintā bhaviṣyatīti tadbhedapratipādanamātraṃ tātparyeṇa anyadupodvātaprasaktānuprasaktyādinā 
yathedamevādhikaraṇaṃ prakṛtānuniṣpādyapūrva bhedānusāra sidhyartha mupohātatvena bhaviṣyati katara smātyadātphalena saṃbadhyamānādasarvabhedābhedāvanugantavyāviti /
yadā niravayavo vākyavākyārthī syātāṃ tataḥ kiṃ pratipadaṃ dharma ityādirasaṃbaddha eva vicāraḥ syādata /
vākyeca padānāmatho iti /
atrāpi codyate 
yadi hi dharmasvarūpamabhidhīyeta tataḥ kiṃ padena padenoccataiti vicāro yujyate lākṣaṇike tvayuktaḥ 
na cātra yo dharmaḥ sa kiṃ padena padenoccataityevaṃ vicāryate kiṃ tarhi yaḥ padena padenocyate sa kiṃ phalasambandhottarakālaṃ vākyārthātmanā gamyamāno dharmo bhavati athetarapadārthānugṛhīta ekaḥ padārtha iti /
tathā ca sarvairekasya dharmatvaṃ pratipāditaṃ bhavati /
sābātphala sādhanamātrasya dharmatvābhyapagamāt /
na ta sarveṣāmekaḥ kaścidarthosti yaḥ sarvaireka ityevamāśrīyeta /
yacca phalapadena sada saṃbadhyate tasyārthaṃ dharmamapūrvasādhanaṃ ca manyante /
tena kiṃ sarvāṇi padāni phalena saṃbadhyante kiṃ vā eka miti vicāraḥ /
kiṃ prāptaṃ pratipadamiti /
kutaḥ aikarūpyeṇa sambandhaḥ pradhāne na ca sidhyati /
tasmātphalapadenaiva sarvaṃ saṃbadhyate padam 
phalena yasya saṃbandhastato 'pūrva prakalpyate 
yadi hi phala saṃbandhamātraparyavasāyya va vākyaṃ bhavetattaḥ kadā cidapi sarvāṇi phalena saṃbadhyeran/
icha ta tāvanmātreṇāsiddhera pūrvamanyatkalpayitavyaṃ taccānupapatti pramāṇakaṃ, tatraikāpūrvakalpana yopapanne nādṛṣṭāntarakalpanāpramāṇamasti /
yo hyanekā nyapūrvāṇi kalpayati kalpayatya sāve kaṃ taccetkalpitamarthavattvādvā kyā kṣīṇā 'nyathānupapattirnāpūrvāntarasya pramāṇaṃ bhavati /
tasmādekameva pha lasaṃbandhi tasmāccāpūrvam itaratphanavadupakārītyadhyavasīyate /
na cātra virodho bhaviṣyati nāmadheyatvena parihārāt /
agatyā vā daśāpavitreṇa grahaṃ saṃmārśetivanmatvarthalakṣaṇāśrayaṇāt arthāītiprasādhyāṃśadvāreṇa vā dhātvarthairātmīyakaraṇagrahaṇasiddheḥ /
evaṃ sthite kataradekaṃ saṃbadhyatāmiti sarvathānekādṛṣṭa kalpanāparicārād aniyamaprāptau uccate / tantravārtike /
pradhāne phaja saṃbandhi tatsaṃbadhyaṅgamiṣyate /
pradhānāṅgatvamekasya na caikanāvakalpate 
yāvāneva hi ananyalabhyo 'rthaḥ śabdādgamyate sa sarvaḥ śabdārthaḥ /
sarvatra cākhyāte dhātvarthaśca tadanuraktā ca bhāvanā vijñāyate/
tasmādbhāvārthatvavyapadeśaḥ /
tadvyatiriktāstu dravyaguṇaśabdāḥ vijñāyadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
ntaeveti na pṛṣṭāḥ/
tatra dravyādiśabdānāṃ niṣpannārthābhidhāyināṃ karaṇārthatvayogyatvātprāpnoti phalasaṃgatiḥ /
sarvatra di phalaṃ sādhyatvātmirūpaṃ sādhanamapecate na sādhyāntaraṃ, nāmārthaśca siddhatvāttadapeścāpūraṇasamarthaḥ nākhyātāyaiḥ svayameva tāvatsādhyatvā, ttasmāddūvyādibhyaḥ phalamiti prāpta sūtreṇottaraṃ dīyate 
phalasaṃbandho heturapūrvapratipatteḥ  /
saṃbandhaścākāḍāpūrvakaḥ /
sā ca bhāvaśabdebhyaḥ prasappaṃnto dṛśyate na dravyaguṇaśabdebhyaḥ /
tasmādākhyātebhyo 'pūrvabhāvanā gamyate tatra ca dhātvarthasya karaṇatvapratipattiḥ pratyāsatteḥ/
atastenaiva phanakaraṇabhūtenānyathānupapacyā 'pūrvaṃ bhāvyate ityavadhāryyate /
kathaṃ punaryajyādīnpṛthakṛtyakevala pratyayavācya eva bhāvanārthī labhyate bhāvayediti /
kutaḥ 
na ca dhātvantarārthaṃ yajyādayaḥ pratipādayanti svārthamācavyāpatatvāt /
ataḥ śabdarahitamevedamāropyate bhāvayediti /
kriṃ ca 
tadyathā pikamānayetyukte yo nāmārthaṃ na pratipadyate tasmai kokina śabdameva kevalaṃ prayuñjate na kokilaḥ pika iti, tathātra yadyākhyātasya karotirṇyanto vā bhavatiḥ paryyāyaḥ tatastadarthakathane tanmātrameva prayoktavyaṃ nākhyātapratyayopi, na hi tadānoṃ vidhicya jñāyate kenāṃśena kriyā pratyāyyataiti /
atra tu bhāvayetkuryyāditi vā punarapi liṅ prayajyate eva /
ataśca yo 'nena yajateḥ pareṇārthaḥ pratipāditaḥ asau bhāvayaterapi pareṇa tenaivetyadhikāvāpa eva bhāvayatiḥ /
tasmādavaidika iti /
atrābhidhīyate /
sarvatraiva tāvat 
sāmānādhikaraṇyena karotyartho 'vagamyate 
karotiḥ kriyamāṇena na kaścitkarmmaṇā vinā /
bhavatyarthasya karttā ca karote karmma jāyate 
nityaṃ na bhavanaṃ yasya yasya vā nityabhūtatā /
na tasya kriyamāṇatvaṃ khapuṣpākāśayoriva 
karotyarthasya yaḥ katī bhavituḥ sa prayojakaḥ /
bhavitā tamapecyātha prayojyatvaṃ prapadyate 
prayojyakarttakai kāntavyāpārapratipādakāḥ /
eyantā eva prayujyante tatprayojakakarmmasu 
śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ nānuyojyāḥ svabhāvataḥ /
tena nānā vadantyarthīnprakṛtipratyayādayaḥ 
yattūktaṃ na vidhitvavyatiriktā liṅādayo 'rthaṃ vadantīti /
tadayuktam /
kutaḥ 
kevalasyāprayogitvātkartṛsaṃkhyādisaṃgrahāt /
rūpāvināśasiddheśva pratyayo 'pi prayujyate 
bhāvanā gamyamānā ca dhātu pratyayasannidhau kasya vācyeti vispaṣṭaṃ na kadā citpratīyate 
pratyayārthaṃ saha brūtaḥ prakṛtipratyayau sadā /
prādhānyādbhāvanā tena pratyayārtho 'vadhārthyate 
tathā kramavatornnityaṃ prakṛtipratyayāṃbhayoḥ /
pratyayaśrutivelāyāṃ bhāvanātmā' vagamyate 
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
akhyādāvapi kaśe bhāvye 'styeva hi bhāvanā /
anyatrāśeṣabhāvāttuna tathā sā prakāśate /
yadyapi kartturaniṣpannatvād vyatiriktabhāvayitavyābhāvāt atyādiṣu prayojakavyāpāro nātīva lakṣyate tathāpi pratyayasāmarthyābhāvayatotyavagamyate /
kimityapeci cāniṣpanne kartaryanyatkiṃ cidityakalpanādātmānamityeva sambadhyate kena bhāvanena kathamavayavajananādiprakāreṇeti /
trayopi tatra bhāvanāṃśā bhavanenaiva pūryante vyāpārāntarāmambhavāttatra ke cidavayavā bhāvanavyāpṛtāḥ prayujyante ke citmidbhavanāḥ prayojakāḥ /
siddhabhavanāsiddhabhavanavati ca sāmānyamubhayasaṃparkādbhāvanetyucyate /
etena jāyate niṣpadyate sidhyatītyādīni vyākhyātāni/
astiḥ punarjjanisamānārthādbhavatesparitanī mavamyāma bhinnapansattayātmabhavanaṃ bhavagāvayatītyevamākhyātapratyayaṃ labhate /
tatrāpi tu kālakṛtabhedapūrvettara sāmānyasattārūpeṇa pūrvavadeva prayojyaprayojakavyāpārakalpanānusataivyā /
sattyāmapi tvevamādiṣu bhāvanāyāṃ niṣpannacetanakartṛviṣayatvādvidhipratiṣedhayorasambhavaḥ /
syādetat /
dṛṣṭo vi dhirapi tasmātprāyaṇīyasyāha ṛtvijā bhavitavyam /
rathantaraṃ bhavati/
atra adhvaryuḥ syāt /
ihokthyāni syuriti /
satyaṃ dṛśyate na tviha pūrveṇa tulyo bhavatyarthaḥ /
middho hi puruṣaḥ karmasambandhanimittamṛtviktvaṃ bhavadanyaireva vākkāyamanovyāpārairbhāvayedityucyate /
tathā rathantarādiṣu satyapi śrutyā bhavana vidhisambandhe ta tra sambhavādanumīyamānā bhāvanaiva vidhīyate /
yatra tviāmuko bhavediti prayogastatra bhavatestiṣṭhatyarthavācitvātmambhavatyeva vyatiriktaṃ bhāvayitavyam ityevaṃ vijñāyate /
sthānenānyatkiṃ cidbhāvayediti /
tena bhūtabhaviṣyadvarttamānāpadeśamāceṣvevāpāramārthika bhavitṛvyāpārasya bhāvanātvaṃ na vidhyādiṣu /
bhūtādikathane pi yadā samastaṃ vyāpāraṃ dhāturevopādatte nāvayavakānādikṛtabhedāśrayaṇaṃ tadā vispaṣṭādvirodhā dvātvarthamātraṃ kartṛsaṃkhyādayaśca ākhyāta padārthatvenāvadhāryante na bhāvanā /
na ca bhāvanāvyabhicāreṇa doṣa ityuktam /
yattu kṛdanteṣvapi dhātavo bhāvānāṃ na vyabhicarantīti /
satyaṃ dhātvarthā na vyabhicaranti taireva tu gamyamānatvādanabhidheyatvamapi śakyaṃ vaktum /
tathā hi 
yathaiva bhāvapradhānatvādākhyāte tatsambandhādeva guṇabhūtakārakapratītisiddhernna kartṛkarmmaṇorabhidhānaṃ bhaviṣyatyevaṃ karnādyabhiṣānādeva tadanyathānapapattyā bhāvanāsiddheranabhidhānaṃ gamyamānāpedāyaiva ca karotisāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ, yathā pacatiśabdasya devadattaśabdenā,tathābhūtayaiva ca kārakasambandho 'pyupapatsyate /
atha vā bhāvanopasarjjanadhātvarthaniṣpattyarthatvātkārakāṇāṃ dhātvarthenaiva sambandhasiddhiḥ/
sa eva hi tāni svasiddhyarthamapekṣate bhāvanāpi ca tathābhūtānyeva tāni gṛhṇātītyaviruddhaḥ sambandhaḥ /
kṛtyānāṃ tu praiṣavācitvātmatyapi bhāvanānabhidhāne tāvatsvārthaparthyavasānaṃ nāsti yāvadaṃśatrayaparipūrṇā bhāvanā na labdhā /
kutaḥ 
na hi puruṣaḥ svavyāpāra mutkā 'nyadanuṣṭhātuṃ śaktaḥ praiṣāścainadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
manuṣṭhāpayanti /
te yadi tadvyāpāraṃ kathaṃ cinnopādayaḥ na ni yoktuṃ śakkayuḥ ityevamapi bhāvanākṣepasiddhiḥ /
yāvāṃśca brāhmaṇagataḥ kaścitpraiṣaḥ sa sarvaḥ prāptyabhāvādidhireva bhavatīti vināpi smaraṇena kṛtyānāṃ vidhāyakatvam /
ayameva ca vidhipraiṣayorviśeṣaḥ 
tasmātpratyayārthī bhāvanetyupapannam /
nanu ca yadi prayojaka vyāpāro bhāvaneṣyate tataḥ pacāvadhiyādīni yajau ca mānasaḥ saṅkalpa ityādīnāṃ bhāvanātvaṃ taeva dhātvarthā  iti dhātuvāccaiva bhāvanā syāt /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
dhātvarthavyatirekeṇa yadyapyeṣā na labhyate /
tathāpi sarvasāmānyarūpeṇānyā 'vagamyate 
anyadeva hi yāgādau sāmānyaṃ karaṇātmakam /
anyacca bhāvanā nāma sādhyatvena vyavasthitam 
yādṛśī bhāvanā ''khyāte dhātvarthaścāpi yādṛśaḥ /
nāsau tenaiva rūpeṇa kathyate 'nyaiḥ padaḥ ka cit 
sambandhamānamuktaṃ ca dhātvarthabhāvaḥ /
śrutyā tadekāṃśaniveśe ta vyāpāro 'syā na vidyate /
sambandhamātraṃ kṛtvā nivṛttavyāpārāyāṃ śrutāvanyanaraśiniveśo yogyatvādāśrayitavyaḥ /
tadyadi sādhyāṃśādeka pratyayopātena pratyāsannatareṇa vidhitvena pracāvyate tato īśāntareṇa nūnaṃ sampatsyataityevaṃ pratīcyate /
kiṃ ca 
bhavane yasya kartṛtvaṃ kathaṃ cidavadhāritam /
svavākye vā 'nyavākye vā sa sādhyatvaṃ prapadyate 
tato 'vadhuta svargādisādhyāṃśā bhāvanā kena bhāvaye dityevaṃ karaṇamapecate /
tatra ca śāstrādhīnapravṛttitvāttatmanikarṣādāvāśrīyamāṇe pramāṇāntarācca yogyāyogyatvayorajñānādvidhyavirodhācātyanta pratyāsatcyupasthita dhātvarthā tikramakāraṇābhāvātsarvaphalabhāvanānāṃ ca kena cidvātvarthaviśeṣeṇa vinā 'nupapatteryā genetyevaṃ vijñāyate /
yadyapi ca yāga svayameva tāvadaniṣpanastathāpi svasādhana niṣpāditaḥ santmādhayiṣyati /
sarvameva ca kadā cinniṣpannaṃ kadā cidaniṣpannam/
na ca prāk śākhapravṛtternniṣpattiḥ ka cidupayujyate phalasiddhikālamānopayogitvātkaraṇaniṣpatteḥ /
pramāṇavaśācca trikālavarttināmapi sādhanatvāvirodhaḥ /
tasmādyāgādīnāṃ karaṇatvaṃ taccāpūrvadāreṇeti tacchabdebhyo 'pūrvapratītiḥ /
ataścaivamapi sūtrārthaḥ sambhavati /
ye bhāvārthāḥ bhāvanāprayojanāḥ karmmaśabdā yajyādayaḥ tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeteti /
nanu coktana karmakaraṇa sambandha nyāyena sakarma kaṣātuyuktādevākhyātādbhāvanā 'vagatiḥ prāpnoti /
ta thā hi 
yadi vā sarvadhāḍhanāṃ sakarmakatvāpattiratha vā 'karmmakebhyo bhāvanayā na bhavitavyam /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
kutaḥ 
środanaṃ pacati grāmaṃ gacchatīti dhātvarthāpavargalabhyamekaṃ karma, apara punabhāvanākarma /
tatra kadā cidvātvarthakammaiva bhāvanākammatvamapi pratipadyate pākanādanaṃ bhāvayatīti /
kadā citpunaḥ svakarmma viśiṣṭadhātvarthayuktā bhāvanā karmāntareṇa yujyate grāmagamanena svārthaṃ bhāvayediti odanapākena ceti /
taccaitaddvātvarthātparataḥ tadavāpyamātratvena gamyamānaṃ dhātvarthāntaratirohitaṃ bhāvanākarmmatayā sarvatrāvadhārthyate /
tacca prāyeṇaivaṃ kāmaśabdenaiva saṃvandhamāpadyate/
sukhakāma āsīta svāsthyakāmaḥ śīyateti /
satyapi āsiśetyorakarmakatve yaḥ pratyayena karotyaryobhihitaḥ tatkarmmatvena ca svādīnyavadhāryante /
tena karoteḥ sarvadā sakarmakatvāda karmmakākhyātānāmapi ca tatmāmānādhikaraṇyadarśanā tkiṃ karotyāste kiṃ karoti śete iti vimādiṣvapi sakarmikā bhāvanā 
tadujjhitvaiva putrāḥ karmmatvaṃ bhāvanāśritama 
āsanaśayanādau dina niyamenānantaryeṇa vedaṃ taditi vā karma nirūpyate, tenākamakā abhidhīyante /
pacigamyādīnāṃ tu vikvidyattatsaṃyujyamānasākṣātmambandhikamrmmāvyabhicārātmakarmakatvaṃ, na tu bhāvanāviśeṣaṇe kaścidiśeṣaḥ /
seyaṃ bhāvanā aṃśayatantravārtike /
paripūrṇā satī sarvakaraṇāṃnāmupāyānanugṛhītānāṃ karaṇatvānupapatteḥ kathaṃ bhāvayeditītikarttavyatāmapekṣate /
sā ca pratyakṣādīnāmanugrāhaka darśanaśaktyabhāvādatyantaśāstragamyeti yathāsannikaghaṃ tadasaṃbhavādā yathā kathaṃ cidupasthāpyamānā śāstrānusāreṇa śrutyādyupadeśena codanāmāmānyādyatideśena vā atyantādṛṭopakāradvāreṇānyathānupapattyā kalpyate /
tataḥ paripūrṇatvādanuṣṭhātuṃ yogyeti vidhīyate /
tadvidhānāccārthāpatyā yāgādividhānamityupapannaṃ bhāvārthavatram /
bhavanti ke citkarmmaśabdā yāgo yajanamijyeti udāharttavye tatmāmānādhikaraṇyasiddha gye nai kacikāyudāharaṇaṃ yāgādikaraṇatvacodanottarakālabhāvika rmaśabdatve na pāratantryāttujñānam/
svatantrāṇāṃ kathaṃ cidapi bhāvārthatvāśavāsvaṃbhavāt /
yāgādayo hi svātantryeṇāpi kadā cidanumānād bhāvārthīśaṅkāviṣayāḥ syuriti /
ke cidbhāvārthī na karmaśabdā yathā bhāvayetkuryyāditi codāharaṇaṃ bhūtyādayastu prayojyavyāpāravacanatvānnaiva yathāvarṇitabhāvārthā ityanudāharaṇam/
tatra ya thā kathaṃ ciṇijantavyutpattyā bhāvaśabda eko nīyeta netarau /
tāvapi tu prayojyavyāpārāṃśena kathaṃ cid bhāvārthāvityudāhṛtau /
atha vā dvitīyasūtrārthavyākhyānena bhāvanāprayojanatvamaṃgavācitve nāstīti vināpi sakalārthābhidhānādbhavanti bhāvārthāḥ /
kathaṃ punaramī na karmmaśabdāḥ, yadā dhātumātraṃ karmma śavdatvenoktaṃ nirviśeṣasya sāmānyasyānuṣṭhā tuma śakyatvāda karmmaśabdatvam /
a to viśeṣavācināmeva dhātūnāṃ karmmaśavdatvagrahaṇādacodyametat /
yadi hi prayenacitrādarśa paurṇamāsaśabdāḥ phalaiḥ saṃbadhyeran tato yāgakaraṇatvābhāvāttatsāmānādhikaraṇyanimittanāmadheyadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
nvānupapatteḥ prasiddhyādibhirguṇa vidhitvamevasyādataḥ sthitaetasminadhikaraṇe ityāha /
kasmātpunaridaṃ tatraiva na nītaṃ pramāṇantavagonā saṃbandhādatha nāmadheyatvaṃ kasmādatra nānīyate bhedalakṣaṇenāsaṃbandhāttasmādyathānyāsameva sthitayorarthātpaurvāparthyasiddhiḥ /
nacaiṣāmarthiteti phalapadābhiprāyam /
vivibhaktitvāditi saṃbandhanimittākhyātavibhaktivigamādatha vā niṣpannārthābhidhāyisubvibhaktiviśeṣayogo vivibhaktitvam /
tasmānna dravyādiśabdānāṃ phalasaṃbandha iti /
āha ca /
sādhyasādhanasaṃbandhaḥ sarvadā bhāvanāśrayaḥ /
tena tasya na siddhiḥ syādbhāvanāpratyayāhate 
yadi hi bhāvanāvacanasyaivāpūrvapratipādakatvamiṣyate dhātorvā pratyayanirapekṣasya tato nāmapakṣo durbalaḥ syā, dikṣa tu yathaiva dhātoḥ pratyayasaṃbandhānugṛhītasya bhāvanānurañjananimittaṃ karaṇavācitvaṃ bhavatyevaṃ nāmapadasthāpītya viśeṣaḥ /
yeṣāmutpattau sve prayoge rūpopalabdhistāni nāmāni tasmāttebhyaḥ parākāṅkṣā bhūtatvātsve prayoge  yaduktaṃ yadai kasmādapūrvaṃ tadā itarattadarthaṃ bhaviṣyatīti tadganaṃ tāvadvastudharmeṇa viśeṣaṃ darśayati /
katham 
ekasmādadṛṣṭe kalpite yadotarad dṛṣṭārthatvena tādarthaṃ bhajate tato lāghavaṃ labhyate /
asya tu tādarthyasiddhaye tato'pi punaradṛṣṭaṃ kalpyataeva tato varaṃ phalenaiva sarvāṇi saṃbaddhāni /
na ca saṃbandhavaiyaktemāśrayaṇaṃ nāmnaśca phalasaṃbandhe' vaśyaṃ dhātvarthastadanugrahārtho'bhyupagantavyaḥ /
sa casvayaṃ niṣpādyaḥ sidvarūpasya nā mārthasya na śaknoti dṛṣṭenopakarttum /
na hi nāmārthastamapeścate śabdaprayogavelāyāmeva niṣpannatayā gamyamānatvādapekṣaṇīyasya vā siddhatvenāyogyatvātprayujyate 'sminniti cābhidheyaeva pra yogaḥ /
tadādhāraiva hi niṣpanna rūpopalabdhiranutpannatve kriyā pasya vaktavye vināśitva pradarśanaṃ niṣpannasyāpi kṣaṇikatvena panaḥ punarniṣpatyapekṣopapatteḥ /
tebhyaḥ parākāṅkṣānyākāṅkṣā niṣpādyatvena vā pradhānākāṅkṣā na vidyataiti adhyāhāraḥ /
atha vā sebhyaḥ parā dūre ākāṅkṣatyarthaḥ /
kutaḥ bhūtatvādeveti /
svarū pakathanārthamupanyastaṃ niṣpannatvādeveti /
punarante tadeva hetutvenoddiṣṭaṃ sūtrakāreṇa /
yeṣāṃ tūtpattāvarthe sve prayogo na vidyate tānyākhyātāni tasmātebhyaḥ pratītatvātprayo dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
gasya 
akhyātavarttī dhātvarthaḥ mādhyarūpaḥ pratīyate /
tasminphalavatīṣṭe tu nāmno dṛṣṭārthateṣyate 
sādhyātmako 'pi dhātvarthe/
yadā nāmnā 'bhidhīyate /
tadā dravyavadevāsau niṣpannātmā pratīyate 
codanā punarārambhaḥ 
siddhaṃ kṛtvā 'pūrvaṃ tatpratipattyupāyaśabda viśeṣa vicāraḥ kṛtaḥ /
tasya siddhatvamevāprasiddhamatastadeva tāvatpratipādanīyamityata ātantravārtika /
phalāya vihitaṃ karmma kṣaṇikaṃ cirabhāvine /
tatsiddhinnī nyathetyevamapūrvaṃ prati gamyate 
pramāṇapañcakā'jñānādaparvaṃ ṣaṣṭhagocaraḥ /
tasmādanvarthanāmaitanna vastutvena gamyate 
padavākye na caitasya vācaka śṛṇumaḥ kva cit /
śabdagamyatvamapyasya tena naivopapadyate 
dṛṣṭāthī pattistāva mastitvavadevātrāpi nirākarttavyā /
sva bhāvādināpi īśvaradaridrādivaicivyopapatteḥ /
śrutārthīpattirapi kīdṛśī bhavati yatra pratyakṣeṇaivānupapattirdṛśyate /
na ca kalpya māno'rtha kena cihirudhyate /
tadyathā suveṇāvatītyukte na ca kathaṃ cidapi māṃsapuroḍābhādīni tenāvadātuṃ śakyantaiti pratyakṣagamyatvāt /
api ca tatrāpi prasaktaḥ evaṃ kalpyate dravāṇāmiti /
na caiṣākalpanā kena cidvirudhyate śrutānyaśrutapa rikalpanābhāvāt /
apūrvaṃ tu na kadā citphalasāghanatvena saṃ bhāvyate /
yato 'nvakāraṇaniṣedhe sati taddiṣayā pariśetrasiddhiḥ sthāna 
nahi kāraṇāntarapratiṣedhamātreṇāpūrvanimittatā gamyate, śaśaviṣāṇādibhiranaikāntāt /
api ca yadi tāvadapūrvaṃ yāgasya sādhyamiṣyate tataḥ śrutaṃ svagaṃ pariparikalpitaṃ bhavet /
tantravārtika /
atha phalaṃ prati sādhanabhūtaḥ saiva gatiḥ /
na cākārāntareṇa tannirūpayituṃ śakyate /
tenāgamaprāmāṇyādyāgādeva phalena bhavitavyam /
kathaṃ naṣṭaḥ sādhayatīti cet /
ya di śākhādevaṃ gamyate kiṃ bhavato viruddhyate/
śriyamāṇena vā phalaṃ sāghanīyamityatra kiṃ pramāṇam/
api ca ākāśādīni nityāvasthitāni kasmātphalaṃ na sādhayanti/
yadi ca śrayamāṇātirekesthāyitva saṃbhavāda pūrveṇa phalaṃ sādhyataiti kalpyane tato va ramākāśādeva kalpitaṃ, tasya hi sthānasabhāvāvapi tāvatprasidvai/
kevalaṃ phalanimittatvamāśrayaṇīyam /
pūrve tu sadbhāvaprabhṛti sarve niṣpramāṇakaṃ kalpanīyam /
atha yāga saṃbandhinā kena cidavasthitena phalaṃ dātavyamityabhiprāyaḥ, tathā satyapi  yaṣṭurevātmano yāgaissaṃgatasya sthitasya ca /
nimittanvaṃ varaṃ klṛptaṃ lāghavaṃ hi tathā sati 
yadā karmmavināśo'yaṃ phalaṃ naḥ sādhayiṣyati /
aṅgiyāgavidhānādvi tadayatnena kalpyate 
yadi caikānta to brūyaḥ śabdāḥ kālāntare phalam /
tatastenaiva  kalpyeta nimittaṃ vastu kiṃ cana 
pūrvaṃ niścitya śākhārthaṃ prayoge hi pravarttate /
prayogottarakālaṃ tuna śākhārtho 'vadhāryate /
nahi avidvānvihitostīti tāvadavaśyaṃ yāvacchāsagamyaṃ ta tsarvaṃ prāganuṣṭānādavagantavyam /
na ca tatkāle karmmaphalakā la viyogajñānakāraṇamasti /
yacca śāstra pravṛttivelāyā tadantargatanvena nāvadhāritaṃ taduttarakālamevāvadhārthyanaiti kuna etat /
a pica 
sukhaduḥkhātmakatvena samāneṣveva janmasu /
kriyānantarameveha staḥ kharganarakāvapi 
pratiṣedheṣu cāpūrvaṃ na śākhārthena janyate /
tadatikramajanyaṃ tu na bhavecchā khapūrvakam 
aṅgāni yadi vā 'pūrvaṃ kurvantyārādavasthitam /
asambandhātpradhānānāṃ na syāttenopakārthyatā 
na tāvadyugapajjanyaṃ karmmabhiḥ kramavarttibhiḥ /
na cānavayavatvāttatkramaśo 'pi pratīyate 
sarvābhivyaktīnāṃ cayānyatamasaṃskāradvāratvātsaṃskārāntaramavaśyaṃ kalpanīyaṃ tataḥ punaḥ sa eva keśaḥ ityapramāṇatā /
yadi ca kiyānantaramapūrvamupalabhyeta tato 'bhivyajyate iti brūyāma /
yadi cāsya prāgastitve pramāṇaṃ bhavet /
na tu tadubhayamapyastīti sarvathā nāstyapūrvaṃ na caitatsūtraṃ tatpratipādane vispaṣṭamityavyākhyānametat /
atrocyate /
yadidaṃ svamatiparikalpitaṃ vigrahava divā'pūrvaṃ bhavadbhinirākriyatena tenāsmākaṃ kiṃ cidvirudhyate /
yato naitattādṛśaṃ  kasya cidiṣṭaṃ, kiṃ tarhi karmabhyaḥ prāgayogyasya karmmaṇaḥ puruṣamya vā yogyatā śāstragamyā yā parā sāpūrva miṣyate /
pradhānakarmaṇāmaṅgakarmaṇāṃ vā prākaraṇātsvargādiprāptyayogyāḥ puruṣāḥ kratavaśva svakāryyāyogyāḥ /
tāmubhayīmapyayogyatāṃ vyudasya pradhānairaṅgeśya yogyatoṣajanyanaitya va saṃ sarveṇṇābhyupagantavyam/
asatyāṃ tasyāmakṛtasamatvaprasaṅgāt /
saiva ca puruṣagatā ṛtugatā vā yogyatā śāstre 'sminnapūrvamityapadigyate /
yattu pratyakṣādigamyatvamasya nāstīti, satyaṃ śrutārthāpattivyatiriktairna gamyate sa tvadoṣaḥ kiṃ kāraṇam /
nārthāpattiravaikā pramāṇaṃ tasya veṣyate /
śabdakadeśabhāvācca svārtheṣvāgama eva naḥ 
kṣaṇikatvena sarvatra naikasyāpi hi karmmaṇaḥ /
kathaṃ cidyugapadvṛttiḥ phale kimuta bhūyasām 
śaktibhiḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ vyavahārānupātitā/
tenānyadeśakālepi rūpe tābhiḥ sa sidhyati 
yāgādeva phalaṃ taddhi śaktidvāreṇa sidhyati /
sūkṣmaśaktyātmakaṃ vā tatphalamevopajāyate 
kāṣṭhaiḥ paktavyamityukte nirdiṣṭā jvalanakriyā /
aṅgure jāyamāne ca vṛścopyutpanna iṣyate 
vināśitvena vijñātaṃ sādhanaṃ lokavedayoḥ /
sambhāvita sāmarthya sthāyitvaṃ codyate katham 
na cātikrāntayāgebhyaḥ puruṣebhyaḥ phalodgatiḥ /
atikrāntā natikrānta viśeṣastava nāsti hi 
aṅgamadhye 'pi karttava bhaveccedu prakārakaḥ /
prasaṅgasiddheraṅgānāmaprāptirvikṛtau bhavet 
eko rogo hṛto yasya yasya vā 'pahṛtā daśa /
arogitve tayorbhedo na kaścidapi dṛśyate 
na ca karmmavināśebhyaḥ svargādi śrūyate phalam /
viparyyayāca naitebhyo jātaṃ yāgasya tadbhavet 
aihikaṃ cāpi putrādi kramajanmasvabhāvakam /
na karmmānantaraṃ kaścitphalaṃ labdhaṃ vyavasthati 
cirakālopabhogaphantrātmakatvākāmādīnāṃ kiyānantaraṃ tādātmyāsambhave sati yatraivāntarāje nimittaṃ soṇaṃ tatraivāpāraḥ prasajyetetyavaśyaṃ samastopabhogaṃ yāvadavasthitena kena cihnavitavyam /
tataśca prāgeva prayogādityamavadhāraṇātkarṭavaiguṇyābha jhyā 'rthāpatteranai kāntikatvamityayuktametat /
yattu pratiṣedheṣu na stra gamyamapūrvamityucyate   vidheyebhyo yathā 'pūrvaṃ vidhiśāstreṣu gamyate /
tathaiva pratiṣedhebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaistaducyate 
karteva cāśrayastasya kriyā 'pyacaiva ca sthitā /
ātmavāde sthitaṃ hyetatkartṛtvaṃ sarvakarmasu 
yadi svasamavenaiva śaktiriṣyeta karmmaṇām /
tadvināśe tato na syātkartṛsthā tu na naśyati 
śaktiḥ kāryyānumeyatvād yadgataivopayujyate /
tadgataivābhyupetavyā khāśrayā'nyāśrayā'pi vā 
tādarthyena hi śeṣatvaṃ nāśrayāyibhāvataḥ /
rājārthī payikaṃ nityamuṣṭo vahati kuṅkumam 
arthāpattarihāpūrvaṃ pūrvamekaṃ pratīyate /
tatastatsiddaye bhūyaḥ syādapūrvāntarapramā 
pramāṇavantyadṛṣṭāni kalpyante subahanyapi /
adṛṣṭaśatabhāgo'pi na kalpyo hyapramāṇakaḥ 
āvṛttibhiryyathā'dhyāye saṃskāro bhavati kramāt /
vākyāvayavarūpeṇa tathā 'pūrvaṃ bhaviṣyati 
naikarūpaiva bhāvānāmabhivyaktiḥ pratīyate /
ātmasthonmīlanaṃ tena vyaktirasya bhaviṣyati 
tasmādastyapūrvaṃ sūtrasyāpi ca na prakṛtīprayikamanyamarthaṃ pa śyāmaḥ /
tenārambhacodanaivāpūrvasyāpi codanetyayamevārthaḥ /
yadi punaḥ phalavacanasāmarthyāttadeva tadapi naṣṭamityapūrva kalpanānipramāṇakatvaṃ mantrāno barametadityāha /
na hi karmaṇāṃ rūpamu palabhāmacaityayuktaṃ rūpaśabdāvibhāgācetyatra pratyakṣopalabdhyabhidhānāt /
yāgaprastāve ca sati tasyācalanātmakatvādyadāśrayaṃ deśāntaraṃ prāpayatītyasambaddham /
atrocyate tantravārtika /
yadyapi karmmasvarūpamupalabhyate tathāpi kālāntarāṣasthānābhāṃvād na tadupayujyataiti nopalabhāmahaityucyate 
na hi saṅkalpamātreṇa phalaniṣpattiḥ samastātmamastetikarttavyatākācca karmmaṇaḥ phalaśravaṇā, ttatra dvyavadānaprakṣepādīnāṃ gra iṇāsādanādīnāṃ ca saṃyogavibhāgaphalatvātsthāyitve tadāśraye pāvaśyaṃ bhavitavyam/
na cāsāvasti /
na cābhivyaktaṃ rūpamupalabhyate /
saṅkalpādīnāmapi saṅkalpāntarāditirodhānānnātra svarūpāvasthānopapattiḥ /
avasthānaṃ cātmasamavetasya vā syātpradeyaṃdravyasamavetasya vā /
na tāvadātmani calanaṃ samavaiti sarvavyāpinaḥ saṃyujyamānaviyujyamānadeśāsambhave calitumasāmarthyāt /
kathaṃ sarvavyāpitvamasyeti cetsarvatropalabhyamānakāryatvāt /
apratyayena hi caitanyasvabhāvasyātmano 'stitvamātramavagamyate na tu deśataḥ kālato vā viśeṣyate /
tataśca /
anavacchinnasāvaṃ vastu yaddeśakālataḥ /
tannityaṃ vibhu cecchantītyātmano vibhuteṣyate 
śarīramātrāntargatātmavādī tvā /
nanu ta deva deśāntarādāgamanasya liṅgam /
ataśca viruddhacetutvamasyeti /
kutaḥ 
yadi hi śarīrāiddipi kiṃ cidātmakāyyamupalabhemahi śarīrāntare sukhaduḥkhādīnyā tataḥ sarvagatatvamadhyavasyema/
yatastu svaśarīrāntarvaryeva kāryaṃ yatra yatra ca tadgatistatra tatra paryyāyepopalabhyate taccarīrakārthyavadeva tatmahitagatasyopapatsyate/
a nyathā hi śarīramapi sarvagataṃ syā, tasmāccharīravadevāsya tatra tatra gamanāpatteḥ sutarāṃ sakriyatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
sandeho vāstu sādhāraṇānai kāntikatvāt /
āha ca 
tatrottaraṃ na hyasatyāgamane kiṃ ciddhirudvamiti /
yeṣāṃ tu na tu tadeveti pāṭhaḥ teṣāṃ siddhāntavādyeva paryāyeṇa sarvatrātmakāryopacambhanamāgamana liṅgatveṣya viśiṣṭamāśaṅkayottaraṃ vadatīti granthayojanā /
kathaṃ punaridamuttaraṃ na hyasatyāgamanaiti /
tathā hi 
pareṇāpi hi śakyaṃ vadituṃ na hi sati gamane kiṃ ciddiruddhamiti /
atrābhidhīyate 
parisaṃkhyārūpeṇā satyevāgamane na kiṃ ciddiruddhaṃ sati tu bahu viruddhamityāha /
tadupavayete 
yadā mūtānāmapi sūkṣmāṇāṃ candrādityaprakāśādīnāṃ na mṛ tpiṇḍādibhiḥ saha mitratvamupapadyate, tannayana vā mayanaṃ, tadā tmanaḥ svabhāvanātyantāmūrttasya jñānasaṃtānasya vā bhūtairmitvaṃ bhavediti kula etat /
yopi syādvādī bahvātmanāṃ śarīrādatyantavyatirekālābhādastyeva mūrttatvaṃ jīvasyeti brūyāttasyāpi itaremarāśrayaprasaktiḥ miśratvānmūrttatvaṃ mūrttatvācca miśrabhāva iti /
ta smāt muktāvasthā nidarśanena ukṣaṇatosyā mūrttatvāt na śarīrasaṃparkanimittamūrttatvasiddhiḥ /
tataśca śarīrādanyaḥ senāsaṃpṛktaścāspatvācca anākṛṣyamāṇaḥ śarīraṃ gacchati tadgatākāśapradeśavadātmā paścānniḥsṛtastatraiva tiṣṭe,nna hi tasya vāyanā pṛthivyādibhirbī preraṇaṃ yena svatantraparaprerito vā gacchen/
jvālāprabhṛtīnāṃ tu sparśavattvādvāyunā preryamāṇānāmulmukādinā vā nīyamānānāṃ yuktaṃ gamanam /
tena kevalaṃ śarīraṃ gacchat acetanaṃ syāt /
sarvagatatve tu yatra yatra gamyate tatra tatrātmānusyūtirasti iti yuktā caitanyānuvṛttiḥ /
yathā pūrvākāśapradeśatyāge sarvagatatvādeva pa reṇāvakāśadānasiddhiḥ /
kiṃ ca 
jñānasaṃta tipakṣastāvannirākṛtaḥ /
tatra nityaḥ sannātmā śarīrābhyantaravarttī 
yadā hyaṇamātra ātmā bhavati tadā yāvāneva pradeśa viśeṣadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
stanādhiṣṭhitaḥ tanmātragatānāmeva sukhaduḥkhādīnāmupalabdhiḥ prāpnoti, tamaścaikammin kṣaṇe śiraḥpādavedanānubhavo na syāt /
atha laghusaṃcāritvāttatra tatropacabhyataityucyate na tatra pramā pāmasti /
na ca kālabhedo lakṣyane, anava sthitasyopalabdhikālāsaṃbhavānnaikatrāpyupalabhyeta tasmādakalpaneyam /
śarīrāvayavānāṃ cāpariśoṣaṇaṃ puṣṭyādi cātmādhiṣṭhitānāṃ bhavati mṛtāvasthāyāṃ viparyayadarśanā, ttatra ya evāvayavastenotsṛṣṭaḥ sa eva mṛtavacchuṣye,datha śarīraparimita āpaṇābhyupagamyate tatrāpi bar̤a dṛṣṭaṃ kalpanīyam 
sarve hyavayavasadbhāvādayaḥ pratyakṣādyaviṣayāḥ santa utprekṣāmātrekarūyante te śavdavacceca pi pratyākhyeyāḥ /
śarīramācāvadhikānāṃ caiṣāmutprekṣitu mapyānantyamaśakyaṃ na caiṣāṃ dravatvādinā vina kaścitsaṃśleṣa heturvidyane /
na cāsaṃśliṣṭānā mekajīvārambhasāmardhyam/
sarvasaṃyogānāṃ ca viyogāvinābhūtatvād ghaṭāditulya kadā cijjīvasya pradhvaṃso bhavet /
