gātracchede ca tadarttināṃ jovāvayavānāṃ tato niḥstyāvaśiṣṭe śarīrabhāge punaḥ praveśa ityetadapramāṇakam /
yattu viyojitamātrāṇāṃ istādīnāṃ sphuraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ, tada bhighāta preritavāyunimittamiti na tāvatā jīvākyavānuganirvijñāyate /
tathā sati saṃkocavikāsāveteṣāṃ bhavata ityatra tantravārtike /
na kiṃ citpramāṇaṃ paśyāmaḥ /
dīpaprabhāprabhṛtīnāṃ tu kathaṃ citpratyavyatvādupapadyete /
na ca pradīpaprabhāyāḥ saṃkoco bhavati bharāvādikādane śeṣaprabhāvināśādanāvṛtā hi jvālā S'tmasamīpe prabhāmaṇḍalamārabdhaṃ samarthā nācchāditā /
etenaiva ca vikāso 'pi pratyuktaḥ anyaeva hyavayavāstatra pracīyamānā vistāraṃ janayanti na tāvatāmeva vikāsaḥ /
sparśavatāṃ ca parasparadeśapratibandhāddeśāntaravyāptyā vikāso ghaṭate, jīvāvayavānāṃ tvamūrttatvātsarveṣāṃ samānadeśatvāvighātānnitya maṇumā tratvaprasaṅgaḥ syāt /
kathaṃ caikamya jīvasya putikā hastagarīraparimitā saṃkocavi kāsau yujyete /
maraṇakāle cāntarābhavaśarīrasaṃcaraṇaṃ taccāsti kena citpratibandhena sadapi na gṛhyate, tena ca śarīrāntare jīvaniśśepa ityādi niṣpramāṇakam /
tasmātsarvagatatvam /
yattu gyāmākataṇḍulamātrādipradarśanamupaniṣatsu tākyāntarapradarśita vibhutvasyaiva sataḥ svakṣmagrahaṇagocaratvāt /
yadapi dvaipāyanenoktam /
aṣṭhamātraṃ puruṣaṃ niścakarṣa banādyama iti tadapi kāvyaśobhārthaṃ vimpraṣṭamṛtyavyavahāra praśaṃsanārthaṃ ca pativratāpraśaṃsāpare vākye prajāpativapotkhedanādivad draṣṭavyam /
tathā hi tenaiva gītādiṣu anekaprakāraṃ savaigatatvaṃ varṇitam/
nanu ca sarvagatatve vyomavatsarvaśarīreṣveka evātmā prāpnoti/
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
śarīrabhūyasvātpratiśaroraṃ ca sukhaduḥkhopalavdhivyavasthādarśanāt /
itarathā hyekaśaroreṇaiva caritārthatvādanekaśarīravaiyarthyaṃ syāt /
janmāntaraśarīravadadoṣa iti cet na /
tatra kamāntaravaśenopabhogāntarārthaṃ punaḥ punarārambhātsarvaśarīragata khādyapana bdhiśca pratiśarīraṃ syāt /
anyadīyaiścendriyaiḥ śarīrāntaragatasyātmīyatvādupalabdharandhavadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
dhirādīnāmabhāvaḥ syāt /
varṇaviśeṣavyavasthayā ca karmacodanābhedo na syāt /
ekasyaivātmanastena tena śarīreṇa saṃbadhyamānasya sarvavarṇopapatteḥ  /
ātmanānātve tvadoṣaḥ/
sarveṣāmapi ca sarvagatatve mūrtirahitatvātmamānadeśavṛyavirodhaḥ /
tadapekṣayaiva ca caitanyātmakatvādya vibhāgāccopaniṣatsvaikātmyavyavahāraḥ /
kathaṃ punarjñānātve 'pi sarveṣāṃ sarvaśarīraiḥ saṃbandhādanyadīyasukhaduḥkhādyanupalabdhiḥ/
ke cittāvadāhuḥ 
śarīrapariṇātmavādino 'pi kincāyaṃ tulyo doṣastasyāpi garbhātma samānadeśatvānmāśejñastadgatāni sukhādīnyapalabheta /
tatra yastasya parihāraḥ sa sarvātmanāṃ sarvaśarīreṣu bhaviṣyatotyadoṣaḥ /
yadyatropapattirucyeta na tu parapakṣamā myāpattirevopapatti, stasya ca tava cobhayorapyanyena parthyanuyogāt/
api ca tasya tvagindriyaparimāṇatvāt /
antaḥ śarīrākāśe bāhyavadevātmano 'nabhyupragama/nnaiva garbhaśarīreṇa mātṛkṣetrajñasya prāptirasti yena tudoṣatā sthāna /
tasmādevaṃ pariharttavyama 
yadi hyātmanaḥ sukhādīnāṃ ca samānadeśalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandha upabhogakāraṇamidhyeta tatoyaṃ doṣaḥ syāt /
iha tu cakṣurādīnāmiva kṣetrajñayogyatālakṣaṇaḥ saṃbadha, stana yathaiva tvagindriyeṇa sparśasamānadeśānāmapi rūpāḍhīnāmagrahaṇam, evamanyenātmanānyadīyadharmmādharmmopāttasakhaduḥkhādyagrahaṇam/
tasmādātmavādoktakhasvābhibhāvavyavasthānādadoṣaḥ/
evaṃ sarvagatatvātsivamātmano niśca latvam /
atha yavadānasamavetamāsīttata āha /
tadvinaṣṭamiti /
na ca tasyāvināśaḥ tadviparīta dravyāntaropannambhāt /
na cāsya gra pratibandhahetuḥ kaścidasti yena na gṛhyeta /
athārthāpatyā gra haṇapratibandhādi kalpyeta tathā'pi satyapūrvāhahunaramadṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭaviparītaṃ ca kalpayitavyaṃ tāvada vinaṣṭamāste/
tathā na dṛśyate tathā pratibandhahetuḥ /
tasyāpyadarśana nimittaṃ cetyevaṃ tasya tasyānyadityavyavasthā /
tathā kṣaṇikasya karmmaṇaḥ sthānamanupalavdhikāraṇaṃ ca kalpyamityatigauravam /
evamanāśritakamrmāvasthāna kalpanāyām /
athātmāśritameva saṃyogavibhāgāvakurvadāsīt tatrāpi dvaṣṭaviparyayādṛṣṭakalpane sthānām/
tasmādaramapūrvakalpana meveti siḍūṃ mūnādhikaraṇaprayojanam /
dravyādīnāṃ phannasaṃvandhe teṣāmadṛṣṭārthatvātkarmmaṇāmiva pratinidhyabhāvaḥ /
karmmaphanna saṃbandhe tu dravyādaḥ karmotpattyā ''dṛṣṭārthatvātmamāna kāryyatvajñānādasti pratini dhiḥ /
kathaṃ tarhi pūrvapakṣavādinaḥ prakrāntāparisamāptidoṣābhāvaḥ/
samāpanīyameva karmma yena kena cid dravyeṇa /
sadṛśopādane tu na yatitavyaṃ sahabhādapi phanāprāptaḥ, karmaṇaścāvihitasādhana vi śeṣasyānapekṣitasadṛśacādyena kena citsiddhena ca tatpūrve dravyasya pratinidhirityucyate anyārthatvāt asādṛśyāca /
pūrvadravyaṃ hi phannādyapravṛttamāsīdidānīmānīyamānaṃ tu pratyavāyaparihārāya dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
naimittikaphalāya vā pravṛtasya karmaṇaḥ siddhyarthamiti /
nāmadheyasiddhirapi prayojanameva/
sā ta pūrvoktatvānna pradarśitā 
ākhyātatvāviśeṣeṇa bhūtairbhavyārthajanmanaḥ /
siddhe ca sādhyatāśaktaḥ sarvākhyātapradhānatā 
nāmākhyātārthasaṃbandhe yadaklṛptaprayojanam /
tasyādṛṣṭārthatā yuktā netarasyāpramāṇikā 
tu yadravyaṃ na cikīyete tāni pradhānaTHIS bhūtāni dravyasya guṇabhūtatvāt 
yaiḥ karmmabhirdravyaṃ svarūpato dharmmato vā na karttumiṣyate yathā prayājādibhiḥ tāni svasādhanāni prati pradhānabhūtatvād adṛṣṭārthāni bhavanti 
pradhāne hi śrutaṃ dravyaṃ nāṅgadravyasya bādhakam /
prayājejyājyavattena intau syād brohyabādhanam 
nanu ca pūrvapaḍho 'pi pradhānaprayukta śrī hyāśrayatvena prakṛtāvaprayojakatvātprayaṅgave carau pradhānenāgṛhyamāṇān brocīnavaghāto na labhate /
naitadevam /
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
tulyo hi brīddisambandhaḥ śākhādyāgāvaghātayoḥ /
vājinejyādi tunyaṃ ca nāprayojakalacaṇam 
dharmamātre tu karma syādanirvṛtteḥ prayājavat 
srukparidhyagnipuroḍāśasaṃmārgāṇāmuttarottarapradhānapratyāsattibhedenodāharaṇapṛthakkam /
etaduktaṃ bhavati 
tatra pūrvapakṣavādī pūrvoktenaiva yaidravyaṃ na cikīrghya ityanena pradhānakarmmalakṣaṇenāca dravyeṇa niṣpāditaṃ kammaṃ na kiṃ cittasya pratyupakurva dṛśyate /
tasmātpradhānakarmma saṃmārgaprokṣaṇādīti 
anyataḥ siddhaśeṣāṇāṃ yeṣāṃ dṛṣṭopakāritā /
teṣāṃ nāpūrvamastīti intyādīnāmudāhṛtiḥ 
tannāma pramāṇaṃ yuktaṃ yadekāntikam /
anaikāntikī ca prādhānye dvitīyā, guṇabhūtadravyopadeśe'pi hṛṣṭatvātmaktūn juhotīti /
tathā prayājaśeṣeṇa havīṃṣyabhidhārayatītyantareṇāpi dvitīyāmājyaprādhānyaṃ dṛṣṭam /
ato śrīnavantītyatrobhayasaṃbhave 'pyupakāradarśanakṛtameva dravyaprādhānyam /
na dvitīyākṛtam /
na ca tatsaṃmāgaṃprokṣaṇādiṣvastīti  ihāpidvitīyayā dravyamevopadiśyatāmiti /
na tadarthatvāllokavattasya ca śeṣabhūtatvāt 
tiṣṭhatu tāvatprayogaḥ /
kiṃ kāraṇam 
yadi hyācārasyaikarūpyaṃ bhavennaiva smṛtayaḥ prayatnena dhāran /
sa eva tu saṃkīrṇatvādasphuṭaḥ smaraṇena pratipācyate /
smaryateca dvitīyāyāḥ prādhānyamarthaḥ /
‘karmmaṇi dvitīyā' 'kartturīkṣitatamaṃ karme’ti /
tathā lokavedayoḥ prayujyate ghaṭaṃ karoti brījīnavaintīti /
yāni ca loka vyabhicārāśaṅkāsthānāni tānyudāharati /
taṇḍulānodanaṃ paca balbajān śikhaṇḍakān kuru tasantravārtike/
paḍunānadya jur̤adhoti /
taṇḍulairbalvajairiti ca prayoktavye yā dvitīyā prayujyate tannūnaṃ tṛtīyā samānārthā seti gamyate /
tatrocyate 
yadā padārthāntarabhūtaudanaśikhaṇḍakrasādhanatvena taṇḍujabalvajā vivacyante tadā tṛtīyāntapadabhājo bhavanti /
yadā tu bhojanayogyaudanāvasthā pariṇatirūpeṇa taṇḍulā māīvotpatyarthaṃ ca śikhaṇḍakā kāreṇa balvajā dṛśyante /
tathā vedavākyāvagataguṇabhāvāśca te dravyamādhanake 'gnihotre sukhaṇḍitāstiṣṭhanto ramaṇīyatvātkasyāścid brāhmaṇyāḥ svakarmmaśobhādarśanārthaṃ taṇḍunnā homasaṃbadhitvenābhipretāḥ /
saivaṃ preṣyati guṇakāmā vā yajamāna taṇḍunnāndya juhudhīti, tadā dvitīyārthabhākkaṃ bhavati bhavati hi loke bahuprakārā vivaśceti /
guṇabhūte 'pyarthe kena ci tkāraṇena kaścitprādhānyāṃśo vivacyate tathā pradhānabhūteṣu guṇāṃśaḥ /
kaḍhā cidubhau kaढ़ā cinnobhau /
na ca yadvivacyate ta cchabdenā bhidhātavyamityasti pramāṇaṃ, vivakṣāsaṃpattyarthaṃ tu lakṣaṇādyupāyāntarāśrayaṇaṃ na svārthatyāgaḥ /
tasmātprādhānyameva dvitīyārthaḥ /
kathaṃ tu sakkādiṣu guṇatvamiti /
taducyate 
dvitīyā tāvatkarmatvaṃ pradhāna rūpamātmaśaktyā vadati tatvica bannavratā kāraṇāntareṇa virudhyamānatvānnāśrīyate /
tena tū kāraka viśeṣātmakatvādyatkārakamāmānyamavinābhūtaṃ ucyate tada dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
viruddhatvādvivacyate/
tatraitāvānartho vijñāyate homasya kārakaṃ saktava iti /
na ca sāmānya nirviśeṣa vyavahārakṣamamiti viśeṣāpeśśāyāṃ karaṇatvaṃ bhaviṣyati /
dravyāṇāṃ karmmasaṃyogaiti bhūtabhavyamamuccāraṇanyāyāt /
kathaṃ punaḥ saktuprādhānya vivakṣā viru dhyate /
tatrāha 
yasya hi dravyasya va cidupayogo nirvṛtto bhaviṣyatīti vā 'vadhārthyate tatsaṃskārāītvātkarmma prati prādhānyaṃ pratipadyate /
yatpunarnopayuktaṃ nopayocyate vā tasya saṃskāro niṣprayojana iti tadvidhānavākyānarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ /
tecāmo saktavo na homātprāgupayujyante nova~ bhamma mādbhāvādbhasma viniyogavacanābhāvācca /
tasamastaṃ vākyamanarthakaṃ bhavata dvitīyā vā lakṣaṇa /
vṛtteti, sthita tvāhedaprāmāṇyasya lakṣaṇā grahītavyā /
mukhyārthaprayogo dyotsargikatvādapavādadarśanena bhrāntitvaṃ pratipadyate /
sarvatraiva lakṣaṇāśrayaṇamānarthakyaprasaṅganimittam /
anyathā mukhyārthopapatteḥ /
tena virodhātmaktu sādhanakahoma vidhānaṃ prakaraṇasaṃbandhi gṛhyate /
nanu saktūnāmapi iti homavantaḥ saktatropi jyotiṣṭomasyopakṛtyārthavanto bhavivyantītyāha /
siddhāntavādī tu chanjena homasādhanībhūtānāme vārthavattvamabhyupagacchati ko vā brūne neti /
sarvatraiva ca 
yathā homaḥ kriyātmakatvātkimityapekṣamāṇaḥ pradhānakathaṃbhātantravārtika /
venetya manugrā cakatvena gṛhyate naivaṃ dravyam /
na ca tasmādadṛṣṭakarūpanā kriyānirvarttyatvādapūrvāṇām /
yatrāpi tāvad dravyaṃ sājhātphalāya caudyate yathā godohanena paśukāma iti tatrāpyanyaprayojanakriyādvāramantareṇa nāpūrvaṃ bhaviṣyati /
kimuna yadā na kasya cidaṅgatvena saktavaḥ śrūyante /
na ca kiṃ citkalpanāpramāṇamasti /
dvitīyeti cet /
na hītyuttaram /
dvitīyā hi saktūnāṃ prādhānyaṃ vadantī homaṃ tadarthaṃ kuryyānna saktubhyo 'pūrvamiti pravipattim /
tena dvitīyāprasādādbhaveḍḍomaḥ sakkarthaḥ /
kathaṃ nāma homavyāptāḥ saktavaḥ syuriti /
nānyammai prayojanā yā śravaṇa /
te cāmo bhavanti home kute saktavo homasambadvā iti prāgeva prayojanalābhātparthyavasitā dvitīyā niṣprayojaneṣvapi, homaṃ prati prādhānyamātreṇa karmmatva siddheḥ /
tatra siddhe vākyārthe paścānna puruṣasya kratorvopayujyantaiti jñātvā tadvacanādvā'dṛṣṭaṃ kalpyeta prādhānyajñānaṃ vā bhrāntiriti /
tatrāi /
na tadvacanācchakyamanyatkalpayitumiti/
prādhānyāvivaśva nyāyyā/
tataśva tṛtīyārthasiddiriti matvā mahābhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ tṛtīyāyāḥ sthāne dvitīyeti /
tena vaiṣamyaṃ homasaṃmārgayoḥ, saktūnāṃ niṣprayojanatvena tadarthatvātpuroḍāmādeśvānyaśeṣabhāvena parthyagnikaraṇa/disaṃskārāītvāt /
dṛḍhe ca śāstrārthe 'vasthite dṛṣṭopakārābhāve'pyadṛṣṭa kalpanā bhaviṣyati /
loke'pyadṛṣṭārthāḥ saṃskārā ācārādgamyanta yathā gra/māntarādāgatānāṃ śāntyarthamagninnavaṇadadhyaścataprabhṛteḥ śirasa uparibhrāmaṇaṃ śacideśapratiṣṭhāpanaṃ ca /
na cāsyānupapattirācāraprāmāṇyāt /
tenādṛṣṭārthānāmapi tulyaśrutitvātmiko guṇabhāvaḥ /
nanvevaṃ sati sarvatra prayojanavattā kṛtameva dravyaprādhānyamiti na vaktavyaṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
mulya śrutitvāditi, darśayitavye vā yatra prayojanavattā nirapekṣaṃ dvitīyākṛtameva prādhānyaṃ kevalaṭatīyākṛto vā guṇabhāva iti /
taducyate /
prādhānyaṃ tāvadaindryā gāīpatyamupatiṣṭhataityatra liṅgādindrārthatvāvagateḥ gāīpatyaikavākyatvācca tātmādhana kendropasthānaprasaṅge kevala dvitīyākṛtameva gāīpatyaprādhānyam /
tathā sūkta vākena prastara mityubhayoḥ prayojanavattvāviśeṣe kevalaḍhatīyākṛ sūktabākasya prastarapraharaṇāṅgatvaṃ tena vibhaktibhirevāṅgāṅgibhāve 'bhidhīyamāne niṣprayojanatvamapavādo na tu prayojanasadasadbhāvenāṅgāṅgitvamiti vivekaḥ /
prayojanaṃ tvadhikaraṇasya na samyaganumanyante /
tathā hi 
hyutpattivākyā kevala pradhānārthatvena jñāyamānā yuktaṃ yadaṅgeṣu na bhavantoti /
śamīmayatvādi tu srugādimātrānuvādena vidhīyamānaṃ sarveṣāṃ vā śeṣatvasyātatprayuktatvā dityanena vākyasaṃyogabalīyastvātprakaraṇagamya pradhānārthatvabādhenāṅgapradhānārthaṃ vijñāyate /
na cātra viśeṣaṇaṃ kiṃ cidupāttaṃ yena pradhānaga tasrugādimātrapratītiḥ syā, tsadapi voddiśyamānaviśeṣaṇatvānna vivacyeta /
tasmātpūrvapace 'pi yāni ca pradhānasaṃvandhīni khugādīni yāni cārādupakārakasaṃmārgādisaṃbandhīni tāni sarvāṇi śamomayītvādiyuktānītyayukto nānāvṛścanuksaṃmārgaḥ /
syādetat mukhyārtho vāṅgasyācoditatvāditi vaikṛtaviśeṣāṇāṃ kevalapradhānārthatvānnehāṅgapradhānārthatā bhaviṣyatīti /
tadayuktam /
kutaḥ 
yajñātharvaṇaṃ vai kāmyā iṣṭayastā upāṃśu karttavyā iti hi pradhānaireva kāmya śabdopāttairupāṃśutvaṃ saṃbadhyamānamaṅgasyā coditamiti vacyate, na cātra tādṛśaḥ pradhānasaṃyoga iti vaiṣamyam /
nanu cātideśikatvāda prāptāvastheṣvaṅgeṣu śamīmayotvādyupadigyamānaṃ pradhānamātrārthaṃ bhavet /
nāītyevaṃ bhavitum /
evaṃ hi sthāsthati 
avaśyaṃ cānekārthavidhyanupapatteḥ srugādīnyanuvaditavyāni te na pratyakṣopi sannupadeśo 'tideśaṃ tāvatpratīcate /
tatra yāvatā kālena pradhānassrugādīni prāpnuvanti tāvataivāṅgasrugādīnyapītyaviśeṣaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
ya eva hi saṃmārgasucī varjjanopāyastenaiva prayājādisrugvarjanamapi prāpnoti, na caitadiṣṭaṃ yuktyabhāvāt /
yadyapi ca kiṃ citpradhānamātra saṃbandha kāraṇaṃ bhavettathāpi saumikavedidakṣiṇānyāyena prasaṅgasiddhenaṃ prākṛtajātyupasaṃgraho yujyate /
kiṃ ca 
paridhirityagniparidhānārthaṃ dravyamucyate /
tathā homādyarthā juṅkādayastatra saṃmārgasyārthābhidhānakarmma cetyaprayojakatvamapi śakyaṃ vaktum/
tataśca bāṇavatparidhiśravaṇe yadi tāvadaparicitādvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
neva palāśādīnāṃ mārṭi apariṣaya eva saṃsṛṣṭā bhaveyuḥ /
atha tānapi pariddhīta,tataḥ kṛte paridhāne prākṛtārthatā na syāt /
na ca tulyārthānāṃ samuccayo dṛṣṭaḥ /
tasmānna paridhyantaramutpādanīyam /
avabhṛthasya tvapūrvatvādyāvadaktamātra parthyavasāyinaḥ sāṅgasya cāpsu coditasya kena saṃmārge 'gnirvā prāpnoti yenotpādyeta /
tasmā daprayojanānyetāni /
tasyodāharaṇaṃ tvekaṃ satyam /
tatra hi māṃsaṃ tu savanīyānāmiti sidvāntātpuroḍāśamātreṇā saṃvadhyamānaṃ tara samayatvamasavanīyatvānna parthyagnikaraṇapuroḍāśena saṃbadhyate /
na hi savanīyāṅge savanīyaśabdaprayogaḥ /
savanasaṃbandhivi ṣayatvāt /
savanīyāṅgasya cāsavanārthatvāttatrāpi tu vrīhimayatvaṃ durlabham /
brohibhiryajataiti pradhānapuroḍāśamātreṇa teṣāṃ saṃvandhāt /
evaṃ tarhyaniyatadravyakatā paryagnikaraṇapuroḍāśasyeti pra yojanam /
tadapyayuktam /
tathā sati kāṃsyabhojinyāyena tarasamayaparthyagnikaraṇenaiva śāstrārthopapatteḥ siddhāntārthasadṛśakarmaprasaṅgaḥ /
tasmātkathaṃ citprakṛtī brīhimayapuroḍāśaya hāttatmādhanatvaṃ śāstrakatatvātprāpnotīti vaktavyam /
tatrāpi tvekacāyanīnyāyenāprayojakatvāt tadabhāve lopaprasaṅgaḥ /
tena etadeva prayojanamityāśrayaṇīyam /
aniyata vyakatvaṃ vā /
na cāṃtra kāṃsyabhojinyāyaḥ saṃbhavati /
māṃsena puroḍāśatvānabhivyaktaḥ/
savanīyapuroḍāśe kathamiti cet /
naiva tatra puroḍāśatvamiṣṭaṃ vacanādapuroḍāśātmakameva māṃsaṃ puroḍāśasya sthāne vidhīyate yathā dhānādīnām /
na hi kathaṃ cidapi māṃsena dhānādayo bhavanti /
ataśca praiyaṅgavanyāyena pradhānamātre māṃsena puroḍāśo nivarttitaḥ /
paryagnikaraṇaṃ tu puroḍa śa sādhana kamevā sattvaniyatadravyako tantravārtike /
vā kathaṃ ciddhā prakṛtidarśanena brīhiyavadravyakaṃ iti sthitam /
etāni ca prayojanāni khuksamārgasya prakṛtau bahasādhanatvāt kapiñcalanyāyena tritvasya śāstrīyatvāt pātrāvivṛdvāvapi paśucāturmāsyeṣu tisra eva saṃmāṭa̭ntyāḥ pūrvapakṣe /
siddhānte tu sarvāḥ, saṃskārasya pratipradhānāvarttitvāt /
tathā paśunyāyena vivakṣitaikasaṃkhyatvāt eka eva saṃmārṭavyaḥ paridhiḥ pūrvapakṣe /
siddhānte tu sarve /
yatra ca paridhivivṛddhistatra viśeṣaḥ /
evamekapuroḍāśe paryagnikaraṇaṃ sarvapuroḍāśe ca vaktavyam /
tathāpi viṣaye laukikaṃ syādityevamagnimupanidhāya stuvataitiva/
ki kāgnisaṃmārgakaraṇaṃ pūrvapakṣe /
siddhānte tu tasyāprayojanatvenāsaṃskārthyatvātsarveṣāmā havanīyādīnāmiti viśeṣaḥ /
stutaśatrayostu saṃskāro yājyāva d devatābhidhānatvāt 
yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrghyaṃtaityasyāpavādatvena stotraśastropanyāsaḥ /
stutireva stotraṃ śavamapi saivāpragotamantra sādhyā guṇaguṇisavandhakorttanaṃ ca stutiḥ śiṣyate/
sā ca prathamaṃ guṇaguṇibhyāṃ nirvarttyate /
tadabhāve śabdoccāraṇamātrasya stutitvāvyapadeśāt /
tatra guṇānāṃ tāvadakammāṅgatayā niṣprayojanatvādekāntena stutyarthatā/
tannirvarttitā tu stutiḥ kiṃ stutyasya smārakatvena śeṣībhavatyata svaprādhānyenādṛṣṭārthā bhavatīti /
kiṃ prāptam 
yadyatrāvidyamānārtho mantraḥ stotuṃ prayujyate /
tasyārthenāpakṛṣṭatvātprāptabādhaḥ prasajyate 
ya eva hi abhivatībhirindraḥ sṭṛyate sa eva māhendragraheṇejyate tatra satyevārthe kimityapakarṣaḥ syāt /
na ca yāvatkarmāṅgabhūterthe vidyate tatsarvaṃ mantreṇābhidhātavyaṃ, nyūnamadhikaṃ vā 'sau yadabhidhātuṃ samarthastadabhidhatte /
tena nirguṇendraprakāśanaṃ guṇasyātantratvātprakaraṇalabhyatvādā nirguṇadravyaprakāśanavadeva 
na śrutisamavāyitvāt 
naitadasti nirguṇendrābhidhānādanutkarṣa iti /
prasajyata evotkarṣaḥ /
kutaḥ 
yadyavayavavyutpattyā mahāṃśvāsāvindraśceti evaṃ mahendra śabdamancācaścāṇaistadvitānugamaḥ kriyeta, tata indra eva guṇamā viśi ṣṭo'sya grahasya devateti gamyeta /
na tvevamasti samudāyaprasivibanlīyastvenendravyatiriktarūḍhiśabdābhidheyamahendrapratītaḥ /
tathā hi /
vyutpādyate mahendra śvedākyabhedādi duṣyati /
avyutpattī mahendrārthaḥ sphuṭaṃ vastvantaraṃ bhavet 
'samarthaḥ padavidhiḥ' /
'samarthānāṃ prathamāhe'ti ca samāsatadvitavṛtyorviśeṣaṇam /
atastadabhāva naikayā 'pi bhavitavyam /
yadi yugapatmamāsatadvitāvanvākhyāyete tato naikatrāpi sāmarthya labhyate /
kutaḥ 
ekārthobhāvalacaṇaṃ vyapebālakṣaṇaṃ vā sāmarthyamubhayathā'pi sāpekṣasya nāvakalpate /
katham /
anya vastvanapecanve hyanye nai kārthateṣyate /
sāpekṣastvanyavicipto naikāthya~ pratipadyate 
vyapekṣā punarāhatya vigatāpekṣatocyate /
sāpeśatve va dūre 'sāvityevamasamarthatā 
krameṇākhyāyamāneṣu vākyabhedo 'maka chuteḥ /
kṛtvā samāsamuccāya~ punaḥ śabdadvayaṃ bhavet 
mahendra iti hi syānna cendra viśeṣaṇaṃ mahattvam /
na hyupasarjanamabhibhūta svārthavṛtti viśeṣaṇāntaraiḥ saṃyujyate, na ca samāsārthe vṛttasyeti vākyabheda mātreṇaivocyate/
tena kramavṛttirapi nāstoti pratipādya punargyugapadvṛttimeva doṣāntarābhidhitmayopanya tantravārtike/
syati /
aikaśabdye parārthavadityanena nyāyenendraśabdasya mahattvataddhitā /
prati vairupyanimittavākyabhedaprasaṅgaḥ /
vidhyanekavyāpārātmakaśvāparo vākyabhedaḥ /
tathā hi 
vyapadeśācca 
vyapadeśabhedācca bhedaḥ /
evaṃ ca mantrayorvyavasthā bhaviṣyati /
itarathā vikalpe po bādhaḥ syāt /
asati cārthabhede mantrabheda syādṛṣṭārthatā prasajyeta 
evaṃ vyākhyāyamāne tu ruḍhive tadvite sati /
agnīṣomādayaḥ sarve rūḍhitvānna didevatāḥ 
mahadindra śabdayostāvadavaśyaṃ pṛthagarthābhidhānaśaktiḥ kalpayitavyā /
tayośca guṇaguṇyabhidhāyitvādviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyātmakatvamavadhāritam/
tatra yāvadeva saṃhatābuccāritau tāvadeva pūrvānubhūtārthasaṃbandhitayā viśiśarthapratyayo jāyate /
na cāsya nivarttakaṃ kiṃ cidasti /
na ca samudāyasyā pūrva śaktyantarakalpanāpramāṇaṃ vidya santravārtike /
te /
labdhātmikā ca samudāyaprasiddhiravayavaprasiddhiṃ bādhate /
na cāvayavārtharahitārthāntaraprayogaṃ vispaṣṭamantareṇa tadātmanābhaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
pratyakṣepi tāvadarthe 'nekaśabdaśaktaḥ kalpanā niṣpramāṇikā, kimuta yatrārtha sadbhāvo 'pi kalpanīyaḥ /
tadihendra śabdaprayogānyathānupapatyendrastāvadadṛṣṭo 'pi kalpyate, tatra yadi punamahendraśabdaprayogānyathā'nupapattirbhavettatorthāntaraṃ mahendro nāma ka lapyeta /
yadā tu pūrvakalpitābhyāmeva mahadindrapadaśaktibhyāṃ prayogaḥ sidhyati, sa eva cārthaḥ kiṃ cidviśiṣṭa pratyabhijñāyate, kastadārthāntaraṃ kalpayituṃ śakṣyati /
tasmādindra eva mahattvaviśiṣṭo mahendro nānya iti siddham/
naca samāsaṃ kṛtvā tadvite kriyamāai kasya cidasāmarthyaṃ samāsavelāyāṃ tadvitavelāyāṃ cāpekṣaṇīyārthāntarānupādānāt /
na ca dviruccāraṇanimittavākyabhedaprasaktiḥ sakaduccāritaikapadopāttānekārthakathanāt /
vṛttiyātmakaṃ hi māhendrapadam /
ekaikā ca vṛttirvākyārthe varttate /
tatra ya yorvākyayorathā māhendrapanopātau tau tābhyāṃ nirbhidya kathyete /
yaccātrāsakṛduccāraṇaṃ dṛśyate na tadvedavacanasyaiva /
na hi kadā cidapyevaṃrūpo vedo 'sti mahāṃcāsāvindraśca mahendro devatā asyeti māhendraḥ /
na caitadeva vaidikaṃ padamevaṃ vibhajyate vibhāgasya pauruṣeyatvenāvaidikatvāpatteḥ /
kiṃtu 
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
vicitraśaktīni hi padāni ekānekapadārthapratīteḥ /
tathaiṣāmarthakathanaṃ kadā citpadenaivānyena kriyate kadācidvākyena, tenāpyekenāne kena vā dvipadena bahupadena veti vaicityam /
tadyathā kaḥ pikaḥ kokinaḥ ka aupagavaḥ upagorapatyam /
upagunā vā svakāntāyāmutpāditaḥ /
tathā pacatītyukte pākaṃ paragāmi phacamekaḥ karttā pūrvāparībhūtaṃ varttamānakāle nirvarttayatīti kathyate /
na caivaṃ kathayatāṃ vākyabhedaḥ prasajyate /
na vā śabdārthatvamadhyavasīyate /
evameva yadi māhendrapadopātto 'rthastadaspṛśabhireva śabdaśaktividbhiḥ puruṣaiḥ skhavākyenaikenānekena vā ka thyate kastatra vākyabhedaḥ, śatakṛtvo 'pi hi svavākyamuccāryamāṇaṃ na vedaṃ dūṣayati /
na ca tadīyo 'rthaḥ kathyamānaḥ pauruṣeyatvaṃ bhajate /
avaśyaṃ cāneko 'rthaḥ puruṣai /
kathyamānaḥ krameṇa kathayatavyaḥ, so 'pi ca prakṛtipratyaya paurvāparyeṇetyevaṃ kathyate /
māṃsvāsāvindraścetyādi /
na caivaṃ sāpeścatvam /
atha vā bhavati vai pradhānasya sāpeścasyāpi samāsa iti yadyapīndra śabdastadvitāpeśastathā'pi mahattvaṃ prati prādhānyāllabhate samāsam /
ataśca yugapadapecāyāmavirodhastathā 'pi tu vṛttiḥ krameṇaiva /
kutaḥ 
tena yatraiva pradhānaṃ sāpekṣaṃ tatraitayaiva tāvad vṛttyā bhavitavyamiti samāsa eva prathamaṃ bhavati /
yadi vā kṛtvā samāsaṃ tantreṇa vṛtiriṣyeta, tataḥ śad indrastadvitasaṃbandhī śuddhaśva samāsabhāgiti nirguṇasyaivendrasya devatātvāpatterguṇānarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ /
na cendramahattvayoryugapattadvitārthe nipatitayoraruṇaika cāyanyādivatparasparasampravārtike /
niyamo labhyate/
na hyakriyāyāṃ yugapatmannipāto nāpi viśeṣavaśīkārasāmarthyam /
satyapi ca dvandvadevatāpattiḥ /
akṛtasamāsayośca mahadindra śabdayorane katvādvivakṣitaikasaṃkhya prātipadikanimittataddhita saṃbandhābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
tasmānna yugapadvṛttiḥ, iti kramavṛttyā samāsārthasyaiva devatātvam/
ataścendra eva guṇasaṃyukto mahendro nārthāntaramiti pūrvapaca eva śobhana ityanyaduttaraṃ vācyam 
yadyapyabhinno'rthastathāpi vidhiśabdasya mantratve bhāvaḥ syāditi mahendra śabdenaivoccamānasyāsmin grahayāge devatātvaṃ nānyathā /
tatra sakalaparyyāyeṇāpi buidindrādiśabdeno camānasya devatātvaṃ na bhavati kimuta nyūnenaivendraśabdena /
tathā hi 
kutaḥ 
ācāryo mātuśceti dravyaikatve 'pi dṛśyate /
apekṣā hetubhedena vyavahāraḥ pṛthaktayā 
guṇaścānarthakaḥ syāt 
yadi cādimānanādirvā guṇaḥ kevala mindrastutyarthamevopāḍhīyate na devatātve'ntarbhavati, tato''syopādānamevānarthakaṃ syāt /
sarvā ddi devataivamarthamabhidhīyate vidhīyate vā, kathaṃ nāma taduddetantravārtika /
śena karmma kriyeteti /
yadi ca avihite vihite ca guṇe kevalenendreṇa vyavahriyate tato nārtho guṇābhidhānena /
kiṃ ca 
na hi grahasaṃbandha indrasya prāpto, yena tadgatendrānuvādena maha tvaṃ kevalameva stutyarthamucyeta /
na ca mahānindraḥ prāpto yato guṇenopajacya vidhoyeta/
tasmādaprāpta vidherchevatāntaratā /
tathā yājyāpurorucoḥ 
pūrvavanmantravyapadeśabheda vyavasthā 
yatreti vā 'rthavattvāt syāt 
balavatpramāṇavirodhe saṃskārapakṣastyajyeta, na ca so'sti, ciṅgabalīyastvā dutkarṣasiddherityaparyudāsaḥ saṃskārapakṣasya 
anutkṛṣyamāṇa eva vā pragāthaḥ sannidhivaśādavayavadvāreṇa ma hendramavirodhāya harārthatvāya ca prakāśayiṣyati, yathā 'gnīṣomoye manotāyāmagniśabdaḥ prakaraṇātmamāmasthaḥ pratīyamānaḥ sādvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
icaryyātsomamapi pratipādayanmamudāyārtho vijñāyate /
ataścānutkarṣe 'pyadoṣa iti 
na hi yamādonāṃ grahāntareṣvapi devatātvaṃ yenendravadutkṛṣṭairmantraiḥ prakāṇyeran /
atasteṣāṃ tāvadvidhyānarthakyaprasaṅgādavaṇyamadṛṣṭārthatvena bhaktivyam /
tataśca tatmāmānyāditareṣu tathātvaṃ, tamānna saṃskāra karmmatvamiti 
maṇḍūkasūktasyāgnau prayogaḥ, tatra maṇḍūkenāgnivikarṣaṇāmnānāt /
akṣavaktasya rājasvaye, tatrācaivyatīti vidhānāt/
mūṣikā vaktasyaikādaśinyām, ākhaste paśurityupaśaya saṃbandha saṃ kīrttane sati tadvāreṇopaśayasyaiva stutiḥ /
kuṣumbhakasūktādīnāṃ tu yadi kvacidviśeṣarūpeṇārtho nāsti tataḥ sāmānya vidhānenārthavattā bhaviṣyati /
vācaḥ stome sarvamantropadeśāt /
tathā ''śvine sūryodayāvadhi samāptyasaṃbhave sarvāsāmṛcāmupadeśāt /
tatra vacanenaivāsamavetārthamantravidhānasāmarthyāda gatera dṛṣṭārthāśrayaṇaṃ, na cakka cidadṛṣṭārthatvena sarvacaiva dṛśyamānamapyarthaṃ procādṛṣṭārthatvakalpanā yujyate /
tathā hi 
api vā śrutisaṃyogātmakaraṇe stautiśaṃsatī kiyotpatti vidadhyātām 
yaduktaṃ manotāyāmivāgniśabda indraśabdassamāsārthaṃ lakṣayighyatīti/
tadayuktam/
kutaḥ /
etasmādeva doṣāt /
na candra śabdasya svārthamabhidadhataḥ kaścidvirodho yena śrutirvṛttiṃ jahyāt /
sarvā dṛṣṭārthānāṃ ca yathā kathaṃ cimacāyā dṛṣṭārthatvāpādanasaṃbhavādayuktametat /
yattūktam utkṛṣyatāmeveti tadayuktam 
prakṛtastotraśeṣatvaṃ śrutyā sannidhiklṛptayā /
vinā sāmānya saṃbandhālliṅgaṃ cāviniyojakam 
evaṃ ca saptamī ṣaṣṭhī dvitīyā stautiśaṃsatī /
prativṛttā bhaviṣyanti tvatpaśce 'nyārthavṛttayaḥ 
prakāśanaṃ punaḥ paramārthatastāvadātmāghāram /
karmmatvapratipa tyuttarakālaṃ ca vyāpyatvāddevatādhāram /
tatra kavatīnāmaikāntikameva karaṇatvamiti vaiṣamyam /
api ca stauti śaṃsatīti stutibhāvanā pūrvāparībhūtā śrūyate /
tasyāṃ ca dhātvarthaḥ karaṇabhūtaḥ śeṣāṇi ca kārakāṇi nityaṃ dhātvarthaṃ niṣpādayanti saṃvadhyante /
ta yadi mantrāḥ stotranivṛttyarthā bhavanti tato'peścitārthaṃkaraṇācchādṛṣṭamarthaṃ kurvanto dṛṣṭarthā  bhavanti /
prakāśanaṃ tu kurvanto 'coditakṛtvādadṛṣṭārthā bhaveyuḥ /
tataśca varaṃ stṛtīnāmeva dṛṣṭārthatvam /
kiṃ ca 
śabdapṛthatkkāca 
pṛthakkaniveśinī dvidvādaśasaṃkhyā na prakāśanābhede sati śabdenocyate /
sāmānyāvivakṣāyāṃ vā pratyakṣaṃ pratipadaṃ ca tannirvṛttena dādaśatve 'vatiṣṭhate /
nanu ca stutāvapi tulyametat /
tathā hi 
atha stomavaśāhaksamudāyamādhyāḥ stutayo gaṇyante tathā prakāśanānyapītyaviśeṣaḥ 
kiyāḥ phalāpavargiṇyastatsaṃkhyā gaṇanāssadā /
apūrvādaśatvācca dvādaśatvaṃ nirūpyate 
anarthakaṃ ca tadvacanam 
ṛcāmanūhyatvādāgneyagraha codanayaivāgneyīnāṃ stutisādhanatvasiddheḥ āgneyoṣu stuvataityanarthakaṃ vacanam 
abhivānaṃ ca karmmavat 
yadidaṃ dvitīyāpratipādita karmmā īmabhidhānamidaṃ cāparaṃ prādhānye kāraṇam/
pradhānakriyā hi kena cipeṇetā agnihotraṃ juhotyāghāramāghārayatītivadbhavati, na saṃskāra kriyā 'tyantaguṇabhūtatvāt /
atha vā stotra śastrasamākhyayoramidhānatvaṃ tatprādhānyajñāpanārtham /
itarathā hi prakāśanamityevaṃ samākhyā syāt /
avahantyāḍhivadā naiva bhavet 
devataiva pradhānatvātphalaṃ yācyeta karmmavat /
na svāmini sthite kaściddāsātprārthayate phalam 
na karmmāntaratāstyatra banavatpratyabhijñayā /
na copātto guṇaḥ kaścinna ca vākyāntare stutiḥ 
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
na hyatra viśeṣa heturasti kiṃ brāhmaṇavihitamāsādyopacatavidhiśaktimantraḥ smārako bhavatyatha vā viparyaya iti /
tatrobhayoranuvādatvāsaṃbhavādgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvāca iyorapi vidhāyakatvam /
abhyāsācca karmabheda syāt /
bannavatpratyabhijñāyāsvābhyāsādhikaraṇaṇvottaraṃ bhaviṣyati /
tasmānnaivamabhidhāyakatvasiddhiḥ /
ye pyājaḥ 
tairapi sāmānyatohamācaṃ vyarṣādiṣṭam /
kutaḥ /
vidhiśaktiniyogena na mantrasyāpanīyate 
vidhāyakaṃ sadapyarthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ smārayiṣyati /
mantratastu virodhe syāditya caita dvadiṣyate 
api vā prayogasāmarthyānmantotantravārtika /
'bhidhānavācī syāt 
asti tṛtīyaḥ prakāro yadabhidhāyakatvaṃ nāma /
paṇya 
mantragatānāṃ brāhmaṇagatānāṃ cākhyāta śabdānāṃ yeṣāṃ śabdāntareṇa vidhiśaktirapagacchati teṣāmabhidhāyakatvam /
tatra natā naśantītyatra nāvadyacchabdopahito vidhāyako'nuvādatvaṃ prārthayate /
tathā ahe buniya mantraṃ me gopāyetyāmantraṇa vibhatyā /
dāmi gṛhṇāmītyuttamapuruṣeṇa /
yadi somamapacara yuriti yadiśabdena /
te caivamādayaḥ prāyeṇa mantreṣviti mantrā udāharaṇam/
avidhāyakā mantrā iti ca prasiddhiḥ /
brāhmaṇe tu bhūyomaḥ pratyayā vidhāyakāstena tadvidhāyaka miti prasiddham /
arūpe tvavidhāyakā iti tadiha nodācaraṇam/
vidhāyakatvāvidhāyakatve tu tayoryathoktameva kāraṇamiti na mantratvabrāhmaṇatvayorvyāpāraḥ /
tatra tvetāvān vyāpāro  dṛśyate /
rūpādeva brāhmāgatānāṃ vidhitvanivṛttau satyā nimittādipratyāyanārthatā /
na hi teṣāṃ rūpaṃ karmasu prayogāīm /
mantragatānāṃ tu rūpamevopalabhya dāmi gṛhṇāmi nirvaprāmīdamidaṃ ca karomyagnīnvihara bardistṛṇohi imidaṃ ca kurvityādikaṃ śakyametaiḥ karmma smarttumiti viniyogabuddhirbhavati 
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
na tāvaḍhanuṣṭhāna vecāyāmasmṛtaḥ kaścitpadārthaḥ śakyaḥ ka trumityavaśyaṃbhāvinyā smṛtyā yogyasādhanamātrāpekṣaṇādya kiṃ cid brāhmaṇapadārthānusaṃdhānaṃ vā pūrvapadārthapratyavekṣaṇaṃ vā sūtragrantho vā ''tmīyagrahaṇavākyāni vā upadraṣṭādi  vā sādhanaṃ grahītumārabhyate /
tatrānanyaprayojanānmantrānprakaraṇe padyamānānmāmānyena kimapyebhiḥ karttavyamityevaṃ prayogavacanena gṛhyamāṇānupalabhya yādṛśena vākyena smṛtiḥ karttumākācyate taṭrpā etaiti viditvā liṅgaprakaraṇānumitayā śrutyā viniyoge satyabhidhānārthatā vijñāyate /
tataścopāyāntarāṣya pramāṇakatvānnivarttante /
niyamādṛṣṭasiddhiśca mantraireva smṛtvā kṛtaṃ karmābhyudayakāri bhavatītyavadhāryyate /
bhāṣyamapyacaiva yojanīyam /
nāma kṛḍhapyuccāraṇe tatpratyayāditi na prāptatvābhiprāyeṇocyate /
kiṃ tu yacchabdopabandhādasyaiva mantrākhyātasyānyataḥ prāptamacaṃ bravomotyevaṃrūpapratyayāt /
śatakṛtvo'pi hyevamādiruccāryyamāpāḥ svasāmarthyenaiva nāpūrvapratyayaṃ karoti tata eva pūrvaprāptabuddhyu tpādāt 
ṛṣayo 'pi hi lakṣyāṇāṃ nāntaṃ yānti pṛthatkaśaḥ /
lakṣaṇena ta siddhānāmantaṃ yānti vipaścitaḥ 
praiṣānveṣaṇapṛṣṭākhyānānuṣaṅgaprayogitāḥ /
sāmathyaṃ ceti mantrāṇāṃ vistaraḥ prāyiko mataḥ 
śeṣe brāhmaṇaśabdaḥ 
pariśeṣasidvatvādbrāhmaṇalakṣaṇamavacanīyamiti sūtramidamanārabhyamiti pratibhāti /
tatra śeṣaśabdaprayogāllakṣaṇānabhidhānācca sūtravyākhyānamevedamiti draṣṭavyam /
kimarthaṃ punaḥ sūtramārabhyate /
nārabhyeta yadi mantrabrāhmaṇātmaka eva veda iti sarveṣā prasiddhaṃ bhavet/
yeṣāṃ tvaprasiddhaṃ teṣāṃ tṛtīyādiprakāranirākarayārthaṃ hairāśyameva vedasyeti pratipādayitumāha śeṣe brāhmaṇaśadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
bda iti /
eka puruṣakarṭakamupākhyānaṃ parakṛtiḥ /
bahukarṭakaṃ purākalpaḥ/
yatrānyathārthaḥ pratibhātaḥ paurvāparthyālocanena vyavadhāyanyathā kalpyate sā vyavadhāraṇakalpanā /
tadyathā pratigṛhṇīyāditi śrutaṃ pratigrāhayediti kalpayiṣyate /
vidhilakṣaṇa mityatra brāhmaṇavācī vidhiśabdaḥ 
svādhyāye padyamāneṣu yeṣu mantrapadaṃ smṛtam /
te mantrā nābhidhānaṃ hi mantrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sthitam /
kiṃ punare kasminpade ūdyamāne samastasyaivāmantratvaṃ ūhitapadamātrasyaiva veti /
samastasyaiveti prāptam /
kutaḥ 
saṃpradāyakālāvagatarūpānyatvaṃ cetkena cidapyaṃśena jātaṃ na śakyate mantratvaṃ pratyabhijñātum /
athaikadeśepi tatmabhāvābhyupagamaḥ, tataḥ sarvacaiva mantrapadā viśeṣānmantratvaprasaṅgaḥ /
tasmādekavarṇāpāye 'pi mantratvābhāvātma mastatatkāryya nivṛttiḥ /
tataśca yathaiva tadvināśe sarvāvayavavarttini prāyaścittābhāvaḥ, evaṃ mantracchatantravārtika /
ndoviṣayatvena yāvantaḥ śabdaviśeṣāḥ smaryyante tainna bhavitavyamityekapadatadavayavohe tanmantragata sarvacchāndasopodvāreṇa laukika śabda prayogaḥ karttavya iti 
tāvanmātramevāmantra iti /
kutaḥ 
na hi gorgaḍuni jāte viṣāṇe vā bhagne gotvaṃ tirodhīyate tadabhivyakti samarthāvayavāntara sadbhāvāt /
kiyatyapi saṃsthāne śriyamāṇe sarvā vijñāyante /
sā ceyaṃ mantrākṛtirviśiṣṭa svaravarṇānupūrvyādyabhivyaktā na kiṃcidvikāradarśane nabhyatīti pratyayamupalabhāmahe /
tathā hi 
yatra vacanādvarṇalopaṃ vikāra vā kṛtvā prayogaḥ airaṃ kṛtvodgeyamityādau, yatra ca svādhyāyakānadṛṣṭa caisvarthyādiparityāgenaikaśrutyaṃ niyujyate na tatra kasya cinmantrabuddhirapaiti /
syādetadvacanasāmarthyādiha nāpaitīti 
yatra vaidikamanyatvaṃ tatra mantratva miṣyate /
nyāyena kalpyamāne tu na śakyaṃ tannirūpaṇam 
satyamūhasyāpi nāvaidikatvam /
ata evānāmnāteṣvamantratva mityucyate, vedabhāgo hi kaścitpratyacaḥ śrūyate, kaścidanumānādigamyaḥ /
pratyakṣa śrutaścānāta ityucyate /
tatra yatherāpadādīnāṃ viniyogaḥ śrūyate naivaṃ sūryyapadādīnām /
nanu saurthaṃ carumityetadeva śrutisamavāyitvāddevatāyāḥ sūryyapadasya viniyojaka śrūyate /
naitanmantre sūryyapadasya prakṣepaṃ bravīti iviṣastyāga kā lamātre taduccāraṇābhidhānāt /
yastu mantreṣu tatpraśśepaḥ so 'tideśakṛto bhaviṣyati /
na cātideśavacananyāyanabhyatvādevāmnāyate /
tasmādanāmnāta viniyojakatvādamantratvaṃ sūryapadādīnām /
nanvevaṃ sati pravaranāmadheyayoḥ pratyakṣopaṭe śānmantratvaprasaṅgaḥ /
syādevaṃ yadi tatsvarupamānāyeta, vacanārthaṃ tu jñātvā 'nāmnātayoreva pravaranāmnoḥ prayogāna mantratvanirūpaṇāyāmantargatiḥ /
evaṃ tarhi yatrāpi sarvanāmayuktamantrāmnāne sati tasya sthāne 'nyapadaprakṣepaḥ kriyate tatrāpyamantratā syāt /
tathā nāmeti ke cit /
atha vā viśeṣāṇāmānantyādayugapatkā natvācāmnā tumaśaktaḥ svarūpasya sarvanāmaprakāreṇāmnāna mastyevetyapūṭa nyasthānatvānmantrasya śakyamevaṃ nirūpaṇaṃ kartuṃ yadatra padaṃ nivecyate tadānayaṃ mantra iti /
itarathā hi sarvanāmnāmaprayogāītvādyadi viśeṣāmnānameva  tattanopāyeneti na gṛhyate, tatastadaṃśanyūnatvānmantrasvarūpasya vyarthameva sarvanāmāmnānaṃ syāt /
pravaranāmadheyavadeva tu vidhānāttadavakāśasthapadaprayogaḥ kalpyate /
tasmādevamādonyāmnātānyeveti mantradharmaiḥ saṃbadhyeran /
na tu pravarādīnāṃ mantrapāṭhakāle kaścidapi saṃsparśaḥ /
na ca brāhmaṇena rūpaṃ darśitaṃ yena pravacana lakṣaṇatvānmantratvādhyavasānaṃ bhavet /
ataśca vikṛtiṣvabhidhānārṣacoḍhakābhyāṃ sakane mantre prāptei yāvanmātramarthābhāvāyā vanyatpraścipyate tāvanmātrameva laukikam /
avaśiṣṭaṃ tu tathā prāptameva kratvākātipratyabhijñāyamānamantratvaṃ ceti na prāyaścittacchāndasaprayogairvajjainīyamiti siddham 
teṣāmṛgyatvārthavaśena pādavyavasthā 
pramaktāna prasaktyāpatitammṛgādilakṣaṇābhidhānam /
śabdārthasya vṛddhavyavahāragamyatvātkṛte 'pi talakṣaṇe tanmūlamabhiyuktopadeśadvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
meva darśayati /
kriyāpadānupādānādagniḥ pūrvebhirityaparthyavasite'rthe vṛttavaśena pāda vyavasthā /
nanu cāgnimīlaityapi samastā yā ṝca evārthavattvānnaiva pratipādamartha paryavasthati iti na vāyamarthavaśena pādavyavastheti /
kathaṃ na vācyam agnimīle purohita miti tāvatpratyakṣaṃ samāpto'rtho dṛśyate /
parayoḥ pādayosmātmādhūktamihārthavaśeneti /
etasya tu pradarśanārthatvānna vṛttavabhavyāvṛttirityaniṣidbaṭakkam 
gītiṣu sāmākhyā 
teṣāmityanuvarttate 
ekakhaṇḍena śabdena viśiṣṭo yatra gamyate /
viśeṣaṇasya vācyatvaṃ tatra sarvatra jāyate 
śeṣe yajuḥ śabdaḥ 
śeṣe brāhmaṇaśabda itivatsamastaṃ vyākhyeyam 
nigado vā caturtha syād dharmavi śeṣāt 
śeṣe yajuḥśabda ityetaḍyāvarttanārtho vāśabdaḥ /
caturthaṃ mantrajātaṃ nigaḍhaḥ syāt dharmānyatvāt /
yadi tāvaduccainniṃgadeneti vidhistato yajurddharmavādhī mā bhūḍhityarthāntaratvam /
athānuvādaḥ sa naiva prāpnoti vyatirekeṇa vineti bhedaḥ 
vacanād dharmmāviśeṣaḥ 
nyāyaprāpto caimmanuvāḍhatvajñānānna vidhānāditi vyākhyātam /
yaṃ tvete 'rthaṃ vadanti tamupāṃśutvena śaknuyurvaktumiti vacanādityucyate 
guṇārtho vyapadeśaḥ 
brāhmaṇa parivrājakavadbhupena vyapadeśabhedaḥ /
sarveṣāmiti cet 
atiprasaṅgadvāre guṇasya vyapadeśanimittatāṃ vyabhicārayati 
anyato'vagate 'rthe hi loka vākyaṃ pravarttate /tantravārtika /
tatraikārthatva vijñānātsukhabodhaikavākyatā 
nityavākyādhigamyatvādyathā vākyaṃ pravarttate /
vedārthastadasiddhesta na vākyasyārthavaśyatā 
vedavyākhyānapravṛttasya jaimineḥ kaḥ prasaṅgo laukikavākyacakṣaṇābhidhāne /
vaidikavākyalakṣaṇasyāpi bhedalacaṇe kaḥ prastāvaḥ /
kimarthaṃ pramāṇalakṣaṇaeva noktama /
ekaśabdaśca na vaktavyo 'rthaikatvādākyamityetāvataiva siddhatvāt /
kathaṃ ca mantrādhikāre tadasaṃbadbortho'bhidhīyate /
bhāṣyakṛtaśca praśliṣṭapaṭhiteṣu yajuḥsvityupanyāsaḥ pramāṇavānapi vinā kāraṇenātikrāntaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
ṛvasāmayostāvatparimāṇaṃ prayogasamarthaṃ prasiddha miti na kaśvidvākya lakṣaṇāde kavākyatālaṇādopakāro bhavati /
tathā brāhmaṇe'gnihotrādivākyaiḥ sādhyasādhanetikarttavyatāvatyāṃ bhābanāyāṃ niyukteṣu puruṣeṣvekāneka vākyajñānaṃ vopayujyate /
nanvayamupayoga, ekavākyatālaco vākyabhedaṃ paricariṣyati /
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
nāyamupayogaḥ /
kutaḥ 
padatadekadeśatamamahāvṛttiprasaṅgātmakasta dvibhāgalakṣaṇo vā vākyaikatvanānātvajñānanirapekṣaireva doṣatvenāvadhāryate /
vibhāgannaśraṇe gamyamānasaṃbandhaparityāgo 'nekādṛṣṭa kalpanā ca doṣaḥ itaratrāvṛtteraveḍhatvādaprāmāṇyam, iti naikavākyalakṣaṇenārthaḥ /
pauruṣeyavākye  tu lakṣaṇa nirapekṣamya lokasya vyavahārasiddheratyantānāpayikatvam /
yadi cārthekatvena vākyaikatvamavadhāryyate vākyasyāryapratyāyanārthatvāttatsvarūpaikatva jñānottara kālabhāvinā kiṃ vākyaikatvajñānena/
vaktṛṣṇāṃ ca parapratyāyanārtho vākyaprayoga iti nātmārthaṃ lacaṇajñānāpekṣā /
śrotṛṇāṃ punaratyantānavagate  'rthe pravarttamānaṃ puruṣavākyamapi na vedavākyā dbhidyate /
avagatārthaṃ tvanuvādatvādanādṛtyameveti naikāneka jñānamapecyate/
kimarthaṃ ca vaidikānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ noktam /
yadi tvarthāpatyoktameveti tanna /
tyātalamabhidhāyārthā pattyā laukikavākyasiddhirātrayitavyā /
na cārthāpattiḥ saṃbhavati/
na hyetalnau ki ka vākyalakṣajñānamīḍaśena vaidikavākya lakṣaṇena  vinā nopapadyate/
na cai tasyāpi vākyatā siddhā, vākyaikatvavaśenārthaikatva lakṣaṇātantravārtike /
rthāpattyupanyāmāt/
api ca kaḍhā civaidikānā madhyeta lannadāṇam/
atyantaviprakṛ॒ṣṭaṃ vā kiṃ cihnavedityāṅkitatvānna niyogato 'rthāpattiḥ/
na ca parisaṃkhyā, māmānya viśeṣabhedānupādānāt /
yadi hi sāmānyenedaṃ khanaka cidabhidhāya punaḥ kevanapai/rugheyasaṃbaddhamucyeta tataḥ parisaṃkhyāvaśena vaidikānāmiṭaṃ tāvanna bhavatotyetāvanmācaṃ gamyeta /
na tu laṇaviśeṣo'nekopalavāt /
evamapi hi vipayakalpanaṃ saṃbhavati, arthānekatvādekaṃ vākyaṃ nirākāṅkṣaṃ cedribhāge syāditi /
atha vārthakatvānnānāvākyatvamiti /
tasmādakalpaneyam /
kiṃ ca /
kathaṃ cārthānapeśatve vākyaikatvaṃ prasidhyati /
na hi varṇasvarūpeṇa jñātenaitannirūpyate 
tathā hi 
tasmātpadveṣu yāvatsu śrūyamāṇeṣu dṛśyate /
vispaṣṭa maikyamarthasya tāvatāmekavākyatā 
padārthaiḥ paḍhavijñātairvā kyārthaḥ pratipādyate /
lokaminna tatrāsti vākyaikatva nimittatā 
bhāvaneva ca vākyārthaḥ svakāraka viśeṣitā /
tasyāśca jāyate nityaṃ bhedaḥ śabdāntarādibhiḥ 
tantravārtike /
yātratā padasaṃghena smāryate yāgasādhanam /
tāvadyajuśca vākyaṃ ca vaktavyatvānnirūpyate 
ekārthatvaṃ padasya myātmākāṅkṣāvayavaṃ na tat /
sākāṅkṣāvayavaḥ saṃghastasyaiko'tha na vidyate 
dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
bhedo nāma padārthānāmavacchedaḥ parasparam /
sa ca pratipadārthatvānnaikatvaṃ pratipadyate 
ākṛtiparthapa śaktatvagotvayoḥ svarūpeṇābhihitayoḥ sa vidhānāditaretarānūrañjanamartha sadbhedaṃ vākyārthaḥ /
sa ca gove śuktatvasaṃsargaḥ śuklatve vā gotvasaṃmargaḥ sāmastyenai keka vyaktyu pasaṃcārādupacabhyataiti nānā/
yadyapi ca kathaṃ cid dvipade ma e vobhayatrāpi saṃsarga ityekatvaṃ gamyeta, tathāpi bahupada yena yena pradeśena paḍhadayaṃ saṃsṛjyate tena tena saṃsargarūpeṇopalavdhera nekatvam /
kiṃ ca 
yāvaddhi prayojanaikatvaṃ nāśrīyate tāvatsvatantrāḥ paḍhārthā naikatāmāpādayituṃ śakyante iti pṛthageva bhedasaṃmargāvanubhavanti /
a tasmādapi nānā /
yadyapi cāmmākamākṛtipadārthakatvānnaiva bhe dī vākyarthatvenābhipretastathāpi pūrvapakṣavādinā vikalpamātregopanyastaḥ /
sidvāntābhiprāyavivaraṇaṃ prayojanavā citvādarthaśabdasyopapannam/
evaṃ matyeka eva kaścitpadārthaḥ pradhānabhūtarūdviśeṣaṇatvanetaropādānamiti sarveṣāṃ ca tadbhedāttatsaṃmargāccai ko bhedaḥ saṃ sargo vetyapi śakyaṃ vaḍhituma tasmātkamamavāyitvena dṛṣṭārthatvādaśeṣamavitrādi padārthaviśiṣṭa nirvāpaprakāśanaṃ samastasya    paḍhamamūhasyaikaṃ prayojanamiti siddhamudāharaṇam /
parastu nirvā paprādhānyama jñātvā pṛcchati/
nanvatra devasyeti /
middhāntavādāca yadi nirvapāmītyanuṣaṅgalata evaṃ, ma cānuṣaṅgarudgaṇabhāvena bhavet, na cāsya guṇabhāvaḥ prayojanavattvāt /
mavicādīnāṃ cākarmasamavāyādityekārthatvam /
atha kimarthamubhayaṃ sūcitamiti /
yeṣāṃ saṃhatānāmeka prayojanatvaṃ teṣāṃ tadaśaktarvyastā nā mekāntenaiva sākāṅkṣatvaṃ bhavati icavācyaṃ tat/
atha vā vibhajyamānasākāṅkṣatvaṃ saṃhataikaprayojanatvena vinā na bhavati pratyeka kāryeṣu nirapekṣa pravṛttisiṅkeḥ /
ataḥ sākāṅkṣavibhāgenaive tarāśepāttanmādamevābhighātavyamiti pratyudāharaṇaṃ darśayati /
uccataiti /
puroḍāśavibhāgaprakāśanamekaṃ prayojanaṃ nirapekṣāṇāṃ dṛṣṭam /
nirvāpadattottarāpi vibhāganānātvaparicodanā saṃhatya viśeṣaṇānupādānātpunaḥ punaḥ prayuktasyānuṣaṅgadoṣābhāvā dupanyasyate/
tatrottaraṃ na tāvannirapejamādhanabhedāḍhapi kriyānānātvamiti vakṣyāmaḥ /
sādhanaprādhānya tu pratyuktameva /
etatkṛto viśeṣaḥ karmānaṅgatvādvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
danādaraṇīya iti sāmānya prakāśanādekārthatvam /
tasminmīdatyasya pūrvāpeścitve matyapi prayojanameda dvākyāntaratvam /
tasmāsaṃitayārava nakṣatvam 
sameṣu vākyabhedaḥ syāt 
yeṣāmadṛśyamāna karmma samavetārthatvena laiṅgikaviniyogābhāvena vacanādiniyogaḥ teṣāṃ prāgdṛṣṭārthamantrāvadhere kamantratvaṃ m /
tathā hi 
yadā hi bahadṛṣṭakalpanā niṣpramāṇikatyekamadṛṣṭaṃ mavebhyaḥ kalpitaṃ bhavati tadā pratyekaṃ tatsādhanagaktyabhāvāhibhajdamānamā kāṅgatvamapyatīti ekavākyatā /
kathaṃ punarasmin pratīkabhedena viniyoga iṣe tveti śākhāṃ chinatti ūrje tvetyanumātyevamādiḥ /
kathaṃ ca klṛptorvācayatīti bahutvanirdeśaḥ /
taducyate 
āḍhimadhyāvasānagrahaṇenaiko 'pi mantrastatra tatra viniyujyamāno 'pina pauḍyate  /
yāvadviniyogaṃ hi sakala āvattiṣyate khaṇḍasyāprayojanatvāt /
kalpata kalpatāmiti ca punaḥ punaḥ pra yogāṭekavākyatve 'pi bahuvacanāvirodhaḥ /
uccate/
naitadevam 
tiṣṭhatu tāvatprayojanakalpanam, viniyogavākyaṃ vā, na hi ta duttarakālaṃ svarūpanirūpaṇaṃ yuktam /
ajñātarūpasya viniyogāśakteraviniyuktasya ca prayojanakalapanānupapatteḥ /
tattannirapekṣaṃ tu rūpaṃ pāṭhādevāvadhārthyate /
tatkālāvadhūtabhedābhedānuvartitvaṃ tu prayojanaviniyogayoḥ /
pramāṇavaccānekamapi kalpanoyamityuktam/
rūpopalabdhivelāyāṃ ceṣetvāḍhināṃ na paraspara sākāṅkṣatvamekaprayājanatvaṃ copacacyate /
tataśca niṣpratidvandve 'vadhārita bhede paścānna kiṃ cidekatvāpāḍhane kāraṇaṃ saṃbhavati /
na ca prāganupantabdhaṃ sākāṅkṣatvaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyaṃ, tena ca vinā yadyapyekaprayojanavattvaṃ bhavettathāpye kāṅgavaikalyā de kavākyatvābhāvaḥ, kimu ta yadā rūpabhedādviniyogabhedastadbhedācādṛṣṭārthatve 'pi prayojanabhedaḥ /
tvatpakṣe'pi cāvaṇyaṃ yāvadviniyogaṃ tena tena bhavitavyam /
iyāṃstu viśeṣaḥ /
tava samastānmantrānmama vyastebhya /
na caiṣāmahaṭārthatvaṃ brāhmaṇopadiradṛṣṭārthaṃ sādhanatvāt /
taddvalena caiṣāṃ yāvatā vinā coditakaraṇasāmathrthyaṃ nāsti tāvadanāmnātamapi kalpanīyaṃ vinajhotyādi/
yadvā yathaiva rathaghoṣeṇa māhendra stotramupākarotīti vacanādavācakasyāpi viniyogamātrānusaṃdhānena stotrābhimukhyacinhatvaṃ bhavati, evamiṣetvādīnāṃ chedanādimmaraṇahetutvam /
ubhayamapi caitatpramāṇavaditi sūtrakāraḥ kaścitkathaṃ ciḍhā'śritama /
sarvathācaivamadhyavasātavyam /
vikalavākyaprayogāsaṃbhavāt avācaka prayogānupapatteścādhyāhāraḥ/
atha vā yathāmnātaviniyogānusārāttādṛśenaiva smarttu saṃskārādhāne yatitavyam /
tatrānuṣṭhātrabhiprāyādhīno 'nyataraparigraha iti dṛṣṭaprayojanabhedvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
dādapi siddho vākyabhedaḥ /
kiṃ ca /
anyonyanirapekṣāṇāṃ kāryyānyatve niyogataḥ  pratyekaṃ yāga hetutvādyajuṣmavakalpate 
na hi vaidikavākyānāṃ pratyakṣamevaikaṃ pramāṇaṃ, tadadeva hyanumānādīnyapi pramāṇāni /
sarvapramāṇapratyastamaye ca ṣaṣṭhenābhāvaḥ paricchidyate/
tadiha pratyakṣānupalabdha vākyaśeṣe na tāvatyevoparantavyam /
yaścanamānādīnyapi nivartiṣyante tata etāvānevāyaṃ mantra iti kalpayiṣyāmaḥ /
atha tutaiḥ kaścidavagamyate tatastamahato 'yaṃ mantraḥ sakataḥ prāk tasmādūna ityadhyavasyāmaḥ /
ta dihārthāpattyā tāvatmāmānyataḥ kaścidasti śeṣa ityadhyavaseyam/
tataścābhāvasthānavasarāhūnamidaṃ vākyaṃ na prayogāīm/
tatra viśeṣa kāṅaāyāṃ laukikaḥ kampanīya uta vaidika evaṃ pūrvama ntrasthastanavarṣaṣṭhetyādiranuvaktavya iti saṃbhaye laukika ityāi /
tathā hi /
nānyatrotmahate gantuṃ vaidikaṃ sannibandhanam/
yatheṣṭaviniyogaṃ tu sarvārthaṃ vastu laukikam 
yadi tvānantaryāviśeṣādrajāśayetyanenāpi saṃbandho'bhyupagamyeta tato yathāniveśaṃ prayogātpurastādevāsya prayogaḥ prāpnoti/
tamādapi na vaidikaḥ śeṣaḥ iti prāpte ucyate /
vimuktavyāmṛtau vede laukikāvasara sthitiḥ /
tadvyāpāravimoka‍ca sakalānveṣaṇakṣaye 
aṣṭaḥ prakṛtāvarthaḥ pratyaye 'nviṣyate punaḥ /
pade svasminnalabdhastu prārthanīyaḥ padāntare 
tadiha rajāśayāharāśayāvākyayoḥ śeṣaḥ svapadasva vākyayorajamyamānatvā ḍākyāntare nūna mityupasaṃdriyate /
sa ca yādṛgākāścitastāhagavai kānantaraṃ purastādupalabhyate anyasya vyavahitaḥ /
yadyapi cāsau prathamamantre kṛtārthatvānna nāvākāṅkṣati tau tu tena vinānupapadyamānāvātmasamīpe 'nyasyānāmnānādevaṃ puruṣaṃ prayu ghnāte /
sarvasamīpe sakṛtpaṭhitumaśakyaḥ pramāṇāntaranabhyatvācca punaḥ punaraśrāvitoyamāvayorapyarthenāmnātaḥ śeṣo naikasyaiva sannighiviśeṣanimittabhrāntyā kalpayitavya iti yadyapi ca purastādālocyate, tathāpi yatpradeśavarttitvena tābhyāṃ kāścitastatraiva viniyujyate /
kutaḥ 
sa hi sakṛdāmnāyamānaḥ sarveṣāmīsite pradeśe na śakya ā mnātumityekasya yathākramamāmnāta itarayośca yāvatā buddhiviṣa yatāmāpadyate, tataśca gṛhītaḥ san svayamapi pradeśāntare sthātumasamarthastābhyāmapi cānyavṛttitvenānākāṅkṣitaḥ pūrvatra caparastādbhāvitayā dṛṣṭasāmarthyaḥ parastādeva nivecyate /
bhāṣyakāreṇa tu prathama dvitīyayormadhye pāṭhādagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣaḥ śeṣa ubhayorapyānantaryeṇaiva saṃbandhītyuklā tṛtīyasya vyavadhānādasaṃbandhamāśaṅṅkyārthitvāviśeṣādubhayoḥ samudāyāpādanenāvyavadhāne sādhite samudāyaśeṣatvameva sāī prāpnotītyāśaṅṅkya tasyāsadhyavārtika /
prayogāītvātprayogāī samudāyisaṃbandhaḥ, tatrāpi tayoḥ prādhānyādanyathā ca nairākācyānupapatte pratyekaṃ sakalaśeṣasaṃvandhasiddhirityavadhārgya punarvyākhyānāntaramārabdham /
api ca sākāṅkṣasya saṃnnidhāviti/
tatra kaiśvikhyānavikalpa evetyāśritam /
apare tu vadanti pūrvatrāparitoṣa duttaraṃ kṛtam 
samudāyatvaṃ hyekakārthyatvenai ka śabdopādānena vā bhaveta, nacācaikamapyasti /
nancidame kakārthyatva me kavākya śeṣagrahaṇaṃ nāma /
aho nu khalu mantrāṇāṃ kāryaṃ vijñātam /
apekṣā hi tatrobhayoḥ syāt /
kathaṃ tatka/rthyamityucyate /
śeṣaścāsau tayornna tahaśena samudāyatvāpattiryuktā /
paścādapi vā samudāyibhyāmeva tasya saṃgatiriṣṭeti ādita eva samudāyatvaṃ na labhyate /
yadi sa samudāyatvamāpannau tataḥ punaḥ pratyekaṃ saṃbandha iti rājaikaputrakrīḍā ''padyate /
purastādeva ca prayogaḥ prāpnoti tathābhūtena samudāyānantaryyāt /
na vā gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvaṃ deśabhedanimittaṃ nantrabhadāt /
prathamasya hyasau yathākācite deśe sthito notarayoḥ /
tasmādidameva vyākhyānam 
yo hi bahūnāṃ saṃbandhitvena sakadāmnāyate tasyāvaśyaṃbhāvye kenānantaryyamiti na tadeva tadā saṃbandhakāraṇatvenāśrīyate /
manāpyasmādeva kāraṇacayātsaṃbandha siddheḥ /
sannidhiviśeṣānnu ta dvitīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
dāyapratipattyā bhavati bhrāntiḥ /
sā tu sākāṅkṣayogyasaṃnnicitasaṃvandhyantaradarśanānnivarttate, yathā dhātvarthādiṣu vidhibuddhirguṇādyupādānasāmarthyā,devaṃ hi tatra jñāyate /
sarvārtho 'yamāmnāyamānaḥ sarvasādhāraṇānantaryyā saṃbhavādvākyaikatvācca kasya cidekaya mamope padyate /
tammādakāraṇamānantaryamiti /
sannighiriti buddā viparivṛttiḥ /
sā cānantarye saṃbaddhapadavyavāye ca bhavati /
saṃbaddhapadvyavadhirapyanantaryyaprakāra eva /
katham 
yā te agne rajāśayetyanenāpekṣitaḥ śeṣaḥ parastādajabhyamānaḥ purastātparāvṛttyālocyamāno labhyate tanūrvarṣiṣṭheti /
yadā ca tatrārūḍhastadā harāśayetyasyānantarībhūtaḥ punarevameva tṛtīyenāpi saha saṃbadhyate /
tataḥ paraṃ tvanyasyānāmnānāttāvatyevopacoyate /
sarvacaivamapeścā purastātparastācca prasṛtakacāru hotareṣāmanantarībhavantī tāvaḍhapekṣyamāṇā nigṛhṇāti yāvatkiṃ cinna yogyamastyayogyaṃ copacabdham /
tataḥ sarvamālocitamapasaṃhṛtya nivartate /

evaṃ vākye paḍhānāṃ prakaraṇe ca vākyānāṃ saṃbandho yāvatmākāṅkṣeṇa tatsaṃbandhāṇa parasyāpyanantarīkarttu' samarthena vyavadhānam /
avyavadhāne viccheda pīti/

dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
bhāṣyakāreṇa tu svatvaparityāgāṃśena yajatyāditrayaṃ pratyāsannārthatvātsutarāmabhinnamābhāsataityudāhṛtam /
tatra pūrvapakṣacaividhyadarśanātsaṃbhayopanyāsopi tadanuguṇaḥ pratibhāti /
tadyathā /
tisro bhāvanāḥ kimekamapūrvaṃ kurvanti uta cīniti, tathā trayo dhātvarthāḥ kimekī bhāvanā viśiṣanti uta tisraḥ, tathā trayo dhātavaḥ kimekaṃ dhātvarthaṃ vadanti uta cīni, ti /
kārya śabdapūcāpūrvabhāvanā dhātvartheṣu upakāryatvāviśeṣeṇa prayujyate bhāvanā dhātvarthadhātavo hyeṣāmutpādanena viśeṣaṇena pratipādanenopakārakatvātmāghanatvenābhidhīyante /
kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ 
atha vā pāramārthiko'trāyamekaḥ saṃśayaḥ, kiṃ dhātvarthacayānuraktaikā bhāvanā, atha vā pratidhātvarthaṃ bhāvanābheda, iti /
bhāvanaika dhātvarthānuraktā karmaśabdenocyate /
tasyā eva śabdāntarādi bhedakaṃ bhaviṣyati, apūrvasyāna bhidheyatvātkarmabhedānuniṣpādye va taditina pṛthagvicāramarhati /
prāsaṅgikastu dhātvarthaikatvopanyāsaḥ kathamapyasārvatrikaḥ sanyajyādiṣu bhaviṣyatīti nātīva tantrokrttavyaḥ /
tataścaitadapi saṃśayakāraṇaṃ pūrvapaśavādinaḥ pratibhāti, kiṃ dhātvarthānpratyupādīyamānā bhāvanā pratyekaṃ samāpyate, athavā te tāṃ pratyupādīyamānāḥ saṃhatya viśiṃṣantī, ti/
kiṃ tāvatprāptaṃ saṃhatyeti/

iyaṃ vopapattiḥ 
dṛṣṭaśrutavirodhe tu satyadṛṣṭaṃ prakalpate /

tadevāca

tatropadīyamānatvādvātvarthaḥ saṃhatāḥ punaḥ 
pramiddhe bhāvanābheda bhāvyabhedo niyogataḥ /
na cāso samudāyatvameka śabdyādineṣyate 
a cocyate 
yathā raktopadhānena nirudve sphaṭike sati /
kṛṣṇādicodanāyuktaṃ gamyate sphaṭikāntaram 
yasmātprakṛtipratyayayoḥ svārthābhidhāne smṛterācārācca nitya vivakṣitakramatvena pūrvaprayuktaprakṛtyarthavyāpteṣu prattipattṛṣu prattyāṃśaḥ sannipatan kṛtānubandhameva svārthaṃ vadati tasmānna kadā citpratyayārthaḥ śuddho labhyate/
yathoktaṃ prātipadikāduccarantī dvitīyā dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
divibhaktiḥ prātipadikārtho viśeṣaka ityāceti /
prayogavākyaśeṣabhāvena hi samudāyasya sattāsaṃbandha iti /
ekāpūrvakalpanayā di samudāyānuraktabhāvanākalpamataṃ phalasaṃbandha nimittā vāpūrvakalpanā/
prayogavākyaśeṣa bhāvena votpattivākyānāṃ phalasaṃbandho bhavati na svarūpaiḥ/
avatarūpāṇi ca karmāṇi prayogavākyena gṛhyante ityavagate bheda na śakyānye kī kartuṃ, na ca dadātijuhotyoḥ prayogavākyaśeṣabhāvaṃ paśyāmo yajeta svargakāma iti kevala yā gaśravaṇā, nna ca tena dānahomo labhyete /
svārthatyāgaprasaṅgādubhayāśrayaṇe vā yugapacchatilakṣaṇāpattirdoṣaḥ /
tasmānna samudāya kalpanāsti /
ataśca dhātvanyatvena padānta ratvātkevaviśiṣṭatā gamyate /
na ca jñānāntareṇā nivarttate /
na ca dhātvaryaikatvamā, secanapara svatvāpāḍhanābhyadhikatvāt/
na ca tyāgamātralakṣaṇā svārthavṛttitvenāpi vākyasamavāyopapatteḥ /
na ca dāviṇāni nāma guṇaḥ kaścitprasiddha iti sāmānādhikaraṇyānnāmadheyatvameva yuktam /
ataśca vākyānarthakyaṃ mābhūditi homo vidhīyate /
dadātinā tu yāgamanūdya guṇe vidhīyamāne hiraṇyātreyasaṃbandhe vākyabhedaprasaṅgādguṇādapi bhedaḥ saṃbhavatītyacaikaguṇo ekasyaiva punaḥ śrutiraviśeṣādanarthakaṃ hi syāt 
śabdāntarādhikaraṇapratyudāharaṇarūpeṇābhyāsasya pūrvapakṣaḥ sukhamabhidhīyataiti tadanantaramārambhaḥ /
tatra samidho yajati tatavārtika /
nūmapātaṃ yajatītyādiṣu samidādiśabdānapoddhṛtya yajatītvetatpañcakṛtvo 'bhihitaṃ kimekasya karmaṇo vācakamathāne kasyetyudāhṛtaṃ tadākṣipyate 
ṣaḍapi bhedahetavaḥ pṛthagbhūtāḥ svasāmarthyamācavyāpāraphalā darśayitavyāḥ, tadyāvadatra guṇanāmadheyayorbhedakaratvaṃ nāpanīyate na tāvadabhyāsasya parabhāgalābho'stītyanyadudāharttavyam/
na ca ta tsaṃbhavati kutaḥ 
aindravāyavaṃ gṛhṇātītyevamādoni hi sarvāṇi paramparā saṃgacyai/tpattikaguṇayogādbhidyante /
bhinne juhoti skanne juhotī tyādonyapi phalaṃ vā karmasannidhāvityanena nyāyena nimittaṃ pratyupādīyamānatvādbhidyante /
nimittasaṃbandhaparatvācca nābhyāsānarthakyamityabhedakatvam /
ye tu pañcaśāradīyeṣu tānparyagnikṛtāṃstānparyagnikṛtānityevamabhyāsamudāharanti teṣāṃ prākṛta  paryagnikaraṇānuvādaprasmaraṇasāmarthyaṃ tat /
na vā 'tra yajatiḥ śrūyate yasyābhyāsādbhedaḥ syāditi na kiṃ cidudāharaṇam /
yathodāhṛtedhveva tu samādhiḥ 
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
yānyupādeyārthāni nāmapadāni tāni tāvadākhyātaparatantratvāttadanusāroṇi santi tadvṛttiṃ pratīcante, taccetprakṛte niviṣṭaṃ nāmapadamapi tasyaiva guṇavidhirnāmadheyaṃ vā  /
atha tenāpūrva pa rikalpita, matastadgāmi nāmapadamityevaṃ bhedābhedayosvagatayoḥ pa svādāgacchatmamidādipadama kiṃcitkaratvādudāste tena tadpohatyākhyātamācaṃ vicāryate /
nanvevaṃ sati saṃjñāguṇayorabhedakatvapramaṅgaḥ /
tatra to bhedako yatrākhyātapaḍhana vyāpriyate tathā codāhariṣyati /
athaiṣa jyotirvājibhyo vājinamiti /
vājine tāvannaivākhyātapadaṃ śrūyate, jyotirādākpyākhyātasya guṇa phalasaṃbandhavyāpāreṇa prakṛtaniveśasaṃbhave sati tataḥ pūrvapravṛttayā saṃjñayaiva bhedo bhaviṣyati /
yatrāpyākhyātasya svarasena prakṛtakarmaniveśopalave sati tatrāsaṃbhavan guṇo vidhīyate tatrāpyasau bhedakā, yathācaivābhyupetyavāde vakṣyati ma eṣa devatāyāgasaṃbandho vidhoyamāna ityādi /
taccākhyātasya bhedaśaktau vihatāyāṃ bha batauti tadeva tāvatprathamaṃ parokṣyate /
kimekamapūrvamiti phastutaḥ karmabhedābhedopanyāso, yadā kimekaṃ karmāpūrvaṃ codayacyuta pañcāpi karmaṇyapūrvāṇīti /
kiṃ prāptamekamapūrvamiti /
kutaḥ 
C yathaiva yajatiśabdaḥ sakṛtpratyakṣeṇāvagataḥ punaruccāraṇesa eveti pratyabhijñānānna bhidyate/
tathā tadarthoopi, yathā cātraiva buddhabodhanakṛtpratyakṣa manarthakamapi bhavanna śaknoti śabdāntaratvaṃ karttu,mevaṃ punaḥ śrutirarthāntaratvam/
na hyānarthakyaṃ nāma va citpramāṇavarge'ntarbhavati /
yacca vedo 'vabodhayati tanmātrameva tatpramāṇavādibhirabhyupagantavyam /
tadihaikaśabdenābheda vedenāvagamite yo 'nyatvaṃ kalpayati tena veda evāpramāṇīkṛtaḥ syāt /
na ca pramāṇāvagatamānarthakyaṃ doṣāya/
asti veyamapi gatiḥ /
prayogavacanasaṃspṛṣṭaḥ śabdo 'rthamavadadhatsvayaṃ prayogitvena gṛhyataitya, thavābhīkṣṇyādicotanārtho'bhyāso bhaviṣyatyasti hi loke dvirvacanādatirekeṇāpi yāvatkṛtvobhyaste vivaścitārthaprakāśanaṃ bhavati tāvatkṛtvo 'bhyāsastathā ca pañcendropākhyāne vṛddhakumārīvaraprārthane patiṃ me dehīti pañcakatvobhyāsaḥ śrūyate /
na ca yathā tatra devatāyāḥ chalagrāhitvamevamiha kasya cidyena patipañcakabatpañcayāgakalpanā syāda,tha vā sarveṣvapyuccāraṇeṣu vidhāvāśrīyamāṇe karmaikatvaṃ vijñāyate /
yathā śākhāntarīyeṣu jyotiṣṭomādivākyeṣu /
tena tulyārthānāṃ vaikalpikatvāttadeva karma kadā citmamiḍākyenābhidhāsyate kadā cittanūnapādākyena /
na hi samānakāryatvena brohiyavayore kasyā nartha kyā darthāntara sādhakatvaṃ vijñāyate /
atha vā tanūnapāḍhādidevatā vidhānārthatvānnānarthakāṃ karmavidhāne hi sati nāmadheyatvaṃ bhaveda, nuvāde tu nāmadheyavidhirna saṃbhavatīti guṇavidhitvaṃ tasmādapyakarmāntaram/
yatrāpi ca pradeśāntara tāveva śabdārthoṃ/
pratyabhijñāyete tatrāpi hi gṛhānnirgadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
tasya punargṛhajanapratyabhijñāyāmivārthāntaratvamaśakyaṃ vaktum /
kimutedānantaraviparivṛttyā bannīyasyā'varudvāyāṃ buhā /
yadi ca pratyuccāraṇamarthānyatvaṃ bhavettadā 'nityavyaktiśabdārthatvapramaṅgaḥ 
gatvā divanna caiteṣu yāgatvaṃ vyatiricyate /
vyaktyaikatve nirūḍhaṃ ca kathaṃ karmāntaraṃ bhavet 
ākhyātapratyayaḥ pūrvaṃ vidhatte karmaśaktitaḥ /
anyenākṣiptaśaktistu tadākāṅkṣatyanūditam 
anuvāda viśeṣatvaṃ prakṛtapratyayādbhavet /
tatmāmānyapravṛttistu svavākyadeva labhyate 
vidhāyikā hi śrutiranyānāścitā dhātvarthabhāvanayoreva saṃniruvā tatraivāprāptaviṣayasvabhāvaṃ vidhitvaṃ prasuvānā pañcamasthānākhyapramāṇakṛtāṃ prāptabuddhimupammṛdya vidheyatvaśramaṃ karmāntaraṃ ka lpayati /
sa cedvidhiḥ śrutimanurudhyeta karmāntaramadhyavamyatya, ya sannidhiṃ tato na karmāntaratvam /
yatra punarvidhiśrutiranyatra vyāpriyate tatrāvirodhātsaṃnidhikṛtaṃ kakatvajñānaṃ bhavati/
tasmādiha vidheyayāgavyaktiphanatvopāttasāmānyaikatva nimittaiva pratyabhijñānabhrāntiḥ /
na hi vyaktipratyabhijñāne kiṃ citkāraṇamasti /

nanu cātra yaji śrutyaivaika karma vijñānānna vaktavyaṃ sannidhikṛtamevaikatvamiti/
naitadevam 
vyaktayo hi vidhīyante sāmānyenopalaścitāḥ /
tasmāttadgata mevātra bhedābheda nirūpaṇam 
yanmātramekaṃ karmeti svarūpeṇa vadhāryate /
tataḥ paraṃ na bhedosti prāktasmādbhedaniścayaḥ 
na ca yatra pratyakṣeṇa kevalena bhedo'vagamyate tadevaikaṃ bhidyate /
śabdasyāpi prāmāṇyā viśeṣāt ato'tra śabdāntarādiṣaṭkāvadhireva bhedo 'vadhārayitavyaḥ /
na hīṣṭipaśusomaikā hāhī nasatreṣu paropādhirbhedapratyayo viparyeti vā kadā cit /
tena tāsu vidheyarūpāsa vyaktiṣveva nityāskhabhivyañjakāni bhidyante /
tebhyaśca phalasvarūpasiddhiryāgatvameva vaikamavānsarasāmānya nānyatkiṃ cit/
nanvekāhatvādīnyapyavāntara sāmānyānīṣyante /
na, kālaviśeṣayogādeva daṇḍyādivadabhinna śabdapratyayapravṛttisiddheḥ /
ekena hyahnā yogāḍhakāitvam yāḍhibhirahīnatvaṃ pragdādaśāhātma tu kathamapyubhayātmā tadavadhikameva cāsahasra saṃkhyavatmarakānayoga nimitta satratvaṃ havirviśeṣayogādiṣṭyāditvamiti siddham /
śrathāpyavāntara sāmānyāni punaḥ karupyante, tathāpyasmatpaścāvirodhaḥ /
evaṃ yadi jyotiṣṭomatvādīni deśakālādibhedācca tāktayotyantātira kiṣyo bhavanti tathāpyadoṣaḥ /
tathā yadyapi devatoddeśadravyatyāgātmakatvātsarva evaiko yāgaḥ kalpya'te teṣvapi bhedapramāṇaistadanuṣṭhānanānātvāvagamāyavahārasiddhiḥ /
nanvevaṃ mati jyotiṣṭomagrahābhyāsavatmamidādiyāgābhyāsaghvakarmāntaratvaprasaṅgaḥ /
sarvathā tāvadaparvamedāirmavyavasthāḍhīni si dhyanti, tathāpi tu yeha karmabhedabuddhigrahayāgeṣu cābhyāsabhedadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
prasiddhiḥ /
tacaitannimittam i sakalayāgarūpānuṣṭhānabhedacodanā tatra punaḥ samastābhyāsātmakasya jyotiṣṭomasaṃjñatvādyadyapi pratyabhyāsa yāgatvamasti na ta jyotiṣṭomatvamityabhyāse avayavabuddhirnetaratrāvayavyantararūpānupādānāditi viśeṣaḥ /
etaujjñānasya ca prayojanaṃ paśusomādhikaraṇe vacyāmaḥ /
tasmādabhyāsitavyo yāga iti ca bhāṣyametatpaśyanaiva /
athavā bhināskheva vyaktiṣu sāmānyāpecamabhyāsavacanam /
nanūktaṃ na śakkrotyarthāntaraṃ vidhātumiti vidhiśaktestanūnapādādidevatābhidhānāpe sati viparivṛtya virodha iti manyase /
tatra tatprakhyaṃ cānyaśāstramityevaṃ samidādipadānāṃ kramaviniyuktaiva liṅgamantravarṇakalpitadevatāsaṃbandhadvāreṇa nāmadheyatve sati avidheyatvānnāsti vidhiśaktyākṣepa iti vaktavye devatāyāgasaṃvandha vidhānopanyāsobhyupetyavādena /
yattāvadbhavānaprāptatvātprathamasya yāgavi dhitvaṃ manyate tadayuktaṃ tasyāpi pradhāna  yāgānuvādatvāt /
tatra samidādiśabdaidravyaṃ devatā vā vidhīyate /
ubhayamapi cāgneyo 'ṣṭākapāla ityādibhirutpattivākyairvihitena dravyadevatena viru dhyate /
avaśyaṃ caitadvākyakṛto yāgasaṃbandhaḥ  karttavyaḥ, saca yā gāntarāite na saṃbhavatīti pratipādite  guṇavidhitve karmāntaratvamāpadyate /
evaṃ pūrvatra karmaṇyuttarottara guṇaviṣyasaṃbhavātsarveṣāṃ karmāntaratvamiti vyartho guṇavidhyapanyāsaśramaḥ /
guṇavidhitvamapi santravārtika /
na tāvad dravyamohana śabdena saṃbhavatīti vyākhyātaṃ sakvadhikaraṇe /
viśeṣeṇa ca yajateḥ karmabhūtadravyasaṃbandho na ghaṭate, na vāyaṃ devatāvidhiriti navame vacyate /
tasmātkarmavidhibhireva bhedasiddhiḥ 
aṅgapradhānacinteyaṃ caturthādhyāyagocaraḥ /
kena nāma prasaṅgena prastutā bhedalaṇe 
na bhede ca dṛṣṭasāmarthya samaprādhānyasiddhaye /
kathaṃ śabdāntarābhyāsau hetutvenopavatā 
śrīvaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ dravyaṃ devatā mānnavarṇikī /
rūpavantāvato yāgau vidhīyete pṛthaktayā 
niveśaḥ keṣu tcittveva pṛthakkenābhidhānayoḥ /
phalaṃ ca tadviśiṣṭebhya iti sāmyaṃ na yujyate 
prasiddhenāpramiddhasya nityamiṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇam /
tasmādyajyanurodhena nāmā/
nirūpyate  
vāccakālayujo yāgāḥ prakṛtāḥ manti ke cana /
dvisaṃkhyotpattiyuktāśca prasiddhiryeṣu vidyate 
yadyāpyāgneyādiṣu svābhidheyakānayogātprātipadikaṃ varttata tathāpi teṣāṃ bahutvād dvitvānapapattera samarthaṃ padaṃ, yatrāpi dvitvamastyāghārayorājyabhāgayorvā tatrāpi prātipadikasyātyanta maśaktiḥ /
na cārthaprakaraṇaśabdānta rairvispaṣṭaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyamasti, yena kena cidvarṇasāmānyādākhyāvikāranyāyena gauṇatvena vā tadviṣayatvamadhyavasīyeta/
