myādetat /
eteṣāṃ madhye yayoḥ kayośiyataphala saṃbandha iti tadayuktam 
vinā viśeṣahetunā yāgatvakāla saṃbandhasāmye sati yāveva gṛhītau tatraivetareṣāṃ prādhānyaprāmāṇyabhājāṃ satāmaṅgatvāpāढ़nāt viruddhatā syāt /
atha vikalpena sarveṣāṃ pāściko 'nugrahaḥ karupeta tatrāpi tasyaiva kadā citpradhānatvaṃ kadā cidaṅgatvamiti vipratiṣiddham/
ubhayātmanāṃ cāṅgatayā pravṛtteḥ pradhānatvena ca nivṛtterāgneyādīnāṃ vikṛtigamane yāvajjīvaṃ saṃśayaprasaṅgaḥ /
sarvasaṃkhyāpūca kena cidavāntarasāmānyāvacchedena saṃkhyeyeṣu varttante /
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
na vāpūrvayoragneyādīnāṃ vā samastānā mekadeśe vā kiṃ cida vāntarasāmānyaṃ dṛśyate yena dvitvamavadhāyeta /
ya eva hi gṛhīta staṣyaitra yāgāntarāpekṣayāhūtena bahutvena kevalātmā peśeṇa caikatvena dvitvaṃ bādhyate /
tataśca dvivacanasyāprasiddhiḥ /
siddhānte tu śabdadayena samudāyadvayāpādanāda samudāyī kṛtayāga vaicacapaṭyādavāntaradharmayogātsaṃbhavati ditvayogastadaśena ca kālayogākathaṃ ciddarśapūrṇamāsaprātipadikayorapi vṛttisiddhirityupapadyate yāgaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ, na tu pūrvapace samudāyatvāpādanābhāvātsaṃkhyāvṛttiriti prakṛtayāgamātraeva phala saṃbandhaḥ atha kasmādaṣṭāveva yāgāḥ paurṇamāsya māvāsyā kālagatadvitvāpekṣayā labdhaviśeṣaṇāḥ santo na vidhīyante /
yathā siddhānte samudāyagata dvitvāpeścayā ṣaḍ vidhāmyante /
neharśanāsphuṭena prakṛtayāgamātrāvalambyākhyātaṃ śakyaṃ nivarttayitum /
na cātyantavyatirekātkālagatā saṃkhyā yāga  sāmānādhikaraṇyanirdeśā bhavati /
samudāyamamudāyinostva vyatirekādaviruddhaḥ saṃkhyāsaṃbandhaḥ siddhānte /
tasmātpūrvapace yajivaśenaiva nāmapadavṛttera viśeṣeṇa sarve yāgāḥ samapradhānāḥ /
tathā prāpte 'bhidhīyate /
prakaraṇaṃ paurṇamāsyamāvāsyā saṃyuktayorālambanaṃ syāt /
prakriyataiti prakaraṇam /
athavā prakaraṇaṃ tayoḥ sahakāri bhavettataśca tanmātrapratipādyo 'tha grahītavyaḥ /
kutaḥ 
na hyanena yajinā paurṇamāsyamāvasyāpaḍhābhyāṃ vā yāgamātre buddhiḥ kriyate/
na ca prakṛta karmagracaṇaṃ tvatposti /
tatrājñātarūpe sati apūrve karmaṇi na kathaṃ citpravarttyata /
 tataṅkaca vākyamevānarthakaṃ bhave, tprakṛtagrahaṇe tu teṣāṃ dravyadevatāyogādetatkālavarttitvācca rūpajñānādarthavaśvam/
nanūktaṃ matyace 'pyasti dravyadevatamiti /
satyam /
yathā kathaṃ cimabhyeta dravyaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ sthitam /
tathāpi devatā nāstītyarūpatvānna mucyate 
yadi hi sarvalokaprasiddhaḥ kālona na samaveyāttatastadatikrameṇa karmaṇī gṛhayātām/
api copapannatarā kālavacanatve sa pramī, tasya sarvacaiva kālasyādhikaraṇatvānna karmaṇodhikaraṇatvāhitopādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
nupapatteryathā kathaṃ citkalpanīyaṃ syāt /
yattu kiṃ kālasya mantrasaṃbandheneti, yadi tādarthya evaikaḥ saṃbandho bhavetma cātrāsmābhirucyeta tata evaṃ yujyate vaktum idda svājyabhāgau prati tā darthye vyavasthite saṃkare ca prāpte kālabhedena prayujyamānayaॉrmantrayorvyavasthāmācaṃ kriyate vārcaghno paurṇamāsīsthayorājyabhāgayovṛdhanvatī amāvāsyāsthayoriti /
kiṃ ca 
sarvacaivākāṅkṣāpūrvakaḥ saṃvandho bhavatyā, jyabhāgau ca prajñātāgrīṣomadevatyau tadabhidhānamamarthamantrākāṅkṣitvāt ayatnena mantrān gṛhṇota, svatpane tvapūrvayoḥ karmaṇora jñātadevatatvānna mantrāpevā, tataśca mantratadviśeṣa dvitvāḍhi kalpanādanapeścitānekārthavidhiprasaṅgaḥ saṅgaḥ /
punaśca māntravarṇikānekadevatā kalpanā, na hoka karmaṇo nekayā devatayānekayānuvākyayā kāryamasti /
punaścāśrutayā jyā kalpanāśrayaṇāmājyabhāgayoścāśrutapuronubākyā kalpanam /
yaccaikā yājyā ekā vānuvākyā bhaviṣyatīti /
na tadnavākyā samākhyābādhāt /
api ca tvatpakṣa liṅgasyāviniyojakatvāt vākye ca karaṇatvenāśrayaṇāt vaiṣṇavī manū cetyādi baḍhadṛṣṭārthapramatarna prakāśakatā prakāśyenānapeścitatvāt /
mā ntravarṇakadevatā kannātaśca varamārādupakārakatvam /
ājyabhāgayoḥ punarditvātprajñāta hidebatatvācca prakāṇyā kā ḍināḥ prakāśakā mantrāḥ niṅgakrama viniyuktāḥ santaḥ ekāntena dṛṣṭārthatāṃ pratipadyante /
tatra ca mantrataviśeṣaditvādiṣu prāpteṣu kāladdāraṇa vyavasthāmātravidhānālāghavaṃ vākyasya, na vā'narthakyaṃtantravārtike /
naci sannidhānāvasthā siddhā/
tasmānna devatāvidhira saṃbandhāt/
ataśca rūpavattvāt akarmāntaratā kiṃ punaḥ samastānuvādasya prayojanaṃ, paśya 
uccate /
yathaivotpattivākyānāṃ prayogavacanāṅgatā /
tathaiva tadupāḍhānād dvitvasijhā 'nayorapi 
ekakājābhisaṃyogādbhinnānāmapi karmaṇām /
samudāyārpaṇaṃ śakyame kadaṃśasthavṛkṣavat 
paurṇamāsoṃ yajataiti yajisāmānādhikaraṇyāta yāganāmadheyametaditi gamyate /
na cāgneyādīnāṃ samudāye yāgatvaṃ samavetaṃ,kiṃ tarhi pratyekamāgneyādiṣu, tammādyayaivaiteṣu pratyekaṃ yaji revaṃ nāmadheyamapi /
na ca samudāyotpattirekena kālena yuktā, āgneyādīnāmutpattikānte parasparānapeśatvena samudāyatvānupajananān/
tataḥ kāntavaśenāpi pratyekaṃ nāmadheyamiti śakyaṃ vaktuṃ, yadi ca samudāyinairapekṣyeṇa samudāyayorete nāmano syātāṃ tataḥ prayogavākyenāpi mamudāyo phale vidhīyatāṃ tato'vayavānāmasādhanatvātmamudāyādekamapūrvam /
ataśca pratyekāparvāṇāmabhāvātkarmabheḍhavaiyarthaṃ prasaṅgaḥ /
savaidharmāṇa caikāpūrvanibandhanatvātmaṃkīrṇavṛttitvaṃ syāt /
na ca pratyeka mitikarttavyatayā S'gneyādayaḥ saṃbadhyeran /
tataśca tadgatatantrāvṛttiprayogādivicārāsaṃbadvatvaṃ bhavet/
na ca pratyekavikāre sauryādau samastetika taṃ yatātideśaḥ syātma istrādiśabdavaccāvayavavṛ tyabhāvāde kapuroḍāśā paiaumāsī sānnāyyaracitā 'māvāsyetyevamādivyavahārocchedapramaṅgaḥ /
saṃghātasyācoditatvātsaṃghātasya guṇatvādityevamādiṣu spaṣṭamevaṃprakārāṇāṃ samudāyivacantvamabhyupagatam, itarathā hi sa eva śabdābhihitatvāccodyeta phalasaṃbandhācca pradhānaṃ bhavet/
tasmādupasarjanībhūtamamudāyāḥ samudāyina evābhidhīyante /
teṣāṃ tu bahatvāt bahuvacanaprasaṅgena lakṣaṇayaikavacanayoga ityabhipretya samudāyaśabdatayāvaka spiṣyata ityāha /
tathā ca bhavati hi bahūnāmekavacanā tantravārtike /
ntaḥ samudāyāpeśa itya peśāmātrameva samudāyasya bravīti nābhidheyatvam/
yūthavanaśabdāvapi yadā mamudāyopamarjanasamudāyivacanau tadā sākacyena dṛṣṭāntau yadā tu samudāyameva brataḥ tadā tannimittaikavacanannābhamātreṇa dṛṣṭaśantatvam /
etena darśapūrṇamāmaśabdāvetatparyāyai/
vyākhyātai 
anyathaiva hyayaṃ kānaḥ karaṇāṃśena yujyate /
anyathotpattivāṛyastho nirapekṣaḥ parasparama 
kālo yasya na vijñātaḥ svarūpaṃ ca na naśyati /
tasya kālaḥ paropādhirucyamāno na duṣyati 
aṅgānāṃ mukhya kā natvāhā kyāmmādinā 'pyayam /
kālostyeveti naitasya vacasoca nimittatā 
nanu dūrasthānyupakarttuṃ na śaknuvanti saṃnikṛṣṭasyairupakarttavyamityetadvā kutaḥ sarvaca, vacanānusāreṇopakārānupakārāṃśī vi jāyete /
tatra sannikarṣavacanābhāve viprakṛṣṭaṃ nopakarotīti na kiṃ citpramāṇam/
nanu cā'nyenaiva vākyeneṣa tantra prayogaḥ sidhyati, yaiṣṭyā paśunā somenetyādīnāṃ tatrāpi karaṇavibhaktinideśādiṣṭeḥ svamamudāyisvāṅga sahitāyāḥ kālaṃ pratyupādānādīhabhī vivacā labhyate /
satyaṃ labhyate na tviṣṭaḥ prayoga sidhyati /
tathā ddi 
na tāvattrikasyeṣṭi śabdena grahaṇamityavadhāyate /
tatra pratyeka yāgatveneṣṭi śabda pravṛttere ke kasyāmamāvāsyāyo paurṇamāsyāṃ vā prayoga iti na samyakprayogasiddhiḥ /
atha samastānāmagneyādī nāṃ kathaṃ cidraḍheḥ pravṛttatvādiṣṭeḥ mome pravṛttiritivad grahaṇam /
evamapi prayogavacanaikatvātmamudāyadvayasyāpi paurṇamāsyāmamā vāsyāyāṃ vā 'nuṣṭhānaṃ syāt /
tatra sa evotpattiśiṣṭa kāla virodhaḥ tadanurodhena vyavasthitavikalpāśrayaṇamiti cet /
evamapi yathotpattyanurodhātpratyekānuṣṭhānaprasaṅgaḥ /
tathāṅgānāṃ bhedena paurṇadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
māsyamāvāsye pracupādānābhāvādyatra ka canaikatra pradeśe 'nuṣṭhānaṃ syāt/
tasmānnaitadvākyaṃ tābhyāṃ tunyārthamiti prakṛtāva kiṃcitkaratvāt vikṛtoreva sadyaḥkālatāyai gacchati/
nanvanena tantra prayogaḥ siddhyet /
same darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajeneti deśasyānupādeyatvāsāhityavivaśvopapatteḥ /
tatrocyate 
bhedenāpici prayujyamānānāmananyadeśagamanamātreṇa deśatantratvasiddhiḥ /
athetaretarayogavaśādyadaivaikaḥ samena yāgo yujyate tadaivetaropīti tantratvamucyate /
tathā satiṣaṇāmapi yugapadupādānāttathaiva prayogaprasaktaḥ sa eva virodho, yadi punarutpa ttivākyānurodhena pravarttate /
tataḥ pratyekaṃ kālasaṃyuktānī samaṃ pratisāhityaṃ saṃpādanīyamiti ṣaṭsleva paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāsu prayogaḥ samāpyeta /
aṅgāni ca tāvataḥ kālādanutkṛṣyamāṇāni prayoktavyānoti yatra ka camāntarāle kriyerana 
yadyutpattau na vidyeta yāgānāṃ kālasaṃgatiḥ /
samudāyānuvādatvaṃ nirnimittaṃ na labhyate 
viśeṣadarśanāca pūrveṣāṃ sameṣu hyapravṛttiḥ syāt 
yadi caite karmāntare syātāṃ tata āghārādīni samapradhānāni syu,stataśca karmaṇastvapravṛttitvātphalaniyama kartṛ samudāyasyānanvayastadvandhanatvādityanena nyāyenāuneyā davata prayājādīnāṃ karaṇaṃśopanipātādihitakaraṇayā vikṛtibhāvanayā kathaṃbhāvākāṅkṣiṇyā tatparaṇāmamarthānāmagrahaṇātprāpta prayājānuvādana klaṣṇalavidhānaṃ nopatradyeta /
tasmādāgneyaguṇatvaṃ  prayājādeḥ kathaṃ syāditi samudāyānuvāda 
codanā vā guṇānāṃ yugapacchāstrācodite hi tadarthatvāttasya tasyopadiśyeta 
naiteṣṭā kapālādayo guṇa viṣayaḥ /
kutaḥ 
karmotyattivākye hi pratyayo bhāvanāmaprāpnatvāt vidhāsumupakramate /
sā ca yāvaddvātvarthaṃkāra kainna paripūryate tāvadanuṣṭhātumayogyeti na vidhitvaparyavamānaṃ, tatra bhāvanātmabhibhūtāvagatakārakasāmānyānyathānupapattyātiviśeṣopalibhāyāṃ svavākyocāritakāraka vibhaktyanta pada pratītairviśeṣairbhāvanāmātrākāṅakṣibhiḥ vākyādeva viśeṣyate /
pratipadaṃ ca yāvatkiṃcid dravyāśrimaṃ jātiliṅgasaṃkhyādi tatsarvamekapaḍhopādānalacaṇaśrutipratitavyaviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvamapratipanna paraspara śeṣaśeṣitvaṃ vibhaktiśrutyaiva kārakātmanā bhāvanārthatvaṃ pratipadyate /
evaṃ yāvanti padāni saṃnikarṣaviprakarṣasthāni tāni sarvāpayanuṣaṅgādhikaraṇoktena mārgeṇānādṛtya saṃnikarṣaviprakarṣai/
yugapatsaṃnipatanti /
sataḥ sarvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭāmanuṣṭhānayogyāṃ bhāvanāmāmādya vidhiḥ samāpyate /
sa caikenaiva prayatnena to viśiṣṭa viddhātīti nātāṃ neka makti kalpanāpattidoṣaḥ /
tathā hi 
viśiṣṭāyāṃ bhāvanāyāmādhāya śrītaṃ vidhitvaṃ yadyanyatrāpi śrutyaiva punarvyāpriyeta tataḥ punaruccāraṇadoṣama vaidikatvāpattyā svabheta /
ayaṃ punaḥ makkadvidhāya nivṛttavyāpāraḥ svārthānyathānupapattyā sarvaviśeṣaṇeṣu pratyeka niṣṭhāni vidhyantarāṇyāvirbhāva yan samāmnāyāvagataikarūpāparityāgenaivāsa kuduccāraṇaphanḍe varttate 
viśiṣṭanimittatvādarthāpattiḥ paścādbhavanto yadyapi viśeṣaṇavidhīnuttarakālamavagamayati tathāpi tvākṛtyadhikaraṇanyāthena viśeṣaṇānyanupādāya viśiṣṭavyāpārāsaṃbhavānnūnaṃ pūrvaṃtaraṃ viśeṣaṇaviṣayo niṣpannāḥ, yatastadadhīna siddhirviśiṣṭa pratyayo dṛśyate iti, tena bacava evaite vidhaya iti pratyakṣārthāpattilabdhā yugapaskrameṇa vā vyāpriyanta ityaneka vidhyantaraprasavasamarthaika viśiṣṭavidhiprasādenā nekaguṇa vidhānamapūrvabhāvanāvidhipaśce sulabhaṃ netaratra /
katham 
yadā hi bhāvanā 'nyataḥ prāptā bhavati tadā tasyāḥ piṣṭapeṣaṇavatpratiitaśaktirvidhāyakastāmavidadhānaḥ na tatsaṃgatārthānekavidhivyāpāraprasava hetutvaṃ pratipadyate/
viśiṣṭavidhāne ārthāpattyā vidhyantarāṇi kalpyante /
na cātra tatsaṃbhavatītyanupayukta śrīnavyāpārāvastha eva pratyaya ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣvityanena nyāyena bhāvanāto 'vatīrya tatsaṃbaḍhāni kārakāṇyupasarpati /
tatra yāvantye kapadopagattaikakāraka viśeṣaṇāni jātiniṅgadravyasaṃkhyāhoni tāni viśiṣṭabhāvanāvidhinyāyenaiva tatkārakā kṣepāt sarvāṇi vidhīyantaiti prāptāyāmapi bhāvanāyāmanekārthavidhyu papattiḥ /
yadā tvanekapadopāttāneka kārakopanipāto bhavati tadā kārakāṇāṃ paraspara saṃbandhābhāvāttattatpa devapya saṃbadhyamāneṣu yadyekatra vidhirgacchati tadā netaratra gato bhavati, evamitaragamane'pyanyagamanānupapattirasaṃbandhādevaṃ ca na bhāvanāvaḍhe kena vihitenetaradarthāḍhāvetuṃ śakyate /
tatrārthanabhyavidhyantaraprasūtāva satyāmekātmakaḥ śrauto vidhirekatropakṣīyamāṇo yadyanyatrāpyastīti kalpate tannāmakṛduccāraṇāhate miṭatīti pauruṣeyo 'nekoccāraṇaprasaṅgastaddarśayati /
codite hi prāpte karmaṇi tadarthatvāgaṇārthatvāttasya tasya guṇanya vidhaye punaḥ punarupadiśyetocāryeta pratyaya ityarthaḥ 
tatrācāṣṭakapālasaṃbandhasidvyartha  māgneya śabde 'nūdyamāne paurṇamāsogatasya kā devateti na jñāyate yugapadupakṣaṇavidhikarūpane vākyabheda ityanenaiva mārgeṇa kṛtyadhikaraṇamukhapradarśitairvacanavyaktiprakārairvā kyabhedānantyaṃ prapañcayitavyaṃ, tenāvaśyaṃ vidhātavyo 'tra dravyadevatāsaṃbandho na ca sa pūrvaprāpte karmaṇi saṃbhavatīti gu bannavārtika /
ṇaścāpūrvasaṃyoga iti karmāntaratvam /
karmāntaratve ca sati tadavasthaṃ rūpāvacanamityanuvādatā/
avaśva bajādekavacanalakṣaṇādyāśrayaṇīyam /
kiṃ ca navā'nanya kriyāyoge vākyametatmamāpyate  na ca svārthā samāptatvādākyāntaramapekṣate 
tathā coktam 
vyapadeśaśca tadvat 
ekeṣṭiryadyamāvāsyāsānnāyyoṣadhayostataḥ 
karmabhede hi bhinnaviṣayatvātmānnāyyapuroḍāśasamuccaye sati saṃbhriyantaiti samastasaṃbharaṇaṃ prathamottarābhidhānaṃ cāvakarūpate nānyathā, prathamapaśceca caturthamapyaparamastītyuttarāṇīti syānotare iti 
paurṇamāsyāṃ yadā timro he darśaviṣaye yadā 
tasmā samudāyānuvādāviti siddham /
śraca ca /
pādheiyasya prakṛte śabdaśaktitaḥ 
tatropāṃyājamantarā yajatīti tāvatsakandaḥ prāgukto nyāyo 'sti /
kutaḥ 
teṣu tāvattavyapratyaye nai kāntiko vidhiḥ /
tatra yadīdaṃ yāgāntara karapyate tataḥ prāptaṃ rūpājñānamadṛṣṭāntarakalpamaṃ ca kiṃ prajāmikaraṇaṃ caiṣu pratyekamavagamyate /
jāmidoṣeṇa copāṃyājopanyasanaṃ kṛtam 
yathā vaiśvānaravākye dvādaśakapālenopakramopasaṃhārābhyāmaṭatvādaya ekavākyatāmāpadyamānāḥ pṛthagvidhitvaṃ na pratipannā, sta thā'pi jāmi vā etaditi vidhyapakrame doṣasaṃkīrttanaṃ kasya dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
ciddhidhīyamānasyākātiṃ tadapanayanadvāreṇa stutyarthamiti gamyate /
jāmitā capuroḍāgayorantarāje kasmiṃścidavidhīyamāne bhavatīti yadantarālakālasaṃyogena vidhāsyate tasyājāmikaratvaṃ praśaṃsetyavadhāradupāṃśuyājamantaretyasya stutyatvena jñānādiṣvādiyukteṣu ca tadapeścitājāmirūpastuti saṃkīrttanādanapeścitaṃ vidhitvamanādṛtya mutyarthatā gṛhyate/
na ci viṣṇvādisaṃyukteṣvantarālakālasaṃyogo 'sti yegopakramottayā jāmitayā tadvidhistadgataṃ vā jāmitvaṃ stāvakata yāpecitaṃ saṃbadhyeta /
antarājakāja saṃyuktavya punarvaspaṣṭajāmyupakramavākyavidhānā ītvā tadarśana cetareṣā stāvakatvopayoge sati nānekā dṛṣṭa kalpanānubandhiviśyabhyupagamo yuktaḥ 
na hi devatāḥ stavānastatpū jāvyāpatopi sankaścidyaja iti ucyate /
rūpā samavāyitvā ca nātithivaddevatā pūjyamānatāṃ pratipadyate /
na ca yajistatpara iti navame vacyate 
tena yatra saṃpradānatvanirdeśaḥ tatraitaduktaṃ bhavati /
parasvatva bhivāpādayituṃ taduddeśena dravyaṃ tyajediti /
yatrāpi karmanirdeśaḥ tatraiṣortha,styaktaṃ dravyaṃ devatāmu hiśediti /
tathā ca kevaloddeśavyāpāreṣu tyaktṛtvarahiteṣu yajeti praiṣo bhavati tadetadubhayamapi lākṣaṇikam /
tatrāpi saṃpradānatvaṃ tyāgāṃgāvyabhicāritvādasamastātmakatvāddūṣitamapi satpratyāsannataraṃ devatātvasya /
karmatvaṃ tu kriyāntareṣvapi vyāpyamānatvasaṃbhavātmavyabhicāra miti viprakataraṃ devatātvasya /
na hi taddevatātvavatmakalaṃ yajiṃ prati karmetyavadhāryate /
paramārthataḥ punardevatāśabdena taniśabdena vā devatātvamabhidhīyate, na kāraka vibhaktyā kayā cit/
tathā ca /
devatā taḍitotpāde na hi pāṇininā tathā /
idamagnayaityevaṃ tena krītamivoditam 
yādṛśī hyākhyātena svapradhānā pūrvāparībhūtā bhāvanāntarākhamanupādeyaṃ pratyupāttā, na tādṛśī viṣṇuryaṣṭavya ityādibhirupasthāpyataiti notpattividhikalpanābhaṅgaḥ /
tatra satyapītareṣāṃ karmavidhitve karmāntaraṃ syānna prakṛtānuvāda iti matvā ''cha /
karmāntaratya vācakaḥ syāditi/
devatāyāḥ punarupādeyatvātkarmoddeśena vidhiḥ saṃbhavatīti nānuvādabuddhirapaiti /
karmavidhyabhyupagame tu satyapi prakṛtasadbhāve tadrūpāṇāṃ prakṛtānāmabhāvādityabhiprāyaḥ /
atha vā yadidamāgneyādibhyaḥ karmāntaraṃ caudyate ta stropāṃyājaṃ yajatītyayaṃ vācakaḥ syānnetareṣām /
tasmādantarāsnānupādeyatvavaśenāsyaikrāntike karmavidhitve matītarairarthavādareva bhavitavyam /
dhātvarthaṃ cānyatra vidadhatpratyayaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭa vṛttirbhaviṣyati /
sa tu vidhīyata upāṃśutvādisaṃbandha ityupāyā jaśabda guṇāvidhiṃ manyate /
yattvavācakatvamantei kutprasaṅgāditi /
tatroccate tulyametattvatpaś /
kunaḥ /
vācyavācakasaṃbandhaḥ iṣṭaḥ śabdārthayoḥ purā /
paścādvidhyanuvādatve syātāṃ sādhāraṇaśraye 
na ca tatprakhyarūpeṇa nāmaitadupapadyate /
vicitaṃ na paśutvaṃ śāstreṇānyena kena cit /
na tāvadviṣvādiyuktena vihitamarthavādatvāt/
nopāṃśu parṇamāsyāmityanena kānavidhivyāpatenā nekavidhyamakteḥ /
tasmāda tpattitsyenaiva vidhīyate /
tathā ca sūtrakāro vakṣyati /
guṇopabandhāditi/
jāmitvāpanayanaṃ ca sarva prakāra dravyataḥ kharato devatātaśca jñāyataeva yathā viṣṇuryaṭavyaḥ prajāpatiranīṣomo veti yāge codite 'vagyaṃ bhāvinyāṃ devatāyāmaniyamaprasaktī ke ci dviṣṇvādayaḥ prādhānyaprasiya/
vaicitryapradarśanārthaṃ saṃkīrttitā, te na yadyapi paramārthena na yaṣṭavyāḥ tathāpi stutiparatvādupādānaṃ muṇavādena kathaṃ ciducyate, śākhāntare vidhānātprāptā ityanudāiraṇāda sphuṭa mebamabhidhāya na hi kiṃ ciḍhasādhyaṃ syānna ca tasminmani daśame tadvaca devatāyāṃ sthādityādi vicārya viṣṇurvā syāhai/
trāmnānādityādinā māntravarṇikatvaṃ jaiminirāśrayiṣyati /
yadyapyaprāptiriti cecāpi svayamevāśaṅkā darśitā /
yadapyuktamu pāṃśudharmatvātprāptau tasmādyatkiṃ citprājāpatya miti tadadhyayuktam /
vacanavyaktiviparyāsā,nna hyeṣaṃ vacanaṃ yadupāṃśu tatprājāpatyamiti kiṃ naī yatprājāpatyaṃ sadupaśvata tena nopāṃśutvena prājāpalānā cabhyā/
yadagnīṣomayostu vidhāyaka udādbhiyama aivetyema dapi caturthotadvitamantravarṇānātmakatvādavidhāyakam /
yadi hitāvagnīṣomāvabrūtāṃ tato'smākaṃ kimiti hi vijānanto yajamānā na vayaṃ devatāyāṃ pravarttitā iti kalpayeyuḥ /
kālavidhiparatvācca na devatā 'pyanena śakyā vidhātuṃ devatāparatve vā kānta vidhiparityāgātyai/
rṇamāsośabdenāpi nānṛdyeta iti pūrṇamāmaśabdenā grahaṇādasati pradhānatveṅgatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
chatrakāreṇa ca dagame 'māvāsyāyāmupayājamanicchataitadeva paurṇamāmīkānavidhiparatvenopanyastam /
atra samādhiḥ māntravarṇiko davataḥvidhiriti sthita,mupāṃśuyājakrame hi vaiṣṇavaprājāpatyāgnīṣomīyāni yājyāpugenuvācyā yugannāni āmnāyante /
taiśca sulyārthatvādikalpamānaiḥ vaikalpika eva devatāḥ prāpyante /
tadeva cha/traṃ śākhāntaramityāhādhvaryavepi tu ka cidastyeva yājyānuvākyāmnānaṃ trarūpeṇeti tadabhiprāyaṃ vā śākhānta ravacanamupāṃśudharmatvaṃ vāsyaiva dyotanārtham /
anyā hi devatā 'trānīyamānā''tmīyaṃ dharmamuccaiṣva jahyāt paradharmamupāṃśutvaṃ prāpnuyāditi viruvam /
viṣṇuprajāpatyosta pratyāsannadharmakatvādavirodhastathāgnīṣomayostviti vidhāyaka devanāvidhyasaṃbhavādyathāsaṃbhavagrahapona paurṇamāsīkālasya vidhāyake ignīṣomānuvādaḥ prāśimupoinnayati 
prāye vacanāca 
hṛdayamupaśuyāja iti yajñapuruṣasya pradhānaprāyeṇāvayavena saṃstavātpradhānamityavagamyate /
kathaṃ punarapradhānatvaṃ pūrvapace prasajyate /
ucyate 
sāvatāmagnīṣomāviti yo 'gnīṣomadevatyaḥ sa evaikaḥ kāna viśeṣa saṃyuktaḥ pūrṇamāsagrahaṇena phale codate /
tatra vaiṣṇa ghaprājāpatya yorguṇābhāvātma kalopaśuyājaprādhānyavacanānupapattiḥ /
nanu tavāpi vaikalpikadoṣatvāddevatāsu yadaivāgnīṣomīyadevatyaḥ tadaiva prādhānyamiti nityavatpradhānatvasaṃkīrtanaṃ naiva ghaṭate /
naiṣa doṣaḥ 
yadi hyagnīṣomayoreva paurṇamāmosaṃbandhaḥ kriyate tato vi ṣṇuprajāpatipañce na syāt /
ayaṃ punarhevatopanaścitasya yāgasya saṃbandhaḥ /
sarvatra copalakṣaṇāpāye 'pyupancacyaṃ gṛhyate yathā vakṣyatyanapāyaśca kālasya lakṣaṇaṃ hi puroḍāśāviti /
na vaikasyaiva karmaṇaḥ kadā citpradhānatvaṃ kadā ciḍhaṅgatvamityupapadyate /
nānāve tvaviruddhaṃ syāt /
na ca saṃbhavati tat /
tasmādeka karmatvāyopāṃśuyājamantarā yajatītyayameva vidhiḥ 
tantravārtika /
āvārāgnihotramarūpatvāt 
ūrdhvamāghārayati taṇḍulairju hototyādibhirevaṃbhūtā eva āghārā homāśca vihitā viparivarttante /
na hi viṣṇurupāṃśu ya ghṛvya ityādivad dravyaprādhānyena yāgahomabhāvanayorabhibhavaḥ 
na caitrāmekavākyatvaṃ na ca stutiparā śrutiḥ /
aikāntiko vidhistena guṇavatkarmagocaraḥ 
vidhitvaṃ prayayopāttaṃ na nāmapadammṛcchati/
taddidhirbhāvanātaśceścaiva pūrvaṃ vidhīyatām 
saṃjñopabandhāt 
api ca 
sāmānyaṃ svādidaṃ jñeyaṃ jñātatvānna kriyāntaram /
tadajñeyatayā'nyatra vidhānamavakalpate 
āghāramagnihotramiti dvitīyānirdeśaḥ kriyeśitasya kā rakasya yujyate /
na ca juhotyāghārayatibhyāmātmaivāpnu mithya te/
svātmani kriyāvirodhā, tmamudāyaḥ punarniṣkṛṣya śabdenārthāntarātmanoccamānaḥ śakyaḥ sādhyatvenābhidhātuṃ, yathaudanapākaṃ pacatīti viśeṣaḥ sāmānyenetitamaḥ karmatvenocyate /
nanu ca samudāyasyāvyatirekānna kathaṃ citmādhyatvamavasīyatasannavārtika /
ityayuktameva karmatvaṃ, na avayava kriyāpracayasādhyatvātmamudāyasya /
samastābhyo hi samudāya syāvyatirekādevamupādānaṃ na syāpracekarūpātu samasta rūpamarthāntaramiṣṭaṃ, na ca pratyeka rūpairvinā samastarūpaniṣpattirityupapannamomitatamatvam /
nanu caivamādayaḥ samudāyitracanatvenāvadhāritā iti samudāyināṃ svātmani kri yāvirodhastadavastha eva syāt /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
samudāyivacanenāpi prātipadikena samudāyopi lakṣaṇayā gamyate /
tatasyaikatvavatkarmatvaṃ samadāyasya pratyeṣyate /
na ca sāmānya viśeṣabhede nāpi bhavataḥ kriyātvakarmatve pākavatsaṃbhavataḥ sāmānya viśeṣa śabdayobhedanānupādānāt /
etacca paurṇamāsīmityatrāpi sidvānte yojyaṃ, tasmāttaddadeva samudāyānuvādatvam 
codanā vā śabdārthasya prayogabhūtatvāttatsaṃnidherguṇārthena punaḥ śrutiḥ 
karmacodane syātāmiti vaktavyentaragrahaṇamupāṃśuyājādhika raṇavanneyam/
ācārayatijuhotyorananyāścipta vidhiśaktitvātka prayogavidhānameva śabdārtha ityavagamyate /
na ca prakṛtāghārahomasadbhāvaḥ, prakṛtavākyasthānāṃ vidhīnāmaprāśadadhyādyākṣiptāyāṃ vidhiśaktau karmānuvādabuddhyanapāyāt /
na cedanyena śiṣṭā iti vāpavādānna viśiṣṭa vidhānanyāyaḥ saṃbhavati /
taddarśayatyasminhi sati vidhāne pratyakṣaṃ na saṃbandhaḥ śaknotyarthādānepnumityarthaḥ/
atha vā asminhi sati saṃbandhividhāvitareṇa guṇavidhānena saṃbandha etra kevala āśrīyate /
tasmānnaita dvākyanirapekṣaiḥ saṃbandhavidhibhiraryādaparau kalpayituṃ homāghārau śakate ya innenānayoranuvādatvaṃ syāt /
bhāvanādhātvarthāvujhinvā na vi dhidhyādibhiḥ saṃbadhyataiti cetsatyameta,nna vidhitvaṃ bhāvanāta uttāryate tadgatenaiva tu guṇaḥ saṃspṛṇyate, guṇasya kāraka vibhaktyā bhāvanāmadhyanikṣepāt/
tenaitadupadiṣṭaṃ bhavati sarvacaiva viśiṣṭavi dhānottarakālaṃ kiṃ prāptaṃ kiṃ na prāptamiti anveṣaṇāyāmaprāptamātraviṣayopasaṃhārāt vidhirbhāvanādhātvarthayoranuvāda itya bhidhīyate /
na tvādita eva tāvanūdya guṇo dravyaṃ vā vidhīyataiti kadācidapi śākhārthābhivyaktiḥ /
tatra paścāttane vyāpāre mandabuddhipratipattyarthaṃ sthūlena nyāyena kathyamāne śāstrakṛtā evai! tā vacanavyaktaya iti manyamānāḥ svayamivānyeṣāmapi bhrāntimutpādayituma śrutiprakārān paradaurbalyavataḥ ke cirśayanti /
prathamaḥ kina śrutiprakāro dhātvarthavidhānaṃ, dvitīyaḥ saguṇaṃ dhātvarthavidhānaṃ, tṛtīyaḥ kiṃ ciduddiśya dhātvarthavidhānaṃ, caturthaḥ tatraiva viśiṣṭavidhānaṃ, pañcamastu dhātvarthoddaśenānyasya dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
vidhānaṃ, ṣaṣṭhastu dhātvarthenānyayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ, saptamaḥ punarvātvarthaviśiṣṭena pratyayenānyayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ, aṣṭamasta mukkā dhātvarthamanyayoreva saṃbandha, iti /
tatra tāvadyaducyate agnihotraṃ juhotītyetadvātvarthavidhānamiti tadayuktam /
na hi vidhirbhāvanāmutsṛjya dhātvarthe nipatati, na ca bhāvanāṃ mukkā 'nyatra puruṣaḥ pravarttate /
sāhi puruṣasya svavyāpāro dhātvarthastu kadā citkarmāśritoṣi bhavati /
yathāyameva praśnapo dvyavadānāśrito, na cānyadīyaṃ vyāpāramanyaḥ śaknoti katrtumityavagyaṃ bhāvanāviśeṣaṇatvādeva dadhyā divadvātvartho vidhātavyaḥ /
idaṃ ca bhāvārthādhikaraṇe 'bhihitaṃ yayā na dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatvena vidhīyataiti /
na hyakaraṇabhūto sau sādhyāpeścatvāi/kyāntareṇāpi phanne vidhātuṃ śakyeta /
somena yajenaityatrāpi tadbhūtādhikaraṇoktena mārgeṇa dhātvarthakārakāpāmarupaukāyanyādivatparaspareṇāsaṃbadhya bhāvanāsaṃbaddhānāmutarakālaṃ parasparopakāritvam /
tathā ca saptamanavamādyayorvacyatīti na viśiṣṭadhātvarthavidhānam/
bhāvanāṃca prati yāgamya kāraṇatvād dravyaṃ prati karmatve satyeka śabdye parārthavadityetadāpadyataityayuktametat /
tathā śrī donproścatītyatra na prokṣaṇena brīcīniti kaścimaṃbandhastenobhayoḥ karotyarthasaṃbandhāna dhātvartho vrīhiṣu vidhoyate /
yadi tu bhāvanābhiprāyeṇānyatra vidhānamucyate ta tsarvatrāviśiṣṭam/
na cāsya viśiṣṭavidhānād durbalatvamastīti /
tṛtīya sthānaniveśo 'pyayuktaḥ /
pakṣadvayoktamapi nirākaraṇaṃdaśāpavitreṇa grahaṃ saṃmāṣṭotyatrāpyāpadyate ityayuktamanyatra vi śiṣṭadhātvarthavidhānam/
ḍhaghnā juhotītyatrāpi na kadā vidhihome karotītyayamarthaḥ śabdenocate /
na hi homasyādhikaraṇatvaṃ tantravārtike /
śabdādastuto vā sivaṃ, na ca dadhnaḥ karttavyatā nityaṃ karaṇātmakatvāt /
iyamapi ca śrutirddhividhādapi viśiṣṭa vidherbalīyasī ekavidhisaṃbhave 'nekaśaktikatvānupapatterubhayapakṣabhāvinaśca viprakṛ ṭārthavidheraparyanuyojyatvāt nikṛṣṭāsaṃbhavakṛtameva cāsya viprakṛ ṭasya grahaṇaṃ, tatrobhayāśrayaṇe yugapadvipratiṣid saṃbhavāsaṃbhavāpattiragatyaiva gṛhate 'nyatra viśiṣṭadhātvarthavidhānānnātigurkhe veti na pañcame sthāne niveśayitavyā /
kāmaṃ vā śuddhadhātvarthavidhānāt tasya vā 'nyatra vidheranantarā karttavyā/
yattu prākāśāvadhvaryave dadātītyanena dadātidhātvarthe prākāśādhvaryusaṃbandho vidhīyataiti tadayuktam /
vacanavyaktya vivekātmarvatra hi ya cchabdenānūdyamānamupanivadhya tacchabdayaktaṃ vidheyamupanīyate/
tadina yadi tāvadyadahātītya trādhvarguprākāśayoḥ saṃbandha iti vidhīyate tataḥ sakaladānānuvādātma mastadakṣiṇāvikārapramaṅgaḥ /
pratyayasya cānekavidhiśaktikalpanā codite sati karmaeyaparihataiva/
saṃbandho hi vidhīyamānaḥ saṃbandhinaṃ tāvadākṣipe,dvātvarthe tu punaḥ sa vidhānavya eva saṃbandhī anyathā saṃbandhasyaiva saṃbandhī śeṣaḥ syāt na kriyāyāḥ /
tatraitalyādvātvarthānuraktaḥ pratyayo viḍhadhaḍhavaśyameva tatra vidhāsyatīti /
evaṃ tardhuttarayorapi śrutyoracaivāntarbhāvādbhedenopādānaṃ vyarthaṃ, na hi vāyavyaṃ śvetamālabheta ḍhaghnendriyakāmasya juhuyāditi dhātvarthānanuraktaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃbandhaṃ vidadhātīti /
prakṛtiliṅgamātraphala śvānnabhati ruccāryamāṇo na dravyadevatāsaṃvandhividhāvātmānurañjanena kiṃ cir̤hapakaroti /
na cā'sau saṃvandha ājabhatinā saṃpādayituṃ śakyo yāgaviṣayatvād dravyadevatayoḥ /
yadi cānyadvitīya pāda /
saṃvandhakaraṇe pratyayoccāraṇasiddhivyatiriktaṃ kiṃ cid dhātuḥ kuryāt /
tato dadhīndriyasaṃbandhavidhāne kimiti homaḥ parityajyeta kimiti vā prakaraṇāntabhyo 'bhyupagamyeta /
tasmānna dhāsvarthe'nyasaṃvandhavidhiḥ /
pūrvavacca dhātvarthādhikaraṇatā kārakakarttavyatā ca nirākarttavyā /
na ca dhātvarthe saṃbandhasyāpi prāgbhāvanāsaṃgatervidhirityuktam /
evaṃ tāvanna dānamātre saṃvandhavidhiḥ /
athādhvaryu viśiṣṭaṃ dānamanūdyatām  adhvaryurvā tadviśiṣṭaḥ evamapi śiṣṭānuvādā  dvākyabhedaḥ/
śudvādhvarśvanuvāde tu yadyapi saṃpradānaśruterarthāhānamā cipyate tathāpi saṃpradāna saṃpradeya saṃbandhasya dadātimantareṇānupapadyamānatvād dravyadevatā saṃbandhādiva yajeḥ kapana miti na dhātvarthe 'nyasaṃbandha iti vacanavyaktiḥ saṃbhavati/
vayaṃ cātrādānādhvarkhe codakena prāptatvātprākāśāveva vidhātavyaiau
vidhitve bhāvanāsthe 'pi tādathyaṃ pravibhajyate /
viśeṣaṇaphane cāsminvākyabhedo bhaviṣyati 
samadāyānuvādasya na tāvat dṛśyate phalam/
prayogavacanaikatvaṃ lapsyate rājasvayavat 
agnibhyo'pūrvasiddhiḥ syādādhāratvopalaścitā /
caikenāvarudvatvādādhārāntarasaṃbhavaḥ 
yattu sāyaṃprātavāṃkyayora nekārthatvātkarmavidhitvamiti /
tatra brūmaḥ /
sāyaṃ juhoti prātarjuhotīti vākyāntaraprāptaḥ kālo devatāvyavasthāpare vākye saṃkorcyate /
nanvevamapi kāla viśiṣṭakarmānuvādādākyabhedaḥ syāt/
na, prakaraṇalabdha karmaṇi kālamātre devatāvi dhānāt /
sa tu kālo na svarūpeṇa devatayā saṃvadhyataiti prakaraṇa nabhyakarmānuraktaḥ saṃbadhyate /
atha vā vidhīyamānasaṃpradānabhūtadevatākāṅkṣitaprakṛtahomaparyupasthāpane na kālasyopa yogaḥ /
na ca lakṣaṇayā ubhyamāno homo vākyaṃ bhinatti /
na ca sāyaṃkālenānyatra sthito lakṣitaḥ tena sāyaṃhomasyāgniprajāpatī bhaviṣyataḥ /
evaṃ pratamasya sūryaprajāpatī iti siddham /
namvevamapi bhinnapadopātte dve dve devate vidadhatī vākye bhidyeyādvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
tām /
na, ekakārakatvāditi ke cit /
kārakānyatve hi vidhervyāpārabhedo bhavati ekakārakanibandhanaṃ tvarthasahasramadhyekaprayatna sādhyamityuktam /
atrābhidhīyate 
vibhaktyā hi kārakaṃ pratyāyyate /
sā ca yatraikāgnīṣomādau tatra sakṛdeva pratyayasya vyāpāro bhavati /
yatra punaḥ bhinna vibha 'ktasaṃbaddhānekapadopāttamekamapi kārakaṃ bhavati yathā 'caivāyeca prajāpataye ceti, tatra yugapatpratyaveśaṇābhāvāda vaśyaṃ bhedenāgniprajāpato pratyayenānocāyatavyaiau /
kāraka vibhaktiāī nāma padārthālocanāya pratyayaprayuktā sā ca nānoccāritānāṃ naiva prayuṅkte ityāvṛttiprasaṅgaḥ /
tasmānnaiṣa parihāra ityevamabhidhīyate /
vākyadaye'pyasminprajāpatiraveko vidhīyate /
agnisūryayoḥ punamaintravarṇādeva prāptiḥ vākyāntaraṇetyevaṃdevatyā ma ntrī vihita 
kāmyaḥ sarvāṅgasaṃyuktaḥ prayogaśca phacārthinā /
sāyaṃprātarvikalpena prayoktavyastadā bhavet 
dravyasaṃyogācodanā paśusomayoḥ pra karaṇe hyanarthako dravya saṃyogo na hitasya guṇārthena 
paśorduṣpratipādanataratvātpūrvābhidhānam /
hau vātra śabdā sahāyānuvādatvenāśayate paśuśabdastadagnīṣomasaṃbandhānumitaśca yajiḥ /
īdṛśaṃ hyetadvākyaṃ śrutānumitaikadeśaniṣpannaṃ yadagnīṣomīyeṇa paśunā yajeteti 
yathāgneyādivākyānāṃ na prāgyāgānumānataḥ /
svārthaparyavasāyitvaṃ tathā some 'pi gamyatām 
api ca taveha caindravāyavā divākyeṣu ca /
matpane tu teṣveva kevaleṣviti viśeṣaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
ekacaiveśe guṇe śrayamāṇe vidhiśaktiḥ saṃkrāmatītyagnihotre 'bhihitam/
ato na karmānuvādabuddhirapaitītyanuvādatvaṃ yajeḥ /
tatra somaśabdena dravyameva gṛhṇātinā sāmānyākṣiptaṃ niyamyate /
atha vā somaṃ krīṇāti somamabhiṣuṇoti somaṃ pāvyatītyādibhiḥ prākaraṇikairguṇavākyaiḥ somarase kalpite gṛhāticodanāḥ pravṛttā iti somo na vidhīyate /
tataśca svābhāvikakaraṇatvayukta yāgasāmānādhikaraṇyāttatprakhyaṃ cānyaśāstramiti nāmadheyī bhavati /
nanu jyotiṣṭoma ityaparaṃ nāmadheyamadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
styeva /
yadīdamapyavagamyate kiṃ no bādhyate/
tathā ca yājñikānāṃ vyavahāreṣu nāmadayamupannabhāmahe /
samastavākyānuvādasya tu ta deva prayojanaṃ yat prayogavākyagataikatvopajananaṃ nāma /
tasmādanuvādaiti /
bhavedana dravyadevatāsaṃyogāḍhavam /
paśau tu vatmamālabhetetyetatmahaśena devatārahitahṛdayādidravyamātra saṃyoginā 'vadyatinā kathaṃ yāgavidhānaṃ, kathaṃ vā hṛdayādyanuvādaḥ paśugrahaṇeneti vaktaram /
uccate 
hṛdayādibhiḥ prakṛtidravye 'peścite mantravarṇācchāge labdhe ta dantargataṃ paśutvaṃ tābadanūdyate /
tatra tu devatāyāṃ vihitāyāṃ yāgo vidhīyatāṃ nāma /
athavā sāṃnāyyaṃ vā tatprabhavatvādityanenaiva nyāyenāyamavadyatiḥ sārūpyātmāṃnā vyāvadyatiprakṛtiḥ sa ca darśapūrṇamāsayāgadravyasaṃskārārthaḥ prasiddhaḥ /

sopyanabhyastaḥ tathā 'vasthitaṃ na śaknoti sarvaṃ saṃbhāvayitu,miti prayojanavaśenābhyasyate tena tatrāpi sūtram /

tata eka eva saṃbandhaḥ saptadaśānāṃ dravyāṇā me kasyāśca devatāyā ityekakarmatvam /
atha tu prajāpatirdevatā 'syeti prājāpatyaśca prājāpatyaśceti saptadaśakṛtva uccārya prājāpatyā iti sarūpaikaśeṣaḥ kriyate tataḥ saptadaśaiva dravyadevatāsaṃyogāḥ pṛthakpradarśitā iti pratisaṃyogaṃ yāgānumānātkarmabhedaḥ /

ekakarmeti /
kutaḥ 
yo hi prājāpatyaḥ prājāpatyaścetyevamekaśeṣaṃ karoti tenobhayoḥ prakṛtipratyayayorasāvabhyupagato bhavati tasya ca nimi taṃ bahuvacanānyathānupapattiḥ /
na ca tatprātipadike bahuvacanamupalabhyate yena tasyāpyeka śeṣaḥ kriyate /
na ca tadekaśeṣamantareṇa pratyayārthasya darśayituṃ na śakyate /
vigṛhyamāṇavelāyāṃ sarvanāmnā kathyamānatvāt /

kiṃ ca 
kṛtvāpi hi tadvitantenaiva caikaśeṣaṃ na tāvanmātreṇa mucyate punaradṛṣṭā śrutāni karmāṇya pūrvāṇi ca kalpayitavyāni, na ca tāni yatheṣṭaṃ kalpayituṃ labhyantaityuktaṃ śabdāntarādhikaraṇe /
ya mātreṇa vinā coditadravye  devatāsaṃbandhānupapattiḥ tanmātramevādṛṣṭānamarthāpatyā kalpayituṃ śakyate nānyat /
tenābhyadhikaṃ na labhyate /
avaśyaṃ hyekādikrameṇa saptadaśa karmāṇyapūrvāṇi ca kalpayitavyāni /
tatra prathama kalpanenaivānuṣṭhāna tantratvavada gṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvātsarvadravyāṇi yāgavanti jātānīti nopariṣṭāgantuṃ śakyate, kiṃ ca 
yadi hi dravyabhedānkriyāṇāṃ bhedaḥ syāt/
tato hṛdayādibhedena dvyavadānabhedenāpi vā bhedaḥ syāt /
na cārhati bhavituṃ vakṣyati hyapi vā vyatirekādrūpaśabdā vibhāgācceti /
prakṛtau ca kṛtsne paśau yāgasādhanatvena codite tathaivotsraṣṭavye prāpte hṛdayāghekādaśāvadānaprakṛtitvena paśunā yāgaḥ sādhayitavya iti vākyāntaravaśādavagamyate /
tenāsā paśordharmo na yāgasya /
ichāpi sapradaśānāṃ yāgasādhanatve 'vagate 'tideśena pratyekaṃ sarvadharmāḥ prāpyantaityeko 'pi yāgaḥ saptadaśāvadānagaṇānatideśena gṛhṇanna vihanyate /
tasmādekaṃ karmeti prāpta ucyate 
na hotadetāvatyeva vākyaṃ paryavasyati prājāpatyānpaśṭaniti, kiṃ tarhi prakṛtivadityaparo vākyaśeṣaḥ /
ekakarmatve cātra sava nīyaḥ prakṛtirbhavet /
taca caiko 'vadānagaṇe yāgasya  sādhanadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
māsīdityatrāpyeka eva prāpnoti, sopika saṃpa niṣpanna āsīditi tādṛgeva karttavyaḥ /
tataścainaiva paśunā si dvattvānna paścantarāṇi prajāpatinā saṃbadhyante iti khapadopāttaṃ bahutvaṃ vākyaprāptaṃ ca saptadaśatvamubhayamapi nānuṣṭhoyeta /
yadā tu saptadaśa yāgā iti buddhiḥ kriyate tadā pratikarmāvasāyibhisrodakaistā vanta evāvadānagaṇāḥ prāpyante, tatsidyarthaṃ cāśrutānāmapi saptadaśānāṃ paśūnāmāgamaḥ kriyate, kiṃ punaḥ śrutānāmupādānam /
nanu ca pratyakṣaṃ yāgaikatvamutsṛjya na yuktamānumānika codakānurodhena nānātvaṃ kalpayituṃ paśyaḥ /
yāgopadeśavelāyā mekānekatvakalpanā /
tadaśenānideśava nopade śasta dāśrayaḥ 
saṃdigdhe vākyaśeṣebhyo nirṇayaḥ prāksamarthitaḥ /
sāmarthyāca tadatrāsti iyanirṇaya kāraṇam 
prājāpatyapaśuyāgena bhāvayetkathamiti hyapecyate, na paśunā kathamiti, tyajyamānatvena dravyasya jñānaprakāratvāt /
prakṛtāvapi caikapaśuniṣpannaikādaśāvadānagaṇasādhyatvaṃ yāgadharmaḥ /
na paśorniṣphalatvāt /
tadrmatvapakṣe hyavadānairasau saṃskriyeta dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
na ca tena  prayojanaṃ vināśitatvāt /
yāgena tu siddhenārthasta saṃbandhinā 'pūrveṇa veti sarvamidaṃ tannirvṛttiprakāratvenāśrīyate /
tasmānnaiko yāgonekagaṇaṃ samarthe/
grahītum/
na ca tadagrahe 'nekapaśugrahaṇam /
yadyapi cāvadānaprakṛtere katvaṃ saptadaśasaṃkhyayā bādhyata iti nānāpaśuniṣpanna eka eva gaṇo gṛhyatāmiti buddhirbhavet tathāpyekādaśa paśava upayujyeran na saptadaśa /
na tvekasminnapi yāge saptadaśabhiravadāna gaṇairyacyata ityanekādṛṣṭa kalpanābhayātpaśuśabdenāvada/
nagaṇaṃ yāgapratyāsattecayitvā tatpa ricchedārthā saptadaśasaṃkhyā vidhāsyataiti manyate /
naitadevaṃ jakṣaṇākāraṇābhāvāt /
na hyasati virodhe lakṣaṇā yuktā tenaitahasaṃkaṭamāpadyate /
saptadaśa paśavaḥ karttavyāḥ ekena cāvadānagaṇenaikapaśu niṣpannenaiko yāgaḥ sādhayitavya iti /
na caitatkathaṃ cidanuṣṭhānaṃ  śakyam /
athānyatrāpi śrutā saṃkhyā nyatrāpi nīyate tato 'pūrvapratyāsannatareṣu vara yāgeṣveva kalpitā /
na cāvirodhasaṃbhavātkiṃ cidapi codakasya bādhanīyamityuktam /
pramāṇavaśāccānekādṛṣṭakalpanāpi nirderdoṣā /
kṛtsnavākyagama nikārthaṃ śṛṅgābhiprāyādyupanyāsaḥ /
etaduktaṃ bhavati /
ye saptadaśavarṇādibhedabhinnāḥ paśavasteṣāṃ kaścitprājāpatyaḥ karttavya iti tatrāha /
te hi śyāmāsvaparāḥ  śrūyante tasmātsaptadaśa yāgā iti /
prayojanaṃ yadyapi pūrvapakṣavādino nābhipretaṃ tathāpyekasyaiva sājhādyāgasādhanatvamitare tatsaṃkhyāsaṃpādanārthamupādīyante ityeka smādavadātavyam /
tadvināśe cetarepyāvartteran /
atha vā 'rddhakṛteṣu saṃ skāreṣu ya eva naṣṭastatraiva samastānāmāvṛttiḥ /
nanu ca yathaiva saptadaśasu yāgeṣu sadda kriyamāṇeṣu ekavināśe satyahargaṇe tu yasminnavaccheda ityanena nyāyenetareṣu pratīcyamāṇeṣu sa evāvarttate tathaiva dravyasāhityepi syāt /
naitadevaṃ, tathāhi saptadaśasaṃkhyaikārthamamavāyi vyāsaṅgi yāgasādhanatvamiti tādṛśasyaivopākaraṇādibhirmavitavyam/
tatra yadeva dravyaṃ naṣṭaṃ tenaiva vinā yathāmādhanavināśo jātaiti sarve saṃskārāstiṣṭhat khapi dravyeṣu sādhanātpracyutā iti punarādita eva karttavyāḥ /
tathā yasyāpyabhinavānītamya te kriyante tasyāpi te sādhanabhūtasya śrutāḥ /
na ca saptadaśatvena vināsya sādhanatvamastīti tatmidvaye 'vaśyamitare'pyapekṣitavyā iti/
siddhānte tvanyonyanirapekṣa sādhanatvaśaktiyuktānāṃ sahaprayogamātraṃ kriyate ityupapannā tanmātrāvṛttiḥ /
nanvevaṃ sati pūrvapakṣanyāyena stotraśastreṣu tāṃ caturbhirādatte ityādiṣu caikamantravināśe samastāvṛttiḥ prāpnoti /
na, tatra pratyekaṃ sādhanatve sati vacanena samuccayāśrayaṇāt /
yatkurvāṇā hi te mantrāḥ stotrādīni mādhayanti tatraiṣāṃ pratyekākāṅkṣānivarttanasāmarthyam/
anyathā hyekamantranaiva syāt /
bhinnaireva ca prātyātmikairmantrakāryaiḥ saṃhatya kāryāntaramārabhyate na mantreṣu vyāsaṅgi māghanatvam /
paśūnāṃ tu vyāmaṅgītyuktam /
mantrakā ryāṇāṃ tarhi saṃhatyakāritvādekavināśe samastāvṛttiḥ syāt /
naitadasti sādhanavinā śavyatirekeṇa kāryavināśābhāvāt /
sādhaneṣveva puruṣasya vyāpāra iti tadvināśānurodhenaivānuṣṭhāna mi ti viśeṣaḥ 
anukta karmaśabde yā saṃjñā pūrva pravarttate /
na vastvantarabuddheḥ sā kathaṃ cidapanīyate 
saṃjñānadīvyavacchinno yajiḥ pūrvaṃ na gacchati /
na ca pūrvastamityevaṃ banādarthāntaraṃ gataḥ 
siṃcaśabdaḥ kva cigauṇo māṇavādau nirūpitaḥ /
nājambheśrayamāṇopi tadarthaḥ parigṛhyate 
tantravārtika /
guṇacāpūrvasaṃyoge vākyayoḥ samatvāt 
ataḥ paraṃ prāka prakaraṇabhedād guṇanimitto bhedābhedavicāro varttiṣyate /
cāturmāsyeṣu vaiśvadeve parvaṇi vaiśvadevyāmiśceti dravyadevatāsaṃyogānumitaṃ yāgaṃ vidhāyocyate vājibhyo vājinamiti /
tatra saṃdehaḥ /
kiṃ tasminneva karmaṇi guṇavidhiḥ utānenāpi dravyadevatā saṃyogena yāgāntaraṃ kalpyate /
tatrobhayamapi dravyadevataṃ pūrvatra vidhīyate iti pakṣaḥ saṃbhavannāpi nopanyastaḥ /
pramāṇāntara prāpte karmaṇyaneka guṇa vidhānasya paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇe ni rākṛtatvāt /
tena vājinameva kevalaṃ kiṃ pūrvasminkarmaṇi tayā ca devatayā saṃbadhyate, uta devatāntareṇa yāgāntareṇa cāpūrveṇa saṃbadhyataiti /
kiṃ prāptam pūrvacaiva vājinaguṇa vidhānamiti /
kutaḥ anantaropadiṣṭena vājenānnena vājinaḥ /
viśve devāḥ pratīyante tacca karmeha vājinam 
guṇāntara/varudvatvātpūrva karmaṇya saṃbhavāt /
kriyāntaramatiṃ kuryādātmasaṃgataye guṇaḥ 
tadvitena caturdhyā vā mantravarṇena ceṣyate /
devatāsaṃgatistatra durbalaṃ ca paraṃ param 
devatāsaṃgatiḥ śrutyā tadvitantāpratīyate /
caturthyantāttu vākyena padadvayasamīpataḥ /
vaiśvadevīti hi śrutyaiva devatāsaṃbandhaḥ pratītaḥ  /
itaratra tu vājibhyo vājinamiti padadvayasāmopyādgamyate /
nanciāpyāmiścāpadasaṃnidhānavaśenaiva dravyadevatāsaṃbandhaḥ pratīyataiti tulyaṃ vākyagamyatvaṃ bhavet/
śratha vaiśvadevīti śrutya /
devatātvaṃ vākyena dravyasaṃbandhaḥ sa ihāpyaviśiṣṭaḥ /
caturthośrutyā devatātve'bhihite vākyena dravyasaṃgatimātrakaraṇāt /
atha dravyamātrasaṃbandhe tadvitāntenaiva kṛte viśeṣamātramāmiśrāpada sannidherbhaviṣyatītyucyate /
tadapya viśiṣṭa mitaratrāpi /
vājibhya ityeka padenaiva saṃpradānaṃ bruvatā saṃpradeyādinā taḍhanupapatteḥ sāmānyākṣepe sati vājinapadasaṃnidhānena viśeṣamātrapratīteḥ /
api ca bhavatu nāma tadvitaśruterdravyamātra saṃbandhaḥ /
tattu dravyamācaṃ vājinepyavi śiṣṭamiti na virudhyate /
viśeṣa yo svāmikṣāvājinayorvirodhaḥ /
tayośvobhayatra vākyannabhyasaṃvandhatvādaviśeṣaḥ /
tena vikalpaḥ prānotyeva /
taducyate 
viśve devā devatāsyā iti cina sarvanāmnā dravyasāmānyamabhidhīyate /
kiṃ tarhi sannihito viśeṣaḥ sa eva vyavadārakṣamaḥ nānirūpitaṃ dravyamātrama/
ataḥ prātipaṭikena yortha upāttaḥ sa dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
pramāṇāntaragamyasya dravyaviśeṣasya devatetyetattadvitena śrutyaivīcate /
tataścāntarṇīta saṃbandha devatopasarjanadravya viśeṣapratyaye padāntaranirapeśeṇa tadvitāntena padena nirvattita kaḥ punarasau dravyaviśeṣo yasya taddhitena devatoktetyanveṣaṇāyāmayamityāmijhāpadenopanīyate /
tatra yadā tāvatprāgeva viśiṣṭa pratyayātsaṃbandhobhihitaḥ tadāna lakṣyamāṇo bhavati /
athāpi prakṛtipratyayayoḥ svārthavṛttayoreva nairantaryādantarāle saṃbandhavigamyamāno bhavati tathāpyatraikapadasthatvātpadaiya saṃnidhigamyāinīyānvijñāyamānaḥ śrīta ityucyate /
tesaṃbandhāveko dravyadevatāsaṃbandha/paro viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ /
tatra pūrvaḥ śrotaḥ uttaro vākyalakṣaṇa iti viśeṣaḥ /
aśva naivātra nīlotpalādivadarthadvāra vaiśvadevyāmikā śabdayorviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ, kiṃ tarhi 
naivātra tadvitāntenaikorthobhihitaḥ/
āmikṣāpade nānyaḥ paścātayorviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatā, taddhitāntavācyasya prathamapratītaḥ/
kiṃtahi tadvitāntasyānupayukta midhānabhaktareva pratīkṣamāṇasyopapadena viṣayadānamācaṃ kriyate /
tenāmikṣāpadmannidhibanā īśvadevīśabda eva tāmabhidhatte /
na cedānīmā miśca padasyānuvādatvaṃ, tena vinā taddhitāntasya tadviṣayatvāpratīteḥ /
na ca vākyārthatvaṃ, ta dvitāntapadārthasya pṛthagaprasiddheḥ /
na hi hai/
svatantrī padārthāvagṛhītvā vākyārthaḥ pratīyate tenābhidheyopanayanamātrakāritvānna taddhitaśrutairāmiśrāpadenārthaṃ viprakarṣaḥ kriyate /
tathā cāha /
śrutyaivopapadārthaḥ sarvanāmnābhidhīyate /tantravārtika /
tadartha stadvitenaivaṃ trayāṇā me kavācyatā 
vājibhya iti tu nātra prātipadikena vibhaktyā vobhābhyāṃ vā dravyasāmānya viśeṣatatsaṃbandhānāmanyatamada pyabhidhīyate /
kiṃ tarhi prātipadikārthaḥ saṃpradānamityetāvanmātramityuktam /
tatra na kathaṃ cid dravyasaṃbandhaḥ padentargata ityavaśyaṃ vākyenaiva vājinapada sāmīpyāta pratyāyayitavyaḥ /
api ca /
yathehāsya padārthopi tadvitentargataḥ smṛtaḥ /
na saṃpradānamasyeti catuyevaṃ vidhīyate 
sarvaprakāramāmikṣāsaṃbandhasya sannikarṣannavaṇaṃ śrautatvam /
vājinasaṃbandhe ca viprakarṣādā kyīyatvaṃ, tadyathā /
yadyapi tāvad dravyaviśeṣasya taddhito na brūyāddevatātvaṃ tathāpi sāmānyasya tāvad bravīti na caturthyantena sāmānyamapyucyataiti viśeṣaḥ /
yattu sāmānyaṃ vājinepya viruddha miti tadayuktam /
vaiśvadevīti hi strīpratyayena samānapadgatenaiva strodravyaṃ kimapi sannicitamityavadhāryate /
na ca vājinasya khītvaṃ sannidhirvāstīti anāśrayaṇam /
api ca /
vājibhyo vājinaṃ kuryāditi naivāsti saṃgatiḥ /
tatra tatmiye'vaśyaṃ dānādhyāhārakalpanā 
na cātra sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃca paṇyāmaḥ /
na ca vājibhya iti kāraka vibhaktiḥ kriyāpadādanyena saṃbadhyate na ceca tadupāttam/
tatrādhyā cārakalapanādeko viprakarṣaḥ/
tripada saṃbandhagauravādaparaḥ /
itaratrāpi yajikarūpanāda viśeṣa iti cet /
na, tasyasaṃbandhottara kālānumeyatvā, dvaiśvadevyāmikṣeti hi niṣpanne saṃvandhe yajiranumīyate na tadadhīnā saṃbandhapratītiḥ /
tava tu parakhatvāpādanāsaṃbhavātma ca bhaviṣyatyarthasaṃbandhārtham, āditaśca dravyadevatāpakavākyatva siddhaye dadātiriti viśeṣaḥ /
kalpite dadātau kārakayoḥ parasparasaṃbandhābhāvāttena tāvatma saṃva ndhaḥ /
tata ekārthatvātparasparaniyama iti viprakṛṣṭatā/
na tvāmicāyāṃ taitkiṃ ciditi sannikarṣaḥ /
satyapi ca vājivājinayoḥ sākṣātsaṃvandhe vaiyadhikaraṇyādviprakṛṣṭatvam /
vaiśvadevyā mitetitu sāmānādhikaraṇyātmannikṛṣṭatā /
tathā ca vayati samarthatarāṇi hi samānavibhaktīni bhavanti durbalo vivibhaktiriti/
kiṃ ca /
saṃpradānatvamātraṃ ca caturthī vājināṃ vadet /
devatā lakṣyamāṇā tu punarpūraṇa vājine 
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
vājibhya iti rūpasāmānyātprasaktaṃ sadyāvatpañcamotvamapanīya caturthītvaṃ sādhyate tāvanmativikṣepaḥ /
nanu taddhitepyanekā patyādyarthasaṃdecāttulyametat /
viṣama upanyāsaḥ /
śabdasaṃdeho mayopanyastaḥ tvayā arthasaṃdehaḥ /
sarvathā tāvattadvitatvamasaṃdigdham /
arthaḥ punayogyatvāditarāsaṃbhavena devatātmako nirpoṣyate bhavatastu nirṇo te'pi śabde catuṭayarthānekatvādupapadakāra kalavaṇa saṃdehādastyeva viprakarṣaḥ /
nenārthasaṃdeha ubhayoḥ samatvānneka śvodyate śabda saṃdehattva sādhāraṇatvāccoditaḥ /
kiṃ ca 
yathā cotpattiśiṣṭasya balīyastvaṃ na ca kriyāmācaṃ niṣkṛṣya guṇāntaraṃ vidhātuṃ śakyate tathoktaṃ citrādhikaraṇe vaiśvadevādhiraṇe ca /
vaiśvadevādhikaraṇanyāyena ca prakaraṇamapekṣitavyamapara vājinavākyena /
kutaḥ /
dravyadevatasaṃbandho yāgamātramapekṣate /
āmiyāyāga eveti tatra prakaraṇābhavet 
vājina iti hyavayavaprasiddhyā viśvadevāḥ pratyāyyante /
vākyārthaccāvayavārthī samuccitya saṃvandhaṃ kalpayitvā sā bhavantī śrutimātropanipātalabhyāyāḥ samudāyaprasiddherdurbalā bhavatīti dubelataraḥ saṃyogo vājinasya /
vājiśabdopi vā 'śva suniḥ svabhāvataḥ /
kleśanaiva vinā kāryādviśvadeveṣu  varttate 
sarve hyagnyādayaḥ puroḍāgādibhirannairvājino vijñāyante tatrāmijhāyāṃ tāvadannaśabdaḥ prayukto na puroḍāśādā vityekaḥ klemaḥ /
punarapi cāmikṣāmātragrahaṇe sati vaiśvadevyāmikṣayaiva tadvatāṃ grahaṇamityaparaḥ /
tataśca svarasena śrutiranyatrāpi varttamānā satī prakaraṇenaiva viśeṣe sthāpayitavyā, na ca tatra kiṃ cinnimittamasti /
guṇabhāvenopādīyamānatvāddevatāyāḥ /
saṃskāryatve ca vrohīnprocatītyādiṣviva kathaṃ cidapūrvasādhanalaśaṇayā  prakadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
tagrahaṇaṃ bhaveta, na cātra tadasti /
vināpi tena karmaṇa prayoja navattvopapatteḥ /
kāmaṃ vājinasyaiva pratipattiḥ saṃskāro bhaveta, na devatāyāḥ /
prakṛtagrahaṇe cāgnyādīnāṃ sadbhāvādanavadhāraṇam /
atha viśvadeveṣu sarve saṃgṛhītā bhaviṣyantīti teṣāṃ grahaṇam /
nadayuktam /
sarvasaṃgrahasyāpramāṇakatvāt /
bahuvacanaśrutyā sarvagra haṇamiti cet /
na tasya triṣveva caritārthatvāt na, triṣvavadhāraṇajñānamiti cet /
na makhyaṃ cāpūrvacoda nāmo kavadityavadhāraṇahetu sadbhāvāt /
tasmānna viśvedevagrahaṇe kiṃ citpramāṇam /
sākāṅkṣā ca devatā dravyeṇa saṃbadhyeta mā cātra vājiśabdena dravyavatyevo?pādīyamānā nirākāṅkṣava pratyāyiteti na dravyāntarasaṃbandhaṃ kṣamate, tasmādatulyavannatvam /
kiṃ ca 
anyena navaruddhe hi guṇo yatra vidhīyate /
tasminguṇavidhiḥ śakya iti karma na bhidyate 
homo hi prakṛtaḥ śuddhaḥ svavākyādavadhāritaḥ /
sosmin didhiviśiṣṭatvādvibhāgenaiva gamyate 
tānyutpattimapekṣante sā cāvyavahitā yataḥ /
guṇādīnāṃ tvasaṃvanvāyavadhiḥ syātparasparam 
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
vākyāntareṇa tatkarma yathā danā viśeṣitam /
taṇḍulādibhirapyevamiti naikātmakaṃ bhavet 
dadhyatra daśame pakṣe tadbomasya viśeṣaṇam /
nityaṃ cendriyakāmasya tenāpi na nirūpyate 
yatta dravyaṃ na pratyabhijñāyate na tatkarmabhedakāraṇam /
tasmāttadeva karma gumātrābhyadhikaṃ phaje vidhīyate/
naitadevam/
kutaḥ /
prāptaṃ karmaṇyane kāryavidhiḥ pūrvaṃ nirākṛtaḥ /
tvatyakṣaṃ 'neka saṃvandha vidhiśvāna prasajyate 
karmagabde'guṇe'pyatra karma bhūyo vidhīyate /
phalaṃ hi śrutametasminkarmatastacca yujyate 
nāsminparama sādṛśyaṃ dṛśyate kṛṣihomayoḥ /
kiṃ citmādṛśyadṛṣṭistu dravyepyastītya niścayaḥ 
yadyasya kāraṇabhūtaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ siddhe dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇi taccetmādhyepi pakṣe kāraṇabhūtamiti gamyate bhavati tattasya sādhaka miti /
a to vacanātkāryakāraṇayoreva gamyagamakabhāvo bhāṣyakārābhidvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
preta iti ke cinmanyante /
tattvayuktam /
akāryakāraṇabhūtānāmapyanityatvakṛta ṛtvādīnāṃ gamyagamakabhāvaprasiddha /
kāryakāraṇayorapi ca na tathā kāraṇaṃ gamakaṃ vyabhicārabahatvādyathā kāryam /
tasmāniṅgameva vyāpyatvena dṛṣṭaṃ sapane vyāpakasyānyatra sādhyabhūtasya gamakatva saṃbhāvanayā gṛhyamāṇaṃ kāraka  mityukta miti draṣṭavyam /
evaṃ ca hetvadhikaraṇe vyākhyātam /
tathā ca vivṛṇoti /
tasmātmādṛśyamapi sādhakamasādhakaṃ veti viparīvitavyamiti /
yadi tarhi parīkṣitena ca  kāraṇenābhihitena kāryamidamabhidhīyate /
danendriyakāmasyetyatra vākye yatkarma tatphannavatkarmatvāt kuṣyādivat /
karmamādhyaṃ vedaṃ phalaṃ phanmatvād śrīhyādivat ityetadnumāyātha yatkarma tatphannavaditi pratisādhanābhidhānenānai kānti kī karoti /
uparate karmaṇi dravyāpaṇa tantvādīnāṃ tatsaṃyogādīnāṃ ca dravyāntaraṃ paṭādi phannaṃ dṛṣṭamiti /
uparatagrahaṇaṃ ca karmavyatireka pradarśanārtham /
evaṃ hi śate kadā cidihāpi karmanimittameva phalaṃ vadet /
tena bravīti /
indriyakāmavākye dadhi phalavad dravyatvāttantuvat /
indriyaṃ vā dravyaṃ janyaṃ phannatvātpaṭādivat /
api ca kṛṣernādṛṣṭamiti hetorvirudvatvaṃ vadati /
yathaiva hyayaṃ hetuḥ karmaṇaḥ phalavatvaṃ phalamya vā karmajanyatvaṃ sādhayati evaṃ dṛṣṭaphalatva  ma śabdagamya phannatvaṃ brīhyādyanyatamaphalatvaṃ vā sādhayati /
tasmānnaivajātīyaka kāryakāraṇabhāve samastahetudoṣasaṅgādetadbhavati /
kvacid dṛtantravārtika /
ṭādanyatrādṛṭasthāpi siddhiriti /
yadyetadanumānaṃ tvayaiva nirākṛtaṃ kathaṃ tarhi homānnyāyyaṃ phanamityucyate /
yaddā itikaraṇānta eva praśnaḥ /
ucyate /
śabdenāvagamyametatphala miti bhāvārthādhikaraṇopanyāsena uttaram /
tasmādbomātphala miti nyāyyam /
dadhnaḥ phalamiti cānyāyyamityarthasiddhaṃ madyaducyate tattulyabannavatvanirākaraṇārtham /
kaḍhā cihni iyamapi nyāyyaṃ bhavet /
api ca dadhyubhayamasamarthaṃ kartumiti/
na tāvatkarmānapekṣasya dadhnaḥ karaṇatvamasti /
yena kevalaṃ phannasaṃbandhyeva syāt /
ata ubhayatra vi dhātavyaṃ, na ca taccakyamiti /
nan kambala nirṇojana vaḍhiti prāsaṅgika karmasaṃbandhābhiprāyeṇa vastvamāmarthyanirākaraṇārthaṃ vā /
tathā hi /
dadhyabhayamamamarthamiti yathāśrutena paravacanena vamtvasāmarthyamevoktamiti dṛśyate /
na brūmaḥ ekasyobhayoḥ prayojanaṃ na yuktamiti /
na vayaṃ vastusāmarthyamapahumahe, kiṃ tarhi samarthepi vastunyavicitāḍhanuṣṭhānādavabhyaṃ dadhyabhayārthatvena vidhātavyam /
na caitadasti, aneka saṃbandhakaraṇe vākyabhedapramaṅgāt/
sannikṛṣṭāsaṃbhavena viprakṛṣṭortho vidhīyate /
tadiha dadhihomasaṃbandha saṃnikṛṣṭa dadhiphalasaṃbandhe ca viprakṛṣṭe yugapachighoyamāne yugapadeva saṃbhavāsaṃbhavāvabhyupetavyau syātām /
tammādanyataraparityāge sati tvatpaścasivirbhavatīti saṃnikṛṣṭa vaśena  ḍhayapi homena saṃbadhyate sopi phaleneti karmayukte sati phanne siddhaṃ karmāntaratvamiti 
bhavetphalaśrutiryā tu guṇasaṃvarite vidhau /
sā tadgatavidhispṛṣṭā tena yātyekavākyatām 
praśnaḥ /
siddhāntavādī tu pratyayārthavidhitvaṃ dhātvarthānuvādatvaṃ ca tyanupapattekha yataḥ kurtāvaddhātoḥ para uccārayitavyaḥ /
tataśca vibhaktaṃ paśyannāda juhuyāditi /
nanu śrutyā homasaṃbaddha meṣa yatra ka cana dhātāvupādātavye prāpte prakaraṇaprāptahomopādānamabhāvanocyate /
satyaṃ bhāvārthādhikaraṇanyāyena śrutivalīyastvāprāptonuvadiṣyate /
yathā ca na vibhaktervacanamevaikaṃ prayojanamiti devamanyatrāśritam /
iha ca ye bhavadīyaṃ pakṣamāśrayeste śrutima grahādiṣu kārakamātrapratipattyarthamuccāryamāṇanāntarīyakatvāpavādheraṃstarām /
katham 
tyayānugrahārthamapi dhāturuccāryamāṇaḥ saṃbandhabacādavivakṣitamapi svārthaṃ pratyāyayati/
na hi tasyārthapratyāyanamātramevaikaṃ prayojanamiti vaktavyam /
nanūcyamāne 'pi iti pratyayānugrahārthaṃ dhāturustokāryavidhisaṃbhave tāvadvidhāyako bahutarārthavidhānamupeca te/
homasya ca phanabhāvanākaraṇatvādbhāvayeṭindriyaṃ homenetyecāryamāṇaḥ svārthaṃ pratyāyayatīti/
na cāsya grahakatvavada vivadyāvamavasthitasya karaṇabhūtenaiva daghnā samatvātsaṃvandhe 'nupapadyamākāraṇaṃ kiṃ ciḍhasti /
tasmādyathābhilaṣita kevalakarotyarthāsaṃbhane 'vaśyaṃ matvarthanakṣaṇā parigrahītavyā dadhimatā homeneti /
vādasamarthameta diti/
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
satyapi homasaṃbandhe karotyana ca tasyāṃ kiṃ citpramāṇamasti /
na ca dadhiśabdasyāsati rthānapāyāttāvanmātreṇa prayojanasiddhiḥ /
yastu homasaṃbandha kṛto pravṛttinimitte karmanāmadheyatvaṃ ghaṭate /
soyamubhayasmād bhraṣṭo viśeṣo nāsau kiṃ cidviruṇaddhi /
prakārāntareṇa vā bhāvanāṃ dadhiśabdo 'narthaka eva prāpnoti /
tataśca śabdadharmasaṃnikarṣānuviśecyati/
nanvevaṃ sati sa eva doṣa iti /
aparityajyagraheṇa dharmyeva śabdaḥ parityāgādvādhita iti bādhyetatarāṃ śrutiḥ /
mānopi homo balātkāraṇībhavatīti manyate /
siddhāntavāguṇasamabhivyācārapakṣe tu na kasya cihnādhaḥ /
tatraitaducyate /
judo tvāha /
vākyāntarābhyastamya juhuyāditi śabdasyaitatmā madhyaṃ hotīti śabdo bādhita iti tatparihārārthamāha avaśyaṃ juṅayena taveyaṃ bhrāntirbhavati homa eva karaṇamiti /
nipuṇatastu yāditi vaktavyam /
katham /
pabhyatāṃ yathaiva pratyāsatteḥ sādhyāṃpramupadhāvannayogyatvātpracyāvyate tathātra daṣipadānurodhena sādhanāṃbhā, dyathā ca tatra pratīyana dadhīndriyasaṃbandho bhāvanāpratyayādinā /
pratyayastāvadavaśyameva dadhīndriyaviśiṣṭāṃ bhāvanāṃ vidhātumuccārayitavyaḥ, saca kevalaprayogāsaṃbhavādvānuvyaniriktaprakṛ ṅgīkṛtam/
daṣisaṃbandho 'pi cāsya prakaraṇādevāśrayāḥ davivakṣitāmapi saṃkhyā pratyāyayatīti vacyate tathā 'tra pra mānaṃ bhāvanāviśeṣaṇa  maṃśāntare 'vasthina mevamichāpi guṇāśrayatvenāvasthāsyate /
yathoktaṃ vṛttikāraṇa/
homāśrito guṇaḥ phanḍaṃ sādhayiṣyatīti /
kaḥ punarāśrayāśrayisaṃbandho nāma kiṃ kena kathaṃbhāvavyatirikta utāvyatirikta iti /
ke cittāvadāḥ /
vyatirikta evāyamiti /
katham /
yathaivāṃśatrayāpekṣā bhāvanā 'nyatra gamyate tathā guvaśiṣṭāyāṃ caturtheśo 'pyapekṣyate 
ke cittāvadāhaḥ /
agnihotramevetikarttavyateti /
ta tvayuktam /
karaṇavyatiriktatvāditikarttavyatāyāḥ /
homasya ca prāmuktena nyāyena karaṇāṃśāvyatirekādato 'gnipraṇayanādikaivāgnihocetikatrttavyatetyu cyate /
kuta etaditi /
kathamadhātvarthasthetikarttavyatā saṃbandha ityabhimānāta/
phalasādhanasya dadhna iti /
yathaiva homasya karaṇatvāditikarttavyatānugrāhyatvaṃ bhavati evaṃ tata eva kāraṇāno 'pīti/
asyāścetikarttavyatāyāḥ sannidhānāditi /
saṃsthādhikaraṇavipratiṣiddha samāna vidhānatvābhyupagamāpattecodanāliṅgasya ceti /
punaratideśanyāyopanyā sādasaṃbaddhatvam /
yadi tāvatmannidhānātsaṃbadhyate kiṃ codanāliṅgasadbhāvana/
atha codanāliṅga sadbhāvaḥ pramāṇaṃ sa dūrasthasyāpya viśiṣṭa iti vyarthā sannidhānavācoyuktiḥ /
ata evaṃ vaktavyam āśrayayopasthitena homenopakāra pradānakrameṇetikarttavyatāyāḥ sannidhānādavideśanimittasya ca codanāliṅgasya juhotyarthasya darśanāt /
yasmādeva cāyaṃ codanāliṅgatvena ja hotyarthaḥ prakaraṇātprāpto 'nuvadivyate tasmādasyotpatteḥ phalaṃ vā prati pratyayo na vidhāyakaḥ /
kena prāptasyānuvāda iti cet /
ata āha na cānyadbomasyotpattivākyaṃ vidhāyakaṃ nāstīti /
ke civanyathā 'sya vacanasyārthaṃ varṇayanti/
na cānyaddadhiphalādindriyādagnihotrahomasya svargādi phalaṃ nāsti/
svavākyena prāptatvāditi/
tattvanāśaṅkitā prastutopanyāsādasaṃbaddha miti pūrvoktameva jyāyaḥ /
tasmānna karmāntaraṃ, kiṃ tarhi tasminneva karmaṇi danaḥ phalaṃ homaścānugrāhakaḥ /
athavā tenaiva tantravārtika /
kāraṇena dadhiśabdasyāpramāḍhapāṭhāt kevanācca dadhnaḥ phalasid dhyasaṃbhavādumaya siraskāreṇa saṃbandhādeva phalamubhayośca dadhihomayostādarthyam /
atra tu pūrvoktena nyāyena dadhihomasaṃbandhakṛto vākyasyāsya caikavākyatvābhāvādhiphalasaṃbandhaṃ cānirvṛtte homasaṃbandhaḥ prākaraṇiko nāstītyanenaiva vākyena homasaṃbandhaṃ kṛtvā phalaṃ prati vidhāvāśrīyamāṇe'nekārthavidhānādākya bhedaḥ syāt /
ato dadhna eva phannamityeṣaiva vyākhyā yujyate /
tathā ca samā prāvupasaṃhṛtaṃ tasmāddaghno homena saṃbadhyamānātphala miti /
tena yad veti vikalpamātrapradarśanārthaṃ draṣṭavyam/
anye tu vadanti /
eka evāyaṃ paścaḥ sopapattika ādita ārabhyopasaṃhiyate /
ta smāinaḥ phannam /
ato dadhiśabdasya vivakṣitatvāditi ca pāṭhaḥ /
atha veti tu pramādalikhitamiti /
śakyaparihāraṃ tvidam/
katham/
yadaiva dadhnendriyakāmasya bhāvayediti saṃbadhyate tadaiva karaṇabhūtāighnaḥ phalamityavagamāt karaṇatvānyathānupapattikāritaḥ kriyāmātrasaṃbandho 'vagamyate śaktirūpa eva ca kriyākārakayoḥ saṃbandha iti karaṇa vibhaktyantargatatvātpratyayārthasya ca prādhānyāt prātipadikārthopasarjanaḥ saṃbandha eva phalāya vidhīyate /
tasmiṃstu vihite pūrvavadeva prakaraṇātkriyāviśeṣo homo labhyate /
tatra tu dravyadevatāsaṃbandhanyāyena kriyākāra kasaṃbandhasya phalasaṃbandhe vṛtte kosau kriyāviśeṣa ityapekṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasaṃbandhaṃ karttu prakaraṇena homa upanīyate /
tenoccate dadhihomasaṃbandhaḥ phalāya vidhīyate iti /
tataśvātha veti sadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
myakpāṭha eva /
samāptyupasaṃhārastvā dyapakṣasya draṣṭavyaḥ /
atha vā 'syaiva saṃbadhyamānagrahaṇena daśupasarjana saṃvandha nirdeśa ityadoṣaḥ /
nandadhneti cendriyakāmasyeti ca padadvayavyāpāra  dvākyaṃ bhidyeta/
naiṣa doṣaḥ/
kutaḥ /
naiva hyanekasaṃbandhādvākyabhedaḥ prasajyate /
aneka vidhiśaktyā hi bhedo, nāsti ca sotra naḥ 
tathā hi /
revatīvāravantīyasaṃbandhavyāmṛte vidhau /
śrūyate phalamatrāpi yāgo 'to na vidhīyate 
yastu revatīvāravantīyasaṃbandhotpattividhānāttasya ca phalaṃ prati vidhānātpratyayāvṛttilakṣaṇo vākyabheda āśayane sopi nāśaṅkitavyaḥ /
svayameva veḍhena tatphannamyopāttatvāt /
revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ kṛtveti niṣpādite hi saṃbandhe yajeḥ pareṇa liṅā phantasaṃbandhaḥ kevantaḥ karttavyaḥ /
tena nāvṛttidoṣo bhaviṣyati /
tatrāpyādhāranirdeśādrevatīnāṃ parārthanā prādhānyādvāravantīya phalaṃ prati vidhīyate /
guṇopādānavaśena dhātvarthāduttārito vidhāyakaḥ phalāya guṇaṃ vidadhadyadanyatrājñātaśeṣatvaṃ vidhatte /
revatyaśca saptamīnirdeśādvāravantīyaśeṣabhūtatvātprayojanāntaramanapeśamāṇā na phalena saṃbadhyante, tadguṇakaṃ tu vāravantīyaṃ dvitīyānideśādavagataprādhānyaṃ karotyabhihitāṃ bhāvanāṃ prati dhātvarthasthānīyaṃ pratīyamānaṃ prayojanāpekṣatvāta phalavattā pratipadyate /
atha cobhayatiraskāreṇāpi saṃbandhādeva phannamiti vaktavyam /
evaṃ ca sati viparivṛttiprāpno yajiḥ, prakṛtārthāvalambī vaitacchandaḥ, tasmācca yajisamānādhikaraṇātparā ṣaṣṭhī phalavatā guṇena saha prakaraṇātprāptamāśrayā śrayisaṃbandhaṃ vadantī, pramāṇābhāvācāyāntarāsaṃbandhāttannivṛttirūpapravṛtta evakāraḥ, pūrvoccaritena va canāntareṇa ca prāptamagniṣṭomasāmasaṃbandhaviśiṣṭaṃ vāravantīya,dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
mityādiva  tsarvakarmāntaratvānnityaprāpta manūdyamānaṃ na pratyayamāyāmayiṣyati /
karmāntarapakṣe tu sarvamaprāptatvādvidhātavyam /
na ca tallabhyate /
kutaḥ /
ekaśaktiḥ svabhāvena sarvadeva vidhāyakaḥ /
alpārthavidhisaṃtuṣṭo nānekārthavidhikṣamaḥ 
āśrayatvena gṛhṇāti yo guṇāḥ prakṛtī kriyām /
tatsaṃbandhānuvāḍhatvottatra bhedo na gamyate 
tathā hi /
devatādravyakartṛbhyo nātiriktamapekṣate /
yāgaḥ sādhanamityevaṃ sāmnā naivaiṣa sādhyate 
āha ca /
stotrasādhanabhūtatvaṃ sāmno yogyatayā sthitam /
stotraṃ ca prakṛtaṃ nāstītyāśrayo na pratīyate 
phacāya vihitaṃ sāma svatantraṃ rūpamātrataḥ /
vedasvādhyāyamevai kamutpattyarthamapekṣate 
naikaprayatna mādhyatvaṃ kriyāntara viśeṣaṇe /
tena kriyāṃ vidhāyānyastatra kāryaḥ punarvidhiḥ 
kṛtvāśabdārthamevaikaṃ gṛhṇote bhāvanottarā /
sopi khagocaraprāptaṃ grahīṣyati viśeṣaṇam 
revatovāravantīyasaṃbandhaṃ niṣpādyottarabhāvanāpekṣo 'vasthitaḥ svaviśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ kṛtvāśabdārthaḥ kratunā gṛhyate /
ataśca svaviśeṣaṇāśceṣa eva kratoḥ /
sa tu tatsaṃbandhaṃ sākṣāḍhanupajīvangu ṇabhūtatvādaṅgeṣu niścipannatideśavijñātasthānavāravantīyavaśena revatīrapi tadviṣayāḥ kalpayati /
tena yadyapi atra vākye 'gniṭomasāma na vidhīyate tathāpi ṛtuviśeṣaṇamapi tatra saṃkrāmatītyadoṣaḥ /
ataśca prakṛtayāga saṃbandhastvatpate vāravantīyasya nāsti /
paśya /
ātmanā hyakriyā rūpairguṇairāśrīyate kriyā /
vāravantīyagītesta kriyayā kiṃ prayojanam 
sarvacaiva yatredaṃ kṛtvedaṃ kuryāditi śrūyate tatra yadi tāvakvāntadhātuvācyā kriyā 'nyata eva prāptā tato nimittārthaṃ śravaṇāṃ bhavati /
atha tu na prāptā tata uttarasyāḥ karaṇaṃ pūrvanirvṛtyutta rakālatvena vihitaṃ tāmananuṣṭhāya yathā karttuṃ na śakyataityarthā davaṇyaṃ karttavyā satī vihitavadvijñāsyate /
na ceha revatīvāravantoyasaṃbandhaḥ prāgvidheḥ kutaścitprāpto yena nimittatayā 'śrīyeta /
tasmādanuṣṭheya eva vijñāyate /
yadi tarhyanuṣṭheyatvena saṃbandhaḥ upapannaḥ kathamuttarayā'nuṣṭheyatvopāttayaiva saha saṃbadhyate /
tadarthamāha/
dvāvetāvathā kṛtvetyeṣa śabdaḥ śaknoti vaditumiti /
kathame kenā nekārthāvagatiriti cedata āha dṛṣṭā hi ka cidiyamapi gatiḥ /
yathā śoṣamānayeti pramāṇāntaraprāptepyānayatau raktośvaśvodyamāno na raktāśvaśabdābhyāmivābhihito vākyabhedaṃ janayati /
tathā ''tra klāśabdopāttā nirvṛttiḥ pūrvakālatvaṃ ca iti /
atha vā /
tatraiva na vidhīyeta viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇam /
yatra dravyāṅgabhūtaṃ tanna karmāṅgaṃ pratīyate 
nanu revatyopi vidhīyantaiti /
yadi śrutamātrānupātyevānekārthatvaṃ bhavettata eṣa parihāraḥ syāt /
ete ta sarve vidhīyamānatvātprayojanabhūtā,stasmādanekārthatvamastyeveti /
ucyate /
vidheyamātramapyatra nārtha ityabhidhīyate /
pradhānavidhiyukto'rthaḥ sa caiko 'tra vidhīyate 
yāgaṃ hi phanne vidadhatpratyayo na viprakuṣyate /
na cānutpa ttiparaḥ mannutpattimapi kalpayiṣyati/
anekārthavidhānaṃ ca yayevotpattividhau karmavidhānanimittaṃ labhyate tathā phanavidhāvapi dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
phaloddeśena karmavidhānādityevaṃ manyamāno vadati /
atha revatoṣu kṛtena vāravantoyena paśukāmo yajeteti /
stotradvāreṇa yāgamāghanatvopapatteḥ karatoyeṣā /
atha vetyaṃbhūtanaṇānenaivetthaṃbhūtena paśukāmo yajeteti /
tatrottaram /
naivaṃ śakyamṛgantarapramāṇāhiśeṣadānādvaiguṇyamiti /
yadi tadevedaṃ karma tatastatya vāyavyāsvagniṣṭomasāma vihitaṃ tahagantara revatyākhye gīyamānaṃ pūrvavihitavāyavyākhyaviśeṣajñānādviguṇaṃ bhavet /
na ncidānīmevātmīye pakṣe bhavataiva tatra revatīṣa ṛccanyānyapi sāmāni prāpnuvanti evaṃ paryanuyuktenābhihitaṃ, naiṣa doṣaḥ/
kṛtveti hi nirvṛttaḥ saṃbandho yāgāyo  cyate /
dvāvetāvartho kṛtvetyeṣa śabdaḥ śaknoti vaditumiti /
siddhāntavādī tvapūrvakarma vidhāvanekārthavidhānaṃ śakyaṃ nānyatreti manyamāna āha /
sati vacane matpaśce śakyaṃ bhavatpakṣe tvasati vāravantīyagrahaṇamātreṇa nabhyamānāsu revatīṣvaśakyamiti /
paraḥ punarāha vacanaṃ tarhi bhaviṣyatīni tenaivābhiprāyeṇa /
phaje viśiṣṭa karmavidhānātkṛtvāśabdasya cāvidhāyakatvāt yajiranuvāda iti ca satyapi phalaṃ prati vidhātumutpatyavidhānābhiprāyeṇa /
siddhāntavāḍhī svābhipretāne kārthavidhyanyathānupapattiphalaṃ kathayati /
yadi baca naṃ siddhaṃ tarhi karmāntaram /
na pūrvasyaivānito guṇavidhānamiti /
nanu tato yajeneti yāgānuvādāditi /
vacanenānirākṛtatvādadyāpi svapaśvameva bīyāṃsaṃ manyate /
naivaṃ śakyamiti siddhāntavivaraṇam /
yadi hi revatīguṇakaṃ vāravantīyaṃ yāgaṃ prati guṇatvena vidhīyate tato'vaśyaṃ sa uddeṣṭavyaḥ /
tataścoddiśyamānatvādeva phalapadaṃ na tena guṇena vā saṃbadhyataityanarthakameva syāt, saṃbadhyamānaṃ vā vākyaṃ bhindyāt /
guṇaviśiṣṭakarma vidhāne vā pratyabhijāyamānatvāde kāntena karmāntaratvam /
na ca yatpapūrakāmo yajetetyaprāptatvādanuvādaḥ saṃbhavati /
etena revatīvāravantoyavidhiṃ pratyasya nimittatvaṃ pratyuktam /
ataśca na vāravantīyaṃ kena cihnalavattareṇa pramāṇena revatībhiḥ saṃbaddhamiti viśeṣahānādiguṇaṃ bhavet /
atha yāgasaṃbandhī 'nuvāda iti /
guṇādeva phanne sati prakaraṇādavagataṃ yāgāṅgatvamasmin vākyenuvadiṣyanaiti/
kaḥ punarāśrayāśrayisaṃbandhātpūrvanirākṛtādasya viśeṣo yenopanyasyate /
sa ucyate /
tatra hyānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣu ityetanirākṛta, maṅgatvajñāne tu tatsaṃbhavādagniṣṭomasāmasaṃbandhaḥ sulabha ityabhiprāyaḥ /
tannirākaroti /
prakaraṇādvi vākyaṃ balavattaramiti/
yāyisaṃbandho hi phalasaṃvandhānuguṇatvātsaṃbhavangṛhyate ma tuna saṃbhavati ityuktam /
aṅgāṅgisaṃvandhastu ṛtu kathaṃbhāvagrahaṇātsyāta/
tacca nāsti asaṃyukta prakaraṇāditi va cyati /
saṃyuktaṃ caitatphalena /
tasmādavirodhādguṇaphanna viśiṣṭa karmāntaravidhānam/
tacaitatsyāt /
satyapi karmāntaratve tadanugṛhītāt guṇādeva phalamiti /
tadvikalya bhāvārthādhikaraṇanyāyena pratyayasaṃnikarṣeṇa yāgaphanta saṃbandhāvagamānnirākaroti /
tasmātkarmavidhiḥ /
aya punarviśiṣṭe yāge vidhīyamāne kriyāntarasyāgniṭomasāno viśeṣaṇena kathaṃ saṃbandha iti /
tatrottaram /
vacanāditi /
pragukta nyāye nātideśikaṃ vacanaṃ draṣṭavyam/
agniṣṭomasāmnaḥ kārya iti /
na kiṃ cidagniṣṭomākhyaṃ sāmāvasthitaṃ vi dyate yasya vāravantīyaṃ kāryāpannamiti kalpate /
tena prākṛtayadvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
jaya jīyakāryāpattyabhiprāyeṇoktam /
atha vāgniṣṭomasāmna iti stotrasyaiva kārye tādarthena varttivyataityarthaḥ /
tasmātmameṣu karmayuktaṃ phalaṃ syāditi siddham 
punarvidhāna sāmarthyātsvārthatvācca phalaśruteḥ /
phannabhayastvalābhācca hīṣāheraparaṃ phanam 
sarvasya coktakāmatvāttasminkāmaśrutiḥ syānnidhanārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ 
uccate 
doṣāvṛṣṭiṃ kuryāttāṃ ca nidhanabhūteneti vākyabhedaḥ, tadasaṃbandhe cānarthakyama asmatyate na kiṃcidanarthakaṃ, sarvasya saubharamya va canāntarairuktavṛṣṭyādi kāmatvena tatpadānāṃ ca prāptatvāvīṣādisaṃbandhamātre vidhīyamāne vākyabhedābhāvaḥ /
na ca vacanamanarthakaṃ nidhanaviśeṣaniyamārthatvāt /
vināpi ca guṇakāmatvenāstyevātra sāmānya viśeṣalakṣaṇā bādhaḥ saubharaśabdasya sarvabhaktisāmānyavacanatvātsaubharaśrutyā hi parokṣavṛtyā nidhanāntaraṃ prāpnoti, idaṃ punaḥ pratyakṣaṃ, tammāinnīyaḥ /
yathā cārthāḍhāttipyamāṇaṃ śrautena nivarttyate tathā parokṣavṛtyāpīti /
atha vā sobharaśabdavācyāyā gītenaiva kiṃ cidvādhyate aravidhānenāśarāntaramātrabādhanāt/
yadi hi gītyantarāvayavo vidhīyeta tataḥ saubharāvayavāpi bādhyeta, stobhāvara bādhastvayaṃ nidhanaviṣaya ityadoṣaḥ /
tasmānni ghananiyamārthā punaḥ śrutiriti /
evaṃ tu vyākhyāyamāne'sti kiṃ cidvācyam /
taducyate 
hīṣiti nidhanamiti vyavahitakalpanādoṣāda niṣṭaḥ saṃbandhaḥ /
tathottarapakṣe 'pi /
nidhane hoṣvidhānaṃ cedṛṣṭikāmaviśeṣite /
viśiṣṭārthānuvādatvādvākyabhedaḥ sphuṭo bhavet 
vṛṣṭikāmapadenaiva saṃbandhe sati saṃśayaḥ /
phalena sādhaneneti vākya sāmarthyavīśraṇāt 
phalasaṃbandhapace tu na prayogavacanaḥ samartha ityarthavattā /
kiṃ ca 
anyathā'nena saubharaṃ prakaraṇāvagatamapi vṛṣṭisādhanaśaktiyuktaṃ lakṣyeta /
na ca tadāśrayaṇe kiṃ citprayojanamasti /
tathā śruticakṣaṇāviṣaye ceti bruvatā bhāṣyakārasyāpyetadeva vyākhyānamabhipretamiti gamyate /
siddhāntastu 
sarvasyaiva saubharasyāyaṃ kāmasaṃyogaḥ pūrvokta eva pratyabhijñāyamānaḥ koryata iti nāpūrvaphalapratipattiḥ /
kimarthā tu prāptasya punaḥ śrutirityata āha nidhanārthā punaḥ atiriti /
kasmātpunaḥ śrutyupāttena phalenaiva hīṣādayona saṃbadhyante /
tatra ucyate /
yathaiva vāravantoyaṃ neṣṭamāśrayamāptavat  /
phale tathaiva hoṣādi nāpnotyāśrayamocitam 
na tāvatsaubharāvayavena nidhanena sādhitena prakaraṇanabhyasaubharaṃ sādhitaṃ bhavati avayavasya saubharatvenāpratītaḥ /
na ca yathā śaknu yāttathā 'śrayedityeṣā kalpanāstītyuktam /
upetyāpi tvāyatvamaneka prastāvādibhaktini saubhare katamasyāṃ bhaktau doṣādayaḥ prayujyantāmiti naiva jāyate /
mukhyaṃ vā pūrvacodanālcokavaḍhiti prastāve vā prāpnuvanti /
tatra nidhanamityanuvāḍho nāvakalpate /
athocyeta yathokthyādīnāṃ phalāya coditānāṃ prakaraṇājjyotiṣṭomamāśrayatāmasamastavyāpitvenā nekāvayavatvepi sati vākyāntaravaśenānte niveśo bhavati evamacāpi phanne vihitānāṃ doṣādīnāmāśrayatvena saubharamupasarpatāṃ samāmnāyavaśena labdha sthā nānāṃ nidhanatvam anuvadiṣyate iti 
dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
ananya viṣayatvena sthānamukthyādiṣu sthitam /
doṣādista bahusthānaḥ ka syāditi na gamyate 
ekatvepi hi śabdasya śaktibhedaḥ prayojane /
tatra kāryāntarasthānaṃ na syātkāryāntareṣvapi 
prapadyate rūpavināśabhītegatirna gotyantarabhaktiyogam /
ataḥ samastai vikalpṇamānā yathāmamāmnāyamasau niyamyā 
ato nānyadīyanidhanavidhānam /
ta ekaṭeśaniyame mati kāṃsyabhojinyāyena samastaniyamaḥ /
e ṣopi cātra vākyārthaḥ saṃbhavati /
ubhayoḥ prāptayoḥ saṃbandhamātraṃ vidhīyate/
yadṛṣṭikāmāya saubharaṃ yacca hoṣityevaṃ nidhanaṃ tadekatra saṃpādanīyamiti /
tasmātmamastagītiniyama iti siddham 
śubhaṃ bhūgat /tantravārtika /
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ /
guṇastu ṛtusaṃyogātkarmāntaraṃ prayo jayetsaṃyogasyāśeṣabhūtatvāt 
jyotiṣṭome prathamaṃ bṛhadrathaṃtare vaikalpike pṛthak  pṛṣṭamādhatvena codite tataḥ punaḥ śrūyate yadi rathaṃtaramāmā somaḥ myādaindravāyavāgrān grahāngṛhṇīyādyaḍhibahatsāmā śukrāgrāniti /
tatra saguṇaṃ karma śrayamāṇaṃ saṃdihyate kiṃ karmāntaraṃ jyotiṣṭomā, duta tasyaiva grahāgratāviśeṣa prati rathaṃtarāvacchinnasya nimittārthaṃ śra varṇamiti/
tata etatsidvyarthamidaṃ vicārayitavyaṃ kimayaṃ kṛsnakatusaṃyogo rathaṃtara, atha mattāmātrasaṃyoga iti /
tatmiḍyarthamapyetaccintanīyam, kiṃ ṛtuviśiṣṭaṃ rathaṃtaramuta rathaṃtara viśiṣṭaḥ kraturihāśrīyate /
nanu ca yadiśabdopabandhādiha nimittaṃ pratīyate tasya coddiśyamānatvāt viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo nāvakalpetaṃ /
bhavannimittārthatvametasya yadi yādṛgayaṃ pratyeṣyane tādṛśasya kutaścitprāptirvijñāyeta /
aprātipakṣe tu bajāvidhānamāpadyate /
dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
nimittatvamapi ca yāhaśasyehayate yadi tādṛśo jyotiṣṭomastatastasyaiva gaṇārthatvena śravaṇamiti saṃsthate  yadi tu nāṅ na bhavati tatastāhaśatvamāpādya nimittīkarttavyaḥ /
yatsaṃbandhāca prāṅgimittatvameva nopajāyate bhavati tannimitasyāpi viśeṣaṇaṃ, yathā''baṃdhikaraṇe vacyate mṛṣyāmahe haviṣā viśeṣaṇamiti, na smāna viśiṣṭānuvādadoṣa iti /
kiṃ tāvat prāptaṃ prakaraṇādrathantarasāmatvasya bṛhatmāmatvasya ca vacanāntareṇa prāpteryadiśahana ca prāptyapeścatvanimittatvapratīteḥ grahāgratāviśeṣasya ca prayogavacanena grahaṇa ilīyasā ca virodhinā guṇāntareṇānavarodhāttastaṃnidherguṇārthena punaḥ śrutirityakarmāntaratvama/
evaṃ siddhāntaṃ prāptaṃ tuśahena vyāvartya satraḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ parigṛhyate karmāntara mi ti 
samāmaḥ mati sāmarthya taccāpīṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇe /
viśeṣaṇaṃ vyavacchettu jyotiṣṭome ca nāsti tat 
evaṃ cānyapadārthavidhānāttatpradhāno bahubrohiranugrahoṣyate/
a nyathā hyupamarjanaparatvaṃ lohitoṣṇīṣādivākyavaḍhagatyā pariṭhahota /
yadi ca grahāgratāvidhānena mahatadakaṃ vākyaṃ tatastaccāpi rathantaravidhānaṃ cānekatvāḍha pūrva bhāvanā vidhinaiva nistoryate /
somaḥ syāditi cānantaryāt tatkarttavyataiva vijñāyate, rathantaramāmatvakarttavyatā ta vyavahita kampanayaiva syāt /
somaśabdena tu ca prakṛtiliṅgena jyotiṣṭomaprakṛtirevārya bhaviṣyati/
tasmātka rmavidhi, ridameva bhāṣyakāro darśayati yaḍhi rathantarasāmetyasya kothaṃ ityādinā /
grahāgratāviśeṣaśvāsyaiva kratorvākyenāvāntaraprakaraṇena vā bhaviṣyati /
yadyapi mahāvākyeyvavāntara vākyānyapramāṇaṃ tathāpyarthāsaṃbhavādavivakṣite mahāvākye 'vāntaravākyāśrayaṇādvidhiśaktairabādhaḥ /
parityāgādaramadhyāhṛtya paraṇāmiti matvā athavā yadi rocateti darśayati 
parastu dṛṣṭāntasyaivāmiṅge kathaṃ punariti pṛcchati /
vyatyayena saṃbandhaḥ, kāmapraveḍhane ca niṅicchāṃ pratyāyayatīti siddhānta vivaraṇam /
tatraiṣa vākyārtho bhavati /
yadyaindravāyavān grāna grahotumicchedrathantara māmānaṃ ṛtuṃ kuryāditi /
tataśca yaḍhiśabdara hitaṃ somaḥ syāditi paḍhadvayaṃ vidhāyakaṃ, grahān gṛhṇoyāditi etattu yadyapyavidhāyakaṃ tathāpīcchārthatvādyā hi yadicchati ma tatkarotītyevaṃ vidhiphanlaṃ lapsyate/
atha vecchāmātrayuktamupāttaṃ grahāgratvaṃ sthāḍhityeṣaiva niṅa vidhāsyati /
vinaiva vyavahitakalpanayā'pyayaṃ pakṣo bhavan bannavattara iti manvāno 'tha vā heta hetu matorliṅityupanyasyati /
tatra momaḥ syāditi heto liṅ, gṛhṇīyāditi vidhāveva tenaitaduktaṃ bhavati /
rathaṃtarasāmasoma hetukānendravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇīyāḍhiti/
na cākriyamāṇe'sau hetutvaṃ pratipadyataityarthādvihito bhaviṣyatīti /
athavā hetumati gṛhṇīyāditi liṅ momaḥ syāditi vighāvanuktamapi ca momasya hetutvaṃ hetumadākṣepātsaṃnidheśca bhaviṣyati /
tatrāpyeṣortho grahāgratāviśeṣakārapābhūtaḥ somayāgaḥ karttavya iti 
iti pakṣavikalpa saṃgrahaślokaḥ /
sarvaṃ caitadveṣṭyadhikaraṇasidvāntaevopayocyataityatra prapaccitama /
kiṃ ca /
niṣpannena nimittena niṣpādyaṃ pratibhūyate /
na rathaṃtarasattā ca niṣpannā kratumattvavat / vārtika /
prātaḥsavane hi grahagratā bhavati mādhyandine rathaṃtaraṃ, na cāniṣpannasya nimittatā yuktā /
kāraṇaparyāyatvānnimittaśabdasya,mama tu naiva kiṃ cinnimittam /
atha vā kratuḥ sa cādita eva vidyate jagatmāmā ca na jyotiṣṭoma iti jagatmāmni sāmābhāvāditi vacyate/
ataśca tatmāmānyāditareṣu tathātvamiti karmāntaratvamiti 
atha vā rathantarādividhānājjyotiṣṭomasya gaṇavākyairevamātmakatvaṃ coditamiti nāthantaratvaṃ pratīyate /
tataśca karmekatvam /
yattu viśeṣaṇābhāvāt sāmāntara sāpakṣaviśeṣaṇatvāddā rathantarasāmeti samāso nāvakalpataiti /
tatra brūmaḥ 
yadi hi rathantara nityaṃ jyotiṣṭome 'nyasahitaṃ vā syāttato na vyavacchindyādapi, yatastvarathantaropi jyotiṣṭomaprayogostyeva tatastadvyavacchedamukhenāsti viśeṣaṇaphalam /
yadi caivakāraṃ vinā viśeṣaṇabuddhirna bhavati tata evamasau darśayitavyo yadi rathantaraṃ sāmāsyāstyeveti 
yadā yadi rantatharaṃ sāmaivāmya bhavatīti, tatra kortha evaśabdasya tadvi rathaṃtaraṃ yadyapi sarvadā māma tathāpi yadā tau na bhavati tadā taṃ prati sāmakāryāmattvāḍha sāmaveti, sattāpace rathaṃtaraṃ sāmeti vacyate /
avaśyaṃ ca kratvapecamevaitatmāmatvaṃ vaktavyam /
rathaṃtarasvarūpe sāmatvasya nityaṃ paunaruktyāt /
na ca rathantarasya māpenatvaṃ jyotiṣṭome, yena samāso na syāt /
dvandvanirdiṣṭeṣu hyekastotraviṣayeṣu caitat bhavati /
kevaleṣu tu bhinnastotraviṣa yamādhaneṣu pratyeka nirapekṣameva sādhanatvamiti sāmarthyaṃ na viddanyate/
yahā paunaruktyā deva sāmaśabdastatsādhya stotrana kṣaṇārthaḥ ma n rathantaraparyupasthāpitaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ lakṣyati/
athavā buhadrathaṃtarayoravāntaraprakaraṇāḍhavāntara kāryayogācca virodhinoḥ sparddhamānayoryathāvasthitānuvāda sāpyātmāmāntarā eyanapekṣya parasparāvaccheṭenaiva viśeṣaṇatvamiddhiḥ /
tenopapannaṃ rathantara viśiṣṭasya kratornimittatvam /
atha vā'stu rathantaraṃ kratuviśiṣṭaṃ nimitta miti /
nanu ca tadeva na pratīyate/
ucyate/
satyaṃ na pratīyate kiṃ tu yaḍhā samastakratusaṃyogābhāvādrathantara viśiṣṭaḥ kraturna gṛhītaḥ tadā vigṛhyamāṇe mamāse yo viparīto viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ pratīyate rathantaramasya sāmeti ma grahīṣyate /
ṣaṣyantatvācca kraturviśeṣapāmeva samāsābhivyaṅagya viśeṣyatvabhāvāttathā vivakṣiṣyate /
yadyapica kratvantareṣvapi vastusvarūpeṇa rathaṃtaramasti tathāpyatra tāvadvidyate tāvanmātreṇa ca viśeṣaṇatvopapattiḥ /
svavākye cāmādhāraṇatvaṃ viśeṣaṇakāraṇaṃ na vastunavaṇaṃ, mā bhūnnīlamutpalaṃ devadattasya gaurityevamādīnāṃ viśeṣaṇatvocchedaḥ 
yaḍhi ca vastuta evāmādhāraṇatvaṃ bhavennaiva śabdena viśeṣaṇa pāḍhīyeta/
na hyatra viśeṣāphalamasti agniruṇaiti /
tasmādavaśyaṃ vākyagatamevāmādhāra pātvamā śrayitavyam /
asti cātrāpi ta ta jyotiṣṭomagatasyaiva rathaṃtarasya nimittatveneṣṭatvāt 
tadvaśena prayogakauśanāgyāmādimiddheḥ /
na ca nimittaṃ naimittikasya rūpasaṃnidhānenopakaroti kathaṃ tarhi jñāyamānatvena /
tammādaprayuktamapi saṃkalpitatvādrathantaraṃ nimittaṃ, yadā tvekaṭeśasthenāpi tena viśeṣataḥ ṛturnimittaṃ tadāsa varttataevetyavirodhaḥ 
aveṣṭau yajñasaṃyogāt kutupradhānamucyeta 
rājā rājasūyena khārājyakāmo yajetetyasya prakaraṇe āgneyo 'ṣṭākapālo hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇetyāḍhibhirdravyadevatāsaṃyogairaveṣṭisaṃjñakāmiṣṭiṃ vidhāyayate/
yadi brāhmaṇo yajeta bāīsu tyaṃ madhye nidhāyājatimāhatiṃ tvābhighārayedyaḍhi rājanya aindraṃ yadi vaigyo vaiśvadevamiti /
tatra pūrvavadeva saṃdehaḥ kiṃ rājasvayamadhyasthāyā evāveṣṭarvarṇaviśeṣasaṃvandhaṃ prāptameva nimittatvenoddiśya tatra naimittikaṃ vidhoyate utāprāptameva brāhmaṇādisaṃbaddhaṃ prayogāntaramuddiśyataiti /
tatsiddhyarthaṃ caitat vicārayitavyam /
kiṃ rājasvaye 'dhikārastrayāṇāmapi varṇānāmuta kṣatriyasyaiveti /
tatmiddhyarthamadhikāriviśeṣaṇabhūto rājaśabdaḥ tathaiva vicāraṇīyastatopyetadvi cārayitavyam /
kiṃ kṣatriyatvanimitto rājaśabdauta rājyakaraṇanimitta iti /
nanu caitayā'nnādyakāmaṃ yājayediti varṇaviśeṣeṇāsaṃbandhaṃ pṛthagrājasūyaprayogavacanādevāveṣṭarvacanamastīti varṇatrayasyāpi prāptasya nimittārthameva śravaṇaṃ bhavennaitadevam/
taḍhā hi nirjñātaca triyakartṛkāyāḥ karjantare vacanāntareṇāvidhīyamānāyāḥ pṛthak prayogakāraṇābhāvācca rāja sūyamadhyasthāyā evaṃ kasya bhayatve saṃyogapṛthakvamityanena nyāyetantravārtika /
na sādhāraṇaṃca pvārājyaṃ phalaṃ prātyātmikaṃ cānnādyaṃ vijñāyate /
pṛthagvā rājanyenaiva phalārthinā prayujyate na varṇāntarasaṃbandhaḥ /
tadyathā 'dhyayanādhānayonnijatatraivarṇika kartṛkatvāttadadhīna sidvonāṃ karmaṇāmathiṃmātrasaṃvandhāvagamepi satyapaṣṭadraviṣayatvamevāvatiṣṭhate /
yathā cācaiva khārājyakāmāviśeṣepi rājakartakatva vaśena bhoktṛviśeṣo bhaviṣyati /
tasmādrājasūyādhikāreṇevaibhava vacanaiḥ prāptiriti dvāveva pacau 
kartā rājyasya rājeti sarvalokeṣu gīyate /
mahāviṣayataivaṃ ca śāstrasyāpi bhaviṣyati 
rājasūyādhikāraśrutiśvānalpaviṣayatvena svarasāt pravartamānā na nivatitā bhaviṣyati /
tasmādrājyaṃ kurvantaḥ sarvatraivarṇikā rājānastaca rājyaṃ janapadaparipālanaṃ nāma sarvalokaprasiddhama /
tataścoddharaṇaṃ rājye 'pi kaṇṭakodvāraṇamabhipretam /
āryāvarttavāsina iti śāstrasthā vā tannimittatvādityasya pradarśanārtham /
rājñaḥ karma rājyamityetadabhiyuktā upadiśantītyetad bruvatā nanu rā jagandasyaiva prakṛtibhūtasya svātantrāmabhyupagataṃ bhavati /
tathā ci naivauda meghisaṃbandhādudameghaḥ prasidhyati /
svatantreṇodameghena sa eva tvanugamyate 
rājā nirjñāta eveha svātantryeṇa ciraṃtanaiḥ /
tadyogāt kalpitaṃ rājyamasmākaṃ tu viparyayaḥ 
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
sarvathā tāvadrājyakaraṇāttābhyāmapi rājatvaṃ labdhaṃ tāvatā ca rājasūyacodanāyāḥ prayojanaṃ, yau tu nyāyānyāyau tayoḥ puruṣadharmatvāt naikopi kratunā gṛhyataityaviśeṣaḥ 
uktaṃ hyetaddarhirā jyā diśavdeṣu yathaikadeśeṣi jātinimittatve labhyamāne nimittāntaraṃ na kalpanīyamiti /
paraḥ punaryaiaugika grahaṇamātropakārakamiti pradarśayati prakaraṇavaśādyadiśabdasamabhivyācārācceti /
na karmāntara vidhāyiṣyata iti prayogāntarābhiprāyeṇa /
athavā /
yadā yadi śānti bhuñjītetantravārtike /
tyādayo vacanaprakārā gṛhyante tadai kenaiva vākyena brāhmaṇa saṃbadho bāīspratyābhighāraṇaṃ ca na śakyate kartumiti mukhyameva karmāntaratvam /
evaṃ tāvadubhayaprasiddhiṃ pramāṇīkṛtyoktamidāna tu rājyarahite prayogaḥ pramāṇameva na bhavatīti prastūyate 
ṛtusaṃbandha evāyaṃ brāhmaṇāde vidhīyate /
prāptattvānna rājā hi rājyayogāta pratoyate /
dātriyavacana evāyaṃ rājaśabdo na yaugikaḥ, sahi rājyayogāḍhā bhavedvātvarthānumāre dīptiyogādvā ubhayathāpi cānupapannaḥ /
tadracitarūḍhiśabdadarśanāṭe kadeśasthāpi rūḍhiravayavaprasiddhiṃ bādhate /
na cāvagravaprasiddirapyanai kāntiko vidyate, nahi dośramāneṣvagnyādiṣu rājaśabdo vidyate /
na cānabhiṣikte ja napadaparipālanavyāptepyāyukta ke /
nanu cāyuktakasya paraprayuktakāritvāhatvija iva yajamānatvaṃ na rājatvaṃ bhaviṣyati 
abhiṣekopi dharmajñaiḥ kṣatriyasyaiva padyate /
mahāsau rājaśabdena tena nākṣatriye mataḥ 
nityāḥ śabdārthasaṃbandhā yathāvasthitagāminaḥ /
nāśrayantyadhruvaṃ hetuṃ svacchanda parikalpitam 
sā ca nityatā vastvapekṣayā vā vidhyapekṣayā vā nirupyate 
taityapi vānyajātīye nabhidhānaṃ draviḍānām tasmādapi na caivarṇiko rājā tathā ca rājāpatyaṃ rājanya ityaikānti kakṣatriyajātivacanasya rājanyaśabdasya rājaśabdaprakatitvamevāncācacate /
anyathā caivarṇikānāṃ rājatvātsarveṣāṃ caivarṇikānāmapatyeṣu rājanyaśabdaprayogaḥ syāt /
kutaḥ /
rājanyaḥ atriye ruḍho rājānaḥ sarvaeva cet /
apatyāpatyavadyoge vaiṣamyaṃ vada kīdṛśam 
prakṛtau tadapatye ca jāniśabdasya tucyatā /
tena rājaiva sarvatra rājanyo 'pyabhidhīyatām 
paryāya eva hi rājaśabdasya rājanyaśabdo'nena prakāraṇānvākhyāyate sa tvekajātiviṣayatve sati tathānvākhyātuṃ yujyate nānyathā 
naiva tāvadubhau śabda/
svātantryeṇa prasidhyataḥ /
lṛptāyāmakaśakta/
hi dvitīyā yaugiko varam 
ācārayorasaṃbandhe saṃdeha sati nirṇayaḥ /
sannibandhanayā mṛtyā banīyastvādavāpyate 
tasmādiyameva vacanavyaktī rājñaḥ karma rājyamiti 
sakalaśca rājetiśabdo rājyenupraviṣṭa iti sa yaugiko yuktaḥ na su rājyaśabdo rājanyanusyūtaḥ sakanna ityayaugikatvam /
satyameva rājyaśabdasya yaugikatvamupapadyate 
asādhāraṇabhāvena sarvatreṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇam /
tena tasyaiva karmeti cintitādi na guhyate 
ṛtumadhyaprayogo hi svāra rājyenaiva pūritaḥ /
sākāṅkṣastvitarastasmāttasyaiva phalasaṃgatiḥ 
virodhitvātprasajyete vikalpāvṛttikalpane /
bādhastenābhyupetavyo vyavasthāyāṃ tu naiva te 
na ca rājasūyeneti sāmānyaśabdaḥ paurṇamāmīśabdavat, prakṛta  samudāya viśiṣṭa samudāyivacanatvāta ata eva tatkṛtamapi na daurbalyaṃ labhate /
iyastui viśeṣa ekena bahavo guhyante anyenāspe/
na ca tāvatā kaścidatiśayo'sti /
nanu caitayeti śrutyaiva pratyakṣavacanādasti viśeṣaḥ /
syādviśeṣo yadi etacchabdaḥ phalena saṃbadhyate /
yadi vā 'thaiṣa jyotirityādivat prastūyamānaṃ brūyāt, pratyayasaṃnnikarṣāttatrāpi yajiśabdagu hī taivāveṣṭirannādyena saṃbadhyeta /
etāvacca rājasūyayajāvapyastītya viśedvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
ṣaḥ /
prakṛtamapi ca bruvannetakanda āgneyādivākyālocanāhate naiva bravītīti/
tataśca rājasūyayajirapi tāvatā yatnena śaknoti grahītumiti tulyabannatvam /
nanvavāntarādhikārasyāsti viśeṣaḥ 
ayameva viśeṣo yadekatra bahūnāṃ grahaṇamaparatra cārapānām /
grahaṇavenā tu tutyaiva /
yadi caikāntikamatrākamantaratvaṃ sthāna tata evama cyeta, karmāntaramapi cainadini darśitam /
tataśca viṣayāntaratvādeva svārājyānnādyayoravirodhaḥ /
karmāntaratvepi ca bāīspatyādiniṅgadarśanātprakṛtāveṣṭiprakṛtitvameva pratipattavyam /
rājanyasyāpi tulyapravṛtteḥ phanapadānuṣaṅgāca brāhmaṇavaiśyavadeva karmāntareṇa prayogāntareṇa vā saṃbandhaḥ /
evaṃ ca tasyāpi madhye nidhānavākyaṃ tantra prayoge satyupapatsyate 
ādhāne sarvvaśeṣatvāt 
vamante brāhmaṇomonādadhītetyādiṣu prāpyaprāptyāśaṅkāyāṃ pū rvavadeva saṃdehaḥ 
sāmarthyā ciptamādhānaṃ sāmānyavacanena vā /
tasmāddarṇaviśeṣāṇā nimittārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ 
siddhānta hetustu 
na tāvannityamarthasya prāpakatvamasti, upāyāntareṇāpi pratimahādinā puruṣāntarāhitānāmātmanepadenāniyatāno sunnabhatvāt /
pratyaścavacane satyanyathānupapattipaśśe satyarthāpattinabhyaśrutyaparigrahācca /
ya evaṃ vidyānityapi varttamānāpadeśaḥ pratyacāya liṅi brāhmaṇāḍhivākyeṣu upannabhyamānāyāṃ na vidhiśakti slabhate /
asti caitadupanyāsasya pratyakṣavidhiyuktodakopasarjanādisaṃbhāra vidhānāthatvamityaprāptameva brāhmaṇādiviśiṣṭamādhānaṃ vidhīyataiti /
kiṃ nimitta sāpyamiti yadiśabdādyanupabandhābhiprāyam /
brāhmaṇādīnāṃ ca vasantādividhibhiḥ samuccāraṇamiti parapadasaṃbandha saṃcāritāyāṃ vidhiśaktī nimittaphalatvās 
na tveṣāmāghānasaṃbandho na vidita iti 
evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ 
na nvādhānamagnīnāmabhyupāya iti /
tatra nāma rūpamācaṃ gṛhyate yatnau ki kopāyasādhyaṃ bhavati vastraśakaṭādi na cāhavanīyādayo laukikopāyāstasmāda vaśyameṣāṃ vedanaivopāyo 'pyā kṣetra vyaḥ /
sa ta nādhānavyatirikto'stoti tadapyāścitamiti /
uccate /
nānaikāntikatvāta agnīna santravārtika /
hi yājjākayāpārādayo'bhyupāyāḥ santi sarveśca tairāhavanīyāḍhimātraprārthinyaḥ kāmaśruto nirākāṅkṣāḥ kriyante /
tasmānaikāntenādhānaṃ prāptamityasti niyamavidheravakāśaḥ 
hasṭyām satyaṃ prathamamādhānādutpadyante 'gnayastrayaḥ /
paścāttu śrīdivatteṣāṃ nopāyāntaravāraṇam 
tataśca yathā ghaṭādīn kumbhakāra utyādyotpādya vikroṇāti ḍhadāni ca tathaivaikaḥ kaścit punaḥ punaragnīnādhāyāparebhyo dadyāt, ataḥ pratipuruṣamādhānaṃ paśce prāptaṃ paśce netyasti vidhānasya viṣayaḥ /
pakṣepi vā naiva prāptirastīti vakṣyāmaḥ 
arthā cepapakṣe tvānumānikyāḥ śruterātmanepadaparasmaipadavivekābhāvāḍha kartṛviṣaye 'pyavirodhādupāyāntarāpina nivarterana ato'vaśyameva vidheyametaditi /
api ca /
satīṣvevādhānaśrutidhviti pākṣikīmapi prāptiṃ nirākaroti /
parvameva hi vyākhyātaṃ niyamādīnāmaprāptavidhitvaṃ śrutasaṃbhāvanāyāma śruta kalpanā navasarāt 
na hyanupasarjanādīnāmādhāne naikavākyatā saṃbhavati /
bhavedatrārthabhede nānāvākyatvaṃ yadyādhānaṃ vidhīyata /
tat brāhāṇādisaṃyuktairvicitamiti guṇārthameveha punaḥ śrūyate/
kuto nu khalu nirṇayaḥ kataradanayorutpattivākyamiti /
taducyate 
yadi hote he api vākye vidhātṛṇotāṃ tataḥ samānaviṣaye matī spardheyānāṃ katara dvidhattāmiti /
atra punarekaṃ vi dhāyakamekaṃ stāvakam /
