na ca stāvakena brāhmaṇādi saṃyukta mya vidhāyakatvaṃ nivāryate tadānuguṇyā, dyadi tu ya evaṃ vidvānityapi vidhisarūpaṃ syāttato vicitasya punarvidhānānupapatterasmatpa caṃ nirundhyāt, liṅā tu vihitasya saṃbandhisaṃbhāravidhiprarocanārthaṃ tu stutisahinasya punaḥ śravaṇamitya vidhāyakam/
liṅā ca sāvadvātvarthavidhānaṃ svapadenopāttatvāt śrautaṃ prāśastyaṃ punarvākye na, tataścānumāniko vidhiriti viprakuṣyate /
nanvidamapi vākyamiti brāhmaṇādipadārthāparityāgābhiprāyam /
siddhāntavādīmantravārtika /
badati ādhānaṃ tāvat śrutyā śeṣaṃ vākyena nāma bhavatu khapadopāttāyāḥ stuterabhāvāt /
evaṃ dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyamavattiṃ mahatadtya/dipadasaṃbandhanaiva stutiriti vākyam /
kartṛkāla viśiṣṭa pradhā nādhānavidhānācca vākyabhedaparicārāt siddhaṃ prāpakatvam 
dācayaṇayajñādīnāṃ tu yāgasāmānādhikaraṇyātpūrvayāge cāprayukta tvā  dātma rūpāvacchinnayāgāntarapratipādanamaviruddham /
na ca kaściddaṣyādibhiḥ tulya evaṃsaṃjño guṇāḥ prasidvastasmādbhāvārthādhikaraṇanyāyena phale yogavidhānāt yāgāntaram 
samāptaṃ ca phale vākyam 
phanjasyānupādeyatvānna brohibhiryajataityādivatkarmoddeśena vi dhiḥ saṃbhavatotyavaśyaṃ karma tatra vidhātavyam /
tataśca siddho bhedaḥ 
dadhyādivadevācāpi vaiyadhikaraṇyenaiva saṃbandhaḥ 
tasmāddarśapūrṇamāmayorevāvasthāntararūpāt vikārāt phalaṃ na karmāntarāt 
liṅgadarśanāca 
triṃśatpūraṇaṃ  paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāsaṃkīrtanaṃ vā bhedaṃ bodhayati/
na hi darśapūrṇamāsika striṃśadvarṣapacaḥ karmāntareṇa parayituṃ śakyate/
na ca niyamasyātideśo, yena karmāntarasyevaitat pañcadaśavarṣapakṣavidhānaṃ syānna ca ḍhākṣiṇāyanayājitvena nimittena darśa pūrṇamāsayoreva paccadaśavarṣapaca upajāyate saṃbandhābhāvāt /
ḍehi paurṇamasyauhe amāvāsye iti cāsyānupapattiḥ 
samāptira viśiṣṭā 
yadyapi karmeddeśena na phalaṃ vidhoyate tathāpi karmaphalasaṃvandhābhāvāḍhakarmāntaratā /
yathaiva hi karmaṇaḥ phannamiti bhāvārthādhikaraṇe sādhitaṃ tathaivātulyatvāttu vākyayorityatra guṇaphanasaṃbandhāparyavasāyitvamapyuktamiti saṃdehe sati padāntarānugrahāthaṃ guṇādeva phalaṃ na karmaṇa iti siddham 
katham /
yadi tāvadānambhanirvāṇa prakṛtya śrūyeyāna tataḥ prakṛtapratyayānuvṛttireva prasajyeteti karmāntarāśaṅkā na syā, danāramyavāde tu sati śvetādiguṇasyopādeyatvātkadā ciddūrasthānuvādana guṇo vidhoyate kadā cidvā viparivṛttyabhāvātkamantaramiti jāyate saṃdehaḥ 
tannirākaraṇamapi ca prakaraṇabhāvāda sādhāraṇopacacaṇṇābhāvācca na prākṛtayonīkikavyāvṛttarūpayoḥ pratītirastītyevaṃ bhaviṣyati /
guṇavidhivi ṣayatvācāla bhanirvāpaiau guṇavidhiśabdenoktau /
kiṃ tāvat prāptam/
yathaivāyaneṣu guṇasaṃbandhapare vākye karmavidhiśabdābhāvāṭakamantaratvaṃ tathedāpi bhaviṣyatīti caśabdenānvādiṣyate/
ka cāso guṇavidhiriti viṣayāvadhāraṇārtha maprakaraṇagrahaṇam /
atha vā yadyapyetāvan pūrvavaināṇyenāprakaraṇe śrūyate tathāpi karmaṇo vidhiśabdānavarodhādgārthaiva punaḥ śrutiriti darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ śakraṭaṃṣā sā śvetīkṛtyānavdhavyā nirvāpaśca caro kartavyaḥ caruparimito vā bhūtibrahmavarcamakāmayośca sarvebhyo darśapūrṇamāsāvityevaṃ prāptayoranuvāda, stathā vāyavyamiti sarvavanaspatīnāṃ vāyudevatātvāt kathaṃ ciḍhīṣāyā evānuvādaḥ /
sauryamiti cāgneyasyaiva tejodevatyasāmānyādanavādastasmādbhuṇe vidhīyataiti 
vāyatryapadaṃ pūrvavaḍhevopecya phalapadaparigraheṇa tāvat pratyavasthīyate /
yadi hyālambhanirvāpāvanūdya śvetaca vidhīyate tataḥ phalapadamanarthakametra syāt/
sarvakāmaprāptānuvādepi pākṣikatvānityavadgrahaṇaṃ virudhyeta/
viśeṣaṇatve vākyabhedaḥ syāt 
guṇaviśiṣṭālabhavidhāne tu na kaściddoṣaḥ /
tenocyate karmaṇaḥ pratimūtvāditi /
karmātra vidheyatvena śrutimūlaṃ na guṇaḥ, sa hyacodanāla cā eva syāt /
atha vā yāvaduktameva syāt na yajimat /
kutaḥ ka rmāḥ śrutimūlatvāt 
yajatistu dravyaphalabhoktṛsaṃyogādeteṣāṃ karmasaṃbandhāt 
yathā phalapaḍhaṃ prekṣya guṇapakṣo nirākṛtaḥ /
devatāpadamālokya tathaivānambhamātratā 
liṅgadarśanācca 
saumāraudramityukte vināpi yajatiśabdena pariśrayaṇa vidhipare vākye yajatinānudyamāne yajatimatkarmavidhāyitvamevamādīnāmityavagamyate /
agnīṣomoyapi cānenaiva yajimattvamidviḥ /
pūrvaṃ caitāvadeva vicāritaṃ kiṃ prakṛtānuvāditvamuta vidhāyakatvamiti /
siddhe tu vidhāyakatve kimātmakaṃ tatkametyetadadhikaraṇādhīna me vaitadityapāna maktyam 
iti ye vadanti tān pratyucyane na kiṃ citsādhanamapradarśitaviṣayaṃ svārthaṃ sādhayati /
sūtrakāreṇa ceda hetumātramu dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
pāttam /
na cārthaprakaraṇāḍhibhira pyudāharaṇapratijñā saṃśaya he tūnāmanyatamamupalabhyate /
tasmādgamaka sūtre satyavaśyaṃ doghapratimamādhānārthaṃ vṛttikārādibhiryatitavyam /
matyeva saṃbhave 'ṣyācārādivarjanamuktam /
sarvathā śiṣyaprajñā saṃskāra sūtrakārādīnāṃ pravarttamānānāṃ yenaiva tadanuguṇaṃ yatkṛtaṃ ta deva grahotavyam nāmadgrahaḥ kartavyaḥ /
padaṃ sūtrakāreṇa nopāttamidaṃ vṛttikāraṇetyetatpradarśanārthametadvayanti /
taḍhiha bhagavānapavarṣaḥ kināgnihotre dhaṃnudohādhikāre śrutamidaṃ vākyamudāhṛtavān vatmamālabheteti, tatra ca pūrvavadeva tredhā saṃśayamupanyastavān /
kiṃ prākṛtaevānambhe vatso vidhīyate tathālambhamātramubhayaṃ yajatimadatatkarmeti /
tatra viśeṣaṇābhāvāt prākṛtapratyayo nāstīti pūrvādhikaraṇasiddhameveti nopanyantaṃ tenaivānukrameṇa yajimadabhidhānabuddhā prasaktāyāmapabāḍhoyaṃ kriyate /
tatra bhoktṛsaṃyogapratyudāharaṇatvāgataprāyopi pūrvapaścaḥ śroṭabuddhivaicigyāt kriyate, yo nāma tārkikavāsanayā sāmānyato dṛṣṭena vedārthamunninīṣet tasya tannivṛttirapradaśitāśaṅkā na śakyā kartumiti pradaśyate/
tatra keṣāṃ cit pūrvādhikaraṇaevālabhatiryajatiparyāyatvena prasiddho 'nyeṣāṃ yajvanamāpakatvena, tadubhayamacāpi tathaiva manyante /
tatrāpūrvayāgavidhānaṃ prāpta vā vatmavidhānamiti pūrvapakṣe dvaitam /
siddhāntastu dravyadevatāsaṃbandhānyathānupapatyā pūrvamasmābhiryajaḥ kalpito nādṛṣṭapūrvaśaktyā labhatyabhidhānena vyabhicāryanumānābhāsena vā, na cehāmāvastīti yāvaduktatā /
tathā ca dohanādisaṃskāra karmaprāyadanamupapadyate dṛṣṭārthatvaṃ ca gopranavana hetutvāt 
saṃyuktastvarthaśabdena tadarthaḥ śrutisaṃyogāt 
pūrvamānnambhasya pratyudāharaṇa, midaṃ tu carudvāreṇa nirvāpasya, devatāśaṅkā cātrābhyantare'dhiketyārambha, statrautpattikameva caruparoḍāśādonāṃ yāgāṅgatvaṃ, sarvathā caitasyātmīyatvaparityāgaḥ kartavyaḥ /
cammupaddhātīti ca dvitīyānirdeśāt upadhānaṃ pratipattiḥ /
na cānyatrānupayuktasya pratipattiryuktā ityākāṅkṣite yo gyatvāt yāgopayogitvameva vijñāyate /
vākyaśeṣe ca bṛhaspatiḥ śrayamāṇo yadi vidhyadeśena saṃvadhyate ānarthakyameva syāt /
tasmādāgne prakṛtikaṃ bāīspatyacaruyāgaṃ nirvartya śeṣakāryāntarāṇyakṛtvā upadhātavyaśvarurityevaṃ prāptam /
evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ carvādīnāṃ svabhāvena naidamarthyamavasthitam /
yathāpramāṇamevaiṣāṃ viniyogo 'vagamyate 
na ceyaṃ pratipattiriti prathamaṃ prayojanavattvānavagamāt /
artha karmaṇyapi copadhānaṃ prati prādhānyamasti tenāsaṃskṛta stha na nirvarttayatīti dvitīyā nirdeśāvirodhaḥ 
novārasaṃbandhaḥ san bṛhaspatiścarāvanumātavyaḥ /
tathā vākyaśeṣastho vidhyuddeśamanākājitadevatāsaṃbandhaṃ netavyaḥ 
yeṣāṃ ca bāīspratyo bhavatīti carusāmānādhikarapayena taddhitena vākyaśeṣe devatāśrayaṇaṃ teṣāmapi prathamamupadhānārtha vidhyaddeśāt siddhenākāṅkṣitatvāddevatā vidhātumaśakyeti vartamānāpadeśānurodhena yādṛśaṃ vayamasya bāīspratyatvaṃ vartamānaṃ paṇyāmastādṛśamevaitat praśaṃsā kīrtitamityavagamāt ya eva śākhāntarīyasya vacanasya bṛcaspatervā etadannamityetasyārthaḥ sa eva bāīspatyo bhavatītyatyāpi taitirīyavacanasya niścīyate /
tasmā deṣopi na yajimaddacana iti yāvaduktatva siddhiḥ 
na ca tvaṣṭurabhāvena pratyabhijñāyate ' saḥ /
paryagnikṛtayogācca vākyabhedaḥ prasajyate 
na cāsau kālasya baktā yena paryagnikaraṇakāla evotsṛjatīti kalpyeta 
etenāvasthāvidvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
dhiḥ pratyuktaḥ /
codakenaiva tāvat paryagnikaraṇāvastha utsṛjyataiti prāpitam /
athottarāvasyā parisaṃkhyocyate tatra vidoṣasvamuktameva /
tammānna pūrvakarmaṇi kiṃ cidvidheyamasya vākyasyeti karmāntarameva dravyadevatā saṃyuktaṃ, devatāguṇasāmānyena ca pūrvaprakṛtika magniṣomoya prakṛtikameva vā vidhīyataiti prāpte 'bhighīyata 
pātnovataśabdastāvat manovāyāmivāgniśabdaḥ satyapyubhayaviśiṣṭatve śaknoti prakṛtaṃ yāgaṃ vaktaṃ, paryagnikṛtamutsṛjanīti prakaraṇāt tasyaiva guṇavidhivijñāyate 
tatakhaitāvantyevā syāṅgānītyavadhāraṇāt svarūpaprāptimā codakenāpi siddherutarāṅgāvacchedārthamevedaṃ vākyamiti phalena vya padapūtvāvaccheda iti /
evaṃ ca sati yāgāntarāpūrvāntarānumānādikkeśo na bhavatīti /
na ca parapadasaṃbandhavidhānaviprakarṣaḥ /
paryagnikaraṇānta viśiṣṭe tatmarge vidhīyamāne yadyapyutsargasvarūpaṃ prāptameva tathāpi saduddeśenāṅgakalāpa tantravārtika /
vidhānāinatyanta viprakarṣātma eva vidheyatvenoktaḥ /
tvatpace tu dadhnendriya kāmasyetyādiṣviva dhātogatyantapārāyaṃ syā, tasmādapyakarmāntaratvam /
prakaraṇādapi ca paryagnikaraṇāntāṅgagrahaṇamiddheḥ patnīvatagrahaṇaṃ tyānuvāḍhatvāḍhatantramiti viśiṣṭānuvādaikadeśe vyapadeśo pānnambha parihāra, stasmādga, pavidhiriti siddham 
prakṛtādapi bhettṛtvaṃ nāmadheye vyavasthitam /
kimutāprakṛtebhyo 'tra yatra naivāstyabhedaṣīḥ /
na tannāmadheyaṃ prakṛtī kasya cit prasiddhaṃ yasya punaḥ śrutisāmarthyād dvirabhyāsaḥ kriyate /
tasmādgṛhṇāticodanāsāmānyena jyotiṣṭomaprakṛtirekāhoyaṃ codyataiti manyāmahe /
na va vatmānambhatulyatvam /
ekatra yajateḥ pratyaścatvāt anyatra cāvyabhicāriṇyā saṃjñayā 'nyatve kalpite gṛhṇātinā samastajyotiṣṭomadharmaprāpterdravyadevatāsaṃbandhasiddhiḥ /
ato yāgāntaratvami'ti prāpte 'bhidhīyate 
devatā tāvat dūrabhraṣṭaiva yadi gṛhyamāṇaṃ dravyaṃ tadapi na kena cidupāttam /
na hi jātyā guṇena ca vinā dravyamupalacayituṃ śa kyam /
na ca yāge'navadhārite jyotiṣṭomavadbhāvorita yena somagrahaṇametaditi vijñāyate /
na ca gṛhṇātirjyotiṣṭomaṃ na vyabhicarati upādānamātravacanatvāt /
na caite yāganāmanī yena taṃ bhindyātāṃ, grahaṇasāmānādhikaraṇyādvi tannāmatvamanayo, rivyataevāsmābhiratra grahaṇabhedaḥ /
na ca tāvatā yāgāntaratvaṃ bhavati /
dravyadevatāsaṃyogepi caivaṃjātīyakānāṃ yajimāvaṃ nirākatam /
acodakāca saṃskārā itya, ca punastadapi na vidyate 
agnistu liṅdarśanāt kratuśabdaḥ pratīyeta 
sampravārtika /
agniṃ cinutaityatrāpi cedhaiva saṃdehaḥ 
yadā 'gnimagniṣṭomādi saṃstheryā gairanuyajatītyukte yadyagniryāga evamasāvanuyaṣṭuṃ śakyate /
savaṃtra hi tumlyarūpāṇāṃ tutyadharmaṇā vibhāge paurvāparyaṃ bhabati /
tadyathā devadattamanugakatīti yadi devadattopi gachatyevamanugamanamavakalpate tathā 'nuyajanamapi /
tasmāt śrunānumitetikartavya nāṣat ṛtuvidhānametaditi paścime tu vyā'gniśemādibhyaḥ paścāt kiyamāṇoyaṃ tadaṅgameva bhavatīti phalaśrutirarthavādaḥ syāt /
pūrvatra tu svatantratvāt phalamātreyo nirdeśa/ diti phavidhitvātpuruṣārthamiti viśeṣaḥ 
na dhagniśabdaḥ udbhidādivadyaugikaḥ /
nāpi vākyabhedatatprakhyatajhapadeśatvairyukto yena karmanāmadheyatvaṃ vijñāyate /
yattu tatprakhyamastītyuktaṃ bhavettadyadi ṛtvaṅgatvenāgnividhīyate, sa tu prāptakratvaṅgabhāva eva cayanasaṃskāratayā śrūyate 
katamadravyamiti cayanasāmānādhikaraṇyāvirodhābhiprāyeṇa praśnaḥ siddhāntavādī tu śrīhīnavadantītivat vaiyadhikaraṇyenaiva saṃskāryasaṃskāra saṃbandhopapatteravirodhaṃ matvāca yadetat jvalanaiti /
tasmādagniśabdasya prasiddhārtha grācitvāccinoteśca yāgābhidhānāśaktadravya devatābhāvāccāgniṃ cayanena saṃskarotītyetāvāneva codanātha 'va dhāryate 
yadi hyayamagniśabdaḥ samānādhikaraṇaḥ syāttato dukhaṃ nīyeta /
yadi baiṣā karmaṇi dvitīyā syāt /
ayaṃ tu vyabhikaraṇaḥmantravārtika /
karmapravacanīyayukta dvitīyā atrāyamartho agnicayanamanvagniṣṭomādibhiryaṣṭavyamiti 
na cāvaṇyaṃ tunyajātīyayoreva paurvāparyaṃ bhavati /
atulya jātīyayorapi paurṣāparyaṃ bhavati /
tathā pākamanubhuṅkta iti avirodhopapatteḥ 
tatsaṃyogāt ṛtustadākhyaḥ syāttena dharmavidhānāni 
agneḥ stotramityādiṣvagatyāśrayaṇaṃ  jvalanena saṃbaddhaṃ stha ucyate nāpi tadvān kratuḥ /
na caikatra khacaṇāśrayaṇamiti sarvacaiva sā ''śrayitavyeti /
tasmātmatyāṃ gatau dravyavacanatvameva yutam /
yatvacaivādhikaraṇe bhāṣyakārāntareṇāgneḥ phalavadaphalatvaprākṛtavaikṛtatvanityānityatvottara vedivikārāvikāratvavicāraḥ kṛtaḥ sa udāharaṇāntaredhvadhikaraṇāntarasiddha iāsaṃbaddhopi smaraṇamātra darpeṣovanyasta ityupeścitavyaḥ 
dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvama 
gataṃ guṇalakṣaṇabhedaprasaktānuprasaktaṃ kīdṛśo guṇaḥ pūrva trāsaṃbhavan bhinatti kīdṛśo vā tatraiva saṃbhavatīti /
idānīṃ paryavasiteṣu pañcasu bhedakāraṇeṣu prakaraṇāntaralakṣaṇo bhedaḥ prastūyate /
tatra tāvad 
yathaiva vannabhyāṃ pāṭaliputre vā agnihotrādiśabda uccāryamāṇo nārthāntaraṃ pratipādayati evaṃ prakaraṇāntarepi /
na hi prakaraṇāntaraṃ tasyārthābhidhānaśaktimabhivyanakti 
na cāvaśyamaṅgaireva kratvantaraṃ gantavyaṃ pradhānamapi paripūrṇe karaṇāśe tantravārtika /
svabhabdena vidhīyamānaṃ virudhyate /
tasmādevamapi tānyevāgnidocādīnīti prāpta ucyate 
yadi hi māsaḥ śuddvo vidhoyeta tataḥ pūrvakarmānuvāde buddhirbhavedapi /
na tvetadasti upasaduttarakālatvena śravaṇāt vidyamānābhirupasadbhiḥ śakyaḥ kālo lacayitum /
na ca naiyamika tāḥ svārthāḥ parārthā vā vidyante /
yadi tu tāstaduttarakājavaṃ māsava vidhīyeran evaṃ satyane kāryaviṣānādvākyabhedaḥ syāt 
yadyapi prakṛte tasminnagnihotre bhavedidam /
tathāpyasaṃbhavāttasmin brūyātkarmāntare guṇaḥ 
tatraitatsyādicāpyupasaddhicaritvetyanuṣaṅgādagni pocatutyatva miti /
sa dayaktam /
kutaḥ 
tatrānuṣaṅgo yukto yaca tena vināna kiṃ cidukta bhavati /
yathā'traiva māsaṃ vaiśvadevenetyādiṣu yāvat yajataiti nānuṣajyate tāvaśa kiṃ ciduktamityavagyamanuṣaktavyam /
ica punarśapūrṇamāmādivākyāni tāvat skhapadereva nirākāṅkṣībhūtāni /
paściritvetyayamapi pūrvacaiva caritārthatvānna kiṃ cidapekṣate tatra na kaścidapi ceturasti yenānuṣajyeta /
yantu vākyabhedaprasatyartha mevānuṣaṅgamicchet kuryādapi saḥ/
tatra tu punaḥ punaścaritve tyasya vidhānāt yāvadanuṣaṅgamupasadāmanuṣṭhānaṃ prāpnoti/
aniṣṭaṃ caitat vedābhyanujñānābhāvāt /
athāgnihotrasyaiva purastātkṛtābhiḥ sarvānuṣaṅgārtha saṃpādanamityucyeta tathā sati śabdoccāraṇamapyevamevāvasthitam agnihotrādīnāṃ pāṭhakamānurodhena upakariṣyatīti nārtho 'nuṣaṅgeṇa /
tasmānnaiyākhyānamupapadyataityevaṃ varṇanīyam 
idda tāvat naiva prakaraṇāntara sadbhāvāta bhedo 'vagamyate kiṃ maī pūrva prakaraṇavicchedāt 
sarvatra ca vicchinnaprakaraṇasya karmaṇaḥ saṃvandhitantravārtika /
diprakāraṃ śrūyate /
upādeyamanupādeyaṃ ca /
tatra yadupādeyaṃ yathā ''vanīyapratipaḍhādi tatpradeśāntarasthoddeśanāpi śakyaṃ vi dhātum /
yattvanupādeyaṃ deśakālanimittaphala saṃskāryātmakaṃ tasya pradeśāntarāvasthitamya karmapratividhyaśaktareṣā vacanavyatirbhavati /
tatraiva karma kartavyamiti 
atha nopanayati tataḥ sa evotpādayatyapīti nirūpyate /
tadiha māsastāvat dūrasthahomānuvādena na śakyate vidhātuṃ, na hi kaścidbomādyanurodhenādyaiva māsaṃ saṃpādayituṃ samartha, stenātyantaṃ svatantramanupādeyaṃ māsameva pratiṣhomādiṣu vidhīyamāneṣu dūrasthairutpattividhibhirutpādanaśaktāvalupyamānāyāmidānīmevotyattiḥ kriyate /
na cotpannasya punarutpattiḥ saṃbhavatītyapūrvavidhānaṃ vijñāyate /
nanu cāgnihotrāḍhipadenotpattisahacāriṇā tatkatpattāṣapanīyamānīyāṃ māsasaṃbandhamājavyāpato 'yaṃ vidhidvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
rutpādakatvādinyeta /
tataśca 
yatra vākyāntaragatamapi sannidhānamātrādeva pratyabhijñāyamānaṃ na bhidyate tatra skhavākyagatena nāmnopanīyamānaṃ na pratyabhi jāsyataiti kuta etat /
ucyate
sannidhānena hi yādageva deśādivākyeṣu karmāvagamyate tāigevopatiṣṭhataiti na bhidyate /
nāmadheyaṃ punarārāditastāvadākhyāta paratantratvāt naiva bhedābhedayorvyāpriyate /
tasmiṃścākhyātapravṛttipratīściṣyavasthite māsaṃ juhoti māsaṃ yajataiti juhotiyajatipada mātra saṃgatāvānlo cyamānā yāmanyasya juddotyādaḥ svavākyasva prakaraṇeṣvaviparivartamānatvādapratyabhijñānam /
kiṃ ca /
nāmnā dhātvarthamātraṃ ca saṃnighāpyeta śaktitaḥ /
bhāvanā tvanupasthānādbhidyamānā 'vadhāryate 
dhātvarthepi yathā''khyāte sattvabhūtaḥ pratīyate /
sattvābhidhāyinā nāmnā tādṛṅgevopanīyate 
na ca tādṛśamyaiva dravyabhūtaliṅga saṃkhyā yogyārthābhidhāyibhiragnihotrādipadairabhiṣīyamānatvamityapratyabhijñānātmopi bhidyate 
bhidyate bhāvanāmātraṃ dhātvartho nāyajiśruteḥ /
nāmnā hi tadupādānamātmanopāyi codite /
nāmavilacaṇadhātuśravaṇe hi tadarthabhedo bhavati /
satre tu yajyaśravaṇāt nāmamātropanītaprakṛtayāgapratyabhijñānāttadbhāvanāmātrabhedaḥ /
tasmātmādhūktaṃ prakaraṇāntare prayojanānyatvamiti /
bhāṣyakāra upasadbhiścaritveti tavacitakāla mevānupādeyarūpaṃ bhedacetutvena darśayatīti draṣṭavyam /
athocyeta upasadopi vidhoyantaityādi cābhyāmādhikaraṇavadabhyupetyavādena samarthayitavyam 
tatra phalamudāhṛtameva saṃskāryaṃ ma pyudāhṛtaṃvyam/
caiṣātavyā doghaṇoyeti yajamānasaṃskārārthatvenopādānāt /
anārabhya kiṃ ciditi prakaraṇāntarāvarodhābhāvajñāpanārthaṃ, tatra yāgoddeśenā havanīyādivat phalaṃ vidheyaṃ, śakyaṃ hi tatpuruṣeṇa darśapūrṇamāsasthenāpi kāmayitu miti ma tvāi prākṛteṣu phala vidhiriti /
siddhāntavādī tu svargakāmādhikaraṇasiddhaṃ pratyarthaṃ cābhisaṃyogāditi phaloddeśyatvaṃ matvā vadati na śakyate phalaṃ vidhātumiti /
vidhīyamānaṃ kiyāṅgatvādaphalameva prāpnoti /
kriyāpi vā vidhīyamānā tādayeṃ pratipadyamānā niṣphancaiva syāt 
phalagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanamātraṃ sarvāṇi tu deśādīnyapyudāirtavyānīti same darśapūrṇamāmābhyāṃ yajeta paurṇamāsyā paurṇamāsyā yajeta yāvajjīvaṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajeta darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajeta śeṣāt sviṣṭakṛtaṃ yajatīti sarvatra pūrvādhikaraṇena degādīni prati vidhīyamānatvāt karmāntaratvaṃ prāptam /
śrāi ca 
deśādyuddeśena tu vidhīyamānānāṃ karmaṇāṃ svarūpānuvādakampanaṃ yugapadvidhyanuvādadoṣādayuktam /
tasmātkarmāntarāṇīti prāpte 'bhidhīyate 
na cāpyuddiśyamānatvamanuvādatvakāraṇam /
nopādānaṃ vidheyatve prāptyaprāptivaśe hi te 
viparivṛttireva cehāvibhāgagabdenoktā viśeṣeyātvaveṣṭaveitacchabda pratyayāditi /
prayojanetu codayanti karmāntarevi kinnaitacchabdakatāt sādṛśyapratyayāt āgneyādīnyeva ivaṣoti kathamanya iviṣko yāga iti /
tattvacodyama /
jyotirādivadetacchabdasya prastūyamānamukhārthepipattau satyāṃ sāibhyanaśaṇānupapatteḥ /
tasmātmaṣṭhakta karmāntare'nyahaviṣko yāga iti /
evamuktāni māpavāḍhāni ṣaṭ bhedakāraṇāni/
vṛttyantare tu catvāryeva bhedakāraṇāni śabdāntara saṃjñāguṇaphalānyudāhṛtāni /
punaḥ śrutisaṃkhyayoḥ śabdāntaraevāntarbhāvāt prakaraṇāntarasya ca phalādyanugrahamātrārthatvāt /
tattvayuktamiva dṛśyate 
vakṣyati caivaṃjātīyakānā mekatvamapi cāvyatirekāhū paśabdāvibhāgādveti /
tasmādakaśabdaye satyeva kāraṇāntarādbhedamapaśyataḥ śabdāntarakalpanaṃ tatra bhavato bhāṣyāmantravārtike /
ntarakṛtaḥ, prakaraṇāntaratvācca vinā phalādīnāmabhedakatvamuktamapi na dṛṣṭaṃ ‘sannidhau tvavibhāgāt /
tatsannidherguṇārthena punaḥ śruti' rityā dau/
tena pratyabhijñānanimittatvāt phalādyanugrahītaṃ prakaraṇāntarameva bhedakāraṇaṃ bhavedapyupeścitam /
phalaṃ ca prakarapāntarāntarbhūtatvena na nirościtam /
yadapyekaṃ vā saṃyogarūpacodanākhyāviśeṣādityekatve hetu viparyaya catuṣṭayamasya jñāpakamityuktam /
tadapi prastute 'dhikaraṇe 'nyeṣāmasaṃbhavāditi nānocitam /
tasmādyayoktāḥ ṣaḍeva bhedahetavaḥ /
tatrāpi ta siddhānte saṃjñāśabdāntarayorguṇasaṃkhyayośca bhedo vaktavyaḥ sa nokta ityabhidhīyate 
saṃkhyāpi yugapadane kotpadyamāna samavetā pūrvāsaṃbhavadgaṇāntarādbhidyataiti 
punaḥ śrutirananyārthā bhedikatyavadhāritā /
dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
tādṛśī ceyamityeva dvirāgneyaḥ prayujyatām 
tatra paścāntaramāī 
anyārthā vā punaḥ śrutiḥ 
sarvathā punaḥ śrutiprayojaneṣva trānviṣyamāṇeṣu guṇasṭyāśravaṇāt parisaṃkhyāyāśca tridoṣatvādarthavādārthavve 'bhyupagate kasmārthavāda bārtika /
iti vivicyā saṃkīrtanāt nūnamāgneyasyaiveti matvā vadati sārthavādakena vihitena kiṃ pradeśāntarasthenaikavākyatāmanāgacchatā'rthavādeneti /
vidhiśeṣatvaṃ ārthavādānāmavasthitam /
paricodanā tu pūrvapañcābhiprāyeṇa kṛtā tatra yathā stumā vāstuta vā saiva devatetyavivaraṇānna vijñāyate kiṃviṣayamiti /
na tvetadātekāntālocanena mahendrādhikaraṇe guṇaścānarthakaḥ syādityatra sūtre 'bhidditaṃ parāmuṣṭamiti dṛśyate 
praśasta gandairavadhāritena vākyāntarāt kevaladevatena/
kartuṃ sahendreṇa punaḥ praśaṃsāṃ punaḥ śrutiḥ samyagihāśriteyam 
yāvajjīviko 'bhyāsaḥ karmadharmaḥ prakaraṇāt 
bahṛcabrāhmaṇe adhvaryubrāhmaṇe vā śrūyataiti nātīvābhiniveṣṭavyam /
nana kartṛdharmaḥ karmadharma iti śeṣanāṇaviṣayatvādii na saṃbadhyate /
ke cidāhaḥ /
paryavasite khakṣaṇārthe nadīyopi vicāraḥ pratyāsatteḥ kriyamāṇo na virudhyataiti /
tattvayuktam /
śākhāntare karmabhedavicārasyādyāpyaparyavasānāt 
tatra yadi yāvajjīvakālaḥ karma dharmatvena vidhīyate tataḥ sāyaṃprātarvākyava śena tatkāla samāpanamagnihotraṃ na śaknoti tāvantaṃ kālaṃ pūrayitu mityarthāt jyotiṣṭomavaḍhabhyastarūpameva prayogaṃ pratiṣatyane 
karmastho hi kathaṃbhāvastadaṅgamabhikāṅkṣati /
kānopadeśapa ca tattathaivopapadyate 
atha vā jīvanaparimitakāladvāreṇābhyāsa śvodayiṣyate /
sa ca karmeddeśena śakyataeva vidhātumityevamupadiśyate /
kartṛdharmapakṣe punarna kathaṃ cita karmoddeśaḥ /
evaṃ caikaprayogatve sati dīrghasa traprayogasaṃstava upapanno bhaviṣyati /
itarathā punaḥ pratidinaṃ paryavasānānna kathaṃ cit satrasārūpyaṃ bhavet, tasmātkarmadharmo'bhyāsa iti 
yāvajjīvapadākhyāta śrutivṛttitva saṃbhavaḥ /
matpate, bhavatastatra lakṣaṇāvṛttatā bhavet 
juhotiyajatibhyāmapyabhyāsaḥ yatra hi vidhiḥ samāpyate sa codanātha bhavati/
bhavataśva jīvanadhātvartha parityāgena kānjābhyāsau vidhīyete/
tena lakṣaṇāparyavasāyī vidhiḥ prāpnoti /
tatraitat syādyā'vajjovamiti yāvacchabdaḥ śrutyaiva kājaṃ bravīti /
tadyathā yāvaddoī svapiti /
yuktamatra kālagrahaṇaṃ vartamānāpadeśo hyayaṃ nātra kā cinnimitāpekṣā tena śrutivṛttaṃ dohanamatikramya kābo gṛhṇate/
yadi tvicāpi yāvaddocaṃ svapyāṭāsīta veti vidhīyeta tataḥ kena vā dohasya nimitvaṃ vāyeta 
na ca yāvacchabdaḥ kālavacanaḥ ka cit prasiddhaḥ kriyāmeva ta mamāptiparyantatvena viśinaṣṭi /
kriyākālayorabhedāt na nacapeti cet 
kiyatā kānlena gaurduhyataityukte niyatānyeva muhūrtādīni pariccheda katvenopādīyante 
tadabhyāsavaśena tu vyāvahārikāṇāmapi prāyikaparimāṇajāmāta paricchedakatvaṃ bhavati/
na ca jīvanaṃ nāma nimeṣādivantriyataparimāṇaṃ yena paricchedakatva sāmarthyāt kālatvenāśrīyate 
na hokena prayogeṇa jīvakālo 'varudhyate /tantravārtika /
vitatenāparijñānādanyathā vā vṛthāśrutiḥ /
anabhyastaṃ prayuñjāno yadi tāvat vitatya prayukta jīvanaparimitasya kānasyāntarā kiṃ cit karmāvayavaṃ yadā kadā cit kurvāṇaḥ tato maraṇasyā nirūpitakālatvādyadi kathaṃ cidantyāyāmavasthāyāṃ samāpayet na ca mriyeta tadūne kāle samāpanādayathā coditāpattiḥ /
śrathā samāpya mriyeta tathāpi prakrāntāsamāpanaṃ doṣaḥ syāt /
na ca sarvasvāra vacanamasti yena mṛtepi samāpyeta /
sāyaṃprātacodane ca yāvajjīvakāmya codanāsamīpānāta satyo vinā pramāṇena kevapna kāmya viṣaye kalpanoye syātāmamminpakṣaṃ, yadi tu tadanurodhena sakṛdeva prayujyobhayaṃ saṃbhāvitamiti manyeta tathā paurṇamāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyā ya jeteti codite tadekadeśakaraṇenāpi śāstrārtha saṃbhāvyataiti na vyāpyate 
varṇamāmyatiriktā harvyavacchedaphalā śrutiḥ /
vyātāvapi tatra myānna tvicaivaṃ pratīyate 
sarvathā divasāntarāṣṭyatikramya paurṇamāsyāṃtāvat kṛtaṃ karma tāvanmātraṃ ca śāstreṇītaṃ na vyāpti, ritaratra punarjīvitavyatirikta kākāsaṃbhavāyavacchedyaṃ na kiṃ cidastīti vyatāvasatyāṃ samastameva vākyamanarthakaṃ syāt /
sāyaṃprāta śvodanayorapi jīvanakālāntargateḥ siddhatvāt yāvacchandaśva samastajīvitāvidhiprarigrahārtha ekadeśānuṣṭhāne dvitīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
bādhitaḥ syāt /
ataḥ sāyaṃprātacodanāmiśreyamabhyāsamanācipantī na śaknoti puruṣaṃ niyoktumityaparihāryā lakṣaṇa
tathā hi 
atha yoyaṃ mama doṣaḥ sa tavāpi doṣa eva, vaktavyo vā vi śeṣaḥ 
mama pratidinaṃ sarvasvodanārthaḥ samāpyate /
kāmyavacca pṛthakteśa tava tvante samāpyate 
tava punarjīvita parimitakāna vidhānāt karmaṇe parisamāptasyaivaindravāyavādigra cābhyāmatulyamanuṣṭhānaṃ taccaitat yāvajjīvacodanākṛtamityāpannamabhyāsavidhānam /
yattvarthādabhyāsa iti 
liṅdarśanācca karmadharme hi prakrameṇa niyamyeta tatra cānarthakamanyasyāt 
atipattiriti svadharmātikramo 'bhidhīyate 
prakrameṇa hi karmakānaṃ saṃspaśadanatikrāntamityabhidhīyate /
na ca kaścidapi pūrṇamāsayājī sannaprakramamāṇa eva jovanama tinlaṅghanyati na sai/
darśapūrṇamāmayājī syāt /
atha svakālāparisamāpanamatipātanamucyeta tathā mṛtasya tadbhavatītyanarthakameva prāyaścittavidhānam /
matya hi pratimāsaṃ darśapūrṇamāsaprakrama samāptyojavane nimitte vidhānāt saṃbhavati atikramastaduttarakālaśca prāyaścittaviṣayatvena /
nanu pūrvapaścepi pra timāsamabhyāsābhyupagamāt tadatikramanimittaprāyaścitta vidhānaṃ bhaviṣyati/
na śakyamevaṃ vaditum /
yatra hi nimitta yaccoditaṃ mena tatra bhavitavyam na yatheṣṭa, miha ca paurṇamāsyamāvāsyātipattirnimittatvena śrutā na cābhyāsastacchabdavācyaḥ 
vyapavarga ca darśayati kālacekamabheda syāt 
darśapūrṇamā māviṣṭveti pūrveṇaiva nyāyenāśeṣābhyāmanirvṛtyuttarakālaṃ somayāgaḥ syāt /
na ca mṛtenāsau kartuṃ śakyaḥ 
anityatvāttu naivaṃ syāt 
yadetanmuṃktakamabhihitametadeva sūtrārūḍhaṃ karoti /
niyamapo hyetadevaṃ syāt /
anityatvāttu bhavatyace naivaṃ syāt /
athavā yāvajjīvaśabdena kāle guhyamāṇe lakṣaṇādoṣa uktaḥ tamabhyupetyābhidhīyate satyāmapi cakṣaṇāyāmanityatvāt naivaṃ syāt /
tannāma kālopalakṣaṇaṃ yuktaṃ yannityaṃ kiyatāpi kālenāvinābhūtaṃ, yadahacandramā na dṛśyate tāmamāvāsyāṃ vidyādityādivat /
na ca sarvaprāṇabhṛtāmeva jīvanaparisamāptiryataḥ kutaścit vyavasthita svarūpā yayā kālo lacyeta, tadetadevamāpadyate yadaivedaṃ bhavati tataścānityatvānnimittamevaitaditi siddham /
kathaṃ tarhi niyatanimittatvānnityamityucyate yāvaṣkarīrabhāvitvābhiprāyametadityadoṣaḥ 
kartustaddha maniya mātkālaśāstraṃ ni mittaṃ syāt 
kartṛdharmapane yadidaṃ tvadabhimataṃ yāvajjīvamiti kānaśāstra midaṃ nimittaṃ bhaviṣyatītyetāvatsūtram /
yattu bhāṣyakāraṇa vyapavargadarśanamuktaṃ tadyadi darśapūrṇamāsāvitadevā bhipretaṃ tataḥ punarukta, mathānyattadapyandā tatvānna jñāyate /
tenānantarājonayaivaṃ yojayitavyam /
tvatpace vikṛtīnāmavyapavargaḥ syāt matyace tu tāmāṃ vyapavargadarśana siddhānta upapatsyate /
atha vā nigamanasametaditi vyākhyeyam /
athavā sūtrakāreṇa kartṛdharmo niyamoyamityuktam /
yāvajjovaśabdamya tu kā gatiriti nābhihitamata āī /
evaṃ sati kānaśāstrameva nimittaṃ syāt /
athavā 'gnihotre darśapūrṇamāsayostāvat yāvajjīvagrahaṇāt kartṛdharmaniyamatvaṃ bhavet paśusomacāturmāsye tu katham /
taducyate /
tatrāpi vīmāyukta kānaśāstrameva nimittaṃ syā, dvamante vamante jyotiṣetyādi /
na tāvadetata kāmyamyopadiśyate /
sahi yāvadicchamaṅgatvenaiva sthitatvāt naivaṃ vaktuṃ śakyate /
athāpi naiyamikasya sakuprayogaḥ syātatrāpi vīmānarthikā bhavet /
na ca vasanteyattāvadhāraṇāpramāṇamasti /
tasmādyāvajjovaṃ ye vamantāstedhviti vijñāyate /
saptamyapi ca bhinne jonatyādivat nimittārthā bhaviṣyati, tenocyate sarvatraivajātīyaka kartṛdharmaniyamāvadhāraṇātkālaśāsvaṃ nimitta māstraṃ pratyetavyam /
etenaiva paśucāturmāsyādiṣvapi naiyamikatvasiddhiḥ 
śākhāntare yathā karma kuttrarūpaṃ pratīyate /
kiṃcidguṇa samāmnānāncaivaṃ vedāntareṣu tat 
dvitīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
pṛṣṭhadayavikapaḥ syān śākhāntara vidhānataḥ /
ma ca prakṛtitaḥ prāptaḥ karmaikatve vṛthā bhavet 
ekaṃ vā saṃyogarūpacodanākhyāvi śeṣāt 
sarvaca pratyabhijñānāt saṃcārūpagupyādibhiḥ /
ekakarmatvavijñānaṃ na bhākhākhapagacchati 
svādhyāyagrahaṇenaikā śākhā hi parigṛhyate /
ekārthānāṃ vikalpaśca karmaikatve bhaviṣyati 
śākhayā hokayā yogāihakarmāvabodhanam /
yujyate karmanānātvāt naika mākhopanakṣaṇam 
kṛtakaṃ cābhidhānam 
kṛṣimaṃ kāṭhakāyuktamāyāpravacanāditi /
na vā 'nādīni bhidyante karmāṇyādimatā satā yadyapi kāṭhakāderjāternityatvānnityaivākhyā tathāpi pravacananimitteyaṃ smaryate /
na ca karmāṇi procyante śabdaviṣayatvāt pravacanasya /
tasmādapi na saṃjñayā karmabheda iti ekatvepi param 
na ca kapālasaṃkhyābhedāi bhedaḥ /
tāṃbandhihārabhedānabhyupagamāt /
tasmādekasmiva karmaṇi sādhanavikalpo bhaviṣyati /
nanu cotpattivākyaśiṣṭatvāddikalpo nāstītyuktaṃ naiṣa doṣaḥ /
ubhayorutpattivākya śiṣṭatvāviśeṣeṇa tulyabalatvāt /
kathaṃ punaraneka vākyotpādita syaikatvaṃ vijñāyataiti tasyottarasūtre pa ricāraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
āgneyavatpunarvacanam 
anubhāṣaṇasūcametat /
atha vā punaruktatva paricārārtha me vai mat /
punaḥ amerarthavādaguṇārthatvenānyathītvāt /
advirvacanaṃ vā śrutisaṃyogāvi śeṣāt 
disīyavyāyāne parivārāntaranivṛttyathe/
vābhandaḥ/
tacānyārthā punaḥnirbhavati yatra bāvanmātrameva śrūyate /
yatra caikavākyagataṃ vidheyāntaraṃ vidyate/
na lie tadekamapi, samastetikataṃvyatopeta pradhānapunaḥ śrutiśravaṇāt /
etameva śrutisaṃyogāvi hinīvāṇyāpaśya caturtha pāda /
śeṣaṃ manyate /
na caiṣā punaḥśrutiḥ /
kutaḥ 
śākhānā yugapattenaṃ punaḥ śrutikalpanā /
na hi tatraikamākhāvat krameṇādhyayanaṃ sthitam 
saṃpradāyāgatāṃ mukkā khāṃ samāyānibandhinīm /
śākhā śākhāntaraṃ yuktaṃ nādhyetuṃ mahaśe śrame 
dvitīyābhyāpapa caturtha pāda /
pradhānānyapi prādhānyena yajamānaniyamaṃ pratyapramavantībhiḥ samāvyābhirarthamānamuddiśya vidhīyamānāni sarvaśākhāgatānyeka kaṃ puruṣamupatiṣṭhante /
tatraikaphalatvādasamuccaye  yena kena cit mādhyamāne phate 'nyeṣāṃ vaiyathyaṃ prasaṅgaḥ /
atha teṣāṃ vikalpenārthavattvaṃ tadaraṃ śākhāntarāṇāmeva vyavasthitapratipādyānāmanāṅavataraṃ parikalpitamityapunaruktatā /
samāptivaca saṃprekṣā 
arthāsaṃnniveśca 
ekasya vedavṛcasya kiṃcitkarmaphantāśrayāt evaṃ śākhāḥ prasidhyanti bahubhākhekabudhavat /
yadi pratibhākhaṃ karmabhedaḥ syāt asamāptivaditi vā chedaḥ /
karmabhedapace yāvadeva yeṣāṃ mana ekamalābhāvādādita evārabhya bhidyamānatvāta samastakasamāmnānaṃ tāvadeva teṣāṃ samāpyataiti na brūyuratrāsmākaṃ na mapyapuṣpaphacāntaranbāt bujhāntaravat vedāntarāpayevocceran /
samāpyataiti /
ancārohā nāma sthalārohaṇamantrāsteṣu maināna śākhāntarāṇi /
ekakarmamūnā vidhiskandharūpatve samotikarmayaṇīyānāṃ samāpyate nāsmākamityabhighānādadhyetṝṣṇāmapi kavyatāyāḥ kacit kiṃ cidaṣikamityālocca sārūpyādupapatraḥ maikatvaṃ prasidvamityavamīyate 
eka kasaṃgatāḥ puṃsāṃ vikalpante vidhāyakāḥ /
tatsamopasamāmnātaṃ grāhyaṃ prakaraṇasya ca śākhāntareṣu vikalpamāneṣu yayaiva pradhānaṃ vidhīyate 'rthinastadīyaḥ kathaṃbhāvastāmeva vyāpnoti na śākhāntarāṇi /
atavānyagatā guṇāḥ kathaṃbhāvena nāpekṣitāḥ prayogavacanenānupasaṃcatā nāṅgaṃ bhavantīti nānuṣṭheyā, stataśca vākyasaṃyuktānāmapatvādiṣīyamānānāmastyupasaṃharaṇaśaktiriti /
na tvetadyuktamiva /
tathā ci 
prativedamapi ca prakaraṇaṃ puruṣasya dharmānupadiśati /
na ca tat vedāntarasthaṃ pratyapramāṇaṃ, tathā śākhāntarepi draṣṭavyam/
karmadharmāścaite vijñāyante taca karma śākhāntareṣvapi tadevetyaṅgatvāviśeṣaḥ /
yadyapi prakaraṇarūpamanyat tathāpi śākhāntarasthenānenaitepi dharmā gṛhītā ityavadhāraṇāt na svaprakaraṇagṛhītebhyo viśiṣyante /
sarvākhapi ca śākhākhadhika viṣayo na kathaṃ cit śākhayā parimitā bhavantītyalpa evāyāsa iti nāśaktiḥ /
samāptivāṣītāpe cayo  papannatvānna bhedaṃ kalpayati 
samāptiḥ pūrvavatvādyathājñāte pratīyate 
ekatvepi samāptirliṃṅgatvenoktā samāptivacca saṃpreśceti samāptivacanaṃ nānātvepi /
tatra pratyayānumāritvā  dekatvasyaiva sādhikā tadvacanasyeyamupapattiḥ pūrvatvādityārambhāpeścatvāt /
athavā śabdaprayogasya prasiddhipūrvakatvādyādṛśīṃ vayaṃ samāptiṃ paṇyāmastādṛgyāmayaṃ prayukta iti niścinumaḥ /
sa ca vastunyasamāptepi tacchākhāvijñeyapadārthanamāptau prayukta iti dṛśyate ta smādavirodhaḥ 
dravye vā coditatvāvināmavyavasthā sthānnirdeśād vyavatiṣṭheta tasmānnityānuvādaḥ syāt 
atha yaduktamekādaśinyāṃ pacave disaṃmānadarśanaṃ na syādiনi/
tatra brūmaḥ  anyathāpi tu naivāti panavedyādimānatā /
ekādaśinyabhāvena stūyate  tvekayūpatā 
  babhvavātika /
guṇārthā vā punaḥ śrutiḥ 
saṃsthāvyavasthārthā vā bṛhadrathantarayoḥ punaḥ śrutirbhaviṣyati 
api vā kramasaṃyogāt vidhipṛthaktvamekasyāṃ vyavatiṣṭheta 
pratibhākhaṃ vā vidhipṛthaktvaṃ vyavatiṣṭheta /
tathā sati hi kramabhedaṃ na yāsyanti svaśākhāvidhitāḥ kiyā, parimāṇaṃca maharti nānyatvaṃ pratipayate 
tenaiva gatatvādavācamiti cet ma sūtrakārasyācaiva prathamābhidhānāt 
dvitopādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
tasmāttadeveti matena karma bhinnaṃ kathaṃ cit pratibhākhamiṣṭam /
na kāraṇaṃ saptamamasti cānyadato yathoktaiva tu bhedasiddhiḥ /
iti mahakumārilakṛtau tantraṭīkāryā dvitīyādhyāyasya turīyacaraṇaḥ samāptaḥ samāptava dvitīyādhyāyaḥ /
śubham 
athātaḥ śeṣalakṣaṇam 
dvijavaṣyāḥ paraṃ śiṣṭaṃ yāvatkaṃcana caṇam /
tatsarvaṃ vaktumārabdhamathātaḥ śeṣanta ṛṇam 
yattu śeṣaḥ para/rthatvādityanantaracaṇam /
tatva vālādādī tanmābagocaram 
samāmaya ḍedhā vigṛha iyorvākyārthayoḥ pradarśanīyaḥ 
sarveṣāṃ di jahaṇāntarārthānāṃ prayojyāprayojya prayojakāprayojakaṣadvidhāmaniyamaphalavakarmaviṣayaka saṃdhikārarūpāppāṃ tāvadaṅgātmaka śeṣa viśeṣa prakāratvākaṇāntaragocarāṇāmapi śeṣana cappāntargatatvāvadhāraṇa sthitiḥ 
prayojakāḥ prayoktāraḥ śeṣāṇāmeva śeṣiyāḥ /
kramopi śeṣa evekaprayogavacanāśrayaḥ /
eka phaṇasādhanānāmarthānī chokaphavadupakāro panivadvānāṃ vaika prayogavacanacoditānā yogapaścānuṣṭhāna /
bhakteḥ sāmathryaināṅgabhūtaḥ krama āpadyamānaḥ śrutthaṃpaṭhana sthānamukhyapravṛttikakamākhyapramāṇaṣaṭ kavaśena vyavasthāpyate 
vayati puruṣa karmārthatvāditi jaiminiḥ /
tathā'nāmnāvaśeṣāṇāṃ śeṣiṇā saptamādibhiḥ /
śeṣa sahāvatadrūpaparimāṇādinirṇayaḥ 
saptamenātideśena śeṣāḥ santoti sādhite /
tatoṣṭame naye yasya yasasesi nirūpaṇā 
prayogaparimāṇaṃ ca tattantrāvāpalakṣaṇam /
etadeva prasaṅgena parārthāṅgopajīvanāt 
māthaśavda ānantaryapūrva prakṛtāpeścādhikārāṇāmekaṃ sarvā gvā vivacitvā prayujyate /
prāguktabheda caṇānasaroktatvām pūrvaprakkṛtamapejya śeṣalakṣaṇamārabhyate /
kuta iti detyapekṣāyāmata iti hetuvyapadeśaḥ /
yasmādbhedama vijñāya na śakyaṃ śeṣancakṣaṇam /
vijñātumata etasya tadanantaramucyate  bhinnānāṃ hi padārthānāṃ śeṣaśeṣitva saṃbhavaḥ /
ekave nāpadiśyeta kaḥ śeṣaḥ kasya śeṣiṇaḥ /
bhedānantaravaktavyaṃ śeṣaṇakṣaṇameva ca /
prayojakakamādīnāṃ śeṣatvādhīnacintanāsa /
ayameva ca savandhaḥ saṃmatodhyāyayoīyo /
mammin ci saṃti sūmokte nānyo bhāṣyakṛtoditaḥ 
arthadvārohyadhyāyādisaṃbandho na granthasvarūpāśraya iti saṃ cepoktipiṇḍokṛta  vṛttavartiṣyamāṇādhyāyārthapradarśanapūrva bhā ghyakāreṇaiva saṃbandhaḥ pūrvādhyāyayorabhihitaḥ /
iha tu sūcakāreṇaivāthātaḥ śabdābhyāmupanibaddha iti sa eva vyākhyātaḥ /
nānākarmalakṣaṇaṃ vṛttamiti ca 
prathamādhyāyapratipādito hi pramāṇavivekavidhyarthavādamantrasmṛtiguṇa vidhināmadheyavākya śeṣārthakṛta saṃdigdhavidhinirṇayapravibhāgaḥ pratyekaṃ bhedā dinma caṇeṣu bhedenopayocyataiti prapañcenānubhāṣitaḥ 
tathārthavādavijñānādviṣvādiguṇakā khayaḥ /
yāgā na kalpitāsteṣāṃ vidhiśaktarasaṃbhavāt 
mantrāṇāmapi yatkāryaṃ vicitārthaprakāśanam /
tantravārtika /
tena godānagoyāgau nābhyāsādbhedamāganī 
tathā śabdārthaṃ saṃbandha smṛtitattvāvadhāraṇāt /
prakṣepādhikatāmātrādyāgādbomasya bhinnatā 
kṛtakaṃ cābhidhānaṃ yadanyairā dimaducyate /
nimittaprabhavatvena sūcakārasya tanmatam 
tenānuṣṭhitamityevaṃ yadi nāma smṛtirbhavet /
karma kāṭhakamucyetaṃ kaṭenānuṣṭhitaṃ hi yat 
guṇaścāpūrvasaṃyoge nāmadheyaṃ ca bhedakam /
bhedopayogitā tena guṇānāmatvabodhayoḥ 
paśusaptadaśatvasya na yāgeyattayā vinā /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
siddhirastīti cārthena siddhaḥ saṃdigdhanirṇayaḥ 
grāhyaṃ na tvetade kāntātsaṃ śepokti prayojanamaḥ/
yataḥ pūrvavadeveca prapañcopyupayocyate 
tathā ca pūrvabhedana karmabhedānusāriṇā /
jyaiauṣadhādidharmāṇāṃ vyavasthāṃ sādhayiṣyati 
prasaktānuprasaktoktamhagyajuḥ sāmancam /
śruterjātādhikāra syādityasminnupayocyate 
evamarthadvaye tāvadatha śabdasya varṇitam /
saṃbandhodhyāyayorukto yahā 'rthātmid eva saḥ 
vaktṛvākyagataṃ yattu syātkiṃ ciḍhadhikārabhāk /
na jijñāsāpadaṃ tasya śrotuḥ svārthanirūpakam 
bhāro yo yena voḍhavyaḥ sa prāgātolito yada /
tadā kastasya voḍheti śakyaṃ kartṛnirūpaṇam 
prayojakopi śeṣāṇāṃ śeṣyanyastvaprayojakaḥ /
kariṣyate parā tasmāttaccintā śeṣalakṣaṇāta 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
svarūpa he tusaṃbandhatatpramāṇabajāvalaiḥ /
nanu jñeyā yathā śeṣāḥ śeṣiṇopi tathaiva naḥ 
jñātavyā ubhaye satyaṃ sūtraṇīyā na tubhaye /
arthāpatyā hi sidhyanti dvitīyā ekanna pāt 
prādhānyāccheṣiṇāṃ sājhādyuktaṃ vā śeṣignadakṣaṇam /
na tu tatkriyate tatra kartavyaṃ hi iyaṃ bhavet 
tenopasarjanamyāpi śetrasyaiveha lakṣaṇam /
kriyate śeṣiṇastvarthāttajjñānenaiva sekyati 
śrutyādimāyecavacyate yadvannāvalam /
taccheṣiṣyavirudvatvāccheṣagocarameva naḥ 
taca kaḥ śeṣa iti svarūpābhidhānapratijñā /
kena hetuneti yenāsau śeṣa ityuccate /
tasya ca kārakakṣetosta irmasyaiva lakṣaṇaṃ vaccataiti pratijñāyate 
tṛtīyapadā tadeva pramāṇa yamupanyasya upakramopasaṃhāradārega ekavākyatvena sidvāntasthāpanāt vināpi vākyagrahaṇena prāyadarśanāditi vākyaviniyogamutkā prakaraṇakrama samākhyābhirviniyogaḥ sūtropanibaddha eva vakṣyate/
tato bannāvalādhikaraṇam /
tataḥ paraṃ ca śrutiniṅgavākyānāṃ prakaraṇe maha viro dhāvirodhacintā tāvadyāvatyaḥ sarveṣāṃ paśuvidhiriti
śeṣalagamā coktāvaryādayā cheṣilakṣaṇam /
ataḥ śeṣaḥ parārthatvādityuktaṃ śeṣanāṇām 
yaccānyada vinābhāvaprayojyatvādikāraṇam /
taca sarvaṃ nirākartuṃ pārārthyamiha gṛhyate 
na śeṣo 'nyaḥ parārthatvānna ca hetvantareṇa maḥ /
anyonyaniyamenaiva pacahetvoḥ parigrahaḥ 
tadbhāvabhāvitvena tāvadyo yena vinā na bhavati sa tasya śeṣaḥ /
tadyathāṅkurastoyādibhirvinā na bhavati /
ghaṭaśca mṛtpiṇḍa ḍha ṇḍacakrādibhiriti tayostāni śeṣatvena jñāyante /
tatrocyate 
sarvadā hyavinābhūtā rūpasparśādayaḥ citau /
na caiṣāṃ tulyakalpatvādbhavatyanyonyaśeṣatā /
svāminā ca vinā dāsā na bhavanti kaḍhā cana /
tathā gṛhādayasteṣāṃ śeṣaḥ svāmī ca neṣyate 
evamaṅgapradhānānāmaṅgānāṃ ca parasparam /
pramajyetaiva śeṣatvamavinābhāvalaḍhāṇam /
etenādhyayanādhānakṛṣidravyārjanādiṣu 
prayojyo yasya yastasya sa śeṣa iti niścayaḥ /
na ca svāmī dāsena rūpasparṇādibhirvā yathodāhṛtairanyonyaṃ prayujyate yenātiprasaṅgaḥ syāt /
na tvetadapi śeṣatvacakṣaṇaṃ ghaṭata /
kutaḥ 
siddhestuṣopavāpena śeṣastattasya ceṣyate /
tathā homāḥ prayujyante bhedana skandanādibhiḥ 
tasya taṃ prati śeṣatvamatirekeṇa lakṣyate /
sarvacaiva phalavatpradhānavidheraṅgavidhayoṅgāni pradhānebhyo 'tiriccantaityetadevātirekalakṣaṇaṃ śeṣatvaṃ yuktamityukte 'bhi dhīyate 
anye vidhyādinirdiṣṭapradhānebhyaḥ parānvidhīn /
dṛṣṭvāṅgānya vyavasyanti vidhyantatva parigrahāt 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
sammādidhyādivihitapradhāna kathaṃ bhāvākāṅkṣā pūrā samarthavi dhyanta vihitatvalacaṇameva śeṣatvaṃ mūtrakārābhipretamityukte 'bhidhīyate 
yadi hi niyogato vākyaprakaraṇānteṣveva vyavasthitāḥ śeṣavidhayaḥ samāmnāyaran tata etadavyabhicāra lakṣaṇamā śrīyeta 
pradhānādau vidhīyante ye śākhācchedanādayaḥ /
vidhyādivihitatvātte nāpnuyurdarśaśeṣatām 
aṅgavidhyapakrameṣu tāvadvākya prakaraṇeṣu tadgata kiṃbhāvākā jitapra yojanakalpanāvelāyāṃ kathaṃbhāvākāṅgāyukta pradhānavidhidarśanāta tadapecitopakāra siddhārthatvena teṣāmavadhāryamāṇānāṃ vidhyādigatānāmapi śeṣatvamastīti na vidhyanta vidhānamevaikaṃ śeṣalakhaṇatvenāvakalpate 
na hi bhinnopakārārthaḥ sa tayevopakārakam /
vede ca nānyadaṅgatvakāraṇaṃ dṛśyate va cita 
tantravārtike /
tasmādapapatramidaṃ sakṣaṇamiti 
mādayaṃmapi naivānyaduprakārātpratīyate /
tenopakāra evaiko vijñeyaṃ śeṣalakṣaṇam 
evaṃ sati pradhānānāmaṅgānāṃ ca parasparam /
aṅgāṅgānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ saṃkīryetaiva śeṣatā /
yathaiva hyaṅgāni pradhānānāmupakurvanti tathaivānuṣṭhāpanenopakārapratigrahaṇācca pradhānānyapyaṅgānāmupakurvantyeva /
kutaḥ 
pradhānānyapyatoṅgānāmaṅgāni sṭuranugrahāt /
syādanyonyopakārācca teṣāmanyonyaśeṣatā 
tasmātparasparāṅgatvamupakārāt prasajyate /
nāyamaṅgakṛtādeṣāmupakārā dilacaṇaḥ /
evamaṅgānāmapyanyonyāpādanaṃ darśayitavyam /
tataścaikapradhānavikāreve kāṅgagamanevi samastasāṅgapradhānagamanāda niyamaḥ prāpnoti 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
nahi tadanugraharahitaṃ kiṃ citmidhyati 
jñātaṃ ca lakṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ nakṣyaṃ jakṣayituṃ kṣamam /
tatra dṛṣṭopakārāṇāṃ tatkṛtā śeṣatā bhavet 
anavagataśeṣatvāvastheṣūpakārādarśana/
sadadhīnāvadhāraṇaṃ śeṣatvaṃ na syāt /
kalpitaupakāre bhaviṣyatīti cet na /
prāgaṅgatvādupakārakapanāpramāṇābhāvāt /
yo hi yasya phalamya pha javato vā śeṣatvenāvadhārito bhavati ma kathaṃ tasyopakariṣyatītyapekṣite sati dvaṣṭamupakāramapaśyadbhiḥ tasmādadṛṣṭaḥ parikalagate /
yāvattu śeṣatvameva nāvagamyate tāvatkena pramāṇe nāha ṭa kalpanā syāt 
na ca prāsaṅgikatvācchāstreṇopakāraḥ pratipādyataiti pratyābhirevopakāraṃ gṛhotvā śeṣatvaṃ gamyeta 
evametasminnapi pakṣe sarva tantraṃ vighaṭate /
tasmāducyate śeṣaḥ parārthatvāditi /
akupoṣṭotadarthavyapaḍhe prabhāk /
upakurvannapi tvanyastadathaṃiti nocyate 
tadyathā maśakārtho dhūma ityapakā riṣyapi prayujyate /
tathopakurvannapi prasaḍagya prayojakayorna tādayena vyapadiśyate /
na hi kaścidapi śālikullyālā mudakaṃ pibanmadarthametāḥ praṇītā ityadhyavasthati 
nanu copakāranirapekṣaṃ naiva sādathyeṃ śakyaṃ kalpayitum /
kutaḥ 
na hi prayājādayaḥ sāmīpyamāce ṇaivopakāra nirapekṣāstābṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
dathyeṃ pratipadyante /
tasmādupakārapūrvakameva tādarthyamiti sa eva śeṣatvakāraṇaṃ prāpnoti 
śrutya tāvattadarthatvaṃ ca citpūrvaṃ pratīyate /
anyatrāpyupakāritvādapekṣāmācapūrvakam 
nahājavagatāṅgatveṣu prayājādiṣūpakāradarśanaṃ kalpanaṃ cāstītyuktam /
ato darśapūrṇamāsayo rupakāramapekṣamāṇayoḥ prayājādiṣu copakāryamapeśamā jeṣvaniṣpannāvasthaevopakāre prakaraṇāttādathyaṃ tāvatpratoyate /
tadanyathānupapattimāceṇopakāraka apanā 
nopakārādeva śeṣatvaṃ tādathyaṃ vetyanavadyam /
evaṃ ca sati śrutyādonyeva tādarthyapratipāṭanarūpeṇa śeṣasya viniyojakānīti tadvivekārthaṃ lakṣaṇamārabdhavyam/
satyapi/
cāṅgapradhānādīnāmupakārasaṃkara'tādarthyāda saṃkarasthitisiddhiḥ /
tasmātparārthatvalakṣaṇameva śeṣatvaṃ nirdoṣaṃ yaḥ parasyopakāre vartataiti pārāśarya mevākāraṇa phalenābhidhīyata ityaṣa gantavyaṃ na tvatrai khakṣaṇātibhrāntiḥ  kartavyā 
parastu tatrāpyupakārakatvāḍhatyeva kaścittādarthyaleśa iti pratyavatiṣṭhate 
namu ca tadadhyāyoktenaiva lakṣaṇena gatārthatvānnāca vaktavyam /
ata āha tatrāpūrthatā vyāvarttitati /
tatra ke cidaṃba vyācakṣate 
tadabhidhīyate 
sarvaviṣayavyāpi śeṣatvam i i nabhyameva  tatra nītamapūrvabha danirākaraṇārtham /
athavā pūrvokta guṇapradhānabhāvalacamanapecyā pūrvavatsaṃprati kāraṇāntarānarāmena parārthatvalakṣaṇe śeṣatve tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
'bhihite yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyata ityanemopakāralaṇābhyupagamāddirodhamāśaṅkya paricarati /
tacāpūrvabhedakalpanā nivṛttyartha mupakāradarśanamuktaṃ na śeṣandā pātvenā, na punaḥ sarvaśeṣāṇāṃ pāramārthikaṃ lakṣaṇamevoccataiti bhinnaviṣayatvādavirodha iti 
guṇopyaruṇādiḥ kriyāyāḥ svasādhanabhūtadravyaparicchedasāmarthyādutpattyaiva śeṣaḥ 
nanu ca bhāvārthādhikaraṇe karaṇatvaṃ bāgasyoktaṃ satyamuktaṃ na tu sādhitam/
svargakāmādhikaraṇādhīnasiddhinā tena nāmapaṭa kara pātvamācanirākaraṇāt 
phantamapi yāgaṃ prati mādhyamānatvātpradhānanaṃ puruṣaṃ prati tvasya śeṣabhāvo naivopāttaḥ 
tantravārtike/
karmāṇyapi jaimini phalārthatvāt 
gatārthametat 
na hikaciduddhipūrvakāryevaṃ kāmayate svarga ātmānaṃ labhatāmiti /
kintarhi mama upabhogyaḥ svāditi 
tenopabhoktāraṃ prati phantamapi śeṣabhūtam 
evaṃ catuḥsūtreṇādhikarona samastaḥ śeṣatvaviṣayaḥ pratipāditaḥ 
yattāvad dravyaguṇa saṃskāra vityatra na tu yāgaphala puruṣeṣu śeṣatvamityabhiṣāyānte puruṣasya śeṣitvanirākaraṇaṃ tadasaṃbaddham /
yattu pratyakṣaścāsya dravyatvātkarma pratiguṇabhāva iti /
tadapi vyāhataṃ punaruktaṃ ca pūrvameṣābhihitatvāt /
na ca yāgaphanābhyāṃ śeṣatvanirākaraṇa dṛdbhyāṃ mahāsyātulya pravṛttitvāduccāraṇaṃ yuktaṃ tasmādasadetat 
tadapi prathamameva dravyagaṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ gi tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
rapekṣaśeṣatvābhidhānāt karmaphannapuruṣāṇāṃ ca dravyādīni prati prādhānyeva sthite sūcaireva parasparāpekṣaśeṣatvapratipādanāduktārthamiti mandaphalaṃ dṛśyate 
na tu yāgaphalapuruṣeṣu siddhāntavādisaṃmataṃ dvyākāratvam/
yāgaphalayorekāntenaiva śeṣitvātyaruṣasya cātyanta śeṣatvā, tsarvathā ya evaika ākāra pratiṣidstanaiva tadyākāratvanira/
karaṇaṃ śakyamiti trayāṇāmapyetāvatā tutyadharmatvātma nirdeśaḥ /
karmāṣyapi jaiminirityādibhirantapatiyākārameva śeṣatvaṃ pratipāditam /
pārārghya lakṣaṇa śeṣatvāṅgīkaraṇāt/
nanvevaṃ sati puruṣasya dravyatvātpūrvapañcavādinaitantravārtika /
vābhyupagamya  śeṣatvaṃ śeṣitve nirākṛte sidvāntavādinā tadeva pratipādanīyamiti na vaktavyaṃ puruṣaśca karmārthatvāditi /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
tena hi yāgaphantayoraśeṣatvāt tasya śeṣitvaṃ nirākṛtaṃ tataśva yāvadeva sūtradayena  yāgaphalayoḥ śeṣatvaṃ pratipāditaṃ tāvadeva yāgopasarjanaṃ phalaṃ prati pradhānatvādubhau prati kevalaṃ śeṣitvameva prasaktamiti pralīne hyākāratve punaḥ śeṣatvapratiprasavārthamucyate puruṣaśca karmārthatvāditi /
atha vā pareṇopakāradvāreṇa śeṣatvamabhyupagataṃ tadayuktaṃ manyamānaḥ phalayāgayorivāsyāpi pārārthyakṛtameveti pratipādayiṣyannāha /
puruṣaśca karmārthatvānna tadupakāritvāditi 
athātra bhagavāniti /
naivedānīṃ bādarimataṃ pūrvapañcaḥ /
kiṃ tarhi śeṣaḥ parārthatvāditi sāmānyena lacaṇamukkā tasyaiva viṣayaprardaśanadvāreṇottaraḥ prapañcaḥ kriyate /
tatra pūrvavyākhyāyāṃ dravyaguṇa saṃskāra ṣveva śeṣatvamityevamavadhāraṇaṃ pūrvapace kṛtam /
idānīṃ tu siddhāntarūpeṇaiva bādarimatamapratiṣedhenānumataṃ kṛtvā lakṣaṇa prapañcābhyāṃ śeṣatvaṃ varṇayiṣyate 
tasmādāpekṣikaśeṣaśeṣitvamātramevebhiḥ sūtraiḥ pratipādyate 
nanu ca dravyatṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
guṇasaṃskārāṇāmapi svāṅgāni prati pradhānatvādyāgaṃ ca prati guṇabhāvādāpekṣikameva śeṣaśeṣitvam /
tathā hi 
yeṣāṃ tu guṇānāṃ niṣpādyā sā tānprati śeṣiṇī /
tathā saṃskāraḥ saṃmārgāvaghātādiragnibrohyāde śeṣaḥ svasādha nānāmidhvamana hanola khalamusalādīnāṃ śeṣo /
tasmānnāvadhāraṇaṃ sidhyatīti /
taducyate 
dravyaguṇasaṃskārā hi phalavantaṃ yāgaṃ prati niyogataḥ śepabhūtāḥ satyapi svāṅgāni prati śeṣitve taṃ prati nāstītyabhidhīyate /
ata eva bhāṣyakāropi niyogato yajiṃ prati śeṣabhāva ityāha /
na bravīti niyataḥ śeṣabhāva ityāpeśika itareṣāmityatrāpi yajiṃ pratītyanuvartate /
tathā ho kaikasya ho /
prati guṇatvaṃ prādhānyaṃ ca dṛśyate /
yāgasya tā vad dravyātmakaṃ nirvartakaṃ puruṣaṃ prati prādhānyaṃ phalaṃ prati guṇātā/
yaśca phacaṃ prati guṇaḥ sa  śakyate phalasya svāminaṃ puruṣa mapi prati sutarāṃ guṇa iti vaktum /
tathā yasya puruṣaṃ prati prā dhānyaṃ tasya tadupasarjanaṃ phalaṃ prati sutarāṃ tadityapi śakyanirūpaṇam /
evaṃ phalasya yāgaṃ prati prādhānyāttatmāghanaṃ puruṣamapi prati prādhānyaṃ, puruṣaṃ prati guṇatvāttadanuṣṭheye yāgepi guṇatvaṃ, tathā puruṣasya phalaṃ prati prādhānyāt tatsādhanaṃ yāgamapi prati pradhānatvam, yāgaṃ ca prati guṇabhāvāttatmādhye phalepi guṇātvam, na tvevaṃ dravyaguṇa saṃskāra sviti viśeṣaḥ /
yattvidaṃ pāraṃparyeṇāpi śeṣatvaṃ prādhānyaṃ coktam idamarthalaścaṇaṃ vastumātrarūpeṇetyava gantavyam/
na vyavahārārthaṃ mā bhūdaṅgatvaśina vikṛta/
phalapuruṣayorapyatideśātmidvāntavirodhaḥ /
tasmādetāvatprakāra eva vacya māṇa prapañcaśeṣatva viṣayasaṃkṣepa iti siddham 
tattvācāryā necchanti /
yadyapyatra vicitrapramāṇavyāpāraparāmarśaḥ tathāpi śrutiviniyogaṇvāca pār̤he liṅgādiviniyogastu dvitīyapādātprabhṛti bhaviṣyatītyuktam  /
auṣadhadharmā ityādyetadadhikaraṇasādhyamapi sidvāntābhiprāyeṇoktam /
nanu saṃyuktā evaitaiti siddhāntavādī śrutibalena saṃśayamācipati paraḥ punaḥ padāntarasaṃbandhakṛtaṃ brīhyādisaṃbandhaṃ śuddhāvaghātavidhinā bādhyamānaṃ manyamāna āi 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
prayujyate padaṃ kiṃ cihinā na hi paṃdāntarāt /
vākyādhikaraṇe coktā śrutibāghapratikriyā /
nahi vrohyādibhiḥ saṃvadhyamānā avaghātādayo nāvaghātādayo bhavanti /
yadi hyevaṃ bhaveyuḥ tataḥ śrutiviruddhatvā dvākyaṃ bādhyeta /
atra punaḥ kevalānā mevāvaghātādīnāmanuṣṭhātu maśakyatvāt avaśyameva saṃbandhyantare kāryā  /
na hi bhavatyakṣepyavaghātādayaḥ kevala kiyate 
atha tu naiva kena citsaṃbadhyate tato vidhyānarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ 
tenaivaṃ vyākhyeyam 
naivācāyaṃ pūrva pacaheturavaghātādayaḥ padārthāḥ svatantrāḥ śrutyā vidhīyante 
vidhīyate 'vaghātādiḥ śrutyā brahmādisaṃgataḥ /
vrīhitvādyarthatā cāsya niṣphanatvena neṣyate 
tataḥ saṃyuktatvātsarve sarvaca na prāpnuyuḥ /
ete punarnavamādyādhikaraṇanyāyena śra/taṃ brocitvamujaṅkhyā pūrva sādhanatvena saṃbadhyante /
tacca pra karaṇa/
peśāpūrva sādhanāṃśannā pāgamyatvādvākya gamya miti manyamāna āha 
teṣāmarthena saṃbandhaḥ /
yadyapi tāvatkevannapadavācyāḥ śrayeran tathāpi kva kriyeran ityapekṣite yatra kriyamāṇāḥ prayojanavanto bhavanti tatra kartavyāḥ/
na caite saṃkīryamāṇāḥ sarvatra prayojanavanto dṛśyante /
satyapi cāpūrvaprayuktatve dṛṣṭaprayojanadāra eva saṃbandho 'vakalpate athavā śāstreṇaiva yatra kriyamāṇāḥ prayojanavanto vijñāyante yaha pūrva mādhanaṃ  brohyādiśabdaiḥ svābhidheyajātyekārthamamavāyi lakṣitaṃ tadarthatvenāvaghātādayo vijñāyamānāḥ saṃbandhābhāvādapūrvāntara sādhane'jakṣite na bhaviṣyanti /
nanu śrūyante ma ve sarvacetyapūrvekavāde cāmati jacaṇāniyamāparijñānātprayojanasya ca vidhyuttarakājalabhyatvānna tadarśanadvāreṇa vyavastheti matvā paricodanā /
etadeva na jānīma iti /
nāvaśyame kamevāpūrva prayojakamapūrvamātraṃ vetyabhiprāyaḥ 
vihitastu sarvadharma syāt saṃyogato viśeṣātmakaraṇāviśeṣāca 
paraḥ svābhiprāyaṃ vivṛṇoti /
phalasya hi sūkṣmasāmarthya rūpāvasyāṅkura sthānīyā pūrvānutpannotpattera pūrvamityuktaṃ prāk /
ta ca phanaikatvāde kame vādhyavasoyate /
tatsādhanatvaṃ cājyaupathasānāyyānāṃ sarveṣāma viśiṣṭam /
atastaduddeśena vihitānāṃ sarvadharmatvaṃ vijñāyate /
yadyapi cāgneyādīnāmavāntarāpūrvāṇi prātyātmikāni bhaveyaḥ /
tathāpi teṣāṃ niṣphalatvādyāgādisvarū pavadeva prayojakaśaktirnāstīti paramāpūrvameva prayojakamavadhāryate /
bhinnāpūrvaprayuktatvepi prakaraṇagatā pūrva sādhanamā coddeśana vidhīyamānānāṃ śeṣāṇāṃ viśeṣeṇānupādānādupādāneca vākyabhedaprasaṅgāt sārvatrika vidhānamastīti sarvadharmatve hetuḥ /
ta tmiḍyarthaṃ ca saṃyogato viśeṣātprakaraṇāviśeṣāccaityuktam /
yadekatyā pūrva sādhanatvaṃ dharmasaṃbandhakāraṇaṃ taditara cāpya viśiṣṭam/
yattu viśiṣṭaṃ vrīhitvādi tad lakṣaṇāmātraupayikatvādaniyāmaka m/
yadapi kārakatvaṃ lakṣyate tadapi sarveṣāṃ pradeyatvāḍhaviśiṣṭam /
tamādapūrvī saṃbaddhama pradeyamaprakṛtāpūrvasādhanaṃ ca varjayitvā sarve sarvatra kartavyāḥ /
yo arthātprāpnotītyacoditaḥ san sāmarthya na laukika prayojanena vā yaḥ prāpnoti sa tadarśana vyavatiṣṭhate /
atha vā yatra pūrvataraprāptaprayojanadvāreṇa dharmāḥ prāpnuvanti na ca dharmebhya eva prayojanakalpanā, yathā vikṛtiṣu, tatra yāvadartha tvaṃ bhavet /
atra punaḥ prakṛtābupadeśena prāka prayojanebhyaḥ svarūpamātreṇa kalpayiṣyamāṇaprayojanāḥ santo vidhīyante 
arthalopādakarma syāt 
dṛṭārthaṃ lopācchāvagamyārthalopādveti nigadavyākhyātaṃ bhāghyam /
phalaṃ tu saha ceṣṭayā śabdārtho Sbhā vādviprayoge syāt 
yaduktamadṛṣṭa kalpanānnaivetaratrāpyarthacopa iti 
yadyāhatya vivarannājyepi prathanādayaḥ /
adṛṣṭārthā agatyā syurdṛṣṭaṃ vā na bhavedyadi 
taccāmnānamanyathaiva dṛṣṭārthatayopapanna mityarthāpatterasaṃbhavaḥ 
anyatra tu ceṣṭāmātram /
na ca saphalaceṣṭānuṣṭhānasaṃbhave viphalānuṣṭhāne vi tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
dhiḥ puruṣaṃ niyoktuṃ śaknoti 
taditaretarāśrayaṃ bhavati /
phalādidhirvidheśca phacamityabhyupagamāt 
tathotpavanādīnāmājyasānnāyyayoriti yojanīyam /
tathā yorthaḥ pratyakṣadṛṣṭopi kratunā puruṣeṇa vā /
nāpecyetopakārāya so' grāhyo na tvayaṃ tathā 
biprayoge tu dṛṣṭasya phalasya tadabhāvajā /
teṣāṃ śabdārthamā atkhātyā dṛṣṭārthakalpanā 
tathā hi 
atha vā tata ete sarvatra vihitā bhaveyuḥ yadi paramāpūrvaprayuktāḥ sarvāpūrvaprayuktā vā syuḥ tadā caivaṃ te bhaveyuḥ yadi bhinnāni vīcādikarmāpūrvāṇi na syuḥ yadi caiṣāṃ prayojakaśaktirna syāt 
tatra bhedastāvadapūrvādhikaraṇe sādhitaḥ /
yadyapi caiṣāṃ sākṣādaphalatvaṃ tathāpi svarūpasiddhyanyathānupapattyaiva prayojakatvaṃ bhaviṣyati /
na ca niṣphajāni, tannāma niṣpha latvādaprayojakaṃ bhavati yadatyantaniṣphalaṃ, tannirapekṣaṃ vā dravyayāgādisvarūpavat labdhātmakam/
āgneyādyavāntarāpūrvāṇi tu paramāpūrvasiddhyaṅgatvātpāraṃparyeṇa phalavanti /
na ca dharmebhyaḥ prāk siddhāni nirjātopāyaparimāṇāni vā /
tasmādātmalābhārthameva prayujyante /
yacca yeṣu dharmeṣu vidhīyamāneṣvapūrvamupatiṣṭhate tatteṣāṃ prayojakaṃ bhavati na yāvatkiṃ cid vīhyādiśabdaiśca svakarmamādhyameva kevanamapūrvaṃmupasthāpyate nānyadasaṃbandhāt 
tadarśayati /
yasmādavacananādiceṣṭayā saha śruteṣu vohyādiṣveva svāpūrvasādhanadvāreṇa vidheḥ phalaṃ dṛśyate tasmānnānyatra saṃkrāntiḥ /
yadi tu tatrāpūrvaṃ na syāt tatorthādadṛṣṭaṃ karapyeta /
vohyādiśabdairanapasthāpitopyupakāraḥ prayojakaḥ kalpyetāsti tu tat 
viprayoge taṇḍulādinivyādyasyāpūrvasya prayojanābhāvātmānnāyyādi  saṃbandhopi vyavahitaparamāpūrvadvāreṇa karmāntarāpūrvadvāreṇa vā śabdārthaḥ syāt 
evaṃ tagneyādyapūrvasaṃvandhāviśeṣāt srugādīnāmavaghātādayaḥ prāpnuvanti/
naiṣa dotṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
ṣaḥ /
kārakāntaratvena teṣāmalakṣitatvā, dyathaiva hi pradeyatvāvi śeṣepi sānnāyyādarapūrvāntarasādhanatvādapratītiḥ evamekāpūrvasaṃbandhepi vīkṣitvaikārtha samavetapradeyarūpakārakatvābhāvāt srugādīnāmagrahaṇam /
yattu tasminnevāpūrve samānakārakatvenopakariṣyati tasya bhaviṣyantyeva dharmāḥ /
yathā yavānāṃ sarvaṃ caitannabame vistareṇa vacyāmaḥ 
sphyāderutpattisaṃbandhaḥ kāryerudnanādibhiḥ /
tatra yajñāyudhānīti prāptamevānukīrtyane /
etāni vai daśa yajñāyudhānīti vaiśabdasaṃyogādasyānuvādasārūpyaṃ na cātra bhāvanāvacano vidhāyakosti yo viniyuñjīta vidadhyādeti /
bahutarāṇi ca vākyāni tvatpaśce 'narthakāni bhaveyuḥ /
na hoṣāmanuvādatve kiṃ citprayojanamasti /
sāmāccaitāni svābhidhānairudnanādiṣveva viniyujyante /
parokṣavṛcyā yajñāyudhavākye yajñaśabdasyāṅgalavaṇārthatvādāyudhaśabdasya ca yusādhanavacanasya kriyāntara sādhaneṣvaupacārikatvāt/
na cāsa saptadaśāratninyāyovakalpate /
na hyatra vājapeyasyetivatsaṃbandhamātrābhidhāyinī yajñaśabdātyarā ṣaṣṭhī dṛśyate /
satyapi cānarthakyāttadaṅgāvataraṇe sāmānyaśāstrāṇi viśeṣaśāstrairuḍanamādisaṃyuktarupasaṃhriyamāṇāni na karmāntaraiḥ saṃbadhyeran /
tasmādunanādivākyaprāpitānāṃ satāṃ yādṛśaṃ vayaṃ yajñāyudhatvaṃ paśyāmaḥ tādṛśametāni vai daśetyanenānūdyate /
yattvapūvabhedaḥ prayojako nāstīti /
tatra brūmaḥ/
kapālādīnāṃ tāvadastyeva paroḍāga dyapūrvabhedaḥ /
itareṣāmapyudvananādidvāratvādanyatra ta skṛtopakārābhāvāda saṃkaraḥ /
tadyathāvaghātādayaḥ samānāpūrvanivandhaneṣvapi srugādiṣu kārakāntaratvānna kriyante 
nanu ca piṅgācye kahāyanī śavdayorapi guṇavacana tvānnevāca vākye dravyamasti kathaṃ gaṇavacanatvamiti cet 
bahuvoddisamāsoyaṃ matubarthe vidhīyate /
soyāstīti pya saṃbandhe matvarthīyaḥ pravartate 
na hi gobhirasaṃbaddho gomānityabhidhīyate /
tasmādviśeṣaṇaṃ tatra saṃbandhaḥ pūrvamiṣyate 
pratyayastu tatra vartata ityupādatte /
sa cedupāttastenaiva saṃbandhipratyayasiddherabhidhānaśalipratibandhāt viśeṣyānabhidhānam /
na ca viśeṣyapratyayātsaṃvandhapratyayo bhavati /
prāk saṃbandhādviśeṣyatvābhāvā, siddheśca viśeṣyatvena saṃbandhe na paścātkiṃcitprayojanamastītyapratītirevāsya prāpnoti /
tasmātprathamatara pratyāyyatvātpratyayārthaḥ saṃbandhaḥ /
itaśca pratyayārthaḥ saṃvandhaḥ /
śabdavṛttinimitte hi bhāvapratyaya iṣyate /
devadattasya gomattvaṃ saṃvandhaśca pratīyate 
tathā devadattasya gomattvamityukte gavi pratipattyabhāvātsaṃbandha niṣkarṣa pratī eva bhāvapratyayārthodhdavasīyate 
yadi ca matupā saṃbandhobhihitaḥ tataḥ prakṛtipratyayau pratyayārthaṃ saha brūta  iti gomatprātipadikādutpanno bhāvapratyayaḥ tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
saṃbandhamabhighāta marhati nānyathā /
tasmādapi saṃbandhorthaḥ /
etena sarve yaugikāḥ kṛttadvitasamāseṣu vyākhyātāḥ /
sarvatra hi bhāvapratyayaḥ saṃvandhamabhidhatte /
rājapuruṣatvamāpagavatvaṃ pācaphatvami, tyata evaite yaugikāḥ yatastena nimittena vartante /

kiṃ ca 
ekaṃ hāyanamasyā iti ṣaṣyantenānyapadārthaḥ pradargyate /
ṣaṣyathaṃsya ca pratyayārthatvādiha prādhānyam /
tadrūpadarśanārthameva    sarvanāmaprayogaḥ kevalāyā vibhaktaraprayogātsarvanāmārthapratītyabhāvācca /
ṣaṇṭyāśca svaskhāmisaṃbandha samūhavikārāvayavādisaṃbandho vācya ityetatprasiddham /
śratopi saṃbandhābhidhānaṃ bahubrokṣiṇā /
na cāpyanyapadārthagvaṃ jāteradhyavasīyate /
na hi piṅgācisaṃbandha stasyā nāpyekavarṣatā 
vayovasthābhidhīyeta yadyapi tvekadāyinī /
tathāpi guṇa evāsau na dravyamiti gamyate 
uccate 
yadyeka hāyanyādibhiḥ śabdaḥ saṃbandhobhidhīyeta tato nodāhriyeran /
na tvetaiḥ saṃbandhobhidhīyate /
katham atigauravāt /
idda hi saṃbandhamātraṃ vābhidheyaṃ kalpyeta tahiśeṣovā /
yadi tāvatsaṃbandhamācaṃ tataḥ sarvayaugikānāmeka viṣayopanipātātyaryāyatvaprasaṅgaḥ 
tataśca tamabhidhāya saṃvanvābhiṣāyāmatigauravaṃ syāt

punastasyābhiṣāśakti kaḥ śruteḥ parikalpayet

yattvapratīte saṃbandhe viśeṣyaṃ na pratīyataiti /
tatra brūmaḥ 
devadatto hi gobhiravacchinno vivakṣitaḥ 
na viśiṣanti gāvorthaṃ pṛthivyāmanavasthitāḥ /
tatra kiṃ śakyate vaktaṃ pṛthivyapyabhidhīyate 
tantravārtika /
vaktṛvyāpāramātraṃ ca saṃbandha pratyavekṣaṇam /
sa hi gobhirasaṃbaddhaṃ na gomantaṃ vivakṣati /
sarvatra hi vaktakama viparyayeṇa śrotuḥ kramo bhavati/
sahi prathamaṃ tāvatkiṃ cidviśeṣyaṃ vivaśati tatastasya kena cidviśeṣaṇena vinābhidhātumabhakteḥ viśeṣaṇavivacāṃ karoti tataḥ śabdoccāraṇam/
śrotā punaḥ prathamaṃ tāvacchandaṃ pūṭaṇoti tato viśeṣaṇaṃ tato viśeṣyaṃ tatastadupapattyarthāni vasvantarāṇi pra padyate /
tena yadyapi vaktrā pūrva saṃbandha ālocitaḥ tathāpi śrotā paścādevainaṃ grahīṣyati /
na tvatra vaktrāpyasai/
pūrvataramacadhāritaḥ 
viśeṣyatvena saṃpannaṃ tadviśeṣaṇasaṃgatam /
goviśiṣṭoyamityevaṃ gomacchabdobhidhāsyati 
vibhaktivācyarūpeṇa saṃbandho nāvagamyate /
rūpāntareṇa vaktavya iti nāsti ca lakṣaṇam 
tatra tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
kimasattvabhūtasaṃbandhābhidhānamāśrīyatām uta saṃbandhyevārthasabhyatadviśiṣṭobhidhīyatāmiti taducyatām  
yattu siddhe viśeṣye na paścātsaṃbandhapratyayena kāryamiti /
satyaṃ nāsti, vināpi tu tena nāntarīyakatvātpratīyataiti kiṃ kriyatām yacca bhāvapratyayenābhidhānādasya matvarthatvamityatrāphi bramaḥ 
gomato bhāvo gomattvamiti hi

ata ṭaṇḍiśabdena saṃvandhyevocyate yathā /

yahadhyekaṃ cāyanamanyā ityanyapadārtho ṣaṇyarthaprādhānyātsaṃbandhe bahuvrodhiriti /
tatrābhidhīyate 
yadi tvanyapadārthaḥ ṣaṇyanta eva saṃbandhī sthāna tato yathaiva rājaḥ puruṣa ityatra ṣaṇyanmatvādrājā puruṣaviśeṣāṃ bhavati /
prathamāntatvācca paruṣaḥ pradhānarūpeṇa samāmārtho bhavati evameva citragvādiśabdairdevadattādiviśiṣṭā gāva eva pratoyeran na citragoviśiṣṭo devadattādiḥ 
yadyapyanyathā vigrahaḥ tathāpyuttarakālamohagarthadarśanādevameva vigrahoṣi kartavyaḥ 
tacca  na pūrvottarapadārthayotṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
napyanyatarasyetyanya padārthabhūtadravyaprādhānyādhyavasānam 
citravyaktiriyaṃ jātidravyaṃ nānāguṇaṃ tvidam /
guṇone kāśrayaḥ kaścidi kāśrayā kiyā 
tadiheka chāyanamasyā iti jāteranāditvānna viśeṣaṇaṃ saṃbhavatīti vyaktirāśrīyate 
ānantyepi hi bhāvānā mekaṃ kṛtvopalakṣaṇam /
śabdaḥ sukara saṃvandho na ca vyabhicariṣyati 
na ca tadupalakṣitābhyonyatra prayoga ityavyabhicāraḥ 
sarvathā dūramapi viśeṣaṇamālāyāmanuvartamānāyāṃ prathamopalakṣaṇasyābhedātsaṃbandhadarśanamupapatsyate /
sarvaprathama sarvāntyayośca śa vdārthatvam /
āntarādhikānāṃ tu lakṣaṇāsiddhajñānatvādanabhidheyatvam /
ataśca piṅgatvākṣitvābhyāṃ svavyaktayo guṇāvayavātmikā lakṣyante tābhiravayavi dravyamupalakṣyate 
yuktaṃ devatātadvitādāvananyaprayojanatvācchandādhikyasyā nyapadārthābhidhānam 
iha tu citragurityevamādiṣu citragośabdayoratyantavyatiriktārthābhidhāyitvāt devadattādiśabdaiśca na tyā kṣaṇayā vā sāmānādhikaraṇyamavakalpate /
prāgapi ca devadattādiśabdādanyapadārthapratīteḥ na vākyārthatvakalpamā/
na ca kevalaṃ samāsavelāyāṃ yā padārthāvavadharito to de vatādyaryasaṃbandhino yato vākyārtho devadattaḥ syāt /
tasmādavabhyaṃ pratīteḥ smaraṇācānyapadārthomya vācca ityabhyupagantavyam /
evaṃ ca prādhānyamaviruddhaṃ bhaviṣyati/
ataścaivamādiṣu bahuvrīheranyapadārthābhidhānaśaktirdṛṣṭeti yatrāpi kathaṃ cijñaṛṇā saṃbhavati tatrāpi pūrvakṛtabhaktyanapāyāda bhidheyatvame vādhya vasīyate /
tasmādupapanaṃ piṅgācyādīnāṃ dravyavacanatvam /
yattvaka cāyanīti vayovacana iti tadanupapannam 
tena tarhyayamevārtho niścīyataiti krayasaṃbandho nāśaṅkitavyaḥ /
tadarthamāha /
na cāśanīyamarthaṃ pramāṇabhūtaḥ śabdobhidhāsyatīti /
yadetatmamānavākyopādānaṃ karaṇavibhaktinirdeśaścaitenāpi krayaika cāyanī viśeṣaṇatvabuddhirhaḍhā jāyate /
tena śabdaprāmāṇyādvastuvisaṃvādācca kiṃ samañjasaṃ kimasamañjasamiti jāyate sandehaḥ /

vaidika śabdasyātibhārābhāvāt /

atha tuna kathaṃ canopapate tato vākyabhedamabhyupagamya prakaraṇadharmamenamadhyavasyāmaḥ /
na cātra vātantravārtike /
kyabhedaḥ pratyayādyanyatamāvṛttilakṣaṇaḥ /
kastarhi vibhāgarūpaḥ /

pṛthak bhavadākya bhedayatīti vākyabhedaḥ /
tādṛśaṃ cābhyupagamya prakaraṇadharmāvyavasānam/

kiṃ tāvatprāpta mata

tasmātsarva karaṇānyaruṇīkartavyāni /
yatpunaryajamānādi vihitaṃ kārakāntaram /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
na tasyāyaṃ guṇaḥ śeṣaḥ sarvārthopyavadhāritaḥ 
tathā cāntareṇāpi matvarthoyaṃ dravyamāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ pratipadyante 
śabdānāṃ na hi lopena vācyorthaḥ pratipādyate /
tasmādubhayamāmarthyamevaṃ tatrāvagamyate 
na ca kṣaṇātu śāstreṇānyākhyānaṃ kriyate /
rūpādīnāmapi ca nakṣaṇopapattermatupā vinā vṛttiḥ syāt /
candanasya gandha iti vaccāntaraṇa bhāvapratyayaṃ gorarupaṇa ityapi prayogaḥ syāt /
yathā ca gandhatvamityakte candanādisaṃbandhamapāsya tadviśeṣāṇāṃ gandhatvasaṃbandho bhavati /
evamarupātvamityapi dravyasaṃbandho na syāt /
pādiśabdavadeva cāruṇāḍherapi dravyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na syā, dyo hi manyate lakṣaṇayāmpādiṣu sāmānādhikaraṇyamiti tasya rūpādiṣvapi tathaiva svādaruṇatvādiṣu vā, na hite kiṃ cidrapyadhikaṃ vadanti /
etenārutvādibhyo matublopaprasaṃktirvyākhyātā /
kiṃ ca 
nanu guṇavacanānāmāśrayato liṅgavacanāni bhavantītyevaṃ setyati/
na, rūpādiśuklatvādiyvapi prasaṅgāt /
api ca /
guṇavacana iti na guṇābhidhānamātreṇoccate/
kiṃ tarhi guṇamukkā yo dravye vartate /
na hyanyathā vacanaśabdaḥ prayujyate  /

yeṣāṃ tāvatkāryadravyāpayeva ghaṭādīni paccante yathā paiṭharāṇāṃ tanmatenābheda eva/
pailūkānāmapi tu paramāṇuṣu vyabhicā raḥ /
yādṛśaṃ tvatmābhirdravyamabhihitaṃ tādṛśasya sarvatra guṇamātrameva bhidyate na svarūpam 
ataścākṛtivyavahārāddūre sthūnatarīyamityapeśalatā 
yattu mukhya pratyayānnaivamiti tatroccate 
agnirmāṇavaka ityatrāgnimāṇavakayo ratyantabhedātmādṛśyeka śabdaḥ pravartamānaḥ pratyayavainacaṇyānnābhivāteti sarveṇa jñāyate /
ye tu jātiguṇavacanā bhūtvā dravyaṃ pratyāyayanti teṣāmabhidheyantra cya māṇavastunorvivekābhāvātpratītā va pya vivekaḥ sthita eva, sa kathaṃ cidanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ nipuṇaiḥ parīkṣakairapanīyataiti /
lokasya tu makhyabuddhireva /
na ca parīkṣakāṇāmanabhidheyatvaṃ vadatāṃ lokavirodhaḥ /

ta smāda virodhaḥ /
kathaṃ na rūpāḍhiśabdeṣvapi te lakṣapāyā  matublopaḥ, kathaṃ vā jaṭāṇāvṛttiḥ śāstreṇa nvā khyāyata itya nābhidhīyate 
ica keṣu ciḍhartheṣvabhidhānavadeva naṇāśaktirapyanādikālapravṛttatvena nirūḍhā yathāśakkādiṣu /

keṣu citpunaḥ kartumapi na śakyate yathā śavdatyarśarūparasagandheṣu /
kathaṃ punarihā viśiṣṭe saṃ badhe sati na jakṣayeti /

abhidhānaśaktiḥ khābhāviko lakṣaṇā tu na saṃbandhādadhikaṃ nimittamapekṣataiti /
uccate /
yaddacchāśabdatve etadevaṃ syāt /

tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
satyapi ca phanānumeye dṛśyamānārthapratyāyana sāmaye, satyapi cāsmākamapyadṛṣṭaśaktigauravatulyatve, abhidheyamātrapratyayena nivṛttavyāpāre śabderthapratyaye cākṛtārthe sati kalpyamānatvādarthaśaktiḥ pramāṇavatī na śabdaśaktiḥ /
tenādṛṣṭa kalpanātu syatvena pacayostunyabanatvam 
pradhānatvāpradhānatvapratītiratu dravyaguṇayoḥ svābhāviko nityaṃci rūpādiṣu svaprādhānyenābhidhīyamāneṣu dravyaṃ viśeṣatvenocate śukādiṣu viśeṣyavenā, ta eva cānādikāla prasiddārthatvādasyā lakṣaṇāyā matubnopānāne nānugamaḥ 
etāvāṃstu viśeṣotra yatrāpi viśeṣaṇam /
viśeṣyaeva śaktatve śuklo dravyaviśeṣaṇam 
tenaitasya dirūpatvaṃ gandhādarekarūpatā /
tathā ca śuqa ityasya punaranyā dvirūpatā 
paṭasya śukla ityatra niṣkṛṣṭo guṇa āditaḥ  /
paṭaḥ śukta iti tvatra dravyanī nobhidhīyate 
bhāṣyakāreṇa tvetameva paricāra manasi kṛtvoktaṃ bhavati gaṇavacanasyāpi kholiṅgatā/
yathā karuṇābuddhiśabdayoḥ /
gandhādi śabda tucyāvapi caitau pradarśanamātra viśeṣa dudāhṛtau /
etaduktaṃ bhavati yepi tāvatsvapradhā naguvacanāstepi kathaṃ ciliṅga saṃkhyābhyāṃ yujyante kiṃ punaryeṣu dravyaprādhānyam /
evamanayā yuktyārupoti guṇavacanaḥ /
guṇavacanaśveta kroṇātinā na saṃvadhyata ityapasaṃhate paraḥ punarāda 
śakyate hi guṇavacanasya dravyasaṃbandhaḥ kartum /
siddhāntavāḍhī tu śrutyā kriyāsaṃbandhāvagamāt dravyasaṃbandho vākyalakṣaṇo durbalatvādvādhyataityetatpratipādayitumāha 
tadiha kevalaguṇaguṇivacanatvādaruṇaikahāyanomabdayoḥ śrutisāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ tāvanna vidyate /
nāpi ṣaṣṭhīśrutirasti tasmāttṛtīyāśrutibanīyastvāt na dravyaguṇayoḥ saṃbandha iti 
kevalāruṇavācitvaṃ liṅgādyadyapi gamyate /
tathāpyagatito vākyāta taṇāvṛttirāśritā 
tatrāpyagatyaiva pratyavasthānam /
nanu guṇāsṭya kiyāsaṃbandhābhāvāditi /
tasyottaraṃ tṛtīyānartha kyaprasaṅgāditi/
na hyagatyānabhidheyorthaḥ śakyaḥ pratyetum /
na cātra lakṣaṇayāpisaktadvitīyāvat tṛtīyārthavatī kāraka sāmānyasyāpyaniṣṭa svāt /
paramvāha niṅgasaṃkhyāvāśrayadvāraprāptaṃ kārakamanadya prātipadikārtho vidhāyataiti /
asti hotadapi darśanaṃ yadguṇaśabdebhyo vināpi kārakatvena kārakaviśeṣaṇatvād dvitīyādayo bhavantīti/
naitatkāra miti /

katham 
sarvatra tu bādhite padārthaiti koyamupanyāsaḥ /
ucyate 
aruṇā śabdastāvadavaṇyameva kena cid guṇinā saṃbandhanīyaḥ

ato guṇapadenāpi saṃbadhyatāmiti /
naitṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
tadastītyabhyupetya dravyaguṇasaṃbandhaṃ yāgagatadravyasaṃbandhanirākaraṇātkrīṇāteviṃdhyanuvādayogapadyāśrayaṇe virodhaḥ /
yatra tu kriyāviśeṣaṇāni sarvāṇi bhavanti tatra viśiṣṭa vidhānādakleśo bhavati /
yatra ta kriyā vidhīyate dravyasya ca kiṃ cittatra pratyayāvṛttinakṣaṇaṃ vākyabhedamabhyupetya niyamābhāvo bhavatītyucyate /
viśeṣaṇaṃ hi prasiddhaṃ bhavati /
na ca vidhīyamānāvasthaḥ krayaḥ prasiddha iti prakaraṇagataika cāyanīmātrasaṃbandhaprasaṅgaḥ 
sadṛśanyāyeṣa vodāharaṇāntareṣveva tadbhaviṣyati /

paraḥ punarekacāyanī vairū pyābhyupagamavāda labdhaprasaraḥ śaṅkate/
nancapūrvopi vidhīyamāno manasi viparivartamānaḥ pra saṅgādeva viśecyati/
naitadeva mityattaram /
yāvadyāvaddhi padāthī viśeṣyate tāvattāvacchataḥ kharasabhaṅgaḥ, tena satpravṛttāyāḥ kimavaguṇṭhanenetyevamekena kena cit viśeṣitaḥ pareṇāpi viśevyatāmityabhyupagantavyam/
na cānarthakyaṃ prakaraṇerthavattvāt /
tatrāpyevameva saṃbandha iti cet na, vākyāntaraprāptadravyānavādana guṇavidhai/
vairūpyaprasaṅgābhāvāt /
bhavatyakṣepi svarūpataḥ somaṃ ca tantravārtike /

evame kahāyanyapi krayaṃ guṇaṃ ca prati vairupyāncaiva saṃbadhyate

evaṃ prāptebhidhīyate

aikakarmyāditi punastadeva hetutvenopadiṣṭam /
atha vā vākyārthaikatve yatraikavākyatā saṃbhavatītyarthaḥ

na cāpyanyonyasaṃbandhe vidhireṣāṃ pravartate /

yathā ca dravyamicchanti sādhakatvena karmaṇām/
tathā guṇamapītyevaṃ nāruṇya yā nyasaṃgatiḥ 
tathā guṇaviśeṣeṇa dravyaṃ yāvadalakṣitam /

tathā ca dravyaguṇasaṃskāre dhviti guṇagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam/

tathā hi 
tṛtīyādhyāpasya prathamaḥ pāda /
