sarvatra vidhipratiṣedhātmakatvāhedasya yāvatkaṃ cicchūyate ta tsarvaṃ tatsaṃbandhitvena gamyate 
tatraika stāvatpasaḥ 
na tvanyathā viśiṣṭā vihitā syādityevamekatvaviśiṣṭagraha viśiṣṭa saṃmārgaviṣyanyathānupapatteḥ arthāpattyantareṇaikatvavidhānamevaṃ viśeṣaṇamālāyāmapi satyāṃ saṃyukta saṃyogapāraṃparyeṇa sarvavidhipratyayaḥ 
atha vā yadi nāma dravyaviśeṣaṇaṃ yāvadvidhipratyayo na gacchettata ekayaivārthāpattyā sarvaṃ vidhātumiṣyate 
bhinnaviṣayatvādyā virodhābhāvaḥ /
yadi chubhayatrāpi tādarthyalakṣaṇa evāśrayāya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyarūpo vā saṃbandhaḥ syāt tataḥ samānaviṣayatvaṃ pratīyeta /
na tvekamapyasti gra haikatvayorāśrayāśrayarūpeṇa viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvābhāvanayā ca saha śeṣaśeṣitvābhyupagamāt /
tena grāśritenaikatvena saṃ mārgabhāvanāṃ kuryādityenamavagamayiṣyāmaḥ 
atha vā yadai katvaṃ svārthatvena graho nopajīvituṃ samartha ityavadhāritaṃ bhavati tadāsau tadbhāvanāṃ vākyenāpi gacchanna nivārayati 
atha vā grahārthamevaitadastu /
tacca grahārthatvaṃ yena prakāreṇopapadyate sa darśayitavyaḥ /
tatra yadi grahaḥ svarūpamātreṇa bhāvanāyāmanupraviśetata ekatvaṃ paścāgaviṣyadagṛhītaṃ bhāvanayā bhāvanāgataṃ na syāt /
grahasvarūpasyaitra syādatosāvekatvapuraḥsarameva tatsamānadeśaṃ vā pṛthakpadopāttāruṇādivadevātmānaṃ pratipadyate 
viśiṣṭo hi vidhiḥ kvatsno nāpraklṛptaviśeṣaṇaḥ /
viśiṣṭo vibhinaṣṭīti tatpūrva praviśatyasau 
evaṃ ca sati bhāvanāpraviṣṭaṃ tadvidhināpi saṃspṛśyamānaṃ dravyaguṇayorniyame sati grahasya jātaṃ bhavati /
atha vā śrutibalīyavādasya dravyasaṃbandha uccate 
prātipadikopāttaṃ hi dravyaṃ samānapadopāttatvena pratyāsannaṃ syāt 
kārakaṃ ca vibhaktipratipāditamā virbhūtapūrvāparībhūtabhāvanaikadeśa ityaktam 
tasmādupādīyamānapaśvādivadevoddiśyamānasyāpi saṃkhyā vivacitā puṃpaśuśceti prasaṅgādudāhṛtam 
sarveṣāṃ vā lakṣaṇatvādaviśiṣṭaṃ hi lakṣaṇam 
vyaktīruddiśya yatkarma svajātyādyupanaścitāḥ /
vihitaṃ guṇabhāvena tatsarvārthaṃ pratīyate 
tatrāpi grahatvasya saṃmārgānaītvāktayaḥ saṃskāryatvenāvatiṣṭhante 
yad grahakāyeṃ tatsaṃmārgeṇa saguṇāṃ bhavati 
nahi tadānīṃ grahāntareṣvagṛhyamāṇeṣu kasya tṛtīyādhyāpasya prathamaḥ pāda /
cidvaiguṇyaṃ dṛśyate 
athāpi śāstratantratvātmārgaḥ pratigraham /
tathāpyakaraṇe tasya jñānaṃ bādhyeta tadgatam 
tasmād grahatvāpūrvasaṃyogāviśeṣātprakaraṇāviśeṣāśca sarvapratyayaḥ 
tatrottaram 
vihito viniyuktaśca gṛhyate caśrutoṣi san/
śrutopi tu na gṛhyeta yorthastābhyāmupekṣitaḥ 
vacanavyaktibhedana sarveṣāmeva darśanāt /
vihito viniyuktaca kaḥ, ko neti vicāryate 
vartamānasarūpeṇa ciṅarthasmṛtisādhunā /
pañcamena lakāreṇa kiṃ nāmātra vidhīyate 
sākiṃ dhātvarthamātreṇa saṃmārgeṇa viśeṣyate /
lokaprasiddharūpeṇa śakyānuṣṭheyatātmanā 
tulyārthatvātma bhedena nānyaiḥ saha vicāryate /
grādīnāṃ ca kiṃ ceha niyogena nirūpaṇā  saṃmārgagrayoḥ kiṃvā vikalpotha samuccayaḥ /
saṃbandhaḥ samudāyo vā vibhinaṣṭīca bhāvanām 
tathā kṛtvā dvayoḥ pūrvaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatām /
tṛtīyena sakena tādṛśyeva vicāraṇā  tathā 
tatra kriyāpradhānatve sāhityaṃ dravyasaṃkhyayoḥ /
sakṛcca tādṛśīṃ kṛtvā kṛt kartā kṛtī bhavet 
tatrāpi tu grahasyaiva saṃmārgaḥ kiṃ vidhīyate tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
ekatvasyaiva kiṃ, kiṃ vā vikalpena iyorapi 
graheṇa vā viśiṣṭāṃ kiṃ saṃkhyāṃ prati vidhīyate /
kiyāṃ vā pratyupādānaṃ kiṃ grahasyaiva gamyate 
kimekatva viśiṣṭasya grahasyaiva vidhīyate /
kiṃvā grahaviśiṣṭekasaṃkhyā saṃmārgagāminī 
yena yena prakāreṇa saṃkhyopādīyate grahe /
saṃmārge vā vidhīyeta sa tamāpādayiṣyati 
yāṃ yāṃsa vacanavyakti vidheye ravayiṣyati /
vākyabhedana māṃ tāṃ tu siddhāntī dūṣayaṣyati 
grahaṃ cohigya saṃmārgavidhānāśrayaṇe sati /
tanmācaoṇaśaktitvāṭekatvaṃ na vidhāsyate /
na tāvattadgrahe śakyaṃ vidhāmapunaḥśruteḥ /
hai/
vartanīyau hi syātāṃ grahavidhāyaka 
grahopyāvartanīyaḥ syātsaṃbandhadvaya siddhaye /
vidhāyakaca, naikena vidhinā to hi sidhyataḥ 
saṃkhyāsaṃmārgasaṃbandhau grahoṣi prāpnuvannubho /
diranuccāryamāṇastau prāpnuyāca makvacchataḥ 
punaruccāryamāṇaśca samāmnāyā iciḥ sthitaḥ /
pratyayaḥ pauruṣeyatvādapramāṇaṃ prasajyate 
kena cittu prakāreṇa vidhirasya bhavedyadi /
grahādivahanuṣṭhāne ka ekatvaṃ parityajet 
yadi kriyāpradhānatvaṃ lapsyate pūrvapakṣiṇā /
tataḥ sarvavivacāpi taddāraṇāsya sevyati /
tasmānna śrutamātratvaṃ vidhigrahaṇakāraṇam /
ataḥ śaklādibhistulyaṃ naitadanyai viśeṣaṇaiḥ 
tatra dravyaviśeṣaṇaṃ tāvannirākriyate 
tatra svarūpaprakṣepa viśeṣaṇapha tāvatsarveṣvapi saṃsṛjyamāneṣu saṃbhavatyeva 
ataśca grahatvasaṃvandhena prāpta ekavacanena cāpratiṣiddhaḥ kimiva dvitīyādeḥ saṃmārgo na kriyate 
prātipadikādevaikasminnane kasmiṃśca grahe saṃmārjanīye prāpte punare kavacana śrutirguṇārthavādatvenāsaṃbhavanto parisaṃkhyārthā bhaviṣyatīti/
naitadevam /
kutaḥ 
tacca nānāvākyatve satyeva bhavati, isa tvekenaiva vākyena prāptiḥ parisaṃkhyā ca kriyataityuktaṃ, taccātyantamevānupapannam 
prātipadikena hi sarvagrahasaṃbandhaḥ prāpyate 
anya hi vacana vyaktirvākye prāpakadāyaka /
yathā tathā padavyaktibhedopyatra prasajyate 
kiṃ ca 
nirdoṣatvaṃ hi tatrāsyā vidhāne sati labhyate /tantravārtika /
kalyatvena hi tasyaiṣā  klṛptādāśrīyate phacāt 
ityādattaimi hāsmādākhyātāhidhisaṃbhavaḥ /
saṃbandheśvābhidhānyāṃtu nāsti kaścidvidhāyakaḥ 
na vārthaviprakarṣosya raśanāṃ prati kaścana /
saṃyogato viśeṣeṇa yugapatpratyayāiyoḥ 
padatrayādinā nāmasaṃbandho nāvakarūpate /
ityādattaiti tveṣa dvābhyāmeva samāpyate 
mantropi raśanāṃ śīghraṃ yathā yāti sphuṭam /
na tathā grahaṇaṃ kaṣṭaṃ chāndasīyapadoditam 
pūrva sādhanatvāṃśāṇāvaśyameva hi /
sarvavidhiḥ syānniṣprayojanaḥ 
tasmānnādatta ityetadrū pātprāśamanūdyate /
na vetyaśvābhidhānīmityetadatra vidhīyate 
rūpaprakaraṇadvārā śrutirthāvattu kalpyate /
tāvatpratyayā tyā vidhiḥ śīghra samāpyate 
prayojanaṃ vidheḥ kiṃ syādasyeti tu nirūpaṇe /
na gardabha bhidhānītaḥ phalamanyannivartanāt 
na ca gardabhabandhanyāṃ prāptonanumitaśrutiḥ /
mantro yena nivartyeta vājirajjupunaḥśruteḥ 
aśvaśrutyaiva śīghratvānmantre prāvihite sati /
tantravārtike /
nirākājīkṛtāmnāye tathā prakaraṇinyapi 
soyamābhāṇako loke yadaśvena hṛtaṃ purā /
tatpaścādgardabhaḥ prāptuṃ kenopāyena śaknuyāt 
yadānumitayā pyeṣa śrutyāvaraśanāṃ prati /
prāpnuyādeva mantraḥ kiṃ tvarayā vicitastvayā 
yadyaśvaraśanāprāptiṃ kevacāmānumānikī /
pratyakṣa śrutivatkuryāttataḥ sā syādanārthakā 
kevalāśvābhidhānyāṃ hi vidhiḥ pratyayā yathā /
na syāttathānumānikyā śrutyetyāmnāyate isa/
ataścāpunaruktatvātpratyakṣārthavatī śrutiḥ /
tasyāṃ satyāṃ nirākāṅgrānmatrānnānyānumīyate 
yadā tu pratibaddhatvātmāmānya viniyogakṛt /
naiva cecchu tirastīca na prāpnoti tridoṣatā 
tataśca bhāṣyakāreṇa yadihoktama cintitam /
vākyabhaṅgyataraṃ tatra kartavyotīva nādaraḥ /
na caikatva saṃvandhamātra vidhiḥ śakyaḥ saṃmārgagrahasaṃbandhamājavi bhānopakṣīṇaśaktitvādvidhāyakasya /
yathaudanopaghāta nivāraṇavidhipare vākye śrutānāmapi śvamārjārādīnāmaviṣoyamānatvādaviśeṣaṇatvam 
na hyannabhanaṣādra cyāḥ śramārjārādayo naḥ /
tulyānnādyopaghātāttu kākāderepi vāraṇā /
tathācāha /
kākebhyo racyatāmannamiti bālopi coditaḥ /
upaghātapradhānatvānna vādibhyo na rakṣati 
padārtha eva kākādiḥ sarvo hyatrāvivaścitaḥ /
saṃkhyāmācāvivakṣā tu grahastheti vilakṣaṇam 
sthitasiddhāntodāharaṇamapi paśuprakaraṇe śrūyate 
ma davattaṃ tatpañcasaṃkhyaṃ kāryamityetadvidhipare vākye vapāgrahaṇamānavaścitaṃ vākyabhedaprasaṅgāditi daśame vakṣyati /
tatra śramārjārādisaṃbandhāvivaścodāharaṇaṃ ghaṭate 
saṃkhyāmātravibakṣāyāṃ loke yacchūyate vacaḥ/tantravārtika /
tadudāharaṇaṃ deyaṃ vṛṣalasyavaḍatvavat 
baḍatvasyā vivakṣitatvāt 
na hoko vi dhāyakaḥ śaknoti saṃmārgabhāvanāṃ ca vidhātuṃ grahekatvasaṃbandha ca 
yadi tāvad grahaḥ saṃkhyāṃ kriyāyai na prayacchati /
śudvenaiva viśiṣṭatvānna viśiṣṭaviśiṣṭatā 
na hyanyathā viśiṣṭena viśeṣitā syādityevaṃ bhāvanāpye katvaviśiṣṭaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇatī naikatvamagṛhītvā tadiśiṣṭaṃ grahaṃ śaknoti grahītam 
taccopariṭānnirākariṣyāmaḥ 
tantra viśiṣṭa vidhinā bhāvanāviśeṣaṇamātrāce paryavasāyinā nārthāntarākṣepaḥ śakyaḥ kartuṃ na hi bhāvanāṃ viśiṣatastasya tadekatvaṃ viśeṣaṇam 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
nāpi bhāvanā viśiṣṭasya mā bhūtpunarapi bhāvanāviśeṣaṇatvameva 
tasmānmaulikena vidhinānākāṅakṣitatvānna dravyaviśeṣaṇāl̤epaḥ saṃbhavati 
abhyupetyāpi tu saṃbhārgavelāyāṃ naikatvamādartavyaṃ svatantramya grahasyaivaikatvasaṃbandhavidhānāt ! na hi vidhīyamānāvasthaḥ krayo guṇena saṃbadhyamānaṃ dravyaṃ vibhinaṣṭīvyaktamaruṇādhikaraṇe 
athaitadekatvaṃ saṃmārgabhāvanāyācodyate tathāpi na guṇatvena nāpi pradhānatvena saṃbhavati 
na ca dravyasaṃskārā tasaṃskāro 'nyatvād, grahasya vāyamekatvadvāreṇa vidhīyate 
anuṣṭhāna kā lepa caya hasyātmīya eva saṃmārgaḥ pratyabhijñāyataiti naikatvanimittabuddhiḥ syāt 
kathamaruṇatvasya guṇatvamiti cedata āha 
hi guṇopyanaṅgameva syāt /
nanu pradhānabhūtamanoti 
na hi śeṣamāśritaḥ śeṣaḥ, kiṃ tarhi upakāriṇamānita upakarotīti sarvatra sthā payiṣyāmaḥ 
katham 
yattābaduktamamūrtatvātsaṃskartuṃ na śakyataiti 
athāpi vyaktidvāreṇāsyāḥ saṃskāraḥ sa saṃkhyāyāmapi tulyaḥ 
atha jātermūrtatvaṃ dravyāvyatirekaṃ cāśritya sāścādeva saṃskāra ityucyate tadapye katvasyā viśiṣṭam 
atha grahaśabdasya vyaktivācitvātparihāra uccate tata ākṛtyadhikaraṇanyāyo bādhyeta /
na hānekadeśakānnavartijyotiṣṭomaprayogasthagraha vyakti saṃbandhānubhavorita 
na ca tad grahanvādanyatsaṃbhavatīti tadeva viśeṣatvātpūrvamabhidheyamāpadyate 
na ca tatsāmānyaṃ dravyāntarebhyo nivṛttaṃ teṣu teṣu cānuvṛttaṃ grahatvādanyadasti /
tasmāttadeva vācyam /
yattu grahasya kriyamāṇaḥ saṃmārgastadīyatvāvadhāraṇenainṛtīyādhyāpasya prathamaḥ pāda /
katvaviṣayo vijñāyataiti mandaphalā ca punaḥ śrutiriti 
ekatvenāpi saṃvadhya tāvatyeva kriyā yadi /
tato niṣphalatodhyeta bhedastvastye ka saṃskṛteḥ 
tasmād dravyaguṇayorniyama siddhera tya ruṇā śabda sṭye vai katva saṃvandhasya pṛthaka prayojanamiti saṃskāryaṃ tvopapattiḥ 
mandayuktika evāyamabhyupagamaḥ yadguṇamevā śra tena guṇenopakartavyamiti 
sākṣādayogya saṃbandhāḥ kriyāsaṃbandhini sthitāḥ /
asaṃbadvairasaṃvadvāḥ sādhayanti guṇāḥ kriyām 
na tu tadgataguṇapradhānatvayoḥ kaścidviśeṣa iti tayorupekṣā 
etāvacca saṃbandhe kāraṇam 
yā guṇasyopakurvāṇamātmasātkurute guṇam /
grahīṣyatitarāmeṣā taṃ tu saṃskāryavartinam 
yathā pradhānagataḥ ko nu khannu mama pradhānasyopakurvantyāḥ kiṃ ciḍhanugrahaṃ kuryāditi /
mahāścāyamanugraho yatpradhāneyattāvadhāraṇaṃ nāma 
sa evātra nyāya ityaviruddhaṃ pradhānāśrayaṇāṃ guṇatvam 
tatrāpi hi dravyadevatāyāgaviśiṣṭabhāvanāvidhipara vākye yadi liṅgasaṃkhyāsaṃbandhoparaḥ kriyāyāṃ dravye vā vidhīyate tato vākyaṃ bhidyeteti śakyaṃ vaditum 
ta dikṣaitāvāneva viśeṣovaśiṣyate yad graha uddiśyamānaḥ pa śarupāḍhīyamānaḥ, na caitāvatā kiṃ citsidhyati /
anyathā pa śugrahasaṃbandhamātrabhedenāpi vivakṣitāvivaścitatvasiddhiḥ syāt /
api cāsminneva vākye grahamuddiśya saṃmārge vidhīyamāne pi daśāpavitrata dekatvādīnāṃ vivābhyupagamyate na ca vākyadaḥ, tathā grahaikatvepi bhaviṣyati /
yasta padāntaropādānāt viśeṣaṃ brūyāt tasya sarvatra yaḥ kaścidviśeṣostotina kka cid dṛṣṭāntenopamā tulyanyāyānāṃ viṣayābhāvāt 
padāntaragato yasya guṇobhīṣṭo vivaścitaḥ /
tasya tulyapadopāttaḥ kathaṃ syādavivakṣitaḥ 
anyathā hi vināpi graheṇa saṃmārge kṛte tatkṛtaḥ śāstrārtho bhavet/
atha prāptatvād grahasyāvi dhānamacyeta tadayuktam 
a thāsau yāge'prāpto vidhīyate tad grahasyāpyaviśiṣṭam 
śakyaṃ hi yo graha itivadyaḥ parityapi vaktum 
tathā hi 
tasmādviśiṣṭa saṃbhārgaviṣyāopād grahatvavade katvasyāpi vidhisaṃsparśe satyarthād guṇapradhānabhāva ityekatvaṃ niṣprayojanatvād guṇabhūtaṃ grahaśca prayojanakattvātpradhānabhūtaḥ 
saha vidhyavidhī yuktau na caikapadagocarau /
padabhedona ca nyāyyaḥ prakṛtipratyayau prati 
na ca vibhaktiḥ padāntaraṃ, svātantrye pāniyatapūrvāparatvena cāprayujyamānatvāt /
gamakatvātpada miti cenna /
dhūmādiṣvaniprasaṅgāde kasminnapi cākhyātā ḍhipratyayenai korthaḥ pratīyataiti pratyarthaṃ padatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
padamiti ca laukikaḥ śabdaḥ sa yatra lokena prayujyate yatra ca smaṭebhiḥ smaryate na tato 'panetuṃ śakyate /
suptiṅantaṃ padamiti ca smṛtiḥ /
tatraiva ca padaśabdaḥ prayujyate 
vārtika /
vibhaktyu pāttakamaṃtvavivakṣā cediheṣyate /
saṃkhyāpi tadupāttatvānna śakyā na vivacitum 
tadica yadi tāvatsaṃkhyāparityāgādvibhaktiḥ parityaktā tataḥ karmatvaparityāgopi prāpnoti 
prayojanavattvāt saṃskāryatvamiti cet na, kārakavibhaktimantareṇa kriyāsaṃbandhābhāvāt /
na hyavibhaktikasya gra ha ityetāvataḥ saṃmātyanena saṃbandhovakalpate 
saṃmārgo yadi sarveṣāmekatvasyā vivakṣayā /
na kasya cihnavedeṣa grahakarmāvivacayā 
śrutaśabdābhidheyānāṃ nārthānāṃ yugapattathā /
grahaṇāgrahaṇaṃ yuktamakukkuṭipākavat atra pratividhīyate 
yadā hi grahaikatvoddeśena saṃmārgo vidhīyate tadohiśyamānayoḥ parasparasaṃbandhābhāvātpratyekaṃ vākyaparisamāptilakṣaṇatṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
stāvadeko vākyabhedaḥ /
upādeyanānātve punaḥ sarvaviśiṣṭabhāvanāprayojana tvāde kakāryatve tyāñjasyenaivaikavākyatvaṃ syāt 
uddiśyamānānāṃ punaravaśīkṛtatvātpratye kaṃ kriyāgrahaṇasāmarthyātkriyaiva vaśīkṛtā tairākṛṣyata ityekai kasvānyonyanirapekṣasya kartavyatāvagamyate/
tadiha graha ekatvanirapekṣaḥ saṃskartavyaḥ, ekatvamapi grahanirapekṣaṃ saṃskartavyam/
tatra yadi tāvad grahagatamevaikatvaṃ saṃskriyate tataḥ sāpekṣakaraṇādubhayornirapekṣasaṃbandhāvadhṛtaṃ prādhānyaṃ vihanyeta /
atha dravyāntaragataṃ, tat na jāyeta kimiti /
na grahavatkiṃ cidekaṃ nāma prakaraṇe paśyāmaḥ 
na teṣāmapi bahatvātkimiti nirūpaṇāśaktaḥ /
atha sarveṣāṃ kamānna bhavati na, tatrāpi coditānyacoditakaraṇāpatteḥ 
guṇabhūtena ho kenaikatvayuktena kriyā mādhyamānā nānyamapekṣataiti yatkiṃ cidapyupādāya śāstrārthaḥ kṛtaḥ syātprādhānye punayaṃdevaikatvayuktaṃ na gṛhyeta tasyaiva vaiguṇyaṃ prasajyeta 
tathā hi 
sarveṣvapi saṃskriyamāṇeṣvanuṣṭhānabelāyā me kaika eva dṛśyate tasmādavirodha ityucyate 
nahi kaścidapi yugapadaneka grahaṃ saṃmārṭi, tataśca vivakṣitepi sādṛśameveti mandaṃ vivakṣāphalam 
naitadasti pratyekaṃ gṛhyamāṇānāṃ tahadeva saṃskā re sati yogapadyaprasaṅgābhāvā, dabhyupetyavādamātraṃ caitatsvatantrai katvāpratīteḥ 
yadyapi ca dravyāntaragatatvena tadvivakṣitameva tathāpi grahasya tāvadavivaścitamiti siddhaḥ sarveṣāṃ saṃmārgaḥ 
śraya tu guṇabhūtamekatvaṃ vidhoyeta tatra dvitīyā tāvad gu pābhāvaṃ naiva bravītīti vyākhyātaṃ sakkadhikaraṇe /
sā yadyavivajitehitārthā kārakamātralacaṇārtheti vivacchate tataḥ sa eva tāvadeko doṣa ityekatvavacca grahasyāpi guṇātvaprasaṅgaḥ 
tacaitalyāt aika rūpyārthamekatvavad gra isyāpi tāvad guṇatvamevāvagamayet, tataḥ prayojana vattāvaśena grahasya prādhānyam
kathamādāvasanneva guṇabhāvo vivacyate /
kathaṃ ca saṃbhavacchabdādarthātprādhānya miṣyate 
athāsya kathaṃ cidasaṃbhavaṃ kalpayitvā jakṣaṇāśrīyate tataḥ punaḥ saṃbhavakalpanā virodhātmatyapi prayojanavave śākhavaśena guṇatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
yugapasaṃbhavāsaṃbhavaparigra dātprādhānya guṇatvayoḥ prādhānyānocanena vilepāca śabdakteśaḥ 
na hyartho nāma kiṃ citpramāṇaṃ, kiṃ tarhi śabdaśakti kalpanā hetuḥ /
ataścāneka kalpanānimitto hyastyeva vākya bhedaḥ 
vidhīyamānamapyarthamanyato vāvadhāritam /
avaśyaṃ bhāvinaṃ prāpya na śabdonyatra vartate 
śrutyā cāvaśyaṃ bhāvini grahaprādhānyavidhāne labhyamāne ko jātu cidarthātleśena kalpayiṣyati 
tasmācchabdasāmarthyā dubhayatra prādhānyaṃ grahītavyam
bhāṣyamapyeteṣveva vākyabhedeṣu yojitavyam
yadya pyeṣā ṣaṣṭhī viśe ṣaṇatvād guṇabhūtamivāgniṃ pratipādayati tathāpi saṃbandhāntarābhāvādaṅgāṅgisaṃbandha eva jñāyate /
tatrāpyagneḥ prayojanakattvātṛṇāpacayasya tadabhāvāt rājñaḥ puruṣa ityatra yathā rājā puruṣasya svāmyevamagnistṛṣṇāpacayasya svāmītyetadeva gamyate 
tṛṇānītyetadapi bahuvacanamavivakṣitamiti vyākhye yam tathā bhinne juhotītyādiṣu /

athaikatvamupādeyatvena pratipādyeta bhinnamanupādeyatvena tato yadyapi guṇatvapradhānatvavirodho nāsti tathāpi pūrvavadeva virodhaḥ /
ekavākyatve nātṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
nārūpatvaṃ nāmetyavivakṣā
nanu bahuṣu vivaściśeṣa bahuvacanamitya vivacitopya vidyamānortho na śakyo vaktumiti manyate /
tatra vedasya nityatvādyathocaritārthānveṣaṇamātre puruṣāṇāṃ vyāpāra iti na karteva paryanuyujyate /
tena prātipadikārthānugrahārthā vibhaktiriti draṣṭavyam 
api ca grahaḥ prātipadikārtha iti yadānviṣyamāṇamapi kriyā saṃbandhitvaṃ na ghaṭate tadā tulyāyāmavivaśāyāṃ varaṃ dravyaviśeṣaṇameve damityabhiprāyaḥ /
tataśca saṃmārgastena vināpya vigupo jātisaṃkhyā caiṣā pratyekaṃ saṃmṛjyamānavyaktigatā vā samathaṃnīyā 
saṃskārādvā guṇānāmavyavasthā sthā t 
ekatvavadeva grahatvasyāpi pradarśanārthatvācca sameṣvapi saṃmārga ityupanyasya pradarśanārthatve pramāṇābhāvādvākyena ca saṃbandhopādānāt gracādavacchidya śrutvā kevala saṃmārgavidhāna tpūrvapakṣaḥ parigṛhītaḥ iha tvavaghātādivadeva bhaṅgodvārā kartavyo 
satyaṃ nāramyeta yadi grahādhikaraṇenā  vivadyā kānuṣyabuddhirnayādevaṃ  tvekatva vivaśvāsaṃtrāsitaḥ sarvamevāvivakṣitaṃ manyate /

ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣu 
yadi matadaśāranirvājapeyasyeti vidhīyate yūpaśabdo yathā kathaṃ cittaḍhanuvādaḥ tataḥ ṣoḍaśipāce niveśaḥ /
athāpi yo vājapeyasya saṃbandhī ma saptadaśāraniriti vidhīyate tathāṣyevam /
atha yo yūpaḥ sa saptadaśāraniriti vacanavyattiḥ vājapeyaśabdo yathā kathaṃ cidviśeṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇa prāptānuvādo vā tatastadaṅgapaśuyūpasyedaṃ paribhāṣāmiti /
kiṃ prāptam

asti tveṣāpi jitṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
jñāsā yadi bājapeyasya sākṣādyūpaḥ syāditi /
yadā tu sa nopalavdhatā paścāttaramavannambitama/
kiṃ ca 
sākṣāttāvana saptadabhāratnitvaṃ yujyataityuktam /
saṃbandhimātramapyanirdiṣṭaṃ vājapeyasyetyetāvanmātreṇa na jñāyeta yūpaśabdārthastvatatsaṃbandhitvāt dūrabhraṣṭaḥ /

tasmāna kena citpramāṇena virodha iti 
kutaḥ 
na tāvadabhikramaṇena domaṃ karotīti vaktaṃ śakyama to na prayājaiḥ saṃvadhyate /
tataścāruṣṇādhikaraṇapūrvapaścavadvākyabhedaḥ syāt /
nanvanenaiva hetu nānyatrāpyana bhiniveśa ityaruṇācodyameva/
parihāraśvākhyāte karnarguṇabhūtatvācā homasaṃbandhāḥ /
na juhotinā gṛhītena prayājādīnāṃ karcā saṃbandhaḥ /
anyatra tu prakaraṇagṛcītasya pradhānabhūtasya kartuḥ saṃbandhī na virokyate /
sākāṅkṣaṃ tvekavākyaṃ syādasamāsaṃ hi pūrveṇa 
sarvathā tāvadabhikrāmamityetatpadaṃ na kriyāntaramantareṇa nirākāṅkṣī bhavati/
na hyetad dravyasaṃbandhaṃ kathaṃ ciḍhapi bravīti /
tasmātprakṛtaprayājayahijokavākyatvātādarthaṃ vijñā yate /

apekṣitā cāhavanīyapratyāsattiradhvaryoḥ prayājairarupaṇatvavadeva vārthād dravyasaṃbandha iti karturupasarjanatvepi na kaścid doṣaḥ /
evaṃ co tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
pakārarūpeṇa karmāṇi karmamādhyaṃ bhavatītyetadapi siddham 
yadapyasamātaṃ hi pūrveti tanna vākyāmamāpyabhiprāyeṇa kiṃ kaīsamāptaṃ hyabāntaraprakaraṇaṃ pūrveṇa prayājasvarūpaguṇavidhinevarthaḥ 
saṃdigdhe ta vyavāyādvākyameda syāt 
middhe karmaṇāṃ karmasamavāye 'dhunāvāntaraprakaraṇamahāprakarāyoḥ katarahiniyojaka mityupavītamudāhṛtaṃ tatra sāmighenyanuvā ka vibhāgapradarśanaṃ sāmidhenīprakaraṇa sadasadbhāvavivekāryam /
nanu darśapūrṇamāsayoreva prakaraṇamiti mahāprakaragāgrastatvānnaivāvāntara prakaraṇānyāvirbhavanti 
naitadevam 
nānyaprakaraṇāpattiḥ saṃskāro vā vidanti tam 
dṛṣṭepi ca phannenaiva sāpekṣā na pravartate /
dṛṣṭenaiva tu kenāpi sopāyena nivartyate 
evaṃ tarhi tasya sannikarṣeṇa balīyasvāttadaṅgatvenaiva bhavitavyamiti kuto mahāprakaraviniyogāśahā/
uccate /
satyametadevaṃ syādyadi tasya nivitpadavyavadhānena tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
prakaraṇavicchedāśaṅkā na syāta/
evaṃ tarhi vicchinne tasmina jitaṃ mahāprakaraṇeneti 
abhitaḥ sāmidhenīnāṃ kīrtanāt prakriyā sthitā /
para prakaraṇe pāṭho nividāmatha vāṅgatā 
vicchinnā sāmighenīnāṃ nividbhiḥ prakriyā yataḥ /
na hi kāmyaiḥ punaḥ kalpaiḥ saṃdhātuṃ sā hi śakyate 
yadi punarnividoṅgaṃ bhaveyustato godohananyāyenāśrayadapi tāvatkāmyeṣu prakaraṇānuvṛttiḥ syādathāpi kā myānāmaṅgatvaṃ bhavettathāpi pūṣā dyana mantraṇavatprakaraṇāvādhaṃ niviḍhāṃ kathaṃ ciḍhanusaṃdhānenādhyavasthema 
nanu ca yadi vicchinne prakaraṇe kāmyāḥ kalpāḥ śrayante tata ekaviṃśatyā pratiṣṭhāṃ bhāvaroṭikamāniyeta prakaraṇe nāśraye'nupanīyamāne sākāṅkṣatvādaparipūrṇatā prāpnoti /
atha vākyenāśraya upanīyeta tataḥ prāpte karmaṇi saṃvandhayakaraṇādvākyaṃ bhidyeta /
tatra yadi vākyamedo 'bhyupagarakheta kathaṃ cidvā pariṭriyeta tato retīvāravantīyasaubharādiśvapyevameva vākyena prakṛtāśrayadānāsiddhānta hāniḥ /
thāśrayāmārthaṃ kathaṃ cidanuvarteta prakaraṇaṃ tata upavītamapi tathaiva prāpnoti sarvathā saṃkaṭametat 
guṇātkāmā na yuktotra vicchinnaprakriyāśrayāt /
anekārthavidhiḥ śakyo nāpūrvātkarmaṇo binā /
naivātrai kaviṃśatyā darguṇātphalaṃ kiṃ taī tāvantīkaviṃśatyādarguṇātphalaṃ yāḍhivāya vaḍhevānenāpi viśiṣṭaṃ karma vidhīyate /
tataśca bhāvārthādhikaraṇa nyāyena dhātvarthātphanam /

ya dīpi cātra karmāntaratvākarmāntaratvayoḥ phalaṃ nāsti tathāpi vākyamevamavakalpataitītyaṃ varṇitam/

naitadevam /
kutaḥ

tathā prāpte 'bhidhīyate

sarvaṃ cāyuktametat /

kimanenāśrutāpanāśanānyathāpyetadupapadyataeva 
vadanti sāmidhenīvannividognisamindhanam /

yathaiva hi grahatvena camasā nopalacitāḥ /
āgneyatvaṃ tathā na syād dvidevatyopalakṣaṇam

nāgnīṣomīya āgneya aindrāgno vā taducyate

yattu prāśitravaḍhiti tatrocyate /
deśaviśeṣajrakṣaṇārthāsminnāgneya guṇa śrutiḥ sāmānyavākyena sarvatra prāśināvadāne prāpte mastakavitṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pāda /
roga  viśeṣa vidhānārthame tadvacana miti vaiṣamyam

avaśyameva sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaṃ prati gacchati/

idānīṃ liṅgaviniyogaḥ stūyate /

śākhādibhyo ya ityevamivārthe mukhya ityayam /

athoṣapaḍhasya dyotakatvaṃ parityajya tulyakalpatocyate yasmānnityaṃ māṇatra kāgniśabdasamudāyādasyārthasya pratītiḥ ato 'śvakarṇādivatsamudāyavācyatve satyavayavasya gauṇatvamiti /
tatṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
ducyate 
tatra samudāyaprasiddhirbhavati yatrāvayavārthī tirodhāya vyaktabhedaḥ samudāya eva pratīyate /
gamyate tvacāgniśabdasya paiṅgalyaṃ māṇavaka śabdasya ca piṇḍasvarūpaṃ viviktaṃ vācyamata ubhāvapi prātyātmikayorapi vācakatvānmukhyāviti /
idānīmavayavānusāreṇaiva samudāyārthatvaṃ samarthayamāna āha /
anugata svārtha paḍhadayagamyatvānnīlotpannavadvākyārtho 'taca tasya padārthapratyāyyatvācchabdaṃ prati pūrvavadeva gauṇatvamiti tannirākaroti 
na tvatra tadīyo mukhyārtho'gnitvamasti /
na ca bhavataḥ paiṅgalyaṃ vācyamasmatyakṣābhedaprasaṅgāttasmānna vākyārthaḥ /
tena ccalane māṇavakasya ca paiṅgalye tunyavacchanda pravṛttiriti mukhyatvama/
māṇavakasyeti bhāṣye paiṅgalyavyatireka janitā ṣaṣṭhī nābhidhātṛvyatire kajanitā /
na hi māṇavaka svarūpamagniśabdāgamyate/
na hi paryāyatve māṇavakaśabdaḥ prayujyeta /
athocyeta yaḥ prasiddha iti mukkopapadavyāpāraṃ yatkṛtaṃ tasyāśrayaṇamanāśrayaṇaṃ ca te eva mandasuṣṭuprasiddhī gauṇamukhya vibhāgāya darśayasuṣṭhu ti/
tatrottaram 
idānīṃ śroṭagataprasiddhibhedamūnaṃ vaktṛgataṃ bahvalpaprayogitvaṃ  vibhāgārthaṃ darśayati /
yasya ca bahuśaḥ prayoga ityādi /
tannirākriyate 
iccāpi ca gośabdasya pṛthivyādau mandasuṣṭuprasiddhiprayogo darśayitavyai 
maṇḍakairva iśastṛptiḥ kadā cikhaṇḍamodakaḥ /
na cātra maṇḍakā mukhyā gauṇā vā khaṇḍamodakāḥ /
idānoṃ viśeṣaṃ kathayati /
satyapi tāvanmāṇavakasāmānādhikaraṇye 'ruṇāśabdanyāyena sati sādṛśye 'bhidhānādasati cānabhidhānādanyatrāsādṛśyavati vṛttidarśanādasati cādarśanādiśeṣaṇatvāda vaśyaṃbhāviprathamapratyāyane sādṛśyameva prathamaṃ pratyāyayitavyam /
na cānavagate'gna tatpratīyataiti prathamataramagnerabhidhānam /
tataśca tatsaṃbandhādeva śeṣapratīte  rvyaktivadanabhidheyatvam/
manti caivamādiṣu kāni cidrapādisāmānyānītyuktam /
tasmādasti gauṇa mukhya vibhāga ityārabhyamadhikaraṇam /
evaṃ ca  tatmidvisūtroktaḥ saha nava gauṇapacā draṣṭavyāḥ 
evaṃ ca sati gauṣṭyā vṛttyā pūṣādiśabdaragnyādyabhidhānādanutkarṣo bhaviṣyatya, nyathā yatra pūṣādayastatra noyeraṃ, stathāgnyādiśabdaiḥ sūryādyabhidhānādavikāre satyārṣacodako 'nugrahīṣyate /
ityevaṃ prāpta brūmaḥ /
arthābhidhāna saṃyogānmantrāṇāṃ kratuśeṣatā /
mukhyena ca kṛtārthānāṃ na gauṇe śrutikalpanā 
api ca 
pākṣikatve 'pyanityatvātpakṣenarthakatā bhavet /
nityaṃ mukhyāparityāgānmatpaśto bhavet 
tenaiṣa sūtrārtho yasmādarthābhidhāna saṃyogānmantreṣu śeṣabhāvasta smaḥ da /tpatti ke naivārthenaiṣāṃ saṃyogaḥ syāt /
kuta, stenaivāvyabhicā ritayā nityasaṃyogāt 
yāgānumantraṇānīti samākhyā kratuyojinī /
tasmācchaktyanurodhena prāptistadevate ṛtau 
to viśeṣacintāyāma śakyeṣva niyojanāt /
śabdārtha  viniyogāya liṅgavyāpārasaṃbhavaḥ 
gauṇatvaṃ yatra nāma syākka cid brāhmaṇamantrayoḥ /
tatrānavādarūpatvā mantrāṇāṃ gauṇateṣyate /
gāīpatyastāvad dvitīyayā pradhānasya pratyayārthasya karmeti śrutyā gamyate /
tenaindrayā sa prakāśayitavyaḥ /
tatra yadyathārthatvaṃ  vajanānurodhena saṃjātaṃ tathā nāmetyadhyavasātavyam/
avaśyaṃ bhāvi hyatra brāhmaṇasya mantrasya vā gauṇatvam/
tatra brāhmaṇasyātyantāprāptavidhitvātprathama pravṛtteścānanyapramāṇake 'rthe gauṇatvamayuktam /
mantrasya tu brāhmaṇacoditārthaprakāśanāt tatparatantravṛ tteḥ virodhinaṃ svārthamatotya mukhyaṃ yukto hi gauṣārthanimittabhāvaḥ 
na cāvayavasaṃbandhādindro gṛhapateryataḥ /
tena gārhapatyaḥ syādṛḍhyā 'gnipratyayād dṛḍhāt 
gauṇepi tāvadetasya vṛttiḥ lośena jāyate /
atyantāsahaśatvāttu na gauṇopyatra dṛśyate 
na vādeṅguṇavaccha/
strādindrogniḥ pāribhāṣikaḥ /
na hi śabdārthasaṃvandhaḥ prasiddhaḥ śāvacetukaḥ 
syādagnegaṇamindratvaṃ yajñasaṃbandhakāritam /
indatyarthānumārādvā svakārye sopi hīśvaraḥ 
na kālavidhiyoditatvāt 
cirabhyāsaparatvāttu na mantrotra vidhīyate /
lakṣaṇe ca śaturvṛttiḥ prāptaṃ cānyadanūdyate 
yogyatvena ca siddhatvātkāyopi na vidhīyate /
abhimānamevāssa vidhirityabhidhīyate 
tathā ca yāvajjīvakobhyāsa ityatra kālābhyāsayoranyonyavidhihetutvaṃ vyākhyātam/
atha yaduktaṃ intireva  iviṣkṛsaviṣyatīti /
tatroccate 
athavā paḍhottarametatmatram /
trirabhyāsaparatvāttu na maṃntrotra vidhīyate /
rūpādevāvaghātāṅgaṃ bhavatviti taducyate 
āmantraṇa vibhaktiśva praiṣaśvehoti madhyamaḥ /
vyartha mantre  bhavetsarvamavaghātapare sati 
liṅgāca 
evaṃ ca vāgityartharūpeṇaikāntikenaiva strītvena saṃstavo bhaviṣyati /
anyathā'nupāttasvīliṅgakriyā dipadenā nekāntāvyakaliṅgena śavdadharmatayā kathaṃ citkalpyaḥ syāttasmādāhānāṅgatvamiti 
tathotthānavisarjane 
atideśasūtratvātsarve pūrva sūtrārthā yojayitavyāḥ /
pūrvānuvāde kālārthatvamuktam idānoṃ vidhānārthepīti viśeṣaḥ /
triramyānaparatvācca tatra mantropadeśo na jāto na vi tatheti pūrvapakṣe bojam/
utthānenāgniridhyataityanenotyānaṃ prakāśyataiti pratipādyate 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
muktavāke ca kālavidhiḥ parārthatvāt 
devatā prakāśanugdhāraṇābhyāṃ kṛtārthatvādaṅgāṅgibhāvāpekṣā nāstīti kālārthatā /
sarvatra ca kṛtārthayoḥ saṃbandhe kālārthatvaṃ sthāsyati tṛtīyāṃ cetthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇārthī manyate /
prastarakṛtārthatvābhidhānaṃ ca pratipādyamāna pradhānatvādasya sūktavākāṅgatvaṃtahācyadevatāṅgatvaṃ vā na ghaṭataityasya pratipādanārtham /
tathā sadeva tasya sūktavākasyāpi tadaṅgatvamiti /
upadeśo vā yājyāśabdo hi nākasmāt 
sūktavākena prastaraṃ pradaratīti pratyakṣātkriyāsaṃbandhātkaraṇa tvaṃ gamyamānaṃ na śakyamutsraṣṭuṃ kāraka vibhaktivalīyastvā,devaṃ ca śrutivṛttaḥ saktavāka eva kāryeṇa saṃbhaṃsyate 'nyathā tahaścitaḥ kālaḥ saṃbadhyeta /
tathā cāṅgatve sati sādharmyādyājyāśabda upapatsyate /
sūktavāka eva yājyeti /
kiṃ punarasya pāramārthika me va yājyātvamutopacāramātram /
kaścātra viśeṣaḥ /
sati yājyātve tad mairbhavitavyam /
āsīno yajatyanavānaṃ yajati /
yājyāyā adhi vaṣaṭkaroti /
paronuvākyāṃ ca prathamaṃ prayukai tyādibhiḥ /
atha stutimātraṃ tato naiṣāṃ kaścidādartavya iti /
kiṃ prāptaṃ bhavitavyaṃ dharmeḥ yayejyate mā yājyā sūktavākena cejyate tammādasti yājyātvam /
tatraitatyādakhīliṅgatvādanuci tantravārtike /
strīpratyayo na prāpnoti/
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
samidādiyājyāsvanakṣvapi yājcātvaprasiddheḥ /
athocyetāvardhaveṣu darvihomasādhaneṣu satyapi yāgakaraṇatve yājyātvaṃ na dṛṣṭamato naitaṭai kāntikaṃ kāraṇamiti /
yatraiva yājyāśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ saiva kevannā yājyā tena tarhi saktavāka eva yājyetyatrāpi prayogādbhavitavyaṃ dhamaiṃ, na cāsyaupacārikatvaṃ mukhyakāraṇasannidheḥ pratyakṣatvāt /
a pi ca sāmānya śabdoyaṃ yājyeti sa na śakyo lakṣaṇamantareṇa prayogato viviktaviṣayo 'vadhārayitum /
tatraivalakṣaṇaṃ syāt /
caitreṇa yenejyate tadvastu yājyeti /
tathā sati sūktavākrepi prasaṅgaḥ/
tasmānmukhyamevāsya yājyātvamityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ 
prakṛtau hi sarva̭meva tādarthyotpattyā vastu nirūpyate /
yājyātvaṃ ca tyajyamāna havirdevatoddeśārthavihita mantratvenāvadhāritam /
na ca sūktavākastyajyamāna prastaradevatoddeśārthamutpannaḥ /
iṣṭadevatābhidhāna svarūpatvā, liṅgaṃ śrutyā bādhyataiti cet na /
śruteliṅga viniyogābhyanujñāmantareṇāgni se kādivada sāmarthyāttathā cottarasūtre vacyāmaḥ /
tena svatastāvanna yājyātvam /
na cānyā kā cidevaṃviṣayā yājyāsti yasyāḥ kārye vartamāno yājyādharmakabheta /
prākca yasya yāgatvamavadhāritaṃ tasya sādhanaṃ paścāccodyamānaṃ yājyetyavagamyate /
na tvatra prāksūktavākasaṃbandhātkena cidyāgatvamavadhāritam  taditaretarāśrayaṃ prāpnoti/
yājyāyogādyāgo yāgasaṃbandhādyājyeti /
athaivaṃ parihriyeta vinaiva tāvadyājyāvyapadeśena sūktavākamātratayā gṛhyamāṇo yāge viniyujyeta tato yājyātastadabhidheyadevatāsaṃbandhanabhyayāgatvapradhānapraharaṇasaṃbandhādyājyātvaṃ labhyataiti /
ta ducyate 
yo hi yūpādiśabdo na ka citprasiddhiḥ sa evaṃ prasiddhaṃ labhate /
ayaṃ punaryājyāśabda utpattivelāyāmeva viniyogavelāyāṃ vārthaṃ labhamāno nottarakājabhāvamapekṣate /
yepi ca yājyādharmāstepi prathama siddheṣu yāgeṣu labdhātmāno nedaṃ kleśena labhyamānaṃ yājyātvaṃ pratīkṣante /
yadi tu vikṛtirbhavettataḥ paridhikhanjevālyoriva yūpatvaṃ kāryeṇa yājyātvamadhyavasīyeta /
prakṛtisviyaṃ nākāryapūrvakaṃ dharmanirūpaṇamatopi na yājyādharmāḥ /
tathā ca saktavāka eva yājyetyevakāra upacāraṃ dyotayatyayājyāyāṃ hi yājyopacāre satyevamupapadyate na mukhyaeva yājyātve /
mukhyāyāṃ tvāitau naivakāraḥ prayuktaḥ tadāhutiḥ pāramārthikī 
ādhārādi yathā dravyacāraṇādbomatāṃ gatam /
tathā prakṣeparūpatvāvaraṇasyāpi homatā 
ayājyā evaṃ nigaḍhā ṛcaiva yajatīti hi niṣiddhamapi yājyātvaṃ praśaṃsārthamihoditam 
sa devatārthastatsaṃyogāt 
yattviṣṭadevatāsaṃkīrtanena sūktavākasya kṛtārthatvānna bhūyo viniyogaḥ saṃbhavatīti tatrābhidhīyate 
yattvasya svasāmarthyena devatā prakāśanasādhanatvaṃ prastarapraharaṇepi viniyujyamānasya tannaivāpagacchati /
tatrāpi prakārāntareṇānupayujyamānatvādiri hi yadiṣṭadevatābhidhānasāmathrthyaṃ tatmūktavākenetyanayā śrutyā mahāvirodhaṃ prārthayate /
śrutirapi ca prastara pracaraṇānabhidhāyinaṃ santamasati sāmarthya viniyoktumaśaknuvantī sāmarthyāntaraṃ cānutpādayantī yadayamabhidhātuṃ samarthaḥ kathaṃ nāma tadevābhidadhanmadarthaṃ kuryādityevamapekṣate /
sarvatra kriyāṃ tatsādhanaṃ vābhidadhanmantroṅgabhāvaṃ gacchati /
tatrāpi prathamaṃ tāvadiyaṃ gatiḥ yatprasiddhaṃ śeṣiṇi rūpa tanmantreṇābhidhātavyamiti /
yadā tvasāmarthyāttādarthyaṃ na pratipadyate tadārthādviparyayo bhavati /
yadayamabhidhatte tannūnamasyāṃ kriyāyāmastīti /
na canyathā tasya śrutamaṅgatvamupapadyate /
tasmātsūktavākenetyanayā śrutyaitatpratipādyate /
yattvamabhidhatse tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
tadevābhidadhānaḥ prastarapraharaṇaṃ sādhayeti /
mantroṣi cetyameva bravīti /
iṣṭadevatābhidhānaṃ kurvannadaṃ yatkaromi tatsarvaṃ karomīti /
tatra yadīṣṭā devatāḥ pūrvayāgasaṃbandhinya eva kevalā bhavanti tato na kiṃcitpraharaṇasya kṛtaṃ syā,datha tu nā evāsyāpyaṅgabhūtāstatastatprakāśanadvāreṇa sūktavākena prastaraḥ prahato bhavati /
na ca tāsāṃ devatātvādanyena prakāreṇopayogo vijñāyataityatrāpi devatātvamataśva prastara dravyasya haviṣvasaṃkīrtanādagnyādīnāṃ ca devatātvādyāgoyaṃ vijñāyamānī haraṇe tu juhotiriti prakṣepādhikatvādboma ityavadhāryate /
tasmādavirodhaḥ śrutiliṅgayoḥ /
evaṃ ca sūcamicāpi sa devatārtha eva /
kutaḥ /
tābhirasyāpi harateḥ saṃyogā  kānārthatāpica pramaṅgādbhaviṣyatyeva mantrapāṭhakrameṇa sūktavākasya jñātakālatvādyadyagniridaṃ havirajuṣatetyevamāyeva yeteti /
prāgapi sūktavākeneti śruterasya vaikadeśasya praharaṇaṃ prati sāmarthyamiti darśayati /
yadyapi ca sādhāraṇaṃ mantrasya sāmarthya tathāpi śrutyanugrahārthaṃ prastara eva yadanena iviṣeti nirdeṣṭavyaḥ /
ṛtha vā''dita evārabhyedaṃśabdena prastara nirdeśaḥ puroḍāśādīnāmapratyakṣatvāt /
ajuṣanetyanarthakamiti cet na /
pūrvasevitaprasiddhidāreṇa stutyarthatvādata upa pannamaṅgatvam 
kathama pradhānakarmaṇaḥ sūktavāko 'gnyādayo vāṅgamityata u ttarasūtraṃ paṭhati 
kṛtsnopadeśā dubhayatra sarvavacanam 
adhikāramupajīvancicārayati /
kimubhayoīrśapūrṇamāmayoḥ sakataḥ sūktavākaḥ prayoktavyaḥ uteṣṭadevatānurodhena niṣkarṣa iti /
kiṃ prāptam/
ekaikatra sakala iti /
kutaḥ 
tataśvāsūktavākenaiva prahṛtaḥ syāt /
yathārtha vā śeṣabhūta saṃskārāt 
evamādīnāmapakarṣa ityuktaṃ stutaśastrādhikaraṇe pūṣādyanumantraṇeṣu coktam /
yadyetāni kevalapraharaṇāṅgabhūtāni devatānta rāṇi bhaveyustata ubhayatra sakataḥ prayujyeta /
taeva tviāpyagnyādayaḥ pratyabhijñāyantaiti na bhedaheturakhyata śveṣṭa devatāprakāśanopajīvitvādaprayojakaṃ pradaraṇaṃ sūktavākasya pradhānaprayutadevatāśrayatvātta tadadhīnaṃ vijñāyate /
tāni ca pradhānāni yathādevataṃ prayuñjate nāviśeṣeṇa /
tasmādapakarṣa iti 
vidhiryadi pradhānānāmitikartavyatāṃ prati /
ubhe prati tataḥ kṛtsnaḥ muktavāko bhavedayam 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīya pāda /
yāgasya phanna saṃvandhātpratyeka samavāyinaḥ /
samudāyaḥ phalārthaḥ syāditi kenāvagamyate 
bindau ca samudāye ca toyaśabdo yatheṣyate /
saṃsargidravyarūpatvātsūktavākapadaṃ tathā 
tena tridhaiva mantavyaḥ saktavākaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ /
svādhyāye karmakāle ca prakṛtau vikṛtāvapi 
niṣkraṣṭadevato madhye prakṛtī samudāyayoḥ /
sūryādipadamadhyaśca  vikṛtāvavadhāryate 
liṅgakramasamākhyānātkāmyayuktaṃ samāmnānam 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
yena krameṇaindrāgnādīni kāmyāni karmāpayāmnātāni tenaiva krameṇa tadaivatyāni kāmyasamākhyāyuktāni yājyāpurona vākyāyugannāni tāni kiṃ kramamunlaṅghya taddevatvakarmamānārthāni liṅgāivanti uta kena ciprakāreṇa tādeva kāmyāviṣṭiṣu yathākramaṃ viniyujyanta iti /
udāharaṇabaḍatvaṃ hi mūcopāttaviśeṣaṇaviṣayaprakalpanārtham /
tatra liṅgātsarvārthatve prāpte 'bhidhīyate 
liṅgaṃ hi devatāsaṃbandhaṃ kuryāt /
na ca tatsvarūpa prayutatve phalamasti /
yajña saṃbandhitā tadanuraktadevatā saṃbandhitā vā naitāvatā vākyaprakaraṇādirahitena śakyopādātum /
na ca jñāyate kāṃśe viniyoga iti /
tenāvaśyaṃ samākhyā tāvadāśrayaṇīyā /
tayā hi yajñasaṃbandhaḥ kārya viśeṣaśva sidhyatījyate 'nayeta yāgasaṃbandhaḥ tasyāśca iviḥpradānārthatvātkāryaviśeṣo 'pyavadhṛtaḥ /
tataśca kena yajñena saṃbandha iti liṅgāttaddevatyeneti vijñāyate /
nanvevasapīṣṭaṃ na sidhyatyeva /
kathaṃ na sidhyati /
yadā kāmyaṃ yājyākāṇḍamityetāvatyā samā khyayā kāmyeṣṭiviṣayatvaṃ niyatam /
api ca /
yadyapi samākhyā yajñamātra saṃbandhaṃ kuryāttathāpi balīyasā krameṇa bādhyetaiva /
tasmā kāmyeṣṭiyukta mevaitatmamāmnānamiti /
kimarthamubhayaṃ mūtritamiti /
kramānugṛhītena niṅgenaiva kāgyeṣṭiviṣayatva saṅke, ratha vā kāmyaṃ yājyākāṇḍa mityetāvataiva sarvaṃ siddhamiti manyate /
ta cābhiṣīyate/
satyamaindrāgnādiṣu liṅgakramamātreṇāpi sidhyehacāṃ yājyānuvākyātvā  danyatrāviniyogā, dyāni tvāgneyādīni karmāṇyagnaye vratapataya ityevamādicoditānitatra sthānadayaṭacāmagniprakāśane sāmidhenītvaṃ yājyānuvākyātvaṃ ca /
sāptadabhyāmnānācāsti sāmidhenīnāṃ he ṛcau pratyapekṣā /
tatra yadi yājyāsamākhyā viniyojikā nāśrīyeta tataḥ sāmidhenīṣvapi liṅgakramāvupapadyate iti /
prathamātikrame kāraṇābhāvāttacaiva viniyogaḥ prāpnoti/
samākhyayā tu tannivartitaṃ bhavati /
tena tarhi tanmātramevāstu nārtho liṅgakramābhyāmiti /
taducyate /
yadyatreṣṭiparimitā evātyantaṃ taddaivatyā śvānāyeran tata etadevaṃ syā,dicha tvanyadevatyasya svānurūpayājyānuvākyāpūritasya karmaṇaḥ krame yā āgneyya ṛcaḥ padyante tāḥ samākhyayā kevajayā viniyujyamānā yājyākārye viniyajyeran /
na cāsti saṃbhavaḥ viciṅgatvādanyābhyāṃ talliṅgābhyāṃ bādhitatvāt /
tenāviniyogaevaṅgakramāśrayaṇe punaḥ samākhyāyāṃ nivṛttavyāpārāyāṃ tābhyāṃ viniyoge sati sāmidhenīṣu prayogaḥ siddho bhavati /
taṃ viṣayaṃ darśayati /
āgnivāruṇyā iṣṭeryājyāpurīnuvākye paṭhitvā saumārairaudrīṇāmiṣṭonāṃ yājyāpuronuvākyāvanāgatāsu manoṣṭacaḥ padyante /
tāḥ sāmidhenoṣu dhāyyā avantīti /
tathā pṛthupājavatyāvapi draṣṭavye/
tatrāpi pūrvasyāḥ sāmidhenīkramamatikramya yājyāpuronuvākyottara kālapāṭhāduttareṣṭiviṣayatvaṃ vijñāyate /
yadi ca kramo nāśrīyeta tato liṅgasamākhyāmātreṇa prathamamaitṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
ndrāgnayugalaṃ dvitīyasyāmaindrāgnyāṃ viniyujyeta dvitīyaṃ ca pra thamāyāṃ, krame tu sati samākhyātaḥ pūrvataraṃ tena kratusaṃbandhakaraṇāttatsaṃniruddvameva ciṅgaṃ śrutiṃ kalpayanīti akrama viniyo gaḥ parihato bhavati /
tasmātsamyak sūcita miti /
adhikāre ca mantravidhiratadākhyeṣu śiṣṭatvāt 
jyotiṣṭome prathamamāgneyyainyādayaḥ stotraśastrādisādhanatvenāgna āyāhi vītayaityevamādayo viśeṣa rūpeṇammātā vi hitāśca punaśca sāmānyenāgneyyāgnī pramupatiṣṭhataityādiṣūpadiśyante /
tatra saṃdehaḥ kiṃ tayatiriktā grahītavyā uta tā vā anyā vā 'tha vā tā eveti granthāttrayaḥ pakṣāḥ pratibhānti /
na tviāprakṛtā evetyasya pakṣasya pramāṇamasti /
mahatā hi prabandhenā viśeṣagrahaṇaṃ pratipādyate na kevalāprakṛtaniścayo yena hi pramāṇenāgneyośabdāviśeṣeṇāprakṛtā gṛhye rastenaiva prakṛ tā api /
na ca kiṃ citkāraṇamasti yena prakṛtāḥ parityajyera, nna ca bhāṣyakāraṇa trayaḥ pakṣāḥ pradarśitāḥ kiṃ tarhi aviśeṣapaśca evādāvapiśabdarahitenāprakṛtaśabdena parigṛhītaḥ /
yenāprakṛtā eveti bhrāntirbhavati /
yattu tatra pramāṇaṃ tadaviśeṣapadāmeva sādhayati /
tathā ca parastādvivṛtamaprakṛtepi pratyayo bhavati prakṛtamapyupādadīraniti ca /
yadi tvavaṇyaṃ tṛtīyopi pakṣaḥ samarthanīyastata etāvatī śrotriyopapattiḥ /
prakṛtasya kāryāntaropayogena yātayāmatvādagrahaṇam/
athavā sāmānyavidhānami dantāni tvāgneyo viśeṣavidhānāni, parihatya ca viśeṣavidhiviṣayaṃ sāmānyaśāstrāṇi pravartante /
yadi tu tatrāpi viśeṣagraiṇaṃ na syāt tatastadapyanenaiva tulyamityudāharaṇatvena gṛhyeta /
tammādaprakṛtā eva grahītavyāḥ /
atha vāgneyādiśabdara viśeṣapratyayo jātaḥ /
na cānyat prakṛtagrahaṇadyamaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ paśyāmaḥ /
prakaraṇamya grāhakatvenāviśeṣakatvāt /
sannidhilakṣaṇalo kikaprakaraṇasya ca yaugikaśrutijanitā viśeṣapratyayena bādhyamānatvāttasmātsarvapratyayaḥ /
upadiṣṭopadeśo hi na nyāyya iti /
idha upadiṣṭasyaivetyarthaḥ /
evaṃjātīyakasyeti viśeṣaṇarahitasyetyarthaḥ /
kathaṃjātīyakasyeti /
asti vināpi viśeṣaṇena viśeṣagrahapramāṇaṃ prakaraṇāmiti siddhāntavādī manyate /
paraḥ punaḥ svābhiprāyeṇaiva siddhāntavādyabhimatāṃ viśeṣagrahaṇopapattimanabhimatāmeva parikalpya kathaṃ yadi talliṅgaṃ tasyopalavaṇa tvenetyāca /
na cātropari vacya māṇadevatāliṅgābhiprāyeṇa liṅgapadaṃ prayuktam /
kiṃ takhyāta pratyayasāmathyeṃ tadvihitatvaṃ vā/
tadupakṣīpathaktau tasminvidhyabhāvaprasaṅgopanyāsāt /
nāsau sāmānyena sa liṅgenetyagninā cina sarvāsu pratīyamānāsa sphuṭena vi śeṣaṇena vinā na śakyo mantraviśeṣaḥ pratipattumityabhiprāyaḥ /
tadiha yadi viśeṣaṇamiṣyate tato dārśaparṇamāsika nirvāpālambhanyāyena kartavyatāvacanena liṅgena viśeṣṭavyam /
tadvyakamaṅgabhūtebhyo dāśatayebhyo  nivṛttamata eva viśeṣaṇaṃ tathā darśayati /

tatasāviśeṣitāgneyīmātragrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ /
tenopadiṣṭasyaiva tadupalakṣitasya punarupadeśa ityapramāṇakam /

nanu prakaraṇa sāmarthyāditi siddhāntābhi prāyeṇoktam /

upariṣṭāt bahuprayogagatopi liṅgaśabda evameva yaugika śrutivacano vyā khyeyaḥ /
āha virodhe satīti yadi prakṛtamanāgneyaṃ gṛhṇīmaḥ tato virodho bhavetprakṛtāgneyagrahaṇe tu iyamapyanugṛhyate /
tathā tadūtādhikaraṇe śrutivākyayoravirudvatvamuktam /

itarastu vyaktyabhidhānābhiprāyeṇa dāśatayaprāptinivartanādvirodhaṃ samarthayate /
nanu vyaktirapadārtha ityabhiprāyapratyādeśaḥ /
parastvācha /
etadeva na vijānī mastaliṅgavattā sāmānyabhūtātrāṅgaṃ na veti /
yadi hi gavādiśabdavaktyabhidhānāsambhavastataḥ sāmānyacodanāyāṃ satyāmatavyaktigrahaṇānuṣaṇī prakṛtavyaktigrahagopya ḍhoṣo'tha tu devatopalacitā vyaktireva śabdārthaḥ tataḥ prakatagrahaṇe sati śrutijanita pratyayaikadeśabādhaḥ syātmā ceha vyaktireva sādhanaṃ na sāmānya nāma kiṃ cit kiṃ punaridānīmākṛtyadhikaraṇokta sāmānyāpanhavaṃ bhāṣyakāraḥ karoti /
neti brūmaḥ /
tasyāṅgatvā saṃbhavamātramāheti ke ci, ttadayuktam /
tathā sati vyaktīnāmaśrutatvādaparigrahepi doṣābhāvā, dataḥ prakṛtāpekṣayā sāmānyamapahūyata iti vaktavyam/
vyaktiśabdo hyayaṃ yaugikatvāt na jāti mabdatvaṃ pratipadyate/
na cātra jātiḥ kā citpratīyate nānārūpāsu nānācchandaskāsvapi ca devataikatvamātreṇāgneyyā diśabdaprayogāt /
na āgnaāyāhi vītayegniṃ hotāraṃ manye dākhantamityeta yodevatāvyatiriktaṃ kiṃ citmāmānyaṃ dṛśyate /
devatāsaṃbandha mevaiṣa na vyabhicarati vyabhicarati tu ṛgjātiṃ dravyakamadiṣvapi prayogāt /
ato devataivātra samānetyāha /
saṃbandhasta samānaḥ sannapi nābhidheyatvenārthasidvatvādbhāṣyakāreṇopanyastaḥ /
tasyā eva ca devatāyāḥ samānatvāyattyānantyādidoṣanivṛttiḥ /
pūrvābhihite 'pi ca viśeṣaṇe prakṛtipratyayayoḥ śaktibhedātpratyayena viśeṣyābhidhānamaviruddham /
yatra tu tāvāneva śabda ubhayatra vyāpārayitavyastatra viśeṣyānabhidhānaṃ yathā gavādau /
na cātra viśeṣaṇābhidhānamātrasyāgniśabdasya kadā cidapi viśeṣyeṣu prayogo nāpyāgneyīśabdasyāgnau yato vi śeṣyaṃ yāvannīyeta /
yadi ceca viśeṣaṇamātramabhidhīyeta tatastasyaiva kāryakṣamatvānnaiva viśeṣyaṃ parigṛhyeta /
tasmādyataya evātrābhidheyāḥ /
taduktaṃ piṅgāccaikacāyanīśabdayoḥ /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
tataśca pakṣe prakṛtamapyupāda dīran /
nanvetaduktamityādyapakṣābhiprāyeṇa /
nanu tvayaiva yātayāmatvādidoṣāttasyānupādānamuktam /
parastu madhyamapakṣaṃ parigṛhyāca /
kevalaprakṛtagrahaṇe hi pratyayasya yugapadvidhincakṣaṇavyāpārādvirodho 'bhitiḥ matyace tu na niyogataḥ sa evātrāgnīghrādyupasthāne kiṃ tarhi viśeṣavacanena sa cānyaśvetyāvirodhaḥ /
nanvetaddaṣyatīti vinā kāraṇena prakaraṇapīḍāmasahamāno vadati /
parastu devatāliṅgayuktiśrutibalīyastvamevottaraṃ dadāti /
api ca na liṅgayogika atyātmakaṃ prakaraṇaṃ cānugrahītavyamiti lokasyātisaṃmugdhāṃ vācoyuktiṃ nirākartumupanyasyati /
sarvapramāṇavyavahāreṣveva na pramāṇa manugrahītuṃ puruṣāḥ prameyeṣu pravartante kiṃ tatmānam tataḥ kimiti cedata /
etadato bhavati /

naikāntātkama saṃbandhamupapādayituṃ namaḥ

na vasāvapyavidhīyamānaḥ saṃbhavatīti darśayati /

punarekavākyatā /

tena bhakṣasya pratyāsannavareṇa ma ntrādinā varuḍatvāḍhateṣāmapi ca svayamanyatrāpravṛtterapakarṣaḥ /

coditārthānurodhena mantraḥ sarvaḥ pravartate /
tena tvaṣṭravadevātra triṃśatāgnerabhiṣṭutiḥ /
pātnovatacodanārtha smaraṇahetunā mantreṇa na śakyamacoditamagneḥ pariveṣṭutvamitareṣāṃ ca bhoktṛtvaṃ prakāśayitum /
ato mantrasya parārthatvānna codanāmatikramya svātantryeṇa trayastriṃśa prakāśana sāmarthyamavakalpate/
vidhānasāmathrthyaṃ tu dūrabhraṣṭameva /
na ca triṃśato devatātvameva smārayati coditāgnyaiśvaryaprakāśanaparatvena trayastriṃśatprakīrtanāt 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
yadi hyaprattāvasthameva dravyatvaṃ dehoti mukhyamevocyate tataḥ pratāraṇameva syāt /
atha tu tvamevāna dātā svāmī na vayaṃ svāmina ityetatparaṃ bhavati yathā loke kaściducyate kiṃ tvayi bhavati nimantrita tvayaivānye nimantraṇīyā iti tato vākyaṃ saṃbaddhaṃ bhavati /
coditakaraṇāca dṛṣṭārthaṃ bhavati /
mādayaskhetyapi mukhyasya mantrārthasya  saṃbhavādetebhya ityetalāyati /
dātṛttvamapyagnerdṛṣṭārthameveti saṃpradānalakṣaṇārthaṃ vijñāyate /
vi spaṣṭaṃ ca tadvitena yadanyanirapekṣamavagataṃ tanmantrānurodhena bādhitaṃ na syāt /
kathaṃ punaḥ pātnovatamiti coditegnidevatāvagamyate na puna striṃśaddevatā syāt /
ata āpatnīvāṃścāgniriha gṛhyate /
na trayastriṃśadagnaāi  patnīvanniti sāmānādhikaraṇyadarśanāt /
nanu triṃśatāpi saca sāmānādhikara eyamasti patnīvata striṃśata miti /
satyamasti /
tathāpyatrāgniḥ patnīvān gṛhyate /
tadvitanirdeśena hi prātipadikārthasya saṃkhyāviśeṣābhivyaktirbhavati /
tatra prātipadikārthānanyathāsaṃbhavādekavacanāntena vigrado bhavati /
patnīvāndevatāsyeti /
triṃśaca nityaṃ bahuvacanāntaḥ /
tasmānna tebhyastahita iti devatātvābhāva iti 
yathā paścāttanaḥ pātā pūrvapātrupalakṣaṇam /
tantravārtika /
aprākṛtaṃ na kurvīta tathaināmapi devatām 
chandaḥpratiṣedhastu sarvagāmitvā t 
sthitāduttaram /
na yathādevatamūhaḥ kiṃ tarhyanendrāṇāmamantrakameveti 
yadi hyabhyāsāḥ  pṛthakkarmāṇi bhaveyustataḥ prakṛtivikā rabhāvaḥ syānna tvevamasti /
na caiṣāṃ somo dharmā vā kena cidihitāḥ /
yena tu prakāreṇaiko gṛhṇāti tena sarve /
yathā vakṣyati tadatmavanāntare grahāmnānamiti /
na ca mantravaśenaindraviṣayatā somasya /
pratyakṣayā śrutyā sarva viṣayatvabodhāt /
na ca yathā 'nāramyavādenāivanīyaḥ sarvahomārtha iti tadrahita karmāntarābhāvādanā hitāgneradhikāraḥ evamiha mantraḥ sarvasomārthaḥ  /
prakaraṇapaṭhitaḥ sāmarthyādindrārthaṃ pra kāśayiṣyati/
anyastu tenāprakāśita eva grahīṣyate māsyate vā /
athavā vivekābhāvātsarvasminneva gṛhyamāṇe saṃkalpamātreṇa vyavasthāsyate /
atha vā subrahmaṇyāvanmukhyatayendra prakāśanārthī/
tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
bhavati /
tatprabhṛtaye devatāsamudāyāyetyarthaḥ /
atha vā vidhiśabde vasumattvasyābhāvāttaka prakāśanaṃ vyarthamiti vasumattveneta radevatāsahitāyetyetadabhidhīyate /
tasmātsarvatra samāna vidhānaḥ somaḥ /
tataśca vikāratvābhāvaḥ /
yattvanuṣṭupchandaso vināma vi dhānādikkṛtitvamiti tatmamānavidhānatvepi tṛtīyasavanatvājjagacchandastve prāpte viśiṣṭavidhānatvenopapatyate /
atha vā saṃsthānāṃ vikāratvādupapanna evātroha ityadarśanameva  /

kutaḥ /
na devatātvamindrasya tatpītatvena kathyate  /
tena nāgneyatulyatvamasāmarthyādiheṣyate 
ekasminbā devatāntarādvibhāgavat 
satyaṃ yadi devatāvyāpāraḥ pātṛtvamiha viśeṣaṇaṃ syāt /
tata aindrāgnopi gṛhyeta /
na tvasmākaṃ devatā pibati /
kiṃ tarhi saṃkalpaviṣayatvenaivopayujyate /
na ca miśrasaṃkalpe 'nyataravyapadeśaḥ saṃbhavati taddhitavatsamāsasya sāpekṣeṣvapravṛtteḥ /
tasmādāgneyacatukaraṇavadeva kevalendra devatyaviṣayatvānnaiva vyapadeśa ubhayadevatyaḥ saṃbhavatīti mantranivṛttiranenaiva ca viśeṣeṇāsyāpunaruktatvam /
yat pūrvapakṣavādī na devatātvaminha viśeṣaṇaṃ kiṃ tarhi saṃpradānagataṃ pāttṛtvaṃ tacca pratyekamapyastīti manyate /
sidvāntavādī tu mukhya pāttṛtvā saṃbhavāddevatātvamevānena uccataityāpādayati /
yadyapi ca mukhyaṃ pātṛtvaṃ devatāyāṃ bhavettathāpi dravyasya tatpītatvamaśakyaṃ vaktum /
katham 
camasastho hi indrapītatvena vyapadiśyate /
na cāsāvindrapītaḥ ita viṣayatvādindra pītavyapadeśasya /
tasmādavaṇya vidyamānadharmābhidhānādindrāya saṃkalpita indrapītaḥ pratyetavyaḥ /
tataścāpanaṃ devatātvamevopacakṣaṇamiti /
na ca itasomagataṃ pītatvaṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pāda /
tatropacarituṃ śakyam/
ātmadharmeṇaiva saṃkalpenābhidhānopapatteḥ /
ekadeśepi hi hūyamāne sarvamidaṃ dravyaṃ devatoddeśena tyajyamāna yāgaṃ sādhayati /
atosa/
nirvapateriva yajirevātra pibaterarthaḥ /
te naindra yāga sādhanādindra pīta pratyaya sāmarthyānmantra nivṛttiḥ 
sarveṣu vābhāvādekacchandasaḥ 
yatra nāmopapadyeta nirapekṣaṃ viśeṣaṇam /
sāpekṣasyāgrahastatra na tu yatrāpi nāsti tat 
sarveṣāṃ vaikamantraya maitiśāyanasya bha ktipānatvātsavanādhikārī hi 
sthitāduttara, manindrapīteṣvapi avikṛta eva mantraḥ prayoktavyo nāmantrakaṃ bhakṣaṇam /
kunaḥ /
indre yasminsavane pītaḥ somo nirūpyate /
tasya yonyopi saṃbandhī sa evaṃ vyapadiśyate 
śrīrāmacandrāya namaḥ /
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ /
śrutejatādhikāra syāt 
evaṃ liṅgaviniyogamupavarṇya saṃprati vākyaviniyogaḥ prastūyate /
tatrodāharaṇam /
uccairṛcā kriyate ityādi vākyam /
ta dyadi ṛkta ulbaṇaṃ kriyate gāīpatyaṃ paretya bhūḥ svāheti juddhayādyadi yajuṣṭo yadi sāmata ityādi ca /
tatra kimhagyajuḥsāmaśabdaiḥ uccaivopāṃśutvadharmavidhau mahāvyāhatyagnitrayasaṃbaddhahomavidhau ca pūrvottarapada  nirapekṣābhidhānaśrutivaśena teṣāmṛgyatrārthavaśena pāḍhavyavasthetyevaṃcakṣaṇānāmṛgādijātānāṃ grahaṇam uta samastamantrabrāhāṇātmakānāṃ vedānāmiti /
kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ ekavākyopakramopasaṃhāra śrutyorvipratipatteḥ /
upakrame hi vedāḥ śrūyante /
upasaṃhāre tu ṛgādijātāni /
tatra yadi vopakramasthavedapadamavayavabhūtajātacakṣaṇārtham atha vopasaṃcāra sthamṛgādijātaṃ sabrāhmaṇa ka samudāyanna kṣaṇārthamiti samañjasā samaja sayoḥ saṃdehaḥ sa cāktāḥ śarkarā itivadācepaparihārābhyāṃ samarthanīyaḥ /
evaṃ tarhi tenaiva gatatvānnaitadāravyavyam/
nāyamupālambhaḥ saṃdigdheṣu hi vākyaśeṣasya tatra prāmāevamuktam /
iha punarvidhyuddeśavarttināmṛgādiśabdānāṃ niḥsaṃdigghamantrabhedajātavacanatvādasaṃdigdha eva vidhyuddeśaḥ /
tena vyavadhāraṇakalpanayānyatarapakṣāvadhāraṇaṃ kāryamityārabhyate/
kiṃ prāptam/
tadoyapūrvapakṣanyāyenaiva vidhyuddeśaśrutibajoyastvājjātādhikāra iti kiṃ ca 
na kathaṃ cit ṛgādiśabdena brāhmaṇaṃ vaktuṃ śakyam /
śaknoti tu vedaśabda ekadeśepi varttituṃ samudāyaśabdānā mekadeśevapyupalabdhaḥ yathā grāma āyāta iti /
tathā cādhyetārasta naiva sutarāṃ prayuñjate vedama ghīmahe vedo varttataiti /
na ca brāhmaṇamadhīyānāstathā vadanti /
kiṃ ca 
ṛco hi tā eva kāścittriṣvapi vedeṣu padyante tathā yajūṃṣi /
tatra yadi vedatvaṃ dharmasaṃbandhacetustatastādṛśeṣu na jñāyate ko dharmaḥ kriyatā mityanyāyyo vā vikalpa āśrīyate vedāntaravyapradeśasya tulyabalatvāt /
jātipakṣe tu naiṣa doṣo na hyekasminvarṇasamūce jātidvayaṃ samavetam /
jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇaṃ caivamanugrahīṣyate anyathā vedasya samasteṣṭipaścekā chāṃhīnasa caviṣayatvādyāvahedānusārī dharmaḥ prakaraṇamujhaṅghya sārvatrikaḥ syāt /
nanu jātādhikāropi vedavajjātasya prakaraṇāntaradhvapi bhāvāttulyametat /
atha prakṛtajātātikramakāraṇābhāvādiha vyavasthā sā vedapakṣepyaviśiṣṭā yāvānprakaraṇe veda ityavadhārapyāt /
naitattalyam
sarvargādisamūheṣu jātaṃ vyāsaṅgi cedbhavet/
prakṛtau na samāpyeta tatastadapi vedavat 
samūhāstvekavākyānāṃ ye pādapadaparvaṇām /
ṛgyajuḥ sāmajātāni pratyekaṃ teṣu santi naḥ /
yathā vanādisaṃghātāḥ prāvasāmānya samanvitāḥ /
tathargādisamūhānāṃ sāmānyaṃ jātamucyate 
dvivaca pade jātigaśabdatvaṃ na kalpitam /
vākyatvavatkathaṃ nu syurṛgyajuḥ sāmajātayaḥ 
yaugikānāṃ yathā jāte ranyatmāmānya miṣyate /
tathā samūhasāmānyaṃ jātaṃ jāti vilakṣaṇam 
vedo vā prāyadarśanāt 
kimidaṃ prāyadarśanāditi /
nedamanyaiḥ prāyadarśanaiḥ tulyamiti paśyanpṛcchati /
prāyavacanācetyatra hi pradhānaprāye yatrānyāni pradhānāni tatra vacanādityuktam /
tathā viṣaye prāyadarśanāditi saṃskāraprāye yatrānye saṃskārā godohanādayastatrāsya darśanamiti/
na tviha yatrānye vedāstatraiṣāmṛgādīnāṃ darśanamityapi śakyaṃ vaktum /
na hyetadvyatiriktā vedāḥ santi yeṣāṃ madhyapāte saṃkocerana ato neha prāyadarśanamastīti /
tatrottaramāca vedaprāye vedopakrame veḍhabuddhijanitasaṃskāravyāpte manasi ime śabdāḥ śrūyante taddarśayati prajāpatirvā idameka āsīt /
yattu vidhyuddeśananīyastvā darthavādapadastho vedaśabdo 'vayava viṣayo bhaviṣyatīti /
tatra brūmaḥ 
J ye hi vidhyuddeśātparastādarthavādāḥ śrayante teṣā masti daurbalyaṃ ye purastāt śrūyante te mukhyatvāilīyāṃso bhavanti /
sarvasyaiva hi śabdasya svārthātinlaṅghane virodhaḥ kāraṇaṃ, sa ca prayogidṛṣṭe vi rodho vijñāyate, tadiha yadā trayo vedā asṛjyantāune gveda ityādi śrūyate na tadā jātavacanānāmṛgādīnāmuccāraṇāma sti, yadarśanena vedaśabdo 'vayavacakṣaṇārtho bhavet /
atastena tāvat śrutivṛttenaiva vyāptā buddhi, rathedānīmmṛgādiśabdāḥ svārthaparāḥ santo na saṃbadhyate iti balāt laścaṇāṃ pratipadyantaiti tena tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
satyapi vidhyuddeśagatatve daurbalyaṃ mukhyaṃ vā pūrvacodanālokavadivyevamitarabannīyasvāt/
nanu paurvāparye pūrvadāvalyaṃ prakṛtiva dityanenotpannamapyarthavādānmukhyavedajñānaṃ bādhitvā vidhyuddeśajñānameva gṛhota/
naitadevam 
ye hi bhinnavākyagatāḥ parasparanirapekṣā virodhino 'rthāḥ śrayante teṣāṃ pūrvasyottarānupamahenaiva lavyātmakatvāduttarasya pūrvepamana vinātmanābhānupapatteḥ paurvāparyabanīyasvanyāyo bhavati /
yatra tvekavākyatayā parasparāpekṣā śravaṇaṃ na tatraitajñavati /
tatra hyākāṅkṣāvaśena ekavākyatā bhavati, pūrvapratīte cottaramātmāna guṇamadhikaṃ vākāṅkṣati, ataśca yadanadhikamananuguṇaṃ vā tadanapekṣitatvāt naiva tasminvākyasti /
na cāvidyamānena pūrvabādhaḥ śakyataiti pūrvabanīyastvaṃ bhavati /
nadi vidhyarthavādayoḥ samānaviṣayatvāt yāvadevārthavāde vedāḥ saṃkīrttitāḥ tāvadeva kimapyeṣāṃ vidhāyataityetadavadhatam /
tataśca kimeṣāṃ vidheyamityetāvanmaśate na tu kasya kiṃ vidhāsyataiti /
tenottaramādavayavāda peścitamātraṃ gṛhyate vidheyaṃ vāpeścitaṃ na vidhiviṣaya ityuccaitvādimācaṃ saṃbadhyate na tu ṛgādayaḥ /
tata svāvivaścitatvānnaivaiṣāṃ vidhyuddeśestitvamiti nārthavādaṃ bādhante arthavādasya eva tu vidhyuddeśaviṣayatvenāpi, vedovadhāryate /
tasmādalaṇārthatvamṛgādīnām /
vedaśva vyāpakatvāda hetunakṣaṇayuktaḥ sanna śaknotyevāvayavaṃ lakṣayitu,nṛgādayastu niyamyatvāsamudāyaṃ caścayanti yathā cānyatrārthavādānāmanuvādatvajñaḥ tantravārtike /
kṣaṇāvṛttiradoṣaḥ tathācārthavādāvagataviṣaye vidhau ṛgādiśabdānāmanuvādakatvāt ṇāyāmapyadoṣa, stenaiṣā vacanavyaktiḥ yasmādevamete vedā jātāsta māṭepāmuccaisvādi karttavyamiti vaktavye tamevārthasiddhamaṅgīkṛtya ṛgādaya uccāryante anyathā hyasaṃbaddhameva syāt /
vidhyarthavādayonnanāviṣayatvāttasmādvedādhikāra iti 
vyatikrame yathāśrutīti cet 
anubhāṣaṇametat 
vedasaṃyogāna prakaraṇena bādhyeta 
bādheteti vā pāṭhaḥ /
 dharmopadeśāca na hi dravyeṇa saṃbandhaḥ 
jātadharmapakṣe ṛyadhyūḍhaṃ sāma gāyavyavasāmayoraviyomādvagdharmeṇaiva sāmadharmasiṭṭevṛthā punarupadeśaḥ /
na hi kaścitmāmādhārabhūtāmṛcamuccairuccārayan sāmānyanyathoccārayituṃ samartho, vedādhikāre tvanyadṛgvedena vidhīyate anyacca sāmavedenetyartha vadupadeśadvayam /
anṛkprajāpatihṛdayādyarthamitaracāpi bha viṣyatīti cet na /
tasya jyotiṣṭomānaṅgatvāt /
prakaraṇe hyayaṃ stotrasāmnāmupadeśaḥ /
na ca teṣāmanukāṇāṃ prayogo'lpaviṣayatvācca mandaparihṛtamevānarthakyam/
tasmādapi vedādhikāra iti siddham 
guṇe svarūpato dharmaḥ pradhānadvārato 'paraḥ /
yatra syāttatra vijñeyaṃ guṇadharmasya bādhanam /
avaśyaṃ karttavye 'nyataradharmātikrame guṇadharmo 'tikramitavyaḥ /
tathā hi pradhānamaviguṇaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati/
tacca guṇanyāpi kāryam /
sopi hi tadarthameva pravartate /
yadi tvātmīyadharmānurodhena pradhānaṃ viguṇaṃ kuryāttatosya yadarthaiva pravṛttistadeva dīyeta /
tatkharūpe ma guṇe jāte yadyapyaṅgaṃ viguṇameva tathāpi tatra guṇatvasyācikorṣitatvānna kaścidvirodhaḥ /
tammāḍhādhānasya yāzarvedikatvāttadaṅgabhūtānāṃ sāmnāmupāṃśutvaṃ karttavyamiti /
nanu yāvanmātramādhānasya yajurvedavihitaṃ tanmātrasyaivopāṃśatvamityavagamānnaiva sāmagānasya prāpnoti pradhānamātraṃ cāṅgāntarāṇi ca yājurvedikāni tena teṣāṃ kevalamupāṃtvamiti /
naitadevaṃ vacyati hi aṅgāni tu vidhānatvātpradhānenopadiśyeranniti /
tathā vidhestvekaśrutitṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīya  pāda /
tvādaparyāya vidhānāditi /
tasmātpradhānaprayogavacanaparigṛhītatvādanyatrāmṛtyajñānāmaṅgānāṃ yatraiva pradhānaṃ tatraiva vidhi, rataśca sāṅgasyaitra pradhānasya yājurvedikatvādupāṃśutvenaiva bhavitavyamiti /
evaṃ tarhi svayamevāṅgānāṃ yājurvedikatvādupāṃśatvaṃ na guṇapradhānadharmavirodhadvāraṃ yacca sāmagatamupāṃśutvaṃ tadaṅgavarttitvādu cai stvena tulyaṃ, naitattatra varttamānaṃ pradhānasyeti śakyaṃ vadituṃ, nāpi tadgate bādhite pradhānadharmabādho na hi tadā pradhānamupāṃśu na kṛtaṃ syā,datha kena citprakāreṇāṅgadharmepi pradhānasyābhidhīyate tata uccaimtvamapi pradhānadharma eva svāditi punastulyabanatvam /
uccate 
yadi hi yajurvedaevaiṣāmutpattiḥ syāt tatsvarūpanimitta mevopāṃśutvaṃ sthā, deteṣāṃ tu sāmavedotpannānāṃ svarūpata uccaistva prasaṅge pradhāna saṃparśa nimittamupāṃśutvamiti pradhānadharmatā /
nanu yajurvedena sāṅgaṃ kuryādityupabandhātmāṅgasyaivopāṃśutva mityavadhāraṇādastyevāṅga svarūpa saṃsparśa iti /
na /
sāṅgakathanenaivāprādhānya nirdeśāt /
upasarjanabhūtāṅgaṃ hi pradhānamevaṃ niddiśyate /
tena pradhānameva yājurvedikamupāṃśutvaṃ tu taddharma eva sannaṅgānyupasarpannevaṃ kathyate/
na tvevameva codanāpyasti /
tataḥ pradhānadharmeyamaṅgaṃ prāptotikramyeta, pradhānena hi svadharmeṅgeṣu vikṣiptaḥ sa yatraiva vādhitastatraiva pradhānaṃ viguṇaṃ na tvevamuccaistvaṃ pradhānadharma ityavadhāryate/
na hyaṅgadharmāḥ pradhānāni saṃkrāmanti /
nanvevamapyaṅgadharmaḥ sākṣātprāpnoti pradhānadharmaḥ punaḥ paradāreṇa parokṣa tantravārtike /
iti viparītaṃ balābalaṃ prāpnoti /
satyaṃ sāśātprāptāṅgadharmaḥ śīprataramavagamyate prayogavacanagrahaṇottara kālaṃ tu paścātana eva pradhānadharmaḥ paurvāparye pūrvadaurbalyaṃ prakṛtivadityeva bādhate /
nanu yājurvedikajyotiṣṭomādyaṅgānāṃ stotraśastrādīnāmapyanenaiva nyāyenopāṃśutvaṃ prāpnoti /
satyaṃ prāpnoti vacanāttu sarvatra svarāntarajābhaḥ /
kathaṃ darśapūrṇamāsayostāvaḍedadvayavihiteṣvaṅgeṣu nānāvedambare prāpte guṇāmukhyavyatikramanyāyena yājurvedikapradhā nadharma upāṃśutvaṃ prāpnoti /
tato vācanikaḥ kharo bhavati ma ndrayājyabhāgāntaṃ paraṃ madhyamayottamayānyājādīti /
tathā vikṛtīnāmiṣṭipaśubandhādīnāmetasminneva prākṛte svaratraye prānuvati pratyakṣopadeśavaśena pradhānavedasvaraprasaktau tadgrahaṇādvā svadharmā syādityanena nyāyena prayogavacanasya codakāpekṣitvena durbalatvā codaka prāpita svaragrahaṇameveṣṭam /
evaṃ jyotiṣṭomāṅgānāmapi dīkṣaṇīyādīnāṃ prākṛte svare prāpte pratyacopadeśavaśena bādhyamāne codakabalīyastvena punarusthite jyotiṣṭomasya yājurvedikatvāt klṛptopakāraprākṛtadharmā grahaṇācca guṇamukhyavyatikramanyāyenaiva tadgatopāṃśutvadharmaprasaṅga  sati yāvatyā vācā kāmayeta tāvatyā dīkṣaṇīyāyāmanubrūyādityete svarāḥ gumukhyavyatikrama nyāyaba /
dhenaiva sāṅgānāṃ prāptāḥ/
tathā jyotiṭomasya vācanikasavanavibhāga vihitamandra madhyamottamocāraṇāvadhāraṇāttadaṅgānāmapi sarveṣāṃ prākṛtatulyamandra madhyamottamoccāraṇānyeva pradhānadvāreṇa prāptāni /
tato yatkiṃcit prācīnamagnoṣomoyāttenopāṃśu carantītyapāṃśutve sāṅgānāṃ dīkṣaṇītṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
yādīnāṃ prāpte pradhānamācavācidīkṣaṇīyādiśabdoddeśena vi hitāḥ pradhānamātreṣvete svaraviśeṣā bhavanti /
yāvatyā vācā kāmayeta tāvatyā dīkṣaṇīyāyāmanubrūyānmandraṃ prāyaṇīyāyāṃ mandrataramātithyāyāmupāṃpūsarasvati tatropāṃśutvasya pūrveva sarvavyāpinopāṃśutvavidhinā prāptatvāddīṛṇīyādisvara praśaṃsārtho nityānuvāda eva /
śragniṣomīye tu savanavibhāgasvareṇaiva mandrayājyabhāgāntamityādiprākṛta svarapratiprasavaḥ savanavibhāgatulyaṃ vā sāṅgaṃ prayogaṃ tredhā vibhajya mandramadhyottamoccāraṇasaṃpādanaṃ kāryam /
etenānubandhyāvabhṛtho dayanīyodavasānīyāsvapyuccāraviśeṣā vyākhyātāḥ /
mutyā kālasavanīyādīnāmapyevaṃ kharaṃ prāpte prātaḥ savanādyantargatatvādyathā savanameva kharā bhavanti /
nanu ruva naśabdānāṃ somayāgāvayavavacanatvāddī kṣaṇīyādyaṅgavattadīyakharābhāvapramaṅga iti cet na /
saptamīnirdeśena tatkāla prayujyamātvamātrāśrayaṇāt 
saptamyāṃ tu tadādhāro yāvānmantraḥ prayujyate /
tasya sarvasya mandrādisvarayogoṅgamāśritaḥ 
stotraśālā nuvākyā diśeṣasta savanasya yaḥ /
ṣaṣyabhāvāntra tasyaite yuktā mandrādayaḥ kharāḥ 
yathā hi śakunirvṛce puṣpādyapi tatheṣyate /
tataśvādheyadharmorthaḥ sa iyepi vidhīyate 
nānāvedasvarastasmāt stotrādeḥ prāpta āditaḥ /
pradhānāṅgatayā paścādupāṃśutvena bādhitaḥ 
etena sarve jyotiṣṭomavikārā vyākhyātāḥ /
va punaridānīṃ nānāveda kharasyāvakāśo bhaviṣyati /
uccate /
tadgrahaṇādā svadharmā syādadhikārasāmarthyāda vyaktaḥ śeṣe itivatkalpanīyaḥ yatprākṛtasvarāṅgayuktāyāṃ vikṛtau vedāntaroyamapūrvamaṅgaṃ codyataiti /
nanu tatrāpi guṇamukhyavyatikramanyāyena pradhānadharmabhāva eva /
evaṃ tarhi yā vikṛtiryaṃ sminceḍhe bhavati tasyāḥ śeṣeṣvaṅgeṣu yayāprakṛti prāpteṣu yattasminneva vedeṅgāntaramapūrvaṃ codyate sa vi ṣaya iti soṣi pradhānadvāra va javyatvāttadeva tarhi pradhānaṃ viṣaya iti na tasyāpi prakṛtāvaruddhatvānna tarhi pradhānadvāreṇāpūvaॅsyāṅgasya prāptiriti tadeva viṣaya iti naivamapi yaḥ pradhānasya dharmastasyaiva tatrāpi bhāvāt/
api ca tredhā vibhakteṣu yajñabhāgadharme ca khare sthite yadapūrvamapi tadbhāgapāti bhavati tasya na yūpāvaṭastarapaṇabastittvamiti bhavitavyameva prākṛtena dharmeṇa /
tasmādapi nāsti viṣayaḥ /
prakaraṇāmnānaṃ cātyanta mevānartha kaṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
syāt /
atra samādhiḥ upāṃśu yajuṣeti tāvatsarvadaviṃdo meṣvarthavahaksāmavedayorapi kāmyanaimittikeṣvaṅgeṣvarthavattā /
mandraṃ prātaḥmavanaityādi hi nityatvādanityaiḥ kāmyanaimittikairasaṃbadhyamānaṃ nityāṅgaviṣayameva bhavati /
tena yadṛgvedasāmavedābhyāṃ kiṃ ci kāmyaṃ naimittikaṃ vā codyate tatsarvamaccaiḥ karttavyam tathā taṃ bhinnamabhiṭaśedyate cida miśriṣa ityādi /
evaṃ yājurvedikamapyupāṃtvamudāharttavyam /
tathā yāni sutyottara kānānyaṅgāni teṣu savanagrahaṇābhāvādyathāvedameva svara ityavabhṛthasāmādīnāmapyuccaistvasiddhiḥ anyathā hi yatheṣṭaṃ prayogaḥ syād /
dīkṣaṇīyādiparisāmasuta prācīnamagnīṣomoyādityanenoṣāṃśutvaṃ prava rgyasāmnāṃ punaruccaiḥ pravarmyetyevamuccaimtvam /
ādhānamāmnāṃ tu yā jurvedika pradhāna vidhivicitatvādevopāṃśutvam /
ya evaṃ vidvā nvāmadevyaṃ gāyati ityādīni yajurvedavākyānyeva tasmādinadāharaṇam /
tatra ke cidāḥ /
svarūpotpattimātrāpekṣayā mena kriyataiti na kāraka hetvabhiprāyeṇopanyāsa iti /
tattu na yuktamevaṃ sati yutpattiviniyogabalābala cintaiva kriyate na gupā mukhya virodhacintā /
tatra ca viniyogādhīnatvādanuṣṭhānā taddanīyastvamityeṣa nirṇayaḥ syāt /
tasmātmāmaveda śākhāyāmapi kasyāṃ cidastyeṣāṃ vidhirata udāharaṇamityapare /
tadā tu yajurve ḍhapunaḥ śrutermandaṃ phalaṃ syāt /
athāpi śākhāntara vidhivadāśrīyeta svaravikalpaśca pūrvapakṣe kriyeta yadi udāhiyetānudāharaṇāttu naitadupapadyate /
tasmādutpatti viniyogayoreva gugāmukhyatvamityevamadhikaraṇamārabhyate yatra vedāntarotpannaṃ vasta vedāntareṇa viniyajyate tatra kimutpattivedadharmaḥ kartavyaḥ utta tantrakārtika /
viniyogave dadharma iti utpattiparvakatvādviniyogasyotpattivedadharma iti prāpte viniyogavedadharma iti gṛhyate/
kutaḥ /
utpattestadarthatvādvi niyujyamānasya ca svarāpekṣitvāttadānīmeva yaḥ svarovagamyate sa eva codito notpattisthastatkāle vidhānābhāvāt /
athavā naivātra vyatikramaśabdena bādho virodho vābhidhīyate kiṃ tarhi vyabhicāronyatrānyatra ca vṛttistenaivaṃ cintyate yatrotpa ttiviniyogau vyatikrāntau anyatrotpattiranyatra viniyogastatra kataravedasaṃyogo  bhavatviti /
tathaivotpattisaṃyoge vikalpe vā prāpte viniyogavedasaṃyogaḥ prādhānyādityuttaram /
atha vaivaṃ cintā yatrānyatra ca pradhānam anyatra cāṅgaṃ tatrāṅgasya kena vedena vyapradeśosviti /
tataśca tathaiva pradhānavedana vyapadeśa iti nirṇayaḥ /
asmiṃstu pakṣe tadgrahaṇādvā svadharmā syādityetadvādhitvā pradhānasamākhyāta eka eva prakṛta/
vikatau ca karttā prāpnoti /
aya tu codakabalīyasvāda ṅgaveda samā khyātakarṭa grahaṇaṃ tataḥ svaropi tathaivetyayuktaṃ pradhānasvaragrahaṇam /
ata utpattiviniyogāpekṣayaivaiṣa vicāra ityeṣaiva vyākhyā śobhanā /
tathaivādhānodāharaṇaṃ samarthitaṃ bhavati /
yadi tu guṇamukhya vyatikamoṅgapradhānadharma virodho vyākhyāyate tatoṅgaguṇavirodhe ca tādarthyādityanena mahāpaunaruktyaṃ saṃpraghāraṇīyam 
na śākhāntaravadyuktī vikalpa/
vedagocaraḥ /
tāḍheiko guṇārthe/
kaścideko vidhāyakaḥ /
sa tu jyotiṣṭomādo katama iti /
guṇānāṃ yatra bhūyastvamitikarttavyatātmakam /
tatra tenaiva niṅgena tasya kartavyateṣyate 
yadyamya gamakatvena svaśaktairavadhāritam /
tadatvaṃ bahu vā tasya pratītau na viśiṣyate 
tathe he tikarttavyatā liṅgatvenopanyastā mā yatrāpyalpā tatrāpi karttavyatayā vinā 'nupapadyamānā śaknotyeva gamayitum 
asaṃyuktaṃ prakaraṇāditika rttavyatāthitvāt 
evaṃ tāvat śrutiniṅgavākyāni pradhānajñeyasaṃkīrṇaviviktavi ṣayāṇi pratyudāharaṇaṃ vyākhyātāni/
tatra vidhiviniyogābhidhānātmikāyāḥ śruterviniyogasāmarthyātmakasya ca niṅgasya kevalapadaprayogābhāvātpadāntarasaṃnidheravaśyaṃbhāvitvādvākya mantargataprāyameveti na sākṣāgrahaṇena sūcitam /
athavā veḍho vā prāyadarśanādityapakramopasaṃhāravaśenaiva vedadharmatvāvadhāraṇādidameva vākyaviniyogasūtramiti na pūrvāntargatimātreṇa vākyasya viniyojakatvaṃ vyākhyeyam /
yattu bhāṣyakāreṇāruṇayetyaḍhāitaṃ śakyaṃ tatrāpyaindrīvattṛtīyā śrutireva viniyojita vaktatṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
m /
atha kriyāmācasaṃbandhe śrutyā kṛte viśeṣasaṃbandho vākyenetyabhiprāyaḥ sa aintryāmapi tulyaḥ /
tatrāpi cainyetyupasthātavyamātrāpekṣaṇādgāīpatyamiti ca sādhanamātrāpekṣitvāhiśeṣasaṃbandho vākyenaiva /
tasmādubhayatrāpi tadantargatiḥ śakyā darśayitumiti ubhayoḥ śrutivākyayorubhayamuḍhāharaṇam/
idānīṃ bacābakhacintā pratyāsannetyuttarāṇyapi trīṇi pramāṇāni svarūpeṇa viniyogasāmathryena ca darśayati /
tatra prakaraṇaṃ viniyogājñānasaṃśaya viparyayāṇāmanyatamenopanyasyati sma /
yāvaccānyatra kathyate nāvadajñānaṃ bhavati /
atha vāsadapi prasaṅgābhāvānnākhyātaṃ syāditi saṃdeho 'tha vā naivāttara śravaṇāttatmāmarthyānamaraṇakāṅgitayogyārthapadāntarasaṃnidhānebhyo 'nyaḥ śabdaprakārosti /
ta smānna prakaraṇādīni pramāṇāntarāṇīti prāpte 'bhidhīyate 
kramaśca deśasāmānyāt 
pūrvavadeva kramasamākhyayorapyajñānādibhirupanyāsaḥ karttavyaḥ 
vināpyanuṣṭhānadeśasāmyena yāvati pradeśe brāhmaṇe pradhānaṃ padyate māvatyeva mantreṣu mantra,stayoścāṅgāṅgyapekṣāvelāyāṃ yathāsaṃkhyatṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
nyāyena samānadeśatvādduddau sannidhānaṃ bhavati /
prathamasya ci pra dhānasya mantramanvicchannavaśyaṃ mantrasamāmnāyamādita jhāragyālocayati /
tataśca prathama eva mantraḥ prathamaṃ hṛdayamāgacchati/
na cāsyātikrame heturastīti sa eva gṛhyate /
tathā mantrasya śeṣaṇamapeca māṇasyānayaiva prakriyayā yena śeṣiṇā saha saṃbandho bha vati tataśca tannirākāṅkṣatayā dvitīyādīnāmapyevameva dvitīyādibhireva yogena bhavitavyam/
tatrāgneyādyanumantraṇānāmāgneyādiniṅgatvāttenāpi vyavasthā sidhyatītvavyaktaliṅgamupāṃśayājakramādhītaṃ dabdhirnāmāsītyudāharati /
nanu vākyaprakaraṇātmarvārthatvaṃ vijñāyate taca balīya ityanyatrāpi viniyogaḥ prāpnoti /
atra ke cidāṅaḥ /
upāṃśuyāja grahaṇāddayamapyanugṛhyate tasmāttadgrahaṇamiti /
śakyaṃ tu vaktuma anugrāhya eva kramaḥ prakaraṇapratyayaviruddhatvāditi /
śeṣasya hi sarvārthatve pratipradhānāvṛtteḥ prakaraṇāvagataṃ na śakyaṃ bādhitum /
tacaitāvaduttaraṃ bhavati yenye śeṣiṣṇa agneyādayaste viṣṭalaḥ kramaprakaraṇavadbhimantrānta rairavarudatvānnai namapekṣante /
na ca vikalpo'spaṣṭaciṅgatvena vaiṣamyād /
adṛṣṭārthānāṃ samuccaya iti cenna /
prakṛtayā gapratyavekṣaṇena dṛṣṭārthatvātsatyapi cādṛṣṭārthatve nirapekṣāṇāṃ gatvantare sati samuccayānāśrayaṇādāgneyādibhiḥ kṛtārthairupekṣitaḥ sannagatyā punasteṣveva bhavedasti cāsya gatirupāṃśuyāja iti /
kiṃ ca 
dabdhirnāmāsītya spaṣṭa liṅgoyam/
na ceḍaśaṃ santaṃ prakaraṇaṃ vi tantravārtika /
niyoktuṃ kṣamaṃ mama  tvasiśabdo yuṣmadarthaviṣayatvātmannicitamabhimukhaṃ vābhiṣatte nānya, mupāṃḍayājaśca sannihitobhimukhacetyabhidhānasāmadhyeṃ kramādupāṃśuyājaviṣayaṃ vijñāyate /
tataśca liṅgena prakaraṇaṃ bādhyata evetyadoṣaḥ /
kāmyayājyā kāṇḍa kramastu vyākhyāta evānuṣṭhānadeśakramopi paśudharmāṇāmagnīṣomīyārthatvena bhaviṣyati 
ādhvaryavādisamākhyānāṃ vedaetra prayoga iti na laukikatvacodyaṃ kriyate /
tatrādhvaryuvṛttamātramevāpekṣate kiṃ mayā kattaṃvyamiti/
tadapekṣamāṇasya ca yadi na kutaścidviśeṣo 'vagamyate tato yatkiñciditi bhaviṣyati /
tathādhvaryavasaṃjñitaṃ karma ko me karttā bhaviṣyatītyevameva śeṣamapekṣate /
tatra śabdajasyādita evaiṣotprekṣā pratyekaṃ bhavati yadasyādhvaryoḥ karma tadādhvaryavaśabdavācyaṃ bhaviṣyati /
tathāpyasyādhvaryavasya yaḥ karttā tasyādhvaryurnāmeti prakṛtervā vikārastadanurūpo'numīyate vikārāḍā prakṛtiḥ /
yadyapi śabdāntaraṃ vikāra ityubhāvapyeto parasparanirapekṣau ni tyasaṃbandhī ca tathāpi nityāyā eva śabdapravṛttarnityaḥ saṃbandho nimittamiti sarvayaugikānāmevamanvākhyānam /
na hi rājya śabdasyāpyādimatī pravṛttirityuktam /
nimittanaimittikabhāvastvanāditvepi śabdārthayorivedāviruddhaḥ /
tatra ke cihnadanti tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
prāgetasmātsamākhyā viniyogādadhvayrdhvādhvaryavayorasaṃbandhādaśakyaṃ yaugikatvaṃ samākhyayā vijñātum /
atha tu prathamaṃ siddhe saṃbandhe paścātmamākhyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ tato na samākhyā viniyojikā yādataḥ parasparanirapekṣayoreva rūḍhyoḥ sārūpyādupatiṣṭhamānayoreṣa viniyoga iti /
na tvetadyuktam /
na hi ruḍhānāṃ sārūghyādupasthāpanasāmarthyaṃ dharmasaṃbandhepyasti /
yathā kaṇvarathantare ra thantaradharmānnirākariṣyati kimutātra kriyākartṛsaṃbandhe pāvakāyudāharaṇaṃ vā yuktaṃ syāttasmād yaugikatvamevābhyupagantavyam /
yattu prāk prayogātpramāṇaṃ nāstīti satyaṃ pratyakṣaṃ nāstīti samākhyayaivānumīyamānaṃ bhaviṣyati/
ve hi prathamameva kriyākartṛsaṃbandho niṣpanastasminsati samākhyā pravṛttā vayaṃ tu taṃ saṃbandhaṃ pramāṇāntareṇāpratipādyamānāḥ samākhyādarśanena pratipadyāmace tena jñāyate pūrvaṃ samākhyā paścātlaṃbandha iti /
vastutastu prathamameva saṃbandhaḥ sa cāpratītopi sattāmātreṇaiva samākhyāṃ pravarttitavān yadi hyeṣādimatī syāttataḥ prayoktuḥ prathamaṃ saṃbandhāvagatyā bhavitavyam /
na ca sāna bhavatīti paryanuyujye mahi nitya saṃbandhāśrayaṇe /
nanu tatra nityaprayuktayā samākhyayā nūnaṃ kaścidasti saṃbandha iti pratipādite 'nyathānupapattyā śeṣaśeṣibhāvaḥ paścāhijñāyate tasmādyaugikyaiva samākhyayā viniyoga iti miṭṭama 
eka eva hyaruṇādiḥ śeṣaḥ śrutyā sāmānya kriyā saṃbandhī vā kyena tadviśeṣasya krayasya prakaraṇena jyotiṣṭomikasya satyapi vācanikaprakaraṇa samavāye parasparānugra inimittatvādavirodha iti bacāvalavicāro na bhavati nirviśeṣasāmānyānupapatteḥ /
kraya svarūpamātraprayuktatve cānarthakatvādapekṣite hi śrutivākyābhyāṃ vākyaprakaraṇe /
tasmātkarttavyaṃ virodhagra iṇamiti /
na vā karttavyam /
kutaḥ 
aruṇāḍhatāvacaiva pramāṇamamavāyosti /
na hokatra saṃbhava mātraṃ samavāyaḥ kiṃ tarhi viṣayaikatvama /
ica cāruṇasya kriyāsaṃbandhaḥ śrutvā tasya tu śrutikalpitasya kriyākāraka saṃbandhasya bhūyopyapekṣāvaśena krayaviṣayatvam /
tāvatā ca prayojanānavāpterapekṣāntare satyapūrvasaṃbandhavataḥ krayasya jyotiṣṭomārthatvamiti viṣayanānātvamataśca sarveṣāṃ viniyojakatvamaviruddham /
na cātra viprakṛṣṭagrahaṇe sannikṛṣṭasya bādho dṛśyate na hi krayaṃ gṛhṇayā kriyā saṃvandhaṃ bādhate nāpi jyotiṣṭome kurvankrayatṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīya pāda /
saṃbandham /
yatra tvekaḥ śeṣastāvāneva ca saṃbandhāntara virodhinaikena pramāṇenānyaśeṣyartho vijñāyate /
pareṇā taḍhavāghānupapattinā śevyantarārthaḥ /
eka saṃvandhaṃ ca kṛtārthasyākāṅkhābhāvātpunarviniyogāntarānupapattiḥ /
tatra pramāṇayoḥ parasparāpacāryasamānaviṣayatvajakṣaṇaḥ samavāyaḥ tathā yatra śeṣabhedapye kasminneva śeṣiṇi tulyopakāranibandhana ekena pramāyenānyaḥ śeṣaḥ sāghanatvena pratīyate anyenāparo na caika sādhitopakāraḥ śeṣī śeṣāntaramapecate tatrāpyeka viṣayāpacāritvātsamavāyaḥ sa ca virodha evaṃ sati bhavatīti samavāyagrahaṇenaiva siddho virodhaḥ /
yatra punaḥ spaṣṭa eva śetrabhedo yathā samidho yajatotyādiṣu yatra vā tasyaiva kiṃ cidādhikyaṃ bhavati yathā'ruṇāyāṃ vyākhyātam tathā yatra śeṣibhedo yathāgneyādiṣvaṣṭākapālādīnāṃ yatra vā tadgatamādhiyaṃ yathā darśapūrṇamāmāṅgānāmevopakārabhedastatrāpi viṣayānyatvādamamavāya iti /
yacca śrutvā vi niyujyate yacca samākhyayā tatsarvaṃ tulyaṃ yastu sarvāṅgajanya ekaḥ pradhānopakāraḥ tatraiṣāmaparyāya vidhānādekameva pramāṃṇaṃ śeṣatvaṃ ceti vyāpārabhedādasamavāyaḥ /
tathā yatra sa eva śeṣastasminneva śeṣiṇi sannikṛṣṭena viprakṛṣṭena ca pramāpona viniyujyate tatrāpyekasyaiva pramāṇatvenetarasya prayojanātarārthatvādasamavāya iti /
tasmādvirodhaviṣayameva samavāyagrahaṇam /
tatra paṇāmapi ekacaiva balāvale kathayatavye kramavarttitvāhāco yugapadaśaktareka kasya saṃpradhāraṇā/
yattu dvitīyopādānaṃ tatpratiyoginā vinā baccābacakathanāśaktatenocyate iyoīyoriti /
ekārthavarttitvādāca ityasyāparā vyākhyā / nantravārtika /
yeyaṃ bantābanavāgeṣā pratyekaṃ śrutyādiṣu samavaiti na samudāye /
tāni hi śeṣaviniyogenārthavanti na balābanamatastasyāḥ pratipradhānavṛttitvādayogapaścai nai kekasya saṃpradhāraṇāyāṃ karttavyāyāṃ dvitīyopādānavirodhavacābalabāghānāṃ pratiyoginyanupapattiṃ darśayitumasaṃbhavād dayodayoḥ saṃpradhāraṇetyuktam /
taka ka dvayordvayoḥ /
paccabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ saha vicāre karttavye yadekekena saha kriyate tahādhitabādhyasya bādhakabādhakena bādhasya sujñānatvādyāni hi śrutibādhyainiṅgādibhirvādhyante tāni śrutvā bādhyantetarā miti na tathā saha saṃpradhārayiṣyante /
tatra prathamaṃ tāvalamaprāptaṃ śrutiliṅgayoḥ saṃpradhāraṇamiti /
kimihodāharaṇāmiti /
kevalapaढ़prayogābhāvātmarvatra vākyatve sati na śrutiniṅgayoḥ svasāmarthyā tireko lakṣyate iti manyamānamya praśnaḥ /
vakṣyamāṇavivekābhiprāyeṇecainyā gārhapattyamupatiṣṭhata iti kimindrasyaivopasthānaṃ ka rttavyamutendrasya gāīpatyasya vā 'tha vā samuccitayoratha vā gāīpatyasyaiveti /
yadi liṅgaṃ banīyastata indropasthānamatha tulyabannatvaṃ virodhaśca tato vikalpotha tulyavanatveṣyavirodhastataḥ samuccayo 'tha virodhaḥ śrutivanjoyastvaṃ ca tato gārhapatyasyaivopasthānamiti /
yattu siddhavadgāīpatyārthatvāṅgīkaraṇena vacanāttvayathārthamaindrī syādityuktam tadiha sthāpayiṣyamāṇaśrutibalīyatvābhiprāyeṇa /
tenaiva sarvavākyatvābhiprāyeṇa śrutiliṅgerthe vā kyatvambhrāntyā punaḥ pṛcchati/
kā punaratra śrutiḥ kiṃ liṅgamiti /
tatrottaraṃ gārhapatya śabdaśravaṇaṃ mantramāmathrthyaṃ ceti /
paraḥ punarāha/
yadyevaṃvidhapadasamūhātmake śrutiliṅge hanta tarhi vākyaṃ nāma na kiṃ cidapyasti /
taducyatām atha vākyaṃ nāma kimiti /
siddhāntavādī tu tathaiva śakyavivekajñānatvaṃ manyamāna āha /
saṃhatyārthamabhidadhati padāni vākyamiti /
yadyapi ca na saṃhatānāṃ kathidekobhidheyastathāpi gamyamānābhiprāyeṇoktam /
atha vaikaca kṣyamāṇārthaprayuktatayā saṃghātatvamāpāditāni yadā svārthamabhidadhati tadā tadbhūtānyeva santi vākyatvaṃ pratipadyantaiti /
yadyevaṃ tata ubhayorapyudāhṛta yormantrabrāhmaṇayorvākya lakṣaṇayogāt vākyayoriyaṃ saṃpradhāraṇā na śrutiliṅgayoriti /
yadi vāvaṇyaṃ śrutiṅgiyorvirodhaḥ samarthanīyaḥ tataḥ śrutiliṅgavākyāni lakṣaṇato vivektavyānīdaṃ nāma teṣāṃ parasparamantaramiti /
tadabhidhīyate 
nanu sāmarthya pūrvakatvāduktividhiviniyogānāmaindryā gāīpatyamityatrāpi śabdamāmarthyamasti /
kadā cana starīrasītyatrāpi cendrābhidhānamitya viśeṣa eva śrutiliṅgayoḥ prāpnoti /
tathā hi 
satyamubhayatrobhayamapyasti /
kiṃ tvendryāṅgāīpatyasya noktibhaktyāvagamyate /
indrāṅgatvamatiścāsyā nāścaraśrutikāritā 
yo hi yasyābhidhānāya śakta ityavagamyate /
viniyoge 'pyasai/
śakto na hyaśakto niyujyate 
ekatrāsati sāmarthya mantraḥ śeṣobhidhīyate /
anyatrānuktaśeṣatvaṃ sāmathyeṃ saṃpratīyate 
arthaṃ prati na sāmathyaṃ na ca śeṣatvamucyate /
kevalaḥ padasaṃghātaḥ pratyakṣamupannabhyate santravārtika /
liṅgatvamabhyupetaṃ cedindropasthāna kalpane/
ubhayatrāpi vākyatvaṃ kathaṃ bhūyovakalpate 
yathā śoghrapravṛttitvāliṅgāderbādhikā śrutiḥ /
tathaiva viniyogepi saiva pūrvaṃ pravarttate 
ka cidyasya pramāṇatvaṃ khaśaktairavadhāritam /
na hyanyāpekṣayā tasya sā bhaktirapagacchati 
bādhastu yadi kalpyeta viparītaḥ prasajjate /
na hi pūrvamavādhitvā pareṣāṃ janma labhyate 
tyādinasamartha viniyogovakalpate /
na sāmarthyādirūpaṃ syādekavākyādibhirvinā 
viniyoklo śrutistāvatsarveṣveteṣu saṃmatā /
dhostasyāḥ sannikarṣeṇa viprakarṣeṇa ca sthitā 
nāpecā yasya yatrāsti sa tasmāinnavānbhavet /
yaḥ parādhīnavṛttiḥ sa taddādhaṃ kathamācaret 
na śruteviniyoktṛtvaṃ niṅgādhīnaṃ pratīyate /
vijñāte viniyoge tu tadvaśācchakti nirṇayaḥ 
viśepo yāvatā liṅge syāt śruteranumāpake /
liṅgānumānabhūtāyāṃ tāvataiva śrutāvapi 
viniyogābhidhānasya dūratvā hurbalatvadhīḥ /
tacca pūrvānumāyāṃ syānnottaratra kathaṃ cana 
ekaḍi cicatuḥ pañca vastvantaraṇakaritam /
śrutyarthaṃ prati vaiṣamyaṃ liṅgādīnāmapīṣyate 
vācaka nai kavākyatvādihātahācināṃ satām /
kalpayitvābhidhāśaktiśrutiḥ paścātprakalapyate 
samudāyo ci viniyujyamāno nāvayavānaviniyujya vini yoktuṃ śakyate /
tatra pūrvottarayorbhāgayorekavākyatvaṃ pratyaścam naikārthābhidhānasāmathyeṃ, bhinnārthābhidhānasāmarthyaṃ tvārthaṃ pratyayadarśanātsivam/
tatra samudāyāvayava viniyogāya vākyasāmarthyayoḥ saha prasthitayorasamarthaviniyogāsaṃbhavādyāvadvākyena pūrvo bhāga uttarārthābhidhānasamartha uttaro vā pūrvasamartha ityanumoyate tāvatpratyeka bhāgavartinā sāmathryena parvasyāpi svārthe para sthāpi svārthe śrutiranumitā tataśca yāvaditaratra viniyojikā śrutyanumānāya prayatyate tāvadiha viniyoge siddhe nirākā satvātprakaraṇāmnānamya na kaścidapi hetuḥ śrutyanumānaityanupajātamūlo viniyogo bādhyate /
mantrasyāpi hi pūrvasya pūrvacāthe śogha viniyoga uttarasya cireṇa /
tathottarottarasya śīghra pūrvasya tatra cireṇa /
śoghraviniyuktaśca mantraściraviniyogamādriyate /
tathārthopi prathamāvagatamantrāvarudbo netaraṃ gṛhṇāti /
svapradhānye ca saṃbhavati na paropasarjanatvaṃ pratipadyate tasmāliṅgaṃ bacīya iti bhittvā vākyaṃ viniyoga iti /
nanvevaṃ sati nirvapāmotyādinā lṛptasāmarthyena śīghutaraprāptenāvaruddherthe vi prakṛṣṭaprāptānāṃ devasya tvetyādīnāṃ bādhādaviniyogaḥ prāpnoti /
na caiṣāṃ bhinnaprayojanatvātmama cayastathā satyekavākyatvābhāvā, davaṇyaṃ caitairyathā kathaṃ cinnirvāpa eva prakāśayitavyaḥ nānyaprakāśanaṃ karmānaṅgatvaprasaṅgāt /
ataḥ samānatantravārtika /
viṣayatvātmamavāye sati vākyaprāpyapadāntarabādhena bhavitavyamiti /
anrocyate 
yāni hyasamavetārthavacanāni tāni yadi svatantrī kriyante tatonarthakāni bhavanti /
tena laprasaṃbandhairnirākāṅkṣīkṛtopyartha itareṣāṃ sākāitvātpunastatprakāśayatvaṃ pratipadyate /
yathā prakaraṇapūritānāmapi krameṇa punastadurmaprāptirbhavati /
yathā prakṛtau nirākāṅkṣībhūtā dharmā vikṛtīniyanti tathā ca lṛpta vyākhyātam /
tasmādevamādonyapi saṃbaśyante /
yeṣāṃ tu prakāśyorthaḥ samaveto dṛśyate teṣāmanabhidheyenāsaṃbadhyamānānāmapyarthavattāstīti nānarthakya nimittamavakāśaṃ labhante /
sarveṣāmeva ca vādīnāmānarthakyapratitānāṃ durbalairapi rāyatvamiṣyate /
tadyathā brahmādīnāṃ prokṣaṇādīn prati śrutvā śeṣitvaṃ prāpnuvadddhyatilaṅghya prakaraṇanabhyāpūrva sādhanatvakṛtaḥ saṃbandho bhaviṣyati /
tato 'vasthitavākyāṅgisya balīyastvam /
tathā ca bhavānuvāke darśitam /
vākyaprakaraṇayoḥ prakaraṇamarthaviprakarṣāddurbalam /
tathā hi /
pratyakṣā saṃgatirvākye na ca prakaraṇe tyasaiau /
ko 'numātavyā tākā viprakṛṣṭatā 
ākāṅkṣātaḥ prabhṛtyekaṃ śrutyarthaṃ prati gacchati /
nāmapi tvanyato labdhvā śrutirekasya kalpyate 
tāhi yatmākṛtāṅgamadhyapātitvena notyannaṃ tatparatātparastādvā avasthitakramabhāgbhavati /
prakāraṇasya klṛptopakāraiḥ prākṛtai vyavarttitatvāttatra yannivṛttākāisya kasya citsamīpe padyate 'nyasya cākāṅkṣā tatastadubhābhyāṃ gṛhyamāṇaṃ yāvat kramavato nivṛttama satomākāṅkṣāmupajanayati tāvatprakaraṇāvatā sadhaikavākyatāṃ gacchati yāvacceta rakavākyatā bhavati raniṃ pratyupakāra sāmarthyakaccanā /
yāvaditaratrāsau tāvadakṣa śrutyanumānaṃ yāvaditaraca śrutiranumāsyate tāvadica siddhe viniyoge 'numānavījacīnanāśruti sarvamapramāṇībhavati 
netadevam 
arthānāṃ prathamaṃ kena citprakāreṇānavagatasaṃbandhānāṃ samā khyā pravarttate /
sā ca śeṣaśeṣitvaṃ tāvannaiva pratipādayati kena citmaṃbandhenopapadyamānatvātsaṃbandhamātramapi naivābhidhatte /
nahi yaugikaiḥ saṃbandhobhidhīyataityuktam /
samākhyā 'nyathānupapacyā 'numīyate saṃvandhamānasya caitadrūpaṃ kiṃ cidabhinnameṣāmastotyavagamaḥ tataścāpannaṃ kramājjaghanyatvam /
na hi kiṃ cittatra sāmānya manumātavyaṃ deśasāmānyasya pratyakṣatvāt iha tu tatyadasyāpratyakṣatvādānumānikatva miti viprakarṣaḥ /
sa mākhyā hi yāvatkiṃ citmāmānyamastīti kalpayati tāva krameṇa nūnamanayoḥ kā ciḍhapekṣāsti yenetyaṃ samānadeśī pa ṭhitāviti prakaraṇaṃ kalapyate /
yāvacca kiṃ citmāmānyamapecā kalpayati tāvaditaracaikavākyatā klṛptā tathā yāvadiaareer bhavati tāvaditaracopakāra sāmarthyasiddhiḥ /
yāvavedopakārasāmarthya kalpanā tāvadinaregā śrutirutpāditā  /
tataśca yāvadica śrutimanumātumupakramate tāvaditaratra vi niyoge siddhe nirākāhībhūte prakaraṇapāṭhe sarvametatpracitamapyaripakavicchedādāma sadhyamiva nūnaṃ nirvāṇaṃ bhavati /
tasmādarthaviprakarṣāta paraṃ paraṃ bādhyataiti siddham āha ca 
ekamopānava ko bhūmiṣṭhāparastayoḥ /
ubhayośca javastulyaḥ pratibandhaśca nāntarā 
tena yadyapi sāmathyaṃ pratyekaṃ siddhamanyadā /
tathāpi yugapagāve jaghanyasya nirākriyā 
tasmātraitadālambanaṃ yuktaṃ yat ka ciduttareṣāṃ prāmāṇya mi ṭaṃ tasmāilavadvirodhepi tena bhavitavyamiti /
yattu pramāṇābhāso bādhyate na pramāṇamiti tatra brūmo 'yamapi pramāṇābhāsa eva /
katham 
na hi yatra viṣaye bādhastatraiṣāṃ pramāṇatvam/
kiṃ tarhi prade śāntare kevanānāmupanaścitaṃ sāmānyato dṛṣṭarūpeṇācāpi pratibhāti /
tattu bannīyasā 'pahṛtaviṣayatvātmīdatīti paścā bhrāntitvenādhyavasauyate /
atha vā yastatrāsya vyāpāra āmī tamihāpi prakramataeva /
sa tu javavatānyena viṣaye 'pahate mūlacchedādyadā taṃ na gacchati tatkiṃkriyatāṃ tena bhu gatṛṣṇāḍhivadevāprāpya pramāṇameva bādhyate /
anutpannameva ceha śrutyabhāvāccheṣajñānaṃ bāpyate āntarānikajñāna mithyātvakampanayeti notpattisāmānyena tulcabalatvamataśca jñānasaṃkatantravārtika /
rocchedanādirūpo bādho naivāśaṅkitavyaḥ /
yo 'pi co tpannavādhaḥ tamapi phanlaviyogātmanopapādayiṣyāmaḥ /
evaṃ tāvad dvayordvayorbirodhe varṇitam arthasiddhatvāttu bhāṣyakāraṇetaraiḥ saha na pradarśitaṃ vyākhyādabhistvevaṃ prapañcayitavyam /
yathā śrutivākyayorvirodhe aruṇādirvākyasāmarthyādānantaryasāmānādhikaraṇyāgyā meka cāyanyā diśeṣatvaṃ prāpnuvattṛtīyā śrutyā krayasaṃbandhitvena vijñāyate dvitīyasopānabhūgatārohakayoriva chātra yāvadvākyaṃ sāmarthya kalpayati tā vacchrutyā viniyogaḥ kalpita iti mahadantaram /
śrutiprakaraṇayorvi rodhe prakaraṇāde kaviṃśatyādyanuvacanānāṃ darśapūrṇamāsāṅgale prāpte śrutyaiva pratiṣṭhākāmādiṣu puruṣārthāvadhāraṇātprakaraṇabādhaḥ /
anuvacanānāṃ ca kriyātmakatvāditikarttavyatāmṛpatvātprakaraṇagrāhyatvena tadvirodhodāharaṇatvaṃ timra eva sānhasyopasado dvādaśāhīnasyeti tu dvādaśavasyākriyātvāḍha nitikarttavyatā sati kathaṃbhāvarūpaprakaraṇagrāhyatvānapapatteḥ sannidhimātreṇa prakaraṇākalapanāpūrvaka saṃbandhādhyavasānācchu tisthāna birodhodāharaṇatvaṃ yuktamityeke /
ta na naivamāśritam /
kutaḥ 
itikarttavyatāṃśasthāṃ yenoddiśyopasatkriyām /
hāḍhaśatva vidhistena kathaṃbhāvena gṛhyate 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
tāvatpratyakṣayā śrutyā ṣaṇyaṃ hīnāṅgatāṃ gatā /
neva hyahargaṇādanyadahānyādīnamacyate 
etapaparitryāṇaśeṣo hi ramanā śrutā /
saha dharmenasā yāti krameṇa paśuśeṣatām 
ākāṅkṣāmātramevaikaṃ yāvatkalpayati kramaḥ /
dūreṇa tāvadaprāptāṃ ramanāṃ harati śrutiḥ 
vacanāttvayathārthamendrī syāditivat balavattaraśrutikṛta viniyoga kalpita jaṇādāṇāgnīṣomīyāṅgatvādevaṃ hyāda 
anādiśrutvā liṅgenotkṛṣyamāṇā manotā vāritā dvidevatye 'pyekadaivatyaiva na kevanāgni daivatyatvenāgnīṣomīyāduttāraṇīyetyarthaḥ /
yadvaivakāraṃ svasthānādapanīya yathākramaṃ kāryaivetyatra saṃyojanā kāryavyavadhāryate /
liṅga samākhyāvirodhe tu bhakṣānuvāke grahaṇādivākyāni samākhyānācāṅgatvena saṃbandhasāmānyādikalpanayā bhakṣāṅgatva viniyogāya prasthitāni liṅgena grahaṇāvekṣaṇasamyakkarahyeṣu viniyujyantaiti sthitam /
