yā jyāsamākhyābādhena ca manohacāṃ pṛthupājavatyośca liṅge'na sāmidhenītvena viniyoga ityuktam /
vākyakramayorvirodhe tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
parivyāṇakaraṇakriyamāṇānuvādiparivīra siparivītapadavyatiriṛpadānāṃ yuvā suvāsā śrāgāt sa u śreyānityevamādīnāṃ liṅgaviniyukta parivītapaढ़kavākyatvātmavanīyaparivyāṇe viniyogaḥ /
vākya samākhyayorvirodhaṃ bhavānuvāka eva sadhyāsamityevamādiṣu grahaṇādā viniyujyamāneṣu tadekavākyagataśeṣapaḍhāvṛttiruḍhāharttavyā 
śrutisamākhyā virodhe vājapeyaḥ samākhyānātprāpnotyadhvaryu karttṛkaḥ /
tyā svārājyakāmasya tathādhvaryornirākriyā 
pūrve syonaṃ taityādi sadane sābhighāraṇe /
vākyenāṅgatayā prāptaṃ liṅgācchuddhe 'bhidhāraṇe /
tasminsodetyayaṃ vākyātprāptaḥ śeṣo 'bhidhāraṇe /
liṅgāttu sadanasyaiva tatraivātaḥ prayujyate 
ekasminneva mārge tu yatsaṃkīrṇacatuṣṭayam /
bhāṣa bhāṣyakāreṇa vivektavyaṃ tadātmanā 
tathā paśvaṅga mekatvaṃ padaśrutyā pratīyate /
samāna pratyayaśrutyā bannīyasyā kriyāṅgatā /
tathā dhātvartha karmatve pāda bhāvanāyā vidhiśrutyā puruṣārthasya mādhyatā 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
durbalasya pramāṇasya banavānāśrayo yadā /
tadāpi viparītatvaṃ śiṣṭākope yathoditam 
tathā ca loka /
atyantabalavantopi paurajānapadā janāḥ/
durbalairapi bādhyante puruṣaiḥ pārthivāśritaiḥ 
tatra tulyavanatvoktiḥ svataḥ prāmāṇya vibhramāt /
pradeśāntaradṛṣṭaṃ ca rūpaṃ tulyaṃ dvayorapi 
na hi vijñānasya vijñānasya ca viśeṣa upalabhyataiti/
mantrāmnānave lāyāmindrārthatvaṃ jātaṃ śrutyuccāraṇakālepi gārhapatyārthatvamityuktayorcavyātmanora viśi ṭatvam /
na hyavijñātarūpo mantraḥ śrutyā śakyo viniyoktumiti śrutyā prathamaṃ rūpanirūpaṇaṃ kartavyamataśca tadavadhāraṇavelāyāmindropasthānapratyayo jāto na śakyo nivarttayitumiti manyate /
manu siṅgasya bhaṅgurasyeva rūpaṃ sabicikitso hoti /
śrutau dṛśyamānāyāmanumānāsaṃbhavāgaṅguratvaṃ savicikitso hi tvimaṃ viśvepajanmatvānna hyasya svataḥ prāmāṇya mityabhiprāyaḥ paraḥ punaḥ pratyatannavārtike /
yotpādanamai kāntikaṃ gṛhītvā savicikitsatvaṃ saṃdehaviparyayānadhyavasāyānāmanyatamaṃ manyamāna āha 
itarastu svābhipretamevaṃ savicikitsatvaṃ gṛhītvā caivaṃ ca sati naiva liṅgaṃ nāma kiṃ citpramāṇamabhaviṣyaditi /
siddhāntavādī tu vadati yadi sa viśveṣapratyayotpādanamātreṇa kupitaṃ liṅgaṃ prāmāṇyameva muñcati kāmaṃ mā bhūtpramāṇaṃ bhavati tu saṃbhayo liṅgaparijñāteṣvarthe dhvati 
kathaṃ vā liṅga parijñātatvaṃ siddhavaḍhabhidhoyate /
neṣa doṣo liṅgaparijñātatvaṃ tāvadavirodhavejābhiprāyaṃ saṃdigdhatvaṃ virodhavelāyām 
yadavirodhakāle liṅgasyāvagataṃ viniyojakatvaṃ tanna tathaiva sarvatraivāvatiṣṭhate kiṃ tarhi saṃdihyate anyatrāvirodhādviniyogoṅgokṛtaḥ sa iha kiṃ tathaiva bhavatyatha kena ciyāvarttivyataiti /
yadi vā vispaṣṭamevāprāmāṇya miti tāvadeva saṃdeho bhavati /
yāvatpratyakṣā śrutirdevalabhyate tasyāṃ tu satyāmitara kalpanānupapatteraprāmāṇyam 
na cānuktasya kriyāyāṃ prāmāṇyamasti /
yathā satyapi mā madhye viprarājanyau na vaiśyastomaṃ kurutaḥ tasmānna liṅgaṃ vinitṛtīyādhyāpasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
yojakamiti /
parastu virodhaviṣayamaprāmāṇyābhiṣānamajñātvā sārvatrikramevedamuktamiti bhītaḥ prāmāṇyamārgaṃ darśayati /
prakaraṇavato 'rthasya sannidhāne yamarthamāmanantīti tadetadapi vā prayogasāmarthyānmantrobhidhānavācī syādityanā viśiṣṭastu vākyārtha ityatra varṇitam /
atha vā siddhāntavādināpi virodhe sukhataramapramāṇatvaṃ vacyāmīti manyamānena prathamaṃ svatantrameva māvadaprāmāṇyaṃ darśitam /
tathā ca kṛte svayamevaitasya śrutyanumānadvāraprāmāṇya kalpanamāpatsyate 
tadyathopadeśātideśābhyāṃ prayājādyupakārasya prakṛtivikṛtyarthatvādavirodhaḥ sakucca tasyāmakṛtkaraṇe'pi pradhānānurodhana guṇānuvṛtteḥ sarvatreṣṭatvādindraśabdasya gārhapatye gauṇatvāḍhavayava prasiddhevendra mukhyatvātsamudāyaprasiddhervirodha iti cenna /
prayogabhedena parihārādyugapadupadiśyamānaṃ hyetatsaṃbhavāsaṃbhavāśrayādvirudhyate 
mantroyaṃ gāīpatyāṅga śabdenaivābhidhīyate /
indrāṅgatvaṃ tu sāmathyādaśabdamanumīyate 
parastu sārvatrikameva stiṅgasyāśābdatvamuktamiti manyamāno na tarhi virodhādvāghaḥ kiṃ ta tantravārtika /
rhāpramāṇatvādeveti vivakṣanyadyevamityāha /
siddhāntavādī tu yathā prathamaṃ pūrvapaścavādinā liṅgasya prāmāṇyamuktamāsīttathedānīṃ svayaṃ pratipādayati /
bhavati hi prakaraṇādeṣortho yathā śaknu yāttathā yāgasyānenopakuryāditi/
na ca svārthābhidhānā  danya thā śaknotyasāvupakarttumiti tatra viniyogasvodito bhavati/
parastu madīyamevāyaṃ pūrvoktaṃ mārgamāyātaḥ kedānoṃ gamiṣyatītyutmāhenāca /
yadi śrutimū na śrutyantareṇa bādhituṃ śakyaḥ tena yadi tāvadaśābdoyamarthastato naiva pramāṇam/
atha śābdastatastulyabala iti /
siddhāntavādī tu iyamapi pariharati nāpīti anumānikyāḥ śruteravirodhe satyātmanābho virodhe cānutpādādyatra hi pratyakṣā śrutyā mantro na viniyogaṃ prati nirākāśīkṛta stanāsya viniyogasihyarthaṃ yāvatkalapyate tatsarvamāmnānānyathānupapattimu drāmudritatvādvaidikaṃ bhavati 
sarvacaiva vikalpānāmanyāyyatvamavasthitam /
pakṣe hi sadasadbhāvāvekatrārthe durāśrayai 
śrutyā catra nirākāī mantraprakaraṇe kṛte /
liṅgaṃ sākāṅkṣasādhyārthaṃ tayaikāntāhirudhyate 
sūtreṇa paradaurbalye sūtrite sati bhāṣyakṛt /
ārthaṃ pūrvavalīyastvaṃ vyācaṣṭe tadanādarāt 
tatra yadi vākyaṃ balīyastato maitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyetyātmani ca praiṣāsaṃbhavādbotā yajedatha tu liṅgaṃ balīyasto mantreṇa maitrāvaruṇo niyoktavyaḥ 
sāmānyasamākhyayā pūrvamayaṃ hotureva prāpitaḥ sanvākyena bādhita ā sottadyadā vākyaṃ liṅgena bādhyate tadā samākhyayaiva pratiprasūtathā choṭakarṭakatvaṃ vijñāyate 
yadi hi maitrāvaruṇaḥ prathyettataḥ praśāstuśabdo hotaryanarthakaḥ syāt 
atra brūmaḥ/
sarvathā tāvadanayoranyatarasya virodhe gauṇatvaṃ kalpanīyam /
tatra praśāsṭaśabdasya hotaryatyantamanimittaḥ prayogo hoṭaśabdasya tu choṭakāryāpannamaitrāvaruṇesti nimittam /
sarvaeva pradhānaviṃgvacanāstatpuruṣeṣu prayujyamānā dṛṣṭā na tu viparyayaḥ /
tasmātpraśāstaliṅgatvānmantrastameva viniyuñjīta/
na caitadvākyamatyantamanarthakameva bhavati praiṣāntareṣu caritārthatvādatosminviṣaye bādhyeteti 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
bhinne ete yato vākye purastātpratipādite /
tasmānna samudāyoyaṃ vākyena viniyujyate 
naivātra sakalena vākyena saha vicāraḥ kiṃ tahaśenaiva sahātha vā 
tamminsodetyetatkṛtaṃ sākāṅkṣatvamāśrityaikavākyatvenodāhatamidameva pradhānakāraṇaṃ śakyate tadaśena yatheṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeghyabhāvaṃ kalpayitvaikārthatvenaikavākyatvam /
tadyathā pūrvasyatāvaduttareṇa saha yadakṣaṃ ghṛtasya dhārayā sumukhaṃ tava sadanaṃ kalpayāmi tasminnevamitikarttavyatā ke pratitiṣṭha tvamitītikarttavyatāviśiṣṭapuroḍāśapratiṣṭhāpanamekaṃ prayojanam /
atha vā puroḍāśapratiṣṭhāpanaphalaṃ sadanābhighāraṇaṃ karomītyevaṃ viśiṣṭaphalasadanakaraṇaṃ prakāśanaṃ prayojanamiti śakyamekavākyatvam /
yatta purastādarthanānātvānnānāvākyatvamuktaṃ tadiha sthitaṃ liṅgabalīyastvena yadi hi liṅgaṃ bannīyastataḥ saṃbhavadanyatara viśeṣaṇatvenaikavākyatvaṃ parityajyobhayoḥ pratyekaṃ svaprādhānyaṃ liṅgāvagatamāśritya viśeṣaṇa va dvitiraskāreṇa prayojanabhedādā kyabhedo bhavati tenāyaṃ viniyogadvāre vākyātmanābhasya liṅgaprādhānyasyāca  balābajavicāraḥ tatrāpi pratīto labdhātmaka vākye sati bādhakapratyayasada sadbhāvavicāra iti draṣṭavyam /
kiṃ prāptam /
tulyabale iti /
tadā cedṛśaṃ karma kadā cidvibhajya mantrī prayoktavyau /
kadā citsamudāyonyataratra kadā citma evobhayatreti 
sarvathā yadi pramāṇata evamavagamyate kinno bādhyate 
yonādiḥ kalpayāmyantaḥ svasāmathryena śakyate /
nirākāṅkṣaḥ svakāryāya sākāitvaṃ parāśrayam 
na ca parasyaitena vinānarthakatvāpattiryatastadbhayena nīyate sopi ci pratiṣṭhāpanāṅgatvenārthavān bhaviṣyati /
yadyapi ca tacchabdaḥ pūrvā pekṣastathāpi prakāśitaṃ nivṛttañca pūrvavākyārthamālocya bhinasyāpi pravartamānasya na kaścidirodhaḥ 
kiṃ punaḥ prakaraṇaṃ nāmeti /
sarvatra siddhavatprakaraṇena vyavahāro na caitatka cinnirūpitapūrvaṃ tadidāpi tāvadasya svarūpaṃ nirūpyata nirjñāta svarūpasya hi balābalaṃ sujñāyataitya, tha vā naivāsya vākyakramābhyāṃ bhedaḥ sākāipadasannidhimātraṃ hi vākyami tyucyate tacca prakaraṇe'pyaviśiṣṭam 
kaḥ punarārthaviprakarṣa iti /
samākhyāyāmantarṇītasaṃbandhasaṃbandhyabhidhāyitvāna saṃbhavatīti manyate /
nirjñāta prakaraṇe na kenāpi sakavākyatve iti /
prakaraṇāvirodhinaṃ kramaviniyogaṃ kevala samākhyā pratiyogitvena ca darśayati /
kathaṃ punaḥ prakaraṇaṃ na virudhyate /
yadā tena sarvārthatvaṃ jāyamānamutsṛjya kramavaśena kevalasānāyyārthatvaṃ vijñāyate /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
yadi prakṛte vayaṃ kramaviniyogamabhyapagacchema tata evaṃ svādiha tu prakaraṇenatantravārtika /
darśa pūrṇamāsānyatarārthatve 'vadhārite tadviśeṣākāṅkṣāyāṃ kevala eva kramo vyāpriyataitvavirodhaḥ /
nanu sarvārthatvenāvadhāraṇadyataḥ kutaścidapi nivṛttau prakaraṇaṃ bādhyate /
na cāvaṇyaṃ sarvārthatvaṃ prakaraṇenāvadhāryaṃte mantrasyaikenāpi saṃbadhya kṛtārthatvātprakaraṇināṃ ca mantrāntarairapyarthasiddheḥ /
sāmānyaviniyogaśrutimātrameva ceha kramātpūrvataraṃ niṣpadyate /
tatra yāvadviśeṣa śrutimekaikaṃ pratikalpayati tāvat krameṇāpi kalpitaiveti prākaraṇako viśeṣaśruti rupasaṃdriyate /
samākhyā punaḥ kramaviparītārthatvādvirudhyate/
viprakarṣācca durbalā sarvodi saṃbandhaḥ kena cidavāntara sāmānyena bhavati/
na ca mantrapuroḍāśayostahadaklṛptaṃ kiṃ cidasti /
yathā sānnāyyena saha deśa sāmānyam /
lokikastu śabdaḥ samākhyeti bhakṣānuvāke parihatamapi sahedikasaṃbandhaviprakarṣārthamupanyasyate /
parastu liṅgānirākaraṇoktenaiva mārgeṇa mūnotkarttanenaiva samākhyāṃ nirākṛtāṃ manyamāna ā cha /
yadyevamityādi /
siddhāntavādī tu bhakṣānuvākoktamevottaraṃ darśayati /
yadi hyaṅgāṅgibhāvotra puruṣapratyayābhavet /
tataḥ syādapramāṇatvaṃ sa tu vaidika eva naḥ 
bādhikaiva śrutirnityaṃ samākhyā bādhyate sadā /
madhyamānāṃ tu bādhyatvaṃ bādhakatvamapekṣayā 
bāghasyoktaprakāratvātpraśnastāvanna yujyate /
sthite cāprāptabādhatve prāptabādhopi nottaram 
pūrvaṃ paramajātatvādabādhitvaiva jāyate parasthānanyathotpāḍhānna tvabādhena saṃbhavaḥ 
na bādhasyaikarūpatvameṣitavyaṃ niyogataḥ /
na kiṃ ciḍiruṇadvī nānārūpyaṃ pramāṇavat 
kathamiti śrutyādivecacaṇyavismitasya praśnaḥ /
uttaramāi sāmānyasya kāraṇasya vidyamānatvāditi /
darśitametad brāhmaṇapra tantravārtika /
kṛtivacchandayoḥ /
yattu prāptasya jñānasyānutpādoccheda saṃskāravicchedānāmaśakyatvānnāsti bādhanamiti /
tatrāha naiva nivarttate kiṃ tarhi mithyājñānametaditi pratyayāntaraṃ bhavatīti /
śākhāntaraṃ hyananyagati dṛṣṭvā bhugatṛṣṇādivadeva sāmānyāpahatabuddhermameyaṃ bhrāntiḥ pūrvametadviṣayaparikalpanayā jātetyadhyavasthati /
tasmātprayājādimāṭharādiprāptivelāyāmupajātāpi kuśa/
ṇḍinyabuddhirbhrāntiriti niścitya phalavimuktatvānubaddhamarthaṃ śāstraṃ vā bādhituṃ manyate /
kiṃ nu khalvamithyā jñānasya rūpamiti /
yadyatpannā api pratyayāḥ pratyayāntarityaṃ nirākriyante tato 'nyatrāpi ka śvāsa iti manyate tatkathayati /
yasyānveṣaṇe 'pi kṛte bādhaka pratyayāntaraṃ notpadyataiti /
yattu kāraṇadoṣajñānaṃ dvitīyamupalakṣaṇaṃ tamokaviṣayatvānna vede saṃbhavatoti nopanyastam /
prāsaṅgikamutkā idānīmadhikaraṇamupasaṃhṛtyādhikaraṇāntaramārabhyate 
tatra prakaraṇamya tāvacchatiliṅgavākyaiḥ saha virodhāvirodhā saṃpradhāryete /
jyotiṣṭome śrūyate tisra eva sānhasyopasadaḥ kāryā dvādaśāhīnasceti /
tatra sāndaśabdena tāvaḍhanhā samāpyatṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
mānatvāttaṃ sadaivānhā saṃsthāpayantītyevaṃ jyotiṣṭomo gṛhyate iti cyupasattvaṃ tasya /
dvādaśāhīnasyeti tu dvādaśoṣasattvaṃ kiṃ jyotiṣṭomasyāthā honasya dvādaśāhāderiti saṃdihyate /
yadyahonaśabdaḥ kathaṃ cit jyotiṣṭome 'pyupapadyate tataḥ prakaraṇasyāvirodhāttasminneva niveśaḥ /
athāhīna ityahargaṇanāmadheyaṃ tataḥ śrutyā saṃyuktatvāda saṃyuktagrahaṇasvabhāvena prakaraṇenāgrahaṇa,masti hi tadānīṃ śrutiprakaraṇayorvirodhaḥ /
kiṃ prāptam /
sidvāntenopakramaṃ vāśabdena vyāvartya prakaraṇād jyotiṣṭomārthatvamiti pratijānīmahe /
na ca śrutivirodhaḥ prakaraṇādevāhīna śabdasyāpi jyotiṣṭomagāmitvā, dasti ca nañasamāsāncākhyānena tadabhidhānasāmathyaṃmato yadyapyanhaḥ khaḥ kratusamūhe ityevaṃ vyutpādyamāno 'cargaṇavāccaddīnaśabdo bhavati tathāpi virodhaparihārārthamahāniguṇayogādeva jyotiṣṭomārthaḥ sa marṣaṇīyaḥ  /
sa hi kṛtsnavidhānātmavaiprakṛtitvācca na kuśvidīyate /
na cainaṃ ke cidapi kratavaḥ prakṛtitvena jaiti/
yattu bhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ dakṣi pābhiḥ kratukaraṇairvā na dīyataiti 
asaṃyogāttu mukhyasya tasmādapakṛ vyeta 
mukhyaḥ prathama kāryatvāj jyotiṣṭomo 'bhidhīyate /
dīnaśabdasaṃyogo na tu tasya kathaṃ cana /
asaṃyogāca tenāsya yā saṃkhyā tena saṃgatā /
na sā prakaraṇāttasya senāmādapakṛṣyate 
yattu guṇāttatra pravartsyatīti tahikalpya nirākaroti /
yadi tāva ityupacārātpravṛtto 'bhidhīyate tato na prakaraṇānurodhena śrutyarthaparityāgo yuktaḥ /
na cedamarthavādārthaṃ yenaikāhopi praśaṃsitumahargaṇavadupacaryate /
na cāsya śabdāntaraṃ nāsti yena siṃhaguṇamamūha ivetthaṃ kleśena pratipādyate /
tasmādaupacārikatvaṃ tāvadayuktam /
na ca nasamāsenāvayavavyutpattiḥ sa mudāyaprasidyā tannirākaraṇāt/
na ca nanmamāmasya nakṣaṇamasti natrasamāse hi satyavyayapūrvapada prakṛti svara sattvāt ādyudāttatvaṃ syāt /
madhyodāttastvayaṃ padyate tena khapratyayāntantādhyavasānam /
tathā hi sati āyannādiṣu upadeśivaḍacanaṃ svarasihyarthamityevamīnādeśe āśrīyamāṇe pratyayādyudāttatvena īkāre svaraḥ sidhyati tasmāda cargaṇanāmadheyametat /
api ca 
tataśvānantaryāttritvasyāpi tatsaṃbandha eva prasajyataiti vyavasthārthaṃ sānhagrahaṇamapyarthavat /
tammādapakarṣa iti /
na tu kitadyuktam /
paraprakaraṇe nyadharmavidharanyāyyatvāttena vā saṃbandhapadavyavāyavicchinnasya prakaraṇasya punaranusaṃdhānakleśād dvādaśopasada iti ca dvādaśāhaprakaraṇe vicitatvāttatprakṛtitvena sarvāhīneṣu ta tprāpterata stritvamevāsmin vākye sarvadoṣarahitatvādvidhīyate /
dvādaśatvaṃ khaddīnasaṃbandhivākyāntarādeva prāptamaucitya rūpeṇāsya stutyarthaṃ nivītādivadanūdyate iti /
kathaṃ tadhikaraṇaṃ netanyam /
taducyate 
etaduktaṃ bhavati /
kiṃ jyotiṣṭomohīnastasya cedaṃ  prakaraṇādaṅgaṃ vidhīyate athāhargaṇastasya ca prāptamevānyārthamanūcata iti /
nanvevaṃ satyadargaṇasaṃbaddhamapyetat jyotiṣṭomasyaiva satyarthamupa yuktamiti prakaraṇavirodhāvirodhavicārābhāvaḥ prāpnoti /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
pūrvapa hi dvādaśatvasya vidhīyamānasya prakaraṇaṃ grāhakaṃ bhavatītyanūdyate/
siddhānte tvacagaiṇasaṃyuktasya prakaraṇaṃ neṣṭam iti bādhyeta/
anyatve tadyattathā satyapi prakārāntareṇa prakaraṇaevopayuktamiti /
yadā tu dvitvaba itvanyāyenotkarṣopikathaṃ cidāśrīyate śākhāntaravidhau ca satyapi śākhāntarīyasya prayojanāntararahitasya vidhitvamupapadyate tadā yathābhāṣyameva śakyaṃ samarthayitum /
sarvathā dvādaśāhīnasyetyetattāvada hargaṇaviṣayatvātprakaraṇādutkṛṣyataiti siddham 
pakṣeṇārthakṛtasyeti cet 
prakaraṇajjyiotiṣṭome niveśaḥ /
na cāhīnavada prakṛtyajñasaṃvandhosti yajamānadvitvādisaṃbandhastu nimittamātraupayikatvānnāṅgāṅgibhāvāya prabhavati /
na ca tadvāreṇa ṛtusaṃbandho ghaṭate lakṣaṇāprasaṃṅgāt 
yattu tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīya pāda /
nimittaṃ prakaraṇe nāstīti taducyate 'rthā bhaviṣyati 
na cādyāpi yajamānaikatva katva vivakṣāmavadhārayāmaḥ 
atha vaitadeva pratipadvidhānaṃ dṛṣṭvārthād dibahuyajamānakarttṛśrutiṃ kalpayiṣyāmaḥ 
na prakṛtereka saṃyogāt 
prakṛtigrahaṇaṃ prakṛtapratipattyarthamopadeśikatvādvātyantānatikramārtham 
na cāsyāvi vayāṃ kāraṇamasti 
yadyapyaśaktikṛtaṃ cāpanaṃ tadadhyeko yathā śaknuyādityupanvādanyāṅgaviṣayaṃ vijñāyate śaknoti hi dakṣiṇāparimāṇaṃ parityajyaikopi nirvarttayitum /
utpattiprayogacodanāsthatvācca saṃkhyānugraha eva yuktaḥ tasmādeka yajamānakatvānna prakṛtī nimittamastītyutkṛṣyate 
yadi hyetannimittamanākṣipadanarthakobhavettata ākṣipe,tkathaṃ caitadanarthakaṃ bhavedyadi prakṛ tāvivānyatrāpi dvitvaba itve na syātām /
nanu te anyatra na staḥtantravārtike /
kulāyādau vidyamānatvādiha siddhavannimittatvenopādānādvākyabhedaprasaṅgācca nārthādākṣepamaītaḥ 
bahubhya iti ca virūpaikaśeṣaḥ svaramataḥ bahatvapratīto satyāṃ vidhiniṣpramāṇaḥ kalpyeta 
pratipacchabdādeva ṛtugāmitva pratītī satyāṃ dvitvādinā viśeṣapratipattisiddheḥ 
tasmādyatiriktasaṃyoge satyasti prakaraṇavirodhastatra ca śruterbalīyastvam 
jāghanyā patnīḥ saṃyājayantīti guṇapradhānatvavacanavyaktidvayātmaṃde ho yadi jāghanoṃ saṃskāyaṃtvenoddiśya patnīsaṃyājāḥ saṃskārakā vidhīyante tataḥ saṃskāryasya prādhānyātsvasthānāparityāge sati yatra jāghanī tantra patnīsaṃyājā na yatra te tatrāsau /
sā ca lokasthā niṣprayojanatvānna saṃskriyataityagnoṣomoyagatā kṛtārthatvātsaṃskarttavyā /
yadi tu patnīsaṃyājoddeśena jāghanī vidhīyate tataḥ prakṛtānuvādabuddhyanapāyāddarśapūrṇamāsayoreva jāghanovidhānam 
paraṃ ca karmakathanamevaṃ satītyādi /
yadi punarucyate evaṃ sanīti yojyate tataḥ paricodanāchāyāpatterna ca tadyuktamuttarānabhidhānāttasmādātmavacanatvenai va yojyam
prāpnuyādevam 
na kasya citpadārthasyotkarṣa idameva tu vākyaṃ vikanau kāryaṃ kurva dutkṛṣyate ityucyate 
kutaḥ /
jāghanyuddiśyamānā syātsaṃskāryotkarṣa kāraṇam ihopāṭīyate 'ṅgatvādyā geṣvājyavadeva sā 
pa tnīsaṃyājāścānantaravihitā manasi varttantaiti na vidhātuṃ śakyante /
na ceha sthitena paśugatapatnī saṃyājānuvādo yuktastahuḍyabhāvāt /
na ca jāghanyāḥ kālādivaḍhanupādeyatvaṃ yene maṃ vidhimākarṣotsaṃskāryatvāditi ced na tṛtīyāvagataguṇātvātikramapramāṇābhāvāt /
yadi ca kṛtārthaṃ jāghanoṃ prastutvāyaṃ vi dhiḥ pravartteta tathāpi tāvatkadā citprayājaśeṣavad dvitīyārtheḍhatoyeti vyākhyāyeta /
sā tvapūrvā vidhīyate /
tasmānnotkarṣatanpravārtika /
marhati /
na ca prakaraṇabadvatvāḍhate patnīsaṃyājā utkarṣe sahate /
vākyabalīyastvāditi cenna /
vākyasyāpyevamādaradhikṛtāpekṣitvena prakaraṇād durbalataratvādyadi hyetadeva patnīsaṃyājānāmutpattivākyaṃ bhavet tataḥ prakaraṇādācchindyāt /
ete tu vākyāntarotpattitvātsannidhivaśena yāvatā kālenaitena vākyena saṃgṛhyante tāvatā darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmapi śakyā grahītum /
na ca jāghanyāḥ phalavattvaṃ vijñātaṃ yenaiṣāṃ prayojanākāṅkṣāmapanayet /
ato yāvadasau kimarthetyālocyate tāvatphalavadarśapūrṇamāsaprasūtena kathaṃbhāvenāṅgatvamāpāditam /
na cehāpūrvayāga vidhānaṃ yajimānatvenā śravaṇāt /
patnosaṃbaddhayāgaśravaṇaṃ hyetat tatra yadi jāghanyuddeśena ca karma vidhīyate patnyaścāsya vidhīyante tatone kārthavidhānādai kaśabdye parārthavaditi vairūpyalakṣaṇo vābhedaḥ syāt/
alpārthavidhisaṃbhavācca na viśiṣṭavidhānena parihāro ghaṭate /
tasmādviśiṣṭaṃ yāgamuddigya dravyaṃ vidhīyate /
nanvevamapi viśiṣṭa/nuvādātsutarāṃ vākyaṃ bhidyeta /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
prakaraṇāprāpteḥ patnīśabdasyātantratvādyathaivā bhikrāmaṃ juhotīti sāmānya śabdo'pyadhikārāt prayājaviṣayo bhavati /
tathaiva yatsaṃyājayantītyetāvataivādhikṛtāḥ patnīsaṃyājāḥ pratyeṣyante tasmādanutkarṣaḥ /
ekadeśa iti cet 
yadukta me kadeśadravyaścotpattau vidyamānasaṃyogādaprayojaka iti tatrocyate 
saṃtadanaṃ pratīkrayaṇavada nartha lopāt syāt 
iha vākyaprakaraṇayorvirodhāvirodhacintā/
jyotiṣṭome somābhiṣavādhāratvena phalakadvayamāmnātaṃ tatprakṛtya śrūyate dīrghamīme saṃtṛṇyādbhutyāiti bhittvā saṃghātayedityarthaḥ /
tatra ḍhīrgha somaśabdaḥ kiṃ prakṛtāveva kathaṃ cidupapadyate tataścāvirodhaḥ prakaraṇasyātha dīrghakāla satrāhī nayā hitvādanupapadyamāna utkasampradārtike /
rṣediti saṃśayaḥ /
ete cātra pakṣā bhaviṣyanti kiṃ śuddha eva jyotiṣṭome niveśo dīrghayajamānake vātha vokthyādi saṃsthā svevātha vā matrāhīnayorevātha vāgniṣṭomānyamānaiti /
kiṃ prāptaṃ dīrghasomaśabdasyeṣṭipaśuḍhavihomāpekṣayā prakṛtāvevopapatteḥ /
saṃtaīnaprayojanasya ca dīrghaṃsya saṃbhavāt /
asaṃtarddana vidhinā ca saha brohiyavavadvikalpasiddheḥ prakaraṇānugrahāyānutkarṣa iti /
krayavaḍikalpa ityupariṣṭātsamuccaya sthāpanā tpūrvapakṣeṇa dṛṣṭānta iti vyākhyeyama /
na cāvaṇyaṃ sarvatra siddhānta eva dṛṣṭānto bhavati /
yasya kasya cinnidarśanasya pratipattikāraṇatva siddheḥ 
utkarṣo vā grahaṇādviśeṣasya 
vākyakṛtādvā dīrghasomasaṃyogādutkarṣaḥ /
kutaḥ 
na hoṣṭipaśu darvihomāpekṣayā somasya dīrghatvaṃ yuktaṃ vijātīyatvādanupāttatvācca /
sarvatra pratiyoginyupātte dīrghahasvādivibhāgo bhavati /
na cātreṣṭavādaya upāttā yānālocya jyotiṣṭomo dīrgha ityucyeta /
nanu somayāgabhedo'pyanupātta eva /
yadyapyanupāttastathāpi tulya jātīyatvaṃ tāvadastyapekṣākāraṇaṃ vi śeṣaṇa viśeṣyabhāvācca somatve sati dīrghatvamupādoyamānaṃ somāntaramya vyavacchedārthameva vijñāyate /
teṣāṃ kaḥ punarghaḥ kuto vā dīrgha ityapekṣite jyotiṣṭomastāvanna kutaśviddīrgha iti tato'nye gṛhyante teṣāṃ ca prāthamyātma evāpekṣākāraṇaṃ bhavati /
kartṛto vā viśeṣasya tannimittatvāt 
yayā kathaṃ ciddīrghamomaśabde 'vakalpyamāne na yuktaḥ prakaraṇabādhaḥ 
kratuto vārthavādānupapatte syāt 
ṛtata eva dedhye samānādhikaraṇa samāsa ityarthaḥ 
dīrghe haskhe ca karttari karmaṇastulyarūpatvāddā caitahakarjā viśeṣaṇam/
svato viśeṣaṇaṃ tvantaraṅgam 
saṃsthāsu kartṛvaddhāraṇārthāviśeṣāt 
paricoḍhanāpadottarabhūtametatsūtram /
mā nāmāgniṣṭomasaṃsthā yāṃ niveśo bhūdukyyādiṣu tvagniṣṭomāpekṣayā dīrghasomaśabda upapahasyane prakaraṇaṃ cānugrahīṣyate /
tasmāttisuṣvapi saṃsthāsu niveśa iti prakaraṇāviśeṣaḥ 
saṃtarddanasya punarnityenāgrahaṇātkevacā nitya vi ṣayatvaṃ na virudhyate /
tasmātsaṃsthā niveśa ityukta 'bhidhīyate 
satyapyatra karmakāntayodorghatve tāvānevātideśaprāpto daśamaṣṭiḥ somo 'bhiṣūyate dhāraṇasya tu tulyatvādṛṣṭārthavāḍha yoranupapattiḥ syāt/
pradānavivṛddhyā nyūnapātrāgrahaṇācca somavṛddhirbhabṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
viṣyatīti cenna daśamuṣṭitriparvaparimāpāyoḥ śābdatvātpradānavivṛdvistoyādivṛddhyā saṃpādanīyā tasmādaviśiṣṭaṃ dhāraṇamityuhakarṣaḥ 
anityatvāditi niyataparimāṇatvasyāniyatatvāditi manyate 
na tvetadyuktam 
kutaḥ tantravārtika /
agniṣṭomānyamātre hi dīrghaśabdovakalpate /
athānyene tivattasmātsaṃsthā kratvantara grahaḥ 
prakṛtivacchabdapūrṇatvācca na tāsāṃ prakaraṇamasti /
na hyetad gṛhītaṃ prākṛtaṃ kiṃ ciḍhaṅgaṃ punaruccārya vidhīyate prathamopadigyamānajyotiṣṭomadharmamadhyapātitvāditaśca na saṃsthānāṃ prakaraṇamasti /
katham 
yadi hi saṃtarddanamukthyādīnvidhāyāvāntaraprakaraṇo śrūyeta tataḥ syādapi prakaraṇagrahaṇamidaṃ tu saṃsthādhikaraṇanyāyena tadagrāhau jyotiṣṭomadharmairantaritatvānna saṃsthākathaṃbhāvānuṣaṅgena saṃ spṛśyate /
tasmānna prakaraṇaṃ saṃsthānaṃ vā saṃsthāsu viniyojakam/
kiṃ taī vākyameva tacca dīrghasomatvāviśeṣātma cāhīnedhvapi tulyamiti sarvadharmatā 
tatra kiṃ prāptam 
naimittikaṃ vā kartṛsaṃyogālliṅgatantravārtike /
sya tannimittatvāt 
 yadi prathamaśabdoyaṃ nāma syāt jyotiṣaḥ svataḥ /
tata evaṃ bhavedeṣa prayogakratuvācakaḥ  
tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
dvā 
tannāma viśeṣavacanenopasaṃhiyate yat ṛtusaṃyomāyāsamarthaṃ kathaṃ citparokṣavṛttyā saṃyujyate yathā sāptadaśyam 
etāvattviāvadhārayituṃ śakyam /
nāyamanārabhyavādaḥ prakṛteranyatra gacchati /
yadi gacchettata iṣṭipaśubandhānapi gacchenna va gantumarhati purastādupasadāmiti /
sthānaniyamasya tatrānupapateḥ /
ato yatropasadastatra gacchati /
tataśca prāptikālavaiṣamyātprakṛtau tāvattāḥ santītyantareṇāpi vacanaṃ gacchetkimuta yadā vi spaṣṭameva vacanaṃ, sphuṭa sāmānyasaṃbandha sthāpi caivamāderupasaṃhāra iti vyākhyātaṃ caturddhā karaṇe/
tasmādutpatti viniyogābhyāmevāpunaruktatva, mevaṃ sati yeṣāṃ prakaraṇaeva pravargyapāṭhastaiḥ saha saṃgatārthatā bhaviṣyati /
yadi tarhi dvayorapyekavākyatvenāgniṣṭome pravṛ paktītyayamartho niṣyannastato na prathamayajñe ityetasyāprathamayajñe agniṣṭomaityevaṃ pravarttamānasya na kaściddirodha iti paryudāsānnityamevākaraṇena bhavitavyamata evaṃ varṇanīyam 
kutaḥ 
tataśca yasmādikalpāddibhyadbhiḥ paryudāsa āśrīyate sa tasminsatyapyāgata iti varaṃ śabdasvarasalabhyaḥ pratiṣedha evāśritaḥ, tena prathamāhāre 'gniṣṭome vikalpaḥ /
tatrāpi yadā keṣāṃ cidīdṛśaṃ vacanaṃ kāmaṃ yonūcānaḥ śrotriyaḥ syāttasya pravṛ'jyāditi tadā pratiprasavavacanasya vikalpakāriṇaḥ kartṛviśeṣagāmitvātadviṣaya eva vikalponyeṣāṃ nityamevābhāvaḥ 
satyaṃ prāptasya punarvacanaṃ tāvanmātraphalamanarthakamiti sāmarthyāt prakarṣagatirvijñāsyate /
yathābhirūpāya kanyā deyetyatrābhirūpatarāyeti gamyate /
anūcānagrahaṇaṃ tu brāhmaṇasyānuvacanasaṃbandhāt kṣatriyavaiṣyanivṛttyarthaṃ bhaviṣyati /
tadetadatirāceṣyevameva prāpnoti/
tana prathamayajñaiti pratiṣedhādanagniṣṭomatvena ca pratiprasavābhāvānnityameva na karttavyaḥ/
vikṛtyantareṣu prathamaprayogānupapatternityameva karaṇam /
nanu tatrāpi na prathamayajñaityatideśādagniṣṭomasvarūpasya ca pratiprasava nimittasyābhāvātprathamaprayogeṣvabhāva eva prāpnoti/
naitadevam /
prathamaśabdasyāviśeṣitasya sarvādo pravarttamānasyānyatrāpravṛtteḥ tasmātkaṃbalajyotiṣṭomaprathama prayogatṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
viṣaya eva caiṣa pratiṣedha iti siddham 
tatsarvārthamaviśeṣāt 
carau vārthoktaṃ puroḍāśe vipratiṣe dhātpaśau na syāt 
yadi kaściddadellaukikapiṣṭe pādānenāpi puroḍāśasiddheneṃkāntenārthācepa iti taṃ pratyucyate /
arthe/
nāma prākṛta upakāraḥ tasya prakṛtau peṣaṇaṃ sāghanamāsīdatastena pūrvataraprāptenoktaṃ puroḍāśe peṣaṇam /
pau ca pradhāna vaiguṇyaṃ syāttadvi hṛdayādyākṛtikena tataścāvattena sāghayitavyam /
na ca piṣṭe tadākṛtikādavadīyeta punastadākārakaraṇepi mṛdgavayādivaṅgauṇādavadīyamāne vaiguṇyameva /
utpādanadeśādavadyatīti ca śrūyate /
na ca hṛdayāde piṣṭasya jñāyeta katareṇa pradeśenedaṃ paśorutkṛttamiti /
tasmāccarāvapratiṣidmanarthaprāptaṃ ca peṣaṇamiti tatraiva vidhīyate /
nanvadantako hītihetva viśeṣātyaśupuroḍāśayorapi prāptevidānāni taccheṣāśca piṣṭvā dāsyante /
na ca prāptivipratiṣedhau bhaviṣyataḥ /
ucyate /
yavadānasya pradānaprakramatvāt nāntarā peṣaṇena vyavadhānaṃ yuktaṃ, hetuvannigadasya ca stutimātrārthatvaṃ vacyate /
tena svakrama sthasyaiva preṣaṇasya vidhiḥ /
upanītamātrameva ca peṣaṇaṃ puroḍāśe 'nuvādabuddhyā gṛhyate /
carau ca nivarttamānaṃ pratiprasavatvena paśau punaratyantāprāptavidhitvena /
na caitānyekasyaiva vākyasyaitāvanti rūpāṇi vijñāyante /
tatrāvagya maikarūpye 'bhyupagantavye lāghavādarthaṃvattvācca pratiprasavatvamevāvadhāraṇīyam /
evaṃ siddhaṃ kevalacaru viṣayatvam 
katham /
gatiḥ sarvapadārthānāṃ laukika vyavahārataḥ /
tatra pākaviśeṣaśca carutvenā vadhāryate 
pakṣoktaṃ prayojanamiti mandaṃ phanamuktam /
etāvāntamamādhiḥ aviśeṣepina puroḍāśārtha tvaṃ prayojanaṃ kiṃ tarṣi paścarthatvamiti 
dharmavipratiṣedhāca 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
ita caika daivaye 
piṃṣyādadhaṃ samastaṃ vā didevatye carau bhavān /
pūrvasminpā kavaiṣamyaṃ para smibhāga saṃkaraḥ 
nanu caitatsarvaṃ dvidevatyeṣu bhavatopi samānaṃ tathā hi 
sa cāṅgīkṛto miśrasya haviṣo miśra devatoddeśena yugapaddāne virodhābhāvāt 
yāgāpūrva prayukteṣu dharmeṣvevaṃ bhavedidam /
bhavataḥ peṣaṇaṃ tvetaddevatādharma saṃmatam 
na ca tad didevatye tathāvasthitamityapravṛttireva /
havirantareṣvapi ca hidevatyeṣvevaṃ prakāratvameveti devatā guṇabhūtā 
bhavatā punarasadabhyupagamena dvidevatye peṣaṇaṃ vaktumaśaknuvatā 'vaśyaṃ devatānimittatantravārtika /
tu tvamabhyupagantavyam /
tataśca devatayoḥ prādhānyāde kekā svabhāgamasaṃkīrṇaṃ prārthayataiti tathaiva dānamanuṣṭheyam 
tatra brūmaḥ 
tatrānyasya bhā mādanyama avadīyamāne vaiguṇyaṃ bhavati 
carumiti yāgaṃ pratyupādīyamānatvena vivakṣitaikasaṃkhyasya pātrakṛtabhedāśrayaṇe śāstravādhaprasaṅgā, dato na kathaṃ cidapi pratiṣidvadharmakaṃ dvidevatye peṣaṇaṃ bhavatīti na kartavyam 
kutaḥ /
haviṣo yadi poṣṇasya tadyāgāṅgasya vā bhavet /
anuktatvād dvidevatye na bhavetyeṣaṇaṃ tataḥ 
tenāsatyapyatra pūṣṇo devatātve samavāyamātreṇopanakṣaṇatvād iyoddeśenāpi ca tyajyamānasya samaṃ yādaśrutatvādityanena nyāyeṃnā pūṣṇo bhāga iti gamyate 
athāpi kiṃ na etenāśrutena kṛtenetyevamamātrapeṣaṇa mevādhyavasīyate tathāpi kena citkauśalena pākasaṃpādanayogapadyaniśśepapācaikatvayorvā guṇatvādara bāgha iti nirūpya kārya me va peṣaṇamiti 
tatrābhidhīyate 
tenāgneyendrapīta śabdābhyāṃ samarthāgnīndragrāhibhyāṃ videvatyāgrahaṇaṃ yukta, miha punaḥ pūṣapadasyāsamāsabhākkāt prapiṣṭabhāgaśabdayośca sāpekṣepi pūṣaṇi sāmarthyāvighātāt na kiṃci d duṣyatītyupaścajaṇatā 
na ca sadvitīyasya padantā jāyantaiti hetusāmyādyuktaṃ peṣaṇam 
vacanātsarvapeṣaṇaṃ taṃ prati śāstravattvādarthābhāvāddhi carāvapeṣaṇaṃ bhavati 
vidhitvānnemapiṣṭatvamaniṅga viparyayasādhanaṃ cetyata āāha 
tadyadi tāvadyaścaruḥ sa nemapiṣṭa iti vidhīyate tataḥ sarvaca viṣayāvadhāraye sati somā pauṣṇaśabda ekaṭeśānuvādonarthakaḥ syāt /
atha somāpauṣṇamātramuddiśyate tatopi sarvapeṣaṇameva saddevatyahavi rmātrapratītyā paśupuroḍāśayorapi grahaṇāt /
tataśca pūrvavaccaruśabdānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ /
taṃ prati hi somāpauṣṇamaviśeṣitaṃ pratipeṣaṇasya śāstravatvaṃ viśeṣaṇārthābhāvāt /
etasminpakṣe carāvapeṣaṇaṃbhavati 
na cātyantākatirnaśyena cotsādadeśamohaḥ syāditarotmādadeśasya spaṣṭatvena ca piṣṭopi san pūṣabhāga upacacyate na sarvapreṣaṇavanmuhyeta /
atha vāsminpace vācanikatvādadṛṣṭārthe peṣaṇe satya piṣṭādevāvadīyeta /
naci tadaitaddevatānimittaṃ peṣaṇaṃ syāt /
tasmātmārvatrikatva prasaṅgānna pariśeṣasiddhaṃ caroḥ peṣaṇamiti tacchra tira narthikā prāpnotyeveti carudevatāsaṃbandhavidhipare vākye nemapiṣṭatvamatṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pāda /
ndhana ityavaśyamabhyupagantavyam 
na hyeṣa devatādharmo na tadbhāgasya gamyate /
pūṣadevatyayāgārthaṃ dharmastveṣa pratīyate 
na hi taduddeśatyāgamātreṇa bhāgo bhavati kiṃ tarhi parigraheṇa /
karmasādhano hi bhāgaśabdo bhajyataiti bhāgaḥ sevyataityarthaḥ 
na ca haviraṃśa devatā bhajame bhoktṛtvasya navame niṣedhāt /
athāpi bhajettathāpi tasyāḥ prayojakatvaṃ tatraiva nivārayiṣyate /
tena devatāvadbhāgadharmatvānupapatteryāgadvārāpūrvadharma evāyaṃ /
navamādyanyāyena devatādhika raṇanyāyena ca vijñāyate /
bhāṣyakāreṇa tu devatādharmatva nirākaraṇaparega yāgadharmatvamabhihita miti draṣṭavyam 
tatra vākyasaṃyogādityukte pareṇa svābhiprāye vivṛte bhāgaśabdenaiva mukhyārthāsaṃbhavādyāgopādānamiti darśayati /
parasvakhokaraṇātmakasya bhāgarūpasyāvidyamānatvā, dyasta duddeśena tyajyamānatvanāmāṃśī vidyate tena yāgo lacyate, sa caikadevatye tantravārtike /
pūṣaviśiṣṭeo bhavatīti tadbhāgavyapadeśo ghaṭate, dvidevatye pu narvyāsaṅgo miśraḥ saṃkalponyatareṇa vyapadeṣṭumaśakya iti /
yathaivaindrāmasya puroḍāśaya grahasya cāgneyendrapītaśabdābhyāmagrahaṇaṃ tathaindrā pauṣṇādeḥ pūṣabhāgatvena yadyapi caivaṃvidhaśabdoccāraṇadi samāsopālambho nāsti tathāpyartha eva bhāgaśabdagrāhyo na vidyataityapravṛttiḥ 
hetumālamadantatvam 
yattvadantako hoti hetunidarśanāddevatādharmatvamiti /
tatrocyate 
vacanaṃ param 
nemapiṣṭādiṣu prāptyabhāvādvacanaṃ bhaviṣyati 
aviśiṣṭa vidhiṃ cāpekṣya viśiṣṭavidhirṭarbalo bhavati na tvatrāsāvasti 
iti śrīmahakumārila svāmiviracite tantravārttike tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ 
nivītamiti manuṣyadharmaḥ śabdasya tatpradhānatvāt 
sa eva śrutyāditritayasya prakaraṇena saha virodhāvirodhavicāraḥ /
tatra nivītaṃ manuṣyāṇāmityacaite pakṣā bhavanti kimayaṃ śuddhamanuṣyadharmaḥ karmayuktamanuṣyadharme vā atha śuddakarmadharmaḥ /
athavā prakaraṇe yanmanuṣyapradhānaṃ karma ancāhāryapacanādi tasya dharmaḥ utāprakaraṇe yā manuṣyapūjātithyātmikā tasyāṃ niveśa iti /
yau tu vidhyarthavādapacau tau śeṣalakṣaṇe'naupayako pramāyāca kṣaṇaviṣayatvādvidhivannigadārthavādamadhye ca nirṇotatvādiha naivopanyasanīyau /
yastu bhāṣyakāreṇopanyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ sa kṛtvācintā nyāyeneti draṣṭavyam/
na hi vidhitvamanabhyupetya manuṣyadharmādipañca  upapadyate iti /
vidhiriti kṛtvā prathamaṃ prastutya paścācaṇānurūpaṃ vicāryānte pūrvāvasthita mevārthavādatvamupasaṃhariṣyati /
pareṣvapyadhikaraṇeṣvetadyathāsaṃbhavaṃ yojayitavyam /
tatra vidhirvā syādapūrvavādvādamātraṃ hyanarthakamityanenaiva tā vadvidhiḥ ahīnādyadhikaraṇanyāyena ca ṣaṣṭhīśrutyā manuṣyadharmaḥ /
tantravārtike /
teṣāṃ svatvena tatpratīyate na manuṣyāstadaṅgatvena /
guṇavibhaktinimābhāvāt /
arthādeva ca tatprāpta/
satyāṃ naiva manuṣyagrahaṇaṃ kriyeta, kṛtaṃ caitat, atopi manuṣyadharma ityavagacchāmaḥ 
vidhistvapūrvavatvātsyāt 
vidhirevāyam /
kutaḥ /
pūrvavattvāyanuvādo bhavedatyantaprāptāvityarthaḥ /
na cāyamatyanta prāptaḥ /
tena vināpyavyagratāyāḥ śakyatvāt kaṇṭhavandhaḥ punaḥ prāyeṇāprāpta evetyasti niyama vidheravakāśaḥ 
vākyasya śeṣavatvāt 
dvedhā saṃbhave tādṛśī pramāṇagatirāśrayaṇīyā yā pramāṇāntaraṃ na bādhate yajurvedāmnānācca nivītāderādhvaryavasamākhyopavaddhaṃ vākyam/
tatra yadi karmadharmeyaṃ tataḥ kartṛviśeṣātṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
pekṣāyāṃ satyāṃ samākhyayā 'dhvaryuniyamātmamākhyārthavatī bha viṣyati/
manuṣyadharmāṇāṃtuna samākhyā niyāmiketi vacyāmaḥ 
tatprakaraṇe yattatsaṃyukta mavipratiṣedhāt 
prathamaṃ tāvanmanuṣyadharmabalīyasvena karmadharmatvaṃ nirākaroti /
tathā hi sukhaṃ sūcitaḥ pakṣaḥ parigrahīṣyate/
śrutvā hi prakaraṇasamākhye bādhitvā manuṣyadharma eva prāpnoti/
taducyate sarvānugrahārthamayaṃ pakṣostu manuṣyāṇāmiti tatpradhānakarmavya tirekajanitā ṣaṣṭhī na nivītaṃ gṛhṇāti /
tadapi ca prakaraṇādanvāhāryadānādi pratīyate nānyat /
ata eṣa vākyārtho yadi manuṣyāṇāṃ karma tatra nivyātavyamiti 
tulyavaddhi prasaṃkhyānaṃ dṛśyate sminnidhitraye /
tasmānnarapradhāne syātpitṛdevapradhānavat 
arthavādo vā prakaraṇāt 
sarvathā nācaikopi pakṣo nirdoṣaḥ/
prakaraṇasaṃbandhe vākyasaṃbandhavādhādanvācāryādisaṃbandhe vākyabhedātprakaraṇasya ca viśeṣakatvānupapattera tithyādisaṃbandhotyantanirmūla eva/
ṣaḍbhirapi śra tyādibhirasaṃ yarthāt manuṣyasaṃbandhena tadanumīyate /
tacca na yutam /
tasyā api ṣaṣdyā nivotapaṭasaṃbandhivyatirekajanitatvapratoteḥ /
na hyanupāttasaṃbandhivyatireke vibhakta utpadyante /
tasmānmanuṣyārthataiva prāpnoti /
tatrāpi ca prakaraṇasamākhyānādhaphalakalpanāprasaṅgaḥ  /
sati ca gatyantarena yuktaṃ tadāśrayaṇamasti caudumbarādhikaraṇasidvamarthavādatvaṃ gatiḥ 
 ataḥ paraṃ ṣaṭ sūtrāṇi bhāṣyakāreṇa na likhitāni satra vyākhyātārī vivadante /
ke cidāivistāni /
likhito gra ndhaḥ pracīna ityapare /
phalgutvādupekṣitānītyanye /
anārpeyatvādityapare /
tathā ca digvibhāgaśca tahaditi nivītādhikarapānideśaḥ tadānantaryādupapadyata iti /
vṛttyantarakāraistu duttāḥ 
kiṃ prāptaṃ sarvadharmaḥ syāt /
kutaḥ 
mṛtāgnihotre hi pihṛdevatye śrūyate prācīnāvīto dohayet /
yajñopavītī hi devebhyo dohayatīti /
tadyadi sarvārthamupavītaṃ tato'yaṃ pitrye 'gnihotrasambandhī nityavata yajñopavītānuvādo 'vakalpate /
na cāyaṃ darśapūrṇamāsasthasyaivānuvādaḥ vi prakṛṣṭatvāt/
hetuvannigadārthavādānarthakyācca /
yadi hi tasmiva karmaṇyanyāvastheyaṃ dharmo bhavati tataśca tadavasthā parijihīrṣayā hetuvannigado 'vakalpate /
na tu kratvantarasthaṃ parivarttavyamatyanta viprakarṣevāprasaktatvāta /
na ca devebhya iti bahuvaca naṃ darśapūrṇamāsayoravakalpate /
vaikalpikendra mahendra kadevatyatvāt mānāvyaya /
agnihotre tu sāyaṃprātardevatālocanenopapanna bahutvam /
tasmādagnihotrasthopavītānuvādānyathānupapatteḥ sarvadharmatvamiti 
na vā sarvadharmaḥ /
kutaḥ /
prakaraṇādarśaparṇamā sārthatvapratītaiḥ /
atha yaduktaṃ liṅgadarśanāditi /
parihṛtaṃ tat /
tasyaivaitaddarśanaṃ darśapūrṇamāsasyasyeti /
sannikṛṣṭānuvādāsambhave ca vipralaṣṭānuvādo'pyāśrīyate /
yathāprāptyapeyohi sa bhavati /
bahuvacanaṃ cāvivaścitam/
atha vā prakṛtivikṛtidevatālocanenopapatsyate /
tataśvāyamartho bhavati /
yasmāddevayukta karmāntaradhamayamataḥ pitraye 'gnihotre na karttavya iti 
tadevodāharaṇamupavyayate devalakṣmameva tatkurutaiti tatra vidhiranuvāda iti sandehaḥ /
kathaṃ punaranavadhārite vidhitve sarvārthatvadarśapūrṇamāsārthatvavicāro vṛttaḥ /
siddhena vyavahārādidamarthato'dhikaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ draṣṭavyam /
kiṃ prāptamanuvāda iti /
kutaḥ 
nityodakī nityayajñopavītīti hi sarvadā yajñopavītaṃ prāpnaṃ kratāvapyasti /
na caiṣa vidhisarūpaḥ śabdaḥ tasmādanuvāda iti /
evaṃ ca nivataprācīnāvī tābhyāmavai janaṇyaṃ bhaviṣyatītyevaṃ prāpte namaḥ 
na hi namastānuvā vākyasya kiñcitphalamasti nivītaprācīnāvītasaṃkorttanamapi ca vidhoyamānopavītastutyarthatvenaivārthavabhaviṣyati /
varttamānāpadeśānāmapi ca tadābhāsatvātprayogavacanārthavādapañcamalakārebhyo vidhiśaktirvyākhyātā /
tasmādidhiḥ /
yattu smṛtereva prāptamiti /
tatrāpyapūrvatvādidamevottaramanya eva hyasau puruṣadharmaṃ prāpto'nyaścāyamapūrvaḥ kratudharmo vidhīyate /
tasmānnānuvādaḥ 
udakatvaṃ vā 'pūrvatvāt 
tataśca śabdenāncādiśyate ayamapi vidhirapūrvatvāditi /
prāptipūrvako anuvādo bhavati /
na cātṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
sya puruṣārthatayā 'pi prāptirasti /
na cāsya stutyarthatā'pi yujyate hiśavdādyaprayogāt /
tasmātsidvavaduktānyathānupapatyai vāsyāpi vidhitvamiti 
ācāraprāptasyodagagratvasya dyotakamātraṃ liṅgadarśana me tanna vidhiḥ /
kutaḥ 
yacchabdayogādākhyātatadviśeṣarahitatvācca sphuṭamihānuvā datvamavadhāritam /
tadyathā kathañcidapi prāptau satya nātikamitavyam /
asti cātra prāptiragravanti prāgagrāṇi udagagrāṇi vā 'pavargavanti prāgapavargāṇyudagapavargāṇi veti smṛteḥ /
tasmāttatma mānārtha evāyaṃ siddhavaḍhanuvādaḥ /
tathaiva ca stutyarthaḥ /
purā hyetaduktaṃ na tu sāmprataṃ mṛtāvasthāyāmiti /
sthitādapyetadevottaram /
hiśabdavadākhyātena yataḥ kutacitprāpterapekṣitatvāt /
prakaraṇe ca tadabhāvātkimanavagamyamānameva vidhitvaṃ kalpitam uta yatratatrasthā prāptirāśrīyatāmiti /
tatra prātyāśrayaṇamapekṣitaṃ na tu vidhitvamiti tadeva jyāyaḥ /
prakaraṇabahuvacanayoścoktam astyeva cānyo'tra vidhiriti nānarthakyam 
vidhistu dhāraṇe 'pūrvatvāt 
sarvamabhyarhitaṃ dravyaṃ pracchādanamapekṣate /
yatra kka cana ca prāpte samittatra niyamyate 
dhāraṇe vidhireva syāt na hi prāptiḥ kutaścana /
samitpracchādanāśaktarnācārāduparisthatā 
na cāprāptaṃ hetuvannigaṭena varttamānāpadeśena vā 'nuvadituṃ śakyam /
ato'sya vyavadhāraṇakalpanayā 'nuvādasarūpatvaṃ bhakkā vākyaṃ bhittvā vidhitvamāśrīyate /
pitrye home 'dhastāt srugdaṇḍasya samidvārayitavyā /
daive ca punarupariṣṭāditi /
vidhitve caivamādīnāmuktaḥ kalpanāprakāraḥ /
tasmādvidhiriti 
purā kalpasvarūpeṇa bhajatyarthānuṣaṅgiṇā /
digvibhāgasya sambandhānivītātulyatāmatiḥ 
svābhāvika digādīnāṃ sarvakriyāṅgatvaṃ na nivītavadapūrva vidhātavyam /
tatra manuṣyasaṃbandhe 'pi niyamaphalamājakalpanamevatantravārtika /
na kriyāphalakalpanā/
tadapi ca laukikīnāmeva kriyāṇāmavighna samāpanamapekṣāvaśātkalapyate nānyatsvargādi /
tenaivamābhāti /
yāvatkiṃcinmanuṣyāḥ svārthaṃ karmānutiṣṭhanti tatra pratīcyudīcī cāṅgaṃ bhavati /
yāvacca darbhalavanaṃ tadantarā karttavyaṃ yāvanmīyate tatpūrṇena mātavyam /
yāvacca snehakāryaṃ tatsarvaṃ vilīnanavanītena niṣpakkāyuta śabdavācyena karttavyam /
naitaraudrayo vi dagdhatvāśritatve kartavye prati /
tenā cāpi pūrvatulyatvaṃ sādhayitavyamityārambhaḥ /
tatra manuṣyadharmaḥ śabdasya tatpradhānatvāditi vināpi ṣaṣṭhonirdeśādabhajanteti manuṣyasaṃbandhāttādarthyam itareṣu ṣaṣṭhyeva /
tathā 'padeśo veti saukaryātprāptirabhidhīyate pūrvā cipṛṣṭhata ādityaṃ sukhaṃ vyāpriyantaiti praticīprāptiḥ /
kṛtvā tathāntarājavanapūyoraprayatnasādhyatvātprāptiḥ 
prakaraṇasamākhyābhyāṃ ca karmadharmaḥ /
sarvapramāṇānugrahārthaṃ prakaraṇe manuṣyapradhāne niveśaḥ /
vākyena prakaraṇasamākhyayorvādhātphalakalpanābhayā ccātithyādau niveśaḥ /
tenāpi saha sambandha pramāṇābhāvātprakaraṇe sambhāvinaścānutkarṣātprācīna vidhiśeṣa tvāccārthavāda iti siddhāntaḥ /
samyak śrutayathāvidita viṣayānyaviṣayastutivivekasiddhiḥ 
tasmātpravṛttikaimarthyacintā pravṛttīnāmapyabhidhāyakākhyāsavaśenaidamathyaṃ nirūpyata ityākhyāta śabdāścintayitavyāḥ 
tataścaitasya sarvasyākhyātanirūpaṇāyattatvāttadgatoyaṃ vicāro bhaviṣyati /
kimākhyātena karttā 'bhidhīyate neti/
tatra yadyabhidhīyate tataḥ śrītatvātprayojanākāhiṇī bhāvanā prakaraṇagamyakratvarthatvabādhanena puruṣārthā bhavati /
atha nābhidhīyate tataḥ śrutivirodhābhāvātprakaraṇena kratvarthatā /
nanu satyapi kartturabhidhāne bhāvanāpradhānatvādākhyātena to pratyupādīyamānasya śrautopi sambandhaḥ prakaraṇānuguṇatvādaviruddho naiva kratvarthatāṃ bādhate virodhinau hi tulyakakṣā sambandhī pararasparaṃ bādheyātāṃ na guṇapradhānabhūtau /
tadyathā daśāpavitreṇa grahaṃ sammātyatra daśāpavitropasarjanasya saṃmārgasya grahaṃ pratyupādīyamānasya naivamāśaṅkā bhavati /
kiṃ daśāpavitreṇa sambadhyatāmuta graheṣeti /
tathā'pi guṇabhūtakartṛkāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ kratuṃ pratyupādoyamānāyā na kaścidvirodhaḥ /
yadi tvākhyātena kartuḥ prādhānyamucceta tataḥ prakaraṇagamyena kratuprādhānyena virodhaḥ syāt /
yadi vā karturitra kratorapi guṇatvaṃ syāt /
tata ubhayoḥ śeṣayoḥ śeṣisamavāyavirodho lakṣyate na tu tadubhayamapyasti /
ataḥ śrutyā karturguṇabhāvātprakaraṇena ca kratoḥ prādhānyānnānāviṣayatvenāsamavāyādavirodhaḥ tadbhāvādabādhaḥ syāditi/
naitadevam 
yadvaitadaviśeṣeṇa sthitaṃ kramavaśādubhau /
pratyayārthaṃ sa brataḥ prakṛtipratyayāviti 
na hyasautsargikasya nyāyasya smaraṇasya vāpavādabhūtaṃ nyāyāntaraṃ smaraṇāntaraṃ copalabhyate /
tena kuttadvitāntavadeva pratyayā rthaprādhānyaṃ prāpnoti /
tataśca śabdenaiva dhātvarthasya śeṣatvamuktaṃ nātikramituṃ śakyate /
nanu sāmānyamutsṛṣṭaṃ pratītiviśeṣeṇāpodyeta /
tathāhi 
iyostāvatpradhānayorguṇayorvā sarvacaiva sambandho nāvakalpate /
tatrāvaśyaṃ kalpanīye guṇapradhānatve yathāpratīti vyavasthā sampravārtike /
'vadhāryate /
tatpratītiśca yathā'nyatra prakutyarthe/pasarjana pratyayā rthaviṣayatvenopalabhyate tathā 'tra pratyayārthopasarjanaprakṛtyartha viṣayā sarvasya svasaṃvedyā /
na ca tato'nyat balavatkārāmasti /
tasmādaprasaṅgaḥ karttuḥ pradhānatvasyeti 
dhātvarthasya pradhānatvaṃ na tāvadiha janmani /
śrautsargiko na ca nyāyo matpate hi nivasrtsyati 
sya viśeṣaṇatayā rājā puruṣasyopasarjanam /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
arthayoḥ śeṣaśeṣitve tasyaiveṣṭā pradhānatā 
niḥsaṃdigdhapradhānatvaṃ pācakādiṣu kārakam /
tathāpi tu na mādathyeṃ kriyāṇāmavadhāryate 
prādhānyeneha karttṛtvaṃ yadi nāmābhidhīyate /
tatastātparyato vācyaṃ guṇatvamavadhāritam 
kartṛtvaṃ sādhakatvena siddhaṃ taccābhidhīyate /
svāmitvaṃ tu tataḥ paścātpramāṇāntaragocaraḥ 
acetanepi kāṣṭhādā kartṛtvamabhidhīyate /
na ca tatra phalohe śastasmānnaiṣā 'vadhāraṇā 
bibhrāṇaḥ puruṣaṃ rājā guṇatvaṃ tāvadṛcchati /
svāmitvaṃ bhajate paścādvivakṣā ta yathārūci 
prayogaiyasya vidyamānasya tāvaḍyavasthā hitāvarthadaye sambhavati kimiti vakṣyamāpakriyopayogāpecayā vivakṣābhedamātreṇa kliṣṭāṃ vyavasthāmāśrayiṣyāmahe /
tena bhūtaṃ nimittamālocca śabde prayujyamāne rājapuruṣa ityatropakārāṃśakṛtaṃ śeṣatvameva vivaścitamiti gamyate /
yatrā'pi yogarbhadāsādisvāminyatyantā vidyamānameva śeṣatvaṃ tatrāpyupakārakatvasambhavādupacaritamiti draṣṭavyam 
tirohitaṃ ca karmatvaṃ na gṛhṇīyādapi kriyām /
āvirbhūtaṃ tu kartṛtvamākhyātasthaṃ grīṣyati 
kārakopasarjanībhūtasya dravyasya pratyāsattimātreṇa saṃkhyādayaḥ śeṣāḥ sambhaveyuste tvatyanta pratyāsanna pradhānabhūtena kārake pāpahṛtya kriyāyai nīyante /
na tvevaṃ dhātvarthānāṃ kena cihnanavattaraṇa pramāṇena kratvarthatvamavagamyate yena kartṛtvaśeṣatā bādhyeta 
kartṛṇāṃ śāstragamye 'rthe cetanānāmadhikriyā /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
vidhiśva na bhavetteṣāṃ phalasaṅkalpanāhate 
tenāvaśyamanuṣṭhātṛtvanīcamānaḥ puruṣaḥ kimapi mamaiṣā kriyā sākṣātparamparyeṇa vopakariṣyatotyadhyavasyati sājhādupakārake ca sambhavati na pāramparyopakāra kalpanā labhyate /
na ca saṃskārānaīḥ karttā kratuphalādhāratvena saprayojanatvāt /
kastasyopakāra iti cet sarvathā tāvatmāmānyenopakāramātramavadhāritam /
tāvatā ca kratvarthatvaṃ vyāvarttitaṃ tadviśeṣāvadhāraṇaṃ ca yatheṣṭaṃ kalpayiṣyate /
na tadacopayujyate tasmānna kratvarthatā /
yadyapi ca prādhānyāṃśa kartṛtvavacanenānabhihitastatra cānantargatastathāpi tadanyathānupapatyaiva pratyāyitatvātmambadhyate /
yathā svargakāmādiśabdena puruṣaviśeṣavacanenānuktamapi svargasya sādhyatvaṃ kalpayiṣyate /
tathā svāmitvamapi buddhipūrvakāriṇaḥ puruṣasya phalalipsayaiva ka tṛtvapratītyā pratipatsyate/
tatra yathaiva devatāyāḥ karmaṇābhipreyamāṇāyāḥ prādhānyaṃ yāgasādhanatvapratipattyarthameva jñāyate na prā dhānyasvarūpaparyavasāyitvena tatheha guṇatvaṃ prādhānya siddhyarthameva draṣṭavyam 
yasthā'pi karttā pratyayārthastenāpyavabhyaṃ pratītivaśādbhāva santravārtike /
nābhyupagantavyā/
tatasyaikapratyayopādānātprādhānyācca saiva ka tarimaṅgīkarotīti na dhātvarthāṅgatā bhavatīti /
sa tu bhāvanāyāṃ vyāpṛtastāmanyathā kartumaśaknuvan dhātvartha mevāṅgīkaroti/
na cobhayātmakatvaṃ vipratiṣiddhaṃ viṣayānyatvādeva /
yadi dhātvarthameva prati guṇatvameva kalapyeta tataḥ sakkadupāḍhāne vipratiṣiddhamiva syāt /
iha tu bhāvanā prati guṇatvaṃ dhātvartheṣu prādhānyamityavirodhaḥ /
svabhāvaścobhayātmakaṃ vastu yadi tathaiva śabda upādatte kiṃ tatra vipratiṣidma/
atha vaikaṃ śabdādekaṃ sāmarthyādityavirodhaḥ /
sarvathā 'sti tāvatkarttuḥ prādhānyaprasaktiriti puruṣārtho dhātvarthaḥ prāpnoti /
ayaṃ cāparo viśeṣaḥ 
śabdārtha vastvarthātmanobhayaprakāra syopasarjanatvasyāyaṃ vivekaḥ /
pācakaṃ rājapuruṣaṃ cānayetyatra puruṣasthānayanasambandhinaḥ pācako rājā vā śabdārthamātratayopasarjanatvaṃ pratipanna iti śeṣatvaṃ yāvanna gacchedapi vaḍhedityevamādiṣa tu kartuḥ kāryānsarasambandhānupādānānna śabdārthopasarjanatvamākāśita miti pariśeṣādvastvarthopasarjanatvameva śeṣatvamavadhāryate /
tasmādastyabhidhānapace dhātvarthānāṃ puruṣārthatve pramāṇamiti /
nanvevaṃ satyanabhidhīyamāno 'pi samānapadopāttabhāvanā ucitaḥ prakaraṇātsa eva pratyāsannataraḥ śaknoti dhātvarthasya prayojanākā nirvatayitamityabhidhīyamānapaścatulyatvaṃ prāpnoti/
naiṣa doṣaḥ sa śabdo khacaṇā yāti yaḥ śrutyā nopayujyate /
śrutyarthenopayukte tu lakṣaṇā nāntarīyakī 
vaḍhediti śrutera puruṣaḥ sampratīyate /
vidhirapyarthavānevaṃ kratvarthe 'narthako bhavet 
siddhānte kratusaṃyuktaṃ samāmnāyena vocyate /
yā prakaraṇaprāptyā saṃyukta bādhagocaraḥ 
sarvātāvamatirnityaṃ śrutimūlapramāṇikā /
tena smṛtyarthavācitvānnānuvādo bhavedasau 
yadi prakaraṇaṃ tyatkā puruṣārtheya miṣyate /
tataḥ smṛtisamānārthā naṣṭā mūlaṃ kathaṃ śrutiḥ 
pūrvapakṣāstrayo hyatra bhāṣyakārasya saṃmatāḥ /
pūrvasminmūlamalitvaṃ parayostvanuvādatā 
puruṣaṃ hi parityajya nānṛtaṃ prāpyate ṛtau /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
puruṣe tanniṣiddhaṃ cenniṣiddhaṃ tanāvapi 
vidhirvā saṃyogāntarāt 
kevala puruṣārthatvapace tāvadbhāṣyakāra saṃyogāntaraṃ varṇayati /
smṛtau hi satyaṃ brūyāditi dharmāya satyaniyamaḥ śrūyate nānṛtaṃ vadediti tvanṛtapratiṣedho bhinnau caitāvarthai na cānyat śrayamāṇamanya māṇasyānuvādo bhavati /
tasmādvidhiḥ /
nanu iyyeva puruṣasya vākyapravṛttiḥ satyavacanamanṛtavadanaṃ ca tatra yadā satyaṃ tanniyataṃ tadārthādevānṛtaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ bhavatītyanuvādatvaṃ prāpnotyeva /
naitadevam /
kutaḥ /
saṃyogāntarādeva, sanāmānuvādo bhavati yo 'tyanta samānārthatvenāvadhāryate /
asti ca vidhipratiṣedhayoḥ phalabhedādarthabhedaḥ /
katham 
prajāpativratasthatvāttatrānī kṣaṇayuktitaḥ /
paryudāsena satyasya vidhirityavagamyate 
smārttaḥ puruṣamātrasya saṃyogaḥ svārthasiddhaye /
ayaṃ tu ṛtusaṃyuktapuruṣārthaḥ phalāntare 
kratavo hi svasambandhinā vidhipratiṣedhāvapekṣamāṇāstadatikrame sati viguṇā bhavanti ye puruṣagatā vidhipratiṣedhārate katvantaragatā ivāsya sadasadbhāvayoraviśiṣṭāḥ /
na hi teṣu guṇabuddhimatpanā yenātikame baiguṇyabuddhiḥ syāt /
tena darśapaurṇamāsayoranṛtaṃ vadan narakaṃ ca prāpnuyāt darśapūrṇamā saphala cāvikalamevāpnuyāt /
iti ca smṛtyarthaḥ śrataḥ punaḥ prakaraṇayuktapuruṣadharma ityatraiṣo'rtho vijñāyate /
varjitānutavacana kena puruṣeṇa kṛtau darśapai/rṇamāsau phalaṃ sādhayata iti /
prakaraṇasāmarthyāddhi puruṣagatamapūrvasāghanatvaṃ lakṣayitvā 'nṛtaṃ pratiṣidmatastadatikrame darśapūrṇamāsāpūrvameva vaiguṇyānna syāt/
na tu purupasyaiva kaścitpratyavāyaḥ /
na hi tadānīṃ pratyavāyaḥ kalpyamānaḥ svatantrapuruṣasambandhitvena kalpayituṃ śakyate /
tasmādasti saṃyogāntaramiti vidhiḥ/
evaṃ śukratudharmapace 'pi ṛtapuruṣapratyavāya viśeṣātsaṃyogāntaraṃ vyākhyeyam /
tena nityānuvādastā vanna bhavati /
yastu ṛtudharmatvatadgata puruṣadharmatvayorviśeṣastamupariṣṭādacyāmaḥ /
ubhayathā'pi vidhisiddheridānoṃ nopayujyataiti nocyate /
parastvai /
gṛhṇīma eta dedhiriti pūrvotantravārtike /
ktenaiva kāraṇena puruṣadharma iti vadāmaḥ 
sarvākhyāteṣu kartṛṇāmiṣṭā naivābhidheyatā /
yā tu tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ sā saṃyogāntarato bhavet 
yataḥ kartugata saṃkhyā pratīmaḥ kavacāmataḥ /
tasmādetāvatī śaktistiṅa kāryātpratīyate 
yathaiva kvacidukkāpi karmānyatra na vakṣyati /
tathaivaitasya saṃkhyāpi śabdaśaktervyavasthitā /
yo hi manyate karmaṇaḥ ka cittiṅabhihitasaṃkhyāītvaṃ dṛṣṭamato 'nyatrāpi tena bhavitavyamiti tasya va cittiṅantābhidheyatvadarśanātmarvatrābhidheyatvamapi syāt /
atha tatkathaṃ ciyavatiṣṭhate tataḥ saṃkhyāpi tathaiva vyavasthāsyataityacaudyametat /
tacaitatsyāt ka tṛviśiṣṭā saṃkhyā 'bhidhīyamānā na śakyā karttāramanabhidhāya tantravārtike /
vaktumiti /
uccate 
agṛhīta viśeṣaṇe tadanuraktā viśeṣyabuddhirnopajāyata iti tadguṇamādarttavyam /
na tvanabhihita viśeṣaṇatvena kiṃ cidduṣyati yadi nāmāna bhihitamapi viśeṣaṇaṃ kena ciḍhanyena pratyāyyamānaṃ viśiṣṭa pratyayotpādanāya paryāptaṃ bhavati kiṃ tatrābhidhānānurodhena /
asti ceha bhāvanayaiva pratyāyitasya kartturviśeṣapaṇatvaśaktiriti nābhidhānamapecate /
sarvatra viśiṣṭa pratyayeṣu caitadavasthitam /
na cedanyena śiṣṭā iti /
tatra viśiṣṭapratyaye jāte viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ kiṃ śabdenopāttaṃ kimanyeneti parīkṣāyāṃ yatra yatra viśeṣyamanyataḥ sidhyati tatra viśeṣago śabdavyāpāro yatra viśeṣaṇamanyato labhyate tatra viśeṣye /
sarvatra ca viśiṣṭa pratyayādevārthā pattyaikasya dvayorvā 'vayavayorviśeṣaṇavi śeṣyayorvyāpāraḥ śabde kalpyate /
mā cānyathānupapattirūpatvādananyanabhye viṣaye bhavati /
tadiha viśeṣaṇabhūtaṃ viśeṣyabhūtaṃ caikatvaṃ tāvannānyato labhyate /
yenānabhidheyaṃ kalapyeta /
yadi hi kartā tatpratipādayituṃ śaknuyāttata ākṛtinyāyena sa evābhidheya itarattu vyaktivadgamyamānamityā śrīyate /
tasya tu vyabhicāraṇāśaktatvāde katvamapyabhidheyamevāśrayaṇīyam /
tataśca tatra saṃcaritāyāmabhidhānaśaktau gamyamānāpannaḥ karttā satyapi viśeṣaṇanvenābhidheyaḥ saṃpadyate /
yaḍhā tvekatvameva viśeṣaṇaṃ taḍhāpyavaśyaṃ tadeva prathamāntamabhidhātavyam /
taccedabhihitaṃ cīpaśaktiḥ śabdaḥ karttāramanyataḥ sidhyantamapekṣate /
sidhyati cā tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
sau bhāvanāta iti nābhidhānaśakti kalpanā heturbhavati /
yattvanyānyapi kārakāṇi pratīyante na taiḥ pratītairapratītairvā kaści dupakāro'nupakāro vā bhavati /
sarvathā tāvadyaḥ prārthitaḥ ka rttā sa pratītaḥ yadi tvanyadapi pratīyate kiṃ no bādhyate tena hyapratītena vayaṃ bādhyemāha nābhyadhikapratyayena /
pratītānyapi tu karaṇādīni śabdaśaktivaśātkarca bhinnāṣiṇyā saṃkhyayā na hi tathā yadyatpratītaṃ tattad grahītavyaṃ sarvatra hi pratītyapekṣāyogyatvādigrahaṇe kāraṇaṃ bhavati /
tadatrobhayasiddhena saṃkhyāyāḥ kartṛgāmitvena kāra kānta /
eyanapeścitatvādayogyatvācca sannihitānyapi na sambandhitvaṃ pratipadyante /
na ca teṣāmapi tiṅabhihitasaṃkhyābhilāṣī vidyate /
sarvatra subabhihitasaṃkhyāparicchedyatvāt /
na caiṣā saṃkhyā sāmānyarūpeṇa pratītā satī saṃvandhyantaramapecate /
kathito hi paढ़vākya yorviśeṣaḥ paurvāparyaniyamāt /
tadyāvadeveca dhātvarthaḥ pratītastāvadeva kāpi bhāvanā karttā ca kaścidbhaviṣyatītyavadhāryate /
tataśca pūrvatarapratote karttari saṃkhyā kevalaivābhivoyamānā viśeṣaṇatvaṃ viśeṣyatvaṃ pratipakyate /
yadā bhāvanayā karttā prathamaṃ pratipadyate /
na saṃkhyā saṃgateśvāsti tadatikramakārāma 
nācaudanavyāpārī dhātunā prādhānyenopādīyate yataḥ ka rmaṇo viśeṣapratītamya saṃkhyocyeta mā bhūttasyaiva kartṛlakṣaṇāpanatvātkarmatvamutsṛjya kartṛtva, makartṛtvādeva ca na taḍyāpāro bhāvanā /
tena tathāpi na viśeṣarūpeṇa karmaṇaḥ paryapasthānam /
avaśyaṃ ca puruṣavyāpāra eva prādhānyena vaktavyo 'nyathā hi pa ravyāpāre'sya niyoga eva na bhavet/
ākhyātapadena cākalpitaṃ kartṛtvaṃ padāntaropāttasyāpi nāvirbhavet /
tataśca tvayetyapi tī yā nasyāt /
tayāpāreṇa vānabhibhūtavyāpāraṃ karma tenānāpyamānatvātkarmatvaṃ hitvā ''virbhūtavyāpāratayā kartṛtvameva pratipadyeteti svasaṃbandhatyāgena kartṛsaṃkhyayaiva saṃbadhyeta /
tena pacatiśa bdavadeva pacyataityevamādyabhihitāpi saṃkhyā 'nabhibhūtatvātkatureva prāpnoti na karmaṇa iti /
uccate 
sarvathā 
tadyadi mama karmotpannanakārīṣvapi karttureva saṃkhyā prāpnoti/
tavāpi tarhi tatra kartrabhidhānena bhavitavyam /
atha tatra tava kathaṃ citkatturanabhidhānaṃ tadanmamāpi tatsaṃkhyānabhidhānamityadoṣaḥ /
tadetadavagyamāvāgyāmevaṃ pariharttavyam /
sarvacaiva tāvadīpsitatamatvādastuṇaṃ kārakāntarebhyaḥ karmaṇaḥ prādhānyaṃ bhāvyāṃśena ca tayāpārasya bhāvanāntargatatvam /
tatra yadā tatprādhānyamākhyātenaiva darśayāmīti vivacyate tadā satyapi kartuḥ śabdāryarūpeṇa niṅṅghātubhyāma bhidhīyamāna pradhānabhūtamāmānya viśeṣarūpavyāpāratve tāvatā ca kartṛtvalābhe aparamya vastunakṣāsya prādhānyasya vivakṣitatvātkarmaṇi tatsaṃkhyāyāṃ vā cakārotpattiḥ /
yadā tu khannu tadvidyamānamapyavivakṣitatvādvātu viśeṣavaśena vā naiva tadastītyavagamyate śabdārtharūpaprādhānyamāne vivajñā bhavati tadā supā karmaprādhānyābhivyaktimaṅgīkṛtya karttari tatsaṃkhyāyāṃ vā lakāra utpadyate /
karaṇādīnāṃ tuna vastucacaṇā nāpi śabdalacaṇā prādhānyavivacā 'stīti nityameva bāhya śabdopādeyatvam /
ke citpanarāḥ /
yadaivaṃvidhaṃ śabdasāmarthyamavagamyate yathā'yaṃ karttava saṃkhyāṃ śaknoti vaktumayaṃ karmaṇa eveti /
padāntareṇāpi bhāvanopasthāpanaṃ saiva saṃkhyā 'nanyaviṣayatvenābhihitatvātkarttāramupādāsyate / mantravārtika /
tadyathā śoṇa gando 'ngenānupātte'pyaśve tadgataṃ guṇaṃ vadannātmanaivāśvatvamapi gamayati /
tathā ca satyanenaiva nyāyena sarve gavādayo 'pyanabhidheyāḥ prāpnuvanti /
katham 
etāvatī cekabdaśaktiḥ kalpitā tadgatamevaiṣā guṇaṃ bravīti /
kiṃ tataḥ paraṃ śaktyantarakalpanayā pūrvayaiva vyavahāropapateḥ /
ayaṃ tvevamādiṣvekaśabdopāttatvena saṃbandhaniyamo na śabdaśaktivaśena /
tataḥ kartṛsaṃkhyādiṣvapi tadevābhyupagantavyamityanabhidheyatva hāniḥ /
tatrāpare manyante 
kathaṃ hyaśvatve 'nucyamāne tadavacchinnaraktatva pratyayo jāyeta raktatvaviśeṣo me
aśvatvaṃ naiva śogṇasya viśeṣaṇatayeṣyate /
kasutīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
guṇajātyantaraṃ tvetadvaivāttatsaṃgatiṃ gatam 
sarvapuṃsāṃ svasaṃvedyaṃ pratijāti guṇāntaram /
va cittasya viśeṣeṇa va citmāmānyato 'bhidhā 
atha yaduktaṃ gavādiṣvapi tadgatasaṃkhyādimātrābhidhānādeva jātiviśeṣa siddheranabhidhayatvaṃ prasajyata iti /
tatra bramaḥ 
yadi hi śoṣaṇatvādivagavāśvagatānā mekatvādīnāmapi pratyakṣeṇa viśeṣo jacyeta tata evaṃ kalpyeta /
yadi ca yathā śoṣaprātipadikama vibhaktāvayavaṃ guṇavatvayorvācaka māpadyamānamanekaśaktikalpanābhabādanyata ra vācitvenādhyavasīyamāna maśvatvasya vya bhicāritvenāgamakatvādvyabhicāriguṇāvacanatvenāvadhāritamevaṃ gotvasaṃkhyayorapi samānaśabdābhidhānabhājoranyatarasyāvyabhicāritayā vācakatvamavadhāryeta, na tu tadasti, saṃkhyāyāstāvatmarvatra paricchedātmakatvānna kaścido dṛśyate /
na ca nāvāneka śabda ubhayorvācakatvena saṃbhāvyate /
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ prātipadikena jātyabhidhānādvibhaktyā ca saṃkhyābhidhānā, nna cāneka śabdasyāne kārya kalpanā doṣaḥ /
yadi tatrānekasya śabdasya śaktyanekatvaṃ na kalpyeta tato 'nyatarasyānarthakatvameva bhavet/
na ca saṃkhyā saṃkhyeyayora vyabhicāritvaṃ yenānyataraduccamānamitarasya gamakaṃ syāt /
tathāhi 
nanu ca liṅgaṃ prātipadikenaivoccamānaṃ pratijāti vilakṣa pāmavyabhicārirūpeṇa pravarttamānaṃ śoṣatvāditulyaṃ syāt /
a tadevam 
yadyapi ṭābādayaḥ stroliṅgasya dyotakatvānna bhedena vācakā bhavanti pūrvasyaiva ca śaktyantaramāvirbhāvayanti tathāpi prāk ṭāvādibhyo yacchabdarūpaṃ tastatāvasthe liṅge jātiṃ prati bhaktiḥ kalpitā na paścādapanetuṃ śakyā /
tathā yatra vi bhaktisaṃbandhāt puṃstvaṃ napuṃsakatvaṃ cābhivyajyate tatrāpyevameva jātyabhidhānaṃ yojyam /
yatra tu prāgeva vibhaktestannivṛttau vā satyāṃ śuddhādeva prātipadikādanyataraliṅgapratyayo bhavati ya thā istī nā devadattaḥ śrīḥ marittoyaṃ vārīti /
tatra tathātvābhyupagamepi na kiṃ cihirudvam /
atha vā vināpi śabdavibhāgenārthapratītāvutpādyamānāyāṃ sarvaṃ svasaṃvedyena vibhāgena prathamataraṃ jātiṃ pratipadyate /
kiṃ ca 
tena kāmaṃ liṅgameva jātigamyaṃ bhavenna jātirliṅgagamyā /
nityaṃ copasarjanībhūtamevaitadgamyamānaṃ nārhati prādhānyena pratīyamānāyā jātera bhiṣeyatvaṃ vārayitum /
na ca gopaśvādiśabdadhvanyataraliṅgābhivyaktirjātivadasti /
tasmājjātistāvadabhidheyā sā yatra liṅgaṃ na vyabhicariṣyati tatra gamiṣyatyapi /
yacāpi vyabhicāre satyanyataḥ pratīyate tatra tadeva gamakaṃ tadanugṛhītā vā jātiḥ prātipadikaṃ veti yatheṣṭaṃ kalpyate /
tasmānnatantravārtika /
śoṣāditulyatā /
pacatyādiśabdeṣvapi yadi saṃkhyā sarvakārakāntaravyāvṛttarūpaṇa kartṛmātrānusāriṇī śoṇatvavadupacabhyeta tatastayā nāma karttā gamyatāṃ tāvatā 'pyana bhidheyo bhavatyeva /
yadā tu pūrvoktena nyāyena saṃkhyābhedo na labhyate prativastu cānantānyekatvādijātyantarāṇi na śakyante kalpayituṃ tadā bhāvanāghātvarthābhyāmevopādānamādarttavyam/
kiṃ ca 
yadi śoṇasyāpi kaścidadbhyo 'śvamupanayennaivāsau svayaṃ kliśyet /
saṃkhyāyāśca bhāvānādhātvarthābupanetārāviti na svayamāyasyati /
bhāvanopasthāne cokto viśeṣaḥ /
tasmādanabhidheyasyaiva kartuḥ viśeṣyatva viśeṣaṇatvopapattera pramāṇamabhidhānaśaktikalpana mityavagacchāmaḥ /
evaṃ nyāyenāvadhārite kaścidāgamavirodhaṃ darśayannāca/
prakṛtipratyayā pratyayārthaṃ saha brūta ityācāryopadeśātkarttā śabdārthaḥ karma cetyavagamyataiti /
tathā hi 
nanu sūtrārthenaivāgamavirodhe darśita prakṛtipratyayā pratyayā rthamityetadasaṃbaddvam /
kathamasaṃbaddhaṃ yadā pūrveṇa nyāyena kartuḥ prādhānyamapi pūrvapakṣavādinā darśayitavyam /
tadetadabhidhānaṃ prādhānyaṃ cobhayamapi smṛtisiddhaṃ darśayati /
yasmātprakṛtipratyayau saha brūtaḥ pratyayārthaśca karttā karma ca smaryate tasmātkriyāviśiṣṭayostayorabhidhānādastyeva śrutiprakaraṇavirodha iti /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
tatra laḥ karmaṇi cetyatra tāvaḍekāntenābhidheyatvena kartṛkarmakorupādānam /
katara śavityatra punarekamabhiṣeyatvadarśanam/
anyattu karttaroti parasaptamī na ca śabda saṃniveśe karttā paratrāvasthitaḥ saṃbhavatyata ānarthakyāttadaṅgeṣviti śabde kāryaṃ vijñāyate /
tatraiṣo 'rthaḥ kartṛvācini sārvadhātuke pratyaye paracāvasthitaiti /
sarvathā tāvatpratyayārthaḥ karttavyuktamācāryestasmādayuktamanabhidheyatvānumānamiti /
taducyate 
tatra nāmāgamavirodho yukta udbhāvayituṃ yatra nyāyāgamau samānaviṣayau bhavata, iha tu nyāyasyānya eva viṣayaḥ kiṃ vācyaṃ kiṃ gamyamānamiti /
anya eva vyākaraṇa mate, rekārthaprayuktānāṃ kaḥ sādhuḥ ko 'pabhraṃśa iti /
na cānya viṣayeṇānyaviṣayasya durbalasthāpi bāgho yuktaḥ kimuta vāccagamyamānaviṣayatvena pratyakṣameva sarvasvasaṃvedyasya /
tena yadyapi karttā śabdārtha iti evamācāryā vadeyustathāpi svaviṣayādanyatra vadanto nādarttavyā bhaveyuḥ /
te tu naiva tathā vadanti /
nanu pratyakṣameva sūtramudāhatam /
satyaṃ na tu śāstra svarūpamānocca /
kiṃ takadeśālocanena /
na ca tāvanmātreṇa śāstra viśeṣodbhāvanaṃ śakyam /
kutaḥ 
anya evaikadeśena śāstrasyārthaḥ pratīyate /
anyaśca paripūrṇena samastāṅgopasaṃhanau /
viśeṣeṇa tu vyākaraṇe /
tatra hokekasminpade prāyeṇāṣṭādhyāyī vyāpriyate /
tena laḥ karmaṇi cetyasyaikadeśāntara paripūrṇa yorthastena saha virodhaḥ pariharttavyaḥ /
iha caitāvatā pratyayavidhiḥ paripūryate /

vā 'sarūpo 'striyām /
varttamāne laṭ /
karttari kṛt /
laḥ karmaṇi ca bhāve cākarmakebhyaḥ /
lasya /
tibādayaḥ /
anudāttaṅita ātmanepadam /
śeṣātkarttari parasmaipadam /
yuṣmadasmadupapadā diṣu madhyamādayaḥ /
tiṅastrīṇi cīṇi prathamamadhyamottamāḥ /
tānyekavacana dvivacanaba huvacanānyekaśaḥ /
bahuṣu bahuvacanam/
hyekayordivacanaikavacane iti /
parāṇi ca saṃjñāparibhāṣādirūpeṇa lopāgamavarṇavikārādiśāstrāṇi sarvāeyekaṃ vākyam /
ekavākyatā ca sati viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāve bhavati nānyathā/
sopi ca sāmānādhikaraṇyena vā bhavati samānavibhaktyantānāṃ vaiyadhikaraṇyena vā kriyākārakarūpaḥ śeṣaśeṣirūpa/
tadihānāpayikatvādavayavāntarāṇyapecya lādeśāḥ katari karmaṇi ca bhavantye kasminnekavacanam /
iyorḍirvacanam /
bahuṣu bahuvacanamityeteṣāṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ sāmānādhikatṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
raṣyavaiyadhikaraṇya pravṛttiva cintyate /
tatra tāvaddahaḍokaśabdāḥ saṃkhyāvacanāstāmanabhidhāya saṃkhyeye vṛttyasaṃbhavādityākṛtyadhikaraṇe sthāpitam/
pātañjale'pi ca keṣu bahudhviti praśnapūrvakamupakramya tatra doṣānabhidhāya saṃkhyāvacanatvamevāvadhāritam /
bahutve dinvaikatvayoriti vivaraṇāt /
kathamantareṇa bhāvapratyayaṃ bhāvapradhāno bhavati nirdeśa iti pṛṣṭe bhavati yadā prathama eva guṇaḥ svaprādhānyena vivacyataiti vyākṛtam /
tathā pūrvameva guṇaḥ kaścitvātantryeṇa vidhīyate /
kaścid dravyāṅgabhāvena tato niṣkṛṣya cāparaḥ 
hye kasaṃkhyeyasaṃghāte bahutvamupajāyate /
iye keṣviti bhavettatra yadi saṃkhyeyatantratā 
anekasminnapi prāptiḥ karttari syāttipastathā /
sarvakāraka saṃsthe ca saikatve ca pramajyate 
śāstre hi kāryavaśenāna bhidheyasyāpyabhidheyatvaṃ pāribhā tantravārtike /
ṣikamāśrayate /
na ca tāvatā loke tathaiva prasajyate na cakarmādayo 'nabhidheyā evetyetacchāmle 'bhikṣitam /
kiṃ tarhi ekāntābhidheyakatvādiviśeṣaṇaṃ tāvadbhavantītyetahyākhyātameva /
tasmādviśeṣaṇatāmevaite pratipatsyante /
tadyatra na śāstreṇa na nyāyenābhidheyatvaprāptistatrānabhidheyā vijñāsyante /
yatra punaḥ śāstroktāṃ viśeṣaṇatāmana bhidhīyamānāḥ pratipattuṃ na śakṣyanti tatra nyāyalabhyāmananyagatitvāt abhidheyatāmapi pratipatsyante /
arthāpattyā vā śāstreṇāpyabhidheyanayoktā bhaviṣyanti /
tatra tiṅkṣa bhāvanopasthānāviśeṣaṇatva siddhernāvaśyamabhidheyatvamaṅgīkarttavyam/
susu punaḥ prātipadikārthānāmekatvādona cākārakeṣu kārakāntareṣu ca vyabhicārādanyatarapratipādanaśaktau vijñatāyāmanyasya ca bhāvanāṣātvarthā dargamaka syānabhidhānānna kiṃ cidupasthāpakamastīti svayaṃ kārakamanabhidhāya tadviśiṣṭa saṃkhyā bhighānānupapatteḥ kārakamapyabhidheyaṃ bhavati /
nanu ca kevalakāraka padaprayogābhāvādavaṇyaṃ bhāvyākhyātapadābhihitabhāvanopanītānāmeva kārakāṇāṃ ticiva saṃkhyāsaṃbandho 'vakalpiṣyate /
kathamavakalpate /
yaḍhā vākye svaniyatapadakrameṣu kaढ़ā cidākhyāta śabdātprathama prayuktena subantena vṛścamiti kāraka pratyayo janyamāno nābhidhānamantareṇa sidhyati /
nanu tatrāpi kriyāsaṃbandhātprākārakatvānupapattestāvatkāraka vibhaktyā notpattavyaṃ yāvatkriyāsaṃbandho nopadarśitaḥ /
tataśca kriyāpūrvakatvaṃ saṃpratipadyataiti /
satyam /
vakturevaṃ, śrotā punaḥ prathamameva vṛkṣamiti śruṇoti na tena kriyā tatsaṃbandho vānyataḥ pūrvamavadhāritaḥ 
iyoḥ saṃbandhinoravaśya me kasyetaranirapekṣaṃ pratītisūlamamdhupagantavyam /
tadiha yadi kriyāgamyaṃ kārakaṃ tataḥ kriyā kena pratyāyyataiti vaktavyama /
na ca tāvar̤acaprātipadikaṃ kriyāyā vācakaṃ śākhādimajjātimāṃtravacanatvāt /
nāpi prātipadikārtho gamako vināspi kriyayopapatteḥ /
athocyeta na jātu citkaścinniṣkriya saṃbhavatyato'sti tiṣṭhatyādikā kā cidekāntenāciptā kriyā bhaviṣyati /
atha vā'stirbhavantīparaḥ prathamapuruṣo 'prayujyamāno 'pyastīti gamyataityevaṃ sakriyatvātkārakāpekṣaḥ sekyatīti /
tadnupapannam /
kutaḥ /
tiṣṭhatyādāvupāte 'pi kriyāmātre hyakarma ke /
kartamātramupāttaṃ syānna karmādi niyogataḥ 
sarvacaiva yasya kasya citkāryasya sadasadbhāvadarśanādirūisadasaḍāvātmakatvānabhyupagame satyaikarūpyaṃ parigṛhyate /
tatsadbhāvaḥ parigrahītavyaḥ /
satāmapi pratibandhātkāragāntarābhāvādanyato vā siddheḥ kāryānā rambhāvirodhādasataśca kāryavelāyāṃ devairapyaprāpteranimitta kāryotpādapramādityukta saṃbandhanityatve /
tatkalpitā vācakaśaktinīma pūrvaṃ tāvatprayoga vyāpariṣyate /
viparyaye punarudāsiṣyate /
labdhātmakatvāddā śrautatve satyanumānapratyayaṃ nirākurvanto kāryamārarāsyate /
ataśca siddhā supāṃkamadiyo 'pyarthāstiṅāṃ tu niyatapaurvāparyavaśādekāntena dhātvarthabhāvanābhyāmupasthāpitayoḥ kartakarmaṇoḥ paścātsaṃkhyā 'vagamyataiti na kadā cidapi kārake viśeṣago vācakatṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
śaktikalpanāvasaraḥ /
tataśca nityānumeye karṭa karmaṇo iti siddham tantravārtika /
abhedavarttitvaṃ hi tatpadasāmānādhikaraṇyamasaṃdigdhavācakeṣu kṛdanteṣu paktā devadattaḥ pakka odana ityādiṣu dṛṣṭam /
yatra ca kartakarmavacanatvaṃ nāsti tattra sāmānādhikaraṇyamadṛṣṭaṃ yathā pākādiśabde /
kiṃ ca /
ṭa tacchabdopāttatadbhuta saṃkhyābhedānuvarttanāt /
tathaiva vācakatvaṃ syāt dṛṣṭāntau tāvihāpi ca 
ataśca vācako yenā nabhihitādhikāravihitakārakavibhaktipratibandho dṛśyate /
pacati devadattaḥ pacyate odana iti /
yadi hi vācakatvaṃ na syāt tato 'nabhihite karmaṇi dvitīyā kartṛkara gāyostṛtīyeti ca vibhaktiprāptirna kena citpratibadhyeta /
yathā paccate devadatena pacatyodanamiti /
yatastu khalu pratibandha stenāvagagyate paktṛpakvasādharmyeṇaiva vācakatvaṃ sādharmyādanya hai dharmyaṃ tadevaṃ darśayitavyam /
yatva ca vācakatvaṃ nāsti tatva kārakavibhaktipratibandho 'pi nāsti yathā paccate devadattena pacatyodanamiti /
itaśca bodhakaḥ śabdasta hiśeṣāvabodhanāt /
yathā śrotramakārastha bodhakaṃ śabdabodhanam 
itaścābhidhīyete viśeṣaṇaiḥ saṃbadhyamānatvādiha śobhanaḥ pacati śobhanaḥ pacyate /
yavānayorviśeṣaṇa saṃbandhastavābhimeyatvamapi dṛṣṭaṃ yathā śobhana paktā ramaṇīyaḥ pakka iti /
yatva tvabhidheyatvaṃ nāsti tatra viśeṣaṇasaṃbandhī 'pi na dṛṣṭo yathā śobhanamāsyataiti /
na ca gamyamānasya viśeṣaṇasaṃbandho yathā dhūmaśabdādagneravagatasya na jvalanādibhi saṃbandha iti /
tadetatsarvaṃ nanu karttarekatvādekavacana mityādinaiva darśitatvādvāṣyakāreṇa na prapacitam /
tadgatasaṃkhyāyogyatvaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyādibhivinā nopapadyate /
tasmādabhidhānapakṣa eva nyāyya iti /
atrābhidhīyate /
yattāvaduktaṃ vācakaḥ pacatyādiśabdaḥ kartṛkarmaṇoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāditi /
tatra yadi vācakaśaktyā istitvamanumoyeta tataḥ pūrvoktanāthapattimaṅgena sarvapramāṇānupapatteranupalabdhivirodha sarvaśaktīnāṃ cārthāpattirevaikaṃ pramāṇaṃ sā cehānyathā 'pyupattarnirākṛ tā /
anumānavirodhaśca /
nābhidhātā kartṛkarmaṇoḥ patantravārtika /
catyādiśabda stadatyantāvinābhūtārthābhidhāyitvāt /
yo yadatyantāvinābhūtārthābhivāyo ma tasya na vācakaḥ yathā śiṃśapāśabdo vṛkṣatvaniyataśiṃśapātvasya tathā karta karmaṇī nābhidheye tiṅā tadabhidheyāparityāgāt /
tadyāpārādinā 'pi ca pratīyamānatvād dravyatvavat /
tasminneva śiṃśapāśabde catvavat /
kārakatvādākhyātānabhidhānaṃ karaṇādivat /
tiṅśabdasyāvā cakatramā khyātatvādāsyataityādivat /
etadapi śakyaṃ vaktum /
nanvacandraḥ śaśītivade tallaukika viruddha manumānam /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
yadi vayaṃ pra tyāyyatvaṃ pratyāyakatvaṃ vā ninḍavīmahi tato lokaviru iṃ brayāma /
vācyavācakaśaktipratiṣedhastvayaṃ kriyate na ca tena lokaprasiddhivirodhaḥ /
pratyayotpādamātreṇa kṛtārthasya lokasyābhidheyagamyamānadyotya viṣaya rūpārthacatuṣṭaya vivekā nādarāt /
yadi tu lokaprasiddhaṃ pratyāyya pratyāyakatvamātraṃ sādhyeta tataḥ prāguktena bhāvanāhārapratītyabhyupagamātsiisādhanam /
lokavirodho'pi tavaivāpadyeta /
kutaḥ /
loko yadanyataḥ siddhaṃ nābhidheyaṃ tadicchati /
yathā śrotragṛhītatvātsvarūpaṃ nābhidhīyate 
yathaiva pācakādiśabdeṣu dravyaprādhānyātmattvarūpa pratyayo bhavati evaṃ suptiṅanteṣvapi syāt /
tataśca yathaiteṣveva pācakaṃ brahi pācakena kṛtaṃ pācakāya dehīti kārakāntarayogo bhavati evaṃ pacatyodanamityādiṣvapi prāpnoti /
tammācchaktimahuvyakārakapakṣe 'dhyavaśyaṃ niṣkṛṣya śaktimātraṃ muptiṅbhyāmabhidheyameṣṭavyam /
tathā sati hi /
āvirbhūtaikayā śaktyā dravyamātmavaśīkṛtam /
na śaktyantarayogitvaṃ tadaiva pratipasyate 
pacati devadatta ityava kartatvaṃ tāvadbhāvanayaiva bodhitaṃ yā 'pi saṃkhyā sā'pi tiṅā kimanyadavaśiṣyate ya darthaṃ vibhaktirutpadyeta kathaṃ punara nekakārakasaṃnipāte sati kartatvameva bhāvanayā devadattasyāvagamitaṃ na kārakāntaratvamiti /
yogyatāvaśeneti ke cit /
devadatto hi pākasya kartṛtvayogyo na karaṇakatvādiyogyaḥ /
na cākārakasya sataḥ śrākhyātena saṃbandho 'vakalpate /
tasmātkatṛtvaṃ gṛhṇātīti na tvetatkāṣṭhāni pacantītyatva saṃbhavati /
na hi tāni kartṛtvayogyāni kiṃ tarhi karātvāṇīti prasiddhametat /
athocyeta naivāva kāṣṭhānāṃ katattvaṃ kiṃ tarhi karaṇatvamevedamuktena nyāyena kartṛtvava tvāṃ vibhatinotpādayati /
evaṃ sthālī pacatotyadhikaraṇatvaṃ saptamaum taṇḍulāḥ pacantīti karmatvaṃ dvitīyām kuśūla pacatītyapādānatvaṃ pañcama brāhmaṇāpacantoti saṃpradānatvaṃ ca caturthī sarvatra yogyatvasya nirṇaya kāraṇatvāditi /
tadnupapannam /
kartṛpratīteḥ sarvasya svasaṃvedyatvāt /
āha /
naiveyaṃ kartṛtvapratītirnānākārakapratotireva tu satī tiṅācya kartṛtvaprasiddhivāsanāvaśena tatmāmānādhikaraṇyabuḍyā kartṛ vadābhāsate /
yastu nipuṇa paśyati tasya bhavatyeva tava tava kāraka vivekaḥ /
tathā hi /
sthālyāderyo 'pi kartṛtvaṃ tadānīmadhyavasyati /
nādhārādanyathābhūtaṃ vyāpāraṃ so'pi vindati 
sarvatraivārthadaye sambhavatyanyatararūpavivacā yuktā sambhavati ca sarvakārakāṇāṃ khavyāpārāpekṣayā kartṛtvamiti purastātpratipāditam /
na hi pradhānakriyāgataṃ kārakavaicityaṃ mvavyāpāraviṣayāt kartṛtvādinopapadyate /
tasmā ttadeva vivacitamiti nyāyyam na kārakāntarasaṃkhyābhidhānamiti /
evaṃ ca sati yatkarmasaṃkhyā 'pi kvacidabhidhīyate tavoktaṃ kāraṇaṃ na ca tadanyāvastīti vyavasthā /
tadā tvanabhihitādhikāro 'yevaṃ kariṣyate /
anabhiṣṭite karmaṇa ekatve dile bahutve cetyādi /
kutaḥ /
vibhaktayo vidhīyante yatra tastha viśeṣagām /
yujyate 'nabhidhānaṃ hi na punastahiśeṣaṇe 
yasya ca karmādayo vācyā yasya ca tahiśiṣṭā ekatvādayastayorubhayorapyanabhihitatvaṃ karmādiviśeṣagām /
anabhihite karmaṇi dvitīyā nimihite vā karmaṇi ye ekatvādayo varttante teṣu dvitīyeti /
yadyapi copasarjana karmādayastathāpi viśeṣagona saṃbadhyante /
samosasyaṃ hyupasarjanaṃ viśeṣaṇairna sambadhāte vākyasyaṃ tu ṛisya rājñaḥ puruṣa itivatsaṃvadhyamānaṃ dṛṣṭamevamādi /
evaṃ ca vṛttivākyayorviśeṣo bhaviṣyati /
vākyasthāca karmādayo 'taḥ satyapyupasarjanatve śakna vanti samānavibhaktikānabhihitādhikāra viśeśyatāṃ pratipattuṃ tataśca pacati devadatta iti tiṅādibhiranabhihitastha kartuḥ saṃkhyāmabhidhātuṃ tṛtīyā prāpnotyeva /
gatārthavādaprāptiriti cenna /
bhīṣmādibhiranekāntāt /
uktaṃ hyetatkaṭadvitīyayokte 'pi karmaṇi bhauṣamādibhyastadutpattiriti /
yadi ca tṛtīyā gatārthatvānnotpadyate tataḥ prathamāvācyā 'pi saṃkhyā gataiveti kāmaṃ sā notpadyate /
kevalaprātipadika prayogāsambhavāttadutpattiriti cet /
na evaṃ sati yathāvihitatatoyāprasaṅgāt /
na caiṣa nyāyena prasaṅga āpāditaḥ kiṃ tarhyāgamena /
na cāgamavirodhe nyāyaḥ kāryakṣamo bhavati /
tasmādanabhihitaśabda eva lakṣaṇayā viśeṣātmanā 'navagatṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
tatve varttate pacativa vyateśabdābhyāṃ ca saṃkhyāsaṃbandhādarāhiśeṣa rūpeṇa karta karmaṇo gamyete tammāttattadvibhaktirnotpasyate kārakāntarāṇi na kadā cidevaṃ viśeṣarūpeṇa pratīya ntaiti svavibhaktaurutpādayanti /
kārakatvāviśeṣe 'pi ca yathā karttakarmaṇoreva viśeṣapratītiḥ saṅkhyāsambandhaśca bha vatīti tathoktam /
yatta, bhāvotpannalakārapakṣeṇa vyabhi cāge 'neha pacyate neha bhujyate ityādiṣa pacimālavivakṣāyāṃ karta karmaṇoranāśrayaṇāt dhātvarthabhāvanayorāśayate tataścāgamakatvamiti /
tatrocyate /
tulyo 'bhidhānapakṣe 'pi sa doṣaḥ śabdagocaraḥ /
vācakasyāpyanekānto gamakasyeva neṣyate 
lakāraṃ yamāṇamutsṛjyādeśā gṛhyantaiti śrutibādhaḥ /
athāpi lakārasyaiva vācyā kamadiyo 'pyucyante tathā 'pi tenānabhidhīyamānāḥ santaḥ prāgādeśotpatterna śakyāstathā 'dhyavasātum /
ante ca nyāyavirodhaḥ sthita eva /
ataśca kasmiṃścidasama ase 'vaśya kalpanoye varamabhidheyatvameva pāribhāṣikaṃ kalpita me kāntasyāśrayaṇīyatvāt /
na hi kathaṃ cidapi lāvasthāyāmapāribhāṣikamabhidheyatvaṃ sambhavati /
tena laḥ karmaṇi cetyādeśadvāreṇa lokavedārthamarthādeśanasuta svaśāstre vyavahārārthamiti parīkṣāyāṃ yadi lokavedayostiḍācyatvaṃ yuktyā 'vakalpayiṣyate tatastādardhyaparikalpanaṃ yuktam athānavaklṛptistataḥ svaśāstrārthatvamiti /
tatra tu lokavedārthatvasya pūrvaṃ nirākṛtatvāt pariśeṣataḥ svaśāstrārthatā /
tenaitaduktaṃ bhavati /
pāṇinermama kartṛ karmaṇī lakārābhihite draṣṭavye iti /
kiṃ punarasya prayojanaṃ yadā na lokavedayoste tathopalabhyete /
yadyapi ca tatra nāsti prayojanaṃ svaśākhe tvasti /
kathaṃ nāmānabhihitādhikāreṇa lakāraprayāge tayorabhihitatvāśrayaṇātparyudāsaḥ syāditi /
tasmādyadyapi paramārthato nābhidhīyete tathā'pi śākhe 'bhihitavadāśrayaṇāinabhihitādhikāravihita bibhakto na lakṣyete iti parihṛtaḥ kārakavibhaktiprasaṅgaḥ /
yattu tadviśeṣābhidhānāditi ta cchiṃśapādiśabdara nai kāntikam /
śiṃśā śabdo hi na tāvaha kṣatva pārthivatvadravyatva sattā prameyatvajñeyatvānāmabhidhāyako 'tha ca tahiśeṣameva śiṃśapāmabhidhatta /
tena yathā 'sya sāmānyamanabhidhāya viśeṣābhidhānaśaktirna viruvyate yathā ca cakṣuṣaḥ sāmānyamanityatvamagṛhato 'pi rupagrahaṇaśaktirna virudhyate yathā ca bhavato 'pi dravyamamabhidhāyaiva tiṅā tadviśeṣaḥ kartṛtvamucyate tathā sama ka bhidhānāhate tadviśeṣasaṃkhyābhidhānaṃ draṣṭavyam /
yadapi gamyamānasya viśeṣaṇasaṃbandho nāstyatastatsambandhadarśanādabhidhānamiti tadapyākṛtyaruṇādhikaraṇayorubhayathā pi darśanānnirākṛtam /
api ca madhuro rasaḥ snigdhaḥ śoto guruścetyanenā nai kāntikatvam /
ava hi madhurarasasya guṇatvāt guṇāntaraiḥ śītādibhiḥ saṃbandho nāvakalpate ityetatpratipāditaṃ dravyaṃ saṃbadhyate na ca kathaṃ cidapi rasaśabdasya dravyavacanatvam /
tathā 'khasahasreṇa nagaraṃ muṣitāmati gamyamānānāmeva sādināṃ moṣakriyāsaṃbandhaḥ /
yatta va ciḍūmādī rūpādau vā na dṛśyate na tāvatā sarvatra sthitiḥ kalpayituṃ śakyate /
tasmānnābhidheyaḥ karttā tatantravārtike /
taśca śrautatvābhāvāntra prakaraṇaṃ vādhyate /
yattu karmadharmapakṣe darśapūrṇamāsa vidhinaiva vihitatvāt prātyātmiko vidhiranardhakaḥ syāt tasmātpuruṣārthateti tatra brūmaḥ /
yāvanna vidhisaṃmparśastāvannāsya prayojanam /
vinā ca tena dhātvartho na kratvaṅgaṃ pratīyate 
smṛtau ca yadannṛtavadananimittaṃ prāyaścittaṃ tadeva kataṃtryaṃ yadyanuvādaḥ /
vidhau punarasya yājurvedikatvāt bhraṣasya yajurvedato yajño vinaṣṭa ityanvāhāryapacane bhuvaḥ gvāheti hotavyam /
smṛtestvanyataramūlatvānavadhāraṇād na vedabhreṣanimittaprāyaścitāvadhāraṇaṃ syāt /
evaṃ mūlamūlibhāvābhyupagame 'pi smṛtyaiva tadarthastadatikramañcānusṛta iti tadīyameva prāyaścittam /
nanu tavāpi yājurvedikatvātjñānāttadvedaprāyaścittameva bhavet /
naitadasti /
etaḍyāhavanīyādiviṣayatvādāhitāgtyadhikāramavalambate 'nṛtapratiṣedhaśca puruṣamāvatrarmatvādanāhitāgnerapyavasthitaḥ /
tenāsya tāvadavaśyaṃ smārttaṃ prāyaścittamapekṣa goyam /
taccedapekṣita me katvānnimittasyā hitāgnerapi ta deva yuktamiti vaidikaprāyaścittābhāvaḥ /
kiṃ ca /
yajñe 'nyatamavedāṅge bhraṣṭe naimittikaṃ śrutam /
ayajñāṅgavināśe tu na tasyāvasarī bhavet 
sarve hi samidādayaḥ kratvantaragatāḥ skhobaśakhajapādayaśca pūrvapacavādinaḥ puruṣasaṃskārāḥ te ca yājamānāstapradhānatvātkarmavaditya nenādhikaragona yājamānāḥ syuḥ tatva samaudādaunāṃ yāgātmakatvād dravyatyāgavyāpāreṇa dīkṣaṇoyādivadubhayathāpi yājamānatvāt /
tahadeva ca yajamānaviṭaḍāvapi tantreṇa prayoga iti na kaściḍiśeṣo dṛśyate /
ye tu stotraśakhajapādayaste guṇabhūta kartṛkarmaniya masamadhīṃ pradhānaniyamānadhikṛtāṃ pradhānaugātrādimamākhyāṃ bādhitvā dantadhāvanādivadyajamāna kartakā bhaveyuḥ /
yajamānabiṭaḍau ca sādhāraṇadravyatyāganyāyena tantratvaṃ na sambhavatīti pratiyajamānaṃ bhidyeran /
pratiṣedheṣvapi ca yadā vidhyaṃśa evamavadhāritaḥ kratuyuktapuruṣopakāryanṛtavadanamiti tadā'syaivānṛtaviśiṣṭapratiṣedhādayamartho bhavati yajamānenātmasaṃskārārthamāśīḥ prayogādiṣu yaducyate tatra vaikalpikāvadhāraṇe kharūpoccārago vā mṛṣātvaṃ na karttavyamanyava tvanyeṣāṃ ca yatheṣṭavāditvamiti /
śuḍakratudharmapratiṣedhe tu yāvat katau kiṃ ciddadanaṃ yajamānasyavijāṃ vā'nṛtaṃ prasajyate tatsarvaṃ na karttavyaṃ kratusaṃbandhitvāviśeṣāt ataśca yathaiva yajamānena vrīhimayaṃ saṃkalpya na yavamayo dātavyaḥ /
tathaivādhvarthyādibhirapyanantaraṃ pakṣaṃ kariṣyāma ityuktā na lāghavādivaśena punarvisaṃvaditavyam /
yadapi ca punaḥ saṃskārārthaṃ kiñcittadapi kratvarthāśenaiva varjayitavyam /
nanu ca pratiṣedhārthe guṇabhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ tata ādhvaryavasamākhyā niyāmiketi praṇītāyanādivadadhvaryurako 'nnṛtapratiṣedhamavalambeta /
satyamavalambeta yadi pratiṣedhārtho'nuṣṭheyo bhavet /
ayaṃ tvanuṣṭhānābhāvātmakatvānna karttṛviśeṣamapekṣate /
śrutyaiva ca pratiṣedhaḥ prāptyā saṃbandhaḥ sa yatna prāptistatva khasāmadhyena gacchan na śakyate samākhyayā vārayitum /
nanu vadedityetāvaddidhyāṃśamātramālocyamānaṃ samākhyā niyaṃsyati tataśca pratiṣedho 'pi tadanusāritvānniyato bhaviṣyati /
naitadevam /
paryavasite hi śāstrārthe tatkarttarapekṣāyāṃ satyāṃ samākhyā vatarati /
na ca vadedityetāvataḥ śāstrārthatvaṃ vijñāyate /
pra tiṣedhasaṃvandhādi tadanuvādatvena sthitam /
na cānūdyamānasya śrutamapi viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavatīti grahādhikaraṇe sādhitam /
kisuta mamākhyayā vidhīyamānapadārthakartaviśeṣasaṃbandhamāla eka vyāpriyate /
tasmādandyamānatvāidanaṃ na viśeṣyate /
pratiṣedho 'pi tadgāmau viśeṣṭuṃ naiva śakyate 
snānaṃ tāvadyogyatayaiva malāpakarṣaṇārthatvātpuruṣārthaṃ gamyate tīrthaviśeṣaṇaṃ ca sukhāvataratvād duḥkhāvatārādatoryādyāvartayat puruṣasyopakaroti na kratoḥ /
yadapi ca smaraṇaṃ bhojanādipūrvabhāviniyamarūpeṇa tadapi tadarthasyaiva niyamādṛṣṭaṃ puruṣagāmyeva karoti tenāvadhāritaprayojanena saṃbadhyamānamtīrthaniyamo 'pi puruṣārtho vijñāyate /
ta trāpyakaṃ tāvaddaṣṭameva prayojanamavataraṇa sukham /
athāpyuddhṛtodakādinivṛttirūpo niyamo na dṛṣṭaṃ sādhayatītyadṛṣṭaṃ kalpyate tathā 'pyastyeva phalaṃ tīrthameva hi sajātānāṃ bhavatīti /
na caivaṃ vākyāt puruṣārthasaṃyuktasya prakaraṇamauśvaramasaṃyukta prakaraṇāditi sthitatvāt /
tathā yadyapi brayādityanana karttā nopāttastathā'pi jañjayamānaśabdaḥ kṛdannatvātkarttari kṛditi cānatyaparassāra puruṣasaṃyuktasyeti ka pu pā /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
gātkarṭa viśeṣagaṇaṃ puruṣamupādatta tena svāvākyopāttana saṃyukta mantrābhidhānaṃ prakaraṇagrāhyatvaṃ na pratipadyate puruṣasaṃyoge cāstyeva tatphalam /
prāṇāpānayorātmani dhāraṇacirajīvitvam /
tasmātpuruṣamātradharmā evaṃjātīyakā iti /
prakaraṇaviśeṣādā tayuktasya saṃ skāro dravyavat 
puruṣadharma ityetābadlīmaḥ /
yattu puruṣamāvadharmastataśvotkarṣa ityetadasahyam /
kutaḥ /
avirodhātmamāveśe lagyamāne pramāṇayoḥ /
bāgho na yujyate karttuṃ na ca dūrātphalaśrutiḥ 
yathā hi vraudyādi prokṣaṇādibhiḥ saṃbadhagramānaṃ na ca tāvatprakaraṇena viśeṣyate/
atha cānarthakābhayādiprakṛṣṭaphalakalpanāpramāṇābhāvācca kratusādhanatvena prayojanavatvācca prakṛtaṃ gṛhyate /
tathā 'tra phalakalpanābhavātpratyāsattyanurodhena prākaraṇikana abhyamānagrahaṇaṃ kriyate /
na hi tatsambhave 'nyaphalakalpanāpramāgāṃ labhyate /
nanu ca klṛptamevānayoḥ phalamityuktam /
satyamuktaṃ na tvaudṛśa na śabdena phalamucyate kāmaśabdopabandhābhāvāt /
etadeva ca nāva vidhāyakaṃ śabdamupalabhāmahe ityāha /
phalavidhānaṃ haudṛśana śabdena na kriyataiti vakṣyāmaḥ /
itarathā punarbrūyādityavāpyastyeva vidhivibhaktirityayukta meva vidhāyakābhāvavacanam /
na hi dhattaityetasyāvidhāyakatvādapālambho bhavati /
sarvacaiva phalāṃśasyāvidheyatvāt /
tasmādyayoktameva yojanīyam /
dravyasaṃskāra karmasvityanena cārthavādatvaṃ vacyate /
phalaṃ tu tatpradhānāyāmiti ca kāmapadopatradāyāṃ tadarthatvam /
āha /
puruṣasya saṃskārakamiti gṛhṇīma iti saṃskāraśabdoccāraṇātkratuyuktapuruṣadharmatvamabhyupagacchati na hi svatantraḥ phalavatvā tsaṃskāra ityabhidhīyate /
darśapūrṇamāsāveva kurvata ityetanneti kā 'bhiprāya /
sarvathā tāvajjanyamānadharmatveneṣa gamyatṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
māna ānarthakyena laukikānnivaryeta /
yastu jyotiṣṭomādau nañjabhyamānaḥ sa dārśapūrṇamāsikavadeva saprayojana ityaśakyo varjayitumityataḥ kratumātrayuktapuruṣadharmo bhavati /
asyottaraṃ gūḍhābhiprāyam /
saṃskṛtena tu tena prayo janaṃ nāstīti /
kutaḥ /
na saṃbandhī nivatasya yathaivātithyakarmaṇā /
śrutyādibhira saṃyogāttathaivāsya kriyāntaraiḥ 
vidhestve kaśrutitvādaparyāyavidhānādityatra sarveṣāmevāṅgānā meka prayojanakalpanayaikaṃ vidhiṃ vaccati /
sa ca prayogavacanena vidhīyamānānāṃ bhaviṣyati prātyātmikavidhīnāṃ paryāyapravṛtta /
puruṣaśca yena pravartyate sa vi dhiḥ /
aṅgapradhānavatyāṃ ca bhāvanāyāṃ yugapatpuruṣani yogaḥ /
tasmāt prātyātmikānāmanuvādatvama /
atrābhidhīyate /
hāvayetau granthau sādhū /
katham /
pūrvastāvantra cāvihitamaṅga bhavatītyanayā copapattyā na viruḍaḥ /
ukta hyatahidhādanāśrīyamāṇe dhātvarthamātrasya mādhyatvānniṣprayojana ve sati na śakyamaṅagatvaṃ kalpayituṃ tena tāvaddidhiḥ /
atha cānuvādaḥ kathaṃ parveṇa vidhināṅgatvaṃ prakalpya prayogavacanaṃ yāvannīyate tāvantaṃ ca kālamasau vidhiṇāvatiṣṭhate /
prayogavacanagrahaṇe tu satitadaṅgatāsaṃsparśādeva puruṣapravṛttisidderanuvādatvam /
ataḥ prāk prayogavacanasamarpaṇāddidhiravena vinā na vyavahāraḥ sidhyatīti vidhiḥ /
uttarakāle tu tata eva pravṛttisiddheranuvāda iti ubhayamapi sādhūktam /
vyapadeśādapakṛṣyeta 
prakaraṇa honasyātyantamavidyamānatvā ḍākyasaṃyuktaddā tadbhutavidhisaṃsparśādeveti ka pu pā /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
daśopasattvaṃ prakaraṇenāgṛhyamāṇamutkṛṣyata ityadṛṣṭānta /
śaṃyau ca sarvaparidānāt 
śaṃthāviti brāhmaṇāvagoraṇādipratiṣedhavākyopalakṣagām /
tatra pūrvavadeva pakṣāḥ teṣāmapi prākaraṇikaṃ saṃbandhaiyamadhyekīkṛtya nirdaṣṭaṃ kratudharmaḥ śuddhapuruṣadharmaśceti hāveva pacau /
samastena cānnṛtavadanapratiṣedhanyāyena kratvarthasyāvagoraṇasya pramajyamānasya pratiṣedhaḥ /
kā ca tatra pramakti /
caturbrāhmaṇa sādhyatvāddarśapūrṇamāsayostadāna tyartha sāmadānabhedadaṇḍeṣu pramajyamāneṣvanvāhāryadānenānamayediti gamyate /
yadā tanmātreṇa nānamanti tadā punaryathā dānādānatirbhavati tathā prayatyamāne laukikopāyaprasaktau satyāmayaṃ daṇḍaprakāro 'vagoraṇādiḥ pace prāproti sa pratiṣidhyate /
na karttavyaṃ tena tadyatirekopāyāntarāśrayaṇaṃ kāryamityuktaṃ bhavati tathā prāpte'bhidhīyate /
vākyena sarvasaṃyogātsarvebhyo varadānataḥ /
phalasya kalpitatvācca neṭa prakaraṇagrahaḥ 
tāmaparudhya yajeteti hi sāmānyataḥ sarvammādeva kratvanuṣṭhānādasau nirvārttitā kathaṃ saṃvāde prasajyeta /
puruṣasya tu svātantryātsarvakālasaṃvāde prāpte niṣedhasyārthavattā /
yadi ca smṛtirevamarthā vidyate tato mūlamūlibhāva evābhyupagantavyaḥ na hi kena cinnityānuvādatvamuktam /
annapratiṣedhāca 
itaśca puruṣamāvadharmaḥ /
kutaḥ /
prāyovacananirṇeyaṃ saṃdigdhaṃ vastu varṇitam /
asaṃdigdha puṃdharmo nāsyā annamiti smṛteḥ 
prakaraṇāmrānastha hotadeva prayojanaṃ kathaṃ nāma tadaṅgatvaṃ vijñāyeteti yadyaprakaraṇādhītasyāpi karmāṅgataiva syātataḥ prakaraṇāmrānamanarthakaṃ bhavet /
yatastu vedenaiva prakaraṇāprakaraṇāmnānavivekaḥ kṛtaḥ tato 'vagamyate nūnaṃ prakaraṇādhītānāṃ puruṣadharmatvamiti /
adravyatvāttu śeṣaḥ syāt 
yadyapi tāvaddiśiṣṭavidhānaṃ tathā 'pi karmaśeṣa eva syādanyathā hi phalaṃ kalpyeta /
nanu kratusaṃbandho 'pi ka lpayitavya eva /
satyaṃ pramāṇavato hi tatkalpanā /
kamaiṇaśca sāmānyena prayojanākāṅkṣāyāṃ karmaivopatiṣṭhate tena tatsaṃbandhaḥ pramāṇavān na khargasaṃbandha evaṃ ca manyate /
ya thā yāgadānahī mānmuktvā nānyat pradhānakarmatvaṃ pratipadyate na ceha yāgāditvamasti saṃpradānādyabhāvāt /
ata śrītpattikenāṅgatvena karmaśeṣatvam /
atha vā dhāraṇa metat śrūyate taccotpattyaiva ghāryamāṇaśeṣabhūtam /
na ca laukikasya niṣprayojanatvātsaṃskārārhatvam /
ataḥ karmāṅgabhṛtayorvāsohiraṇyayorvidhiḥ /
