atha vā tata evānekārthavidhidoṣātsati ca saṃbhave balādguṇe vidhiśaktisaṃcāragājiraṇyadhāraṇaṃ hiraṇyaṃ hastena bhavati atha gṛhṇāti hiraṇya haste saṃpradāya ṣoḍaśinā stuvataityevamādivākyavihitamandā suvargātā vidhīyate vāsaḥ paridhattaiti caitahihite vāsasi śobhanatvam /
evaṃ ca sūtrakārāṇāṃ hi ragayamiti jātahṛpaṃ pratīyādityādiparibhāṣaṇasyaitadeva mūlam /
anyathā rajatajātarūpasādhāro sati hiraṇyaśabde 'nyatarāvadhāraṇamūlamanyat kalpyaṃ syāt /
adravyatvāditi ca nāva dravyaṃ vidhīyate kiṃ tarhi taviśeṣamātravidhānametat ataśca yaca dravyaṃ tavānena gantavyamiti /
yattvatra bhāṣyakāreṇa devatāgrahaṇaṃ kṛtam /
tadutsūtvamayuktaṃ ca pradhānaṃ hi japādyapi 
homāstu vyavatiṣṭherannāhavanīyasaṃyogāt 
yaśca vyavatiṣṭherannete homā vaidekeṣveva na sarvatra bhaveyuḥ / kutaḥ/
samānadeśatā nityamiṣyate 'ṅgapradhānayoḥ /
na ca kṛṣyādibhiḥ sākrameṣāṃ syāt tulyadeśatā 
varuṇo vā evaṃ gṛhṇāti yo 'śvaṃ pratigṛhṇātīti pāpena grahaṇaṃ yasmintraśvapratigṛhe sa nimittaṃ pratīyate ta dapi ca pāpagṛhaṇaṃ prāptamanadyate /
yadi hi vidhīyate tataḥ kadā cidetaddākyasāmarthyādeva vaidike'pi syāt /
na tu vidhauyate sarvaphalānāmavidheyatvāt /
na ca tatra karmavidhānaṃ vidheyasya karmaṇa pāpaphalatvāsaṃbhavāt /
na cehāśvapratigṛha pratiṣidhyate tadaśravaṇāt /
nimittasaṃbandhamātropayogācca /
tammādatyanta saṃbandhād yatva pratiṣedhastava doṣaḥ /
sa ca laukikasya pratiṣedho na kesariṇo dadāti nobhayatodataḥ pratigṛhṇātauti /
nanvayamapi pra tiṣedhaḥ sāmānyenaiva śrayate /
satyaṃ tanaitra tu laukikasyeti brūmaḥ /
itarasya viśeṣavidhisaṃsṣṭaṣṭasya pratiṣedha viṣayatvāsaṃbhavāt /
ataśca doṣasamabhivyāhṛtādiṣṭirapi laukikaviṣayā syāt /
nanu ca nimittabhāvāduddiśyamāno 'khaprātagaho na doṣeṇa viśeṣṭuṃ śakyataiti vidhīyamāneṣṭistutimātrapare doṣasaṃkīrttane vaidiko 'pi nimittaṃ bha vet /
uvyate /
viśeṣaṇatayā naiva doṣo 'yaṃ kalpyate mayā /
doṣanirghāta kāryeṣṭi sāmarthyāllaukikāṅgatā 
yadi vaidike dāturiṣṭiriti kṛtvā satyapyapratigādyāthājyayājananimitte pratigṛhītṛṇāṃ pāpe doṣarahitanimittamucyate /
tato laukike 'pi śūdrādibhya upādāne davyatyapi pratigrahītari dātustadvāreṇāduṣṭatvāddoṣarahitameva nimittam /
atheha pratigṛhauṭavyāpāro nimittaṃ sa ca duṣṭa iti gṛhyate tattulyaṃ vaidike 'pi /
atha vaidike dāturlaukike pratīgṛhīturiṣṭiriti kalpyate tatrāpyupapattiviśeṣo vaktavyaḥ /
kiṃ ca /
yo 'śvapratigṛhādeva doṣaḥ so 'va pratīyate /
dāḍhadoṣastu sarvatra tulyo 'śvairna viśeṣyate 
yadi pratigraho na vidhoyeta kathaṃ tasyetikarttavyatā vidhīyeta /
kimiti vā tasminnakṛte karmavaiguṇyaṃ syāt /
atra vadāmaḥ /
ṛtviggdho dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāditi dānaṃ vidhīyate /
lobhādevārjjanāṅgatvātmāptasteṣāṃ pratigrahaḥ 
karmavidhānavāko yo doṣaḥ śrūyate sa nirdhātyatvenāvadhāryate /
yaścātra doṣa upātto nāsau laukikasya satyapi pratiṣiddhatve kutaścitpramāṇadgamyate jalodaraṃ hyatra varu gagahaṇarūpeṇāpāttam /
naca kasyāñcidvaidya kasaṃhitāyāṃ laukiko śivapratigraho nidānaṃ śrūyate nāpi pratyakṣānumānādibhigamyate /
na ca vākye na kesariṇo dadāti nobhayatodataḥ pratigṛhṇatoti śrūyate /
nāpyetasya vā kyasya tatpratipattau vyāpāro vidyamānānuvādena tatra nirghātārthakarmavidhimālaparatvāt /
yastu doṣaḥ pratiṣedhavākyānnarakapātātmakaḥ kalpitaḥ sa iha nopātantravārtike /
to varuṇo vāetaṃ gṛhṇātītyanenābhidhātumaśakyatvāt /
atha pāpamātraṃ dṛṇotīti varuṇastadgṛhṇātītyevamabhidhīyate tato yā tāvaḍaruṇagṛhītaśabdasya jalodaraviṣayā samudāyaprasiddhiḥ sā parityaktā /
yā tvavayavaprasiḍiḥ sā vaidike'pi tyāge duḥkhadarśanāt /
pratigrahe ca rakṣaṇapoṣaṇādinā kleśātkiṃciharuṇātmakaṃ vidyataityeva saṃbhavatīti na śakyaṃ tadddā reṇeṣṭellaukika viṣayatvamavadhārayitum /
rakṣaṇapoṣaṇadinā kleśeneti pratigrahoṭavyāpārasya nimittatvenānivāritatvādevaṃ bravīti /
atha vā dāturapi prāk parakhatvāpādanādeṣa kleśo 'stīti gamayitavyam /
dharmo'pi ca śṛṇotyeva naraṃ saṃsāravarttinam /
na hi kevalapāpena dehenācchādyate naraḥ 
yatra vidhyuddeśaḥ saṃdigdhaḥ tatra vākyaśeṣānnirṇayo na virudhyate /
yava svasaṃdigdhastava tahalauyastvāddākya śeṣabādhenaiva bhavitavyam /
ata iha yadyapi prajāpatirvaruṇāyāśvamanayaditi prajāpatirdātā saṃkorttito varuṇaḥ pratigrahautā punaśca samvāṃ devatāmiti prajāpatireva sa mānavibhaktyantaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyenopāttaḥ khā ca tasya devatā varuṇaḥ pūrvaṃ saṃpradānatvenopāttatvāt /
nātmā katṛtvasaṃ pradānatvayorvirodhinorekava kalpane 'nyatarasya gauṇatvāpatteḥ /
nāpi prajāpatervaruṇo dātā vibhaktivyatyayaprasaṅgāt /
tena prajāpatirapūvaṃ datvā varuṇaṃ prāpta i ca iti ka pu pā / tantravārtike /
tyarthaḥ /
sa tathābhūtaḥ paridaurṇa udaramasya śvayathanā vi dogām /
saetaṃ vāruṇaṃ catuṣkapālamapaśyatta niravapadipti prajāpatereva tacchabdena parāmarśāt /
tannirabapaditi ca kartatva nirdeśa tasyaivābakalpate na varuṇasya saṃpradānatvena sthitatvāt /
na varuṇasyātmoddaśena yāgaḥ saṃbhavati /
na hyātmane saṃkalpyamānaṃ tyaktaṃ syāt /
tena prajāpatinā 'śvaṃ datvā varuṇāya varuṇagṛhautena vārugaṇa dyā tadunmocanamātmanaḥ kṛtam /
ato'nyo 'pi datvaivaṃ kuryāditi dāturiti vijñāyate /
kiṃca /
yajñāṅgatvācca taccheṣā  pradhānenaikakarṭa kāḥ /
pradhānasya ca yaḥ karttā svāmī dātā sa vājinām 
pūrvādhikaragonaivaitatpratipāditaprāyaṃ yaduta dāturiṣṭiriti /
yadā hyaśvapratigrahavataḥ karmaṇo'ṅagamevetyavadhāritaṃ tadā pradhānānāme ka deśakāla kartṛkanyāyādya eva kratoḥ karttā tenaiveyamapi karttavyā yaśca kratoḥ karttā sa khāmikarmaparikraye ityevamaśvasya dātā tasmādasaṃdigdhameva dāturiṭyā bhavitavyam /
etayaṅgasya sā tannavārtike/
marthyaṃ yatpradhānenaikakartṛkaṃ sadupakāraṃ śaknoti karttu na bhinnakartṛkam /
tena pradhānavadeveta raistasyā madhyātvijaṃ katavyama na yājamānamiti /
evaṃ siddhe 'pi vākyopakramopasaṃhāravirodhakṛtabhrāntisaṃśaya vyadāsa māvārthamuttaramadhikaragāmārabdhavyam /
tasyāpi ca vākyasaṃbandhopakramopasaṃhārasyedvaśameva sāmarthya yahāturvidhatte na hotāvadeva vākyaṃ yāvato 'śvān pratigṛhṇīyāttāvataścatuṣkapālānvāruṇānnirvapediti /
kiṃ tardhyanyo 'pyupakrama prajāpatirvaruṇāyāśvamanayahityādirasya vidyate /
sa ca dāturiṣṭiṃ pratipādayatotyuktam /
nanvetadapyuktaṃ vidhupradeśabalauyastvābādhyate 'sāviti /
naitadasti /
kutaḥ /
statilabdhātmakatvena vidhāheśena bādhyate /
pratigrahītari tvava vidhupradeśo na kalpitaḥ 
satyapi pradhānaguṇabhāve vidhārthavādānāṃ pūrvāparoccāraṇakṛto 'nyo viśeṣo bhavati /
sarvacaiva tāvanmukhyaṃ vā 'pūrvacodanāllokavaditi ca śrutiliṅaṅgādhikaraṇanyāyena ca pūrvaṃ vijñānamanupajātapratiindri dvitīyavijñānāntarānutpattyavasthatvādāñjasyenātmānaṃ labhate paścāttanaṃ tu pūrvavijñānāvaruddhajñāna viṣayaupajāyamānaṃ satyāṃ virodhāvasthāyāṃ tadānuguṇyātiriktena rūpeṇotpattumeva na śaknotīti anyathātvamapi pratipadyate /
tadiha vidhārthavādatvakṛtaṃ viśeṣaṃ pūrvapaścādbhāvitayā 'nāśrityopakramopasaṃhārayotipratigrahītaviṣayatvena vipratipadyamānārthatvāttathā sati caikavākyatvāsambhavāt /
pṛthatke cobhayorapi parasparasaṃnidhivaśenā kalpitavidhyantara prarocanāntaraśaktyoḥ sākāṅgatvenā paripūrṇārthayorānarthakyaprasaṅgādavaśyaṃbhāvyekavākyatvavaśena samānaviṣayatve kalpyamāne'nupajātavirodhāvasthapūrvāvadhāritadātṛgāmitvaparityāgāsaṃbhavāduttara malabdhāvasthameva pratigṛhītajñānaṃ gauṇagṛhātikalpanayā dātṛviṣayatvenādhyavasauyate /
kiṃ ca /
bhūyasāṃ ca sadharmatvamasminpace bhaviṣyati /
anyathā hi bhavetpūrvaṃ sarvamevāsamañjasam 
yathodāhṛtena tāttaittirīyaśākhāvākyena dāturiṣṭiḥ siḍā sā na nyāyāntareṇāpanauyate na vacanāntaregā /
yadyapi pratiṣedhavacanaṃ syāt tathāpi vihitapratiṣiḍavāhikalpī bhavenna khokatanyāyavyudāsaḥ /
yatta pratigrahoturvidhāyakaṃ tadyadi tāvatkarmāṅgavaśena vināyupakramaviśeṣātpūrvavākyārthānusāryeva bhavati tatastenāpi dātudeva /
atha tu svātalyāt pratigṛhṇātivaśāt pratigrahītumtataḥ pūrvavākyācca dāturityubhau kariṣyatastatpratiguhoṭagatā ca karmāṅgatvābhāvātpuruṣārthā sato laukikepi syāt /
yastvāvije syādityetatsūtraparaḥ san pūrva vākye nāpi pratigrahautureva vadati tena tatkartṛkāyā karmāṅgatva /
bhāvātvijāmitareṣāṃ ca puruṣārthaphalakalpanātulyatvena lokikepi prāptau satyāṃ kena pramāṇena tasmādyajñe pratoyetetyetadabhidhīyataiti vaktavyam /
tasmādanena tāvahāturiti siddham /
pānavyāpacca tait 
ayamapyanāramyavāda eva /
saumendraṃ caru nirvapedyaḥ somaṃ vamatīti /
tatrāpi pūrvavadevādhikaraṇahayamapi vi cāryate /
laukikasomapāne rasāyanādyarthaṃ kṛte vamanena vyāpanne somendrayāgaḥ uta vaidike utobhayatrāpi /
tava tahadityanena sāmānyapakṣo doṣāttviṣṭirlokike syādityayaṃ cātidiśyate /
atha vādhikaraṇaiyamapi siddhāntarūpeṇādhikaragāiye 'pyatidiśyate kena cihiśeṣeṇa pūrvapacaracanā /
tatreha tāvavairikena pānena dravyapratipādanasya kṛtatvānna kadā cid bheṣe punaḥ pratisamādhānāpekṣā 'stotyanartha kamiṣṭividhānam /
laukike tu vamanena vyāpanne rasāyanaguṇābhāvādindriyeṇa vīryeṇa ca vyaddhiḥ saṃbhāvyate /
na jalodaravadatyantāsaṃbhāvanā /
tatsaṃyoge ca śrūyamāṇeṣṭistatsamādhyarthaiva vijñāyate /
tasmāttatra syāditi /
dopāttu vaidike syādarthāhi laukike na doṣaḥ syāt 
taireva vaidikatvasāmānyādibhirvedike bhavatīti ka smānnocyate /
na hi vamane vaidikatvaṃ saṃbhavati acoditatvāt ato ya eva doṣo laukikagāmitve hetuḥ sa eveha vaidika viṣayatve syāt /
tathā hi /
samyak jaraṇarūpāntā pratipattirvidhīyate  sadyāpadi pradhānasya na bhavetpūrvavatphalam 
' yaḥ somaṃ vamati sa nirvapediti yacchandata cchabdayogādyāgavamanayorekaḥ karttā gamyate /
tatra naimittikaṃ tāvalyāmikaḷkatvenāsaṃdigdhaṃ tenāsaṃdigdhena saṃdigdhaṃ vamanaṃ nirgīyate /
tadapi khāmikarṭa kameva sannimittamiti /
na ca svatantrameva nimittaṃ śuddhenākhyātena nimittapratyayānutpādāt /
yacchabdopabaddhaṃ tannimittaṃ pratipādayati /
tena cetsaṃbaddhaṃ pūrvataraṃ samānaka katvaṃ pa śvānnimittatvapratītiḥ /
atharirvajo devatārtha mṛtvikaparikrayārthaṃ ca dravyaṃ tyajanti tatasteṣāṃ svātmani parikrayavirodhādavaśyaṃ tairapyanye 'dhvavadayo varītavyāḥ /
ādhānagatena tvātmanepadenāgnīnāmā ghātṛvyatiriktapuruṣasaṃbandhābhāvātvātmārtheṣvagniṣu yaṣṭavyam /
tataśca yadi tābahāntasomakarmopakārabuḍyā kurvanti tato deśakālakabhedādviguṇaṃ na tena pradhānena gṛhyate /
na cāhatya deśādibheda āmnāyate yena tatsadbhāve 'pya vaiguṇyamāśraye ta /
svābhivamanena ca kṛtārthatvānnānenaiva śākhā deśāntarādīnāmanujñānam /
kathaṃ vaikameva śāstraṃ khāmiyamanapakṣe samānadeśāditvamāśrayehatvigvamane ca tadbhedam atha vātmārthabudhava te prayuktoran /
evamapi kratvarthenāvadhāritamya punaḥ puruṣārthatvābhāvāttādarthena kriyamāṇasya ānardhakyameva syāt /
atha tu etatsiyarthaṃ puruṣārtha taiva śāstreṇāśroyate tathā sati upasthitakratutyāgāisantrihitasvargādikalpanāñca viprakarṣaḥ /
sadṛśaṃ laukikavamane 'pyetaditi na yājñe syāt tacca pūrvameva nirākṛtam /
tasmātyāmivamane syāt /
atha tvadhvarkhādivamane pi khāmyeva dravyaṃ tyajet tathā sati tadeva bhinnakaṭa katvamāpadyate /
tatsamarthane vā 'śrutaṣaṣṭyartha kalpanā sāmānādhikaraṇyabādhaśca tathā kalpanāyāṃ ca svāmivamanasyānimittatvaprasaṅkaḥ /
ubhayāśrayo vā vairupyanimitto vā ṛyabhedaḥ syāt /
yaḥ somaṃ vamati yasya somamṛtvigvamatoti cāśrayaṇānyataraparigrahe tu svāmivamanagrahaṇaṃ yuktam śabdasāmañjasyāt /
evaṃ tāvadārādupakārakatve /
yadā tu vākya śeṣopanautayāgaśeṣadravyapratipattiniyamabhreṣopajanitaṃ phalalābhāyogyatvamato na pratisamādhīyate iti kalpyate tadā yajamānaphalotpatteratyantāhaṣṭatvāttadāśaṅkati tenaiva pratisamādhāneṣṭiḥ karttavyetyasaṃdigdham /
yattu dakṣiṇālābhātmaka mṛtvijāṃ phalaṃ tatsati cāsati vamane lakṣyamānaṃ dṛśyataiti nirāśaṅkatvādanapekṣitapratisamādhānaṃ neṣṭiṃ gṛhṇāti /
yadā 'pi prakṛ takarmakartṛ niyamāṃśena bhakṣayitṛsaṃskārārthaṃ bhakṣaṇamataśca badveṣe karttavaiguṇyamupajātaṃ dravyasaṃskārasya tadupayogātmakasya nivṛttatvāditi kalpyate tadā'pi taddveṣakṛtathājamānaphalavighnaprasaṅgāt tannivṛttyarthatvāṭyattaccha vdanirdeśācayajamānavamanaeva bhavitavyam /
etenāpūrvasaṃskārārthatvamapi vyākhyātam /
yadā 'pi hi somavamanānna vihitākaraṇaṃ nāpi pratiṣiḍasevanamāpadyataiti kṛtvā doṣanighatārthatvamiṣṭeranāśritya nimittaṃ karmāṅgaṃ tadāpi ca yacchabdena puruṣasyopāttatvājjammānanyāyena prakaraṇāgatapuruṣasaṃskāratā 'dhyavasīyate tadāpi yājamānāstvityanenaiva tatkarṭa katā /
vamavasamānaviṣayatvācca yajamānavamanameva nimittam /
yattvadhvaryyādivamanepi dravyapratipatibhreṣaḥ kartṛ saṃskārāt vināśo vā samādhimapekṣataiti /
yadyapyapekṣate tathāpyavidhānānna grahīṣyate /
saveṃṣu ca kutvarthapuruṣārthapakṣeṣu cartvigvamane vidhānamityuktam /
ataśca yadi tahamanamaduṣṭameva tatastūṣṇīmevāsitavyam /
atha duṣṭaṃ tatasmā mānyavihitaṃ kiṃcitkarttavyam /
na cātra kutvarthādyanyatamapakṣātradhāraṇaprayojanamastīti nātauvāvadhāro yatitavyam /
athāpi tattvajñānaṃ prayojanaṃ tato jañjabhyamānapakṣa parigrahautavyaḥ /
tathā ca sūtrakāra svāmino 'tadarthatvādityāha /
liṅgadarśanāca 
vyudhyataiti sa vaktavyo yasya somapānāvṛddhiḥ prārthyate /
tadvaiguṇyācca vyṛddhirāśayate svāminaśca tadubhayamapauti tasyaiveṣṭiḥ /
sarvapradānaṃ haviṣastadarthatvāt 
aṣṭākapālādiśabdaiḥ samastaṃ dravyaṃ devatārthamavagamitamāhanīya prakṣepegā ca haviṣo devatārthatā bhavati /
yadāhavanīye juhvatīti vidheragnimukhā vai devā iti cārthavādāt /
evaṃ ca sati tataścet kiṃ cidapyapanauyeta tadā 'nyat śrutamanyatkriyeta tasmātsarvabhakṣepaḥ /
kiṃ punarayaṃ pūrvapakṣavādī śeṣakāryāṇāṃ sviṣṭakṛdiḍāprāśitraśaṃyuvākakālabhacaturdākaraṇānāṃ vidhiṃ na paśyati /
satyaṃ na paśyatīti ka cit /
na tvetadyuktamiva na hovaṃ kva citpūrvapakṣo na bhavet /
ataḥ paśyannevāne nābhiprāyeṇa mantrayataiti vaktavyam /
vidyamāneṣu śeṣeṣu dravyāṇāmaprayojakāḥ /
bhaveyuḥ śeṣabhājo hi niśeṣa tu prayojakāḥ 
yathaivājyena śeṣaṃ saṃsthāpayatīti pūrvakarmaṇaḥ paryavasāsānādadhike pūrvasadṛśe vā śeṣaśabdaḥ prayujyate yathā ca tataḥ śeṣeṇa viśiṣṭa deśajātyādimanto janma pratipadyante iti svarmaphalakarmaṇo niḥśeṣopayogādatyaphalasya cānyatva vyāpārāsaṃbhavāttato 'nyeneta vaktavye tataḥ śeṣeoti gautamācāryeṇoktam /
evamihāpi yatpradhānahaviyo̭ 'nyaṣṭavistenaivānyatvenādhikyena vā bhaviṣyati /
atha vā guṇatvena vā śeṣādityevamabhidhāsyate śeṣaśabdo chapayuktataravidyamānaṃ bravīti /
na ca pradhānahaviṣāṃ ki ciddidyate 'nyeṣāṃ ca sarvametadrūpamasti tasmād dravyāntarāṇi gṛhyeran /
yathā vakṣyati /
nirdeśāttasthānyadarthāditi cet iti /
athāpyatyantaṃ śeṣaśabdānurodhaṃ kṛtvā teṣāmeva ki ciccheṣyate tathā 'pyastyevānyadvicārasya prayojanaṃ nāvaśyaṃ pakṣoktenaitra prayojanena bhavitavyamitramapi saṃbhavati /
yadā pradhānavācyādaśeṣapradānaprasaktau satyāṃ śeṣakāryavaśeja śeṣāḥ sthāpyante tadā yathaiva pradhāna tasya haviṣaḥ prayojakamevaṃ sviṣṭakṛdādīnyapīti /
tadarthāvadānanāśadoṣāpahāraṣvapi pradhānavadeva havirantaramutpādota /
yadā punaḥ pradhānacodanākṣiptasyaiva śeṣasya khiṣṭakadādoni grāhakāṇi bhavanti tadā teṣāṃ paraprayutadravyopajīvanādaprayojakale sati nāśadoṣāpahāredhvapi akriyā siḍā bhavati /
tasmātmatyapyubhayoḥ pakṣayorasarvapradāne 'sti prayojanamityarthavānvicāraḥ /
niravadānāttu śeṣaḥ syāt 
yadyāgneyo 'ṣṭākapāla ityevamādova bhavettataḥ sarvapradānamevāvadhāryeta /
atra punastasmātpuroḍāśāderniṣkṛṣya kiṃ cideva hotavyaṃ śrayate dirhaviṣo 'vadyati madhyātpūvaḍāca hiravadyati aṅguṣṭhaparvamālamavadānaṃ bhavati /
dyavadānaṃ juhvatītyevamādivākyālocanena hi kiṃ cideva hotavyamavagatamataḥ śeṣayitavyaṃ kiṃ cit /
upāyo vā tadarthatvāt 
yadyetāni vākyānyutpattivākyāvagatamaśeṣa homamabādhamānāni na niviśeran yadi caitāni pradhānasya pra tyāsannatarāṇi bhaveyustato bāgherannetāni tu saṃskāravākyāni avirodhenaidopapadyante /
śakyate hyaṅguṣṭa parvamāvairmadhyapūrvāḍḍa tairdiśaḥ pratairavadānai saṃskṛtya saṃskṛtya niḥśeṣaṃ haviḥ pradātum /
ataḥ sarvavākyavaśenaivaṃ śāstrārtho bhavati /
yadaśeṣaṃ havirjahoti tadevasupāyamiti tena na kasya ciḍoma pratiṣidhyate /
tasmātsarvapradānaṃ karttavyam /
yattu yathāśrutetikatrttavyatāko yugapanna śakyate ka tumahāvadānahomaprasaṅgāditi /
jyotiṣṭomavadamyasitantravārtike/
tavyo homaḥ /
tadarthatvāha vatārthatvādyā gārthatvādapūrvārthatvāḍā kasnasyāṣṭākapālasya /
naikadeśamāvahomenotpattivākyārthasaṃbhāvanā bhavet /
śratha vā vidānasaṃskārasya dravyārthatvāt /
kṛtatvāttu karmaṇa sakqatsyāṭ dravyasya guṇabhūtatvāt 
naitadasti /
punapunahiravakhaṇḍanaṃ tahāṃśca homo 'bhyasitavya iti /
kutaḥ /
khaṇḍanaṃ guṇabhūtatvādabhyasyeteha yadyapi /
homaḥ pradhānabhāvāttu nāvṛttiṃ pratipadyate 
āgneyacodanāyā hyānumāniko homasaṃbandhaḥ sarvapuroḍāśāvayavasāmānya pravṛttaśca sa yāvannaiva nirvartate tāvadastyeva hyavadānaṃ juhototyanena niṣkṛṣya saṃbandhaḥ kalpitaḥ /
tasmiṃśca siddhe nānumāniko 'vakalpate /
tena yatmāmānya pravṛttamā gneyatvaṃ tad dyavadānacodanayā sāpradaśyamiva prākaraṇa kaidya vadāna viṣaya mevopasaṃkriyate /
tatraiṣo'rtho vijñāyate yavadānamāgneyaṃ karotītyato'vayavāntarāṇāmacoditatvānna homaprasaṅgaḥ /
kiṃ ca /
na cāvaśya pradānena havirāgneya miṣyate /
dyavadāne gṛhote hi sarvāgneyatvasaṃbhavaḥ 
sāptadaśyaṃ hi sāmidhenaunāmuktamanāramyavādena na kratūnām /
tasya tu kratusaṃbandhastadvāreṇānumānikaḥ kasapyo na ca pratyakṣasaṃbandhe satyānumānikaḥ kalpyataiti yukta upasaṃhāraḥ /
na tvaṣṭākapālasyāsphuṭo devatāsaṃbandhastaḍitā 'bhihitatvāt /
sa hi hāvadānasyaivānumānika syāt /
utpattivākye ca karmaṇo'ṣṭākapālena saṃvandhaḥ śrayate /
hāvadānena punarutpannavākye /
tavaitatsyāt /
karmasaṃbandho'ṣṭākapālasyānumāniko jhavadānasya pratyakṣastagāve vā''numānikakalpanaṃ na saṃbhavatīti /
naitaktam /
evaṃ sati jhavadānaṃ juhototyetadevotpattivākyamabhyupagataṃ bhavet /
yadi hyaṣṭākapālavākyaṃ juhotivākonopasaṃhṛtaṃ tato 'nenaiva karmotpattiḥ kriyeta /
tataścāgneyavākye codite hi tadarthatvāttasya tasyopaditṛtīyādhyāyasya caturtha pāda /
śyetetyevaṃ vākyabhedaḥ prāpnoti /
na cānanumāya yāgamāgneyādivākyānāṃ vākyāntarāpekṣā tatsaṃbandho vā 'vakalpate ityuktam /
ato yadyapyānumānika saṃbandhastathā 'pi svārthaparyavasāyitvānyathānupapatteḥ prathamataramanumita iti siddhe saṃbandhe na śakyaṃ pratyakṣaśatenāpyanyathātvaṃ karttam /
na ceha sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati avayavāvayavinoḥ sāmānya viśeṣavyavahārābhāvāt /
aṣṭākapālaco nayā hi pratyakṣameva samasta puroḍāśa upadiśyate /
dhavaḍhānacodanayā 'pi tatastalyabalatvam /
nanu hāvadānavyatiriktāvyavaprāptiḥ sāmānyena puroḍāśaśabdena kriyamāṇā durbalā syāt /
uccate /
yadi hyavayavārthena puroḍāśo vidhīyate /
tataḥ sāmānyavṛttiḥ syātsa tu sākṣādvidhauyate 
devatāyai hi dātuṃ dravyaṃ tyajanti na vibhavena /
tatra yaha vatārthādanyadadhikaṃ tadgṛhāvasthitadravyāntaravadaparivyaktam /
na cātra tyāgasya bhedena vidhānamasti /
devatāsaṃbandhakaraṇa vidhinaiva hyasāvarthāpattyā''cipyate /
sā cāthapattiryāvatā vinā devatāyeṃ dānaṃ na saṃbhavati tāvatyaṃ vāvasthitā nānyatra /
na hi śeṣadravyaparityāgādinā unupapattiḥ /
sarvatra ca samāptividhānamiṣyate tenāpi yāvata eva yāgasamāptyaṅgatvaṃ tāvata evākṣipta yāgavidhirnāvayavāntarāṇām /
ato yathā caturmu ṭyatiriktānāmanasi sthitānāṃ vrohiyavānāṃ na nirvāpavelāyāmalyāgādasvatvamevamihāpi nāvayavāntarāṇāṃ tatsyāditi /
athocyeta nirvāpavelāyāmanupajātamadhyapūrvādivibhāgaṃ dravyamanabhipretatyāgamapi balātparityaktavyam /
na hi tadānīṃ vijñāyate kebhyo vrauhigyo hyavadānaṃ niṣyatsyate kebhyo netyagamyamāne viśeṣe yāneva na tyajettegya eva kadā cidavadauyeta /
tatra tyaktānāmadānā datyaktānāṃ ca dānādayathātakaragāprasaṅaḥ /
tasmātsarvatyāga hani naitadevam / na hi sāmānyaśākhegā vyavahāre kṛte sati /
viśeṣaśāstrāvasarastammādādita eva saḥ 
yadyāgneyādicodanayaiva haviprakṣepo 'bhidhīyate tato hyavadānacodanayā parisaṃkhyā tumaśakyatvātsarvaprakṣepaḥ prāpnoti /
tadā ca tathā ''gneyacodanayaiva prakṣepaścodyeta yadā yāgahomayorabhedaḥ /
tayostu bhedaḥ śabdāntarādhikaraṇanyāyasiddhaḥ /
tadakte śravaṇājjuhotirāsecanādhika syāditi sūtrakāraṇoccamānaṃ tavaiva samarthayiṣyāmahe /
yathā devatoddeśena svatvatyāgamātraṃ yāgo devatoddiṣṭa tyajyamāna svatvadravyaprakṣepo juhotiḥ /
tatra ye doṣā darśapūrṇamāsajyotiṣṭomādiṣvahomatvādāhavanīyo na bhavedityādayastānapi tatraiva parihariṣyāmaḥ /
ubhayośca bheṭe sati āgneyo 'ṣṭākapāla ityanena tāvaddākona yāvatā vinā 'ṣṭākapālasyāgneyatvaṃ na bhavati tāvadeva codyate /
tasya ca svatvaparityāgadevatoddaśau kevalāvantareṇāgneyatvaṃ na jāyate na prakṣepamapi tatra yadi vākyāntaraṃ na syāt tata īdṛśaṃ karma bhavet /
supakkama vikalamaṣṭākapātantravārtike/
lamācaritaḥ śrutau deśe nidhāya devatāmuddiśya nāyaṃ mameti saṃkalpaḥ karttavyaḥ /
tatparipālanārthaṃ ca punaḥ kadā cidapi na svatvaṃ dravye badhnīyāt /
yadi hi bannauyātataḥ pūrvasaṃkalpaṃ vināśayedanṛtaṃ ca vadet /
yo hi prathamameva jānāti punarapyahamatra svatvamādhāsyāmīti tasya na mamaitaddevatāyai tvetaditi saṃkalpa eva na bhavet /
tena devatoheśatyāgottarakālaṃ yadasya bhavati tadbhavatvityavadhārya na kaścidyāpāro vo ḍhavyo bhavet /
tathā prāpte tu vākyāntarāṇi bhavanti upastuṇāti hirhaviṣo 'vadyati abhighārayati caturavattaṃ juhotītyevamāṭoni taimtāvadidamavadhāryate yadadānaṃ haviṣo hotavyamiti /
sarvāṇi caitāni prakṛtadravyālambitvagattadpādāya pravarttante nāpūrvadravyagrāhitvena /
tathā hi /
caturavattaṃ juhotītyava homasyāprāptatvānna tamuddiśya dravyaṃ vidhīyate caturavattaṃ ca pūrvavākya kalpitaṃ prayojanāpekṣamasti /
tasmāttasyānena prakṣepamātraṃ śakyaṃ vidhātumiti na caturavattaviśiṣṭa homavidhānamavakalpate /
homasyāpi ca tryaṃśasya samāptiparyantatvāt sarvāntyeṃśe prakṣepe codyamāne tyāgata hevatoddeśayoḥ kimapūrvayorarthāpattyā vidhi kalpyatāmuta kutaścitprāptayorevāśrayaṇaṃ kriyatāmiti tatrāgne vyadhikaragānyāyena lāghave sati gauravasyāpramāṇakatvādavagatatyāgoheśāṃśahayānyaṣṭākapālādaunyeva gṛhyante /
na ca teṣāmautpattikaṃ yāgasādhanatvaṃ virudhyate /
pratiṣyamāṇānāmagniyāga nāmapi tadyāge iti ka pu pā tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pāda /
sādhanatvā vighātakatvāt /
devatāntarasaṃbandhena hi yāgaviparītakriyā saṃbandhena vā virodha syāt na tvasāvasti /
tenaiṣo 'rtho bhavati aṣṭākapālena yava kva citpradeśe sthitena yajeta tadīyaṃ ca dyavadānaṃ yatva kva citpracipediti /
tava vedyāṃ havīṃṣyāsādayati barhiṣautivacanāttatra sthitena puroḍāśenejyate /
yadāhavanauye juhotīti vacanāttatra hāvadānaṃ hayate sa tu homa kiṃ pūvādyāgādarthāntaramitikarttavyatā bhavati uta tasyaiva yāgasyāṃśānta raviraḍyā rūpāntaraṃ jātamiti cintanīyam /
tatraiva rūpāntaropajananamiti brūmaḥ /
karmāntarasve hi dravyāntaraṃ devatāntaraṃ ca nāriṣṭhahomādivatprāpnati /
yathoktena nyāyena sa eva yāgaḥ pracitataro juhotitvamāpadyate /
na caitāvatotpattikaya jirūpavighāta śrāśayo juhoteryajiviśeṣatvāt /
sāmānye hi kaścihiśeṣo na bhavatyapi /
na tu niḥsāmānyaḥ kaścihiśeṣa upapadyate /
tataśca yathā vṛkṣamānayetyukte śiṃśapāmityavirodhātpaścāducyamānaṃ na virudhyate tathā yajetetyukte juhotitvāvirodho 'vagantavyaḥ /
so 'yaṃ yāga eva grākāraḥ samastena puroḍāśena kriyate hāvadānena juhotyavasthānītaḥ śeṣeṇa tu sāmānyarūpa ekasminnapi ca caṇe jhākāro'pi niṣpadyate /
yadaiva hi ḍāvadānamāhavanauye nicipyate tadaiva yājyānuvākyābhyāṃ samastaviṣayadevatāsaṃkalpotyāpanaṃ kriyate tena naivaṃ bhramitavyaṃ yammājjuhasthaṃ hāvadānamāśravaṇa pratyāśravaṇābhyāṃ tyāgāyor̤ataṃ ca tasmāttadeva kevalaṃ devatāyai saṃkalpitaṃ netaraditi vidvadbhyāmadhvaryayajamānābhyāṃ vedārthamanusṛtya samastaparityāgadevatoddeśau yathāīṃ karttavyo adhvaryaṇā hyavadānaprakṣepo 'tiriktonuṣṭheya iti /
na caitāvatā yāgasya vairupyamaśobhanaṃ mantavyam /
vacanasāmarthyādīhaśasyaiva śobhanatvapratīteḥ /
yathā kasya citpuruṣasyaikaḥ pādaḥ purastāita iti na tāvatā kiṃ cidrelakṣaṇyaṃ bhavati /
tathā 'va ḍāvadānapāde'dhikamapi prakṣepāṃśaṃ gate satyutpattivākyaśiṣṭaṃ yāgasādhanatvaṃ samastenāṣṭākapālena pratipannameṃ vetyavirodhaḥ /
tasmād jhākāramevaitavyadhānaṃ draṣṭavyam /
atha vā yastatra yāgastasya prādhānyaṃ yastu prakṣepaḥ so 'ṅgameva /
tathā hi /
phalavākye yajereva saṃbandhaḥ śrayate mphuṭaḥ /
tatsaṃnnidhau samāmnānājjuhotaraṅgateṣyate 
aprayojakatvādekasmāt kriyegn śeṣasya guṇabhūtatvāt 
yadāhavanīye prakṣepeṇa akṣapito haviśeṣa pratipāditastadā śeṣakāryāṇi sviṣṭakṛdādīni kathaṃ kriyantāmiti vicāryate /
tatrārthakarmatvaṃ manyamāna ekasmādityāha /
satyapyarthakarmatve yadi tadarthamevaitāni dravyāṇi utpannāni bhaveyustataḥ sarveṣāṃ sambhāvanāya paśvavadānānāmivaikammādapi sidhyati yāge sarveṣāṃ saṃbandhaḥ kriyeta tattu nāstyaprayojakatvāt /
atastuṣopavāpakapāla dekenaiva siddhiḥ /
saṃskṛtatvācca 
yaśca pradhānānāmevādṛṣṭaḥ saṃskārama ekadravyaniṣpāditaiśaśeṣa kāryesmidhyatīti na dravyāntaramapekṣate /
sakqacchandaśca sakṛdavadānābhiprāya /
itarathā tu sarvāvadāne 'pi tanveṇa prayogātmakṛttvopapatteravaktavyataiva syāt /
atha vā tataḥ śeṣa kāryāṇi sarvebhyaḥ kriyeranyadi saṃskārakāṇi bhaveyarna tvetāni saṃskārakāṇi /
kutaḥ /
saṃskārāntaraireva saṃskṛtatvāt /
ayamapyavirodhābhaviṣyatīti cet /
tatrāpyeṣa sūvārthaḥ /
saṃskārakramasyātikrāntatvāt /
yā vayakṛtaprayojanaṃ dravyaṃ bhavati tāvatsaṃskāramapekṣate pradhānaniṭatyuttarakālaṃ tu kṛtaṃ saṃskārairiti saṃskārāṇāmanavasaraḥ /
sarvebhyo vā kāraṇāviśeṣātsaṃskārasya tadarthatvāt 
yaistu dravyaṃ cikīrṣyate ityevaṃ saṃskārakarmāṇyetāni /
tava hyutpattau yena saṃyuktamiti pratipattayastāśca sarvaiḥ kṛtārtha cāviśeṣādapekṣitāḥ /
yadyapi caitābhirdravyāṇi na prayocyante tathā 'pi dravyaireva tāsāṃ prayuktatvātsarvaviṣayatā nirṛtte 'pi ca pradhāne tadīyānāṃ satāmeṣāṃ kā pra tipattirbhavatvityapekṣite śakyaḥ pratipattiniyamo vidhātum /
liṅgadarśanācca 
sakatma kṛditi sviṣṭakadravadānavopsā sarvebhyo 'vadāne saṃskārapakṣe vā 'vakalpate nānyathā /
prayojanasūtrāṇi caitāni /
yadi nāma śeṣakāryavaśena pūrvapakṣe 'dhya sarvapradānaṃ kiṃ bhavati tadā vicārasya prayojanamiti /
tatra yaḥ pūrvamasmābhirabhihito 'rthastavaiva sūtraṃ yojyam /
pūrvapate havīṃṣi śeṣakāryāṇāmaprayojakānautyeka mātkriyeran /
balāttvapahāraḥ pradhānebhyaḥ sakṛtkṛte samasta kṛta iti saṃskṛtatvānnānyato 'pi karttavyaḥ /
siddhānte tu sarvahaviṣāṃ prayojakatvāviśeṣātsarvebhyo liṅgadarśane ca paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇavatprayojane 'vasthitasiddhāntaṃ dyotayati /
ekammāccedyāthākāmyaviśeṣāt 
yāthākāmyamityasyaiva buddhisāmānādhikaraṇyena strovivakṣāyāṃ ṣigaurādibhyaśceti ṅauṣi kate halastadditasyeti vyaṅyakāre lupte yāthākāmo bhavati /tantravārtika /
mukhyāḍā pūrvakālatvāt 
śeṣanimittakaṃ hi vihitāvaśyakarttavyatānimittaṃ ca śeṣakārya prathamasya tāvatpāṭhakramānusārātpūrvamāpatati /
na ca tadā kaścivirodha iti kriyate /
kate nivṛttavyāpārā codanā na nimittībhavatīti virodhādakāraṇam /
bhakṣāśravaṇāddānaśabdaḥ parikraye 
puroḍāśasya catukaraṇe idaṃ brahmaṇa ityādini deṃśaḥ śrūyate /
kathaṃ ca tattadbrahlādivyapadeśyaṃ bhavati yadi tebhyo dauyate tena dānaṃ vihitam /
tattu kimatvijāṃ yatheṣṭaviniyogārthaṃ parikrayāyāmnāyate atha bhacyamāṇaśeṣa pratipayarthamiti /
parikrayārthamityāha /
na hyava yajamānapañcamā iḍāṃ prāśnantautivat dravyaprādhānyaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ vā śrūyate tasmād dravyāṇāṃ karmaśeṣatvātkarmayukto bhyaśca dānādantareṇāpi parikrayaśrutiṃ dakṣiṇādānavatpa rikrayārthamiti /
tatsaṃstavācca 
eṣā vai darśapūrṇāmāsayordakṣiṇeti dakṣiṇā ghṛtvijāvaira mutsāhakāriṇī parikrayasya caitadrūpam /
bhakṣārtho vā dravye samatvāt 
na caiṣa vibhāga parikrayārthaḥ /
kutaḥ /
parikrayo hi sarvatra svena dravyeṇa kalpate /
devatārthe parityakte svāmitvaṃ na ca kasya cit 
brahmādibhirbhāgānāmupakurvadbhirna kathaṃ ciṭ dṛṣṭamityuktaṃ vadeti dravyacapaṇasyāpekṣitasya dṛṣṭatvāt /
bhāgaistu brahmādaunāmupakāra kairityanenāpi sutarāṃ parikraya āpadyate /
na cāvaśyaṃ bhakṣagaṇenaiva teṣāmupakriyate gṛhānayanādinā 'pyupakāropapatteḥ /
sarvatra ca dravyasaṃskārārthatāṃ bhakṣasya vacyati /
vratādibhirnivṛttyanabhidhānāt /
puruṣasaṃskārā hi vratairnivarttaran /
tata evaṃ vaktavyam /
satyaṃ bhāgānāṃ pratipattiḥ tathā 'pi tu prakṛtakaṭa niyamasya prayojanāpekṣāvelāyāṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satyadṛṣṭadaurbalyādṛṣṭa eva kartṝṇāṃ sāmarthyarūpa saṃskāraḥ kalpyate /
karṭa saṃskāraśca sarvāntaraṅgo bhakṣaṇaṃ nāma /
gṛhamapi ca nītvā yāvadbhakṣaṇaṃ na kriyate tāvattadanupayo gādanupakāraḥ /
tenāvaśyaṃ sudūramapi gatvā bhakṣaṇe paryavasitavyam /
tava prathamātikrame kāragābhāvādyogyatāvaśena ca vyādeśadvāraprakrāntabhakṣasamāpanasyāvaśyaṃ karttavyatvāt brahmādaunāmeva bhakṣaṇenopa karttavyamiti gamyate /
śeṣasthāpi ca capaṇāpekṣasya bhacagākṛtameva capaṇaṃ yogyatayā vidhāryate /
vyādeśāddānasaṃstutiḥ 
dakṣiṇeti prāsaṅgikopakārāpekṣayā brahmaṇa ityādinirdeśa sārūpyādā bhaviṣyati /
tasmāicārtho 'yasupadeśa iti siddham /
iti śrībhaṭṭakumārilakhāmiviracite maumāṃsātanvavārttike tṛtīyasyādhyāyasya caturthaścaraṇaḥ samāptimagamat /
tantravārtike /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pāda /
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ /
ājyācca sarvasaṃyogāt 
sarvebhyo vā kāraṇāviśeṣādityasyātiprasaktasyāpavādaḥ kriyate /
tameva tāvatpūrvaṃ pakṣaṃ smārayati /
tathā ca sarvebhyo havirbhya ityanuvāda upapadyate /
niḥśeṣahaviviṣayatvāt /
kāraṇāca 
purākalpe ca yatkāraṇaṃ sviṣṭakṛdarthe 'vadāne saṃkorttitaṃ tadājye 'pyaviśiṣṭaṃ yaddevebhyo havirasau vahati tasya tena bhāgaḥ prārthitaḥ /
ājyamapi copāṃśuyājadevatābhyastenāvaśyaṃ voṭavyam /
ataśca tato 'pyasya bhāgena bhavitavyam /
ekasmin samavattaśabdāt 
ekasminniti kasmiṃścitkarmaṇotyarthaḥ /
athavā yuṣmadabhiprāyeṇa ekasminhaviṣi viṣṭakṛtyavadīyamāne sati samavattaśabdo 'nyasahitādavadīyamānavacano nāvaka 'atiprasaktasye'ti ga pustake nāsti /tantravārtike /
lpeta matpace tu ājyamapi tatrāvadīyataityavakalpiṣyate /
kka punaridaṃ śrūyate tadabhidhīyate /
ādityaḥ prāyaṇīya payasi carurityeko yāgaśvoditaḥ punastatraivoktam /
ā jyasyainaṃ carumabhipūryājyamāgāḥ pathyādayaścatasro devatā yaṣṭavyā te ca dravyasāmānyādapāṃśuyājavikārāścatvāro 'pi yāgā ādityacakarāgneyavikāraḥ tatrāgnaye viṣṭakṛte samavadyatauti śrūyate /
tadyadi carorekasthātideśena viṣṭakṛtmā prastato'vadyatītyeva syāt /
yadā tu prakṛtādājyādapyupāṃśuyājadravyāt viṣṭakṛttadā vāpi ya ṣṭavya ityubhayoścarvāccayoravadāne samavattaśabdaḥ samarthito bhavati /
tasmādapi santyājye śeṣakāryāṇīti /
ājye ca darśanātsviṭakkadarthavādasya 
avadāyāvadāya dhutrāṃ pratyabhiṣārayati sviṣṭakṛte'vadāya na pratyabhivārayatīti dhruvāta evāvadāyeti pratiśabdāt dṛṣṭārthatvāccāvagamyate /
yadapi sviṣṭakṛte vidīyate tadapi dhruvāta eva yena tadarthe 'vatte dhruvāyā pratyabhighāraṇaṃ pratiṣidhyate /
na hi tataḥ parāmāhutimitihetuvacanātpūrvāṇi pratyabhidhāraṇāni sviṣṭakṛdarthānīti darśayati /
tataśca tatmāmānyāditareṣu tathātvamiti sarvaiḥ śeṣa kāryairbhavitavyam /
aśeṣatvātta naivaṃ syātsarvāṃṭānādaśeṣatā 
sati pradhānadravyaśeṣe śeṣakāryāṇi kriyante na copāṃśutṛtīyā dhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pāda /
yājahaviḥśeṣo vidyate sarvādānāt /
kathaṃ sarvādānamiti cet /
taduttarasūtreṇāha /
sādhāraṇyānna dhruvāyāṃ syāt 
dhuvāyāṃ tāvannopāṃśuyājasya śeṣo vidyate /
dhauvasthāsaṃyuktotpatteḥ sarvājyakāryārthamādānātsarvamai vā etad yajñāya gṛhyata iti vākyāt /
taittirīyāṇāṃ tu katipayopastaraṇābhighāraṇādikāryānukramaṇāt /
tanmadhye copāṃśuyājasyāpi saṃkīrttanāt tāvatāṃ sādhāraṇamupastugāntrabhighārayantrājyasya yajanniti vākyāgamyate /
sādhāragoṣu ca pariṣadanopahāragoṣṭhaubhojanādiṣviyaṃ sthitiḥ /
yadekasya bhāge 'payātite tāvanmātrameva tasya /
a vaśiṣṭaṃ tu tatsamānabhājāmavadhāryamāṇaṃ na pūrvaśeṣa ityevamakṛtārthatvena na pratipattimapekṣate /
yadā tu sarvaiḥ samānabhāgbhiryathāyoga mur̤atā bhāgā bhavanti tadā tasya sādhāraṇyānuguṇaiva pratipattyapekṣā bhavati /
tadihopāṃśayājārthe bhāge upanaute na kaścidapi tadīyaḥ śeṣo vidyate śiṣṭasya parastā dvāvyuparastaraṇābhighāraṇādigṛhītatvenākṛtārthatvāt /
kṛtārthapratipattayaśca śeṣakāryāṇi na svayamevākṛtaprayojanamapi dravyaṃ prayuñjate /
tasmānna dhruvāyāṃ śeṣo'sti /
yastu samastakāryani ṭacyuttarakālaṃ sādhāraṇaḥ śeṣo bhaviṣyati tasya samiṣṭayajurākhyaṃ pratipattyantaramāmnātam /
yadī tvidamapyupastaragādivadevārthakarmāvadhāryate tadā sutarāṃ śeṣābhāvaḥ / śakyaṃ tu taittirīyavākyāpekṣayotpattāvanyasaṃyogāt samiṣṭayajuṣaśca juhoticoditatvenāyajñatvā vyatipattitvamavadhārayitum /
niḥśeṣatvena cāsāvavasthiteti śeṣakāryāntarāṇi bādhate /
tasmāt dhruvāyāṃ tāvannosti śeṣaḥ /
avattatvāttu juhāṃ tasya ca homasaṃyogāt 
tatraitasyāt yatkevalopāṃśuyājārthe juhvāmavattaṃ tasyaiva grahavamaseṣviva somasya śeṣo bhaviṣyatīti /
tadanupapannam /
kutaḥ /
tasya samastasya caturavattaṃ juhotīti homasaṃyogāt /
uktaṃ hyetadupadhānārthaṃ caro nānyatra śrutama nyava viniyoktavyamiti /
tasmānna juhvāṃ śeṣa upapadyate /
camasavaditi cet 
atha yaduktaṃ camasavat satyapi homasaṃyoge śeṣobhaviṣyatīti tatpariharttavyam /
na codanāvirodhāiviḥprakalpanāca 
naitatsomena tulyaṃ tatra hi grahacamaseṣu haviprakalpanamātre kṛte yathā na sarvahomastathā some vacanāmaco na vidyata ityatrādhikaraṇe vacyāmaḥ /
tena codanāvirodhaṃ tatva vakṣyamāṇaṃ pariharatāṃ na sarvahomo bhaviṣyati /
śe avattatvāśceti ka ga pu pā /
ṣakāryānyārthadarśanaṃ ca momasyāgne vohotyanuvaṣaṭkarotī tyādi sarvataḥparihāramāśvinaṃ bhakṣayatītyādicamasasamākhyā ca na virokhyate /
anyathā tahirodhaḥ syāt /
atha vā na tavāsamastahome sati kā ciccodanā viru dhyata ityāvirodhādasarvahīmaḥ /
iha tu virodhaḥ syādayameva cāvirodhā heturiti sūtragamanikā /
yathā tu bhāṣyakāreṇa pūrvaṃ camasamanudāhṛtya camasavaditicediti sūtramupanyastaṃ tathā paricodanāsūtrameva homasaṃyoga naikāntikatrapradarśanārthaṃ kalpayitvā parihāro vaktavyaḥ /
tatra vacanāntarakṛtatvāccheṣa syādava vacanāntararahitatve sa tauti viśiṣṭasya hetoravyabhicārāt /
atha vā 'vattatvātta juhvāmityetadeva tuśabdasyāne caśabdaṃ kṛtvā pūrvapa cavādipratyavasthānaṃ vyācacāṇaiścamaso dṛṣṭānto dātavyaḥ paraṃ vā 'nubhāṣaṇasūtraṃ vaktavyam /
etaduktaṃ bhavati /
a vattatvāttu juhvāṃ camasavaccheṣo 'stu /
tasyottaraṃ tasya ca homasaṃyogāditi gatārtham /
utpannādhikārātsati sarvavacanam 
yastu sarvebhya iti prātyapekṣo 'nuvādastava yādṛrśa vayamiha sarvatvaṃ paśyāmaḥ tādṛśasyaivānuvāda iti manyāmahe /
sarvacaiva ca paramasarveṇa vyavahārābhāvādadhikṛtāpekṣaḥ sarvaśabdo gṛhyata iti na virodhaḥ /
tena yeṣāṃ śeṣamabhāvena pratipattikāryādhikāro 'sti ye vā vidyamānatvena prakṛtaśeṣāḥ tebhyaḥ sarvebhya iti gamyate tantravārtika /
jātiviśeṣātparam 
pūrvavadeva samavadyateḥ anuvādatvādyathāsaṃbhavamā jye 'pauti carāvavadīyamāne saumyāttadavayavasyācikaurṣitamapyavadānaṃ balāivati /
tadetatsaṃsṛṣṭadravyajātihayamapekṣya saṃśabdo 'nuvādaḥ /
antyamarekārtham 
antya yattu kāraṇaṃ sviṣṭakadartho 'rthavāda ityukta ta dammatpace 'pyupapadyataevārakārthatvāt /
sviṣṭakṛte 'vadāyeti tāvadyatastamyāvadānaṃ bhavati yādṛśaṃ vā saṃbhavati tādṛśamiti gamyate /
puroḍāśādibhyaśca tasyāvadānaṃ dhruvātaścopastaraṇābhighāraṇe /
na caturghyantena dhauvamevāvadānaṃ saṃbadhyate /
sā hi devatārthadravyāntarāvadāne'pyupastaraṇābhighāraṇopayogitvātpratyabhidhāraṇamapecataeva tena prāka sviṣṭakataḥ parastādapi dhauvopayogo 'stautyavatte avatte pratipūrayitvā tataḥ paraṃ tu na kiṃ citkāryamiti nārthaḥ pratipurona /
na hyetatpratipūraṇaṃ pūrvasthā vadānasya saṃskārakamadṛṣṭārthatvaprasaṅgāt /
arekastūttarakāryārthaḥ pratyakṣastanmādantareṇāpi striṣṭakṛdarthatvaṃ tadavadhikārekārthatvenopapanno 'rthavādaḥ /
sākaṃprasthāyye sviṣṭakkṛdiḍaṃ ca tadvat 
 'yathā sambhavamartho 'pī'ti ka ga pu pā /
tadavayavasyā'nusyūtasyācikīrpitamiti ka pu pā  ceti ka ga pustakayornāsti /
amāvāsyāyāṃ nityaṃ sviṣṭakadiḍaṃ sāntrāyyādavadīyate taha, gavikāraśca sākaṃprasthāyyaḥ śrata ihāpyavadātavyamityetāvatā viśeṣegātulyāśaṅkāyāmatideśaḥ kriyate /
tahadevāśeṣatvānnaivaṃ syātmavaṃdānādaśeṣateti /
evaṃ hyatra savaṃdānaṃ homāyeṃ prasarpataḥ saha kumbhaubhiriti anavattasyaiva dohasya kumbhībhyāṃ saheti vidadhadaśeṣahomaṃ vidadhāti ato na śakyaṃ kiṃ ciccheṣayitum /
sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca graheṣu 
tahaditi varttate /
sautrāmaṇyāṃ surāgrahā payograhāścāśvinādaya ātrātāsteṣāṃ pṛthakprakalpanamātrātmakatvāt camasavatsarvahomaprāptirnāstīti viśeṣāśaṅkāyāmatideśāttatrāpi yathāgṛhītānāṃ homārthenādānena saṃbandho yathopāttānāṃ ca homena thūyate /
yathāgṛhotān grahāndatvija upādadate uttare 'gnau payograhān juhati dakṣiṇe surāgrahāniti /
tadacca śeṣavacanam 
ananyaśeṣabhūtaśca pratiṣedho 'nuvāda ucchinaṣṭi na sarvaṃ juhotīti /
ucchinaṣṭauti vidhiḥ tadanuvādastu niṣedhaḥ aśeṣahomaprātyā śeṣakāryanittiṃ darśayati /
vācanikasya ca śeṣasya pratipattyantaramarthakarma vā 'nyadastīti tato 'pīti viṣṭakṛdiḍaṃ ma karttavyamiti /
dravyaikatve karmabhedātpratikarma kriyeran 
tantravārtika /
idānoṃ sarasu śeṣakāryeṣu tahiśeṣāścintyante /
tatra sarvaṣṭaṣṭhā yāmanyonyanirapekṣa caturthyanta parikalpitaiḥ ṣaḍirgagobhinnadravyadevatāsaṃgho gairdevatāntarāvaruḍayāge devatāntarāsaṃbhavāt guṇena bhedakena ṣaṭa karmāṇi /
teṣu keṣāṃ cihninnānyeva harvauṣi anyeṣāṃ punareka eva rathacakramātra puroḍāśa nātaḥ /
sa yadāṅgīkriyate tadā vicāra kiṃ karmabhedāccheṣakāryāṇāṃ bheda uta dravyaikatvāttanvamiti /
nanu caikādaśavicāro 'yaṃ tatra nirṇeṣyate /
ekadravye saṃskārāṇāṃ vyākhyātamekakarmalamityatrāta iha na vicāraṇīyam /
ucyate /
pratipādyamidaṃ dravyaṃ bhedena sahate kriyām /
khaṇḍaśaśca pradhānānāmaṅgatvānnāsti tantratā 
karmasaṃskārapakṣe hayamānasaṃskārapakṣe vā tahedāīdo bhavet /
śeṣasaṃskārastvayaṃ sa ca śeṣa sādhāraṇastasya ca dakṣiṇottarārḍe gṛhyate /
na pradhānāvadānadeśastasya prakṛtāvacoditatvāttataśca śakyamagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvaṃ vatam /
yadyapi hye kapradhānoddeśenottarāīṃ gṛhṇauyuḥ tathā 'pi tathā coditārthasaṃpattyā pradhānāntarāṇyapi kṛtārthāni bhaveyuḥ /
tasmāttantram /
yattu pratipādyaṃ vibhavatauti pratipacyantare catukaraṇe tadupayujyate /
aindravāyave tu vacanātpratikarma bhakṣaḥ syāt 
some vacanāico navati sāmānyena bhakṣavicāra kṛtvā viśeṣavicāro 'yaṃ karttavya āsīt /
yattu prathamataraṃ kriyate tatpūrvādhikaraṇāpavādalena śīghratarīpasthānāt /
pūrvavadi dravyaikatvātmakṛikṣite kṛtaḥ śāstrārtha iti nyāyāt prāpte vacanād dirbhakṣaṇaṃ hiraindravāyavastha bhakṣayatīti /
bhavanti cedvathānyapyadhikaraṇāni yeṣāṃ nyāyema pūrvapakṣaṃ kṛtvā vacanena siddhānto bhavati /
ma tvetadyuktam /
saṃdehābhāvāttava vai tat kriyate yatra nyāyena pratipādito vavanād bādhitaḥ tadabhāvātmamānanyāyeṣūpakariṣyati /
sa ceha gyāya pūrvādhikaragonaiva pradarśita iti mandaphalo vicāraḥ /
tasmānnaivaṃ varṇanīyaṃ kiṃ tarhi tantravārtike /
sarvapṛṣṭhāyāva pratikarma sviṣṭakṛdiḍaṃ karttavyaṃ pradhānabhedāt /
tathā hi /
siḍavatpradhānabhedamaindra vāyava saṃskārahetumāha hiraindravāyavasya bhakṣayati dihyetasya vaṣaṭkarotauti tasmādyābaddaṣaṭakāra śeṣasaṃskāra ityuktottare datte dṛṣṭāntamanubhāṣya sūtreṇa parihārī vaktavyaḥ aindravāyave tu sakṛcaṇe prāpte vacanāda hirbhakṣo na pradhānabhedanimitto hetvadhikaraṇe hetornirākṛtatvāt /
evaṃ ca sati pūrvādhikaraṇaśeṣeṇaiva satā somabhakṣasāmānyavicārasmāraṇānna kramakopo bhaviṣyatīti /
some 'vacanāico na vidyate 
aindravāyave tāvaddiśiṣṭavidhānādapi bhakṣo bhavet athetaragrahagate camasasthe ca some saṃdehaḥ /
kiṃ bhakṣo 'sti neti tatvāpi sarvataḥ parihāramāśvinaṃ bhakṣyatītyādiṣu aindravāyavanyāya eva syāt /
idaṃ tu sarvathā tatrāpi vicāryate kiṃ prāpte bhane viśeṣaṇamātraṃ vacanena vidhīyate uta viśiṣṭavidhānametaditi /
kaścātra viśeṣaḥ sa yadi vācanikastato yācadacanameva karttavyo 'tha tvayataḥ kutaścittata ekadeśasthamapi liṅgaṃ sthālopulā kanyāyena samastadyotakaṃ bhaviṣyati /
trayaśceha pakṣā saṃbhavanti kimanyārthadarśanānāṃ prātyapekṣatvādavidhānācca naiva bhakṣaḥ uta prātyabhāvādagyārthadarśanānyeva vacanaukṛtya yāvaddacanaṃ bhakṣa uta samākhyāvaṣaṭkārahomā bhiṣavanimitto 'pi bhakṣa iti/
kiṃ prāptam ājyasā kaṃprasthāyya saunāmaṇīgrahaṇavat samastahomasaṃyogāccheṣa eva nāsti kutaḥ punarbhaca iti /
na cāva prakṛtitaḥ prāptirna ca pratyakṣopadeśo yo 'pyupadeśa iva so 'pyanyaparatvādasamarthaḥ /
tasmānnāsti bha ca iti /
syādā 'nyārthadarśanāt 
vacanāni tvaparvatvāttasmādyathopadeśaṃ syuḥ 
yadyanyārthadarśanāni bhaveyustato 'nyatrāpi prāptiḥ syāicanāni tvetāni tasmādyathopadeśaṃ bhakṣo 'yaṃ nānyatreti /
camaseṣu samākhyānātsaṃyogasya tannimittatvāt 
gṛhṇīma etadyathopadeśamiti sa tu samākhyādibhedabhinna upadeśo 'nusatavyaḥ na tu śrutaviśeṣamātraniṣṭhaḥ /
tatra camaseṣu tāvat yadyapi brāhmaṇagataḥ pratyakṣopadeśo nopalabhyate tathā 'pi praiṣagatayā samākhyayā 'numoyate hoṭacamasatvodiviśiṣṭaṃ hi dravyanayanapreṣaṇaṃ na kathaṃ cidupapadyate yadi teṣu hotrādayaḥ somaṃ na camanti /
katham /
camasa iti adanārthasya cameroṇādike 'dhikaraṇasādhane asanpratyaye kṛte praiṣavelāyāṃ bhūtabhaviṣyadvarttamānānāṃ kva citsaṃbandhe 'pekṣyamāṇe bhūtavarttamānayoradarśanādbhaviṣyattvamanumauyate /
na hyanyathā hotuścamasaḥ maitvityetasyānuṣṭhānaṃ śakyate /
tasmāccamitavyaṃ hovādibhiḥ /
somaśeṣavantaścamasā preṣitā iti tasyaivāpecitapra tantravārtike /
prakatipattiviśeṣasya pratyāsattarbhakṣyatvaṃ gamyate /
saśeṣaścamaso hayate alpaṃ juhotauti vacanāt /
na cānyadodanādidravya pratīyate yasya camanāccamasatvamupapadyate /
na ca taccamanasya karmāṅgabhāvaḥ syāt /
tatra raṇaṃ bādhyeta /
praiṣo 'pi cotkṛṣyeta somacamasasamākhyā ca bādhyeta yadi caudanādi bhacyeta tata ucchiṣṭena pātreṇa punarhomo na kriyeta /
śuyarthaṃ tava lakṣaṇādyāśrayo yasya hoṭacama satvādyavadhāritaṃ tasya vināśāt dravyāntaraṃ tatmamākhyaṃ na bhavatīti samākhyātaiya sādhanakahomavidhānabāghaḥ sthāt /
etena camasāntaropādānaṃ pratyuktam /
tadutpādane ca śrutacamasasaṃkhyātikramaḥ syāt /
na ca vacanasāmarthyādacchiṣṭena hotuṃ śakyam /
vacanasyāntareṇāpyācārabhaṅgaṃ somabhace sāmakāśatvāt /
somabhakṣe 'pi sarvametattulyamiti cennaitadevaṃ na somenocchiṣṭā bhavantīti śruteḥ /
tasmāccamasibhibhecayitavyaḥ soma iti /
bhāṣyamapyanenaiva krameṇa netavyaṃ na yathālikhitam /
upapattyantarāgāmupapattyantaravyavadhānena kliṭatvāt /
tammāccābrāhmaṇasya somabhakṣaṇaṃ pratiṣedhati /
yadi ca prayajamānasyeti samākhyayā na somabhaca  prāpyate tataḥ phalacamasavidhau sa yadi somaṃ bibhakṣayiṣeditina somamiti ca pratiṣedhanasaṃkīrttanaṃ nāvakalpeta tasmādasti camasināṃ somabhakṣa iti /
udgāṭacamasamekaḥ śrutisaṃyogāt 
idānīṃ vaṣaṭkārahomābhiṣaṣabhacānanutkaiva prasaṅgāt samākhyābhacaviśeṣānusaraṇameva tāvatkaroti /
tasminneva praiṣe prodgātṛṇāmiti śrūyate tava catu saṃdehaḥ kimeka evodgātā bhakṣayeduta sarvartvija uta stotrakāriṇaḥ āho khiccatvāro 'pi chandogā iti /
ke cittu dvitīyacaturthayoḥ pakṣayorekatvamicchanti /
sūtraiye 'pi sarvaśabdaprayogāt lakṣaṇāyāśca pratyāsatteḥ kevalacchandogaviṣayatvāt /
kutaḥ saṃdehaḥ /
visaṃvādaḥ sphuṭo hyatra prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ /
tatra kasyānurodhena kasya vṛttirbhavediti 
smaranti hi udgāturimityaṇpratyayaṃ na tu tasya karteti pratyayalopam /
tasmānnaudgāvaśabdādeṣo 'nugantavyaḥ /
tathā ca varaṇanimittamiti vakṣyati tenāyuktamidaṃ vyākhyānamiti /
ucyate /
udgātā gauṇa evāta mukhyodgāturasaṃbhavāt /
kalpito 'yaṃ parāvṛttyā brāhmaṇādiṣu rājavat 
yathaiva vyaṅgaiḥ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ yajatītyatra nāṅgānyanūdya vitvaṃ vidhīyate kiṃ tarhi pūrvaniṣpannaḥ samāsārtho vidheyo bha vati tathehāpi paripūrṇāṃsya padasya padāntarayogāt kadeśaniṣkarṣe ca sāmarthyābhāvādaśakya mevānuvadituṃ yo vaṣaṭkartturbhaca iti /
na hi prāksamāmāgacasya vaṣaṭkasaṃbandho yuktaḥ sāpekṣatve sati samāsānupapatteḥ /
nanu ca bhavati vai pradhānasya sāpecasyāpi samāsa iti satyapi vaṣaṭkartṛ saṃbandhe samāso 'vakalpiṣyate /
bhavedetadevaṃ yadi bhakṣa evaikaḥ sāpekṣa syādiha tu prāthamyamapi vaṣaṭkartṛ saṃbandhitvātmāpekṣam /
na hi prāthamyasya bhakṣo nimittaṃ kiṃ tarhi vaṣaṭkartṛtvamato vaṣaṭkarttuḥ prathama ityevaṃ saṃbandha āpadyeta tataśca vispaṣṭamasāmañjasyaṃ syādyo vaṣaṭkarturbhaca iti cānūdyamāne viśiṣṭānuvādadoṣo bhakṣamātreṇa vaṣaṭkartturanākṣepāt /
vaṣaṭakartṛtvasya ca kriyāntareṣvapya nai kāntyādanyatarānuvāde tu sarvabhakṣāṇāṃ prāthamyaṃ vidhīyeta sarvavaṣaṭkartṛvyāpārāṇāṃ ca /
taccāśakyaṃ katta mato vaṣaṭakarṭa prāthamyaviśiṣṭāpūrvabhakṣa vidhānametat /
tayośca parasparaniyamādatyantasamānaviṣayatvamato yāvati viṣaye vaṣaṭkārastāvatyeva prathamabhacaḥ /
kathaṃ punarvaṣaṭakārī nimittabhūtaḥ sannupādīyate kathaṃ cānupādīyamānasya niyamo 'vakalpate /
ucyate /
niyama sarvathā tāvadeka karmanimittakaḥ /
upādānānupādāne na viśeṣaḥ pratīyate 
  mūlyaṃ prāpaṇavyayaśca = deyaḥ /
anyairmahāśayaiyaiḥ kānicit khaṇḍāni saṃgrāhyāṇi teśca pratyekaṃ khaṇḍānā  mūlyaṃ prāpaṇavyayaśca = deya iti 
hauvasamākhyayā hi prāk yajamānasya yājoti to vacanāt sarvaṃ hotuḥ prāpitaṃ tava vacanena yājagrāmācaṃ yajamānasaṃbandhi kṛtaṃ vaṣaṭkārādayastu hotustadavasthā eva /
yadi punaryajamānādapanaya iti vyākhyāyeta tata stasya yājagrāmācaṃ prāpitaṃ sadapanauyataiti vaṣaṭkārādiprātyabhāvādapanayāśava na syāt /
tasmādyajamānasya yājepratyanena yājagrāmātrāpanayāddaṣaṭkārasya ca yājāto 'tyantavyatirekā daṅgāṅgitvābhāvācca yajamānena prayujāmānāyā upari hotā vaṣaṭkṛtya bhakṣayet /
vaṣaṭkāranimitto hi bhakṣo na bājānimitta ityanapanītaḥ /
yaṣṭurvā kāraṇāgamāt 
yadi yajamānasya yājyetyetāvanmālameva śrūyeta tataḥ kadā cinnāpanīyeta bhakṣaḥ iha tvevaṃ śrūyate svayaṃ niṣadya yajatīti /
vaṣaṭkāreṇa ca haviḥpradānārthatvādijyate na kevalayā yājyayā /
tathā inavānaṃ yajatoti yājyāta ārabhya yāvadyanaterarthaḥ samāpyate tāvannāvānitavyam /
ekakartṛkatve ca yājyāvaṣaṭkārayoridamupapadyate nānyathā /
tasmāt yatra yājyā tatra vaṣaṭkārabhakṣāvapītyantaregā/
pyekatvamaṅgabhāvaṃ cāpanayo vijñāyate /
pravṛttatvātpravarasyānapāyaḥ 
yattu pravaravaditi tatrocyate /tambavārtike /
pravaro na tvatikrānto yāvyākāle panīyate /
bhakṣaṇasya tu bhāvitvācchacyā upanaya kalpanā 
tṛtīyārthaśca kalpyaḥ syād dvitīyārthasya bādhanam /
samastasomavādhaśca yajiniṣkarṣa kalpanā 
yadi tāvadapūrva eva bhakṣaśvodyate tato'pyāra dupakārakatvaṃ na bhavatyadṛṣṭa kalpanātmakara gāviniyogaviprakarṣādasaṃbaḍopakāritvācca /
tathā taṃ prayacchediti dvitīyayā vispaṣṭaṃ saṃskāryatvaṃ gamyate /
anyathā hi teneti prāpnoti tasmātsaskāraḥ/
saṃskārasya caiṣa svabhāvo yadupayukta su santravārtike /
payeocyamāṇaṃ vā dravyamavalambate /
tatrāpi bhakṣitasya pu narupayogāsaṃbhavādupayuktasaṃskāratvameva jñāyate /
tena phalacamasaḥ saṃskārabhūtaṃ bhakṣamupasarpanneva śakyo niyokta yadi kka cidupayogaṃ gacchasi tato bhakṣaṇena saṃskṛiya se nānyathā sa copayajāmānatvaṃ prārthayamānaḥ prakaraṇādyāgopayogitvaṃ pratipadyate /
tatrāpi yāvatyanupayujāmāno yajamānabhaca saṃskāryatvaṃ na pratipadyate tāvataiva yajñabhāgenārthāpacyā saṃbadhyataityavadhāraṇādyajamānaca masābhyā senaivaikena saṃbadhyate na hi grahacamasāntareṣvanupayujāmānasyāsya yajamānabhakṣatvamanupapannam ataḥ somo 'pyanugrahīṣyate /
yahā aprotiṣṭomaprakaraṇena saṃbaddho 'yaṃ bhanaśabda uccāryyamāṇaḥ prakṛtaṃ somabhakṣamevāvalambate /
sa ca yāgopayuktadravyaśeṣasaṃskāratvena prajñāta iti phalacamasamapi tādṛśameva saṃskatta" śaknoti /
na tvasāvidānaumanya prayojanaḥ śakyaḥ kalpayituṃ na ca tasya karmāntaratve kiṃ cicchandāntarādi kāraṇamasti /
api ca sa yadi somaṃ vibhakṣayiṣediti svavākyopātta naiva somabhakṣaṇana saṃbandhī vijñāyate anyathā hi tadupādānaṃ vyartha meva syāt /
na ca na somamityanuvādo 'vakalpate /
yadi bhakṣānta ra mevedamārādupakārakaṃ codyeta tataḥ samānakāryatvābhāvānnaiva somaṃ nivarttayedanivarttite ca tasminna pratiṣedhānuvādaḥ syānna ca vidhiyukto vākya bhedānekādṛṣṭa kalpanā prasaṅgādasaṃbaī ca vākyaṃ bhavet /
yadi somaṃ bhagona saṃskatta micchettataḥ phalacamamabhakṣaṇa mārādapakārakaṃ kuryātphalacamasaṃ vā saṃskuryāditi /
yadā tvayamartho gṛhyate yena bhataṇena yathābhūtaṃ somaṃ saṃskattu micchetṛtīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pāda /
phona tathābhūtameva phalacamasa~ saṃskuryāditi tadā 'rthāpattyā yajamānacamasayāgābhyāmasaṃvandhaḥ kṛto bhavati tasmādivyāyāmayaṃ somavikāra iti siddam /
saiṣā vyavadhāraṇakalpaneti /
yathaivāśvapratigraheṣdyāṃ yāvato 'śvānpratigṛhauyāditi śrute pratigrāhayediti vyavadhārya kalpitaṃ tathaivāla bhakṣaṃ prayacchediti śrute yāgasādhanaṃ prayacchediti kalpyate /
etena pūtīkānabhiṣuṇuyā dilyādauni vyākhyātāni /
homāt 
homānuvādena darbhataruṇaka vidhirijyāvikāratve 'vakalpate /
camasaiśca tulyakālatvāt 
saṃdigdhayāgasādhanonnayanaikavākyatā caitattulyatve 'vakalpate nānyathāve /
liṅgadarśanāca 
somapratiṣedhānuvādaśca liṅgamiti vyākhyātam /
anuprasarpiṣu sāmānyāt 
daśapeye śataṃ brāhmaṇā somaṃ bhakṣayanti daśa daśaikaikaṃ camasamanuprasarpeyuriti tatra rājanyacamaso 'pi kiṃ brāhmaṇaireva daśabhirbhacayitavyaḥ uta rājanyairiti maṃdehaḥ /
kaḥ punaḥ saṃdeha hetuḥ ke cidāhuvacanavyaktibheda iti /
yadi hi daśadaśaikeka miti vidhistatastulyajātantravārtike /
toyeṣu daśakeṣu sarvatra vihiteṣu śataṃ brāhmaṇā iti yaṃthāprāptānuvādī brāhmaṇagrāmavaddūstā bhavatīti rājanyā daśa /
atha punaḥ śataṃ brāhmaṇā iti vidhirdaśadaśaikaika miti anuvādastato vidhau gauṇatvāsaṃbhavātsarvatra brāhmaṇaireva bhacayitavyamiti brāhmaṇā daśa /
kiṃ tāvatprāptamanuprasapeṃyurityasya vidhisāmarthyābhakṣayantīti cānuvādena sāmarthyāddaśadaśaikaikamiti vidhau sati ke daśetyapekṣāyāṃ tulyajātīyeṣu saṃkhyāvṛttikhābhāvyādbrāhmaṇacama seṣu brohmaṇā rājanyacamase rājanyā daśeti gamyate /
sāmānyāditi ca daśasaṃkhyāṃ coyitvā nivṛttavyāpāre śāstre tatpūraṇārthamatāsu vyaktiṣūpādīyamānāsu yāsāṃ kiṃ citpratyāyakamasti tā grahautatryāstulyajātīyānāṃ ca sāmānya gamakaṃ vidyate na jātyantarānugatānām /
atha vā sāmānyāditi viṣayasāmānyādarthekatve dravyaguṇa yoriti hi phalacamasaṃ pratyupādoyamānayoḥ kṣatriyatvadaśatvayoḥ parasparaniyame sati yāvata viṣaye daśatvaṃ tāvati rājanyatvamityavagamyate iti balāddaśa rājanyā vijñāyante /
atha vā sāmānyāditi tulyakāryaṃ tulyajātīyaṃ ca tulyasya bādhakaṃ bhavati /
tadyadi rājasūyacodanāto rājanyatvaṃ prāptaṃ prakṛtitaścaikatvaṃ tatva daśatvaṃ vidhīyamānaṃ sāmānyādātideśikatvāccaikatvaṃ bādhate na jātibhinna kāryatvāttataścā nivṛttajātireva yajamānacamaso daśatvena yojayitavya iti daśa rājanyā bhavanti /
nanu ca daśatve vidhauyamāne yadekaikaṃ camasamanuprasarpantoti viśiṣṭānuvādādākyaṃ bhidyate /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
camasamiti dvitīyāntaṃ kevalamanūdhate tābatā tu saṃskāryatvaṃ gamyate /
na ca camasānāṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ mukkā 'nyaḥ saṃskārastena sa evānuprasarpaṇaśabdena lakṣyate tatra ca pratyekameva bhakṣaṇaṃ prāptamiti tadapyanudyate /
tasmānna vākyabhedaḥ /
brāhmaṇā vā tulyaśabdatvāt 
na vā rājanyā bhakṣayeyuḥ kutaḥ /
śatabrāhmaṇasaṃyukto vidhiravāvagamyate /
anyathā tadupādānaṃ gauṇaṃ vyarthaṃ ca te bhavet 
padārthātideśapace śāstrātideśapace vā tadbhedāt kadā cidbhedo bhavedyāgagatastu vyāpāro 'tidiśyataiti daśame baccāmaḥ sa ca niravayavatvāyugapada tidiśyate /
anena cātmasiyartha yugapadeva prayājādyapūrvāṇi gṛhyante taiśca prayājādayaḥ prayājādibhirapi svaśāstrāṇi tena prakṛtivadityevaṃ rūpasyātideśasyaikatvā tsarvāṅgeṣvaviśiṭasya sarvatra pravṛtti pravṛttirvā naikadeśeṣu /
śarairapi kuśāḥ prāptā eva bādhyantaityuktaṃ balābalādhikaraṇe /
tadyadi tāvadanārabhāvādānurodhana khādiratvādiviṣayo'tideśaḥ parityajyate tata evāṅgāntareṣvapauti sarvanivṛttiprasaṅgaḥ tatra coktam /
atha keṣāṃ cit prākatānāmanurodhena tadviṣayo 'tideśa pramāṇaṃ kriyate tataḥ khādiratvādiprāptirapya viśiṣṭeti sphuṭaṃ dviruktavaṃ prāpnoti /
yāgagatavyāpārāpecilāñca khaprakaraṇāmnānamapyatikramya vikṛtayaḥ prākṛtaṃ tāvad gṛhṇantīti sarvatra sthāpayiṣyāmaḥ /
tenāpyanārabhāvādādatideśaprāpteḥ prāthamyamavaśyaṃ ca prakṛtiṣu sra vādiprāptirapekṣitavyā /
yāvatā ca yatra na suvādayaḥ prāpnuvanti tāvatā khādiratvādayo 'pauti nopadeśaviṣayatvaṃ ghaṭate /
na caiṣāṃ kratusaṃbandhī vispaṣṭaḥ /
so'pyanyathā'nupapattyā sruvādihāraṇa kalpayitavyaḥ /
sarvārthatvavādī ca prakṛtisaṃbandhaṃ tāvadabhyupagacchati /
tena ca parihṛte śrānarthakye vikṛtisaṃbandhī niṣpramāṇakaḥ /
pramāṇavattaro hyatideśena kratusaṃvandhaḥ yeṣāṃ tu kratusaṃbandha eva pratyakṣaste 'nāramyavādā api sarvārthā eva /
yathaiṣa vai prajāpatiḥ saptadaśo yajñe 'nvāyatta ityevamādayastasmāt khādiratvādi prakṛtyarthamiti siddham /
prakaraṇaviśeṣāttu vikṛtau vi rodhi syāt tantravārtike/
apavādādhikaraṇametat /
tatra pūrvādhikaraṇenaiva sāmidhenausāptadaśyānārabhyavādasya prakṛtyarthatve prakaragāvītena pāñcadaśyena saha vikalpa iti viśeṣāśaṅkāṃ nivarttayati /
kathaṃ punaḥ prākaraṇikena viśeṣavidhinā sahātulyabalasya vikalpo 'bhidhīyate /
āha /
tatra nāma viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya nirākriyā /
pratyakṣo yatra saṃbandho viśeṣeṇa pratīyate 
sāmidhenau svarūpa prayuktatve 'narthikā saṃkhyetyavaśyaṃ yāgāpūrvasāghanatvakāritaḥ saṃbandho 'bhyupagantavyaḥ /
na ca yāgāpūrvasāghanatvaṃ prakaraṇāhate lacayituṃ śakyate iti navame vacyāmaḥ /
tena prakaraṇānugraha viśeṣātyāñcadaśyamapūrvasaṃbandhapramāṇapratyāsattaṃ rbalauya /
vidhirapi hi pūrva prayojanavati puruṣaṃ niyute sāptadaśyāca pāñcadaśyaṃ śīghrata prayojanavadavaghāryataiti vidhikālavaiṣamyādatulyabalatvam tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
api ca kratumaviguṇaṃ kartta puruṣaḥ pravarttate na sāmidhenī /
kratvaṅgatve ca sāptadaśyasya na kiṃ cit śrutyādi pramāṇamupalabhāmahe  yathā pāñcadaśyasya prakaraṇam /
tasmādetatpāñcadṛśyaṃ sāmidhenīnāṃ darśapūrṇamāsayośca vākyaprakaraṇābhyāmavadhāryate /
sāptadaśyaṃ tu kevalaṃ sāmidhenyarthameva tasyedānomānarthakyaparihārāya khādiratvādivat kratusaṃvandhaḥ kalpyate /
yadi tvasau pratīcchenna tvasau saṃkhyāntarāvaruḍaḥ san pratīcchati /
tava sāmidhenaunāsubhayathā 'pyavaiguṇyaṃ bhavati krato punaḥ pāñcadaśyena /
tataśca kāṃsyabhojivadamukhye 'pyavirodhaḥ syāt kimaṅga punaryavāṅgaguṇāvirodha eva spaṣṭaḥ /
tasmātkratvavaṣṭambhadarpitena pāñcadaśyenotkālitaṃ sāptadaśyaṃ kliṣṭena yāvadatideśena pāñcadaśyaṃ naiva vika tīḥ prāpnoti tāvadopadeśikena sāptadaśyena prathamatarāvaruḍatvāttābhyo nirākṛtaṃ kevalaprakṛtiviṣayatvenaivāvadhāryate iti vyavasthāyāmuktāyāmucyate /
na sāptadaśyaṃ balavadhikṛtiṣvaupadeśikam /
anārabhyavidhestaddhi sāmidhenyaṅṅgatāṃ gatam 
yathā prakaraṇa prāptaṃ prakṛtī balavattaram /
tathā 'tideśavijñātaṃ kratvaṅgavikṛtiṣvapi 
vāṅgena pāñcadaśyena vyāptīstā hyatideśataḥ /
vihitaṃ sāmidheyaṅgaṃ sāptadaśyaṃ na gṛgahate 
sūtrakāro'pi vikatau virodhīti yadabravīt /
praka tau naitadastīti tadetāvadvivakṣayā 
to yadyapi daurbalyaṃ vākyātprakaraṇasya naḥ /
tathā 'pi viṣayānyatvātkratau tahiniyojakam 
viśeṣaścāyamevāsya yadasādhāraṇaṃ kratoḥ /
sāmidhenauṣa tulyatve śeṣatve vākyakalpite 
naimittikaṃ tu prakṛtau taḍikāra saṃyogaviśeṣāt 
yadvaiśyādinimittana sāptadaśyaṃ vidhīyate /
tantu syātpraka, tāveva pāñcadaśyasya bādhakam 
pāñcadaśyamabādhitvā hyātmānaṃ na labheta tat /
madveṣu tena sarveṣu prayogeṣu śrutaṃ hi tat 
prayogāḥ santi tasyānye viprarājanyakartṛkāḥ /
sāptadaśyamabādhitvā yeṣvātmā tena labhāte 
nekatraikena saṅkhyātāḥ saṅkhyāyante pareṇa tāḥ /
nityasya bādhaśakirhi nārthāpattyā va kalpate 
asañjātavirodhaṃ hi nityaṃ sarvaṃ vidhīyate /
naimittika tu tadyāptaviṣayatvāviruṣyate 
kica prayogasāmānye nityaṃ sarva vidhīyate /
naimittika viśeṣe tu tammāttailavattaram 
kāmyanaimittikānāṃ tu vākyopāttaṃ prayojanam /
ataḥ śīghra prayuktatvānnityāta balavattarāḥ 
śrutyeva puruṣārthe hi śīghraṃ karttā pravarttate /
naimittike hi ṭūrasthe cireṇāsau pravarttate 
pūrvādhikaraṇa naiva pūrvapakṣo 'tra sūvitaḥ /
nityasyāsti viśeṣo hi kāmyātprakaraṇe yataḥ 
bādhyeta phalalobhena nityaṃ kāmyena tava cet /
paśyato madhu durbuherbinipātastato bhavet 
āśrayastādṛśo hoṣṭo yādṛśaḥ praka taḥ kratuḥ /
khādiratvādibhirnityairvyāptaścāsau pratīyate 
tena gṛhṇāti hi svārthaṃ na tu kāmyaṃ kathaṃ cana /
itikarttavyatārthitvātsaṃyuktaṃ hi na gṛhyate 
tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
tvarthayo'pyasya svārtharūḍo na labhyate /
pūrvādhikaraṇanyāyastasmānnaimittikeṣvapi 
asaṃyogādavādhana saṃyogo 'sya viśiṣyate /
punaḥ karṭa viśiṣṭasya prayogasya parigrahāt 
na tvatulyārthayorvādhaḥ kratvarthapuruṣārdhayoḥ /
na yukto na virodho 'sti bhinnagocarayostayoḥ 
na sādhayati paśvādona kratvarthaścamaso yathā /
godohanaṃ tathā 'nyārthaṃ na kratvarthasya sādhanam 
anyā hi vacanavyaktiḥ phaloddeśena taddidhau /
anyā praṇayanoddeśe tasmānna iyasaṃbhavaḥ 
ataḥ kamipadākṣepānnāsya praṇayane vidhiḥ /
avidhānādaśeṣatvānna śeṣāntaravādhanam 
tena praṇayanābhyāsaḥ kārya kāmyaguṇaṃ prati /tantravārtika /
yathendra vāyudaivatye graho mitrādyasaṃbhavāt 
iyoretramavaiguṇyaṃ kratośca syātphalasya ca /
na hi svasādhanatyāgādanyasādhanasādhitaiḥ 
ṛtvarthaṃ karma gṛhṇāti sa eva svārthasiddhaye /
nirvyāpāro guṇaḥ kāmaṃ na sādhayati kaścana 
sāca prakaraṇenāmmai dattā praṇayanātmikā /
tayāṃ ca camasaḥ pūrvaprāpto 'nyo vidyate guṇaḥ 
tadavādhena naiveha tasya kaścidvidhi śrutaḥ /
kāmyena gṛhyamāṇā ca kriyā praṇayanātmikā 
karaṇe tasya doṣaḥ syānniṣiddhasyeva saṃgatī /
bhinna prayojano'pi hi kāmyo guṇo 'vāntarakāryaikatvādvirodhiguṇāntarajñāna mithyātvāvadhāraṇa samarthaḥ /
tathā hi /
prāmāṅgakoṃ kratoḥ siddhiṃ kāmyo hi kurute guṇaḥ /
gṛhṇanti na ca siddhārthāḥ kratavaḥ svaguṇaṃ tadā 
haviḥsaṃyavanārthānāmapāṃ praṇayanaṃ hi yat /
tad gṛhotvā guṇaḥ kāmyaḥ prayuṅgena kriyāntaram 
tena praṇayanābhyāsaḥ kratvartho'pi na vidyate /
niṣphalatvādato vādhaḥ prayogātkamā sakṛt 
prayogamātre hi camaso godohanaṃ viśeṣe pūrvaprāptasvāsau tadabādhena labdhātmā naivaṃ godohanaṃ sāvakāśa tantradhārtika /
cāsau netarat dūre cāsau puruṣārthasya godohanaṃ tu saṃnikṛṣṭārthaṃ puruṣārthā ca sarvaśāstrapravṛttiḥ /
yaśca tādardhyātādakato viśeṣo nāsau tantramiti vaccati arthasyavikatatvāditi /
mando hyaṣa viśeṣaḥ kratvarthenaiva kratvartho viśeṣādivihitena bādhitavyo nānyārtheneti /
tenobhayoḥ sannidhivaśātparasparaśaktivilopānniyama /
praṇayanasyāpyanyatra prayoge siḍātmakasya svasādhanopasaṃhāraśaktilopa godohanasyāpi praṇayanāntarakalpanāśaktivighātaḥ /
paśukāmaprayogavyatiriteṣveva camamasya śāstrīyatvaṃ tasmāttahikārī goṭohanam /
yathā tu vikatau camasa eva bhaviṣyati tathā Sṣṭame vacyati nivṛttirvā karmabhedāditi /
tena prakṛtāvevaitadvikārakamiti /
iṣṭārthamagnyādheyaṃ prakaraṇāt 
anārabhyavādaprastāvenāgnyādheyasya prathamaṃ tāvadanārabhyavādatvameva pratipādyate prakaragona tāvatpavamāneṭārthatvaṃ prāpnoti/
tyā tu śuḍāgnyarthatvamataḥ prakaraṇaviśeṣāddā tadyuktasya saṃskāro dravyavaditi iṣṭayarthāgnisaṃskāratvāt śrutivākyaprakaragauraviruḍe riṭārthāgnyarthatvamavadhāryate /
śuddhā gnyarthatve ca niṣprayojanatvāttaddāregauvāgnyādhānagrahaṇa sāmarthyaṃ tasmādiṣṭayarthaṃ sāmānyābhidhānam /
api ca prakaraṇādeva pavamāneṣṭiviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam /
na vā tāsāntadarthatvāt 
yadyārādupakārakamādhānaṃ bhavettataḥ prakaraṇādiṣṭyarthamiti gamyeta vākyasaṃyogātta, dvitīyānirdiṣṭā gnisaṃskārārthametadevaṃ ca sati yadyagnayaḥ pavamāneṣṭārthā bhaveyastatastareṇādhānamapi tadarthaṃ bhavet /
tāstu niṣphalatvādagnyarthā ityuktamataśca guṇānāṃ ca parārthatvādityanenaiva parasparānaṅgatvaṃ na hi dvitīyā śrutiḥ pra karagona bādhyate /
liṅgadarśanācca 
tenaivaṃ punarnavaṃ karotīti cāgnisaṃskārārthatāṃ darśayati /
tatprakṛtyarthaṃ yathā 'nye 'nārabhyavādāḥ 
siddhe 'nāramyavādanave khādiratvādivadeva prakṛtyarthattvamagnihāreṇa prakṛtyanupraveśāt /
sarvārthaṃ vā ''dhānasya svakālatvāt 
sūtrāttāva diyaṃ buddhirbhavati yadi prakṛtikālā dhānaṃ kriyeta tataḥ prakṛtyarthaṃ bhavetsvakāle tu vasantādau kriyamāṇamagṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvātsarvārthaṃ vijñāyate /
tathā cānuṣṭhānasādhāraṇya masyaikādaśe vaccati dravyasyākakālaniṣpatteḥ prayogaḥ sarvārtha syāditi /
prakṛtyarthatve ca darśapūrṇamāsajyotiṣṭomārthametad bhavet /
tatra ca pradhānavaśavarttitvāisante pūrṇamāsyamāvāsyayośca kriyeta tathā ca sati vasante paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāyāmādadhītantravārtike/
tetyetāni vacanānyanarthakāni bhaveyuktasmātsarvārthatvamiti /
na vetadyuktam /
na hyādhānasya prakṛtyā vikṛtyā vā saṃ bandhe kiṃ citpramāṇamasti prakaraṇe sati yatpavamāneṣṭārthaṃ na jātaṃ tahinaiva śrutyādiṣaṭake nānyakarmārthaṃ bhaviṣyatīti kuta etat /
nanvevaṃ sati pūrvādhikaragonaiva gatametat /
satyaṃ gacchedyadi pavamāneṣṭiva harśapūrṇamāsādaunyapi niṣphalāni bhaveyuḥ /
teṣāṃ tu phalavattvādguṇānāṃ ca parārthatvādityeṣa nyāyo nāstīti śakyamagnihāreṇa ka maṅgatvaṃ kalpayituṃ niṣphalasyādhīnasyāvaśyakalpanīye prayojane 'gnihāreṇa khādirattvādivatkammarthatvamāpadyate /
śaknuvanti hi prayogamadhyasthā vanhayaḥ karmāṇyupasthāpapitum /
yathaiva procaṇādīnāṃ vrohyādisvarūpamatikramya khādirattvādināṃ ca suvādisvarūpaṃ kammāpūrvaprayutatvaṃ kalpitaṃ tathā ''dhānasyāpi agnisvarūpātikrameṇa kalpayitavyayaṃ yadi cāgnisvarūpamā prayuktamevādhānaṃ bhavettataḥ kamāṇyanāhitenāpyagninā sidhyeyaḥ /
taiśca puruṣasya saguṇaiḥ kāryaṃ nāgnibhiḥ /
tenāvaśyaṃ bhāvini kamasaṃbandhe prakatyarthatvamahimatātvādupanyastam /
yattu svakālatvaṃ tadupadeśātideśaprāptasya yūpacchedanavatprayogasādhāraṇyārthamiti na sarvārthatvaṃ gamayati /
yadapi basantādigrahaṇaṃ tadasyaprāptaviṣayamarthavadbhaviṣyati /
nahi darśapūrṇamāsārthasyāvānasya vasantakālatvaṃ prāptaṃ pratyarḍamāsaṃ prayogapramakteḥ /
nādhyagnihotretaradarvihomārthasya paurṇamāsyamāvāsyākāla praptiḥ /
nava prayogasādhāraṇyaṃ svakālavacanāhate siyatauti nānarthakatvamata evaṃ vyācaṣṭe /
na kasya citkarmaṇo'ṅgamādhānaṃ kiṃ tarhi dvitīyā saṃyogātṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
dagnyarthameva /
te tvagnayaśca svakālatvādityanena sarvārthā bhaviṣyantīti tadvāreṇa sarvārthivamityucyate /
svakālatvādityapi svātantryāmnānādityarthaḥ /
yattvitarānārabhyavādavaditi tatrābhidhīyate /
siddhe'ṅgatve tatasteṣāṃ kimarthatvaṃ vicāritam /
na tu karmaṅgabhāve hi pramāṇaṃ kiṃ cidasti te 
docāsu hi somakrayasamaupe agnīṣomauya samābrāyate /
tasya ca yadyapi vacanasāmarthyātpaśudharmasamope anuṣṭhānaṃ bhaviṣyati tathā 'pi prakaraṇena naiva vyāṭataṃ sarvakaraṇānāmutpattideśānatirekāt /
sabanīyānāmapi sutyākālamutpattivākya maupavamadhye tu gugā/
dhaiva śrutiḥ /
na ca tathā prakaraṇaṃ bhavati /
anubandhyāttu dūrasyaiva somānte kriyamāṇatvāt tasmādabāntaramakaraṇatṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
bākyasaṃyogābhyāmapratibaddhena jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇenāgnīṣāmoyasya sthānaṃ viprakaṣṭārtha bādhitvā jyotiṣṭomārthāstāvadete ityetatkalpyate /
tasya ca somadravyakatvānna paśudharmeṃ kiṃ citprayojanamityānarthayāttadaṣvityevamaīṣvevāvataranto SSṅgatvā viśeṣātviṣvapyavataranti /
satyapi tadaṅgatve yogyatvābhāvānna docaṇauyādiṣvavataraṇam /
satyapi ca yogyatve sāmānyasaṃbandhābhāvāntra tadaṅgapaśūnām /
tasmāttrayāṇāṃ samānaṃ vidhānamiti prāpte 'bhidhauyate /
sthādetadevaṃ yadi jyotiṣṭomahāreṇa prakaraṇāviśeṣa syāt /
asti tu viśeṣaḥ savanauyānāmaupavamadhye 'hanyutpattarāgnayamajamagniṣṭāmaālabheta aindrāgnamukthye hitoyamityādinā hi paśudharmasamaupe savanauyā utpāditāḥ /
tasmātkevala savanauyārthā eveti /
sthānāca pūrvasya 
kathaṃ punaridaṃ śrutiliṅgādhikaraṇaviparītamabhidhīyate /
na hi tatraivamiṣṭaṃ prakaraṇāddidevanādayo rā jamūyārthā sthānāccābhiṣecanīyārthā iti /
tathā śrutyaindrī gārhapatyārthā liṅgenendrārtheti /
yukta tava prakaraṇāmānena balīyasā pramāṇena nirākāḍokṛte jaghanyapra māṇānutyānātmamuccayānāśrayaṇam /
na hi aba punaḥ kalpanayā vinā śeṣasya na kiṃ citmiyati nāpi śeṣiṇāmindrāgnyādīnāmupāyānta reṇāpi smṛtisiddheḥ /
dhūṃha punaḥ satyapi savanīyasaṃbandhāirmāṇāṃ nairākāṅkṣā 'gnīṣomoyasya paśuvammarvinā siyabhāvātmātyantaramavaśyaṃ kalpanīya mubhayoravipratipattaḥ /
na caitasya tadā darśapū māsaprakṛtitvaṃ bhavet /
yo hi prakṛtibhūtaḥ paśūnāṃ sa darśapūrṇamāsavikārī bhavati itare tu prāṇidravya katvasāmānyāttavikārāstatra kiṃ savanauyārthāttataḥ sārūpyahāraprabhavenātideśenāgnīṣomoyo gṛhātyathopadeśagandhena kena cidityupadeśāntargatatvātkrameṇa viniyogo yuktaḥ ṣaḍividhopadeśapratyastamaye hyatideśaḥ kalpyate /
tasmādyadhaivānyatropadeśātideśābhyāṃ prakṛtivikṛtyarthatvaṃ yāgagatasya vyāpārasya tathaiveha sthānaprakaraṇābhyāmubhayārthatvamamūtragdhyāyāstu sarvopadeśābhāvādatideśenaiva prāptirbhaviṣyati /
tasmādanupālambhaḥ sūtrasya /
śvastvekeṣāṃ tatra prāk śrutirguṇārthā 
yaduktaṃ sthānādagnīṣomauyārthā ityetad gṛhomaḥ /
yattu prakaraṇātmavanauyārthā ityetanna mṛṇyāmahe kutaḥ /
guṇārthopavasadhye 'nhi savanauyapunaḥśrutiḥ /
utpattiḥ prakriyā caiṣāmāśvinagrahaṇottarā  vapayā protaḥsatrane pracarantīti anenaiva vacane motkaṣṭe pradhāne pradhānadeśatvādaṅgānāmupākaraṇādiṣvapyutkṛṣṭeṣu kālāniyame prāpte satyāśvinagrahaṇānantaryyaṃ vidhauyate /
tena tadeva guṇārthaṃ śravaṇamitarathā hi vākyaṃ bhidyeta /
pa rivyāgopākaraṇayoḥ kālavidhānāhuvyadevatāyuktasya ca yāgasya vidheḥ /
nanu cātideśaprāptameva parivyāṇaṃ ta sminneva kāle yāge vidhīyamāne'nuta /
satyamatideśena prāptaṃ na tu tadidānoṃ kriyate yūpasādhāraṇyena tatkālāstvityetramagnauṣomoya kāla kṛtādavopakārasiddheḥ /
evaṃ tarhi sādhāraṇyādeva prāptaṃ vidyamānamahota na śakyaṃ ta danuvadituma pratyabhijñānāt /
tannāmānyataḥ prāptamanūdyate yattā draṣyeṇa prāptaṃ pratyabhijñāyate /
na ca pūrveyuḥ kṛtasyāśvinagrahaṇottarakālaṃ varttamānatvenānuvādo bhavati /
nahi tadā'sau parivyayati /
na ca pūrvakṛtasya paryagni kṛ tādiśabdavadohaśena śabdenānuvādaḥ pūrvottara kālakamavadhidayaparicchinnatvāt /
evaṃ tahya smāḍācyātprāptamanūyatāṃ sa āśvinaṃ grahaṃ gṛhītvopaniṣkramya yūpaṃ parivyayatīti /
tadapi nāsti pratyabhijñānābhāvādeva /
yadetadaprākṛtaṃ savanīyaparivyāgaṇa metasya śuddhasya śravaṇādraśanāyāśca prākṛtaparivyāṇa nibandhanatvādyena kena cihāsaḥ prabhṛtinā karaṇe sati trivṛttvānuvādo na prāpnoti taṃtrāne kārthavidhānādākyabhedaḥ /
tadā caivaṃ bhāṣyagranthaḥ /
i tarathā hi parivyāṇamya kiṃ cihiyeta yatsaṃbandhivenopātaṃ vid dravyaṃ kālo vidhauyatopākaragaṇasya cetyupākaraṇakālo ṭraॅvyadevatāviśiṣṭaṃ ca karma vidhīye tetyarthaḥ/
tasmādasya guṇārthatvādasti pūrveyuḥ savanīyānāṃ prakaraṇamiti /
naikadeśatvāt 
yadā hi pūrve sāṅgānāṃ savanoyānāmāmrānaṃ tadā tatraiva sarvānuṣṭhāne prāpte vacanāipāpracārādimātvamutṛṣyeta nopākaraṇādauni tadādi vā 'bhisaṃbandhāditi /
ye vapāhīmottarakālā padārthāstatmantripā tino vā tanmātrasyotkarṣo bhavenna prāgbhāvināmupākaraṇādaunāṃ yāni cājñātakālānyaṅgāni teṣāṃ pradhānakālatvaṃ vaccate/
paśkhaṅgāni tvavadhāritapūrveḥ kālatvānna pradhānakālaṃ gacchati /
tasmāipāpracāreṇānutkṛṣṭa sthānenaiva vākyenotkarṣaḥ karttavyastataśca guṇavākye sati anekārthavi ghānādvākyaṃ bhidyeta /
utpattivākye na doṣaḥ tasmādetanṛtpattyarthamiti/
na tviha bhāṣyakāreṇa vidheyānekārthatvaṃ darśitam /
evameva tu guṇārthatanvākā bhidya tatyabhihitam /
śañcastviha pūrvedyaḥ prāptopākaraṇotkarṣamāvavighānāḍākyabhedaḥ pariharttum /
tatra ke cidevaṃ samarthayante yathā kilāgneyyā S'gnaudhamiti jyotiṣṭomasaṃbandhe tahiśeṣe ca vidhaugramāne'nekārthatvamuktametramiha vapāpracāregrānutkṛṣṭasyopākaraṇasyotkarṣaśca karttavyaḥ tahiśeṣaścetyame kārthatvamiti /
na tvidamāgneyauvākyasadṛśam /
tatra hi saṃbandhaviśeṣapare vidhau sāmānyasaṃbandhaprāptimanyato 'pekṣamāṇe kāsu cidāgneśoṣu tatsadbhāvāditara viṣayasāmānyasaṃbandhaṃ pratyanyathā'nupapattiḥ kṣoyate /
atastu vedenānabhyupetaṃ taddidhiṃ kalpayato vākyabhedo bhavati na viha tādṛk pratipakṣo 'sti /
yataḥ sāmānyenotkarṣaprāptiṃ dṛṣṭvā viśeṣaparasyārthāpattikopa kalpyeta /
tatrāpi cettatantravārtike /
darthāpattitrādhinau pratipakṣabhūtā sāmānyaprāptirnābhaviṣyannāgneyaumātrapramāṇaṃ nirākariṣyata /
prāpte 'pi karmagaye kapadopāttānekārthavidhiḥ śoṇādya dāharaustava tava pratipāditaḥ /
tena yadyapi ākhinaṃ gṛhaṃ gṛhītvetyanena iyamapi prātamavanamāśvinaga hottara kālatvaṃ ca vidhī yeta tathā'pi vidhāyakasyaikapadānusārāttasya tasyopadiśyetetyetadāpattirnāsti kimutātraika vidhāne 'rthādevetarasiddheḥ /
ata eva bhāṣyakāreṇāne ka vidhidūṣaṇe 'bhihitaṃ na cāneko 'rthaḥ parasparāsaṃbandhe sati śakyo vidhātumiti /
jānāti hyasau yathā saṃbaḍānāmarthānā mekasminvihite 'nye vinaivāyāsena prāpnuvanti /
tena yā kasmintrihite 'rthādarthasahasamaparamāpadyate na kaścidirodhī vidherāyāso vā ha śyate ityāthīyate /
tasya tvanyathā 'pyupapadyamānattvamevaiko nirākaraṇopāyaḥ /
na cehāsti sa pakṣo yadveṣa vidhiḥ sutyāprātaḥ savanasaṃbandhāvakṛtvā āśvina gṛhaṇānanta vidadhyāttammādadoṣaḥ /
nacaiva tveṣa doṣaḥ yasyānekadravyadevatāviśiṣṭakarma vidhānam /
api ca jyotiṣṭomasutyāprātaḥ savanaviśeṣa kālasaṃyogo 'paraḥ kalpanauya /
sarveṣu cotkarṣāpakarṣeṣu sāmānyaviśeṣarūpo 'neka vidhidoṣostauti prāptakama guṇaviṣya saṃbhavātkamrmāntara vidhitvaprasaṅgaḥ /
tadyathā māhendrasya stotraṃ pratyabhiṣicyataityavābhiṣecanīyasya mādhyandina savanamāhendra stotrakālavidheranekārthatvamevaṃ tiṣṭhantaṃ paśuṃ prati prayajantotyādiṣvapi yojanīyam /
api caikasminpadāyeṃ 'nuṣṭhīyamāna vidhīyamāne cārthāntaraṃ dvedhā ''padyate /
kiṃ citprayatnāntarasādhyaṃ kiṃ cittadanuniṣpādyam /
yathā bhakṣavidho gṛhaṇātṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
daya tṛptiśca /
tatra yatprayatnāntarasādhyaṃ na ca tasminnakate vihitakaraṇaṃ śakyamityavadhārthyate tatvārthāpattilabhyaṃ vidhiśaktyantaraṃ kalapyate /
yā ca yāvatī ca śāstrīyā sā'vagatirbhavati /
yattvanuniṣpādi bahupi puruṣasya śā svasya ca vyāpārantaramantareṇaiva sidhyati na tena kaśvidāyāso bhavati /
na cehāśvinagrahaṇānantarye vidhīyamāne 'nuṣṭhīyamāne vā sutyāprātaḥsavanādisaṃbandhe bhedena vyāparitavyam /
tena nāva kaścidutkarṣa sāmānyaṃ vidhatte /
śrutamātrāśvinagrahaṇānantaryyabhātre vihite yadi tadantargatatvātsutyāprātaḥ savanā'harbhāgaviśeṣa muhūrttanāḍikācaṇalavanimeṣakālatvadravyasattvādayaḥ prasajyante kiṃ kriyatām /
api ca śiṃśapāmānayetyatrāpi vṛtcatvadravyatvasattādyācepāḍākyabheda syāt /
ataḥ pūrvedyuḥ prāptasyopākaraṇasya kālāntaramātramāśvinagrahaṇānantavyaṃ vidhīyataityadoṣaḥ /
anye tu iyoḥ parivyāṇopākaraṇayorutkarṣādākyabhedaṃ samarthayante /
tadapi tu suparihara kevalaparivyāṇotkarṣādeva tadādi vā 'bhisaṃbandhādityevasupākaraṇotkarṣasiddheḥ /
tatraitatyaprakṛtiprāpto dharma uskṛṣyamāṇastadāyutkarṣaṃ karoti nāpūrva iti /
tadayuktaṃ kṛtadeśāttu pūrveṣāmityatvāprākṛtānāmapi videvanādīnāmapakarṣavarṇanena tathā 'pūrvamityasya viśiṣṭa viṣayatvavyākhyānāt /
atha vā sa āśvinaṃ grahamityetadvākyaprātaparivyāṇāntarānuvādādavākyabheda iti /
athocyetāviśeṣita sādhanakatvāttatva trivṛttvānuvādo na saṃbhavatīti tadyuktam /
evaṃ hi siddhāntavādyapi pūrvapakṣavādinā coditaḥ svayaṃ parihāra vaccati so 'syāpri bhaviṣyatantravārtike /
toti /
nanu ca tasyāpūrva karmma vidhānādanekārthavidhirupapadyate nāsyeti naiṣa viśeṣo yatra kakriyā viśeṣagāmanekamupādauyate tatra tahāreṇa tahidhiḥ mulabha iti viśi ṣṭavidhānanyāyo yattra punaḥ khaviśeṣaṇā viśiṣṭā kriyā vi dhauyate vākyāntaraprātasya kriyāntarasya viśeṣagāṃ tatrāvaśyāvarttanīyo vidhipratyayo devatādiviśiṣṭo hi yāgo vidhīyamānaḥ svaviśeṣaṇa mevākṣeptuṃ samartho nāvidhīyamānaparivyāṇaviśeṣaṇam /
tenāpūrvakarmavidhiṣvapyetaddivektavyama/
katarattadviśeṣaṇaṃ kataradanyaviśeṣaṇamiti /
tammādayamubhayapakṣabhātkvānnaikasya codayitavyaḥ /
tatrāvaśyaṃ siddhāntavādinobhayoḥ parivyāṇayoḥ sādhāraṇau raśaneti parihāro vaktavyaḥ /
vakṣyati hi raśanāca liṅgadarśanāditi /
yadyadetasya yūpasya parivyāṇaṃ tasya tasyaiṣā vākyena vijñāyate /
tathā prāptānuvādānna vākyabhedaḥ /
atha vā yattitā yūpaṃ parivauyopākarotīti pūrvadyuḥ prāptamupākaraṇasya parivyāgānantaryya manadyā śvinagrahaṇānantayeṃ vidhīyate /
varaṃ ca vākyabhedādyavahita kalpanāśrayaṇam /
tasmādevaṃ varṇyate avaśyaṃ tāvatsavanauyānā mekenotpattirekena ca guṇo vi ghātavyaḥ /
tatra pūrvestanasya tāvantra kaścidutpattivākyave heturasti /
nanvitarasyāpi nāsti yadyapyevaṃ tathā mi vikalpasamuccayāsaṃbhavātkena cihiśeṣeṇānyatarasminnāthayitavye viśeṣo 'bhidhīyate /
purastādetadeva sthitaṃ yathopādeyo guṇastirohitakamā nuvādena śakyo vidhātuṃ nānupādeyaḥ sa hi kuṇḍapāyināmayane homasyeva balātkarmāntaratvamāpādayati /
tadiha vapāpracāra upādeya mutyākāla sthasavanauyānuvādena śakyo vidhātuṃ kiṃ punaḥ prātaḥsavanaśrutyā taddeśasavanauyapratyabhijñāne sati śvastane punarāmrāne nirjñātaprayojana tvādāśivanagrahagona sahāṅgāsiṃbandhābhāvātkālāyeṃ saṃyoge tasyānupādeyatvātkamaheśena vidhyanupapatteravaśyaṃ kāloheśena karma vidheyam /
athāpyāśvinaṃ pratyaṅgatvena vidhistathā 'pyaṅgino 'nupādeyatvādeṣaiva vacanavyaktirataśca guṇa vidhyanupapateravaśyaṃ prakaraṇāntaranyāyenotpattividheranyenāntareṇāpratibandhādutpattābavadhāyamāṇāyāṃ karmāntara myāt /
'tenāsya tāvatkālāpekṣayotpādakatvaṃ siddham /
ataścetarasya pariśeṣasiddhaṃ guṇavidhitvaṃ na hi tasya kiṃ ciddhedakāraṇam /
ata eva vapāpracāraṇotkarṣo 'sti nāstīti vicāritam /
sati hi vapāpracāragotkarṣe pūrvasyaiva prātaḥsavane viparihatteḥ kālaṃ pratyupādānaṃ pratyabhijñānātkalpyeta /
yathota sannidhau tvavibhāgāditi /
kāle ca karmaṇi vidhīyamāne pratyayasya sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe vyāpāro bhaviṣyati vapāpracārakālasya punaḥ savanauyotpattikriyātaḥ kriyāntara viśeṣaṇatvādduṣpratipādo viśiṣṭavidhiriti vākyabhedaḥ syāt /
asmatpace punarvyathai kavākyatvaṃ bhavati tathoktam /
evaṃ ca parivyāṇasyāpi prakaraṇalabhyo 'ṅgabhāva ihānuvadiṣyate anyathā punarviprakṛṣṭatare gaṇa krameṇa prāptimapecyā nadyeta tammādayamevotpattivi dhiḥ /
kathaṃ punarasminpace bhāṣyakārasya vākyabhedopanyāsaḥ /
ucyate /
karmaṇo bheda evāyaṃ vākyabhedo 'bhidhīyate /
saṃbandhe tvekavākyatvamarthānyatve 'pi gamyate 
somanāśe hi pratinidhyapekṣāyāṃ satyāṃ putīkā vi dhoyante na yāgasādhanāpekṣāyām /
ato 'yaṃ pratinidhiniyama eva bhavati yatsakalasomadharmāsaṃbhave vikalānsaṃ madharmānutpādayettatpūtokagatāniti /
vacyati hi niyamārtha kvaciddidhiḥ /
tannityaṃ taccikorṣā hoti ca /
ataśca naivātra pūtīkalaṃ kama kiṃ tarhi somadharmopalakṣaṇārtha tena śrutilacaṇasthāpi pūrveṇāviśiṣṭatvamiti /
tenehāpi tadeva cintāyāḥ prayojanam /
ata tadāśrayasya tahuḍayanapāyādguṇakāmai pravarttitavyam /
anye vāhuḥ sakalavyaktyāśrayaṇo hi guṇakāmā vaikalyādiha na pravarttante /
nityasya hi karmaṇo'vaśyaṃ prakramātmakāntasya sarvasyāvaśya samāpanīyatvā tkiṃciḍa me vaikalye 'pyavaiguṇyābhyanujñā yujyate yathā tu kāmyānāṃ pratini dhibhiḥ prakramo nāsti tathā guṇakāmaina pravarttitavyam /
yadi tu prakrānte kasmiṃścidgaṇakāmakalpe dravyanāśe sati tantravārtike /
pratinidhīyate tatastasyāvaśya samāpanīyattvāhikāreṇa pratinidhinā vā tulyaṃ samāpana mityūhānuhāveva prayojanam saṃsthāstu samānavidhānāḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt 
aneka graha camasayāgābhyāsātmakaścatuḥsaṃstho jyotiṣṭomo 'vadhāritaḥ sarvasaṃsthāsu tu jyotiṣṭomarūpamanusyūtam /
yathaiva devadattasya sthānopaveśanagamanaśayanādyavasthābhede 'pi devadattatvaṃ nāpaiti tathā jyotiṣṭomātmanaḥ saṃsthāntaropajanāpāye tattvaṃ nāpaiti /
saṃsthānāṃ ca virodhādanyonyaṃ samāveśo nāsti jyotiṣṭomarūpaṃ tu sarvatrāvirudamanuvarttate /
sa ca jyotiṣṭomaḥ phalāya coditaḥ jyotiṣṭomena svargākāmo yajeteti /
tathokthyādisaṃsthānāmapi paśukāma ukthyaṃ gṛhṇīyādityādi phale vidhānam /
tamevaṃvidhaṃ jyotiṣṭomaṃ prakṛtya dokṣagoyādayo dharmāḥ samānātāste saṃdihyante kiṃ sarvasaṃsthajyotiṣṭomohe śenāmnātā uta kevalāgniṣṭomasaṃsthoheśeneti /
na tvayamupanyāso yuktaḥ na hi dharmasaṃbandhavelāyāmuddiśyamānasya jyotiṣṭomasya kā citsaṃsthā vi śeṣaṇatvena śrūyate /
yadyapi kathaṃ cicchūyaṃta tathā 'pyuddiśyamāna viśeṣaṇatvānna vivayeta na cokthyādigrahaṇāṃśena jyotiṣṭomasya grāhakatvaṃ phalasādhanabhāvāddhi tavokthyādaya evetikarttavyatāvanto bhavanti jyotiṣṭomastabāśrayatvenopasarjanabhāvāntra dharmagrahaṇayogyo vijñāyate /
jyotiṣṭomena svargakāma iti caitaḍākyagatasya  vibhāgāditi ka pu pā /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
jyotiṣṭomasya dharmasaṃbandhaḥ sarvasaṃsthāsvaviśiṣṭa ityagniṣṭomasaṃsthamevetyayuktam ata evaṃ vaktavyam /
kiṃ jyotiṣṭomasyaivaitaḍammammānamutokthyādīnāmapi saṃsthānāmiti/
tacca evaṃ samarthanīyametadeva granthenoktamiti /
ya dyapi saṃsthābhiīrmā gṛhyante tathā 'pi tāsāṃ svayamakriyātmakatvāt jyotiṣṭoma evāśrayatvād hārambhavatīti kiṃ sarvasaṃsthaṃ prakṛtyetyāha /
kiṃ dvārabhūtaṃ phalavantaṃ ca prakṛtyota phalavanta mevetyartha /
yadā ca kevalajyotiṣṭomārthatvaṃ tadā tahasādhāraṇatvātpariśeṣāhā 'gniṣṭomasaṃsthasyaiva jāyataiti tatsaṃsthasya vyapadeśa /
ukthyādiṣu hi yadyapi jyotiṣṭomasyāpi grāhakatvamasti tathā 'pi tanna vyajyate kimukthyādigṛhītā dharmā etasya dvāratvāddhavantyutātmīyaphala sādhanatvāditi agniṣṭomasaṃsthā cāsya nijamaṅgamatastatsaṃstho gṛhṇantrayaṃ gṛhṇātīti śakyate vatam /
tasmātsamyagupanyastaṃ dharmasādhāraṇyaṃ copadeśātideśābhyāṃ pakṣahaye 'pyabhyupagamyataeveti vidhānagrahaṇam /
kiṃ prāptaṃ jyotiṣṭomena saha samānaṃ saṃsthānāṃ dharmavidhānam /
kutaḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt jyotiṣṭomo hi phalavatvādupajātakathaṃbhāvastadanuvṛttisannidhau samāmnātān gha man gṛhṇāti na jyotiṣṭomatvena taccokthyā donāmeteṣveva dharmeṣu sarvamaviśiṣṭamupadeśāsaṃbhave cātideśo bhavati tasmādupadeśa eva sādhāraṇa iti /
vyapadeśaśca tulyavat 
jyaśeṣasya pratipattiṃ vidadhattu lyavatsaṃsthā kratuprakaraṇa saṃbandhitvena korttayati /
yadyāgniṣṭomo juhoti tantravārtike /
yadā॒kthyastenaiva śeṣeṇa paridhimanakti yadyatiśavaḥ etadeva homayajuṭīmagne pṛtsa martyamiti japan havinaṃ pratipadyeteti ato vijñāyate sarvo 'ṅgavidhiḥ sādhāraṇa iti /
sāmānyato dṛṣṭamivāyuktamuktaṃ yadi hi vākyavaśena kiṃ citprakaraṇānātaṃ saṃsthābhiḥ saṃbadhyate tataḥ kimasaṃyukta saṃbandhenāpi yukta bhavitum /
na hi hādaśāhīnasyetyādiṣu śeṣadhama/
ṇāmapya honārthatvamā śaṅgitam /
yāvaddacanaṃ cayitvāddacanānāmityevaṃ vyācaṣṭe yadi hi sāmānya vihitamagniṣṭomasaṃsthasyaiva syāhinā 'pi ta dupādānena tadaṅgatvasiḍennavāgniṣṭomaṃ saṃkīrtta yedyatastu saṃkīrttayati ato manyāmahe nūnamaviśeṣitamagniṣṭomasya na labhyate /
taccaivaṃ na labhyate yadi saṃsthānāmapi sādhāraṇaṃ prakaraṇam /
kevalajyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇapakṣe tu punaḥśrutiranadhikā syāt /
tathokthyādīnāmapi yadi prakaraṇamasti tato 'nyataraniraṇārthaṃ yadiśabdopabacaṃ grahaṇaṃ yuktamaprakṛtatve tu hādaśāhīnasyetivaddinaiva yadiśabdena saṃbandhaḥ syāt /
na hi jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe sthitasyaivaṃ vādo yujyate /
yadi jyotiṣṭhomastata etayadi hādaśāhastato 'mukamiti /
aneka sannihitāpekṣaṃ hya tadvacanaṃ bhavatyato 'pi samānaṃ prakaraṇam /
idamaparaṃ liṅgam /
āgneyamajamagniṣṭoma ālabhetendrāgna mukyye hi toya maindraṃ dṛṣṇiṃ ṣoḍaśini tṛtīyamiti /
samānavidhā natve pūrvapūrvo hyuttarottaratva pratyakṣaśrutatvāt kriyataiti dvitīya tṛtīya darśanamupapadyate /
vikārapakṣe tu pratyakṣaśrutairaindrāgnādibhirāgneye bādhite sarvacaika eva syāt /
nanu ca pratyakṣa śrutatve'pi saṃsthāntare saṃsthāntarāsaṃbhavātṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
nirnimittaḥ pūrva pūrvo na prāpnoti /
yo hyagniṣṭomastotre samāpyate so'gniṣṭomo na taddanmātraṃ yaścokthyādiṣu samāpyate nāsau pūrvatra samāpto bhavati /
tena dvitīyadarśanādāpramaṅgaḥ pakṣahaye 'pi tulyaḥ /
satyaṃ saṃsthāni mittatve tulyaḥ stotranimittatve tu samuccayaḥ /
tathā ca bhāṣyakāra āha dve hi tatra nimitta agniṣṭomastovamukthyastotraṃ ceti siḍavadetadvavauti /
kathaṃ puna saṃsthāslovasādhāraṇāgniṣṭomādimamabhihāre tulye stotranimittatvamevāṅgīkriyate na saṃsthānimittatvam /
tāsāṃ hi phalavavena prayojanavatvādakleśenaiva nimittattvamāpadyate /
tatra ke cidāhuḥ /
satyapi śabdasādhāraṇye śāsvasya mahāviṣayatvānugrahārthaṃ stotranimittatvāśrayaṇamityathavā stotraviśeṣitāyā eva saṃsthāyā evaṃśabdakatvātpūrvatarapratītaviśeṣānimittatvasaṃbhave javanyavi śeṣyanimittatvakalpanā na yuktā /
yahā '' kṛtyadhikaragānyāyenaitra stotreṣu mukhyaḥ śabdaḥ saṃsthāyāṃ lākṣaṇikaḥ /
śrutyasaṃbhave ca lakṣaṇā āthayitavyā /
śaknoti ca stotramapi saptamaunirdeśānnimittatvaṃ pratipattum /
niṣphalānāmapi ca bhedanādaunāṃ vacana sāmarthyānnimittatvamiṣṭam /
atha vā saṃdigdheṣu vākyaśeṣādityevaṃ stotrāśrayaṇam /
sa tyapi vā saṃsthānāṃ mukhyatve vyavadhāraṇakalpanayā vākyaśeṣeṇa stotraparigrahaḥ /
evaṃ hi śrūyate /
āgneyamajamagniṣṭomaālabheta śrāgneyo hyagniṣṭāma iti /
katarasminnagniṣṭomeya āgneyaḥ stotrasya ca stutibhāgagnidevatā vidyate na saṃsthāyāḥ /
sā hi vyāpāraparityāgā tmakatvodabhāvabhūtā na cābhāvasya devatayā kāryyamasti /
Botantravārtika /
yāgābhyāse 'pi hi yā devatā sā tasyaivāgneyatvaṃ karoti na saṃsthāyāḥ /
na ca sa eva saṃsthā /
taduttarakālaudāsaunyavacanatvātsaṃpūrvasya tiṣṭhateḥ /
na cānyagatayā devatayā 'nyasya vyapadaśo bhavati /
tathokthyaṣoḍaśinorapi darśayitavyam /
api caindrāgnāni ukthyānīti sphuṭameva stotragrahaṇam /
na hi saṃsthokthyānī tyanena śabdenocyate /
tasmātsati stotranimittatve yuktaḥ samuccaya iti /
nanu vikārapakṣe 'pyadṛṣṭārthatvātpaśuyāgānāmanyonya kāryyāpattyasaṃbhavādupapadyataeva samuccayastathā hi /
nānumānikamātraṃ yattatpratyakṣeṇa bādhyate /
virodhe sati bādho hi virodhaścaikagocaraḥ 
sarve hi paśavaḥ sarvatra prāpnuvanto yatpūrvasaṃsthāsu pare na bhavanti tannimittābhāvātpratyakṣeṇa tu nimittena pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ paratra vākyātprāpnoti /
tatra kiṃ samākhyayaikakāyaṃtvaṃ kalpayitvā bādhavikalpayoranyatara śrāśrīyatāmuta vākyaprāptasamuccayānurodhena kāryyānyatvaṃ kalyatāmiti vākyabalīyastvātmamuccayena bhavitavyam /
yathā prayājānuyājādaunāṃ satyapi samākhyaikatve vākyasāmayatkāyyonyatvaṃ samuccayaśca /
atideśe punaḥ samākhyayā kāvya~katvam atideśena kāryyānyatvaṃ tenāpi samutantravārtike /
nacayaḥ /
tasmāñcopadeśāntargatā samākhyaiva baloyasīti tatkṛtaṃ kāyaikatvamāśritya virodhāddāghaḥ parigṛhyeta /
vikāre ca prakṛtiliṅgasaṃyogāpekṣā vidyataiti kāvyāpattirvijñāyate /
na tu samānavidhipakṣe prakṛtiliṅgasaṃyogaḥ kaścidona kāryyāpattiravadhārthyeta /
ke cittvāḍaḥ /
samānavidhitve parasparānapekṣairdravyadevatāsaṃyogaiḥ kamabhedo 'vasīyate vikāre punaratideśaprāptayāgānuvādena guṇamātraṃ vidhīyate tataścaika eva yāga syāt na dvitīyāṭya iti /
sa tvayaṃ guṇavidhiraindrāgne saṃbhavennendra sarasvatyora ne kadravyadevatāvidhānena vākyabhedapramagādekāntena karmāntaratā /
tenaivaṃ samarthanīyaṃ kamantaramevadaṃ vidhīyamānaṃ kimapūrvāntarasāvanatvaṃ pratipadyatāmuta prākṛtasavanīyāpūrvameva sādhayatviti pūrvaklaptāpūrvaviniyogamātre saṃbhavati nāpūrvāntara kalpayitvā tatsādhanatvādhyavasānaṃ yuktam /
tathā 'tideśaprāptasavanīyāpūrvamapi sādhanāpekṣāvelāyāṃ pratyakṣa śrutasavanīyaparityāgena na savanīyāntaraṃ gṛhṇāti sarvāpekṣāsu prakṛtāsaṃbhavanāma kṛtagrahaṇādyāgagato 'pi vyāpāra prākṛtenaivāpūrveṇa klṛptasaṃbandho na śaknotyapūrvāntarasaṃvandhaṃ pratipattum /
kathamakla ptasāmarthyaṃ savanauyāntara prākṛtamapūrvaṃ sādhayatoti cet yathetarasminpakṣa 'pūrvāntaraṃ yāgagataṃ vyāpāramityadoṣaḥ /
kastā nayorviśeṣaḥ /
uccate /
yadā yāgagatavyāpāragā/
pūrvāṇya pecyante na tadā vaikṛtasavanīyāpūrvaṃ klṛpta yattanminnaṃśa nipatadyadā punarapūrveṇa karmāpaṃcyate tadā savanīyatvaprakṛtiliṅgasaṃyuktaṃ karmāntaraṃ vidyamānamavabuddhya prākṛtaṃ nirākaroti /
prakṛtī d cāpūrvakalpanāva marāhighīya mānasavanīya catuṣṭayātuniṣṇāṭyapūrvacatuṣṭayaṃ kalpyate /
na hi tatva jñāyate kataratyūvataravalṛptaṃ yamya sādhanāntarasaṃbandhaḥ syāt /
kamrmālocanavelāyāṃ hi karmmarūpāṇyeva dṛśyante apūrvakalpanā 'pi yugapaivatīti na jñāyate viśeṣaḥ /
