vikārapakṣe tu jñāyate prākṛtasya pūrvataraṃ valṛptirityavaśyāvaheye'nyataramikammaṇi viprakṛṣṭaṃ prākṛtaṃ hātavyaṃ bhavatīti bādhaprasaṅgaḥ /
nanu ca vikārapakṣe 'gniṣṭomasaṃsthāyā eva vikārabhūtāḥ parāḥ saṃsthā bhavanti na paraspareoti kevalasyāgneyasya prāptasya parairvādhātsarvava dvitīyastha darśanaṃ na syādityetāvanmātraṃ vaktavyaṃ kimucyate tṛtīyasya darśanaṃ na prāpnotīti /
naiṣa doṣo yadi tvayamaindrāgnādaunāṃ paratva prāptānāṃ bādhādadarśanaṃ brūyācano niṣpramāṇakaṃ va dedayaṃ tvadarśanamātraṃ vadati/
taccāgneyasya bādhānmadhyamayoścāprāpterupapannameva tenaiva cāgneyo bādhyetetyāha na pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ pareṇeti /
tasmātsamāgavidhānāḥ /
vikārāstu kāmasaṃyoge nityasya samatvāt 
ukthaprādayaḥ samāptiviśeṣāḥ phalamāghanatvena codyamānāḥ samāptimantamāśrayamapekṣamāṇāḥ prakṛtaṃ japrotiṣṭomaṃ samāśrayantastasya nijāmagniṣṭomasaṃsthāṃ vikatya niviśantaiti vikāraśabdenīcyante /
nanu cokyaprādaunāṃ samāptitve siddhe samāptimadapekṣā bhavati /
na caiṣāṃ prāk jayotiṣṭomasaṃbandhātsamāptitvatantravārtike /
siddhirārambhamadhyāpekṣattvātsamāpti śabda pravṛttaḥ /
atha prathamaṃ tatsaṃbandhastataḥ prathamaṃ kratvaryatve 'vadhārite phalasaṃbanvābhāvātsa nityasya samatvādityevamavikāratvaprasagaḥ /
kiñca /
grahaṇādau ca vispaṣṭe codyamāle phalaṃ prati /
saṃsthānāṃ phalasaṃbandhaḥ kathamadhyavasoyate 
nanu cokthyaṃ gṛhṇīyāditi sāmānādhikaragya prayogānāmapi grahaṇādīmāmeva syāt /
naitadevam /
ukthyastovasaṃbandhādi samāptirevokthyaśabdenocyate tatsaṃbandhādgahaupacaryate /
na ca mukhyasaṃbhave gauṇaḥ parigṛhyate nityaṃ tu yajñasāmānādhikaraṇyenokthyādīnāṃ prayogo dṛśyate /
ukdhyena yajetokthyo yatta iti /
tathā ṣoḍaśinā yajate ṣoḍaśī yajñaḥ /
na vai ṣoḍaśī nāma yajño'stauti sa cāntyantāvyatiriktasamāptivacanatve 'vakalpate na grahastovavacanave /
ṣoḍaśauti ca pulliṅgaḥ samāptivacana etṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
ghopapadyate /
napuṃsakaliṅgasya stovavacanatvāt /" yastu puṃlliṅgaprayogaḥ stotre va ciddaśyate, yathaikaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśauti, sa gauṇa iti pratipattavyam /
iha vākyaśeṣe puṃlliṅgaḥ ṣoḍaśau pratoyate iti saṃsthāvacanaḥ /
atirājeśa prajākāmama iti vispaṣṭameva saṃsthāvacanatvaṃ na hi tava kriyāntaramupāttaṃ yajirapi ca ṇyarthopasarjanatvena śruta kleśena pradhānīkarttavyaḥ /
tasmādrāvimatautya yā samāptiḥ sā phalena saṃbadhyate /
yadi ca grahāstovayoḥ phalasaṃbandhaḥ syāttatastayoḥ kriyātvādāśrayāpekṣā nāstīti svatantrayoreva prayogaḥ prāpnoti tava ca prakaraṇāmnāna prayojanamukthyādiśabdaprayogaśca na jñāyeta /
tasmādapi samāptayaḥ phalavatyaḥ /
kathaṃ tu prāka ṛtusaṃbandhātsamāptitvamiti ke cittāvadāhuḥ /
sapta somasaṃsthā agniṣṭhomo 'tyagniṣṭoma ukthya ṣoḍaśyatirāvo vājapeyo 'ptoyama iti smaraṇātso pramāvasamāptivacanatve siddhe kamāntarāṇyanādṛtya somayāgamātre 'pekṣite prakaraṇāt jotiṣṭomasyāśrayatvasiddhiriti /
anye tu manyante protiṣṭomasya va cidamyāsaviśeṣe samātyantaraṃ vijñāyate yadutpadyamāna me vokthyādivyapadeśaṃ labhate phalasaṃbandhaṃ ca tatra śrutibalīyastvātmakaragālabhyaṃ kratvarthatvaṃ bādhyate /
yastvāśrayāśrayi saṃbandhaḥ so'nuguṇatvādāśrīyate /
aparaṃ darśanam ukthyādiśabdavācyaṃ kimapi prathamameva phalena saṃbadyate kiṃ punasta divyapekṣāyāṃ vacanāntareṇa jagrotiṣṭomasya samāpyantara vijñāyate /
yahā gyāsaviśeṣa evāyaṃ vacanāntarāt jayotiṣṭomasyānte niviśamāna pha lāya codyate tena vā tasminvā kratuḥ saṃtiṣṭhataiti saṃsthāśabdenābhidhīyate /
ke citpanarmanyante /
saṃsthā nāmāntyayāgāmyāsānantaraṃ yā kriyoparatiḥ mā 'bhidhīyate na cākriyātmakatvāttasyāḥ phalamāghanatvaṃ yuktamatastadupalacito 'bhyāmaśrodyataiti /
anye tvāhuḥ /
vacanasyātibhārābhāvādabhāvo 'pi codyamānaḥ phalamādhatvena naiva virudhyataiti /
yathā 'kurvanvihitaṃ karmetyavākaraṇasyāsataḥ pratyavāyahetutvam /
atha vā 'styevācaudāsaunyapratipattirūpaḥ saṃkalpa ityavirodhaḥ /
iha ca yathā guṇātphalaṃ bhavati yathā ca kāmyo guṇo nityamarthaṃ vikaroti tadindriyakāmādhikaraṇagodohanādhikaraṇābhyāmupasaṃharttavyam /
taddarśayati /
guṇādevaṃjātīya ke phalāniṣpattiḥ /
evaṃ hi śrūyate /
paśukāma ukthyaṃ gṛhṇīyānna jotiṣṭomakāma ukthāgṛhaṇakāmo vetyanena kratvarthatvaṃ nirākaroti/
kratvarthatve hi satyantareṇāpi kāmapadopabandhaṃ tadupakārakamevaitatkarttavyamiti vijñāyate /
yadi cokthāgṛhaṇasvarūpamātraṃ cikīrṣyata tato 'rthādukthāgṛhaṇakāmasyaiṣa vidhirbhavedāsyaivaṃ prārthanamukthāgṛhāstra rūpamā kathaṃ nirvarttatāmiti tatta, iyamapi paśukāmopādānādanavaklṛptam /
ataḥ kāmyatvādasti godohanavyāyena vikāratvaṃ tatra kathamiti itikarttavyatākāṅkṣāyāṃ jotiṣṭomagṛhautetikarttavyatā'tidiśyate /
kaḥ punariha pra kāro yanetikartavyatā gṛhyate yadi tāvatsannidhānaṃ tataḥ samānavidhāna meṃ bābhyupagataṃ bhavati na hyatideśasya sannidhi kāraṇaṃ sāhṛpyaprabhavatvena vakṣyamāṇatvāt /
atha kāyipacyā tatrāpi kāraṇāntaratvaṃ nirākṛtam /
na ca dokṣaṇīyādayaḥ saṃsthādharmmāḥ yataḥ kāyāpanne saṃsthāntare bhaveyuḥ na jotiṣṭomasyokthyādayaḥ kārye varttate yatastammanpratipadyante /
etenātideśapacaḥ pratyuktaḥ /
yo hi manyate 'tideśena dharmā bhaviṣyantīti tasyāpyatideśakāraṇaṃ sārūpyaṃ nāstīti yadyadhyagniṣṭomasya saṃ sthayā sāmānyamasti jeprātiṣṭomasya tu na kiṃ cidukyādisāpyamityaprakṛtitvam /
ata eva ca bhāṣyakārī api sannidhānādityetāvanmālamutkā tṛṣṇabhūtastena vattāvyametaducyate /
atideśo 'yamityetatpurastādeva sādhitam /
na ca sārupyamevaikamatideśasya kāraṇam 
yadi yuktyā vinaiveyaṃ nityasyetyabhidhīyate /
kāmyasyaiveti kiṃ naitadayuktataramucyate 
yadi vinaiva pramāṇena kevalanityārthatvaṃ tvamicchasi hanta madicchayā 'pi kevalakāmyārthatvamevāstu /
atha punaridamapramāṇakamiti nāśrīyate tataḥ pramāṇavatsādhāraṇya miṣyatāmiti /
tatrātiśayoktimasahamāno bhāṣyakāra sādhāraṇapakṣe copakariṣyatīti niṣpramāṇakamapi kevalakāmyapakṣameva tāvannyāyena nirākaroti /
yatra yatra guṇe kāmastatra tatra kriyāyāṃ sādhyamānāyāṃ nānyatheti /
yadi nāma guṇaḥ svātantryeṇeti karttavyatāṃ gṛhītuṃ śaknuyāt tata evaṃ syāt /
sa ca kathaṃ śaknu yādyadi karagauravetikarttavyataḥ saṃbadhyeta yadi ca guṇānāṃ svata eva bhāvanāviśeṣaṇatvaṃ bhavet /
na tāvatkaragauritikarttavyatā saṃbadhyataityuktam /
saptamanavamādyayośca vakṣyati bhāvayetkathamityapekṣya bhavati na karaṇe na kathamiti /
yasyāṃ tu bhāvanāyāṃ dhātvarthāḥ karaṇaṃ bha vanti tasyāṃ te vastvantaranirapecāḥ paścāttanamaruṇaikahāyanonyāyalabhyamitikarttavyatāsaṃbandhaṃ labhante /
yasyāṃ punarguṇānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ tasyāṃ dhātvarthaviśeṣādinā karagatvānupapattaḥ sādhyabhṛto dhātvartho uparo 'pekṣitavyo nahi vyāpāramāmānya ya guṇairutpattiḥ śakyā na ca kriyāviśeṣamasādhayan guṇaḥ sāmānyasādhanatvaṃ bhajate tana yasthāṃ bhāvanāyāmavasthito gugā itikarttavyatāṃ gṛhṇāti tasyāṃ prathamatarasaṃntriviṣṭo dhātvartho dṛśyate /
tattaśca tena tāvatsaha prathamataramarugaṇe kahā yanauvanniyamaḥ /
yadi hautikarttavyatāgṛhaṇayogyaḥ sa na bhavettato na gahṇīyātsa tu phalavattvāditikarttavyatādvārabhūtabhāvanāviśeṣakhatvācca na kathaṃ cinna gṛhṇāti tatra catuṣṭayamapyatra prathamataraṃ grahaṇaṃ prayute bhāvanā tāvanna dhātvarthaviśeṣādinaitikarttavyatāṃ śaknoti grahotuṃ guṇo'pi ca na dhātvarthamanupanīya svatantraḥ śaknoti tannirapekṣabhāvanārahitatvānnirviśeṣasya ca karotyarthamāvasyānanuṣṭheyatva davyāpāratvācca grahotumityāśrayati /
tathotikarttavyatā guṇābhimukhaṃ gacchantau na dhātvaryamullaṅghya śaknoti gantumiti ta nmukhe tāvatpatati / dhātvartho'pi svayamitikarttavyatākāsaḥ san guṇārthamapi prasthitāmetāṃ grahaṇasamarthaḥ sankimiti parityajet /
ato 'va phalāya coditānāsukthyādīnāṃ jayotiṣṭomāśrayatvenāvagatānāmitikarttavyatāmākāṅkṣatāṃ prakaṇena dokṣaṇīyādaya upanauyamānā mārgāntarābhāvādavaśyaṃ tāvat jayotiṣṭomamukhe patanti /
na hukthyādayaḥ samāptirūpāḥ tatparihāreṇa grahautuṃ sa marthāḥ khamukhapatitāṃśca na kathaṃ cit jotiṣṭomastānupekṣate taddarśayati nāmau sādhyasyābhavanto sādhanena saṃbadhyate /
sa hautikarttavyatāviśeṣa evaṃ codyate yathā 'nena phalasya sādhanamukthyādisādhakaṃ tathā kuryyāditi yathā sau sādhako bhavati tathā kuryādityarthaḥ /
tataśca karotisaṃsparśādbhāvanayaiva saṃbandhaḥ /
evaṃ ca sati nāsti sa pra kāro yena dhātvarthaṃ pariṝtyānayetikarttavyatayokthyādayaḥ sādhakāḥ kriyeran /
kriyāyāmasādhyamānāyāmananuṭahyamāṇāyāmityarthaḥ /
ye tu tenāsādhyamānāyāmityukthyādineti saṃvandhayanti teṣāṃ pūrvaprastuteti karttavyatāviśeṣaparityāgādasaṃbaḍatvaṃ tatva tava kriyāyāṃ sādhyamānāyāmityanena ca punarutatvaṃ syāttena sādhakasyāpi guṇatantradhārtike sthetikattavyatāmicchatā sādhyasyāsau dhātvayaṃ syetyetadabhyupagantavyam /
evaṃ sāmānyalakṣāmuktā saṃprati prastute viśeṣe yojayati sādhyaśca jotiṣṭāma iti /
ta smānna tāvatkevalakāmyārthatvam /
atha kasmānna sādhāragātvamiti balavatvena dvitīyapacopanyāsaḥ /
siddhāntavādyāha /
nityavadāmnānāditi /
sarvatra hokarudhye sati tantrasaṃbandho ghaṭate na ca dhammanprati jayotiṣṭomasya saṃsthānāṃ ca aikarupyamasti /
dharmā hi kārmānimittasaṃyogābhāvānnityavadāmrāyante yadaiva jayotiṣṭomastadaiva dokṣaṇīyādayaḥ prayoktavyā iti satyapi ca protiṣṭome vinā paśukāmādinokthyādayo na saṃbhavanti saṃsthāntaraprayoge cāvaśyameva saṃsthāntara na saṃbhavati /
na tvetāsu jyotiṣṭomaḥ kadā cinnāsti /
sarvatra samastātmanā pratyekaṃ jātivatmamavetattvāt /
ata ete yathāmnātā protiṣṭomena saha saṃbadhyante nānityābhiḥ saṃsthābhiḥ /
nanu satyapyāsāmanityatve jyotiṣṭomasyaikasya nityatvānnityavadarbhānānaṃ nityārthatvena virotsyate nityāmānaṃ tāvataṃ prati kṛtārtha bhaviṣyati /
yadi tu tamanmatyevānityo 'pyaparaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kalpyate kiṃ no bādhyate /
yo nityārthameva nityavadāmāyate sa virudhyate naivaṃjātīyaka iti /
naitadevamevaṃ sati tanvaṃ tāvatparityaktamaprayojakalacaṇāpannatvādyadā hi nityavadānānaṃ nityārthatvena tāvaddinā na bhavati kapte ca tādaye nirākāṅkṣībhūte pāṭhe prasaṅkāditarasaṃbandha iti na sāmānaviṣyam /
itarathā hyevaṃ dharmavi dhi syānnityametān jayotiṣṭome dhamānkuryyātkadā cicca yadā paśukāmādayo bhavantauti tacca vipratiṣiimekasya vidhānasya /
nanu hāvetau prakaraṇāmānānumitau vidho tayo reko nityabaddidhāsyati aparaścānityavaditi /
satyaṃ prayogavacanayorbhedādavipratiṣedhaḥ prayojāvacanāni tu nityānityaprayogavacanānuvidhānādipratiṣidhyante /
tenaiṣāṃ nityatvāvighātamicchatā 'vaśyaṃ grāhakamapi tamayamevābhyupagantavyam /
ataścāvyabhicārāt jyotiṣṭomārthatvameva yuktamiti /
nanvagniṣṭomasaṃsthāpi kāmyeti yadā sarvasaṃsthānāmanityatvaṃ na ca tadyatiriktaṃ nityaṃ kiṃ cit jyoṣṭomarūpamasti tadā jayotiṣṭamena nityavadhaṇāttahārabhūtena tulyakalpameva sarvāsāṃ dharmopanayanamiti kva nityaḥ prayoga ityanavadhāraṇāt kevalānityārthatvaṃ balāīkalpikanyāyena bhaviṣyatītyataāha sa nityasya samatvāditi /
samau hi kratvarthapuruṣārtho vidhau tau hi hāvāloccaikasya tūbhayatve saṃyogapṛthakvamityevamagniṭomāntasya nityasyaiva kāmasaṃyoga iti itarasya tu kevalakāmasaṃyogādanityattvamiti viśeṣaḥ /
tena yadyapi prayogeṇeyamanityā tathā 'pi jayotiṣṭomasya nityattvā detasyāśca taṃ prati prāptirūpeṇa nityatvāttadgṛhautadharmaparabhāgalābhācāgniṣṭomasyetyevaṃ dharmāṇāṃ vyapadeśo 'tha vokthyādiṣvapi prāptiiye sati protiṣṭomāṃśena yā prāpti sopadeśena yokdhyāṃśena sā 'tideśātmiketi vivekaḥ /
vacanācca samuccayaḥ 
viśiṣṭavidhānasya nātibhāraḥ /
 tadāsyā'pīti kha pu pā /
tantravārtika /
pratiṣedhācca pūrvaliṅgānām 
kratukaraṇeṣu cottara vidhau yatpūrvābhāvamanuvadati sa vikārapakṣe vikalpate /
codakaprāptasya cottareṇa pūrvasya bādhitatvāt /
sāmānavidhye hi pratyakṣa nimittasavidhānātprāpte nimitta naimittikamavaśyaṃ karttavyamiti samuccaya syāttava pratiṣedhaḥ pṛthagvidharupagamyamāno vākyaṃ bhindyāt /
na hyava dvitīyatṛtīyā divaddiśiṣṭa vidhiravakalpate /
vidhipratiṣedhayorvipratiṣedhāt paryudāsāsaṃbhavācca /
sarvaceha savanīyapaśuviṣaya pūrvapakṣavādyakto vyāyaḥ siddhāntasenānusaṃdhātavyaḥ saṃsthānimittatve hi sāmānavidhye 'pi nimittābhāvādabhāvadarśanamupapadyetaiva /
siddhānte 'pi cādṛṣṭārthatvātsamuccayaprasaṅge sati kratukaraṇasamākhyā prakṛtiliṅgamiti yojyam /
ke citpunarāhuḥ /
pracaraṇohomaśeṣapratipattivaddomasya paridhyanena pratipādite sāmānavidhye 'dhyabhāvaḥ sidhyatīti tatra tu vākyena svatantre vidhīyamāne kathamaprastutaṃ pratipattitvamavagamyataiti vaktavyam /
satyapi ca homena pratipādane yāvatā paridhyañjanaśabdārtho nirvarttate kiṃcicca śrutyocyate tābatpunaḥ sambhavatyeva tasmādyathoktena nyāyena darśanamevedamabhāvasaṃkīrttanam /
guṇaviśeṣādekasya vyapadeśaḥ 
yatvaprakṛtasya yadiśabdopabandho hādaśāhādivantrāvakalpataiti /
nokthyādīnāmanyairaprakṛtaistulyatā /
yadyapi hyeṣāṃ nityānityasaṃyogavirodhātmatṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pāda /
karaṇamagrāhakamitikatrttavyatāyāstathā 'pi sannihi tatvādyadiśabdavyapadeśaṃ labhante /
prastutaguṇihāreṇa vā prastutānāmapi guṇānāṃ prastutavyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati /
prakaraṇaprāptaṃ tvagniṣṭomagrahaṇaṃ nityānuvādaḥ /
atha vā stovanimittatvapratipādanaparatvādarthavadevetyadoṣaḥ /
kiṃ bhavati prayojanam /
phalacamasavadeveti ke cit /
idaṃ tu vaktavyaṃ satyametatprayojanaṃ na tu sarvadharmeṣu yāvanto hi sadomānādiṣu guṇakāmāste satyapyatideśe sa evaupadeśika āśrayo 'stauti na vikṛtyantaravadhihanyante /
vikṛtyanta reṣu hi jotiṣṭomasyāśrayasyābhāvād guṇakāmā yathāśrutā na bhavantīti na sidhyanti /
saṃsthāsu tu yadyapyaṅgaphalaṃ nātidiśyate tathā 'pi svayamarthitvātpuruṣasya cikīrṣamāṇasya guṇopādisāyāṃ yathāśrutāśrayasaṃbhave nānupapattirguṇa kāmānām /
ato yanmāla muvathyādi saṃsthā nimitta mukthyagrahaṇastotraśasvādyaprākṛtaṃ tava yaditaragṛhastotraśatradhamā tideśena kiṃ cid guṇakāmagataṃ prāpnoti tantra bhavatīti pra yojanaṃ tatheimaparaṃ yadi samānavidhānaṃ tato vyaktāsu tu somasyetyanena nyāyena ye jayotiṣṭomavikārā vijñāyante teṣu sarvāḥ saṃsthā vikalpena siddhānte tvagniṣṭomasaṃsthaivaikā pravarttate yatva covathayādiviśeṣacodanā tatraiva kevalaṃ taharmmaprāptiriti prayojanaṃ siddham /
iti śraubhaṭṭakumārilaviracitāyāṃ tantraṭīkāyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ /tantravārtike /
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ /
prakaraṇaviśeṣādasaṃyuktaṃ pradhānasya 
samānāsamānavidhānādhikāreṇevaitadapi prastūyate vākyaprakaraṇavirodhāvirodhahāregā /
darśapūrṇa māsaprakaraṇasthā vediḥ taḍarbhāśca khananādayastathā barhistaḍammaśca lavanādayaḥ kimarthā iti /
yadyapi vedyāṃ havīṃṣi barhiṣi havīṃṣi varhirṭzanāti vediṃ khanatīti cāviśeṣitena vākye nāṅgapradhānārthatvabuddhirbhavati tathā 'pi khātantrye sati laukikeṣvapi gṛhācchādanārtheṣu barhiḥṣu dharmaprasa ktātrā nartha kyā davaśyamapūrvasādhanatākāritaḥ saṃbandho 'bhyupagantavyaḥ sā cāpūrvasādhanatā na vākyasāmarthyena pratoyataiti prakaraṇāllabdhavyā /
tataśca pradhānamātrasya ta tprakaragāmityanena viśeṣeṇa pradhānasyaiva dharmā gamyante satyapi ca prakaraṇasyāviśeṣakatve grāhakatvenaiva viśeṣaṇapeṇāviniyojakatvāhiśeṣasthāpana hetutvamityuktam /
asaṃyuktamiti ca satyapi bākyena havirbahisaṃyoge prakaraṇavirodhyarthā'saṃyogābhiprāyam /
śakya hi havirbarhiḥśabdo prakaraṇena samāveśayituṃ nāhīnavadasaṃbaḍāviti manyate /
sarveṣāṃ vā śeṣatvasyātatprayu tatvāt 
sarveṣāṃ vākyasaṃyogāviśeṣādityuktameva /
yattu prakaraṇaṃ viśeṣeṇa viniyojakamiti, tatrāhaatatprayuktatvāt /
na prakaraṇamiha viśeṣakaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ /
kathaṃ punaḥ sthitaṃ prakaraṇasya viniyojakatvaṃ nivartate kathaṃ vā tādaśrīlakṣaṇavyatiriktaṃ ca bahudoṣamupakāralakṣaṇaṃ śeṣatvaṃ pra tijñāyate /
uccate naiva prakaraṇā syaivaṃjātīya keṣu viniyojakatva~ sthitamasaṃyukta prakaraṇāditi hyaktam /
yattu virodho nāstīti kathaṃ nāsti yadā havirbarhiṣāṃ prādhānyātpratyekaṃ dharmasaṃbandhe satyaṅa gārthatvamapi jñāyamānaṃ prakaragānurodhena vyāvarcyate /
parastu yena kāraṇena vākyasyātiprasare bādhite nirvirodhaṃ prakaraṇamavagatavānidānoṃ tadupanyasyati laukike 'pi prāpnoti tataścānarthakyami ti /
tasyottarametadeva vaktavyam /
svarasapravṛtta vākya yāvatyeva vispaṣṭa mānarthakya tāvanmāvādeva nivarttatāṃ na cāṅgavarhiṣāṃ laukikavadānarthakyam atastava bhaviṣyati na cātiprasajātaiti /
anenaiva cābhiprāyegā upakāralakṣaṇaṃ hi taditi tādarthameva phalena vyapadiṣṭaṃ yadayeṃ hi kalpyamānaṃ prayojanavahijñātumā kāṅkṣitopakāraniṣpattyā śakyate tadarthaṃ kalpanīyam /
yatta, bhāṣyakāraṇātiprasaṅganidṛtyarthaṃ prakaraṇādityuktaṃ taditaraparicodanānavatāraprasaṅgādatitvaritoktamityupekṣaṇīyaṃ tāvat /
tantravārtika /
ārādapīti cet 
yadi hyānarthakyāllaukikāirhiṣo dharmanivṛttistato yatra tadānarthakya nāsti karmmāntarārthe barhiṣi tala pravṛttiḥ prāpnoti /
yadi tu kaścittannivṛtyartho hetu soṅageṣvapya viśiṣṭaḥ /
tatra sauryyādivitarathā 'pyatideśena santyeva dharmā ityupadeśātideśaprāptirahitatvātmigaḍapitṛyajña udāharaṇam /
apūrvo hyayamanaṅgaṃ ceti sthāsyati /
tenātyantāniṣṭaprasaṅga iti /
na tadākyaṃ hi tadarthatvāt 
bhavedetadyadīdaṃ vākya svatantraṃ syāirhi veṃdivaḍamarmāṇāṃ tu yadākya tadarśapūrgāmāsābhyāṃ sahaikaṃ tena vākona sahraikavākyatāṃ gatamityarthastena yattadekavākyāntagataṃ barhistasyaivaitaḍama prāptinna bhinnavākyagatasya /
na ca piṇḍa pitṛyajñabarhirdarśapūrṇamāsavākyāntargatamato na saṃbhansyata iti /
nanu yadi darśapūrgāmāsābhyāṃ sa hai kavākyatvamiṣyate tatastatprakaraṇaṃ mukkā nāgyena labhyate taraca prakaraṇaṃ pradhānamātrasyaivetyaṅgānāmasaṃbandhaḥ prāpnoti /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
sarvathā lavanakhananādayaḥ tāvanna sācādaṅagena pradhānena vā saṃbandhuṃ śaknuvanti yava vedibarhiṣī tatra gamiṣyanti vedibarhiṣorapi havirāsādanena saṃbandhaḥ /
tacca darśapūrṇamāmaprayogavacanagṛhītamāsādanaṃ saṃbadhyate evamaṅga havirāsādanamapi tatrāntargataṃ sāgasya pradhānasyaika prayogatvāt /
nanu ca yathā prayājādaya ekaprayogavacanagṛhītatve 'pi guṇānāṃ ca parārthatvādityevaṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pāda /
parasparāṅagatvaṃ na pratipadyante tathāṅa gahaviḥmaṃbandhaṃ bahinna pratipadyate /
naitadevama /
yathaiva hi pradhānahavirāsāinamaṅagatayā saṃbadhyate tathāṅa gahavirāmodanamapi aṅa gāṅagatayā saṃbhansyate /
yadi ca yadarśapūrṇamā sārthaṃ havistaddarhiṣyāsādayatītyevaṃ kalpyata tatastanmātrasyaiva syānna tvevamasyānarthakya bhayāttu svarūpe'tikramyamāṇe kimevamatikramo'stu sa darśapūrṇāṃmāsārthamuta yaddapūrṇamāsopakāroti /
yadi tādarthyaṃ gṛhyate vākāsyātidūraṃ saṃkocaḥ kriyeta /
tadupakāritvagrahaṇe tu bahutara viṣayatvaṃ bhavati /
yathā ca tadbhavati tadanugrahotavyam /
aṅgāṅgamapi vinā'pi tādarthyena tadupakāroti vijñāyate /
tāvanmāvameva ca tadddārayuktaṃ na tādarthyam anupakāriṇi hi sthitaṃ nopakaroti nātadayeṃ tathā ca parāyeṃ tvarthatāmānyamiti vakṣyati /
vinā 'pi tādarthyenābhyuditeṣṭyāṃ dadhipayasostadupakāramāvadarśanātmaṇautādharmaprāptirbhavatoti /
tasmādevaṃ prakaraṇādekavākyatvaṃ kalpyate yasminnakriyamāṇe darśapūrṇamāsāpūrvaṃ na sidhyati taba tatva kataṃvyā iti śraṅgahavirbhirapi ca viguṇaiḥ pradhānāpūrvaṃ na niṣpadyate /
tasmātpradhānāpūrvaprayuktānā mevā'ṅgeṣvapi kriyā yukteti /
liṅgadarśanācca 
yadi caivaṃjātīyakamaṅgapradhānārthaṃ tataḥ prayājaśeṣeṇa havīṃṣyabhivārathatītyetadaṅgapradhānārtham /
tatra ca kramavākya ṣvayaṃ kramo nyāyaprāptaḥ siḍabaducyamāno hetuvannigado 'rthatvādupapadyate sa vai bhruvāmevāi 'bhighāratantravārtike yati /
kutastato hi prathamāvājyabhāgau yaccanbhavatīti /
yadyājābhāgahavirapyabhighāraṇoyaṃ tata evaṃ vaktavyam /
anyathā hi bhuvāyāmupāṃśuyājārthena kevalamabhidhāraṇaṃ syāt /
tatra na cāye 'bhivāraṇaṃ syānna ca tato hi prathamāvājyabhāgāviti hetuḥ samadhyḙta /
tasmātsarvārthatvamiti /
phalasaṃyogātta svāmiyukta pra dhānasya 
yājamānāstu tatpradhānatvātkambhavadityanenādhikaragona yeṣāṃ yājamānatvaṃ siddhaṃ te kiṃ yajamānasya ka tṛtvāṃśenāṅagapradhānāthī uta bhoktṛtvāṃśena kevalapradhānātha iti /
kiṃ prāptaṃ pūrveṇādhikarīna sarvārthatvaṃ savarthe hi yajamāne 'vasthitāḥ śaknuvanti sarveṣāmupakarttuṃ na ca vyāvṛttikāraṇa mastauti prāpte 'bhiṣoyate /
yenetra hetunaiteṣāṃ svāmigāmitvaniścayaḥ /
tenaiva tu pradhānārthapratipattirapi sphuṭā 
graṅa gāṅa gibhāve hi yūpo vā vedyaṅgaṃ bhavet vedirvā yūpāṅgaṃ na caikamapyupapadyate nirākāṅacatvādadṛṣṭakalpanāt vākyabhedaprasaṅagācca /
na tāvatpaśubandhavyāpṛtasya yūpasya vediṃ pratyapekṣā 'sti /
nāpi karṭahavistadupakaraṇa dhāraṇatryāpṛtāyā vede sahasrabhāgāṃśasaṃbandhini yūpe 'pekṣā na cānyatarasya dṛṣṭopakāritvamava kalpate /
kiṃ cāīṃ bahiveṃdautyaśiṣyaṃ vidhyanuvādatvāsaṃbhavāttvatpace /
matyace tu dvābhyāṃ vinā deśaviśeṣopalakṣaṇāsaṃbhavādavaśayaṃ śāsitavyametat /
kathaṃ samastasya yūtantravārtika /
pasyāntarbahirvā māne prāpte īmantaveṃdauti niyamyate dvitīya sthāīsya punarapyaniyamaprasaktau aīṃ bahiveṃdotyapi vidhātavyam /
tataścānekārthatvāḍākyabhedo minotyākhyātānuṣaṅa gakleśaca prasajyate /
pākṣikasya ca nityavadanuvādo 'narthaka kalpayitavyaḥ /
nanu cāīsyāntaveṃdisaṃbandhe vihite vidhyabhāvādarḍāntaraṃ bahirvedi bha viṣyati /
bhavedevaṃ yadi nityamantarvedi bahiveṃdova vā yūpamānaṃ prasakta syātsamastāntarvediprasaṅage hisatyaīpunarvacana sāmarthyātparisaṃkhyāyetarasya bahirmānaṃ ga myeta samastasya vā bahireva prasaṅage 'sthāvihitamiti tadavasya mantara madhyavasoyeta /
na tvetadubhayamadhyasti /
ataścedvaśamavadhāraṇamardhamantarvedova na tvaīmevāntaveṃdoti tathā sati cāntaramaniyatatvātkaṭā cidantarapi prāpnotīti na bahirbhāva miyatīti /
nanu ca yadi samastamantarveti minoti tato 'īmantarvedauti evaṃ vidhinaiva kuryyāt /
kathaṃ na karoti yadaī tattāvantriyamato 'ntaminotyetāvaca vihitaṃ netaratpratiṣidhaṃ tasmādubhāgyāṃ viśiṣṭa eko deśo 'bhidhīyate ityetramavākyabhedaḥ /
sāmidhenaustadanvāhariti havi nayorvacanātsāmidhenīnām 
sadasyo hi bhedena varotavya eva na ca brahmā sadasya śabdenocyate /
ṛtuyajane mati varagona rivaktvaniyamāda dakṣiṇābhāga saṃbandhaddādaśāhadīkṣāvākyayoścāsaṃkīrttanāhatvigiti nocyate /
yathā satyapi varaṇe ṛtuyajanasaṃbandhe ca kāraṇahayāsaṃbhavācca masādhvayaṃva ṛtvijo noktāḥ /
svāminastu yadyapi ca varaṇaṃ nāsti tathā 'pyanyatsarvaṃmastīti yuktamutviktvam /
yattu sadasyo'pi pratyavekṣaṇādyajatīti /
vacanasāmarthyādevāsau briyate na tu kaścitpadārthastadadhīnaḥ yenāsya vyapadeśaḥ syānna ca pratyavekṣaṇaṃ nāma kaścitpadārtho yenāsya karṭa viśeṣaḥ kena citpramāṇena niyasyeta /
tasmātsatyeva sadasye suktaṃ svāmisaptadaśā iti /
yattu bhāṣyakāreṇa kiṃcitsadasyanirākaraṇaparamukta tahatviktvanirākaraṇa parasyātirabhasavacanamityupekṣaṇīyam /
te sarvārthāḥ prayuktatvādagnayaśca svakālatvāt 
evaṃ kartabhedaṃ pratipādodānoṃ samākhyāviniyogasya pūrvapakṣaṃ racayati sma tatva te sarvārthā iti/
na jñāyate kiṃ kratṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pāda /
svarthapuruṣārthābhiprāyasuta kratvarthasarvārthābhiprāyam tacā'pi kiṃ vākyasaṃyukta sarvārthā utā'saṃyukta sarvārthāḥ /
yadi tāvatū puruṣārthā apotyabhiprāyaḥ sa varaṇabharaṇayoḥ prakaraṇāmnānena kratvarthatvādayuktaḥ /
uktaṃ hi /
prakaraṇa viśeṣāhā tadyuktasya tatsaṃskāro dravyavadivyādiṣu /
tathaikādaśe vakṣyati nirdeśādā vaidikānāṃ sthāditi /
tasmādevaṃ tāvanna sarvārthatvam /
nāpi saṃyukteṣu tānpuro 'dhvayaṃvibhajatītyādiśrutānāmanyeṣāmavataraṇamastīti /
yāni tvasaṃyuktāni kāryyāṇi tāni yatra tatra vede paṭhitāni yena kena citkartā yathāsāmarthyaṃ karttavyānauti sarvārthā /
prayuktasvāditi sarvāṇi hi kāryyāṇi śa knuvanti tānprayoktam /
tathā te 'pi kāryyāṇi sarvaṃ puruṣakāryyāmiti yadyatkarmaṇi puruṣaiḥ prāgvacanaviśeṣātasvasāmarthyena śakyate tattadityevaṃ yujyate na puruṣārthābhiprāyeṇa/
ye punarāhavanīyādayasteṣāṃ sarvārthatvamaprastutameva na ca prasaṅgāducyate /
khakālatvasya hetorapyasamarthatvāt /
na ca tasyottarapace kaścitpakṣasya hetova parāmarśo 'sti /
yadi ca laukikakāryyāpekṣayā sarvā yaṃtvamabhidhīyate tato vihāro laukikānāmarthaṃ sādhathetprabhutvādityutkā nirdeśādā vaidikānāṃ syādityava nirṇītatvādavicārthyam /
yadapi vedavihitāgnikāya sarvārthatvaṃ prakṛtivikṛtyoḥ tadapyagnisupanidhāya stuvate ityudāhṛtya viśaye laukikaṃ syātsarvārghaṭavānna vaidikamarthanirdeśāt /
tathotpattiritareṣāṃ viṣṇyāgnaunāṃ syāditi nirṇītatvādavicāryam /
siddhāntavacana mevaitannirākaraṇoktyabhāvāt /
tasmādevaṃ varṇyate /
naivedamagnīnāṃ sa tantravārtike varthatvaṃ pūrvapakṣīkṛtaṃ kiṃ tarhyadhikaraṇāntarasūvoktanyāyapra tipāditānumitapūrvapacaḥ siddhānta evāyaṃ sūtavākyabhedenocyate na caitadagnikāryāpecayā sarvārthatvaṃ kiṃ tarhi prakṛtivikṛtyapekṣayā /
tatvānārabhyavādanyāyenādhānavadeva pūrvottarapakṣau racayitavyau kimāhavanauyādayaḥ prakṛtyarthā āho khitsarvārthā iti /
tatra tatprakṛtyarthaṃ yathā 'nārabhyavādā prakṛtau vā dviruktatvādityevaṃ prāpte 'bhidhīyate agnayaḥ sarvārthāḥ prakṛtivikṛtyarthā bhaveyuḥ /
kutaḥ /
khakālatvātsvatantrotpattitvādityarthaḥ /
tadetadvarṇitaṃ sarvārthaṃ vā''dhānasya svakālatvādityava /
na tvetatsarva viṣayaṃ savārthatvamavakalpate /
dvāraṃ yeṣu parādhīnaṃ teṣu tatprātyapekṣayā /
prāpnuvantaudṛśā bhāvā na svatantrāḥ kathaṃ cana 
yat juhvati tadāhavanauye iti śrūyate na yadyajeranniti tenāvaśyamāhavanauyacodanayā tāvatpratīkṣitavyaṃ yāvaccaturabattaṃ juhoti yadgrahān juhoti yacacamasān juhotauti cātideśena saṃbandhāddāra prāptam /
tataścāhavanīyena sahaivāsyātideśataḥ /
prakṛtau vā viruktatvādityayaṃ niścayo bhavet 
hoṭaśabdastāvantra hauvanimitta iti rājaśabdavadeva pratyayalopaprātipadika pratyāpattyora smaraṇādavagatametat /
na ca rājaśabdādiva rājyaśabdo hoṭaśabdāḍautraśabdaḥ śakyaḥ kalpayituṃ na hi yathā tatra manvādibhiḥ kṣatriyasya ra kṣaṇaṃ vihitaṃ tadrājakarmatvena jñāyamānaṃ pratyayārthatvaṃ pra tipadyate tatheha kena citsāmidhenyanuvacanāde hoṭa kamatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ yantrimittā samākhyā syānna caivaṃ sati sabhākhyā viniyoktītya vasīyate /
kathaṃ tadya satyāmavayavavyatpatto viniyogaḥ /
uktametacchabdasārūpyamāvāditi /
na ttvetadaktam /
yadi hotuḥ kama hauvamiti evaṃ na byutpādyate tatāntareṇaiva kartṛkamasaṃbandhaṃ hṛvyā sārūpyasamākhyayorupapannatvānnārthāpattiḥ śrutiṃ kalpayanna hi va sannavārtika /
sāmānyamātreā śālāmālayoḥ kaścitsaṃbandhaḥ /
tathā ca vakṣyati/
na hi kaṇvarathantare rathaṃtarasabandhaḥ kaścidastīti /
yadapi ca kṛte rājñaḥ karmasaṃbandhe rājyaśabdaḥ pravarttataiti /
tadayukta saṃbandhasyā dimattvapramaṅgāt /
ta māyaiva tava nityayoreva śabdārthayonnityaeva saṃbandhe śāsvataḥ pratauyamāne sādhutvapratipattivelāyāṃ rājaśabdamanvākhyāya rājyaśabdo 'nvākhyāyamāno yaugikastantrimittaścocyamāno'pi nityanimittatvānnādimatvaṃ pratipadyate tathaivāla hauvamiti vṛddhidarśanāḍoṭaśabdāttasyedaṃ katyevamanvākhyānamiti gamyate /
kena tu tattasya kamrmāvagatamiti samākhyādarśanāttadeva tādṛśaṃ vacanamanumāsyāmahe /
nanvitaretarāśrayaṃ prāpnoti samākhyātastavacanaṃ tena te saṃyoge samākhyāsiddhiriti naiṣa doṣaḥ /
samākhyā tāvatpratītirupeṇa pratyakṣā / sā tu kena nimittena pravṛtteti pūrvapravṛttatayaiva nimittama paiṃcate/
na ca tadasti tasmānnūnamohaśī śrutirasti /
yathā hotrā karttavyametaditi sarveṣveva liṅgādiṣvevametadbhavatīti vyākhyātamato neteratarāśrayatvamiti /
nanu cedamākhyā caivaṃ tadarthatvā dityanenaivādhikaraṇena siddham /
satyaṃ siḍaṃ na tu tatra virodhāviradhau vicāritau /
iha tu yogyatvaprakaraṇa viśeṣātsarvārthatvaprasaktyā virodhamāśaya pa riharati uttaravivakṣayā vā'nuvadatītyapunaruktam /
tasyopadeśasamākhyānena nirdeśa 
viśeṣasamākhyā 'pi viśeṣaśrutivadeva śīghrataraprahatterbādhikā bhavati /
tabacca liṅgadarśanam 
sāmānyasamākhyā viniyogasyaivaitalliṅgam /
viśeṣasamākhyāyāṃ tu kiṃ cidanyahṛṣṭavyam /
praiṣānuvacanaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyopadeśāt 
upadeśātmihe samākhyābādhe samastaikadeśaviṣayaśvena vicāra /
jyotiṣṭomapra kara gāevaita ccyate /
ta smānmaivāvaruṇaḥ praiṣyati cānu cāheti pradarśanārthaṃ gnauṣomīyaityuktam /
tava sarvapraiṣāṇāmādhvaryyavatvaṃ sa rvānuvacanānāṃ ca hauvasamākhyānam /
tatkimanena upadeśena samastaviṣayaḥ samākhyayorbādha uta kka cideveti /
kiṃ prāpta praiṣānuvacanoddeśena maivāvaruṇopādānādṛddiśyamānayośca śabda pratipādita sāhityavivakṣā'nupapatteḥ śrūyamāṇañca caśabdaḥ samuccayānvācayamātraṃ pratipādayati netaretarayogasamāhārau nityaṃ samāsagamyatvāt /
na cehānvācayalakṣaṇa mubhayostulyatvādupapadyataiti samuccayaḥ syāt /
sa ca pṛthagapi sarveṣvanuṣṭhīyamāneṣu saṃbhavatyeveti sāmānyavacanātsarvapratyayaḥ puronuvākyā'dhikāro vā praiṣasa nidhānāt 
na sarvapraiṣānuvacaneṣvasau bhavet /
kva tarhi puro'nu/
preṣāntānyanuvacanāni puronuvākyastāśca prakṛtyetadvacanaṃ pravṛttam /
tasmānmaivāvaruṇa iti /
vākyāsutantravārtika /
tāca tādṛśyo hauaeva paṭhitā iti tasyaiba kevalasya prāpnuvanti /
yastu tāmāmante yajetiśabdaḥ sa iṣṭiprakṛti keṣu tāvadaṅgeṣvatideśenādhvaryyoḥ prāpnoti somayāgeṣvapi preṣeṣu ca parādhikārādityevaṃ nivarttamānasteṣāṃ yato viśeṣa syādityevaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyaivātha vā preṣakasyobhayatra karṭa tvāikṣyamāṇena nyāyena preṣyatvaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya kalpayitvā hotureva prāpnoti /
tathā 'dhvayo preṣyeti preṣāntarāmnānādājetyeṣa nivarttamāna pratiprasthātuḥ prāpnoti śeṣāṇi tu praiṣānuvacanāni nirjñātakarṭa viśeṣatvānnirākāṅkṣāṇyaveti na teṣa maivāvaruṇāvidhiḥ saṃbhavati /
puro'nuvākyānāṃ punarubhayāṃśapātivādekapadārthatvena ca nānākarṭa tvānupapatterhoturadhvayaśca pra cyavamānānāṃ sākāṅgatvasannidhānācca yukto maitvāvaruṇa vidhirevaṃ caśabdo 'pi saha prayogādapi prakṛṣṭārthaḥ samarthito bhavati prauṣasannidhānāt /
na ca praṣyetyādayo'pi praiṣāstasyaivātmaviṣayāḥ saṃbhavanti /
prātaranuvāke ca hoṭadarśanāt 
camasāṃścamasādhvayyavaḥ samākhyānāt 
unnayanāsādana homādiyāvatkiṃ cidadhvaryyoścamaseṣu prāpnoti tatsarvaṃ viśeṣasamākhyānāñcamasādhvayu bhiḥ karttavyam /
adhvaryu rvā tannyāyatvāt 
sā nāma viśeṣasamākhyā sāmānyasamākhyāṃ bāghate yā tannirapekṣā pravarttate camasādhvaryu samākhyā tu camaseṣvadhvaryya vad vṛttiṃ pratipādayati /
tadyadi tāvadadhvavyunnaiva juhuyānna tarhi tān juhutaste camasādhvaryyavo bhavanti /
kāmamajuhvata eva tahaḍbhāvaṃ labherannānyathā /
yadi tu sa juhoti tataḥ kadā cittasya vyāṭatatvenāśaktau satyāṃ te juhṛtastaddadbhaveyustasmājjuhotyadhvaryuḥ /
camase cānyadarśanāt 
vaṣaṭkāriṇaṃ prati prayojanāntarābhāvāgacāyeṃ nayane camasādhvarthya netāraṃ bruvannajatasya bhakṣaṇāsaṃbhavādya eva juhoti sa eva prayacchati bhakṣaṇārthaṃ taṃ ca grahotṛtvena camasādhvaryūgāṃ vyāpṛtatvāttebhyo 'nyamadhvaryuṃ darśayati /
aśaktī te pratoyeran 
vedopadeśātpūrvavaḍedānyatve ya thopadeśaṃ syuḥ 
guṇa mukhyavyatikrame tadarthatvāmukhyena vedasaṃyoga ityatra vyākhyātaṃ yathāṅgāni pradhāna vedavyapadeśaṃ labhantaiti /
tasmācchyene sarve padārthācodakaprāptā udgātṛbhiḥ karttavyā iti /
tadgrahaṇādā svadharmaḥ syādadhikārasāmarthyādavyaktaḥ śeṣe 
uktaṃ vakṣyate caitadyathā jaghanyakālatvātprayogaṣa canaścodakāddurbala iti prayogavacanāśrayā ca pradhānasamākhyā sā satyapi pratyakṣatve durbalā /
yāvaccātideśenāṅgāni prāpyante tāvatkasya karttāraṃ niyacchati yadā tu prāptāni bhavanti tadaiṣāṃ klṛptakartṛsaṃbandhānna kaṃdā cidapekṣeti kiṃ samākhyā kariṣyati /
na cātra prāptabādho bhavati śrutikalpanena samākhyāyā vimakṛṣṭatvāt /
utaṃ hyetadyathā klṛptamūlānāṃ pramāṇānāṃ prāptabādho bhavati na kalpyamūlānāmiti /
tasmātmākṛtagrahagona tadadhikārasāmarthyāj jyotiṣṭomavadeva nānākartṛkaḥ syādyadyapi ca prakṛtāvapi samākhyayaiva nānākarttārastathā 'pi klṛptasaṃbandhatvādiha śrutitulyatā /
yattvaprākṛtaṃ kiṃ cidānāyate tasya pradhānasamākhyātaḥ karttā bhaviṣyatīti darśayannāha avyaktaḥ śeṣaiti /
aklṛptāvasthatvādavyakto 'yaṃ karṭa saṃbandhaḥ klṛptādanyava bhavitumarhati /
na tvasya viṣaya samyagdṛśyate /
karāṭakavinodanādauni yaddā pradhānasamākhyāte vede paṭhyante vedāntare vā yadi tāvattatraiva tataḥ samākhyayaiva teṣāṃ kartṛsaṃbandho na pradhānadvāreṇātha tu vedāntare paṭhyante tataḥ pratyakṣatve satyapi tayaiva viśeṣasamākhāyā balīyasyā bhavitavyam /
athātrāpi guṇamukhāvyatikramanyāya śrāśrauyate tataḥ stotraśastrādaunāṃ jyotiṣṭomasyādhvarthyavasamākhānādadhvaryyakartā kastvaprasaṅgaḥ /
na cātra mandraṃ prātaḥsavanaityādivatsamādhānamasti tasmānna pradhānenāṅgeṣu vasamākhagrā bādhyate /
sā tvautpattikena karṭa saṃbandhena viniyuktārthā satī pradhānena gṛ hyate na cāṅgānāṃ pradhānahāreṇādhvarthyavādisamākhagrā yujyate /
na hi pradhānānyādhvarthyavādisamākhayābhiryujyante tṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pāda /
guṇabhūteṣu kaṭaṃ vyāpārāt /
yā ca pradhāneṣu na vyāpṛtā sā sahāreṇāṅgeṣvavataroṣyatīti kuta etat /
ṛgvedādisamākhā pradhāneṣvaṅgeṣu cāviruḍā /
tena kriyate iti ca tatra vyapadeśaḥ /
sa ca pradhānaprayogavacanena vidheyatvādaṅgeṣu yujyate pāṭhakṛtā cādhvaryyavādisamākhā sā yathāpāṭhameva bhavitumarhati /
na cātra guṇasukhāvyatikramanyāyenānabhyupagatena kiṃ cidduṣyati /
kaṇṭakavinodanādayaśca pradhāna vedasamānotpattaya eva draṣṭavyāḥ /
tadātmanā ca śakyamavyaktaḥ śeṣaiti vaktuṃ nāvaśyaṃ pradhānādevāvatarantī samākhagrā 'nugṛhyate sākṣādanugrahe 'pyananugrahe 'pi vā 'nyāṅgeṣu kṛtārthatvenāvirodhāttana prākṛtāsavyatirikteṣu samākhagrā viniyoktīti siddham /
tṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pāda /tantravārtike /
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ /
svāmika parikrayaḥ kammaṇastadarthatvāt 
samākhāpavādatvenaitadapi vicāryyate /
kiṃ parikraya mādhvardhyavādiṣvāmnānātta samākhātaiḥ puruṣaiḥ kataṃvya uta svāmineti /
siī tvetasminnanyo vā syātparikrayāmnānādityetaddṛṣṭavyam /
tathā svāminā laukika upāya āstheyo yathā dhvadayaḥ svadravyeṇetarānparikrauṇate samākhānugrahārthamiti prāpte 'bhidhoyate /
laukikāśrayaṇaṃ tava yatra nānyo 'sti vaidikaḥ /
vaidike dakṣiṇādāne sati kiṃ laukikāśrayaḥ 
ṛtviguddeśena hote vidhīyamānāḥ pratipradhānāvṛttinyāyātsarveṣāṃ bhavanto na śakyā samākhyayā bādhitum /
tasmādiha na vyavasthā sthāditi tathā kāmo 'rthasaṃyogāt 
pradhānakāmasya yajetetyātmanepadātyāmānādhikaraṇyādādhānagatāccātmanepadāvyadhāna kartaviṣayatve 'nyataḥ siddhe ye guṇakāmāḥ sadomānaviśeṣādiṣu śrutāsteṣu minuyādityanena samānakartṛtvādaviruḍayā samākhyayā 'dhvaryuviṣayatve prāpte pradhānagatenātmanepadena samasta prayogaviṣayaḥ phalasaṃbandho yajamānaviṣayo 'vagamyataiti yadi kāmayeta yajamāna iti prakaraṇodavadhāye tajñāgitvaṃ gamyate /
tathā cādhvaryyavyāpāra parasmaipadamupapasyate 'nyathā ḍumiñprakṣepaṇa ityasya karjabhiprāyakriyāphalavivacāyāṃ ñittvādātmanepadaṃ syāt /
anayā ca śrutyā sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ vākyagamyaṃ bādhitamityadoṣastahaśena vo yajamānaprārthanānusāro yo 'dhvaryyo kāma eṣa meṃ yajamāno vṛṣṭiṃ prāpnuyāditi tadapekṣayā sāmānādhikaraṇyamaviruī tathāśabdena ca pūrvādhikaraṇā detāvadatidiśyate samākhyayā na niyamyataiti /
vyapadeśāditareṣāṃ syāt 
anyatra vacanāditareṣāṃ syādiha tādṛśasya vacanasyābhāvādyapadeśādityucyate /
vāśabdopādanādyajamānavyatirekeṇa cātmagrahaṇāccaturthyā ca vispaṣṭatādarghyaprasauterātmane vā yajamānāya veti kartṛdayasya phalasaṃbandha iti śakyaṃ vijñātum /
mantrāścākamakaraṇāstadvat 
akamasaṃyuktā āśīmantrā samākhyayā niya gyante na hi tebhyaḥ phalaniṣpattimantrāṇāmavidhāyakatvādanyasya ca phalakalpanāhetorasaṃbhavāt /
yattvāśāsanaṃ tadyajamānavadadhvaryyoratyutsāha karatvenā viśiṣṭa miti prāple yājamānā ityacyate /
te hi phalāntarābhāvāvyadhānaphalaprāptimāśāsate /
yajamānena ca tadāśāsanauyaṃ naṭivajā tadīyasya dakṣiṇālā bhasyānyathā 'pi mihatvādyajamānācca labhyamānatvenāgneraprārthanauyatvāt /
atha yajamānārthamevāsau prārthayata tatva āyurme dehītyātmaviṣayaṃ sahiruḍayota /
tasmādyajamānenaiva pradhānaphalaprāptirūpeṇāmotsāhanārthe prayoktavyā iti /
viprayoge ca darśanāt 
āśīmanvaṃ ca pravasadyajamānāgnihotreṣvagnyupa tanvavārtika /
sthānārthaṃ proṣitasya darśayati na cartvijaḥ proṣitasya ṛtvikva saṃbhavati kama saṃyogābhāvādyajamānasya tu dravyatyāgenopapadyate /
tasmāttatmāmānyāditareṣu tathātvam /
hyāmnāteṣūbhau dyāmnānasyārtha vattvāt 
jyagrahaṇādimanveṣu sāmānyenādhvaryyave punarviśeṣeṇa yājamāne kāṇḍe paṭhyamāneṣu kimubhau prayokkāro vikalpena samuccayena vā athānyatara iti /
tatrādhvaryyavatve vikalpe vā prāpte dāvityāha /
nanu ca viśeṣasamākhyānātkevalayājamānattvameva syāt /
tatra vayaṃ viśeṣasamākhyāṃ baloyasomicchāmo yatva sakṛdāmnānaṃ ye tu sāmānye viśeṣe ca bhedenāmrāyante teṣu yadi viśeṣasamākhyā 'ṅgīkriyate tataḥ sāmānyapāṭhasyānarthakyameva syādekaviṣayatve ca sāmānyaṃ viśeṣo bāghate satyapi tvatva mantrābhede pāṭhabhedāddiṣayānyatvaṃ pāṭhasya hi bhedena prayojanaṃ kalpayitavyam /
na ca tadubhayaprayojyatvādanyatsaṃbhabati tasmādubhāvapauti /
nanu iyo pāṭhayorekaḥ svarūpaprajñāpanārtha itaro viniyogārtha syāttatrāpi mantrāṇāṃ kamaprakāśanārthatvādaṅga pradhānānāṃ ca samānakartakatvādya vaivājyagrahaṇādi kāryamāmrātaṃ tatraiva samākhyātenaiva karcā viniyogo yuktastatraiva ca mantrasya pra yojyatvenāvagatasya kartṛviśeṣākāṅkṣā bhavati netarava /
rūpamātraprajñāpanasyāntareṇā'pi karmakālaprayogamadhyayanamātreṇaiva sidatvādājyagrahaṇādi cāsaṃdigdha mādhvaryyavam /
tasmānna yajamānena prayoktavyā iti /
uccate /
yājamāne 'pi rūpamābādevāntareṇāpi kāryyaṃ prayojyatvenāvadhāraṇādastyeva karttapekṣeti yajamānakarṭa tvasiddhiḥ /
kiṃ punasteṣāṃ prayujyamānānāṃ prayojyatvam /
ucyate /
yathaivādhvaryuṃṇā padārthāḥ karttavyāstathaiva yajamānenāpramādārthe pratyavecitavyāttāva mantrā nāmrāyante tatropāyāntareṇa pratyavekṣyate iha tu mantrairityarthavattā /
jñāte ca vācanaṃ na hyavidvānvihito 'sti 
yatva yajamānaṃ vācayatīti śrūyate tatvāviddānapi khaṇḍaśa śakyo vācayitumityaniyamaḥ atha vā vihānsvayameva brūyāt /
tatra prayojakavyāpāravaiyarghyaṃ bha vettammādavidvāneva vācayitavya iti prāpte 'bhidhīyate na hyanviānvihito 'stauti /
yadi kāmaśrutiparigṛhītaṃ vedādhyayanaṃ bhavettataḥ prayogakāle 'pyadhyāpyeta tattvādhānavadanāramya vidhīyate tasmātyādhyāyo 'dhyetavya iti /
tathā sati cārthāpatyabhāvātsidamevedaṃ sarvakarmāṇyagnivad gṛhṇanti na śikṣaṇaṃ prayuñjate na ca śikṣito vedo bhavati tasmātmākarmaṇo ye mantrāḥ paṭhitāsteṅgatvaṃ pratipadyantaiti nāviduṣo 'dhikāro ' /
śakyate ca tatrāpi praiṣavatprayojakavyāpārasyārthavattā satyāmapi śaktāvaprayuktī na brūyāditi/
tacca prayojakatvaṃ devā bhavati yadi vā khaṇḍaśaḥ samarpyate 'tha vā brūhotyabhidhīyate iti /
yatheṣṭaṃ karmma kiyatā punaviṃditeneti vaiśeṣikādayaḥ svatantravārtike /
śākhaṇāpyanadhigatenānadhikāraṃ vadantīti spaṣṭanirūpaṇārthaṃ pṛcchati /
tatra vidvattāyāḥ śaktyutpādanahāreṇa pratyaceṇaivopakāritvādyāvatā viditenetyāha /
yadyapi svādhyāyagrahaṇena sakalo vedaḥ parigṛhītastathā 'pi darśapūrṇamāsau kurvāṇasya jyautiṣṭomikamantrabrāhmaṇaṃ na ka cidupayujyataiti asadapi nādhikāraṃ vyāvarttayati iṣṭivedenaiva yogyatāyāḥ siddhatvāttena tadyājinastāvānena svādhyāyaḥ /
yattvasau sakalaḥ paṭhyate tannityakāmyanaimittikānāṃ karmaṇāṃ yathopapannakālatvānna jñāyate kataratkadā kariṣyataiti tatra kadā cidyanna paṭhitaṃ tatphalaprārthanā nimittaṃ vā 'syopajāyate tatva tadaviddattvādaśaknuvanvihanyate tadāna vā 'dhīyānasya vrataniyamavadadhyayanāsaṃbhavātkama bhiśva viśiṣṭakriyopāttavedanirākāṅkṣastādṛśasyāgrahaṇa haiguṇya prasaṅgaḥ /
kāma śrutyaparigrahāca sarvairanārabhyavādavidhyadhauto vedo 'pekṣita ityavaśyaṃ brahmacaryyakālaeva samasto vedo 'dhyetavyo yadi tu kaścidaṃśakto nādhaute sakalamagnihovadarśapūrṇamāsamātraṃ kathaṃ cidadhigacchati na tasya tatvānadhikāraḥ /
evaṃ ca sati bāhyajñānaṃ dūraviprakṛṣṭameva /
yattvātmajñānaṃ tena vinā pravṛttireva nāstyataḥ sarvakarmārthamaṅgokarttavyam /
tu yājamāne samākhyānātkammaṇi yājamānaṃ syuḥ 
ukhādhiśrayaṇāvahantyādīnāṃ hādaśānāṃ karmahandrānāṃ yājamānaādhvaryyave ca paṭhitānāṃ dyāmnātamantravadubhābhyāṃ prayoktumaśakyatvādyājamānasamākhyānāyajamānakaṭakatvamiti /
adhvaryurvā tadartho hi nyāyapūrvaṃ samākhyānam 
anutpannānāṃ indatvāpādanāśaktervighāyakaśabdābhāvācca naiṣāṃ yājamānaevotpattiḥ kiṃ tahyadhvaryyave /
tatra ca karjākāṅkṣā tadarthaśca parikraya ityavagate karttari na indāmnānavelāyāmapekṣā istoti yajamānakartṛtvānupapattiḥ tatra svarūpasyāsati yajamānasaṃbandhe indratā yājamānī kiyeta /
na ca sā karttantareṇa kriyamāṇānāṃ saṃbhavati samāsanna karaṇaṃ hi indatā na cānyakartṛkāṃ krayāmanyaḥ samāsannāṃ karttuṃ samarthaḥ na ca samāsannakaraṇānurodhena kriyāsvarūpamapi yājamānaṃ saṃbhavati /
a to 'ṅgaguṇavirodhanyāyāttadapyādhvaryyavameva yajamānastu ārayiṣyati indatāmiti samākhyā'rthavattā /
vipratiṣedhe karaṇaḥ samavāyaviśeṣāditaramanyasteṣāṃ yato viśeṣa syāt 
parivīrasi yuvā suvāsā ityetayoḥ karaṇakriyamāṇānuvādinoradhvaryyaṇā hovā ca yugapatyakṛtau prayuktayo kuṇḍapāyināmayane hauvādhvaryyavayoreka kartṛkatvādaśakteravaśyāva heye 'nyatarasminkataraḥ parigṛhyatāmiti saṃdehastavāniyamaḥ prāpnoti /
yaddā hotuḥ siddhatantravārtike /
svasyādhvayaivavidhānādajahatsvadharmatayā hauava yakta iti prāpte 'bhidhīyate /
etasminvipratiṣedhe karaṇaḥ prayoktavyaḥ kutaḥ samavāyaviśeṣāttatra ke cidāhu /
pradhānapratyātattiḥ samavāyaviśeṣa iti /
bahiraṅgo dhārādupakārakarūpatvātkriyamāṇānuvādī karaṇastvantaraṅga iti /
tadakaraṇaṃ yadi hi pradhānadāregāṅgeṣu karttā vitarettataḥ sannikarṣaviprakarṣāvupayujyeyātāṃ sa tu samākhyayā codakena ca pradhāneṣvaṅgeṣu cāviśeṣeṇa lakṣyate na kaścidaṅgagugavirodhanyāyaḥ ubhayoraṅgatvāviśeṣānna ca sannipātitvena kriyāntaragatamārā dupakāritvaṃ durbalaukriyate /
na cāyamatauvārādapakārakaḥ kriyamāṇaparivyāṇa smṛtyavicchedena dṛṣṭasaṃskārajananāttammādānumānikāḍaunasaṃbandhātmatya catvenaivā dhvaṭī vasya samavāyasya viśeṣo bhavati /
katham /
eṣā hyatra vacanavyaktiyyaduta hovādayaḥ śrutivṛttā adhvarvādiśabdalaciteṣu karmasu vidhīyante /
tatra hotrasaṃbandho hotuganumānika ādhvaryya va saṃvandhastu pratyakṣaḥ /
yattvajahatsvadharma eva hotā''dhvaryyavegā saṃbadhyataiti /
saṃbadhyeta yadi tatprayogamātrakṛtamevāsya hotṛtvaṃ bhavedyadi vā hauvaṃ pratyadhvayurvidhīyeta hotāraṃ voddiśyādhvarthya, kamavidhirbhavenna tu tatsarvamasti /
hotā tāvadyogyatāmātreāvadhāritaḥ satyapi ca kamenimitatve 'nyāni sahasrāṇi tadupalakṣaṇaṃ kariṣyanti /
na ca hautraṃ pratyadhvaryuṃ vidhiriha hovadha॒ryuṃ śabdayoratyanta vibhinnapuruṣavacanayomukhyasāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvādanyatarasyāvaśyakalpanīye lakṣaṇāvṛttave virodhanimittatvālla caṇā kalpanāyāḥ prathamoccārite hoṭaśabde kiṃ cidapi kalpanābaujaṃ na paśyāmastena mukhyaṃ vā 'pūrvaṃcodanāditi taṃ svārthavṛttameva gṛhītvā 'dhvaryuśabdaḥ karmalakṣaṇārtho'dhyavasauyate /
tatrāpi taduddiśya hotā viṣauyate taḍi kratvarthena prayojanavanna tathā kartā pradhānaṃ caivaṃjātīya ke ṣūddiśyate /
tataśca guṇabhūto hotopadīyamāno yaḥ pradhānāvirodho dharmatanmātrayukta eva saṃbadhyate /
yadi tu hoturādhvayaṃ vaṃ vidhoyeta tatastasya karmāviruī tatpravarttataiti na kiṃ cidapi hautraṃ hāpayedaprākṛtakartṛ saṃskāratvaprasaṅgāñcādhvaryavasya naivaṃ saṃbandha iti pacāntaramabalambitam /
tasmādādhvaya basaṃbandha eva pratyakṣaḥ pradhānaṃ ceti siddham /
atra codayanti naivātvānyatarasthāpi mantrasya hoṭasaṃbandho bādhitavyaḥ /
kutaḥ /
ekakālaprayoge hi virodho manvayorbhavet /
karaṇa prāk kriyātastu parataścetaraḥ sthitaḥ 
iti śrobhaṭṭakumārilakṛtau maumāṃsāvāti ke tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ //
samāptaṃ cedaṃ tantravārtikam /
śubhamastu /
